Nehemiah3:3 Kodukoto odwe luka Kasenaa erute loka Lukecor; kopesikis abaoike, kosipokis ikiriginike, ka igolisike, ka atiketake." 
Psalms40:15 Kosilikis, kanuka ileicikec Lukesuanarete ebe, “Uus, Uus!”" 
SongOfSongs4:14 Lukesai ka saparon, Akalamus ka akinomon, ka ikito kere lukisupurununo; Emina ka icicikwa, ka lueuru ma kere luitelekarito aiokis." 
Jeremiah15:2 Kosodi kanen arai kiremarete jo atiar, ‘Ai bo kilomaria?’ Ŋes konyet ilimokinia kes ebe, ‘Ebala EJAKAIT kwanata ebe: Lukatular neejai atular; Lukekilen, neejai ekileŋ; Luketenei neejai eteŋei: Ido luijoreorio neejai aijoreorio,’”" 
Jeremiah17:13 Wu EJAKAIT, amun naka Isirael, Lukinyeinete ijo kere irumete rwaru ileic; Lukenyounete kere kaneijai iwadikao toma alup, Naarai enyeis EJAKAIT, Atan naka akipi nukajarak." 
Jeremiah51:47 “Aso koany, epote apaarasia, Nuetepesenia aputosia nuegerer nuko Babulon; Irumete akwapuke kere ileje; Luke kere lueario ibirokinos kidinike." 
Lamentations1:12 “Mam ca ma ipodosi, yes kere luitubonoros? Koanyutu, kosesenata, Arai ejaas iean kere lueriakas ka ieanika, Lukeswamakin eoŋ, luketicania eoŋ EJAKAIT, Kotoma apaaran naka anyunyurake naededen," 
Ezekiel23:6 Lukenapenenete lubulului, ikayaitok ka ijaka, kes kere ikarumunak luimielai, ikebwanenok luibwanenete ibalasin." 
Matthew1:1 Eitabo loka aturio nuka Yesu Kristo, okoku loka Daudi, okoku loka Aburaam." 
Matthew1:2 Aburaam kouri Isaak, Isaak kouri Yakob, Yakob kouri Yuda ka ikeinacan;" 
Matthew1:3 Yuda kouri Peres ka Sera kama ka Tamar; Peres kouri Kesuron; Kesuron kouri Ram; 
Matthew1:4 Ram kouri Aminadab; Aminadab kouri Nason; Nason kouri Salumon; 
Matthew1:5 Salumon kouri Boas kama ka Rakab; Boas kouri Obed kama ka Rusi; Obed da kouri Yese; 
Matthew1:6 Yese kouri Daudi ekabaka. Daudi kouri Solomon kama kaŋin nakerai aberu naka Uria; 
Matthew1:7 Solomon kouri Rekoboam; Rekoboam kouri Abiya; Abiya kouri Asa; 
Matthew1:8 Asa kouri Yekosapat; Yekosapat kouri Yoram; Yoram kouri Usia; 
Matthew1:9 Usia kouri Yotam; Yotam kouri Akas; Akas kouri Kesekia; 
Matthew1:10 Kesekia kouri Manase; Manase kouri Amon; Amon kouri Yosia; 
Matthew1:11 Yosia kouri Yekonia ka ikeinacan, apak naka aijoreorio Babulon," 
Matthew1:12 Kokau kaijoreorio Babulon abu Yekonia kouri Sealutiel; Sealutiel kouri Serubabel; 
Matthew1:13 Serubabel kouri Abiud; Abiud kouri Eliakim; Eliakim kouri Asor; 
Matthew1:14 Asor kouri Sadok; Sadok kouri Akim; Akim kouri Eliud; 
Matthew1:15 Eliud kouri Eleasar; Eleasar kouri Matan; Matan kouri Yakob; 
Matthew1:16 Yakob kouri Yosep ekile loka Mariam, naauriei Yesu loenyaritai Kristo." 
Matthew1:17 Kwaŋin aturio kere ameun ka Aburaam kiton Daudi emwaasi aturio atomon ka nuoŋon, ameun ka Daudi da kiton aijoreorio Babulon aturio atomon ka nuoŋon, ameun da kaijoreorio Babulon kiton Kristo aturio atomon ka nuoŋon." 
Matthew1:18 Aurio naka Yesu Kristo ekoni ne. Kedau Yosep aisiner Mariam totoke, koriŋa ejenakina, kotakan ŋesi ejai akoik naka Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
Matthew1:19 Konye ekileke Yosep kineru ainyein ŋes kaiyeiyea naarai korai ekiliokit loedolit, komam ekoto aisurum ŋes ileic," 
Matthew1:20 Konye nakeomoomaa ŋun, koany, kitakanikin ŋes emalaika loka Ejakait kotoma airujasit, ebala ebe, “Yosep, okoku loka Daudi, sirikiyoŋ aimany Mariam; naarai akepotuun erai naka Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
Matthew1:21 Idouni ŋesi ikoku yenisapat, imaikini ekekiror Yesu, naarai ŋes itajari iketuŋa kadiakanaretakec.”" 
Matthew1:22 Iswamatai nu kere, tetere edoli akirot naenerit Ejakait kama ka enabi ebe:" 
Matthew1:23 “Koany, epotuuni abekot, idouni ikoku yenisapat, Emaikinete ekekiror Imanuel” (apolouke ebe, Edeke ejai kaoni)." 
Matthew1:24 Nakenyounio Yosep kajoo, kiswama kwape kicorakinia emalaika loka Ejakait, komany akeberu;" 
Matthew1:25 mam abu kojen ŋes aitodol naauria ikoku yenisapat; komaik ekekiror Yesu. 
Matthew2:1 Nakeurii Yesu koBetelekem loka Yudaya kapaarasia nuka Kerode ekabaka, koany, kodolut lukacoa lukepote kokide Yerusalem," 
Matthew2:2 kobalas ebe, “Ai bo ejai ŋol lokeurio Ekabaka loka Iyudayan? Naarai kipou kaanyutu aaceritike kokide, ido kiponit isio aima ŋes.”" 
Matthew2:3 Nakepupunio Kerode ekabaka ŋun, kiyaloŋoŋ, ka luko Yerusalem da kere nepepe kaŋes." 
Matthew2:4 Kotukonok isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak luka ituŋa kere, kiŋitana kes netieurikinitai Kristo." 
Matthew2:5 Kolimokis ŋes ebe, “Toma Betelekem loka Yudaya, naarai iwadikat enabi kwaŋin ebe," 
Matthew2:6 ‘Ka jo da Betelekem, akwap naka Yuda, Mam irai loidite kokapolok luka Yuda; Naarai kotomakon elomuni ekayaiton, Loicokiei ikatuŋa Isirael.’ ”" 
Matthew2:7 Kosodi konyarau Kerode lukacoa kaiyeiyea, kinyikok aiŋitiŋit kes apak nakitaanyikinor aacerit." 
Matthew2:8 Kijuka kes Betelekem, kotema atiar, “Koloto, komoata ikoku kainyikokin; kidaut aanyun ŋes, kitejenut eoŋ akiro, tetere eoŋ da alosi aima ŋes.”" 
Matthew2:9 Nakedauniata apupun akiro nuka ekabaka, koloto; ido koany, kiŋarenik kes aacerit ya nakeanyunete kokide, aitodol neabwoia kaibois kanaajai ikoku," 
Matthew2:10 Nakeanyuniata aacerit kiyalamikinos aiyalama naepol noi. 
Matthew2:11 Kolomasi togo, koanyut ikoku ka Mariam totoke; kibiroros komaata ŋes; kosodete kopukosi ikeceboro lukakais, kijaikis ŋes ainakineta, esabu ka lukisupurununo ka luesaete." 
Matthew2:12 Kosodi kikwenya kes Edeke kairujasit ebe sirikeboŋosi mama ejai Kerode, koboŋosi obukec kecerot." 
Matthew2:13 Nakedauniata kesi aekar, kitakanikin emalaika loka Ejakait Yosep kotoma airujasit, kobala ebe, “Konyou, koyaŋa ikoku ka totoke, kokeria Misiri, kiboie kaŋina aitodol nekalimokinia: naarai ekot Kerode amoun ikoku amudiar.”" 
Matthew2:14 Konyou ŋesi, koyaŋa ikoku ka totoke kuare, koloto Misiri;" 
Matthew2:15 kiboi kaŋina aitodol neatwania Kerode; tetere edoli akirot nakinerit Ejakait kama ka enabi ebe, “Abu kanyarau okokuka koMisiri.”" 
Matthew2:16 Kosodi nakeanyunia Kerode ebe amodata lukacoa, konyunyurikin noi, kiyakia ituŋa aiar idwe kere lusap lukejaas Betelekem, koidunyetake da kere, lukeraas luka ikar iarei ka lumam edolito ŋul, kwape ejaar apak kaya nakinyikokinia aiŋitun kama ejaas lukacoa." 
Matthew2:17 Kosodi kitodolikin akirot nakinerit enabi Yeremia ebe," 
Matthew2:18 “Aponi kiirarai eporoto koRama, Aibworo ka akuudian naepol, Ibworo Rakel ikedwe, Komam ecamunit aitalakario, naarai emameete.”" 
Matthew2:19 Konye ketwana Kerode, koany, kitakanikin emalaika loka Ejakait Yosep kairujasit koMisiri," 
Matthew2:20 kobala ebe, “Konyou koyaŋa ikoku ka totoke, kolot akwap naka Isirael: naarai atwakata luemootos aijar naka ikoku.”" 
Matthew2:21 Konyou ŋesi, koyaŋa ikoku ka totoke, kodol akwap naka Isirael." 
Matthew2:22 Konye nakepupunio ebe erum Arekelao Yudaya aibois naka Kerode papake, kokurianar alosit ŋina; kosodi kikwenya Edeke ŋes kairujasit, kolot akwap nako Galilaya." 
Matthew2:23 Kolot kiboikin ore loenyaritai Nasaret: tetere itodolikinio akirot naenerito inabin ebe, “Enyarao Enasarayot.”" 
Matthew3:1 Kapaarasia kaŋun kobu Yokana Ekebatisan, elimonokini kamodiŋ naka Yudaya," 
Matthew3:2 ebala ebe, “Kitoronikinos; naarai aapu ajakanut naka akuj.”" 
Matthew3:3 Naarai ŋol ŋes lokinerai kama ka Isaia enabi ebe, “Eporoto loka loiworoi kamodiŋ ebe, Kitemonokisi erot loka Ejakait, Kitetenata ikesokono.”" 
Matthew3:4 Konapenenei Yokana ŋol egoe loka ajul nuka ekaala, ka amunyo kaŋabetekeŋ; ikenyamat da keraas emaase ka esik loka ais." 
Matthew3:5 Kosodete kolomasi mama ejai lukoYerusalem ka luko Yudaya kere, ka lukakwapin kere nuidunyas Yorodan;" 
Matthew3:6 kibatisa ŋesi kes kocor Yorodan, kolimonorete akecediakanareta." 
Matthew3:7 Konye nakeanyunia ŋesi epote Iparisayon ka Isadukayon luipu aibatisao, kolimok kes ebe, “Yes aur naka imusagan, iŋai bo kiikwenyari yes akerit anyunyura naebunit?" 
Matthew3:8 Aso koraata araito nuibusakinito aitoronikin: 
Matthew3:9 kwabo siriwomito kotauonokus ebe, ‘Ejai oni Aburaam papaawok’: naarai kalimokini yes ebe epedori Edeke aitonyoikin Aburaam idwe kotoma amoru kanu." 
Matthew3:10 Nati kwape kwana da ibwaikinitai aep atoromin nuka ikito: aso ŋolikitoi lomam erai araito nuejok ejepario, ka acakakin akim." 
Matthew3:11 “Abeit eoŋ ebatisai kakip kanuka aitoronikin: konye loebuni atupakin eoŋ ketelekarit eoŋ agogoŋ, mam kebusakinit akodit akemuk; kibatisai ŋol yes kEmoyo Lokalaunan, ka akim." 
Matthew3:12 Ejai ekeritei akanike, epiari cut ekepejal; etukonokini akimake odula, konye icwei agugu kakim namam itudeŋio.”" 
Matthew3:13 Kosodi konyou Yesu koGalilaya, kobu Yorodan mama ajai Yokana aibatisao." 
Matthew3:14 Konye kokoto Yokana aitikokin, ebala ebe, “Epuda jo aibatis eoŋ, ijo da ibuni mamakaŋ?”" 
Matthew3:15 Konye Koboŋok Yesu, kolimok ŋes ebe, “Kocam do kwana; naarai kwaŋin ibusakinitor oni aitodol adolit kere.” Kosodi kocam." 
Matthew3:16 Nakedaunia Yesu aibatisao, atipet kodoku kakipi: ido koany, kopukokin akuj, koany Emoyo loka Edeke ijesun kwape ajele, ebuni mamakeŋ;" 
Matthew3:17 ido koany, kobu eporoto kokuju ebe, “Lo ŋes Okokuka lominat, loalelia eoŋ noi.”" 
Matthew4:1 Kosodi Emoyo kitodoka Yesu amodiŋ tetere Satan ecoduni ŋes. 
Matthew4:2 Koluŋ apaarasia akaisaoŋon apaaran ka akuare, kosodi konyet korieb eteŋei," 
Matthew4:3 Kobu ekacodan, kotema ŋes atiar, “Arai tope irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke, kicorak amor nu koraunos atap.”" 
Matthew4:4 Konye Koboŋok ebe, “Iwadikatai ebe, Mam ituŋanan ejari kanuka atap bon, nabarai kanuka ŋinikirot naelomuni kaituk naka Edeke.”" 
Matthew4:5 Kosodi Satan ayaŋaar ŋes ore lokalaunan; kisibwo koswi loka eyekalu," 
Matthew4:6 kolimok ebe, “Arai tope irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke, kosomari kwap: naarai iwadikatai ebe, Einakini ikemalaikan aidar jo, Kidakete jo kakaninikec, Kinyek amoru aiguikin akonikeju.”" 
Matthew4:7 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Iwadikatai bobo ebe, Sirikodununei Ejakait Ekonideke.”" 
Matthew4:8 Koyaŋa bobo Satan ŋes oroŋat loicelelei noi, kitodianak ajakanuto kere nuka akwap, ka aibusesukec;" 
Matthew4:9 kotema ŋes atiar, “Kainakini ŋun kere, arai kibiror aima eoŋ.”" 
Matthew4:10 Kosodi kotema Yesu atiar, “Irwa, Satan; naarai iwadikatai ebe, Komaenenei Ejakait Ekonideke, Kijaanakinenei ŋes bon.”" 
Matthew4:11 Kosodi kinye Satan ŋes; ido koany, kopotu imalaikan kijaanakis ŋes." 
Matthew4:12 Nakepupunio ŋes ebe ekamar Yokana, kolot Galilaya;" 
Matthew4:13 konyou koNasaret, kobu kiboikin Kaparanaum, loidunyas aŋolol, koikorun luka Sebulun ka Naputali," 
Matthew4:14 tetere itodolikinio akirot naenerit Isaia enabi ebe," 
Matthew4:15 “Akwap naka Sebulun, ka akwap naka Naputali, Abear aŋolol, kokekwa Yorodan, Galilaya naka Imo," 
Matthew4:16 Ituŋa lueboiete kamuton, Aanyut aica naepol, ŋul da lueboiete kakwap ka etoribe loka atwanare, Eliyaiki aica.”" 
Matthew4:17 Agear kapak kaŋin kogeu Yesu alimonokin, ebala ebe, “Kitoronikinos; naarai aapu ajakanut naka akuj.”" 
Matthew4:18 Nakitoritor ariri kaŋolol naka Galilaya, koany iinacan iarei, Simon loenyaritai Petero, ka Anderea onaceke, ecakakinete eboi aŋolol; naarai keraas ikalokak." 
Matthew4:19 Kotema kes atiar, “Kotupunai, eoŋ da ketaraun yes ikalokak ituŋa.”" 
Matthew4:20 Atipet kinyeis iboyanakec, kotupasi ŋes." 
Matthew4:21 Kikunyak kiŋaren koany iinacan ice iarei, Yakob okoku loka Sebedayo, ka Yokana onaceke, lukejaas ataker nepepe ka Sebedayo papakec, erucete iboyanakec; konyarau kes." 
Matthew4:22 Atipet kinyeis ataker ka papakec, kotupasi ŋes." 
Matthew4:23 Kimanimani Yesu Galilaya kere, kisisianakini kotoma atukosiakec, kolimonokini da akiro nukajokak nuka ajakanut, kitaŋaleununei ŋinidek, ka akalanyanut kere kotoma otuŋa." 
Matthew4:24 Kikaikin ekeemut Suria kere: koinunai ituŋa kere lukedekas, lukikamunito iponesio luegelegela luka adekesia, ka ariebo, lukajokina, ka lukipumu, ka lukasenyak da; kitaŋaleu kes." 
Matthew4:25 Kotupasi ŋes ikodeta luipu lukepote koGalilaya ka Dekapoli, ka Yerusalem, ka Yudaya, ka okekwa Yorodan da." 
Matthew5:1 Kosodi nakeanyunia ikodeta, kodoka oroŋat: kiboikin, kopotu ikekesisiak mamakeŋ." 
Matthew5:2 Kooŋ akeituk, kisisianak kes, kobala ebe:" 
Matthew5:3 “Isirereŋitoi lukican komoyo; naarai ajakanut naka akuj erai nakec. 
Matthew5:4 “Isirereŋitoi luitururuete: naarai italakario. 
Matthew5:5 “Isirereŋitoi luitasonos: naarai irumete akwapin. 
Matthew5:6 “Isirereŋitoi lueriebi eteŋei ka luejakit akur kanuka adolit: naarai isimonikinio. 
Matthew5:7 “Isirereŋitoi luketimok: naarai itimio. 
Matthew5:8 “Isirereŋitoi luesegara itauon: naarai eanyunete Edeke. 
Matthew5:9 “Isirereŋitoi ikesinapikinak: naarai enyarao idwe luka Edeke," 
Matthew5:10 “Isirereŋitoi luimanitai kanuka adolit: naarai ajakanut naka akuj erai nakec. 
Matthew5:11 “Isirereŋitoi yes nakimuaritotor, nakimanitotor, ka einer nukaronok nuipu nuka aiŋal asurokin yes, kanukaŋ." 
Matthew5:12 Kiyalamikinos, kolakaros noi: naarai epol ekusiropit kotoma akuj: naarai kimana kolo kwaŋin inabin lukigeikinete yes." 
Matthew5:13 “Iraas yesi abalaŋ naka akwap; konye arai kepianiar abalaŋ, itemokinio kinyo? Mam bobo ejai ajokis, dimarai ebukorio kiŋa kicakacakata ituŋa." 
Matthew5:14 “Iraas yesi aica naka akwap. Mam epedori ere aibwaio arai ejai kuju moru. 
Matthew5:15 Ido mam ituŋa inokokinete atala, ka abuburikin ebukit, dimarai ikajakinete ocoget, ecaikini kere luejaas togo." 
Matthew5:16 Kwaŋin kocau akusiica kakonyen nuka ituŋa, tetere eanyunete akusiswamisio nuejokuka, kitopoloosi Papakus loejai toma akuj," 
Matthew5:17 “Siriwomito ebe abunit amudiar ikisila karaida inabin: mam abunit amudiar, dimarai aitodolikin." 
Matthew5:18 Naarai abeit katemari yes atiar, Aitodol naedaunotor akuj ka akwap, mam cut edaun inyukuta idiopet, karaida aitakinet adiopet naka ikisila, aitodol neitodolikinere kere." 
Matthew5:19 Aso ituŋanan kere yenepaluni aicorakinet adiopet kotoma kaŋun kanueraas nudidik, ka aisisianakin ituŋa kwaŋin, enyarao yenididi cut kotoma ajakanut naka akuj: konye ŋin kere yeniswamai ka aisisianakin kes, enyarao ŋin ikapolon kotoma ajakanut naka akuj." 
Matthew5:20 Naarai katemari yes atiar, arai mam akusidolit itelekarit adolit naka ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, mam cut ilomunete toma ajakanut naka akuj." 
Matthew5:21 “Ipotu kiirasi kelimokinitai ituŋa lukolo sek ebe, Siriari; ido ituŋanan yeneari ibusakinit atubokinio," 
Matthew5:22 Konye eoŋ katemari yes atiar, Ŋinituŋanan yenenyunyurikini onaceke ibusakinit atubokinio; ka ŋin da yenemoromoroi onaceke ibusakinit airabis; ŋin da yenetemari atiar, Ibaŋaanal Ibusakinit eupa loidopit." 
Matthew5:23 Aso arai iyauni ainakinetekon otem, kosodi kiitu kanen ebe ejaas onacekon akiro kajo," 
Matthew5:24 kinyek ainakinetekon kotem, kolot ber; kopuco konacekon, kosodi konyet aboŋun ainakin ainakinetekon." 
Matthew5:25 Kocamanaros atipet kalokiwosat jo, apak naijaatatar kaŋes orot; kinyek je lokiwosat ayaŋaar jo mama ejai ekatubon, ekatubon da ayaŋaar jo mama ejai eserikalet, ijo da kiremokinio aidaris." 
Matthew5:26 Abeit katemari jo atiar, Mam cut inyouni kanen, aitodol neitacia ikapu yenikawasia." 
Matthew5:27 “Ipotu kiirasi kelimokinitai ebe, Siridote." 
Matthew5:28 Konye eoŋ katemari yes atiar, Ŋolituŋanan loeseseni aberu kaiŋobel, etielo ŋes kotauke." 
Matthew5:29 Arai kiduporit akonikoŋu nakoteten, kogoru, kocaka: naarai ibus koolio idiopet katutubetakon, kinye akonikuan kere acakario toma oupa." 
Matthew5:30 Arai kiduporit akonikan nakoteten, kojepa, kocaka; naarai ibus koolio idiopet katutubetakon, kinye akonikuan kere alosit toma oupa." 
Matthew5:31 “Kelimokinitai da ebe, ŋolituŋanan loireŋeari akeberu, koinak ŋin ebalua loka aitwar:" 
Matthew5:32 konye eoŋ katemari yes atiar, ŋolituŋanan loireŋeari akeberu, dimarai kanuka adotear, esidotea ŋin: ŋol da loemanyi ya naereŋearitai, adotear." 
Matthew5:33 “Bobo da, ipotu kiirasi kelimokinitai ituŋa lukolo sek ebe, Siriyapoi nukaiŋal, konye kitodolik Ejakait akoniiyaposio." 
Matthew5:34 Konye eoŋ katemari yes atiar, Siriyapoi cut; karaida alimit akuj, naarai erai eicoloŋ loka Edeke;" 
Matthew5:35 karaida alimit akwap, naarai erai iicoloŋ yenika akejeke; karaida alimit Yerusalem, naarai erai ere loka Ekabaka lokapolon." 
Matthew5:36 Kwabo siriyapoi alimit akonikou, naarai mam ipedori aituluor ekonitimat ediopet araun Ioekwaŋ arai loiriono." 
Matthew5:37 Konye nuineras koraas Eebo, eebo, arai Mam, mam: naarai nuedeparito ŋun epote kama ejai lokaronon." 
Matthew5:38 “Ipotu kiirasi kelimokinitai ebe, Akoŋu itia akoŋu, ekelai da itia ekelai." 
Matthew5:39 “Konye eoŋ katemari yes atiar, Sirikinyaŋa yenikaronon: konye ŋinituŋanan yenikibapi eitinyokon lokoteten, kibelok lokokediany da." 
Matthew5:40 Ka ituŋanan yenekot awoosan jo, ayaŋaar ekasokon, kinyeinia ŋes ekooti da." 
Matthew5:41 Ŋin da yenikitiŋaikini alosit amairo adiopet, kolot ka ŋes amairon aarei." 
Matthew5:42 Yenikilipi, koinak, ka yenekot ayuunio kamakon sirikiboŋok epur." 
Matthew5:43 “Ipotu kiirasi kelimokinitai ebe, Komina eidunyetekon, kola lokasurupikon." 
Matthew5:44 Konye eoŋ katemari yes atiar, Kominasi lukasurupokus, kilipanakinete da lukimanito;" 
Matthew5:45 tetere iraunete idwe luka Papakus loejai toma akuj; naarai itacaikini ŋesi akekoloŋ lukaronok ka lukajokak da, isitepikini akiru luedolito ka lumam edolito da." 
Matthew5:46 Naarai arai iminasi lukiminas yes, idumunete eropit enyoin? Mam kereka iketelemak esolo iswamaete nuikote nen?" 
Matthew5:47 Arai da iyogaete iinacanakus bon, iswamaete nunyoika adepar ice? Mam kereka Imo iswamaete nuikote nen?" 
Matthew5:48 Aso iraunete yesi luidolito, kwape edolitor Papakus lokotoma akuj." 
Matthew6:1 “Kocoito kinyeis aswam nukadolitekus kakonyen nuka ituŋa, tetere eanyunete kesi: naarai arai kiswamata nuikote nen, mam idumunete eropit kama ejai Papakus loejai toma akuj." 
Matthew6:2 “Aso naikoria ainakineta nukaitim, sirikituru arupepe kakonyenekon, kwape iswamaata lukesoswai kotoma atukosia, korotin da, tetere itopoloorete ituŋa. Abeit katemari yes atiar, Adaut adumun eropitikec," 
Matthew6:3 Konye jo naikoria ainakineta nukaitim, kinyek akonikan nakokediany ajenun nuiswamai nakoteten;" 
Matthew6:4 korau akoniikor nakaiyeiyea; Papakon da loeseseni kaiyeiyea kiropi jo. 
Matthew6:5 “Nailipiata da, siriraas kwapelukesoswai; naarai eminasi ailip kobwoete katukosia ka asisiarin da nuka irotin, tetere etakanete kotuŋa. Abeit katemari yes atiar, Adaut adumun eropitikec." 
Matthew6:6 Konye jo nailipenenaa, kolomanari toma agolakon, kidau agolokin ekonikek, kilip Papakon lokaiyeiyea, Papakon da loeseseni kaiyeiyea kiropi jo." 
Matthew6:7 “Ido nailipiata sirinyogonyogoete akiro atai, kwape ka Imo; naarai eomitos ebe iirario kanuka akirokec nuipu," 
Matthew6:8 Aso sirikiputokinos kaŋul: naarai ejeŋi Papakus nuipudasi yesi, eriŋa kilipa." 
Matthew6:9 Aso kilipenenete yesi kwanata: Papakosi loejai toma akuj, Ekonikiror kitalaunai." 
Matthew6:10 Akonijakanut kobu. Nuikoto kiswamai kakwapin Kwape iswamaere kotoma akuj. 
Matthew6:11 Koinakinai sio lolo ikosinyamat luka lolo. 
Matthew6:12 Kisionioi sio akosipesenin, Kwape kisionio isio lukapeseninikosi." 
Matthew6:13 Sirikiya sio toma acodunio, Konye koyuunai kama ejai lokaronon. [Naarai ajakanut, ka apedor, ka apolou, eraas nukon, ikar kere, Amen.]" 
Matthew6:14 Naarai arai isioniete yesi luce akeceibucanareta, Papakus da lokotoma akuj kisionie yes." 
Matthew6:15 Konye arai mam yes isioniete luce akeceibucanareta, Papakus da mam kisionie yes akusiibucanareta." 
Matthew6:16 “Bobo da nailuŋiata, siriraas kwape lukesoswai luinyorididos ireeta; naarai emunaunete ireetakec, tetere etakanete kotuŋa ebe eluŋete. Abeit katemari yes atiar, Adaut adumun eropitikec." 
Matthew6:17 Konye jo, nailuŋia, kinyonyoenenei akinyet akoukon, kilosi da akonikonyen," 
Matthew6:18 tetere mam itakanuni kotuŋa ebe iluŋi, dimarai Papakon lokaiyeiyea: Papakon da loeseseni kaiyeiyea, kiropi jo." 
Matthew6:19 “Siriŋadanakinete kanukus abar akwapin, neemunaariata ikajekel ka amasikin da, ido neebokiata ikokolak ka akokwaar." 
Matthew6:20 Konye kiŋadanakinete kanukus abar akuj, nemam emunaariata ikajekel ka amasikin, ido nemam ebokiata ikokolak ka akokwaar da." 
Matthew6:21 Naarai nepejai akonibar, nepenen ejaikin ekonitau da." 
Matthew6:22 “Atala naka akuan ŋes akoŋu: aso arai eteni akonikoŋu, akonikuan kere ecauni." 
Matthew6:23 Konye arai erono akonikoŋu, akonikuan kere emutono. Aso arai emutono aica naejai kotomakon, epol ca ma amuton ŋin!" 
Matthew6:24 Emamei ituŋanan yenepedori aijaanakin ijaka iarei; naarai arai elai ediopet, komina loce; arai bo iketakin kediopet, emeni loce. Mam ipedorete aijaanakin Edeke ka aijaanakin abar da." 
Matthew6:25 “Aso do katemari yes atiar, Siriyaloŋoŋoete kanuka akusiijar, Iuinyamete ka luimasete; karaida kanuka akusiwat, luinapete. Mam kereka aijar itelekarit inyamen, ka akuan da anapito?" 
Matthew6:26 Kosesenata akweny nuka apak, mam eyeete, karaida aidweny, karaida atukonokin Emono; konye itanyami kes Papakus lokotoma akuj. Mam kereka yes itelekaritos ŋun ketiai?" 
Matthew6:27 Iŋai bo kayesi kiyaloŋoŋ epedori aiyatakin akeibut? 
Matthew6:28 Kanukinyo iyaloŋoŋooto kanuka anapito? Koomito aapecelun nuka ais, kwape epolooto; mam itaaritos, ido mam eojiete:" 
Matthew6:29 konye katemari yes atiar, Ka Solomon da kotoma aibusesuke kere mam esiritoi kojokan kwape adiopet kaŋun." 
Matthew6:30 Aso arai itanapi Edeke kwaŋin inya luka ais, luejaas lolo, ecakario moi oupa, mam kereka itelekari aitanap yes, okwe yes luedit aiyuun?" 
Matthew6:31 Aso sirikiyaloŋoŋoto kobalas ebe, ‘Kinyami inyo?’ Arai ‘Kimasi inyo?’ Arai, ‘Kinapi inyo?’" 
Matthew6:32 Naarai emoete Imo ŋun kere; kwabo ejeni Papakus lokotoma akuj ebe ipudas ŋun kere. 
Matthew6:33 Konye komoata ber yesi akejakanut, ka akedolit da; ido kiyatakinio ŋun kere." 
Matthew6:34 “Aso sirikiyaloŋoŋoto nuka moi: naarai iyaloŋoŋi moi kanukeŋ. Edaunit apaaran aronisike. 
Matthew7:1 “Siritubonokinete, yes da kinyeis atubokinio." 
Matthew7:2 Naarai etube loitubete, ŋopeŋol kitubokinere; ka aitemis naitemioto, ŋipeŋin kitemere yes da," 
Matthew7:3 Aso kanukinyo isesenia igugut yenejai akoŋu naka onacekon, komam ipodo akitoi naejai akoŋukon kilopet?" 
Matthew7:4 Arai ilimokini biai onacekon ebe, ‘Kinyek kalem igugut yenejai akoŋukon’; ido koany, ejai akitoi akoŋukon kilopet?" 
Matthew7:5 Yenikesoswai ijo, kolem ber akitoi naejai akoŋukon kilopet; kosodi konyet asesen kotenan alemun igugut kakoŋu naka onacekon." 
Matthew7:6 “Sirikiinakis iŋokwo ibore yenikalaunan, ido sirikicakakis akusilulun kakonyen nuka ipegei, kinyeis aicakacak kakejekec, ka aibelokin agwaragwar yes." 
Matthew7:7 “Kilipa, kiinakinio; komoata, idumunete; kikuŋukuŋoto, kiŋaikinio." 
Matthew7:8 Naarai ŋin yenilipi ijaikinio; yenemoi edumuni; ka yenikuŋukuŋi da enaikinio. 
Matthew7:9 Arai iŋai kereka kayesi, kilip ikokuke emugati, einakini tope amoru?" 
Matthew7:10 Arai kilip agar, einakini tope ŋes emun?" 
Matthew7:11 Aso arai yes lukaronok ijenete ainakin ikusidwe ainakineta nuejok, mam kereka itelekarit noi Papakus loejai toma akuj ainakin ŋul Iuilipete ŋes iboro luejok?" 
Matthew7:12 Aso nuikotosi ituŋa aikonakin yes, kikonakis yesi da kes kwape kwaŋin: naarai ŋun kes ikisila ka inabin da." 
Matthew7:13 “Kolomasi aitor orute loedidiŋ; naarai elal erut, ipajajai da erot, loebei amudiario, luelomarete da kotomake eraas luipu." 
Matthew7:14 Edidiŋ erut, eridid da erot loebei aijar, luedumunete da eraas luikidioko." 
Matthew7:15 “Kocoito inabin Iukeŋalak, lukiponikinete enapito inapen luka amerekekin, konye kotoma eraas ipeen luededeŋ." 
Matthew7:16 Ijenunete kes kakeceraito. Edeŋete kereka ituŋa imusabibun kokito luka ikukwa, arai bo itinin kokodokodo?" 
Matthew7:17 Kwape kwaŋin ŋolikitoi loejok erai araito nuejok; konye do ekitoi loerono erai araito nueroko. 
Matthew7:18 Mam epedori ekitoi loejok aira araito nueroko, karaida ekitoi loerono aira araito nuejok." 
Matthew7:19 Ŋolikitoi lomam erai araito nuejok ejepario, kocakakinai akim." 
Matthew7:20 Kanuka ŋun ijenunete kes kakeceraito. 
Matthew7:21 “Ŋinituŋanan yenikabala eoŋ ebe, ‘Ejakait, Ejakait,’ mere ŋes elomuni ajakanut naka akuj; dimarai yeniswamai nuekoto Papaka loejai toma akuj." 
Matthew7:22 Katemarete luipu kapaaran kaŋin atiar, ‘Ejakait, Ejakait, mam kereka kipou kadwarata kokirorikon, kokirorikon da kereŋeasi ajokin, kokirorikon da keswamata aswamisio nukapedor nuipu?’" 
Matthew7:23 Kasodi alimor mamakec ebe, ‘Mam lem kajeni yes nepecep da: konyoutu kama ajai, yes lukeswamak nukepali.’" 
Matthew7:24 “Aso ŋin yeniirari akakiro nu kiswama kes, ituputoorio ketuŋanan lokacoa, lokeduki eketogo atiida:" 
Matthew7:25 kotep akiru, kolelek akalele, kokuta ikwamin, koleata etogo ŋol; mam ibiroro: naarai kepesikinitai atiida." 
Matthew7:26 Ŋin da yeniirari akakiro nu, komam iswamai, ituputoorio ketuŋanan lobaŋ, lokeduki eketogo asiŋe:" 
Matthew7:27 kotep akiru, kolelek akalele, kokuta ikwamin, koleata etogo ŋol; kibiror; akeibiror da korau naepol.”" 
Matthew7:28 Kosodi kanen, kedau Yesu akiro ŋun, koumokis atukon jokan akeisisianakin," 
Matthew7:29 Naarai kisisianakini kwape etuŋanan loejai apedor, kwabo mere kwape ikewadikakakec." 
Matthew8:1 Kedoku Yesu koroŋat, kotuput ikodeta luipu." 
Matthew8:2 Ido koany, kobu etuŋanan lokatapon mama ejai, koma ŋes, kobala ebe, “Ejakait, arai ikoto, ipedori aiswagar eoŋ.”" 
Matthew8:3 Korio Yesu akekan, kotiro ŋes, kotema atiar, “Akoto; kiswagar.” Atipet kiswagar aketapon." 
Matthew8:4 Kolimok Yesu ŋes ebe, “Kocoite, sirikilimok idiotuŋanan; konye kolot, kitodiar mama ejai esasedoti, koinak ainakinet nakolo kicorakini Musa, araun aitejenunet kamakec.”" 
Matthew8:5 Kosodi nakelomaria Kaparanaum, kobu ekapolokiton erioŋet mamakeŋ, kiŋaiŋa," 
Matthew8:6 kotema atiar, “Ejakait, eperi ekatelepat kotogo edeka eseny, erieba noi jokan.”" 
Matthew8:7 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Abuni aitaŋaleun.”" 
Matthew8:8 Koboŋok ekapolokiton kobala ebe, “Ejakait, mam eoŋ kebusakinit jo alomun kwap kekaswi; konye kolim akirot bon, eŋaleuni ekatelepat." 
Matthew8:9 Naarai eoŋ da arai etuŋanan lokayaitai, ejaas iserikalei luayait eoŋ: ido alimokini ediopet ebe, ‘Kolot,’ elosi; ece da ebe, ‘Bia,’ ebuni; ekabulesit da ebe, ‘Kiswama na,’ ido iswamai.”" 
Matthew8:10 Nakiiraria Yesu ŋun, koumok, kotema kwi luketupito atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, Mam lem adumunit aiyuun naepol naetia na, karaida toma Isirael kere," 
Matthew8:11 Katemari yes atiar, Epote rwaru luipu anyoun kokide koto da, kiboikinos kesi nepepe ka Aburaam, ka Isaak, ka Yakob, toma ajakanut naka akuj." 
Matthew8:12 Konye idwe luka ajakanut ecakario toma amuton nakokiŋa: ejaun kaŋina aimony ka airiamanakin ikel.” 
Matthew8:13 Kotema Yesu ekapolokiton atiar, “Kolot, kwape ejaar akoniiyuun, kojau kwape kwaŋin.” Koŋaleu etelepat kosawa kaŋol." 
Matthew8:14 Nakelomaria Yesu togo loka Petero, koany amuranike eperi edeka ekamidi." 
Matthew8:15 Kotiro akekan, koŋaleu ekamidi; konyou kijaanak ŋes." 
Matthew8:16 Nakitiboŋ, koinunai lukajokin luipu: kireŋea ajokin kakekirot, kitaŋaleu lukadekak kere," 
Matthew8:17 Tetere itololikinio akirot naenerit Isaia enabi ebe, “Kolema ŋesi elopet awokokalanyanut, kibwok adekesiawok.”" 
Matthew8:18 Kosodi keanyu Yesu atukon nuipu irimorito ŋes, kicorak aikwaŋar juwai." 
Matthew8:19 Kobu ekewadikan ediopet mama ejai, kotema ŋes atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, katupenenei jo kama ilosi kere.”" 
Matthew8:20 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Ejaas ikuwei apanya, akweny da nuka apak ejaas akaisikec; konye Okoku loka etuŋanan emamei nama iperikini akekou.”" 
Matthew8:21 Kotema ece kokesisiak ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, kisiikinai ber kalot keda papaka.”" 
Matthew8:22 Konye kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kotupunai; kinye lukatwak kidaata lukatwakakec.”" 
Matthew8:23 Nakedokaria ataker, kotupasi ikekesisiak." 
Matthew8:24 Ido koany, kodakun ekwam loepol kaŋolol, korapasi akailan ataker: konye kejotoi ŋesi." 
Matthew8:25 Koloto ikekesisiak mama ejai kitwekenyut, kobalas ebe, “Ejakait, kitajarai; kimudiar.”" 
Matthew8:26 Kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo ikuriakarotor, yes luedit aiyuun?” Kosodi konyou, kiretak ikwamin ka aŋolol; kojaun aiyamakin cut," 
Matthew8:27 Koumokis ituŋa, kobalas ebe, “Ikoni bo ai etuŋanan lo? Naarai ikwamin ka aŋolol da erimasi ŋes.”" 
Matthew8:28 Nakedolio ŋesi okekwa juwai toma akwap naka Igadarenin, kiriamunos kituŋa iarei lukajokin, lukepote katesin, lukededeŋ noi, komamei ituŋanan yenikepedori aitor korot kaŋol," 
Matthew8:29 Ido koany, kiworoto, kobalas ebe, “Ijo Okoku loka Edeke, anyoika ijo kasio? Ibu kereka ijo aitican sio eroko apakikosi kedolo?”" 
Matthew8:30 Ido kojai esipan loka ipegei luipu edakasi kama elwana. 
Matthew8:31 Kiŋaiŋaata ajokin ŋes kobalas ebe, “Arai kiireŋea sio, kijukarai kalomasi osipan je loka ipegei.”" 
Matthew8:32 Kotema kes atiar, “Kolototo.” Kolomutu kolomasi toma opegei; ido koany, komotar esipan kere nejululuei kibirokinos aŋolol, kotwakikis akipi." 
Matthew8:33 Kokerata ikecokok, kolomasi ore, kolimonokis akiro kere, ka nukedoikinete kwi Iukajokin." 
Matthew8:34 Ido koany, kolomut lukore kere airiamun ka Yesu: nakeanyut, kiŋaiŋaata ŋes anyoun koikorunokec." 
Matthew9:1 Kodoka Yesu ataker, kikwaŋar, kodol ore lokobukec." 
Matthew9:2 Ido koany, koinut ŋes etuŋanan lokasenyan, eperi koitada: nakeanyunia Yesu akeceiyuun, kotema lokasenyan atiar, “Okoku, kotitiŋior; esionii akonidiakanareta.”" 
Matthew9:3 Ido koany, kotemasi ice kokewadikak kotauonokec atiar, “Einyanakini lo Edeke.”" 
Matthew9:4 Konye kojen Yesu aomisio nukotauonokec, kotema atiar, “Kanukinyo iwomitotor nukaronok kotauonokus?" 
Matthew9:5 Ani bo naepatana, atemar atiar, Esionii akonidiakanareta, arai bo atemar ebe, Konyou, kolot?" 
Matthew9:6 Konye tetere ijenunete ebe ejai Okoku loka etuŋanan apedor kakwap aisioni adiakanareta” kosodi kotema ŋesi lokasenyan atiar, “Konyou, kibwok ekoniitada, kolot orekon.”" 
Matthew9:7 Konyou ŋesi, kolot oreke." 
Matthew9:8 Konye nakeanyuniata ikodeta, kokuriakaros, kitopoloosi Edeke, lokeinakini ituŋa apedor naikoni na." 
Matthew9:9 Nakitoritor Yesu kanen, koany etuŋanan iboie kaitelemis esolo, ekekiror Matayo; kotema ŋes atiar, “Kotupunai.” Konyou, kotupa ŋes." 
Matthew9:10 Kosodi kanen, nakiboikin togo ainyam, koany, kopotu luketelemak esolo ka ikadiakanarak luipu kiboikinos nepepe ka Yesu ka ikekesisiak." 
Matthew9:11 Nakeanyuniata Iparisayon, kotemasi ikekesisiak atiar, “Kanukinyo emoriata Ekusikesisianakinan ka iketelemak esolo ka ikadiakanarak da?”" 
Matthew9:12 Konye nakepupunio Yesu, kotema atiar, “Lukaŋaleok mam ipudasi emurwon, dimarai lukadekak." 
Matthew9:13 Konye koloto yesi kisisiata apolou naka akiro nu ebe, ‘Akoto aitim, kwabo mere asuban.’ Naarai mam abunit anyarit ikadolitok, dimarai ikadiakanarak.”" 
Matthew9:14 Kosodete kopotu ikesisiak luka Yokana mama ejai, kobalas ebe, “Kanukinyo kilunia isio ka Iparisayon, konye ikonikesisiak mam eluŋete?”" 
Matthew9:15 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Epedorete kereka luenyaritai oiterane aibworo, naeiaarar ka eteran? Konye eponito apaarasia nuedemarere eteran, eluŋete do," 
Matthew9:16 Emamei ituŋanan yenedonyokini acana naka egoe lokitetet toma ananito namojoŋ; naarai acana naibwaikinio ecili anapito, iyatakini do acilat." 
Matthew9:17 Kwabo mam ituŋa ibwaikinete ebino lokitetet toma oriagin lumojoŋ luka emukule; arai kibwaikis, enedasi iriagin, ebukor ebino, emunaaros iriagin; dimarai ibwaikinete ituŋa ebino lokitetet oriagin lukitetiak, tetere ikuniaete kere.”" 
Matthew9:18 Napelimokini ikesisiak luka Yokana ŋun, koany, kobu ekayaiton, kokukokin kotema atiar, “Adaun akokuka kwape kwana; konye bia ma kidokok ŋes akonikan, ejari do.”" 
Matthew9:19 Konyou Yesu kotupa ŋes, nepepe kikekesisiak." 
Matthew9:20 Ido koany, kobu aberu kokauke, nakedeka alel naka aokot ikar itomon ka luarei, kotiro atwele naka anapitoke;" 
Matthew9:21 naarai kotema kotauke atiar, “Arai katiro anapitoke bon, aŋaleuni.”" 
Matthew9:22 Kibelokin Yesu, koany ŋes, kotema atiar, “Kotitiŋior akokuka; kitaŋaleu jo akoniiyuun.” Koŋaleu aberu ameun kosawa kaŋol," 
Matthew9:23 Nakedolio Yesu ore loka ekayairon, koany luekusere alamarun, ka ekodet eborianete," 
Matthew9:24 kotema atiar, “Kolomasi kiŋa; naarai mam etwanit ipese konye eiotoi.” Kokienatar ŋes." 
Matthew9:25 Konye kedau aitolomar ekodet, kooma toma, kitiŋ akan naka ipese, konyou ŋin." 
Matthew9:26 Kilosikinos akiro ŋun akwap ŋin kere; 
Matthew9:27 Nakitorio Yesu kanen, kotupasi imudukiok iarei, kiworoto kotemasi atiar, “Okoku loka Daudi, kitimoi sio.”" 
Matthew9:28 Keloma ŋes itogo, kopotu imudukiok mama ejai; kotema kes Yesu atiar, “Iyuunitos ebe apedori eoŋ aswam na?” Kotemasi atiar, “Eebo, Ejakait.”" 
Matthew9:29 Kosodi kotiro akonyenekec kobala ebe, “Kwape ejaar akusiiyuun kiswamakin yes kwaŋin.”" 
Matthew9:30 Kokwenyutu akecekonyen. Kicoro Yesu kes noi ebe, “Kocoito, kinyek imodiotuŋanan ajenun.”" 
Matthew9:31 Konye konyoutu kesi, kisiarakis ekeemut akwap ŋin kere." 
Matthew9:32 Napenyounete kwi, koany, koinunai ebaŋ loajai ajokit." 
Matthew9:33 Kireŋear ajokit kiner lobaŋ; koumokis ikodeta, kobalas ebe, “Mam lem etakanunitos nuikote nen kotoma Isirael.”" 
Matthew9:34 Konye kobalas Iparisayon ebe, “Ireŋeari ŋesi ajokin kanuka lokapolon loka ajokin.”" 
Matthew9:35 Kimaniman Yesu ireria kere, kokialon da, isisianakini katukosiakec ka alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka ajakanut, ka aitaŋaleunun ŋolipone kere loka adek ka akalanyanut da," 
Matthew9:36 Keanyu ikodeta, kitim kes, naarai kilworuna ka aisiarakina, bala amerekekin nuemamei ekecokon." 
Matthew9:37 Kosodi kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Ipu idwenyan, konye ikidioko ikeswamak;" 
Matthew9:38 aso kilipa Ejakait loka aidweny kijuk ikeswamak toma aidwenyeke.” 
Matthew10:1 Konyarau ikekesisiak itomon ka luarei, koinak kes apedor mama ejaas imoyon lueroko, aireŋear kes, ka aitaŋaleun ŋolipone kere loka adek ka akalanyanut da." 
Matthew10:2 Ikiroria luka ikiyakia itomon ka luarei kes luta: losodit, Simon, loenyaritai Petero, ka Anderea onaceke; Yakob okoku loka Sebedayo, ka Yokana onaceke;" 
Matthew10:3 Pilip ka Batolomayo; Tomas ka Matayo eketeleman esolo; Yakob okoku loka Alipayo, ka Tadayo;" 
Matthew10:4 Simon Ekananayot, ka Yuda Isikariot, lokebilakini ŋes ebotet." 
Matthew10:5 Kijuka Yesu ŋul itomon ka luarei, kicorak kes ebe, “Sirikilomasi orotin luka lukacekwapin, sirikilomasi da ediore kere loka Isamarian," 
Matthew10:6 konye gwai koloto mama ejaas amerekekin nueoliorito nuka ekek loka Isirael. 
Matthew10:7 Nailosioto kolimonokis ebe, ‘Aapu ajakanut naka akuj’." 
Matthew10:8 Kitaŋaleununete lukadekak, kitajarununete lukatwak, kiswaganarete lukatapon, kireŋeanarete ajokin, Kiinakinitai atitai, yes da koinakis atitai." 
Matthew10:9 Sirikiyaŋaasi koriaginikus esabu, karaida epuesa, karaida aikomon," 
Matthew10:10 karaida ecoe loka alosit, karaida ikootin iarei, karaida amuk, karaida ebela; naarai ibusakinit ekeswaman ikenyamat." 
Matthew10:11 Ido ŋolire arai ekialo loilomanarete, komoenenete yenibusakinit kanen, kosalenenete mamake aitodol neinyounioto." 
Matthew10:12 Nailomariata togo, kiyogaete." 
Matthew10:13 Arai ibusakinit etogo, kodol ainapakinikus tomake; konye arai mam ibusakinit, koboŋu do ainapakinikus mamakus." 
Matthew10:14 Arai mam kisukunyikinio karaida akiirar akirokus, nailomuniata kotogo kaŋol, arai kore kaŋol, kilakilakete adae nuka akejenekus." 
Matthew10:15 Abeit, katemari yes atiar, Epatanikini rwaru akwap naka Sodom ka Gomora atitiŋikin kapaaran naka etube aitelekarit ere ŋol." 
Matthew10:16 “Koany, keyakiari yes kwape amerekekin kokidiŋ opeen; aso kopiriaka bala imunwo, ido kiyapaara bala ajeleik," 
Matthew10:17 Konye kocoito ituŋa; naarai kiyaŋaarete aurianeta, kidaete da kotoma atukosiakec." 
Matthew10:18 Kiriarete akonyen nuka ikayaitok ka ikabakan kanukaŋ, araut ikajenak kamakec, kama kalukacekwapin da." 
Matthew10:19 Konye nakiyaŋanariata, sirikiyaloŋoŋoto epone loineratar karaida nuinerasi; naarai kiinakinio kapak kaŋin nuinerasi;" 
Matthew10:20 naarai mere yes inerasi, dimarai Emoyo loka Papakus loinera kotomakus." 
Matthew10:21 Onace einakini onaceke aario, papa da ikokuke, enyoikinete idwe lukauriakakec aicutar;" 
Matthew10:22 kiŋarunete yes ituŋa kere kanuka ekakiror. Konye yenetitiŋikini kiton awasia ŋes itajario. 
Matthew10:23 Nakireiata yes kore ediopet, kokerata ore ece, naarai abeit katemari yes atiar, Mam idaunete ireria kere luka Isirael aitodol naebunio Okoku loka etuŋanan." 
Matthew10:24 “Ekesisian mam itelekarit ekesisianakinanike, karaida ebulesit mam itelekarit ejakaitike," 
Matthew10:25 Edaunit ekesisian aputoor ekesisianakinanike, ka ebulesit aputoor ejakaitike. Arai enyaraete elopet etogo Beelesebul, edeparete ca do amoromor luejaas okaleke." 
Matthew10:26 “Aso sirikikuriakaros kes; naarai emamei akirot naerapitai namam epukorio, karaida naibwaitai namam ejenunio." 
Matthew10:27 Nukalimokini yes kamuton, kinerata yesi kotoma aica; nuiirarete kaiyeiyea, kolimonokis kokuju otogoi." 
Matthew10:28 Sirikikuriakaros ŋul luearete akuan komam epedorete aiar aijar; konye gwai kokuriaka ŋol loepedori amudiar akuan ka aijar da kotoma oGeena. 
Matthew10:29 Mam kereka egwelete anyiporin aarei apesa adiopet? Emamei adio da naedoi kwap komam Papakus ejeni," 
Matthew10:30 Konye yes, imaritai itima da kere luka akwesikus." 
Matthew10:31 Aso sirikikuriaka; iraas yesi luka etiai adepar anyiporin nuipu. 
Matthew10:32 Aso ŋinituŋanan yenikalimori eoŋ kakonyen nuka ituŋa, alimori eoŋ da ŋes kakonyen nuka Papaka loejai toma akuj;" 
Matthew10:33 konye ŋin yenikaŋeri eoŋ kakonyen nuka ituŋa, aŋeri eoŋ da ŋes kakonyen nuka Papaka loejai toma akuj." 
Matthew10:34 “Siriwomito ebe abu kabu ayaŋaun ainapakin kakwap: mam abu kabu ayaŋaun ainapakin, dimarai ekileŋ," 
Matthew10:35 Naarai abu kabu aitusurupikin etuŋanan ka papake, apese ka totoke, aberu naka okokuke ka tataake." 
Matthew10:36 Lukokale luka etuŋanan kes eraunos lukasurupoke. 
Matthew10:37 Ŋin yenemina papake arai totoke adepar eoŋ, mam kebusakinit; ŋin da yenemina ikokuke yenitelepat arai yenipese adepar eoŋ, mam kebusakinit." 
Matthew10:38 Ŋin da yenimam erioŋi ekemusalaba ka atupar eoŋ, mam kebusakinit." 
Matthew10:39 Ŋin yenedumuni akeijar itooliori, ŋin da yenitooliori akeijar kanukaŋ edumuni." 
Matthew10:40 “Ŋin yenikisukunyikini yes, kesukunyikini eoŋ, ŋin da yenikesukunyikini, isukunyikini ŋol lokejukuni." 
Matthew10:41 Ŋin yenisukunyikini enabi naarai erai enabi, edumuni eropit loka enabi, ŋin da yenisukunyikini ekadoliton naarai erai ekadoliton, edumuni eropit loka ekadoliton." 
Matthew10:42 Ŋin yenitamasi idiopet ka ludidik kalu akoli naka akipi nuelilim bon, naarai erai ikesisian, abeit katemari yes atiar, mam etwaniari cut eropitike.”" 
Matthew11:1 Kosodi kanen, kedau Yesu aicorakin ikekesisiak itomon ka luarei, konyou kanen kolot aisisianakin ka alimonokin da koreriakec." 
Matthew11:2 Kosodi nakiiraria Yokana kaidaris aswamisio nuka Kristo, kijuka ikekesisiak aiŋit," 
Matthew11:3 kobalas ebe, “Irai kereka ijo ŋol loebunit, arai bo kedarata ece?”" 
Matthew11:4 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Koloto, kolimokis Yokana akiro nuiirasi ka nuianyut:" 
Matthew11:5 Ekwenyunete imudukiok, elosete iŋwalasik, iswagio lukatapon, epupete ikimiŋiok, itajario lukatwak, elimonokinio da lukican akiro nukajokak." 
Matthew11:6 Isirereŋitoi da ŋol lomam itiguikin kanukaŋ.” 
Matthew11:7 Kosodete keboŋosi kwi, kogeu Yesu alimokin ikodeta nuka Yokana ebe, “Kilomarete alosit amodiŋ aanyun inyo? Egada lokijaŋijani ekwam?" 
Matthew11:8 Konye bo kilomarete asesen inyo? Etuŋanan lokenapit anapito naanebek? Koany, ŋul luenapito anapito nuunebek ejaas toma otogoi luka ikabakan." 
Matthew11:9 Konye kanukinyo kilomariata? Asesen enabi? Eebo, katemari yes atiar, Loitelekarit enabi." 
Matthew11:10 Ŋol ŋes iwadikatere nu ebe, ‘Koany, ejukari ekakiyakia kakonyenekon, Loitemonokini ekonirot kakonyenekon.’" 
Matthew11:11 Abeit katemari yes atiar, eriŋa enyouno etuŋanan kotoma lukeuriete aŋor loitelekarit Yokana Lokebatisan; konye loedit kotoma ajakanut nakotoma akuj ŋes epol aitelekarit ŋes." 
Matthew11:12 Ameun kapaarasia nuka Yokana Lokebatisan kiton kwana ebuikinitoi ajakanut naka akuj, enatarete da ikabuorok." 
Matthew11:13 Naarai apotu inabin kere ka ikisila kodwarata kiton apak naka Yokana; 
Matthew11:14 Arai ikotosi acamun, ŋes Eliya loedwara abunore." 
Matthew11:15 Yenejaas aki kiira. 
Matthew11:16 “Konye etupusi kinyo atur na? Eputos kidwe luiboiete kagwelanaret luenyaritos ipaupakec kobalas ebe," 
Matthew11:17 ‘Kikut alamarun, mam yes esoma; Kibwolol, mam yes ibworo.’" 
Matthew11:18 Naarai abu Yokana kobu komam enyami karaida aimat, kobalas ebe, ‘Ejai ajokit.’" 
Matthew11:19 Abu Okoku loka etuŋanan kobu enyami emasi da, kobalas ebe, ‘Koany, ekeraŋat lo, ekameran da, epapero loka iketelemak esolo ka ikadiakanarak!’ Konye aswamisioke kes itojokere acoa.”" 
Matthew11:20 Kosodi kogeu aitoron ireria lukiswamaa nukaumokinike nuipu, naarai mam itoronikina." 
Matthew11:21 Kobala ebe, “Itukwi ijo Korasin! Itukwi ijo Betesaida! Naarai arai kiswamatai koTuro ka Sidon nukaumokin nukiswamatai kamakus, ti kitoronikinos ŋo sek, ka ainap da ipukoi ka ekurwon." 
Matthew11:22 Konye katemari yes atiar, Epatanikini rwaru Turo ka Sidon atitiŋikin kapaaran naka etube aitelekarit yes." 
Matthew11:23 Ka jo da, Kaparanaum, kitopoloorio kereka kiton akuj? Kijesario do kiton Okatwak, Naarai arai kiswamatai koSodom nukaumokin nukiswamatai kamakon, ti kesal ore ŋol kiton lolo." 
Matthew11:24 Konye katemari yes atiar, Epatanikini akwap naka Sodom atitiŋikin kapaaran naka etube aitelekarit jo.”" 
Matthew11:25 Kapak kaya Koboŋok Yesu kobala ebe, “Kemalai jo, wu Papa, Ejakait loka akuj ka akwap, naarai ibu kimunonik akiro nu lukacoa ka lukaijen, kopukok da idwe Iudidik;" 
Matthew11:26 eebo, Papa, naarai kwaŋin ibu kitojokia kakonyenekon." 
Matthew11:27 Kainak Papaka iboro kere; ido emamei yenejeni Okoku dimarai Papa, kwabo emamei yenejeni Papa dimarai Okoku, ka ŋin da yenekot Okoku apukokin ŋes," 
Matthew11:28 Kopotu neajai, yes kere luitaaritos ka lukilaŋirikinito, eoŋ da kesiyenuni yes," 
Matthew11:29 Korioŋata ajookotoka, kisisiautu kamakaŋ; naarai etasiono eoŋ, eyapepera kotau, yes da idumunete aiyeŋun kotauonokus." 
Matthew11:30 Naarai imeimeo akajookot, akabwokon da ebenen.”" 
Matthew12:1 Kapak kaŋin kitor Yesu mana naka akima apaaran nakasabato; koriebi ikekesisiak eteŋei, kogeut aijejeunun aluŋuren nuka akima ka ainyam." 
Matthew12:2 Konye keanyutu Iparisayon, kobalas ŋes ebe, “Koany, iswamaete ikonikesisiak namam ibusakinit aswam apaaran nakasabato.”" 
Matthew12:3 Kotema kes atiar, “Mam kereka isomenenete nukiswamai Daudi, nakeriebia eteŋei, ŋes ka ikepaup;" 
Matthew12:4 kwape kelomaria togo loka Edeke, konyam imugatin luka aitodikin, lumam ebusakinit ŋes ainyam karaida ipaupake, dimarai isasedotin bonik?" 
Matthew12:5 Arai bo mam kereka isomenenete kotoma okisila ebe apaaran nakasabato kemunaasi isasedotin koyekalu asabato; komam egwaunete akiro? 
Matthew12:6 Katemari yes atiar, ejai ne yenitelekarit eyekalu." 
Matthew12:7 Konye arai kojenete apolou naka akiro kanu ebe, ‘Akoto aitim kwabo mere asuban,’ timam kititelekaasi lumam egwaunito akiro." 
Matthew12:8 Naarai Okoku loka etuŋanan ŋes erai ejakait loka asabato.” 
Matthew12:9 Konyou kaŋina koloma toma atukosikec," 
Matthew12:10 Ido koany, kojai etuŋanan lokeonit akan. Kiŋita ŋes kotemasi atiar, “Ibus kereka aitaŋaleun kapaaran nakasabato?” Tetere iwosaete ŋes." 
Matthew12:11 Kotema kes atiar, “Iŋai bo kayesi, yenejai amerekek adiopet yenimam iriuni ka alemun arai kibirokin aipany kapaaran nakasabato?" 
Matthew12:12 Mam tope ituŋanan itelekarit amerekek kotiai? Aso ibus aswam nuejok kapaaran nakasabato.” 
Matthew12:13 Kosodi kotema ŋesi etuŋanan atiar, “Korio akonikan.” Korio, koŋaleu, koputokinos kanace." 
Matthew12:14 Konye kolomasi Iparisayon kinerut asurokin ŋes, ka epone loemudiariata ŋes." 
Matthew12:15 Komisiik Yesu ŋun, konyou kanen; kotupasi ituŋa luipu; kitaŋaleu kere." 
Matthew12:16 Kicor kes kinyeis aitakanun ŋes. 
Matthew12:17 Tetere itodolikin akirot naenerit kama kenabi Isaia ebe: 
Matthew12:18 “Koany, ekakejaanakinan loseuna, Eminataka loisiyalamikinit ekatau, Ebwaikini Ekamoyo mamakeŋ, Elimokini lukacekwapin etube." 
Matthew12:19 Mam epega, karaida aiwor; Karaida ituŋanan apupun ekeporoto korotin;" 
Matthew12:20 Mam ebili agada nairiecakina, Mam itudeŋi abirait naepuriei, Aitodol naijukunia etube aipikor;" 
Matthew12:21 Emunokinos lukacekwapin ekekiror.” 
Matthew12:22 Kosodete koinut emuduki ekimiŋ loejai ajokit, kitaŋaleu, kiner ekimiŋ ka akwenyun da." 
Matthew12:23 Koumokis ituŋa kere, kobalas ebe, “Mere caat lo okoku loka Daudi?”" 
Matthew12:24 Konye kiirasi Iparisayon kotemasi atiar, “Mam ŋol ireŋeari ajokin dimarai kanuka Beelesebul, ekapolon loka ajokin.”" 
Matthew12:25 Kosodi kejeni Yesu akeceomisio kotema kes atiar, “Ŋinijakanut naetiakatiakaun asurokin bon emudiar, ere da arai etogo loetiakatiakaun asurokin bon mam icasi." 
Matthew12:26 Satan arai ireŋeari Satan, etiakatiakaun asurokin bon; aso ikonakini ai akejakanut icasi?" 
Matthew12:27 Arai ereŋeari eoŋ ajokin kanuka Beelesebul, ido bo ikusidwe ireŋearete kanuka iŋai? Kanuka ŋun ŋes eraatar ŋul ikusikatubok." 
Matthew12:28 Konye arai ereŋeari eoŋ ajokin kEmoyo loka Edeke, aso adolu ajakanut naka Edeke mamakus." 
Matthew12:29 Arai bo ikwaikini epedori ai etuŋanan alomar togo loka ekagogoŋon ka aiŋat ikeboro, arai mam ber eenit ekagogoŋon ŋol? Kosodi konyet epedori aiŋat eketogo." 
Matthew12:30 Ituŋanan yenimam ejai keoŋ ŋes yenikekoloka, ituŋanan da yenimam etukonokini keoŋ isiarakini." 
Matthew12:31 Kanuka ŋun katemari yes atiar, Isionio niŋironis ka ŋiniinyanakin naka ituŋa, konye mam cut isionio ainyanakin Emoyo." 
Matthew12:32 Ŋinituŋanan da yeninera akirot asurokin Okoku loka etuŋanan isionio; konye ŋin yeninera asurokin Emoyo Lokalaunan mam isionio kotoma okar kalu, karaida kaluepote." 
Matthew12:33 “Kituluosi ekitoi loejok ka akeraito da nuejok, arai bo kituluosi ekitoi loerono ka akeraito da nueroko; naarai ejenunio ekitoi kanuka araitoke." 
Matthew12:34 Yes aur naka imusagan! Ikote ipedorete ai einer nuejok arai iraas luiroko? Naarai inera aituk nuilapununos kotau. 
Matthew12:35 Itolomuni ituŋanan yenejok nuejok kotoma nuiŋadat nuejok, ituŋanan da yenikaronon itolomuni nukaronok kotoma nuiŋadat nueroko." 
Matthew12:36 Katemari yes atiar, Ŋinikirot nakejal naineras ituŋa itodiarete kapaaran naka etube." 
Matthew12:37 Naarai kanuka akonikiro kimarakinio adolit, kanuka akonikiro da kitubokinio aitelekar.”" 
Matthew12:38 Kosodete koboŋokis ice kokewadikak ka Iparisayon kotemasi atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kikoto aanyun aanyunet kamakon.”" 
Matthew12:39 Konye Koboŋok kes kotema atiar, “Atur nakaronon naadote emoi aanyunet; kwabo mam einakinio aanyunet dimarai aanyunet naka enabi Yona." 
Matthew12:40 Naarai kwape keiaar Yona toma akoik naka etiaŋ lokos loka aŋolol adaun apaarasia auni ka akuaresia auni, kwape kwaŋin Okoku loka etuŋanan edauni apaarasia auni ka akuaresia auni kakoik naka akwap." 
Matthew12:41 Enyounete ikiliok luka Ninebe kapaaran naka etube nepepe katur na, itetelekarete ŋes akiro; naarai apotu kesi kitoronikinos kanuka alimonokin naka Yona, ido koany, ejai ne yenitelekarit Yona." 
Matthew12:42 Enyouni akabaka naka Eŋalakimak kapaaran naka etube nepepe katur na, itetelekari kes akiro; naarai abu ŋesi kobu kosaŋe loka akwap akiirar acoa naka Solomon, ido koany, ejai ne yenitelekarit Solomon." 
Matthew12:43 “Kenyou emoyo loerono kotuŋanan, itori aiboisio nuemameete akip emoot nekiyeŋunet, komam edumuni." 
Matthew12:44 Kosodi etemari atiar, ‘Aboŋori togoka nekabunio’; keboŋu edumuni esil, epieitai, epesitai da." 
Matthew12:45 Kosodi elosi eupunos nepepe kimoyon ice ikanykaarei luitelekarito ŋes aronis, elomarete kesi da esalete nen; ejautene loka ituŋanan kaŋin lokawasia eraun loerono adepar losodit. Kwape kwaŋin ejaunia atur na nakaronon.”" 
Matthew12:46 Naperoko ineras kikodeta, koany, kebwoete totoke ka ikeinacan kokiŋa, kokotosi einer kaŋes." 
Matthew12:47 Kolimoki etuŋanan ŋes ebe, “Koany, totokon ka ikoniinacan ebwoete kokiŋa, ekotosi einer kajo.”" 
Matthew12:48 Koboŋok ŋol lokelimokini ŋes ebe, “Iŋai bo erai totoka, lukaŋai da eraas ikainacan?”" 
Matthew12:49 Kitodik ikekesisiak kakekan, kotema atiar, “Koany, totoka ka ikainacan!" 
Matthew12:50 Naarai ŋin yeniswamai nuekoto Papaka loejai toma akuj, ŋin ŋes onaceka; ka inacika, ka totoka da.”" 
Matthew13:1 Kapaaran kaŋin kolomu Yesu kotogo kiboikin ariri kaŋolol. 
Matthew13:2 Kotukokinos ikodeta luipu mama ejai, kodoka ataker kiboikin; kobwoi ekodet kere koitolima." 
Matthew13:3 Kolimonok akiro nuipu kawaragasia, kotema atiar, “Koany, abu ekayean koloma aiye." 
Matthew13:4 Napeyei, kodooto ikinyom ice ariri kerot, kopotu akweny, konyamata." 
Matthew13:5 Kodooto ice aŋaŋam, nemam kipu alup, atipet kobwaŋutu, kanumam idulotor alup," 
Matthew13:6 konye kecau akoloŋ konomosi, kanuamameatar alias korinyosi." 
Matthew13:7 Kodooto ice okukwa, kolibut ikukwa koridakis." 
Matthew13:8 Kodooto ice alupo nuejok koraata, ice akwatat, ice akaisakanykape, ice da akaisauni." 
Matthew13:9 Yenejaas aki, kiira.”" 
Matthew13:10 Kosodi kopotu ikekesisiak mama ejai, kotemasi atiar, “Kanukinyo kineratar kakes kawaragasia?”" 
Matthew13:11 Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Kiinakinitai yes ajenun nukaiyeiyea nuka ajakanut nakotoma akuj, konye kes mam einakinitai." 
Matthew13:12 Naarai yenejai ibore, einakinio luiyatakina luipu; konye yenemamei ibore, ŋin da yenejaas kaŋes edemario." 
Matthew13:13 Kanuka ŋun kinera kakes kawaragasia, naarai naeseseniata mam esesenete, naeirariata da mam iirarete, karaida ajenun." 
Matthew13:14 Ido itodolikinio akirot naka enabi Isaia kamakec naebala ebe, ‘Akiirar iirarete, konye mam ijenunete cut, ido asesen isesenete, konye mam ianyunete cut." 
Matthew13:15 Naarai esiepaikis itauon luka ituŋa kalu, Kimiŋarito akiikec, Itumudakito akecekonye, Tetere mam eanyunete kakecekonye, Ka akiirar kakeceki, Ka ajenun da kikecetauon, Kibelokinos ketaŋaleu.’" 
Matthew13:16 Konye isirereŋitoi akusikonye, naarai esesenete, ka akusiki da, naarai iirarete." 
Matthew13:17 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Apotu kimielas inabin luipu ka ikadolitok aanyun nuisesenete yesi, mam eanyuna, ka akiirar da nuiirarete yesi, mam iirara." 
Matthew13:18 “Aso kopupokisi awaragan naka ekayean. 
Matthew13:19 Naiiraria ituŋanan akirot naka ajakanut, komam ejenuni ŋes, ebuni lokaronon kourupo nukeyeitai otauke; ŋul kes lukeyeio ariri kerot." 
Matthew13:20 Ŋul da lukeyeio aŋaŋam, ŋul kes luiirarete akirot, atipet kiyuutu kaiyalama;" 
Matthew13:21 konye emameete alias kotomakec, kicata nediokasilon, kedolokis ican arai areio kanuka akirot, atipet itiguikinos." 
Matthew13:22 Ŋul da lukeyeio okukwa, ŋul kes luiirarete akirot, konye aiyaloiŋon naka ikar kalu, ka aiŋal naka abar koridakis akirot, mam eraa." 
Matthew13:23 Ŋul da lukeyeio alup nuejok, ŋul kes luiirarete akirot ka ajenun; eraete ŋul, ice akwatat, ice akaisakanykape, ka ice da akaisauni.”" 
Matthew13:24 Koinu kes acewaragan, kobala ebe, “Ajakanut naka akuj; eputos ketuŋanan lokeyei ikinyom luejok amanake:" 
Matthew13:25 konye kejotooros ituŋa, kobu lokasurupike koyeik igitun toma akima, kolot." 
Matthew13:26 Konye kebwaŋut akima, ka aisur, kotakanut igitun da." 
Matthew13:27 Kopotu ibulesin luka elopet etogo kolimokis ŋes ebe, ‘Ejakait, mam tope kiyeit ikinyom luejok amanakon? Kepote bo kai igitun?’" 
Matthew13:28 Kotema kes atiar, ‘Lokasurup ŋes kiswamai ŋun.’ Kotemasi ibulesin ŋes atiar, ‘Aso ikoto kaloto karutosi kes?’" 
Matthew13:29 Konye kotema atiar, ‘Mam; elemuni nairusioto igitun, kimoriununut kakima da.’" 
Matthew13:30 Kinyeisi kere kopolooros kiton aidweny; ido kapak naka aidweny alimokini ikadwenyak ebe, ‘Koruto ber igitun, koenata ikes kicweata; konye akima kotukonokis odulaaka.’ ”" 
Matthew13:31 Koinu kes acewaragan, kobala ebe, “Eputos ajakanut naka akuj; bala ecokat loka ekaradali, lokelemari etuŋanan kiraik toma amanake." 
Matthew13:32 Kedit ŋesi aitelekarit ikinyom kere, konye kepoloor, kiteleka ikui kere koraun do ekitoi, kopotu akweny nuka apak koperenenete atenieikike.”" 
Matthew13:33 Kolimok kes awaragan ace ebe, “Eputos ajakanut naka akuj bala aitubuunet nakelemari aberu kibwa kotoma aitemisio auni nuka akiria, kiton neabuunioto kere.”" 
Matthew13:34 Kolimok Yesu ikodeta ŋun kere kawaragasia; kwabo arai emamei awaragan mam kelimokini akirot. 
Matthew13:35 Tetere itodolikin akirot nakinerit enabi ebe, “Etooŋari akaituk kawaragasia, Alimori da nukibwaitai ameun kapetetait naka akwap.”" 
Matthew13:36 Kosodi kotwar ikodeta, koloma togo. Kopotu ikekesisiak mama ejai, kotemasi atiar, “Kitejenunai sio awaragan naka igitun lukomana.”" 
Matthew13:37 Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Lokeyei ikinyom luejok erai Okoku loka etuŋanan;" 
Matthew13:38 Amana da erai akwap, ikinyom luejok eraas idwe luka ajakanut; igitun eraas idwe luka lokaronon," 
Matthew13:39 lokasurup lokeyei kes erai Satan; aidweny erai awasia naka akwap, ikadwenyak da kes imalaikan." 
Matthew13:40 Kwape etukonokinere igitun ka aicweikin kakim, ikonakinio nen kawasia naka akwap." 
Matthew13:41 Ijukuni Okoku loka etuŋanan ikemalaikan, etukonokinete kotoma ajakanutuke kere nuitiguikinete kere, ka luiswamaete nukepali," 
Matthew13:42 ecakakinete oupa loka akim; ejaun kaŋina aimony ka airiamanakin ikel. 
Matthew13:43 Kosodete ecaunete ikadolitok kwape kakoloŋ kotoma ajakanut naka Papakec, Yenejaas aki, kiira," 
Matthew13:44 “Eputos ajakanut naka aku; bala abar nakibwaitai kotoma amana, nakedumuni etuŋanan kimunona; kosodi kanuka akeiyalama kolot kogwela lukejaatatar kere kogwelu amana ŋin." 
Matthew13:45 “Bobo da, eputos ajakanut naka akuj; bala ekagwelanaran loemoi ilulun luejok;" 
Matthew13:46 nakedumunia elulu ediopet loka etiai loepol, kolot kogwela Iukejaatatar kere, kogwelu." 
Matthew13:47 “Bobo da, eputos ajakanut naka akuj; bala eboi lokecakakinio aŋolol, kotukonok lukecor luka iponesio kere." 
Matthew13:48 Kosodi kilelebun, kiriut ituŋa oitolima, kiboikinos, kotukonokis luejok oboro, konye lueroko kocakasi." 
Matthew13:49 Ikoni nen awasia naka akwap. Epote imalaikan, etiakarete lukaronok kama ka lukadolitok," 
Matthew13:50 ecakakinete kes oupa loka akim; ejaun kaŋina aimony ka airiamanakin ikel.” 
Matthew13:51 Kiŋit Yesu kes ebe, “Ijenutu kereka yesi ŋun kere?” Kotemasi atiar, “Eebo.”" 
Matthew13:52 Kotema kes atiar, “Kanuka ŋun ŋinikewadikan yenituutooritai kajakanut naka akuj; eputos bala etuŋanan elopet etogo loelemuni kotoma abarake iboro lukitetiak ka lumojoŋ da.”" 
Matthew13:53 Kosodi kedau Yesu awaragasia ŋun, konyou, kolot." 
Matthew13:54 Nakedolio bukec, kisisianak kes kotoma atukosikec, koumokis kotemasi atiar, “Kedumuni bo lo kai acoa na ka nukaumokin nu?" 
Matthew13:55 Mam kereka lo erai okoku loka ekekeon? Mere totoke naenyaritai Mariam? Mere ikeinacan Yakob ka Yosep ka Simon ka Yuda? 
Matthew13:56 Emameete akeinacan kere kane kamawok? Aso kedumun bo lo kai nu kere?” 
Matthew13:57 Kitiguikinos kanukeŋ. Konye kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Mam eswaki enabi aitopoloorio dimarai bukec kotogoke da.”" 
Matthew13:58 Mam abu kiswama nukaumokin nuipu kanen, kanu amamus aiyuunikec."

Matthew18:22 Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Mam kalimokinit jo irwan akanykaarei, dimarai ebe akaisakanykaarei irwan akanykaarei." 
Matthew18:23 “Kanuka ŋun ajakanut naka akuj eputosi bala ekabaka lokekoto aimar ikeboro kama kikebulesin. 
Matthew18:24 Kegeu aimar, koinunai etuŋanan ediopet Iokiburao atalantan alukumin atomon," 
Matthew18:25 Kemamikis nutacet, kicorak ejakaitike ŋes agwelario, ka akeberu, ka ikedwe, ka luajaatar kere, kotacakinere apesen." 
Matthew18:26 Kokukokin do ebulesit, kiŋaiŋa, kobala ebe, ‘Okwe Ejakait, kotitiŋikinoi, eoŋ da katacakini jo kere.’" 
Matthew18:27 Abu ejakait loka ebulesit kaŋol kitim ŋes, koosik, kisioni apesen." 
Matthew18:28 Konye koloma ebulesit ŋol, kiriama ŋesi kediopet ebulesit aupake lokiburai adenarin akwatat; kikam ŋes, komied, kobala ebe, ‘Kotacakinai akapesen.’" 
Matthew18:29 Kokukokin do ebulesit aupake kiŋaiŋa, kobala ebe, ‘Okwe, kotitiŋikinoi, eoŋ da katacakini jo kere.’" 
Matthew18:30 Konye koŋer, kolot kibwaik aidaris aitodol naetacakinia apesen." 
Matthew18:31 Kosodete nakeanyuniata ibulesin luce nukiswamas, kokadakis noi, koloto kitejenut ejakaitikec kere nukiswamas." 
Matthew18:32 Kosodi konyarau ejakaitike ŋes kotema atiar, ‘Ebulesit ijo loirono! Abu kesioni jo apesen ŋin kere nakiŋaiŋaia;" 
Matthew18:33 ti mam kereka jo da ibusakinit aitim aupakon, kwape ketimio eoŋ jo?’" 
Matthew18:34 Konyunyurikin ejakaitike, kijaik ikedarak, aitodol naetacakinia apesenike kere." 
Matthew18:35 Ikonakini nen Papaka lokotoma akuj ŋinidiopet kayesi, arai mam isioniete yesi ŋinituŋanan onaceke kotauonokus.”" 
Matthew19:1 Kosodi kanen nakedaunia Yesu akiro ŋun, konyou koGalilaya, kodol oikorun luka Yudaya okekwa Yorodan." 
Matthew19:2 Kotupasi ikodeta luipu; kitaŋaleu kes kaŋina. 
Matthew19:3 Kopotu Iparisayon mama ejai kocodut, kotemasi atiar, “Ibus kereka etuŋanan ainyein akeberu kanuka akirot kere?”" 
Matthew19:4 Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Mam isomenenete ebe Lokesubi kes kageunet abu kosub kes yenikiliokit, ka yeniberu." 
Matthew19:5 Kotema atiar, ‘Kanuka ŋun inyeini etuŋanan papake ka totoke kirotakinos kakeberu, ŋul luarei eraunos adiopetekuan’?" 
Matthew19:6 Aso mam bobo eraas iarei dimarai adiopetekuan. Aso lukimorikikini Edeke, kinyek ituŋanan aitiak.”" 
Matthew19:7 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Aso do kanukinyo kicorakinia Musa ainakin ebalua loka atiak, ka ainyein?”" 
Matthew19:8 Kotema atiar, “Kanuka aninik naka ikusitauon abu Musa kocam yes ainyein akusiŋor, konye ameun kageunet mam arai kwaŋin." 
Matthew19:9 Katemari yes atiar, Ŋolituŋanan loinyeini akeberu dimarai kanuka aelo, komany ace, adotiar; ŋol da loemanyi nakinyeinio adotiar.”" 
Matthew19:10 Kobalasi ikesisiak ŋes ebe, “Arai ikote nen akiro nuka etuŋanan ka akeberu, emamei ajokis aimany.”" 
Matthew19:11 Konye kotema kes atiar, “Mam ituŋa kere epedorete acamun akirot ŋin, dimarai ŋul lueinakinitai." 
Matthew19:12 Naarai ejaas ibwacin lukeurio kopone kaŋol ameun kakoikes nuka nukatotokec; bobo da ejaas ibwacin lukidoŋete ituŋa; bobo da ejaas ibwacin lukibwaciikinete kanuka ajakanut naka akuj, ŋol da loepedori acamun akirot na, kocam.”" 
Matthew19:13 Kosodete koinutu idwe ludidik tetere idokokini akaninike ka ailipakin kes. Koriemeriemata ikesisiak ituŋa. 
Matthew19:14 Konye kobala Yesu ebe, “Kocamutu idwe ludidik kopotu mama ajai, kwabo sirikisimika kes; naarai lueputos kaŋul ajakanut naka akuj erai nakec.”" 
Matthew19:15 Kidokok kes akekanin, konyou kaŋina." 
Matthew19:16 Ido koany, kobu ece mamakeŋ, kotema atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kebusakinit aswam akirot anyoin naejok, tetere adumuni aijar naka ikar kere?”" 
Matthew19:17 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Kanukinyo kiŋisia eoŋ nuka ajokis? Ejai ediopet loerai loejok. Konye arai ikoto alomar aijar, koricite ikisila.”" 
Matthew19:18 Kotema atiar, “Alu?” Kotema Yesu atiar, “Siriari, Siridote, Sirikokoi, Sirisabanakinenei," 
Matthew19:19 Koyoŋitenenei papakon ka totokon, Komina da ikoniidunyet kwape iminar bon.”" 
Matthew19:20 Kobala etelepat ebe, “Aricit ŋul kere; inyo eriŋa kaolikinit bobo?”" 
Matthew19:21 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Arai ikoto araun loitekoro, kolot, kogwela kere luijaatar, kokoranak lukican, ijaunete kabar toma akuj; kosodi kobu kotup eoŋ.”" 
Matthew19:22 Nakiiraria etelepat ŋun kolot itururwei; naarai kejaas iboro luipu. 
Matthew19:23 Kotema Yesu ikekesisiak atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, etionikini ekabaran alomar toma ajakanut naka akuj." 
Matthew19:24 Katemari bobo atiar, Epatanikinit akaala aitor apedot naka ekus itia ekabaran alomar ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Matthew19:25 Nakiirariata ikesisiak ŋun koumokis noi, kotemasi atiar, “Aso iŋai bo do epedori aitajario?”" 
Matthew19:26 Konye kosesen Yesu kes, kotema atiar, “Mam epedorio akiro ŋun kotuŋa, konye kama ejai Edeke epedoros kere.”" 
Matthew19:27 Kosodi koboŋok Petero kotema Yesu atiar, “Koany, kipou isio kenyeis kere katuputu jo. Inyoin bo do kidumuni?”" 
Matthew19:28 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Abeit, katemari yes atiar, kotoma akwap nakitetet naiboikinor Okoku loka etuŋanan oicoloŋ loka aibusesuke, yes da lukiitupunete eoŋ iboikinos toma oicoloŋo itomon ka luarei, itubokinete atekerin atomon ka nuarei nuka Isirael." 
Matthew19:29 Ŋinituŋanan yenikinyeini itogoi, arai iinacan, arai ainacan, arai papa arai toto, arai idwe arai amanat, kanuka ekakiror, edumuni irwan akwatat ka airum da aijar naka ikar kere." 
Matthew19:30 Konye luipu lueraas lusodit eraunete lukawasia, ka lukawasia da eraunete lusodit.”" 
Matthew20:1 “Naarai ajakanut naka akuj eputos ketuŋanan elopet etogo, lokelomuni tupuruc aiboleikin kikeswamak aswam toma amanake naka emusabibu." 
Matthew20:2 Kedau ŋesi acamanar ka ikeswamak ainakin adenari kanuka apaaran, kijuka kes amanake naka emusabibu." 
Matthew20:3 Kolom kwaka esawa lokiwuniet, koany ice ebwoete kagwelanaret ebolwaka." 
Matthew20:4 Kotema kes atiar, ‘Koloto yesi da toma amanaka naka emusabibu, karopete yes nuedolito.’ Koloto kesi." 
Matthew20:5 Kolom bobo kwape isawan ikanykape ka ikanykaoŋon da, kikon kwape kwaŋin." 
Matthew20:6 Kolom da kwaka isawan itomon kalodiopet, kodum ice ebwoete; kobala kes ebe, ‘Kanukinyo ibwoiata kane apaaran kere kobolwaka?’" 
Matthew20:7 Kobalas ebe, ‘Naarai emamei ituŋanan yenikiboleikinit.’ Kotema atiar, ‘Koloto yesi da toma amanaka naka emusabibu.’" 
Matthew20:8 Napekitiboŋ, kotema ejakait loka amana naka emusabibu ekapolokitonike atiar, ‘Konyarau ikeswamak, korop eropitikec, agear ka lukokau kiton lukegeete.’" 
Matthew20:9 Kepotu kwi luka isawan itomon kalodiopet, kodum ŋolituŋanan adenari." 
Matthew20:10 Kepotu lukegeete, koomitos ebe edumunete kesi iyatakina; kodumut kesi da ŋolituŋanan adenari." 
Matthew20:11 Konye kedaut adumun, kirurumakis elopet etogo," 
Matthew20:12 kobalas ebe, ‘Ŋul lukokau eswamata esawa ediopet bon, itiirian ijo kes kasio lukitapasitoi apaaran kere kikanyi adedeŋ naka akoloŋ.’" 
Matthew20:13 Konye Koboŋok ŋesi ediopet kakesi, kotema atiar, ‘Opapero, mam keswamakinit jo erono; mam kereka kiboleikinit ijo keoŋ adenari?" 
Matthew20:14 Koyaŋa naerai nakon, kolot; akoto ainakin ŋol lokokau kwape kajo." 
Matthew20:15 Mam kereka apedori aitwasam ikaboro kwape akotor? Arai bo erono akonikoŋu, naarai ajokuna eoŋ?’" 
Matthew20:16 Kwape kwaŋin lukokau eraunos Iusodit, ka lusodit da eraunos lukokau.”" 
Matthew20:17 Napedokari Yesu alosit Yerusalem, koyaŋa ikekesisiak itomon ka luarei aiyeiyea, kotema kes korot atiar," 
Matthew20:18 “Koany, kidokari alosit Yerusalem; einakinio Okoku loka etuŋanan akanin nuka isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak, etubokinete ŋes atwanare;" 
Matthew20:19 ijaikinete ŋes Imo aboliar, ka aida, ka aibubukin, apaaran nakiwuniet ejaruni.”" 
Matthew20:20 Kosodi kobu toto naka odwe luka Sebedayo nepepe kodweke mama ejai Yesu, kokukokin kilip akirot," 
Matthew20:21 Kotema atiar, “Ikoto inyo?” Kotema atiar, “Kicorak ebe kiboikinos odweka lu luarei, ediopet kakanikon nakoteten, ediopet da nakokediany, kotoma akonijakanut.”" 
Matthew20:22 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Mam ijenete nuilipete. Ipedorete kereka aimat akoli naamasi eoŋ?” Kotemasi atiar, “Kipedori,”" 
Matthew20:23 Kotema kes atiar, “Imasete bo akolika, konye aiboikin akanika nakoteten ka nakokediany, mere nakaŋ aikor, konye erai nakec kaŋul kaluitemokinit Papaka.”" 
Matthew20:24 Kepuputu lutomon, konyunyurikis iinacan iarei." 
Matthew20:25 Konye Yesu konyarau kes, kotema atiar, “Ijenete ebe ikayaitok luka atekerin eyaito kes kagogoŋ, ejaas lukapolokokec kapedor mamakec." 
Matthew20:26 Konye mam ikote nen kamakus; konye ŋinituŋanan yenekoto araut yenikapolon kamakus korau ikusikejaanakinan," 
Matthew20:27 ŋin da yenekoto araut yenisodit korau ikusibulesit; 
Matthew20:28 kwape mam ebunitor Okoku loka etuŋanan aijaanakinio dimarai aijaanakin, ka ainakin da akeijar alakunia ikepuak.”" 
Matthew20:29 Nakeponiata koYeriko, kotupa ŋes ekodet loepol." 
Matthew20:30 Ido koany, kiboiete imudukiok iarei kariri kerot, nakiirariata kesi ebe itorit Yesu, kiworoto, kotemasi atiar, “Kitimoi, Ejakait, Okoku loka Daudi!”" 
Matthew20:31 Kiretak ekodet kes tetere ililiŋete; konye kiyatakis aiworo kotemasi atiar, “Kitimoi, Ejakait, Okoku loka Daudi!”" 
Matthew20:32 Kobwou Yesu, konyarau kes, kobala ebe, “Ikotos keswamakis inyo?”" 
Matthew20:33 Kotemasi atiar, “Ejakait, kikoto kitwekeny akosikonye.”" 
Matthew20:34 Kitim Yesu kes, kotiro akecekonye, atipet kokwenyut, kotupasi ŋes." 
Matthew21:1 Naeapiariata kesi Yerusalem, kodolot Betapage, moru loka Iseitunin, kosodi Yesu kijuka ikesisiak iarei," 
Matthew21:2 kotema kes atiar, “Koloto ore loisesenete, atipet idumunete asigiria naeenitai, ka ikekoku, kolacut, koinut eoŋ." 
Matthew21:3 Arai kitemari idiotuŋanan akirot, iboŋokinete ŋes ebe, ‘Ejakait ipuda kes.’ Kosodi atipet kijaikini kes.”" 
Matthew21:4 Kojaut ŋun tetere edoli akirot nakinerit enabi ebe," 
Matthew21:5 “Kolimokis yesi akoku naka Sion ebe, Koany, ebunit Ekabakakon mamakon, Loitasono, ibwanenit asigiria, Ibwanenit ikoku, ikoku yenikatiaŋ nakebwokan.”" 
Matthew21:6 Koloto ikesisiak, kiswamata kwape kicorakinitor Yesu kes." 
Matthew21:7 Koinut ŋes asigiria, ka ikekoku, kopetanakis ikecenapen; kibwanen ŋesi." 
Matthew21:8 Kopetanakis ituŋa luipu lukotoma okodet ikecenapen orot, ice da kojepununut atenieik kokito, kopetanakis kes da orot." 
Matthew21:9 Kiworoto ikodeta lukiŋarenikinito ka luketupakinito ŋes ebe, “Kosana mama ejai Okoku loka Daudi! Isirereŋitoi loebunit kokiror loka Ejakait! Kosana kuju noi kakuj!”" 
Matthew21:10 Nakelomaria ŋesi Yerusalem, korieŋut lukore kere, kobalas ebe, “Iŋai bo lo?”" 
Matthew21:11 Koboŋokis ikodeta ebe, “Ŋol ŋes enabi Yesu loko Nasaret nako Galilaya.”" 
Matthew21:12 Kosodi koloma Yesu toma oyekalu loka Edeke, kireŋea kere lukegwelanarete ka lukegwelete kotoma oyekalu, kobuburiana imesan luka ikesiecanarak arupian, ka iicoloŋo luka ŋul kalukegwelanarete ajeleik," 
Matthew21:13 kotema kes atiar, “Iwadikatai ebe, ‘Ekatogo enyaritai etogo lokilipet,’ konye yes ituluosi abua naka ikaŋatak.”" 
Matthew21:14 Kopotu imudukiok ka luicodos mama ejai oyekalu, kitaŋaleu kes." 
Matthew21:15 Konye nakeanyuniata isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak nukaumokin nukiswamai, ka idwe lukiworoete koyekalu ebe, “Kosana mama ejai Okoku loka Daudi!” konyunyurikinos;" 
Matthew21:16 kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Ipupi ijo nuinerasi lu?” Kotema kes Yesu atiar, “Eebo, mam isiomitos ebe, ‘Kaituke nuka idwe ludidik ka luenakete, Itodol aiturit?’ ”" 
Matthew21:17 Kinye kes, koloma kiŋa ka ere kiton Betania, koper ŋina." 
Matthew21:18 Tupuruc, nakeboŋoria ore, korieb eteŋei," 
Matthew21:19 Koany etini kariri kerot, kolot neejai, mam eanyuna ibore kokujuke dimarai akui bon. Kolimok ŋes ebe, “Mam bobo iraenenei araito ikar kere!” Atipet korinyo etini." 
Matthew21:20 Nakeanyuniata ikesisiak, koumokis, kobalas ebe, “Ekonaki bo ai etini erinyori atipet?”" 
Matthew21:21 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, Arai ijaas kaiyuun komam ibuonokinos, mam iswamaete ŋin naka etini bon, konye arai ilimokinete eroŋat lo ebe, ‘Koukor kocakar aŋolol,’ iswamaun." 
Matthew21:22 Kere da nuilipete kailipikus iyuunito, idumunete.”" 
Matthew21:23 Nakedaunia alomar toma oyekalu, kopotu lusasedotin lupeti ka imakio luka ituŋa mamakeŋ napisisianakini, kobalas ebe, “Iswamai ijo nu kapolou anyoin? Iŋai da kiinakini jo apolou ŋin?”" 
Matthew21:24 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Eoŋ da keŋisi yes akirot adiopet; arai kiboŋokinete eoŋ, ŋes konyet kalimokiniata yes apolou nakeswamaa nu." 
Matthew21:25 Aibatisa naka Yokana kebuni kai? Kebuni kotoma akuj, arai bo kotuŋa?” Kiŋitanakinos bonik ka bonik, kobalas ebe, “Arai kiitema ebe, ‘Kebuni kotoma akuj’; kitemari ŋesi oni ebe, ‘Aso kanukinyo mam kiyuuniata ŋes?’" 
Matthew21:26 Arai kiitema ebe, ‘Kebuni kotuŋa,’ kikuriana ekodet; naarai eomito ituŋa kere ebe kerai Yokana enabi.”" 
Matthew21:27 Koboŋokis Yesu kobalas ebe, “Mam kijeni.” Kotema kes atiar, “Eoŋ da mam kalimokini yes apolou nakeswamaa nu.”" 
Matthew21:28 “Konye iwomito biai? Kojaas etuŋanan idwe iarei; kolot mama ejai losodit kotema atiar, ‘Ikakoku, kolot lolo kiswama toma amana naka emusabibu.’" 
Matthew21:29 Koboŋok ebe, ‘Alosi Ipapa,’ konye mam eloto." 
Matthew21:30 Kolot mama ejai lokiareit kinera ŋupeŋun; Koboŋok ebe, ‘Mam akoto,’ kokau abu kitoronikin, kolot." 
Matthew21:31 Aso ali ka luarei kaŋul loabu kiswama nuakoto papake?” Kotemasi atiar, “Lokiareit.” Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Abeit, katemari yes atiar, Kigeikinete yes iketelemak esolo ka nudotea alomar toma ajakanut naka Edeke." 
Matthew21:32 Naarai abu Yokana kobu mamakus korot loka adolit, mam yes iyuuna, konye apotu iketelemak esolo ka nudotea kiyuutu ŋes; yes da nakianyuniata, mam ipotu kitoronikinos kokau, ka aiyuun ŋes," 
Matthew21:33 “Kopupokis awaragan ace. Kejai kolo etuŋanan elopet etogo, kira ŋesi amana naka emusabibu, kirigak abwas, kobokik aipany nacues tomake, koduk aiteis, kititiŋ ikeswamak, kolot akwap ace." 
Matthew21:34 Keapu apak naka araito, kijuka ikebulesin mama ejaas ikeswamak, adumun akeraito." 
Matthew21:35 Konye kikamut ikeswamak ikebulesin kodaata ece, koarata ece, ka ece da kibiribiroto kamor." 
Matthew21:36 Kijuka bobo ibulesin ice luipu adepar lusodit; kikonakis ŋul da nepenen. 
Matthew21:37 Kokau kijuka okokuke mamakec, kobala ebe, ‘Eyoŋete okokuka.’" 
Matthew21:38 Konye nakeanyuniata ikeswamak okoku, kineranakinos bonik ka bonik kobalas ebe, ‘Erai lo ekeruman; aso kaarata ŋes, kabeata oni akeirumet.’" 
Matthew21:39 Kikamut ŋes kocakas kiŋa kamana naka emusabibu koarata. 
Matthew21:40 Aso naebunio ejakait loka amana naka emusabibu ikonakini ai ikeswamak kwi?” 
Matthew21:41 Kotemasi atiar, “Emudiari erono ikaronok kwi, ititiŋi amana naka emusabibu ikeswamak ice lueinanakinete araito kedolo apak.”" 
Matthew21:42 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Mam isiomito nuiwadikatai ebe: ‘Amoru nakeŋerete ikadukok Ŋin ŋes keponi kitaraunai nakapolon naka agor; Abuni akirot ŋin kama ejai Ejakait, Erai nakaumokin kakonyenewok.’" 
Matthew21:43 Kanuka ŋun katemari yes atiar, Elemario ajakanut naka Edeke kamakus, einakinio ateker ace naerai akeraito.”" 
Matthew21:44 Yenibirokini kuju amoru ŋin ebilibiliun; konye ŋin yenibirokin amoru, ipicipicari ŋes cut." 
Matthew21:45 Nakiirariata isasedotin lupeti ka Iparisayon awaragasiake, kojenut ebe inerakinit kes." 
Matthew21:46 Nakemoiata aikamun ŋes, kokuriakata ikodeta, naarai aomito ebe erai ŋesi enabi." 
Matthew22:1 Koboŋok Yesu bobo, kiner kakes kawaragasia ebe," 
Matthew22:2 “Ajakanut naka akuj eputos bala ekabaka lokipoikini okokuke epucit loka eiterane. 
Matthew22:3 Kijuka ikebulesin anyaraun lukenyaritai aponare opucit; konye kogiroto kwi aponare. 
Matthew22:4 Kijuka bobo ibulesin ice, kobala ebe, ‘Kolimokis kwi lukenyaritai ebe, Koany, etemonok ikanyamat, adau aiar ikamoŋin ka ikatak lurobok, adau aitemonokin kere; kopotu do opucit.’" 
Matthew22:5 Konye kes mam apotu kopodos, koloto, ediopet omanikorike, ece agwelanarike," 
Matthew22:6 lukesalete da kikamut ikebulesin, kiswamakis nukepali, koarata," 
Matthew22:7 Kosodi konyunyurikin ekabaka, kijuka akejore komudia ikaarak kwi, kicwe da erekec," 
Matthew22:8 Kosodi kotema ikebulesin atiar, ‘Itemokino epucit, konye lukenyaritai mam ibusakinito." 
Matthew22:9 Aso koloto asisiarin nuka irotin, konyarautu ŋinituŋanan kere yenidumunete kobu opucit.’" 
Matthew22:10 Konyoutu ibulesin ŋul koloto orotin, kotukonokis lukedumunete kere, lueroko ka luejok da; kilelebun etogo loka epucit ipejok." 
Matthew22:11 Konye nakelomaria ekabaka aanyun ipejok, koany kanen etuŋanan lomam enapit anapito nakepucit." 
Matthew22:12 Kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Opapero, kilomuni ne biai komamei anapito nakepucit?’ Kobuta." 
Matthew22:13 Kosodi kotema ekabaka ikejaanakinak atiar, ‘Koenata akanin ka akeje, koyaŋaasi kocakakis amuton nakokiŋa; kaŋina ejaun aimony ka airiamanakin ikel.’" 
Matthew22:14 Naarai ipu luenyaritai, konye luseuna ikidioko.”" 
Matthew22:15 Kosodete koloto Iparisayon kinerut ailok ŋes kakiroke. 
Matthew22:16 Kiyakikis ŋes ikesisiakakec, nepepe ka Ikerodian, kobalas ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, kijeni ebe irai ijo lokabeit, isisianakini da erot loka Edeke kotoma abeit, kwabo mam ipodo idiotuŋanan kere; naarai mam iseseni ejautene loka ituŋa." 
Matthew22:17 Aso kolimokinai iwomit biai? Ibus kereka ainakin Kaisar esolo, arai bo mam?”" 
Matthew22:18 Konye Yesu kojen akeceronis, kotema atiar, “Yes lukesoswai, kanukinyo kikoduniata eoŋ?" 
Matthew22:19 Kitodikinai cani apesa naka esolo.” Koinunai adenari. 
Matthew22:20 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Nakaŋai aput na, ka nuiwadikatai?”" 
Matthew22:21 Kotemasi atiar, “Nuka Kaisar.” Kosodi kotema kes atiar, “Aso kotacakis Kaisar nueraas nuka Kaisar, ka Edeke da nueraas nuka Edeke.”" 
Matthew22:22 Kepuputu kesi koumokis; kinyeis ŋes koloto. 
Matthew22:23 Kapaaran kaŋin kopotu Isadukayon mamakeŋ, luebalas ebe emamei ajarun; kiŋita ŋes," 
Matthew22:24 kobalas ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, abu Musa kobala ebe, ‘Arai ketwana etuŋanan, komameete idwe, emanyi onaceke akeberu, tetere edumakini onaceke aur.’" 
Matthew22:25 Aso, kejaas iinacan ikanykaarei kamakosi; komany losodit, kotwana, ido naarai emamei ŋes aur kinyeinia onaceke akeberu;" 
Matthew22:26 kwape kwaŋin lokiareit, ka lokiwuniet, aitodol kere ikanykaarei." 
Matthew22:27 Akaulo kakere, kotwana aberu ŋin da." 
Matthew22:28 Aso, kotoma ajarun, eraun ŋin aberu naka ŋai kakwi kalukanykaarei? Naarai kere apotu kojaas kaŋes.”" 
Matthew22:29 Koboŋok Yesu kotema atiar, “Ipaarete yesi, naarai mam iienete nuiwadikatai karaida apedor naka Edeke." 
Matthew22:30 Naarai kotoma ajarun mam emanyete karaida adukokinio, konye eraas bala imalaikan kotoma akuj." 
Matthew22:31 Bobo da kakiro nuka ajarun kokatwak, mam isiomito akirot nakinerit Edeke ebe," 
Matthew22:32 ‘Arai eoŋ Edeke loka Aburaam, Edeke loka Isaak, ka Edeke loka Yakob da’? Mam ŋes erai Edeke loka lukatwak, konye loka lukaiarak.”" 
Matthew22:33 Nakiirariata ikodeta, koumokis akeisisianakin." 
Matthew22:34 Kosodete kiirasi Iparisayon ebe etubuta Isadukayon, kotukokinos," 
Matthew22:35 Ediopet kakes, ericakisila, kiŋit ŋes aiŋiset naekoduni," 
Matthew22:36 ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, aicorakinet ani erai nakapolon kotoma okisila?”" 
Matthew22:37 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Komina Ejakait Ekonideke kekonitau kere, ka akoniijar kere, ka akonicoa da kere." 
Matthew22:38 Na ŋes aicorakinet nakapolon nasodit. 
Matthew22:39 Ejai da nakiareit naeputotor ebe, Komina ikoniidunyet kwape iminar bon," 
Matthew22:40 Kotoma aicorakineta nu aarei kes icatunitotor ikisila kere ka inabin da.” 
Matthew22:41 Ketukokinos Iparisayon, kiŋit Yesu kes ebe," 
Matthew22:42 “Anyoika nuiwomito kanuka Kristo? Erai Okoku kaŋai?” Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Loka Daudi.”" 
Matthew22:43 Kiŋit kes ebe, “Aso kikwaikini ai Daudi enyarit ŋes Ejakait, koMoyo ebe," 
Matthew22:44 ‘Abu Ejakait kotema Ekajakait ebe, Kiboikin akanika nakoteten, Aitodol neebwaikinia lukasurupokon kwap kakejekon’?" 
Matthew22:45 Aso arai enyarit Daudi ŋes Ejakait, kikonakini bo ai erai ikekoku.”" 
Matthew22:46 Mam apedorit ituŋanan aboŋokin ŋes akirot, ido ameun kapaaran kaŋin amamei bobo yeniketitiŋikinit aiŋit ŋes adiokirot." 
Matthew23:1 Kosodi kotema Yesu ikodeta ka ikekesisiak atiar," 
Matthew23:2 “Iboikinos ikewadikak ka Iparisayon oicoloŋ loka Musa; 
Matthew23:3 aso nukilimokinete kere kiswamata, koricito da, konye sirikiswamata nuiswamaete kesi; naarai inerasi kesi kwabo mam iswamaete." 
Matthew23:4 Eenete arita nuelaŋir nuetioko aibwok, kisirioŋata ituŋa; kwabo mam kes ikulepek ekotosi atiror kebokoritikec," 
Matthew23:5 Iswamaete aswamisiokec kere tetere eanyunete ituŋa; naarai italalaarete ikuniaikec luetoronokinete oreeta; itoojaete da atokito nuka inapenekec. 
Matthew23:6 Ekotosi aibois nakapolon kopucin, ka iicoloŋo lukapolou kotoma atukosia," 
Matthew23:7 ka ayogao kagwelanareta, konyaritos ituŋa kes ebe Rabi." 
Matthew23:8 Konye yes, sirikinyaritai Rabi, naarai ejai yes ekesisianakinan ediopet, yes da kere iraas iinacan." 
Matthew23:9 Sirikinyarata ediotuŋanan papa kakwap, naarai ejai yes Papakus ediopet, loejai toma akuj." 
Matthew23:10 Sirikinyaritai da ikeŋarenok, naarai ejai yes ekeŋarenon ediopet, ŋes Kristo." 
Matthew23:11 Konye loerai lokapolon kotomakus eraun ekusikejaanakinan. 
Matthew23:12 Yenitopoloor bon itidisiario, yenitidisiar bon da itopoloorio." 
Matthew23:13 “Itukwi yes, ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, lukesoswai! Naarai igolokinete ituŋa ajakanut naka akuj; naarai yes ikulepek mam ilomarete, kwabo luelomarete da mam icamakinete alomar. [" 
Matthew23:14 Itukwi yes, ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, lukesoswai! Naarai icamete itogoi luka apuserun, kanuka ejose da ilipete ailipasia nueojak; kanuka ŋun kitubokinio aitelekarit.]" 
Matthew23:15 Itukwi yes, ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, lukesoswai! Naarai irimirimete aŋolol ka akwap, tetere ibelokinete idiopetuŋanan, kedau aibelokin ituluorete ŋes ikoku yenika Geena irwan aarei aitelekarit yes ikulepek." 
Matthew23:16 “Itukwi yes, ikeŋarenok lumudukiok, luibalas ebe, ‘Arai kiyapo ituŋanan kolimite eyekalu, mam akiro; konye ituŋanan yeniyapoi kolimite esabu loka eyekalu, aenikin.’" 
Matthew23:17 Ibaŋiok yesi, imudukiok! Naarai ali bo epol!, esabu arai bo eyekalu loitalauni esabu?" 
Matthew23:18 Ebe da, ‘Arai kiyapo ituŋanan kolimite otem, mam akiro; konye ituŋanan yeniyapoi kolimite asubanit naejai otem, aenikin.’" 
Matthew23:19 Imudukiok yesi! Naarai ani bo epol, ainakinet, arai bo etem loitalauni ainakinet?" 
Matthew23:20 Aso yeniyapoi kolimite etem, iyapoi kolimite ŋes ka ŋinibore kere yenejai tomake;" 
Matthew23:21 ŋin da yeniyapoi kolimite eyekalu, iyapoi kolimite ŋes ka ŋol da loiboie kotomakeŋ;" 
Matthew23:22 ŋin da yeniyapoi kolimite akuj, iyapoi kolimite eicoloŋ loka Edeke, ka ŋol da loiboikin tomakeŋ." 
Matthew23:23 “Itukwi yes, ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, lukesoswai! Naarai itacakinete iitomoneta luka emopim, ka aneta ka ekumin, konye inyeis akiro nuepolok nuka ikisila, kes etube ka aitim ka aiyuun; ibusakinit yes aswam ŋun, komam inyeinete kwa da." 
Matthew23:24 Yes ikeŋarenok lumudukiok, ijililiete esirut, ilikorete da akaala!" 
Matthew23:25 “Itukwi yes, ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, lukesoswai! Naarai itesegarete kiŋa kakolin, ka asanin, konye kotoma ileleba aiŋat ka airaŋanut," 
Matthew23:26 Ijo Eparisayot lomuduk! Kilot ber toma akoli ka asanit, tetere kiŋa da elauni." 
Matthew23:27 “Itukwi yes, ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, lukesoswai! Naarai iputosi katesina nuiworiworitai kakwanis, etakanete kokiŋa ejokuka, konye toma ileleba akojo nuka lukatwak ka amodokok da kere," 
Matthew23:28 Yes da kwape kwaŋin itakanete kokiŋa kaneejaas ituŋa koraas luidolito, konye kotomakus ileleba aisoswanut ka epali." 
Matthew23:29 “Itukwi yes, ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, lukesoswai! Naarai idukete atesin nuka inabin ka aitubus ailiin nuka ikadolitok," 
Matthew23:30 ka einer ebe, ‘Arai kiija isio kolo kapaarasia nuka lukapapaakosi, timam kiimorikikin kakes toma abukor aokot nuka inabin.’" 
Matthew23:31 Kanuka ŋun itejenunos bonik ebe iraas yesi ikecedwe kalukearete inabin. 
Matthew23:32 Aso kilelebata aitemis naka lukapapaakus. 
Matthew23:33 Yes imunwo, yes ailwek naka imusagan, ikuete biai atubokinio naka Geena?" 
Matthew23:34 Kanuka ŋun koany, kejukakini yes inabin, ka lukacoa, ka ikewadikak; iarete ice kakesi, ka aibubuonokin, idaete ice kotoma atukosiakus, irukitotor da koreria kere." 
Matthew23:35 Tetere kibeikinete yes aokot kere nuka ikadolitok nukebukokinos kakwap, ageun kaokot nuka Abel ekadoliton, kiton aokot nuka Sakaria okoku loka Barakia, lokiarakinete kidiŋ aibois nakalaunan ka etem," 
Matthew23:36 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Eponikinete akiro ŋun kere atur na." 
Matthew23:37 “Wu okwe, Yerusalem, Yerusalem, loeari inabin, ka aibiribir kamor ŋul lukiyakunio mamakon! Irwan imwa ai abu kakotor atukonokin ikonidwe, kwape etukonokinia akokor ikemiyoi kwap abebenokake, konye mam yes ekotokino!" 
Matthew23:38 Koany kinyeinere yes ekusitogo esil. 
Matthew23:39 Naarai katemari yes atiar, Mam kianyunete eoŋ bobo cut, aitodol naitemariata ebe, ‘Isirereŋitoi ŋol loebunit kokiror loka Ejakait.’”" 
Matthew24:1 Kolom Yesu koyekalu, ido napelosi, kopotu ikekesisiak mama ejai, kitodikis aduketa nuka eyekalu." 
Matthew24:2 Konye Koboŋok kes kotema atiar, “Ianyut kereka nu kere? Abeit katemari yes atiar, mam esalakini ne amoru kuju kamoru, namam etiyakinio.”" 
Matthew24:3 Nakiboio koMoru loka Iseitunin, kopotu ikesisiak mama ejai kaiyeiyea, kobalas ebe, “Kolimokinai, ejaunete akiro ŋun wori, anyoin da aanyunet naka abunorekon, ka naka esaŋe loka akwapin?”" 
Matthew24:4 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Kocoito kinyek ituŋanan aitapaar yes."
