Matthew24:5 Naarai epote rwaru luipu kokirorika, ebalas ebe, ‘Eoŋ arai Kristo,’ itapaarete kesi luipu." 
Matthew24:6 Iirarete yesi nuka ijiisio ka iemuto luka ijiisio; kocoito sirikiyaloŋoŋoto; naarai ibusakinit ŋun ajaun, konye koroko awasia edoluno." 
Matthew24:7 Naarai enyoikini ateker asurokin ateker, ajakanut da asurokin ajakanut, ejaunun ebel ka amaran naka akwap aiboisio nuegelegela;" 
Matthew24:8 eraas ŋun kere ageunet naka ariebo naka aidoun," 
Matthew24:9 “Kapak kaŋin kijaikinete yes aiticanio, kiarete; kiŋarunete yes atekerin kanuka ekakiror." 
Matthew24:10 Kosodete iguikinete luipu, kes da ebilanakinos ibotei, ka aŋaranar." 
Matthew24:11 Enyounete inabin luipu lukeŋalak, itapaarete luipu." 
Matthew24:12 Ido naarai iyatakina epali, ejoniari amin naka luipu." 
Matthew24:13 Konye ŋin yenetitiŋikini kiton awasia, ŋes itajario." 
Matthew24:14 Elimonokinio Akiro nu Nukajokak nuka ajakanut anatar akwapin kere, araut akajenak mama ejaas atekerin kere; kosodi konyet edoluni awasia." 
Matthew24:15 “Aso naianyuniata etal loemudiari lokinerit enabi Daniel ebwoi kotoma aibois nakalaunan (kojenu ikasoman)," 
Matthew24:16 ŋes konyet ekeriata ŋul luejaas Yudaya oroŋan; 
Matthew24:17 ituŋanan yenejai kuju togo sirikedoku ayaŋaar iboro luejaas togoke; 
Matthew24:18 ido yenejai mana da sirikeboŋu kau ayaŋaar akenapito. 
Matthew24:19 Konye itukwi kes nuepotiete, ka nuitanakete da kapaarasia kaŋun!" 
Matthew24:20 Kilipata yesi kinyek akusikerit adolun kiporo, karaida apaaran naka asabato:" 
Matthew24:21 naarai ejaunos ican luipu, lumam peŋo etakanunito ameun kageunet naka akwap kiton kwana, ido mam bobo ejaunete cut." 
Matthew24:22 Arai kedim iŋoŋaritai apaarasia ŋun, timam kitajari akuan kere; konye kanuka luseuna iŋoŋario apaarasia ŋun." 
Matthew24:23 Kapak kaŋin arai kitemari yes ituŋanan atiar, ‘Koany, ejai Kristo ne,’ arai, ‘Ejai laije’, sirikiyuut." 
Matthew24:24 Naarai enyounete lukriston lukeŋalak, ka inabin Iukeŋalak, itoduunete ŋul aanyuneta nuepolok, ka nukaumokin da; tetere itapaarete luseuna arai epedoros." 
Matthew24:25 Koany, kadau aikwenyar yes eroko nu epona." 
Matthew24:26 Aso arai kitemarete yes atiar, ‘Koany, ejai amodiŋ’; sirikiloto. Ebe da, ‘Koany, ejai toma agola’ sirikiyuut." 
Matthew24:27 Naarai kwape imiliaunia ageun kokide kotakani kiton to; ikoni nen abunore naka Okoku loka etuŋanan. 
Matthew24:28 Naarai neejai akuan nakatwan, etukonokinos da atarukon nen." 
Matthew24:29 “Konye atipet, ketuboros ican luka apaarasia kakwa, itumutonorio akoloŋ, mam elap ecauni, ibirununos aacer kotoma akuj, iianiianio da nukapedor nuka akuj;" 
Matthew24:30 kosodi konyet etakanuni aanyunet naka Okoku loka etuŋanan kokuju; kosodete konyet ibworos atekerin kere nuka akwap, eanyunete Okoku loka etuŋanan ebuni kodouon luka akuj kapedor ka aibuses naepol." 
Matthew24:31 Ijukuni ikemalaikan keporoto loepol loka arupepe, etukonokinete luseunake anyoun kokwamin iwoŋon, ameun kosaŋe ediopet loka akuj kiton loce." 
Matthew24:32 “Kisisiautu akewaragan kama ejai etini; kedaut aketenieik alibun, itolomuni akekui, ijenunete ebe eapie apak naka aidweny;" 
Matthew24:33 aso yes da naianyuniata ŋun kere, kojenut ebe eapie ŋesi, kokek," 
Matthew24:34 Abeit katemari yes atiar, mam atur na edaun aitodol naedolioto akiro ŋun kere," 
Matthew24:35 Edaunos akuj ka akwapin, konye akakiro mam edaunos cut." 
Matthew24:36 “Konye akiro nuka apaaran kaya ka esawa da emamei yenejeni, karaida imalaikan luejaas toma akuj, karaida Okoku, dimikito Papa bon." 
Matthew24:37 Naarai kwape kejaatar apaarasia nuka Noa, ikonakini nen abunore naka Okoku loka etuŋanan," 
Matthew24:38 Naarai kwape kejaatar toma apaarasia nukegeikinete akalele, anyamete, amasete, amanyasi, amanyio da, kiton apaaran nakelomaria Noa toma ataker," 
Matthew24:39 komam kejenete kiton neadolunio akalele kolelea kere, ikonakini nen abunore naka Okoku loka etuŋanan." 
Matthew24:40 Kapak kaŋin ejaikinos ituŋa iarei omanikor; eyaŋaario ediopet, inyeinio loce." 
Matthew24:41 Ejaikinos aŋor aarei iriete; eyaŋaario adiopet, inyeinio nace." 
Matthew24:42 Aso kokwenyete; naarai mam ijenete apaaran anyoin naebunio Ejakait ikus. 
Matthew24:43 Konye kojenutu na ebe, arai kejeni elopet etogo apak naka akuare naebunio ekokolan, tikekweny, kwabo timam kejalaki eketogo abokio." 
Matthew24:44 Kanuka ŋun kokapakina yesi da; naarai ebuni Okoku loka etuŋanan kosawa lomam iwomito. 
Matthew24:45 “Aso iŋai bo ebulesit lomunot loepiriana da, lokedakakini ejakaitike ayait lukokaleke akoranakin kes ikecenyamat apakio nuedolito?" 
Matthew24:46 Isirereŋitoi ebulesit ŋol loedumuni ejakaitike iswamai kwaŋin naebunio. 
Matthew24:47 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Edakakini ŋes ayait luejaatar kere." 
Matthew24:48 Konye arai ketema ebulesit ŋol lokaronon kotauke atiar, ‘Eyapa papaka,’" 
Matthew24:49 kogeu aibuŋa ibulesin lukaupake, ainyam ka aimat nepepe kalukamerak," 
Matthew24:50 ebuni ejakait loka ebulesit kaŋol kapaaran namam ŋes eomit, ka esawa da lomam ejeni," 
Matthew24:51 etubi ŋes katutubeta aarei, itebei ekewai nepepe ka lukesoswai; ejaun kanen aimony ka airiamanakin ikel." 
Matthew25:1 “Kapakio kaŋun ituputoorio ajakanut naka akuj kapesuru atomon nukelemunete atalaikec koloto airiamun keteran. 
Matthew25:2 Akany kakes kebanaaka, akany da kepiriaka." 
Matthew25:3 Naarai nakeyaŋaariata nukebaŋaaka atalaikec, mam apotu koyaŋaasi akinyet da;" 
Matthew25:4 Konye nukepiriaka koyaŋaasi akinyet kokubeikec nepepe katalaikec. 
Matthew25:5 Nakiyapia eteran, kiluranaros kere, kojotooros." 
Matthew25:6 Konye kidiŋebai kojau ecelet ebe, ‘Koany, eteran! Kolomutu kisiriamasi.’" 
Matthew25:7 Kosodete konyout apesur ŋun kere, kitemonokis atalaikec." 
Matthew25:8 Kotemasi nukebaŋaaka nukepiriaka ebe, ‘Koinakinai sio da amodiokinyetekus, naarai aduŋeosi akositalai.’" 
Matthew25:9 Konye koboŋokis nukepiriaka ebe, ‘Diat mam ilosikin sio kayes; koloto gwai mama ejaas ikagwelanarak kogwelut.’" 
Matthew25:10 Konye napelosete agwel, kobu eteran, kolomasi nuetemokino nepepe kaŋes toma opucit; kogolokinoi ekek." 
Matthew25:11 Kokau kopotu apesur nuce da kobalas ebe, ‘Ejakait, ejakait, koŋaarai.’" 
Matthew25:12 Konye Koboŋok, kotema atiar, ‘Abeit katemari yes atiar, mam kajeni yes.’" 
Matthew25:13 Aso kokwenyete, naarai mam ijenete apaaran karaida esawa." 
Matthew25:14 “Naarai esubit bala etuŋanan loelosi apejo konyarau ikebulesin, kititiŋ kes ikeboro." 
Matthew25:15 Koinak ediopet atalatan akany, ka ece aarei, ka ece da adiopet, ŋolituŋanan kwape kejaar apedorike; kosodi kolot akwap ace." 
Matthew25:16 Atipet kolot ŋol lokedumuni atalatan akany, kogwelana, kitobon ameda naka atalatan ace akany." 
Matthew25:17 Kwape kwaŋin lokeinakinitai aarei, kitobon ameda naka atalatan ace aarei." 
Matthew25:18 Konye lokeinakinitai atalat adiopet, kolot kobok alup, kibwa apesan nuka ejakaitike." 
Matthew25:19 Kosodi ketuboros apaarasia nuipu, kobu ejakait loka ibulesin kaŋul, kimar kakes akepesan." 
Matthew25:20 Kobu lokeinakinitai atalatan akany, koyau atalatan ace akany, kotema atiar, ‘Ejakait, ibu kititiŋ eoŋ atalatan akany; koany, etoboŋu atalatan ace akany.’" 
Matthew25:21 Kotema ejakaitike atiar, ‘Ejok, ebulesit ijo loejok lomunot da; ibu korau lomunot kaluikidioko, kadakakini jo ayait luipu; aso kolom ma toma aiyalama naka ejakaitikon.’" 
Matthew25:22 Kobu da ŋol lokeinakinitai atalatan aarei, kotema atiar, ‘Ejakait, ibu kititiŋ eoŋ atalatan aarei; koany, etoboŋu atalatan ace aarei.’" 
Matthew25:23 Kotema ejakaitike atiar, ‘Ejok, ebulesit ijo loejok lomunot da; ibu korau lomunot kaluikidioko, kadakakini jo ayait luipu; aso kolom ma ijo da toma aiyalama naka ejakaitikon.’" 
Matthew25:24 Kobu da ŋol lokeinakinitai atalat adiopet, kotema atiar, ‘Ejakait, abu kajen ebe irai ijo etuŋanan loeninik, idwenyi kama nemam iyeikinit, itukonokini kanemam isiarakinit;" 
Matthew25:25 aso kakurianar, kalot kebwa akonitalat kalup: koany, napekon na.’" 
Matthew25:26 Konye Koboŋok ejakaitike kotema atiar, ‘Ebulesit ijo loerono loeloŋwana! Ibu kojen ebe adwenyi kama nemam ayeikinit, atukonokini da kanemam esiarakinit;" 
Matthew25:27 ti ibusakinit ijo ainakin akapesan mama ejaas ikeŋadak arupian, eoŋ da kabu tikadum nuaraas nukaŋ ka amedakec da." 
Matthew25:28 Aso kodemasi ŋes atalat, koinakis ŋol loeiaas atalatan atomon." 
Matthew25:29 Naarai yenejai ibore einakinio, ido edumuni luipu noi; konye yenemamei ibore, ŋin da yenejaas kaŋes edemario." 
Matthew25:30 Kocakakisi ebulesit ŋol lomam ajokis amuton nakokiŋa: ejaun kanen aimony ka airiamanakin ikel.’ 
Matthew25:31 “Naebunio Okoku loka etuŋanan kotoma aibusesuke, ka imalaikan da kere nepepe kaŋes, iboikini oicoloŋoke loka aibuses;" 
Matthew25:32 etukonokinos atekerin kere akonyeneke, etiakatiakai ŋesi kes kwape etiakatiakaa ekecokon amerekekin ka akinei:" 
Matthew25:33 ibwaikini amerekekin akanike nakoteten ka akinei da akanike nakokediany. 
Matthew25:34 Kosodi etemari ekabaka lukakanike nakoteten atiar, ‘Kopotu yesi lukisirereŋit Papaka, kirumata ajakanut nakitemonokinitoi ameun kaisub akwapin;" 
Matthew25:35 naarai kariebi eteŋei, ipotu koinakis aimuj, kaiakit akur, ipotu koinakis numatan; arai epejonon, ipotu kisukunyikis;" 
Matthew25:36 amujalal, ipotu kitanapa; adeka, ipotu koanyanasi; ajai toma aidaris, kopotu mama ajai.’" 
Matthew25:37 Kosodete eboŋokinete ikadolitok ebe, ‘Ejakait, kipou kaanyutu jo wori kiriebi eteŋei, kesimujata? Arai kijakit akur, ketamata?" 
Matthew25:38 Kipou kaanyut jo wori irai epejonon, kesukunyikis? Arai imujalal, ketanapa?" 
Matthew25:39 Kipou da kaanyutu jo wori ideka, arai toma aidaris, kapotu mama ijai?’" 
Matthew25:40 Kanen eboŋokini ekabaka ebe, ‘Abeit katemari yes atiar, Kwape kiswamakiniata idiopet kalu iinacanaka ludidik, ipotu kiswamakis eoŋ.’" 
Matthew25:41 Kosodi do etemari lukakanike nakokediany atiar, ‘Irwa yesi, lukilamakinitai, kolomasi akim naka ikar kere naitemokinitoi Satan ka ikemalaikan." 
Matthew25:42 Naarai kariebi eteŋei, mam ipotu koinakis aimuj; kajakit akur, mam ipotu koinakis numatan;" 
Matthew25:43 arai epejonon, mam ipotu kisukunyikis; amujalal, mam ipotu kitanapa; adeka, ajai da toma aidaris, mam ipotu koanyanasi.’" 
Matthew25:44 Kosodete eboŋokinete kesi da ebe, ‘Ejakait, kipou kaanyutu jo wori iriebi eteŋei, arai kijakit akur, arai irai epejonon, arai imujalal, arai ideka, arai ijai toma aidaris, komam kijaanakinit jo?’" 
Matthew25:45 Kanen eboŋokini kes ebe, ‘Abeit katemari yes atiar, Kwape mam kiswamakiniata idiopet kaludidik kalu, mam ipotu kiswamakis eoŋ.’" 
Matthew25:46 Elosete ŋul alomar toma aiticanio naka ikar kere, konye luedolito elosete toma aijar naka ikar kere.”" 
Matthew26:1 Nakedaunia Yesu akiro ŋun kere, kotema ikekesisiak atiar," 
Matthew26:2 “Ijenete ebe esalito apaarasia aarei, kosodi ejaun Aleleŋ, ijaikinio Okoku loka etuŋanan aibubukinio.”" 
Matthew26:3 Kosodete kotukonokinos isasedotin lupeti ka imakio luka ituŋa toma alaro naka esasedoti lopeti, ekekiror Kaiapa," 
Matthew26:4 kinerut nepepe tetere ikamunete Yesu kapirianut kosodete aiar. 
Matthew26:5 Konye kobalas ebe, “Mere toma apak naka epucit, kinyek ecelet ajaun kotuŋa.”" 
Matthew26:6 Nakejaar Yesu Betania togo loka Simon lokatapon," 
Matthew26:7 kobu aberu mamakeŋ nakejai ekube loka akinyet naketiai loepol noi, kobukok akouke, iboie enyami," 
Matthew26:8 Konye nakeanyuniata ikekesisiak, konyunyuras kobalas ebe, “Anyoin aimadiŋ na?" 
Matthew26:9 Naarai tikegwelar akinyet na apesan nuipu, akoranakin lukican.”" 
Matthew26:10 Konye kojenu Yesu, kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo itiyaloŋoŋooto aberu na? Naarai keswamaki eoŋ aswam naejok." 
Matthew26:11 Naarai apaarasia kere ejaas lukican nepepe kayes, konye eoŋ mam kija kayes apaarasia kere." 
Matthew26:12 Naarai kanu abukokinia akuanaka akinyet ŋin, eswama kwaŋin tetere itemokini eoŋ aidaio." 
Matthew26:13 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Neelimonokinio Akiro nu Nukajokak kotoma akwapin kere, ŋin naeswama aberu na elimorio akiitunitor ŋes.”" 
Matthew26:14 Kapak kaŋin kolot ediopet kalutomon kaarei, ekekiror Yuda Isikariot, mama ejaas isasedotin lupeti," 
Matthew26:15 kotema kes atiar, “Kiinakinete eoŋ inyo arai kejaik ŋes mamakus?” Kotacakis ŋes atutubeta akaisauni nuka epuesa." 
Matthew26:16 Ameun kapak kaŋin komoote apak naejok aijaikinia ŋes. 
Matthew26:17 Kapaaran nasodit naka imugatin lumam itubuunitoi, kopotu ikesisiak mama ejai Yesu, kotemasi atiar, “Ikoto ketemokis lali konyamak lukaleleŋ?”" 
Matthew26:18 Kotema atiar, “Kolot ore mama ejai mutan, kolimokis ŋes ebe, ‘Ebala Ekesisianakinan ebe, aapu akapak; etodolikini Aleleŋ orekon nepepe kikakesisiak.’ ”" 
Matthew26:19 Kiswamata ikesisiak kwape kicorakinia Yesu, kitemokis lukaleleŋ." 
Matthew26:20 Nakimukoki akwap, kiboikin ainyam nepepe kikesisiak lutomon kaarei;" 
Matthew26:21 napenyamete, kotema atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, ediopet kayes kabilakini eoŋ ebotet.”" 
Matthew26:22 Kitururwoto noi, kogeut aiŋitanar ŋes ediopet ediopet ebe, “Ŋes ca nat eoŋ ya, Ejakait?”" 
Matthew26:23 Koboŋok ebe, “Ŋol lokicunyi keoŋ atibo, ŋes kabilakini ebotet." 
Matthew26:24 Elosi Okoku loka etuŋanan kwape kiwadikatere kanukeŋ, konye itukwi etuŋanan ŋol loebilakini Okoku loka etuŋanan ebotet! Tiejok kama ketuŋanan kaŋol arai mam kewuruunitai.”" 
Matthew26:25 Koboŋok Yuda lokebilakinit ŋes ebotet kotema atiar, “Ŋes ca nat eoŋ ya, Rabi?” Kotema atiar, “Ijo ibala.”" 
Matthew26:26 Napenyamete, kolem Yesu emugati, kisirereŋ, kobilibil, koinak ikesisiak, kobala ebe, “Kolemutu, konyamata; lo ŋes akakuan.”" 
Matthew26:27 Kolem akoli da, kedau aimal, koinak kes, kobala ebe, “Komata yesi kere lo:" 
Matthew26:28 naarai nu kes akaokot nuka aitutuket, nuebukoros kanuka ikepuak alemar aronisio," 
Matthew26:29 Katemari yes atiar, Mam amasi bobo cut nuka araito na naka emusabibu kiton apaaran ya naamasia nukitetiak nepepe kayes kotoma ajakanut naka Papaka.”" 
Matthew26:30 Nakedauniata ayoore ekosio, kolomasi koloto Moru loka Iseitunin," 
Matthew26:31 Kosodi Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Iguikinos yesi kere kakuar kana kanukaŋ; naarai iwadikatai ebe, ‘Ebuŋai rwaru ekecokon, isiarakinos amerekekin nukosipan.’" 
Matthew26:32 Konye kadau ajarun, keŋarenikinete yes alosit Galilaya.”" 
Matthew26:33 Koboŋok Petero kotema ŋes atiar, “Karaida kiguikinos kere kanukon, konye eoŋ mam keguikini cut.”" 
Matthew26:34 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Abeit katemari jo atiar, akuar na, eriŋa ekokoro keruikino, kiŋeri eoŋ irwan auni.”" 
Matthew26:35 Kotema Petero atiar, “Karaida kebusakinit atwanare kajo, mam kaŋeri jo cut.” Kinerata ikesisiak kere da kwape kwaŋin." 
Matthew26:36 Kosodi kodolok Yesu nepepe kakes aibois naenyaritai Getesemane, kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Kiboikinos ber ne, kekunya ŋina ailip.”" 
Matthew26:37 Koyaŋa Petero ka odwe iarei luka Sebedayo, kogeu aiturur ka aburun." 
Matthew26:38 Kosodi kotema kes atiar, “Itururwei ekatau noi, aapiar atwanare; kosalata yesi ne, kokwenya nepepe keoŋ.”" 
Matthew26:39 Kikunyak nediokasilon, kibiror ebuburia, kilip ebe, “Wu Papaka, arai epedoros, kenac akoli na; konye mere nuakoto eoŋ, dimarai kwape ikotor ijo.”" 
Matthew26:40 Kobu mama ejaas ikesisiak, kodum kes ejotoete; kotema ŋesi Petero atiar, “Aso ca mam ipedorete aikweny nepepe keoŋ esawa ediopet?" 
Matthew26:41 Kokwenya, kilipa kinyeis alomar toma acodunio; ekoto bo emoyo, konye ekalanyana akuan.”" 
Matthew26:42 Koboŋo bobo nakiareit kilip ebe, “Papaka, arai mam epedori akoli na ainac komam eoŋ amasi, kiswamai do nuikoto ijo.”" 
Matthew26:43 Kobu bobo kodum kes ejotoete, naarai eluranaros ajo." 
Matthew26:44 Kinye kes bobo, kolot kilip nakiwuniet, inera bobo akiro kwapekwa." 
Matthew26:45 Kosodi kobu mama ejaas ikesisiak, kotema kes atiar, “Iroko kereka ijotoete, iyeŋito? Koany aapu esawa, einakinio Okoku loka etuŋanan akanin nuka ikadiakanarak." 
Matthew26:46 Konyoutu, kaloto; koany, eapie lokabilaki ebotet.”" 
Matthew26:47 Napinera ŋesi kobu Yuda, ediopet kotomon kaluarei, koupas kekodet loepol lokejaas ikileŋa, ka ibelai, epote kama ejaas isasedotin lupeti ka imakio luka ituŋa," 
Matthew26:48 Koinakinite lokebilakini ŋes ebotet kes aanyunet ebe, “Loanui eoŋ ŋes ŋol; kikamutu ŋes.”" 
Matthew26:49 Atipet kolot mama ejai Yesu, kotema atiar, “Yoga, Rabi!” Konu noi," 
Matthew26:50 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Opapero, kiswama nukiyaunito.” Kosodete kikunyakis koriosi akecekanin kikamut Yesu," 
Matthew26:51 Ido koany, ediopet kaŋul kalukejaas kaYesu korio akekan, kout ekekileŋ, kinom ebulesit loka losasedoti lopeti, kojepa akekit." 
Matthew26:52 Kosodi Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Kinyakak ekileŋikon aiboisike; naarai kere luekapito ikileŋa, emudiari ekileŋ." 
Matthew26:53 Arai iwomitos ebe mam apedori aiŋaiŋa Papaka, kejukak kwape kwana irioŋeta luedeparito itomon ka luarei luka imalaikan?" 
Matthew26:54 Aso edolete biai nukiwadikatai ebe ibusakinit ŋun ajaun?” 
Matthew26:55 Kosawa kaŋol kotema Yesu ikodeta atiar, “Ilomutu teni yesi kikileŋa ka ibelai aikamun eoŋ, bala ekaŋatan? Ŋinipaaran eboonokin kotoma oyekalu esisianakini, komam kikamunete eoŋ," 
Matthew26:56 Konye ajaut nu kere tetere edolete nukiwadikato inabin.” Kosodete kojalakis ŋes ikesisiak kere, kokerata." 
Matthew26:57 Lukikamunete Yesu koyaŋaasi mama ejai Kaiapa losasedoti lopeti, neketukonokina ikewadikak ka imakio." 
Matthew26:58 Kotupa Petero kama elwana, kiton alaro naka losasedoti lopeti, koloma toma, kiboikin nepepe ka ikedarak aanyun nuebeikinete." 
Matthew26:59 Aso komoata isasedotin lupeti ka aurianet kere ikajenak lukeŋalak aluikin Yesu tetere earete," 
Matthew26:60 mam edumuna, karaida ketakanut ikajenak luipu lukeŋalak, Konye kokau kotakanut iarei," 
Matthew26:61 kobalas ebe, “Abala ŋol ebe, apedori aiket eyekalu loka Edeke, ka adukokin apaarasia auni.”" 
Matthew26:62 Kosodi kobwo losasedoti lopeti kotema atiar, “Mam ca bo iboŋokini akirot? Anyoika ŋun nuetejenut ŋul aluikin jo?”" 
Matthew26:63 Konye kililiŋ Yesu. Kotema losasedoti lopeti ŋes atiar, “Kesiyapoi jo mama ejai Edeke lokajaran, kolimokinai cani sio arai irai ijo Kristo, Okoku loka Edeke.”" 
Matthew26:64 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Ijo ibala, Konye katemari yes atiar, Amear kwana ianyunete Okoku loka etuŋanan iboie kakan nakoteten naka Apedor, ebuni kotoma odouon luka akuj.”" 
Matthew26:65 Kosodi kocil losasedoti lopeti ikenapen, kobala ebe, “Ainyanaki, Anyoika bobo kipudar ikajenak? Koany, iirasi kwana akeinyanakin," 
Matthew26:66 Iwomitos anu?” Koboŋokis ebe, “Ibusakinit atwanare.”" 
Matthew26:67 Kosodete kimwaanakis aimul akonyeneke, kodipidipoto ŋes; ice da kibapanasi," 
Matthew26:68 kobalas ebe, “Ijo Kristo, kodwarak iŋai! Iŋai bo kibuŋa?”" 
Matthew26:69 Kiboie Petero kokiŋa kotoma alaro: kobu apese mama ejai kobala ebe, “Ijai nan ijo da nepepe kaYesu Egalilayat.”" 
Matthew26:70 Konye koŋer kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere, kobala ebe, “Mam ajeni nuinera ijo.”" 
Matthew26:71 Konye nakelomunia okek, koany acepese ŋes, kotema ŋesi lukejaas nen atiar, “Ajai lo da nepepe ka Yesu Enasarayot.”" 
Matthew26:72 Koŋer bobo kaiyapo ebe, “Mam ajeni etuŋanan ŋol.”" 
Matthew26:73 Nediokasilon kopotu lukebwoete kanen, kotemasi Petero atiar, “Abeit irai ijo lokec, naarai itejenunit ekoniiner.”" 
Matthew26:74 Kosodi kogeu eilam ka aiyapo ebe, “Mam eoŋ ajeni etuŋanan ŋol.” Atipet koruik ekokor." 
Matthew26:75 Kiitu Petero akirot nakelimokini Yesu ŋes ebe, “Eriŋa ekokor keruikino, kiŋeri eoŋ irwan auni.” Koloma kiŋa komonyi noi akiyo." 
Matthew27:1 Napekiwala akwap, kinerut isasedotin lupeti ka imakio kere luka ituŋa asurokin Yesu aiar;" 
Matthew27:2 koenata ŋes, koyaŋaasi, kijaikis Pilato lokerai ekayaiton." 
Matthew27:3 Kosodi Yuda lokebilakini ŋes ebotet, keanyu ebe adaun atubokin aitelekar, kiitok, kinyakak isasedotin lupeti ka imakio atutubeta akaisauni nuka epuesa," 
Matthew27:4 kobala ebe, “Abu kadiak, abilakin ebotet aokot numam akirot.” Konye kotemasi kesi atiar, “Anu nat kamakosi? Nukon bo ŋun.”" 
Matthew27:5 Kocakak atutubeta kwa nuka epuesa aibois nakalaunan, konyou; kolot komiedakin." 
Matthew27:6 Kolemasi isasedotin lupeti atutubeta nuka epuesa, kobalas ebe, “Mam ibus aibwaikin kes aiŋadis, naarai eraas etiai loka aokot.”" 
Matthew27:7 Kinerut, kogweluniata emanikor loka ekajean, aidaanakin nen ikalotok." 
Matthew27:8 Kanuka ŋun ŋes enyaritere emanikor ŋol, Emanikor loka Aokot, kiton lolo," 
Matthew27:9 Kosodi kitodolikinoi akirot nakinerit Yeremia enabi ebe, “Apotu kolemasi atutubeta akaisauni nuka epuesa, etiai loka ŋol kalokitirianitai, lokitirianete ice kodwe luka Isirael:" 
Matthew27:10 kogweliata emanikor loka ekajean kwape kicorakinia Ejakait.” 
Matthew27:11 Kobwo Yesu kakonyen nuka ekayaiton; kiŋit ekayaiton ŋes ebe, “Irai kereka ijo ekabaka loka Iyudayan?” Kotema Yesu atiar, “Ijo ibala.”" 
Matthew27:12 Nakiwosaata ŋes isasedotin lupeti ka imakio mam eboŋokino akirot. 
Matthew27:13 Kosodi kotema Pilato ŋes atiar, “Mam kereka jo ipupi nuetia nen nuiwosaete kesi?”" 
Matthew27:14 Mam ŋes eboŋokino, karaida amodiokirot: koumok noi ekayaiton." 
Matthew27:15 Ketapit ekayaiton kopucit aosianakin ekodet eenat ediopet lokekotonokinos," 
Matthew27:16 Kejaas keenat loajenikina kapak kaŋin, lokenyaritai Baraba." 
Matthew27:17 Naketukokinotor, kotema Pilato kes atiar, “Ikotosi kaosikis yes iŋai? Baraba arai bo Yesu loenyaritai Kristo?”" 
Matthew27:18 Naarai ajeni ŋesi ebe ainakis kanuka ekolo. 
Matthew27:19 Nakiboikinor oicoloŋ loka aitub, kiyakik akeberu ŋes, kotema atiar, “Sirikiswamak ekadoliton ŋol adiokirot; naarai keticani nuipu kairujasit kakuar kana kanukeŋ.”" 
Matthew27:20 Kosodete kisidikoto isasedotin lupeti ka imakio ikodeta tetere ilipete Baraba, ka amudiar Yesu." 
Matthew27:21 Konye Koboŋok ekayaiton kotema kes atiar, “Ikotosi kaosikis yes iŋai ka luarei?” Kobalas ebe, “Baraba,”" 
Matthew27:22 Kotema Pilato kes atiar, “Aso do ekonakini ai Yesu loenyaritai Kristo?” Kobalas kere ebe, “Kibubukinoi.”" 
Matthew27:23 Kobala ebe, “Kanukinyo? Naanyoin aronis nakiswamai?” Konye kiyatakisi kesi aiworo noi ebe, “Kibubukinoi,”" 
Matthew27:24 Kosodi keanyu Pilato ebe mam nuepedori, konye iyata ecelet, kolem akipi, kilot akekanin kakonyen nuka ekodet, kobala ebe, “Emamei eoŋ akirot kotoma aokot nuka etuŋanan kalo loedolit: nukus bo ŋun.”" 
Matthew27:25 Koboŋokis ituŋa kere ebe, “Kobeikisi akeokot sio, ka ikosidwe da.”" 
Matthew27:26 Kosodi koosik kes Baraba: konye kedau aida Yesu, koinak tetere ibubukinio," 
Matthew27:27 Kosodete iserikalei luka ekayaiton koyaŋaasi Yesu toma opuraitorion, kotukonokin erioŋet kere mama ejai," 
Matthew27:28 Kolacasi ikenapen, kitanapa anapito nakareŋan," 
Matthew27:29 Kojeata aboko naka ikukwa, kitanapikis akouke, ka agada da kakanike nakoteten; kokukonokinos kakonyeneke, kokienatar, kobalas ebe, “Yoga, ijo Ekabaka loka Iyudayan!”" 
Matthew27:30 Kimwaanakis aimul, kodemasi agada ŋin kinomonomiata akouke." 
Matthew27:31 Kosodete kedautu akienar ŋes, kolacasi anapito ŋin, kitanapa ikenapen, koyaŋaasi aibubukin." 
Matthew27:32 Napenyounete kore, kodumut etuŋanan Ekurenayot, ekekiror Simon: kitiŋaikis ŋol airioŋ emusalaba loka Yesu." 
Matthew27:33 Nakedolioto aibois naenyaritai Gologota, apolouke ebe, Aibois naka Abelekek naka Akou," 
Matthew27:34 koinakis aimat ebino loinyalakinitai epiu: kedau akiir, koŋer aimat." 
Matthew27:35 Kedautu aibubukin, kokorokorata akenapito, kailamilam eroet." 
Matthew27:36 Kiboikinos kidarata ŋes kaŋina. 
Matthew27:37 Kikaiakis kuju kakouke nueosatai ŋes nuewadikatai ebe, LO ŊES YESU EKABAKA LOKA IYUDAYAN." 
Matthew27:38 Kapak kaŋin kibubukinoi ikaŋatak iarei nepepe kaŋes, ediopet kakanike nakoteten, ka ediopet da kakanike nakokediany," 
Matthew27:39 Lukitorito nen koinyanakinete ŋes, kimuŋumuŋete da akecekwes," 
Matthew27:40 kobalas ebe, “Ijo lokaketan eyekalu, ka aiduk da kotoma apaarasia auni, kitajarun cani: arai irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke, kodoku komusalaba.”" 
Matthew27:41 Kikote nen da isasedotin lupeti kokienatar ŋes, nepepe ka ikewadikak ka imakio, kobalas ebe," 
Matthew27:42 “Etajar ice; mam epedori aitajarun bon. Erai ŋesi Ekabaka loka Isirael; kodoku kwana komusalaba, kiyuuni do ŋes." 
Matthew27:43 Emunokina Edeke; mere cani kitajar ŋes kwana, arai ekoto ŋes; naarai abu kinera ebe, ‘Arai eoŋ Okoku loka Edeke.’ ”" 
Matthew27:44 Ikaŋatak kwi da lukibubukinitoi nepepe kaŋes, korutonokis ŋes akiro kwapekwa." 
Matthew27:45 Ameun kosawa lokikanyetekape kojau amuton akwap kere kiton osawa Iokikanyetekaoŋon. 
Matthew27:46 Bala esawa Iokikanyetekaoŋon kodelo Yesu keporoto loepol, kobala ebe, “Eli, eli, lama sabakatani?” apolouke ebe, “Ekadeke, Ekadeke, kanukinyo kijalakinia eoŋ?”" 
Matthew27:47 Ice kaŋul kalukebwoete kanen, kiirasi, kobalas ebe, “Enyarit ŋol Eliya.”" 
Matthew27:48 Atipet koker ediopet kakesi, kolem acago, kileleb ebino loedwar ria, kibwaik toma agada, kitamat ŋes," 
Matthew27:49 Kobalas ice ebe, “Kinyek; kaanyutu arai cani ebuni Eliya aitajar ŋes.”" 
Matthew27:50 Kodelo Yesu bobo keporoto loepol, kojal ekemoyo." 
Matthew27:51 Ido koany, kocila aigalisit naka eyekalu kaarei, ameun kokuju kiton kwap; komaran akwap; kobwaŋabwaŋas amor;" 
Matthew27:52 koŋaanaros atesin; kitonyounoi awat nuipu nuka lukalaunak kalukolo keiotooros; 
Matthew27:53 kedau Yesu ajarun kolomut katesin, kolomasi ore lokalaunan, kitakanikinos luipu." 
Matthew27:54 Nakeanyuniata ekapolokiton ka ŋul da lukejaas kaŋes idarete Yesu, amaran naka akwap, ka akiro da nukiswamas, kokuriakaros noi, kobalas ebe, “Abeit kerai teni ŋol Okoku loka Edeke.”" 
Matthew27:55 Kojaas da aŋor nuipu ŋina, nukesesenete kama elwanikina, nuketupito Yesu anyoun koGalilaya, ijaanakinete ŋes;" 
Matthew27:56 kotomakec kejai Mariam Magadalene, ka Mariam toto naka Yakob ka Yosep, ka toto naka odwe luka Sebedayo." 
Matthew27:57 Kosodi napekitiboŋ, kobu ekabaran loka Arimataya, ekekiror Yosep, ŋes da elopet kerai ekesisian loka Yesu." 
Matthew27:58 Kolot ŋol mama ejai Pilato kilip akuan naka Yesu. Kosodi kicorak Pilato ŋes ainakinio. 
Matthew27:59 Kolem Yosep akuan, konunukik toma obaputa Ioelai," 
Matthew27:60 kibwaik toma atesike nakitetet, nakebokit ŋesi atiida; kikokorik amoru naepol agolokinio ekek loka ates, kolot." 
Matthew27:61 Kejaas nen Mariam Magadalene ka Mariam ace, iboiete kotereikina ates," 
Matthew27:62 Apaaran naatupakini, ŋes atemar ebe, akaulo kapaaran naka Aitemonokin, kotukokinos isasedotin lupeti ka Iparisayon mama ejai Pilato," 
Matthew27:63 kobalas ebe, “Ejakait, kiitunit isio ebe abala lem ekeŋalan ŋol naarokor ejari ebe, ‘Akaulo kapaarasia auni ajaruni.’" 
Matthew27:64 Kanuka ŋun kicorak kidarai ates kojokan aitodol apaaran nakiwuniet, kinyeis ikekesisiak alosit akokwar ŋes, kosodete alimonokin ituŋa ebe, ‘Ajaru kotoma okatwak’ itelekari do aiŋal nakokau ya nasodit.”" 
Matthew27:65 Kotema Pilato kes atiar, “Ejaas yes iserikalei lukedarak; koloto, kidarata kojokan kwape ipedoriata.”" 
Matthew27:66 Koloto do kidarata ates kojokan, kipucakis amoru ka aibwaikin da iserikalei lukedarak." 
Matthew28:1 Akaulo kasabato, napecila kide kapaaran nasodit nakasabato, koloto Mariam Magadalene ka Mariam ace aanyun ates." 
Matthew28:2 Ido koany, kejai amaran naka akwap; naarai kodok emalaika loka Ejakait kokuju, kobu kikokoro amoru awai, kiboikin kujuke." 
Matthew28:3 Kotakanu bala eimilia, ikenapen da kiliacanito kiac." 
Matthew28:4 Komaranata ikedarak kanuka akurianar ŋes, kosubata bala lukatwak," 
Matthew28:5 Koboŋok emalaika kotema aŋor atiar, “Sirikikuriakaros yesi; naarai ajeni ebe imootos Yesu lokibubukinitoi." 
Matthew28:6 Emamei kane; naarai ajaru, kwape eneritor. Kopotu koanyut aibois naeperikinitoi." 
Matthew28:7 Koloto yesi da atipet, kolimokis ikekesisiak ebe, ‘Ajaru kotoma okatwak’; ido koany, kiŋarenikini yes alosit Galilaya; ianyikinete ŋes ŋina; koany kadau alimokin yes.”" 
Matthew28:8 Konyout atipet kates kakurian ka aiyalama naepol, kokerata alimokin ikekesisiak." 
Matthew28:9 Ido koany, kiriamakin Yesu kakes, kobala ebe, “Yoga!” Kikunyakis kitiŋata akekejen komaata ŋes," 
Matthew28:10 Kosodi Yesu kotema kes ariar, “Sirikikuriakaros; koloto kolimokis ikainacan koloto Galilaya, ŋina kaanyikinete.”" 
Matthew28:11 Napelosete, koany, kolomasi ice kokedarak ore, kolimokis isasedotin lupeti akiro nukedoikinete," 
Matthew28:12 Kotukokinos nepepe kimakio kinerut, koinakis iserikalei arupiyan nuipu," 
Matthew28:13 kobalas ebe, “Kinerata yesi ebe, ‘Apotu ikekesisiak kopotu kuare, kokokwasi ŋes kiiotoi isio.’" 
Matthew28:14 Arai kiirar akirot na kama ekayaiton, kimaimai isio ŋes, kinyeis yes aiticanio.”" 
Matthew28:15 Kolemasi arupiyan kiswamata kwape kisisianakinitere; kisiarakin akirot na toma oYudayan kiton lolo. 
Matthew28:16 Konye kolot ikesisiak itomon ka lodiopet Galilaya, oroŋat lokicorakinit kes Yesu," 
Matthew28:17 Nakeanyuniata ŋes, komaata; konye kobuonokinos ice kakesi." 
Matthew28:18 Kobu Yesu neejaas kinera kakes, kotema atiar, “Kainakin eoŋ apedor kere kokuju kakwapin da." 
Matthew28:19 Aso kolot kituluosi lukatekerin kere ikesisiak, kibatisaete kes kokiror loka Papa, ka loka Okoku, ka loka Emoyo Lokalaunan;" 
Matthew28:20 kisisianakinete kes aricit akiro kere nukecorakinit yes; ido koany, ajai eoŋ nenipe kayes apaarasia kere, kiton awasia naka ikar kere,”" 
Mark1:1 Ageunet naka Akiro Nukajokak nuka Yesu Kristo, Okoku loka Edeke." 
Mark1:2 Kwape kiwadikatere toma Isaia enabi ebe: “Koany, ejukari ekakiyakia kakonyenekon, Loitemonokini ekonirot;" 
Mark1:3 Eporoto loka yenikiworoi kamodiŋ ebe, ‘Kitemonokis erot loka Ejakait, Kitetenata ikesokono.’ ”" 
Mark1:4 Kotakanu Yokana Lokebatisan elimonokini kamodiŋ aibatisa naka aitoronikin kanuka alemar adiakanareta. 
Mark1:5 Kolosenenete lukakwap kere naka Yudaya ka luko Yerusalem da kere mama ejai; kibatisai kes kocor Yorodan, kolimonorete akecediakanareta." 
Mark1:6 Konapenenei Yokana ajul nuka akaal, ka amuny naka emukule kaŋabeteke, konyamenenei da emaase ka esik loka ais." 
Mark1:7 Kolimonokini, kobala ebe, “Ebunit kokaukaŋ loketelekarit eoŋ kagogoŋ, lomam eoŋ kebusakinit akukum alacun amuny naka amukake." 
Mark1:8 Kebatisat eoŋ yes kakip; konye ŋes kibatisai yes kEmoyo Lokalaunan.” 
Mark1:9 Kosodi kanen kapaarasia kaŋun, kobu Yesu koNasaret loko Galilaya, abu Yokana kibatisa ŋes koYorodan." 
Mark1:10 Atipet napedokuni kakipi, koany akuj ecilil, kodoku Emoyo mamakeŋ kwape ajele." 
Mark1:11 Kobu eporoto kotoma akuj kobala ebe, “Irai ijo Okokuka lominat, Kalelakinit jo noi.”" 
Mark1:12 Atipet kireŋea Emoyo ŋes toma amodiŋ," 
Mark1:13 Kojau toma amodiŋ apaarasia akaisaoŋon, ecoduni Satan ŋes; kojaas nenipe kitiaŋ luka ais, kijaanakinete ŋes imalaikan." 
Mark1:14 Kedau Yokana aikamario, kobu Yesu Galilaya, elimonokini Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke," 
Mark1:15 kobala ebe, “Adol apak, aapu da ajakanut naka Edeke. Kitoronikinos, kiyuut Akiro Nukajokak.”" 
Mark1:16 Nakitoritor ariri kaŋolol naka Galilaya, koany Simon ka Anderea onaceke ecakakinete eboi aŋolol; naarai keraas ikalokak." 
Mark1:17 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Kotupunai, ketuluori yes ikalokak ituŋa,”" 
Mark1:18 Atipet kinyeis iboyanakec, kotupasi ŋes," 
Mark1:19 Kiyatak alosit nediokasilon, koany Yakob okoku loka Sebedayo ka Yokana onaceke, lukejaas toma ataker erucete iboyan." 
Mark1:20 Atipet konyarau kes; kinyekis papakec Sebedayo kataker nenipe kikewoteok, kotupasi ŋes." 
Mark1:21 Kolomasi Kaparanaum; atipet apaaran nakasabato koloma toma atukos kisisianak. 
Mark1:22 Koumokis noi ituŋa akeisisianakin, naarai kisisianakini kwape elopet apolou, kwabo mere kwape ikewadikak." 
Mark1:23 Atipet kojai toma atukosikec etuŋanan lokejai emoyo loerono. Kiworo, kobala ebe," 
Mark1:24 “Anyoika sio ka jo, Yesu loko Nasaret? Ibu kereka amudiar sio? Kajeni jo kwape iraar, Lokalaunan loka Edeke.”" 
Mark1:25 Kiretak Yesu ŋes ebe, “Kobuta, kolom kamakeŋ!”" 
Mark1:26 Kitamaran ŋes emoyo lokaronon, kodelo keporoto loepol, kolom kamakeŋ." 
Mark1:27 Koumokis kere, kiŋitanaros kobalas ebe, “Anyoika bo nu? Itet ca ma aisisianakin na! Naarai icorakini kapedor imoyon lueroko da, erimasi ŋes!”" 
Mark1:28 Atipet kisiarakin ekeemut aiboisio kere anatar atutubeta kere nuirimorito nuko Galilaya. 
Mark1:29 Napekelomuniata katukos, kolomasi togo loka Simon ka Anderea, nepepe ka Yakob ka Yokana." 
Mark1:30 Keperi kanen amuran naka Simon edeka ekamidi, atipet kolimokis Yesu akekiro." 
Mark1:31 Kikunyak kitiŋ akekan, kitonyou ŋes. Atipet koŋaleu ekamidi, kijaanak kes," 
Mark1:32 Nakitiboŋ, keloma akoloŋ, koinut ŋes kere lukedekas ka lukajokin." 
Mark1:33 Kotukokinos lukore kere orute," 
Mark1:34 Kitaŋaleu luipu lukejaas adekesia nuegelegela, kireŋea da ajokin nuipu; mam kecamakinit ajokin einer, naarai kejenete ŋes." 
Mark1:35 Tupuruc sek eriŋa emutono, konyou ŋesi koloma kolot aibois naesil, kilip kaŋina." 
Mark1:36 Kibwapito ŋes Simon ka ikepaup. 
Mark1:37 Nakedumuniata kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kimooto jo ituŋa kere.”" 
Mark1:38 Kotema kes atiar, “Kaloto nenice, oreria lueapiete, tetere alimonokini ŋina da; naarai ŋin abunitor eoŋ.”" 
Mark1:39 Kolot ilokidai Galilaya kere, elimonokini katukosiakec ka aireŋeanar da aiokin." 
Mark1:40 Kobu lokatapon mamake, kiŋaiŋa, kokukokin, kotema atiar, “Arai ikoto, ipedori aiswagar eoŋ.”" 
Mark1:41 Konyunyura, korio akekan, kotiro kotema atiar, “Akoto; kiswagar.”" 
Mark1:42 Atipet koŋaleu atapon, kiswagar." 
Mark1:43 Kisiopak Yesu ŋes, kireŋea atipet," 
Mark1:44 kotema ŋes atiar, “Kocoite sirikilimok idiotuŋanan adiokirot. Konye kolot, kitodiar mama ejai esasedoti, koinak nukolo kicorakinit Musa kanuka aiswagariokon, koraut akajenak kamakec.”" 
Mark1:45 Konye koloma, kogeu alimonokin noi, ka aitisiarakin akirot, komam bobo Yesu epedori alomar ore kaitebeikin, konye kojai kiŋa toma aiboisio nuemameete ituŋa, Kopotu ituŋa mamakeŋ anyoun kaiboisio kere." 
Mark2:1 Akaulo kapaarasia ace, nakelomaria bobo Kaparanaum, kiirarai ebe ejai ore," 
Mark2:2 Kotukokinos ituŋa luipu, komamei adiopak naesalit karaida kokek; kolimonokini kes akirot," 
Mark2:3 Kopotu koinut ŋes etuŋanan lokasenyan ibwokito ituŋa iwoŋon. 
Mark2:4 Namam kepedoriata aikunyakin ŋes kanuka ekodet, koketasi eswi kama kejai; kedaut apukor, kijesut akapet nakiperikinitoi lokasenyan." 
Mark2:5 Nakeanyunia Yesu akeceiyuun, kotema lokasenyan atiar, “Okokuka, esionii akonidiakanareta.”" 
Mark2:6 Ikewadikak ice lukejaas nen iboiete, kopegas kotauonokec ebe," 
Mark2:7 “Kanukinyo inerar ŋol kwaŋin? Einyanakini Edeke. Iŋai bo epedori aisioni adiakanareta, dimarai Edeke bon?”" 
Mark2:8 Atipet kojenu Yesu kotauke ebe epegas kwaŋin kotauonokec, kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo ipegatatar kwaŋin kotauonokus?" 
Mark2:9 Ani bo naepatana, alimokin lokasenyan ebe, ‘Esionii akonidiakanareta,’ arai bo atemar ebe, ‘Konyou, kibwok akonikapet kolot?’" 
Mark2:10 Konye tetere ijenunete ebe ejai Okoku loka etuŋanan apedor kakwap aisioni adiakanareta” kanen kotema lokasenyan atiar," 
Mark2:11 “Katemari jo atiar, konyou, kibwok akonikapet, koboŋo orekon.”" 
Mark2:12 Atipet konyou, kibwok akekapet koloma kakonyenekec kere: koumokis kere, kitopoloosi Edeke, kobalas ebe, “Mam lem kianyununei nuikote nen.”" 
Mark2:13 Konyou bobo kolot ariri kaŋolol. Kolot ekodet kere mama ejai, kisisianak kes." 
Mark2:14 Nakitoritor, koany Lebi okoku loka Alipayo iboie kaitelemis, kotema atiar, “Kotupunai.” Konyou kotupa ŋes." 
Mark2:15 Kosodi kanen, nakiboio enyami koreke, kiboiete iketelemak esolo luipu ka ikadiakanarak da nepepe ka Yesu ka ikekesisiak; naarai araas luipu." 
Mark2:16 Kotuparito da ikewadikak luka Iparisayon, ido nakeanyuniata ŋes emorete kikadiakanarak ka iketelemak esolo, kiŋita ikekesisiak atiar, “Kanukinyo emoriata ŋesi ka iketelemak esolo ka ikadiakanarak?”" 
Mark2:17 Nakiiraria Yesu, kotema kes atiar, “Lukagogoŋok mam ipudas emurwon, dimarai lukadekak. Mam abunit anyarit ikadolitok, dimarai ikadiakanarak.”" 
Mark2:18 Aluŋete ikesisiak luka Yokana ka Iparisayon. Kopotu ituŋa mama ejai Yesu, kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kanukinyo eluŋiata ikesisiak luka Yokana ka ikesisiak luka Iparisayon, konye ikonikesisiak mam eluŋete?”" 
Mark2:19 Koboŋok Yesu kes ebe, “Epedorete biai ipapero luka eteran ailuŋ eriŋa eteran ejai kakes? Apak kere naejaatar keteran, mam epedorete ailuŋ," 
Mark2:20 Konye eponito apaarasia nuedemarere eteran; eluŋete do kapaaran kaŋin," 
Mark2:21 Emamei yenedonyokini atutubet naka egoe lokitetet anapito namojoŋ; arai kikonaki nen, atutubet nakitetet ecili ya namojoŋ, iyatakini acilat." 
Mark2:22 Emamei da yenebukokini ebino loitet oriagin lukemukule lumojoŋ; arai kikonaki nen, ecili ebino iriagin, imadiŋikin ebino ka iriagin da; konye ebukonokinio ebino loitet oriagin lukitetiak.”" 
Mark2:23 Kosodi kanen, nakitoritor amanat apaaran nakasabato, napelosete kogeut ikekesisiak aijeje aluŋuren nuka akima." 
Mark2:24 Kotemasi Iparisayon atiar, “Koany! Kanukinyo iswamaata numam ibus kapaaran nakasabato?”" 
Mark2:25 Kotema kes atiar, “Mam lem isiomito nukiswamai Daudi, nakipudar korieb eteŋei, ŋes ka ikepaup;" 
Mark2:26 kwape kelomaria togo loka Edeke apaarasia nukeraar Abiatar esasedoti lopeti, konyam Imugatin luka Aitodikin, lumam ibus ainyam dimarai isasedotin, koinak ikepaup da?”" 
Mark2:27 Kotema kes atiar, “Asubio Asabato kanuka etuŋanan, kwabo mere etuŋanan kanuka Asabato." 
Mark2:28 Kwaŋin Okoku loka etuŋanan ŋes Ejakait loka Asabato.” 
Mark3:1 Koloma bobo atukos; kejai nen etuŋanan lokewonit akan. 
Mark3:2 Kiteikinitoi ŋes, aanyun arai itaŋaleuni kapaaran nakasabato, tetere iwosaete ŋes." 
Mark3:3 Kotema ŋesi etuŋanan lokejai akan nakewonit atiar, “Kobwo kokidiŋ.”" 
Mark3:4 Kiŋit kes ebe, “Ibus kereka aswam nuejok kapaaran nakasabato, arai bo aswam nueroko, aitajar aijar, arai bo aiar?” Konye kililiŋata," 
Mark3:5 Kosesen kes kanyunyura, kokadak kanuka aninik naka ikecetauon, kolimok etuŋanan ebe, “Korio akonikan.” Korio ŋesi akekan, koŋaleu," 
Mark3:6 Kolomasi Iparisayon, kinerutu atipet kaluKerodian asurokin ŋes, ka epone loemudiariata ŋes." 
Mark3:7 Kosodi kogitar Yesu nepepe kikekesisiak, kolot aŋolol, kotupa ekodet loapol lokebuni koGalilaya; koYudaya da," 
Mark3:8 ko Yerusalem ka Idumea, ka okekwa Yorodan, ka ariino da nuka Turo ka Sidon, ekodet loapol, lokiirarit akiro kere nukiswamat, kobu mamakeŋ." 
Mark3:9 Kolimok ikekesisiak aitemokinit ataker aidaret ŋes, kanuka ekodet, kinyeis aridakin ŋes;" 
Mark3:10 naarai kitaŋaleunit luipu, tape da kere Iukiticanete adekesia ebelaros atiror ŋes," 
Mark3:11 Nakeanyuniata ŋes imoyon lueroko, kibiroros kakonyeneke, kiworoto kobalas ebe, “Irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke.”" 
Mark3:12 Kicorenenei kes jokan kinyeis aitejenun ŋes. 
Mark3:13 Kodoka oroŋat, konyarau lukipuda elopet; kopotu mamakeŋ." 
Mark3:14 Koseu itomon kaluarei ajaenena kaŋes, ido aiyakienen alimonokin;" 
Mark3:15 koiaas da kapedor aireŋear ajokin. 
Mark3:16 Koseu lutomon kaluarei lu: Simon, komaik ekekiror Petero;" 
Mark3:17 ka Yakob okoku loka Sebedayo, ka Yokana onaceke (komaik kes ekiror Boanerege, apolouke ebe, Idwe luka airetun);" 
Mark3:18 ka Anderea, ka Pilipo, ka Batolomayo, ka Matayo, ka Tomas, ka Yakob okoku loka Alupayo, ka Tadayo, ka Simon Ekanaanit" 
Mark3:19 ka Yuda Isikariot, ŋes lokebilakini ebotet. Koboŋo ore." 
Mark3:20 Kotukokin bobo ekodet, komam epedorete ainyam idisinyamat." 
Mark3:21 Nakiirariata lukeŋ, kolomasi aikamun ŋes, naarai kobalas ebe, “Amunaar.”" 
Mark3:22 Kobalas ikewadikak lukijesunos koYerusalem ebe, “Ejai Beelesebul, ido ireŋeari ajokin kanuka ekapolon loka ajokin.”" 
Mark3:23 Konyarau kes kolimok kawaragasia ebe, “Epedori biai Satan aireŋear Satan?" 
Mark3:24 Ajakanut arai etiakatiakaun bon, mam epedori ajakanut ŋin aicasit." 
Mark3:25 Arai da etogo etiakatiakaun bon, mam epedori etogo ŋol aicasit." 
Mark3:26 Aso arai enyoikino Satan bon, etiakatiakaun da, mam epedori aicasit; konye enaŋete nuke nen," 
Mark3:27 Konye emamei loepedori alomar togo loka ekagogoŋon, ka aiŋat ikeboro, arai mam ber eenit ekagogoŋon ŋol; ŋes konyet eŋasia eketogo," 
Mark3:28 “Abeit katemari yes atiar, Isionio adiakanareta kere nuka ituŋa, ka ainyanakineta da kere nueinyanakinete;" 
Mark3:29 konye yeneinyanakini Emoyo Lokalaunan mam isionio cut; konye egwaunete akiro nukadiakar naka ikar kere.” 
Mark3:30 Naarai apotu kobalas ebe, “Ejai emoyo loerono.”" 
Mark3:31 Kopotu do totoke ka ikeinacan; kobwaata kokiŋa, kiyakikis akirot anyaraunia ŋes," 
Mark3:32 Kiboie ekodet elukunit ŋes; kobalas ŋes ebe, “Koany, totokon ka ikoniinacan ejaas kiŋa, kimootos jo.”" 
Mark3:33 Koboŋok kes kotema atiar, “Iŋai bo totoka ka ikainacan?”" 
Mark3:34 Kirere ŋul lueboiete elukunito ŋes, kotema atiar, “Koany, totoka, ka ikainacan!" 
Mark3:35 Naarai ituŋanan kere yeniswamai nuekoto Edeke, ŋin ŋes onaceka, ka inacika, ka totoka da.”" 
Mark4:1 Kogeu bobo aisisianakin kariri kaŋolol. Kotukokin ekodet loapol noi mama ejai, kanuka ŋun kodoka ŋesi ataker kiboikin aŋolol; koiai ekodet kere neeonit kariri kaŋolol." 
Mark4:2 Kisisianak akiro nuipu kotoma awaragasia, kolimok kes kotoma aisisianakinike ebe," 
Mark4:3 “Kiirasi! Koany, abu ekayean koloma aiye." 
Mark4:4 Kosodi kanen napeyei, kodooto ikinyom ice ariri korot, kopotu akweny, konyama." 
Mark4:5 Kodooto ice aŋaŋam, nekikidioko alup; atipet kobwaŋutu, naarai kesedeny alup." 
Mark4:6 Nakecaunia akoloŋ konomo; ido naarai kemameete alias, korinyosi." 
Mark4:7 Kodooto ice okukwa; kolibut ikukwa koridakis, mam apotu koraata araito." 
Mark4:8 Kodooto ice alup nuejok, koraata araito, kopolooros, kiyatakinos; koraata akaisauni, ka akaisakanykape, kiton akwatat da.”" 
Mark4:9 Kotema atiar, “Yenejaas aki nuka akiirar, kiira.”" 
Mark4:10 Kosodi nakejaar bon, apotu ituŋa lukelukunito ŋes ka ikesisiak itomon kaluarei kiŋita ŋes akiro nuka awaragasia." 
Mark4:11 Kotema kes atiar, “Kiinakinitai yes ajenun aiyeiyea naka ajakanut naka Edeke; konye mama ejaas kwi luejaas kiŋa eraas kere awaragasia:" 
Mark4:12 tetere aanyun eanyunete komam emisiikinete; akiirar da iirarete komam ejenunete; kinyeis aibelokin ka aisionio.” 
Mark4:13 Kotema kes atiar, “Mam kereka yes ijenete awaragan na? Aso ijenunete biai awaragasia kere?" 
Mark4:14 Eyei ekayean akirot. 
Mark4:15 Ŋul lukariri kerot kama keyeikinio akirot kes lu; kedaut akiirar, atipet ebuni Satan, elemari akirot nakeyeikinio otauonokec." 
Mark4:16 Ikote nen da lukeyeikinio aŋaŋam, kedaut akiirar akirot, atipet ecamunete kaiyalama." 
Mark4:17 Kwabo emameete alias kotomakec, konye etitiŋikinete nediokasilon; kosodete naeponikiniata aiticaneta ka areio kanuka akirot, atipet iguikinos." 
Mark4:18 Ice kes lukeyeikinio okukwa; kes lukiirarete akirot," 
Mark4:19 kosodi aiyaloŋoŋ naka akwapin, ka aiŋal naka abar, ka eraŋa loka acekiro elomarete, eridakinete akirot, mam erai." 
Mark4:20 Ka ŋul da lukeyeikinio alup nuejok kes lukiirarete akirot, kocamut, koraata araito, akaisauni, ka akaisakanykape kiton akwatat da.”" 
Mark4:21 Kotema kes atiar, “Eyaŋaunio kereka atala aibwaikin obukit, arai bo kwap keitada? Mam kereka ibwaikinio kuju ocoget?" 
Mark4:22 Naarai emamei akirot naibwaitai, dimarai kito aitakanunio; kwabo emamei akirot naimunonitai, dimarai kito aikujunio." 
Mark4:23 Arai ejaas ituŋanan aki nuka akiirar, kiira.”" 
Mark4:24 Kotema kes atiar, “Kocoito nuipupete. Aitemis naitemioto yesi, ŋipeŋin kitemere yes, kiyatakinio da." 
Mark4:25 Naarai yenejai ibore einakinio ice; konye yenemamei ibore, edemunio ŋin da yenejaas kaŋes.”" 
Mark4:26 Kotema atiar, “Ikoni ne ajakanut naka Edeke bala etuŋanan lokeyei ikinyom alup;" 
Mark4:27 kojotoor, ka anyoun, kuare ka paaran; kobwaŋutu ikinyom kopolooros, komam ŋes ejeŋi kwape kikonakinere." 
Mark4:28 Eraete alup kanukec, egeuni akiot, kosodi aluŋuret, kosodi konyet akima nuekokito." 
Mark4:29 Konye kekoko araito, atipet ijukari ecilikiki, naarai adol aidweny.”" 
Mark4:30 Kotema atiar, “Kitupusi kinyo ajakanut naka Edeke, arai ketetemo kawaragan anyoin?" 
Mark4:31 Eputos ka ecokat loka ekaradali, loeyeikinio toma alup, karaida kedit aitelekarit ikinyom kere luka akwapin;" 
Mark4:32 konye nakeyeikin, epoloor, eraun lokapolon aitelekarit idiasio kere, kijany atenieik nuepolok, tape edukete akweny nuka apak akaisikec otolimike.”" 
Mark4:33 Kolimok kes akirot kawaragasia nuipu nuekote nen, kwape kepedoriata akiirar." 
Mark4:34 Kwabo mam abu kolimok kes emamei awaragan: konye kitebeik ikekesisiak akiro kere kaiyeiyea. 
Mark4:35 Kapaaran kaŋin, nakitiboŋ, kotema kes atiar, “Kekwaŋaros okekwa juwai.”" 
Mark4:36 Kinyeis ekodet, koyaŋaasi ŋes nepepe kakes kwape kejaar, kotoma ataker. Koupasi atakerin ace da." 
Mark4:37 Kokut ekwam loededeŋ, Koretonokinos akailan ataker, aitodol neapiatar akipi ailelebun ataker," 
Mark4:38 Konye kejai ŋesi elopet okori kataker, ejotoi kaicolonit. Kitwekenyut ŋes kotemasi atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, mam jo ipodo kimudiari oni?”" 
Mark4:39 Kokweny ŋesi, kiretak ekwam, kolimok aŋolol ebe, “Kililiŋ! Kinapakin!” Kopala ekwam, kojaun aiyamakin naepol." 
Mark4:40 Kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo ikuriakarotor? Eroko ca ma yes iyuuna?”" 
Mark4:41 Kolomak kes aiyoŋ naepol, kotemanaros atiar, “Iŋai bo lo, naarai ekwam ka aŋolol da erimasi ŋes?”" 
Mark5:1 Kodolot okekwa kaŋolol, akwap naka Igerasenin." 
Mark5:2 Nakedokunia kataker, atipet kiriamunos ketuŋanan lokemoyo loerono, lokebuni katesin," 
Mark5:3 Kiboienenei ŋol katesin. Komamei ituŋanan yenepedori aien ŋes bobo, karaida kirikoi;" 
Mark5:4 naarai keenenenoo irwan ipu kiloin ka irikoi, koŋedeŋedei irikoi, kobilibil da aeneta; komamei ituŋanan kere yenikejaas kagogoŋ aitapatan ŋes," 
Mark5:5 Apaarasia kere, apaaran ka akuar, kojaenena atesin ka oroŋan, iworoi, ka atubutubo kamor." 
Mark5:6 Nakeanyunia Yesu kama elwana, koker koma ŋes." 
Mark5:7 Kiworo keporoto loepol, kobala ebe, “Anyoika eoŋ ka jo, Yesu, Okoku loka Edeke Loejai kuju kakuj? Kesiyapoi kalimite Edeke, sirikiitican eoŋ.”" 
Mark5:8 Naarai abu Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Ijo emoyo loirono, kolom kotuŋanan!”" 
Mark5:9 Kiŋit Yesu ŋes ebe, “Ekonikiror iŋai?” Koboŋok ebe, “Ekakiror erai Ajore; naarai kipu isio.”" 
Mark5:10 Kiŋaiŋa noi ebe kinyek aireŋear kakwap kaŋin. 
Mark5:11 Kanen koroŋat kojai esipan loapol loka ipegei edakasi. 
Mark5:12 Kiŋaiŋaata ŋes imoyon ebe, “Kijukarai toma opegei, kalomakisi kes.”" 
Mark5:13 Kocamak kes. Kolomut imoyon lueroko kolomasi toma opegei: komotar esipan kere neijululuei kiton aŋolol, emwaasi bala ilukumin iarei; kotwakikis aŋolol." 
Mark5:14 Kokerata ikecokok, kisiarakis akiro ore, kokialon da. Kolomut ituŋa aanyun nuadoikis." 
Mark5:15 Koloto mama ejai Yesu, koanyut lolem ajaas ajokin iboie, enapit igoen, kejokiar adam, ŋopeŋol lokejai lem ajore ŋin; kokuriakaros." 
Mark5:16 Ŋul da luapotu koanyut kolimokis kes nuadoikis lolem ajaas ajokin, ka nuka ipegei da." 
Mark5:17 Kogeut aiŋaiŋa Yesu anyoun koikorunokec. 
Mark5:18 Nakedokaria ataker, kiŋaiŋa lolem ajaas ajokin aupar kaŋes." 
Mark5:19 Konye koŋer Yesu, kotema ŋes atiar, “Kolot orekon mama ejaas lukobukus, kolimonok akiro nukapolok nuetia nen nukiswamak Ejakait, ido kwape kitimio jo.”" 
Mark5:20 Kolot, kogeu alimonokin kotoma Dekapoli akiro nukapolok nuetia nen nukiswamakinit Yesu ŋes; koumokis ituŋa kere." 
Mark5:21 Nakedaunia Yesu aikwaŋar bobo aboŋor kataker okekwa, kotukokin ekodet loapol mamakeŋ; kojai ŋesi kariri kaŋolol." 
Mark5:22 Kobu ekayaiton ediopet loka atukos, ekekiror Yairo; nakeanyunia Yesu, kibirokin akejeneke," 
Mark5:23 kiŋaiŋa noi, kotema atiar, “Ikapese eapikinit airidakin, keŋaiŋait kobu kidokok ŋes akonikanin, tetere itaŋaleuni ŋes, kojar da.”" 
Mark5:24 Kolot nepepe kaŋes. Kotupa ekodet loapol, koridakis ŋes." 
Mark5:25 Kojai aberu nakedeka alele nakaokot ikar itomon kaluarei; 
Mark5:26 nakiticanitoi noi kakanin nuka imurwok luipu, nakitatacio kere lukejaatar, komam eŋaleuni, konye do kinyikokinite adek." 
Mark5:27 Nakiiraria akiro nuka Yesu, kitor okodet kikuny kokauke, kotiro akenapito." 
Mark5:28 Naarai abu kotema atiar, “Arai katiro anapitoke bon ketaŋaleunio.”" 
Mark5:29 Atipet koonik alele naka akeokot; kojen kakuanake ebe aŋaleu ican ŋul. 
Mark5:30 Atipet kojen Yesu ebe aloma apedor kamake, kibelokin kotoma okodet, kotema atiar, “Iŋai bo atiro anapitoka?”" 
Mark5:31 Kotemasi ikekesisiak atiar, “Iany ekodet kiiridak, ibala ebe, ‘Iŋai bo katiro?’”" 
Mark5:32 Kirere Yesu aanyun iŋai kiswamat ŋin," 
Mark5:33 Konye kokurianar aberu komaran, kojen nukiswamakinio kobu kibirokin akonyeneke, kolimok abeit kere." 
Mark5:34 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Akokuka, kitaŋaleu jo akonikiyuun; kolot inapakina, koŋaleu icanikon.”" 
Mark5:35 Napinera ŋun, kopotu lukepote kore loka ekayaiton loka atukos, kobalas ebe, “Atwana akokukon, Kanukinyo itaaria bobo Ekesisianakinan?”" 
Mark5:36 Konye nakiiraria Yesu akirot ŋin nainerai, kolimok ekayaiton loka atukos ebe, “Sirikikurianar, kiyuu aiyuun.”" 
Mark5:37 Mam abu kisunup icetuŋanan atupar ŋes dimarai Petero ka Yakob ka Yokana onaceke. 
Mark5:38 Kodoloto togo loka ekayaiton loka atukos, koany ecelet, ka ituŋa emonyete kibwololoete noi." 
Mark5:39 Nakelomaria, kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo icelatar komonyete? Mam ikoku etwanit, konye ejotoi.”" 
Mark5:40 Kokienatar ŋes. Konye nakedaunia aireŋear kes kere kiŋa, koyaŋa papa loka ikoku ka totoke, ka ŋul da lukejaas kaŋes, koloma nekejai ikoku." 
Mark5:41 Kitiŋ akan naka ikoku kotema atiar, “Talita kumai”; apolouke ebe, “Ipese katemari jo atiar, konyou.”" 
Mark5:42 Atipet konyou ipese kosakasak; naarai kerai yenika ikar itomon kaluarei. Atipet koumokis kaumokin naepol. 
Mark5:43 Kicor jokan kinye ituŋanan ajenun akiro ŋun, kicorak kes ainakin ŋes inyamat." 
Mark6:1 Konyou kanen kobu akwapukec. Kotupasi ikekesisiak. 
Mark6:2 Apaaran nakasabato kogeu aisisianakin kotoma atukos. Nakiirariata luipu koumokis, kotemasi atiar, “Kedumuni lo ŋun kai? Anyoin acoa naeinakinitai ŋes? Anyoika nukapedor nuetia nen nuiswamai kakaninike?" 
Mark6:3 Mere lo ekekeon, okoku loka Mariam, onace loka Yakob ka Yose ka Yuda ka Simon, akeinacan da emameete kane kamawok?” Kiguikis kanukeŋ." 
Mark6:4 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Enabi mam emwaŋio dimarai akwapuke, kaneejaas ipajenake, ka lukotogoke.”" 
Mark6:5 Mam abu kopedo aswam nakapedor adio da kaŋina, dimarai aidokokin lukadekak idis akekanin kitaŋaleu kes." 
Mark6:6 Koumok kanuka amamus aiyuunikec. Kimaniman ireria kere isisianakini. 
Mark6:7 Konyarau lutomon kaarei, kogeu aiyakiar kes iareiarei. Koinak kes apedor kama kimoyon kalueroko;" 
Mark6:8 kicorak kes kinyeis ayaŋaar idiobore yenikerot, dimarai ebela bon; mam karaida inyamat, karaida ecoe, karaida apesan kamunyinikec;" 
Mark6:9 konye konapito amuk; ido sirinapenenete ikason iarei. 
Mark6:10 Kotema kes atiar, “Ŋolitogo loilomanarete, kosalenenete nen aitodol nainyounioto kore kaŋol." 
Mark6:11 Kaŋiniibois kere namam kisukunyikinere yes, karaida akiirar, nainyounioto kanen, kilakilakenenete adae nuejaas akejenekus araut akajenak kamakec.”" 
Mark6:12 Koloto kesi kolimonokis ituŋa aitoronikin. 
Mark6:13 Kireŋeanasi ajokin nuipu, kinyonyoanakis lukadekak luipu akinyet, kitaŋaleut." 
Mark6:14 Kopup ekabaka Kerode ŋun; naarai aruo ekiror loka Yesu. Abakai ebe, “Ajaru Yokana Lokebatisan kotoma okatwak, kanuka ŋun iswamaete nukapedor kotomakeŋ.”" 
Mark6:15 Konye kobalas ice ebe, “Erai Eliya.” Ice da ebe, “Erai enabi, kwape ediopet kotoma onabin.”" 
Mark6:16 Konye nakiiraria Kerode, kotema atiar, “Yokana, lokajepari eoŋ akekou, ajaru ŋol.”" 
Mark6:17 Naarai abu Kerode elopet kijuka kikam Yokana, koenik aidaris kanuka Kerodia, aberu naka Pilipo onaceke; naarai amanyit ŋes," 
Mark6:18 kosodi Yokana alimokin Kerode ebe, “Mam ibus jo ajaut kaberu naka onacekon.”" 
Mark6:19 Kwaŋin kolil Kerodia, kokoto aiar ŋes; mam epedoro;" 
Mark6:20 naarai keyoŋit Kerode Yokana, kojen ebe erai etuŋanan loedolit, lokalaunan, koricite ŋes. Nakiiraria kobuonokin noi; kiiranari ŋes kaiyalama." 
Mark6:21 Kosodi kodolok apak naajok nakipoikinio Kerode ijakake, ka ikapolokitok lukapolok, ka ituŋa lukapolok luko Galilaya epucit kanuka apaaran naka aurioke," 
Mark6:22 Kanen kolom akoku naka Kerodia kikosi, kisiyalamik Kerode ka lukejaas kaŋes opucit. Kolimok ekabaka apese ebe, “Kilipai eoŋ ibore kere yenikoto, kainakini jo.”" 
Mark6:23 Kiyapoik ŋes ebe, “Ŋinibore kere yenilipi, kainakini jo, kiton atutubet naka ajakanutuka.”" 
Mark6:24 Koloma ŋin kiŋit totoke ebe, “Elipi inyo?” Kotema atiar, “Akou naka Yokana Lokebatisan.”" 
Mark6:25 Atipet kisunya alomun mama ejai ekabaka, kilip ebe, “Akoto koinak kwape kwana akou naka Yokana Lokebatisan katuba.”" 
Mark6:26 Kokadak ekabaka noi; konye kanuka akeiyapo, kanuka ŋul da lukejaas opucit, mam abu kokoto aimik ŋes." 
Mark6:27 Atipet kiyakia ekabaka eserikalet, kicorak ayaun akouke. Kolot koiepu akouke kaidaris." 
Mark6:28 Koyau akouke katuba, koinak apese; apese da koinak totoke." 
Mark6:29 Nakiirariata ikekesisiak akiro, koloto koyaŋaasi akekuan, kidaikis ates." 
Mark6:30 Kotukonokinos ikiyakia mama ejai Yesu; kolimokis ŋes akiro kere nueswamata ka nuesisianakis. 
Mark6:31 Kotema kes atiar, “Kogitunos yesi bonik aibois naesil, kibworasi nediokasilon.” Naarai kejaas ituŋa luipu eponenenete koboŋonorete, komam adiopak da naka ainyam." 
Mark6:32 Koloto toma ataker kogitaros aibois naesil. 
Mark6:33 Koanyutu ituŋa kes elosete, kojenata luipu, kokerata ŋina kakejen anyoun koreria kere, koliŋakis adolore." 
Mark6:34 Nakedokunia kataker koany ekodet loapol, kitim kes, naarai kesubito bala amerekekin nuemamei ekecokon: kogeu aisisianakin kes akiro nuipu." 
Mark6:35 Ketubor akwap, kopotu ikekesisiak mamakeŋ, kotemasi atiar, “Aibois na erai amodiŋ, atubor da akwap," 
Mark6:36 Kotwar kes, tetere elosete amanat koreria da luirimorito, kogwelata lunyaman.”" 
Mark6:37 Konye Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Koinakis yesi kes lunyaman.” Kotemasi atiar, “Kilosi ca kagwelata imugatin luka adenarin akwat aarei tetere kiinakini kes konyama?”" 
Mark6:38 Kotema kes atiar, “Ejaas yes imugatin imwaasi ai? Koloto koanyut.” Nakedauniata ajenun kotemasi atiar, “Ikany ka agaria aarei.”" 
Mark6:39 Kicorak aisiboikin ituŋa kere katukon toma anya numel. 
Mark6:40 Kiboikinos katukon, ice akwatat ka ice akaisakany." 
Mark6:41 Kolem imugatin lukany ka agaria aarei, kosesen akuj, kisirereŋ, kobilibil imugatin; koinak ikekesisiak akorokor. Kokoranak agaria aarei mamakec kere." 
Mark6:42 Konyamata kere kimonikinos. 
Mark6:43 Kotukonokinai atutubeta nuabilibila nuelelebete idita itomon kaluarei, ka atutubeta nuka agaria da." 
Mark6:44 Lukenyamete emwaasi ikiliok ilukumin ikany. 
Mark6:44 Lukenyamete emwaasi ikiliok ilukumin ikany. 
Mark6:45 Atipet kitiŋaik ikekesisiak adokar ataker, aiŋarenikin ŋes adokar okekwa Betesaida, apak naatwaria ŋesi ekodet." 
Mark6:46 Kedau aitwar kes, kolot oroŋat ailip." 
Mark6:47 Kimukok, kojai ataker kidiŋ aŋolol, kojai ŋesi da bon oitela." 
Mark6:48 Koany kes itaaritos aikwaŋ, naarai kemeunit ekwam koiŋaren, kedol akwenyunet nakiwoŋonet naka akuar, kobu mama ejaas kicakacakai aŋolol; kokoto adepar kes," 
Mark6:49 Konye nakeanyuniata ŋes icakacakai aŋolol, keomitos ebe erai etoil, kilalaata:" 
Mark6:50 naarai apotu kere koanyut, kokuriakaros. Atipet kinera kakes, kotema atiar, “Kotitiŋioros! Eoŋ lo. Sirikikuriakaros.”" 
Mark6:51 Kodoka ataker nekejaas kesi; kiyamakin ekwam. Koumokis noi kotauonokec; 
Mark6:52 naarai mam apotu kojenutu nuka imugatin, konye keninik ikecetauon." 
Mark6:53 Nakedauniata aikwaŋar, kodolo akwap naka Genesaret, koenata ataker oitolima." 
Mark6:54 Nakedokuniata, atipet kojenut ituŋa ŋes." 
Mark6:55 Kokerata kirimosi akwap ŋin kere, kogeut ayaŋanar lukadekak kakapekec, alosit ŋiniibois nakepupunete ebe ejai ŋesi," 
Mark6:56 Ido kama kelomanari kere, oreria, ka oreria da lukapolok, arai amanat, kiperionokis lukadekak agwelanareta, kiŋaiŋaata atiror atwele naka anapitoke. Luketironorete kere kitaŋaleunoi." 
Mark6:56 Ido kama kelomanari kere, oreria, ka oreria da lukapolok, arai amanat, kiperionokis lukadekak agwelanareta, kiŋaiŋaata atiror atwele naka anapitoke. Luketironorete kere kitaŋaleunoi." 
Mark7:1 Kotukokinos Iparisayon ka ice kokewadikak lukepote ko Yerusalem mamakeŋ," 
Mark7:2 koanyutu ice kokesisiakake enyamete inyamat kakanin numam elaete, ŋes atemar ebe numam ilotaritai." 
Mark7:3 (Naarai mam Iparisayon ka Iyudayan kere enyamete dimikito ilosito noi akecekanin, kiketakina kopone loka imakio." 
Mark7:4 Bobo da keboŋut kagwelanaret, arai mam itesegaaros, mam enyamete: ejaas da akiro ace nuipu, nukeinakinitai kes aiketakinit, kwape aitesegar akolin, ka amoti, ka iboro da luka aisinin.)" 
Mark7:5 Kiŋita Iparisayon ka ikewadikak ŋes ebe, “Kanukinyo emam ikonikesisiak elosioto kwape ejaar epone loka imakio, konye enyamete inyamat kakanin numam elaete?”" 
Mark7:6 Kotema kes atiar, “Abu Isaia kodwar kojokan akirokus yes lukesoswai, kwape kiwadikatere ebe, ‘Ketopoloorito ituŋa lu kaitukekec, Konye elwaka ikecetauon kamakaŋ," 
Mark7:7 Konye kamaete eoŋ atitai, Isisianakinete aicorakineta nuka ituŋa bala aisisianakinikec.’" 
Mark7:8 Inyeinete yesi aicorakinet naka Edeke, iketakina koinono loka ituŋa.”" 
Mark7:9 Kotema kes atiar, “Iŋerete jokan aicorakinet naka Edeke, tetere iricito einonokus." 
Mark7:10 Naarai abala Musa ebe, ‘Koyoŋitenene papakon ka totokon’; ido ebe, ‘Yenemoromoroi papa arai toto, koarai’." 
Mark7:11 Konye yes ibalas ebe, ‘Arai ketema ituŋanan papake arai totoke atiar, Nutikainak jo aiŋarakinia erai Koroban’, ŋes atemar ebe Einakinitai Edeke;" 
Mark7:12 mam bobo icamakinete ŋes aswam imodiobore kere kanuka papake arai totoke. 
Mark7:13 Itapalaunete akirot naka Edeke kanuka einonokus loikopete: ido iswamaete akiro nuipu nuikote nen.” 
Mark7:14 Konyarau bobo ekodet kere kotema atiar, “Kiirasi yesi kere, kojenutu da." 
Mark7:15 Emamei ibore yenejai kiŋa ketuŋanan, keloma tomakeŋ yenepedori amunaar ŋes, Konye nuelomunete kotoma otuŋanan kes ŋun nuemunaarete ŋes. [" 
Mark7:16 Yenejaas aki nuka akiirar, kiira.]”" 
Mark7:17 Nakelomaria togo kinyek ekodet, kiŋita ikekesisiak akiro nuka awaragan ŋin." 
Mark7:18 Kotema kes atiar, “Kiton yes da emamei ajenun? Mam ijenete ebe, ŋinibore yenejai kiŋa ketuŋanan, keloma tomakeŋ, mam epedori amunaar ŋes?" 
Mark7:19 Naarai mam elomari otau dimarai akoik bon, kanen ikiŋaario.” Kanuka ener kwaŋin, abu kitalau inyamat kere." 
Mark7:20 Kotema atiar, “Nuelomunete kotuŋanan, kes emunaunete ituŋanan." 
Mark7:21 Naarai toma otauon luka ituŋa elomunete aomisio nukaronok; adoteu, akokolanut, earit, aelonut," 
Mark7:22 airaŋaanut, ameŋeranut, aiŋal, abenyanut, akoŋu naerono, asabanakin, aiwoŋonut, abaŋaanut:" 
Mark7:23 elomunete akiro nu kere nueroko kotoma, kes da emunaarete ituŋanan,”" 
Mark7:24 Konyou kanen, kolot oikorun luka Turo ka Sidon. Koloma togo, komam ekot ituŋanan ajenun: konye mam abu kopedo aiŋop," 
Mark7:25 Konye atipet kobu aberu, nakejai ikepese emoyo loerono, naabu kiira akiroke, kibirokin akejeke." 
Mark7:26 Kerai aberu ŋin da Ayonanit, aketeker Suropoenike, kiŋaiŋa ŋes aireŋear ajokit kama kikepese," 
Mark7:27 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Kinyek ber idwe kimonikinos: naarai mam ejok alemun inyamat luka idwe acakakin iŋokwo.”" 
Mark7:28 Konye Koboŋok kotema atiar, “Eebo, Ejakait: konye iŋokwo da luejaas kwap kemesa enyamete ararasia nuka idwe.”" 
Mark7:29 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Kanuka akirot kaŋin kolot; anyou ajokit kapesekon.”" 
Mark7:30 Kolot aberu orekec, kodum ikoku iperikinitoi oitada kedau ajokit anyoun." 
Mark7:31 Konyou Yesu bobo katutubeta nuka Turo, kitor kidiŋ Sidon kolot kiton aŋolol naka Galilaya, itorit atutubeta nuka Dekapoli." 
Mark7:32 Koinunai ekimiŋ loiŋejiŋeja; kiŋaiŋaata ŋes aidokokin akekan," 
Mark7:33 Kogita ŋes bon awai kama ejai ekodet, kibwaik ikebokor akike, kimuik aimul kotiro akeŋajep;" 
Mark7:34 kosesen akuj, kiyeŋak, kotema ŋes atiar, “Epata,” apolouke ebe, “Kopukor.”" 
Mark7:35 Kopukoros akike, kolacar aŋajepeke, kiner kotenan." 
Mark7:36 Kikwenya kes sirikelimokis idiotuŋanan; konye kwape kiyatanakinia aikwenyar, kwape kwaŋin eyatanakiniata aitisiarikin akiro." 
Mark7:37 Koumokis noi adepar, kobalas ebe, “Eswama akiro kere ejok, Isipedori ikimiŋiok akiirar, ka lumam ineras da einer.”" 
Mark8:1 Kapaarasia kaŋun, nakejaar bobo atukot naapol, kemameete kes inyamat, konyarau ikesisiak, kolimok kes ebe," 
Mark8:2 “Etim ekodet, naarai adaut apaarasia auni iboiete keoŋ, kwabo emameete kes inyamat," 
Mark8:3 Arai katwara kes alosit oreriakec eriebi eteŋei, iiloros korot; ice kakesi eponito kama elwana.”" 
Mark8:4 Koboŋokis ikekesisiak ebe, “Okwe, epedori biai ituŋanan aisimonikin ituŋa lu kimugatin kane kamodiŋ?”" 
Mark8:5 Kiŋit kes ebe, “Ejaas yes imugatin imwaasi ai?” Kobalas ebe, “Ikanykaarei.”" 
Mark8:6 Kicorak ekodet aiboikin kwap; kolem imugatin lukanykaarei, kimala, kobilibil, koinak ikekesisiak akoranakin, kokoranakis kesi da ekodet." 
Mark8:7 Kejaas da agaria nuikidioko. Kisirereŋ kes, kolimok kokoranakis ŋun da." 
Mark8:8 Konyama, kimonikinos; kotukonokis atutubeta nuabilibila nukesalete, ibukito ikanykaarei." 
Mark8:9 Keraas ituŋa bala ilukumin iwoŋon. Kotwar kes. 
Mark8:10 Atipet kodoka ataker nepepe kikekesisiak, kolot atutubeta nuka Dalamanuta." 
Mark8:11 Kopotu Iparisayon mamakeŋ, kogeutu epeget kaŋes. Kokotos aanyunet naebuni kokuju, kokodokodata ŋes." 
Mark8:12 Koom etau, kokadak komoyokeŋ, kotema atiar, “Kanukinyo emootor atur na aanyunet? Abeit katemari yes atiar, Mam cut atur na einakinio aanyunet.”" 
Mark8:13 Kinye kes kodoka bobo ataker, kolot okekwa juwai." 
Mark8:14 Kimurwokis kes ayaŋaar imugatin; dimarai kejai emugati ediopet bon kakes toma ataker," 
Mark8:15 Kicor kes kobala ebe, “Kokwenya, kocoito aitubuunet naka Iparisayon, ka aitubuunet da naka Kerode.”" 
Mark8:16 Kiŋitanakinos bonik naarai amameete imugatin. 
Mark8:17 Konye kojen Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo iŋitanakinotor, naarai emameete yes imugatin? Eriŋa ber emisiikina, karaida ajenun? Eninik ca ma ikusitauon?" 
Mark8:18 Ijaas kakonyen, mam ca ianyunete; ijaas kaki da, mam ca ipupunete? Mam kereka iitunito?" 
Mark8:19 Naabilibilia imugatin ikany kanuka ituŋa ilukumin ikany, ipotu kotukonokis iditai imwaasi ai lueleleba atutubeta nuabilibila?” Kolimokis ŋes ebe, “Itomon kaluarei.”" 
Mark8:20 Ebe da, “Ka lukanykaarei kanuka ilukumin iwoŋon, ipotu kotukonokis ibukito imwaasi ai lueleleba atutubeta nuabilibila?” Kolimokis ŋes ebe, “Ikanykaarei.”" 
Mark8:21 Kotema kes atiar, “Eriŋa ca yes ejenuna?”" 
Mark8:22 Kodoloto Betesaida. Koinunai emuduki, kiŋaiŋaata atiror ŋes." 
Mark8:23 Kitiŋ akan naka emuduki, kitoloma kiŋa naka ere; kosodi kedau aimuikin akonyeke, ka aidokokin akekanin, kiŋit ŋes ebe, “Ianyuni ibore?”" 
Mark8:24 Kosesen kuju kotema atiar, “Aanyuni ituŋa; konye esubito bala ikito elosete.”" 
Mark8:25 Kanen kidokok bobo akekanin akonyeke; kosesen kotenan, koŋaleu, koany iboro kere ejok." 
Mark8:26 Kotwar ŋes alosit oreke, kobala ebe, “Sirikiloma ber ore lo.”" 
Mark8:27 Konyou Yesu nepepe kikekesisiak, koloto oreria luka Kaisarea Pilipi, Korot kiŋit ikekesisiak kotema atiar, “Ebalas ituŋa ebe arai eoŋ iŋai?”" 
Mark8:28 Kolimokis ŋes ebe, “Yokana Lokebatisan; ice ebe ‘Eliya’; ka ice da ebe, ‘Ediopet konabin.’ ”" 
Mark8:29 Kiŋit kes ebe, “Ido bo yes kibalas ebe arai eoŋ iŋai?” Koboŋok Petero kotema atiar, “Irai ijo Kristo.”" 
Mark8:30 Kicor kes kinyeis alimokin idiotuŋanan akiroke. 
Mark8:31 Kogeu aisisianakin kes ebe, ibusakinit Okoku loka etuŋanan aiticanio nuipu, egirete da imakio ka isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak, ka aiar, kapaaran da nakiwuniet ejaruni," 
Mark8:32 Kinera ŋun aitebeunun. Koyaŋa Petero ŋes, kogeu aitoron," 
Mark8:33 Konye kibelokin kosesen ikekesisiak, kitoron Petero, kotema atiar, “Koboŋo kaukaŋ, Satan; naarai mam iwomit aomisio nuka Edeke konye nuka ituŋa.”" 
Mark8:34 Konyarau ekodet nepepe kikekesisiak, kotema kes atiar, “Arai ekoto ituŋanan aitup eoŋ, koŋerokin ilopet, korioŋ ekemusalaba, katup eoŋ." 
Mark8:35 Naarai ŋin yenekoto aitajar akeijar etwaniari; konye ŋin yenetwaniari akeijar kanukaŋ, kanuka akiro nukajokak da, itajari ŋes." 
Mark8:36 Naarai ajokis anyoin arai kedumu ituŋanan akwapin kere, kitwatania akeijar?" 
Mark8:37 Naarai etacakini ituŋanan inyo alakunia akeijar? 
Mark8:38 Naarai yenirumete ileic kanukaŋ kanuka akakiro da kotoma atur na naadote nakadiakanaran, irumete ileic Okoku loka etuŋanan da kanukeŋ, naebunio rwaru kaibuses naka Papake nepepe kimalaikan lukalaunak.”" 
Mark9:1 Kotema kes atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, ejaas ituŋa kaŋul kaluebwoete kane lumam iirete cut atwanare, aitodol neaanyuniata ajakanut naka Edeke abu kapedor.”" 
Mark9:2 Akaulo naka apaarasia akanykape koyaŋa Yesu Petero ka Yakob ka Yokana, kogitaros bonik, kitodoka ŋesi kes oroŋat loeoja; kituluor kakonyenekec," 
Mark9:3 kimilias ikenapen, kokwanut kiac, kopone lomam epedori ekelotan loka akwap aitwakaŋuunia." 
Mark9:4 Kitakanikinos Eliya ka Musa, inerasi ka Yesu." 
Mark9:5 Koboŋok Petero kotema Yesu atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, ejok oni ajaut ne; ikoto keswamata iswamin iuni, ediopet lokon, ediopet loka Musa, ka ediopet da loka Eliya.”" 
Mark9:6 Naarai mam kejeni nukinera, naarai apotu kokuriakata noi." 
Mark9:7 Kobu edou kiteribo kes, kolom epororo kotoma odou ebe, “Lo ŋes Okokuka lominat; kiirasi ŋes.”" 
Mark9:8 Atipet koŋoleŋoleoto, mam bobo eanyuna idiotuŋanan nepepe kakes dimarai Yesu bon." 
Mark9:9 Napedokunete koroŋat, kicor kes kinyeis alimokin idiotuŋanan kere nuaanyut, aitodol naejarunia Okoku loka etuŋanan kotoma okatwak," 
Mark9:10 Koricito akirot, kiŋitanaros bonik ebe ajarun kotoma okatwak ikoni bo ai?" 
Mark9:11 Kiŋita ŋes, kotemasi atiar, “Kanukinyo ineratar ikewadikak ebe ibusakinit ber Eliya aige abunore?”" 
Mark9:12 Kotema kes atiar, “Abeit ebunit ber Eliya aiteteun akiro kere; ido iwadikatai bo biai nuka Okoku loka etuŋanan, ebe iticanio nuipu ka amwaŋio da?" 
Mark9:13 Konye katemari yes atiar, Adau Eliya abunore, kiswamakis ŋes kere nuakotos, kwape Iwadikatere nukeŋ.”" 
Mark9:14 Nakedolioto mama ejaas ikesisiak, koanyut ekodet loapol elukunit, ka ikewadikak lukepegas kakes." 
Mark9:15 Atipet nakeanyuniata ŋes lukokodet kere, koumokis noi, kokerata mama ejai kiyogata ŋes." 
Mark9:16 Kiŋit kes ebe, “Nunyoika nuipegas kakes?”" 
Mark9:17 Koboŋok ediopet kotoma okodet ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, ayaŋaunit ikakoku mamakon, ejai ajokit naabaŋ;" 
Mark9:18 ido naikamunia kere, ibirokini kwap: ekui ekuetete, iriamanakin ikel, idekererar; elip ikonikesisiak aireŋear ŋes; mam epedoro.”" 
Mark9:19 Koboŋok kes kotema atiar, “Wu okwe yes atur namam iyuunit, etodoli eoŋ ai ajaut kayes? Etodoli ai da atitiŋikinit yes? Koinunai.”" 
Mark9:20 Koyaut ŋes mamakeŋ; atipet nakeanyunia kisiilio ajokit; kibirokin kwap, kibelibel koku ekuetete." 
Mark9:21 Kiŋit Yesu papake ebe, “Apak anyoin adau ŋesi ikoni nen?” Kotema atiar, “Ameuni keiditeu." 
Mark9:22 Ecakanakini irwanipu toma akim, toma akipi da, tetere emudiari: konye arai ipedori akirot kere, kitimoi sio, kiŋarak.”" 
Mark9:23 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Arai ipedori! Epedorio kere kama ejai yeniyuunit.”" 
Mark9:24 Atipet kiworo papa loka ikoku kotema atiar, “Eyuunit; kiŋarak amamus aiyuunika.”" 
Mark9:25 Nakeanyunia Yesu ebe akeru ekodet mama ejai, kiretak ajokit naerono, kotema atiar, “Ijo ajokit naabaŋ naakimiŋ, kecorakinit jo ebe kolom kaneejai ŋesi, ido sirikiboŋok bobo.”" 
Mark9:26 Komony, kitamaran jokan, kolom do: kosubite ikoku bala atwana; kotemasi luipu ebe, “Atwana.”" 
Mark9:27 Konye Yesu kitiŋ akekan, kitonyou ŋes; kobwo do." 
Mark9:28 Nakelomaria togo, kiŋita ŋes ikekesisiak kaiyeiyea ebe, “Kanukinyo mam sio kipedoria aireŋear ŋes?”" 
Mark9:29 Kotema kes atiar, “Mam epedori epone lo aireŋeario kanuka akirot kere dimarai kanuka ailip bon.”" 
Mark9:30 Konyoutu kanen kitoroto Galilaya: komam ŋes ekoto ituŋanan ajenun. 
Mark9:31 Naarai kisisianak ikekesisiak, kotema kes atiar, “Elosi Okoku loka etuŋanan ainakinio akanin nuka ituŋa, kes da earete ŋes; kedau aario, akaulo kapaarasia auni ejaruni.”" 
Mark9:32 Konye mam kes apotu kojenut akirot ŋin, koyoŋata aiŋit ŋes." 
Mark9:33 Kodoloto Kaparanaum: nakejaar togo kiŋit kes ebe, “Nuunyoika nan ipegas korot?”" 
Mark9:34 Konye kililiŋata: naarai kepegas bonik ka bonik korot ebe iŋai bo lokapolon. 
Mark9:35 Kiboikin, konyarau lutomon kaluarei kotema kes atiar, “Arai ekoto ituŋanan araun yenisodit, koraun yenikawasia adepar kere, ido ikejaanakinan yenika luce kere.”" 
Mark9:36 Kolem ikoku, kisibwo kokidiŋikec: kotun ŋes, kotema atiar," 
Mark9:37 “Ŋin yenisukunyikini idiopet kodwe kwaka yen kokirorika, kesukunyikinit eoŋ; ŋin da yenikesukunyikini eoŋ, mam kesukunyikinit eoŋ, dimarai je lokejukuni.”" 
Mark9:38 Kotema Yokana ŋes atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kipou kaanyutu etuŋanan ireŋeari ajokin kokirorikon lomam kiupa kaoni: kesimika ŋes, naarai mam kiupa kaoni.”" 
Mark9:39 Konye kotema Yesu atiar, “Sirikisimika: naarai emamei ituŋanan yeniswamai nakapedor kokirorika, yenepedori atipet amoromor eoŋ." 
Mark9:40 Naarai yenimam kitusurupit oni, erai yenikowaiwok," 
Mark9:41 Naarai ŋin yenikitamasi yes akoli naka akipi, naarai kimaikinitai luka Kristo, abeit katemari yes atiar, Mam cut etwaniari ainak ineteke." 
Mark9:42 “Ido yenidupori idiopet ka ludidik kalu kalukeyuunito, tiejok aenikin akukuse naepol omurisiŋike, ka acakakin aŋolol," 
Mark9:43 Arai kidupori jo akonikan, kojepa; ejok jo alomar aijar koŋwalite itia ajaut kak anin aarei alosit ogeena, neejai akim namam eduŋei. [" 
Mark9:44 Nemam etwania ekurutukec, karaida akim mam eduŋei.]" 
Mark9:45 Arai kidupori jo akonikeju, kojepa; ejok jo alomar aijar icedo, itia ajaut kakeje aarei acakakinio ogeena. [" 
Mark9:46 Nemam etwania ekurutukec, karaida akim mam eduŋei.]" 
Mark9:47 Arai kidupori jo akonikoŋu, kogoro: ejok jo alomar ajakanut naka Edeke idoponyony, itia ajaut kakonyen aarei acakakinio ogeena;" 
Mark9:48 nemam etwania ekurutukec, karaida akim mam eduŋei." 
Mark9:49 Naarai ibwaikinio ŋinituŋanan akim kwape ibwaikinere abalaŋ," 
Mark9:50 Ejok abalaŋ; konye arai kepianiar, itemokinio kinyo? Kojaas kabalaŋ tomakus, kojaas kainapakin bonik ka bonik.”" 
Mark10:1 Konyou kaŋina, kolot oikorun luko Yudaya okekwa Yorodan: kotukokinos bobo ikodeta mamakeŋ; kisisianak kes bobo kwape atapitor." 
Mark10:2 Kopotu Iparisayon mamakeŋ, kiŋita ŋes ebe, “Ibus kereka etuŋanan aitwar akeberu?” Kokodut ŋes." 
Mark10:3 Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Anyoika kicorakinit Musa?”" 
Mark10:4 Kotemasi atiar, “Abu Musa kocam aiwadik ebalua loka alacakin, ka aitwar.”" 
Mark10:5 Konye kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Kanuka aninik naka ikusitauon abu ŋesi kiwadik aicorakinet ŋin kanukus." 
Mark10:6 Konye ameun kageunet naka asubunio, ‘Abu kosub yenikiliokit ka yeniberu.’" 
Mark10:7 Kanuka akirot kaŋin ŋes inyeinia etuŋanan papake ka totoke, kirotakinos kakeberu;" 
Mark10:8 eraunete ŋul luarei adiopetekuan: mam bobo eraas iarei dimarai adiopetekuan. 
Mark10:9 Kwaŋin luadau Edeke airotakin, kinyek ituŋanan aitiak.”" 
Mark10:10 Kiŋita bobo ikekesisiak akirot ŋin naajaar togo. 
Mark10:11 Kotema kes atiar, “Ŋolituŋanan loetwari akeberu komany ace, adotear, adiaka kama ejai aberuke." 
Mark10:12 Ŋin da arai inyeini okilenike, kodukok ece, adotear.”" 
Mark10:13 Koinunai idwe ludidik da tetere etirori kes; kitorona ikekesisiak ŋul lukeyaunete kes. 
Mark10:14 Konye nakeanyunia Yesu kokadak noi, kotema kes atiar, “Kocamutu idwe ludidik abunore mama ajai, sirikisimika kes; naarai lueputos kalu ajakanut naka Edeke erai nakee." 
Mark10:15 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Ŋin yenimam iyuuni ajakanut naka Edeke kwape ikoku yenididi, mam cut elomari toma.”" 
Mark10:16 Kotun kes, kidokok akekanin, kisirereŋ da." 
Mark10:17 Napenyouni ŋesi alosit orot, kokeru etuŋanan; kokukokin ŋes, kiŋit ebe, “Ekesisianakinan lokajokan, keswama anyoika tetere erumi aijar naka ikar kere?”" 
Mark10:18 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kanukinyo kinyaraaa eoŋ lokajokan? Emamei yenikajokan dimarai ediopet, ŋes Edeke." 
Mark10:19 Ijeni aicorakineta ebe, Siriari, Siridote, Sirikokoi, Sirisabanakinenei, Sirirodi, Koyoŋitenenei papakon ka totokon.”" 
Mark10:20 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, aricit ŋun kere ameun keiditeuka.”" 
Mark10:21 Kosesen Yesu ŋes komina, kotema atiar, “Kiwolik adiopekirot: kolot, kogwela luijaatar kere, kokoranak lukican, ijaunete moolo kabar kotoma akuj: kosodi kobu kotup eoŋ.”" 
Mark10:22 Konyorididior ereeteke kanuka akirot kaŋin, kolot itururwei: naarai kejaas iboro luipu." 
Mark10:23 Koŋoleŋole Yesu, kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Etiono ca ma lukabarak alomar ajakanut naka Edeke!”" 
Mark10:24 Koumokis ikekesisiak kanuka akiroke, Konye Koboŋok Yesu bobo, kotema kes atiar, “Idwe, etiono ca ma lukabarak alomar ajakanut naka Edeke!" 
Mark10:25 Epatana ekaal aitor apedot naka ekus, itia ekabaran alomar ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Mark10:26 Koumokis noi jokan, kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Aso iŋai bo do epedori aitajario?”" 
Mark10:27 Kosesen kes Yesu kotema atiar, “Mam epedorio kotuŋa, konye mam ikote nen kama ejai Edeke: naarai epedoros kere kama ejai Edeke.”" 
Mark10:28 Kogeu Petero alimokin ŋes ebe, “Koany, kipou isio kenyeis kere, katuputu jo.”" 
Mark10:29 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, Emamei ituŋanan yeninyeinit etogo, arai iinacan, arai ainacan, arai toto, arai papa, arai idwe, arai amanat, kanukaŋ, kanuka Akiro Nukajokak da," 
Mark10:30 konye edumuni irwan akwatat kwape kwana apak na, itogoi, ka iinacan, ka ainacan, ka nukatoto, ka idwe, ka amanat, nepepe kareio; kosodi moolo toma okar luepote aijar naka ikar kere," 
Mark10:31 Konye luipu lueraas lusodit eraunete lukawasia; ka lukawasia da eraunete lusodit.” 
Mark10:32 Kejaas orot, edokarete alosit Yerusalem; kiŋarenikinit kes Yesu: koumokis; kes da luketupitos kokuriaka. Koyaŋa bobo lutomon kaluarei, kogeu alimonokin kes akiro nuedoikinete ŋes." 
Mark10:33 Kobala ebe, “Koany, kidokari alosit Yerusalem; einakinio Okoku loka etuŋanan akanin nuka isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak; etubokinete ŋes atwanare, ijaikinete ŋes mama ejaas Imo," 
Mark10:34 Eboliatar, ka aimuanakin aimul, ka aida, ka aiar da; akaulo kapaarasia auni ejaruni.”" 
Mark10:35 Kikunyut Yakob ka Yokana, odwe luka Sebedayo mama ejai, kotemasi atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kikoto kiswamak sio kere nukilipi jo.”" 
Mark10:36 Kotema kes atiar, “Ikotosi keswamakis inyo?”" 
Mark10:37 Kotemasi ŋesi atiar, “Kocamakinai sio keboikinos ediopet akanikon nakoteten, ediopet da akanikon nakokediany, kotoma aibusesukon.”" 
Mark10:38 Konye kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Mam ijenete nukilipito. Ipedorete tope aimat akoli naamasi eoŋ? Arai aibatisao kaibatis nakebatisatai eoŋ?”" 
Mark10:39 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kipedori.” Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Imasete bo akoli naamasi eoŋ: ido ibatisao kaibatis nakebatisatai eoŋ:" 
Mark10:40 konye akiro nuka aiboikin akanika nakoteten arai nakokediany mere nakaŋ aikor: konye einakinio ŋul luitemokinitoi sek.” 
Mark10:41 Kosodete nakepupunioto lutomon kogeut anyunyurikin Yakob ka Yokana. 
Mark10:42 Konyarau Yesu kes kotema atiar, “Ijenete ebe ŋul lueomitai araut ikayaitok luka Imo, eyaete kes kagogoŋ: ejai ikapolokokec apedor kamakec." 
Mark10:43 Konye mam ikote nen kamakus: konye ituŋanan yenekoto araut yenikapolon kamakus, korau ikusikejaanakinan;" 
Mark10:44 ŋin da yenekoto araut yenisodit kamakus, korau ibulesit yenika ituŋa kere," 
Mark10:45 Naarai Okoku loka etuŋanan da mam abu kobu aijaanakinio, dimarai aijaanakin, ka ainakin da akeijar alakunia luipu.”" 
Mark10:46 Kodoloto Yeriko: napelosi anyoun ko Yeriko, nepepe kikekesisiak ka ekodet loapol, abu okoku loka Timayo, Batimayo, emuduki ekelipiton, kiboie kariri kerot," 
Mark10:47 Nakiiraria ebe erai ŋol Yesu loko Nasaret, kogeu aiworo, kobala ebe, “Yesu, ijo okoku loka Daudi, kitimoi eoŋ.”" 
Mark10:48 Kiretakis luipu tetere ililiŋi: konye ŋes kiyatak noi aiworo ebe, “Wu ijo okoku loka Daudi, kitimoi eoŋ.”" 
Mark10:49 Kobwou Yesu, kotema atiar, “Konyarautu ŋes,” Konyaraut emuduk, kotemasi atiar, “Kotitiŋior: konyou, kinyarit ŋesi jo.”" 
Mark10:50 Kocaka akenapito, kodetun, kobu mama ejai Yesu." 
Mark10:51 Koboŋok Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Ikoto keswamak jo inyo?” Kotema emuduk atiar, “Raboni, (Ekesisianakinan,) akoto kakweny.”" 
Mark10:52 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kolot: kitaŋaleu jo akoniiyuun.” Atipet kokweny, kotupa ŋes korot." 
Mark11:1 Nakeapiariata Yerusalem, die ka Betapage ka Betaniya, moru loka Iseitunin, kijuka iarei kokesisiakake," 
Mark11:2 Kotema kes atiar, “Koloto kiton ore loisesenete: atipet kilomasi idumunete ikoku yenika asigiria eenitai, yenimam lem ibwanenit idiotuŋanan; kolacut, koinut." 
Mark11:3 Arai kitemari yes ituŋanan ebe, ‘Kanukinyo iswamaata kwaŋin?’ ilimokinete ŋes ebe, ‘Ejakait ipuda ŋes, ido inyakuni bobo ne atipet.’”" 
Mark11:4 Koloto, kodumut isigiria eenikinitai okek kiŋa orot; kolacut." 
Mark11:5 Kotemasi ice kalukebwoete kanen atiar, “Kanukinyo ilacariata yesi isigiria?”" 
Mark11:6 Koboŋokis kes kwape alimokinitor Yesu: kocamakis kes alosit. 
Mark11:7 Koinut Yesu isigiria, kocakanakis ikecenapen; kibwanen ŋesi." 
Mark11:8 Kopetanakis luipu ikecenapen orot; ice da akui nukejepununete kamanat. 
Mark11:9 Kiworoto ituŋa lukiŋarenikinito ka luketupakinito ebe, “Kosana! Isirereŋitoi loebunit kokiror loka Ejakait!" 
Mark11:10 Isirereŋitoi ajakanut naebunit, naka papaakosi Daudi! Kosana kuju noi kakuj.”" 
Mark11:11 Koloma ŋesi Yerusalem, toma oyekalu; nakedaunia asesen iboro kere, naarai kitiboŋit akwap konyou kolot Betaniya nepepe kalutomon kaluarei." 
Mark11:12 Apaaran naatupakini, nakeponiata ko Betaniya, korieb eteŋei." 
Mark11:13 Kiteluo etini kama elwana eribiribi, kolot aanyun arai diat epedori adumun amodioraito kotomakeŋ; nakedolokinio mam edumuna amodioraito dimarai akui bon; naarai mam kerai apak naka itinin." 
Mark11:14 Koboŋok kotema ŋes atiar, “Sirikenyam ituŋanan araitokon amear lolo kiton ikar kere.” Kopupete ikekesisiak." 
Mark11:15 Kodoloto Yerusalem: koloma toma oyekalu, kogeu aireŋear lukegwelanarete ka lukegwelete kotoma oyekalu, kobuburiana imesan luka ikesiecanarak arupian ka iicoloŋo luka ŋul kalukegwelanarete ajeleik;" 
Mark11:16 kwabo mam ecamakina ituŋanan aibwokit ibore kotoma oyekalu. 
Mark11:17 Kisisianak kes, kotema atiar, “Mam kereka iwadikatai ebe, ‘Enyarao ekatogo etogo lokilipet kanuka atekerin kere’? Konye yes ituluosi abua naka ikaŋatak.”" 
Mark11:18 Kiirasi isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak ŋun, komoata epone loemudiariata; naarai kekuriaka ŋes, naarai keumokinit ekodet kere kanuka akeisisianakin." 
Mark11:19 Nakitiboŋenenaa akwap kolomanarenenei kore. 
Mark11:20 Nakitorioto tupuruc, koanyutu etini ŋol kerinyo ameun kakeje." 
Mark11:21 Kiitu Petero akiroke, kotema atiar, “Rabi, koany, kerinyo etini lokilamakini ijo.”" 
Mark11:22 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Kiyuutu Edeke," 
Mark11:23 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Ŋinituŋanan yenelimokini eroŋat lo ebe, ‘Koukor, kocakakin aŋolol’; komam ebuonokini kotauke, konye kiyuunite ebe nuinera edolete; iswamakinio." 
Mark11:24 Kanuka ŋun katemari yes atiar, Akiro kere nuilipete ka nuiŋaiŋaete kiyuunito ebe kiinakinitai, ido kiswamakinio." 
Mark11:25 Naibwoenenaata ilipete, kisioniete, arai ijaas kakirot kayenice; tetere Papakus loejai toma akuj isioniei akusiibucanar. [" 
Mark11:26 Konye arai mam yes isioniete, Papakus da loejai toma akuj mam isioniei akusiibucanar.]”" 
Mark11:27 Kodoloto bobo Yerusalem: ido nakitoritor oyekalu, kopotu isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak ka imakio mama ejai;" 
Mark11:28 kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Iswamai ijo nu kapolou anyoin? Iŋai da kiinakini jo apolou nakiswamaa nu?”" 
Mark11:29 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Mere eoŋ da keŋit yes akirot adiopet, yes da koboŋokis eoŋ, ŋes konyet kalimokiniata apolou nakeswamaa nu." 
Mark11:30 Aibatisa naka Yokana kebuni kotoma akuj, arai bo kotuŋa? Koboŋokinoi.”" 
Mark11:31 Kiŋitanakinos bonik ka bonik, kobalas ebe, “Arai kiitema ebe, ‘Kebuni kotoma akuj’; etemari ŋesi ebe, ‘Aso kanukinyo mam kiyuuniata ŋes?’" 
Mark11:32 Konye arai kiitema ebe, ‘Kebuni kotuŋa’ kokuriaka ituŋa: naarai aomito ituŋa kere ebe kerai Yokana enabi abeit." 
Mark11:33 Koboŋokis Yesu ebe, ‘Mam kijeni.’ ” Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Eoŋ da mam kalimokini yes apolou nakeswamaa nu.”" 
Mark12:1 Kogeu einer kakes kawaragasia ebe, “Abu etuŋanan kira amana naka emusabibu, kirigak abwas, kobok aipany nacues, koduk aiteis, kititiŋ ikakoriok, kolot akwap ace." 
Mark12:2 Kedol apak kiyakia ebulesit mama ejaas ikakoriok, tetere edumuni araito nuka amana naka emusabibu kama ejaas ikakoriok." 
Mark12:3 Kikamut ŋol, kibuŋata, kotwarata atitai." 
Mark12:4 Kijuka bobo ecebulesit mamakec; kobelebelata, kisuruma ileic," 
Mark12:5 Kijuka ece; koarata ŋes: ka ice da luipu; kibuŋata ice, ice da koarata." 
Mark12:6 Aso kesalit bobo ediopet, okoku lominat: kiyakia ŋol da kawasia, kobala ebe, ‘Eyoŋete okokuka.’" 
Mark12:7 Konye kineranakinos ikakoriok ŋul ebe, ‘Lo ŋes lokeruman; aso kaarata ŋes, koraun airum nawok.’" 
Mark12:8 Kikamut ŋes, koarata, kocakasi kiŋa kamana naka emusabibu." 
Mark12:9 Aso ikonakini ai ejakait loka amana naka emusabibu? Ebuni emudiari ikakoriok ŋul, einakini ice amana naka emusabibu,"
