Mark12:10 Mam kereka isiomito nuiwadikatai nu ebe, ‘Amoru nakeŋerete ikadukok, Ŋin ŋes keponi kitaraunai amor nakapolon naka agor:" 
Mark12:11 Abuni akirot ŋin kama ejai Ejakait, Erai nakaumokin kakonyenewok’?”" 
Mark12:12 Komoata aikamun ŋes; konye kokuriaka ekodet; naarai apotu komisiikis ebe enerakinit kes awaragan ŋin: kinyeis ŋes koloto. 
Mark12:13 Kiyakiasi ice koParisayon ka luKerodian mamakeŋ, tetere elokete ŋes kakiro." 
Mark12:14 Nakedolokis, kotemasi atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kijeni ebe irai ijo lokabeit, kwabo mam ipodo idiotuŋanan kere: naarai mam iseseni ejautene loka ituŋa, konye isisianakini erot loka Edeke kotoma abeit. Ibus kereka ainakin Kaisar esolo arai bo mam?" 
Mark12:15 Kiinakini, arai bo mam kiinakini?” Konye kojen ŋesi ekecesoswai, kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo kikoduniata eoŋ? Koinunai adenari, kaany.”" 
Mark12:16 Koinut. Kotema kes atiar, “Nakaŋai aput na ka nukiwadikatai?” Kotemasi atiar, “Nuka Kaisar.”" 
Mark12:17 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Kotacakis Kaisar nueraas nuka Kaisar, ka Edeke da nueraas nuka Edeke.” Koumokis noi jokan." 
Mark12:18 Kopotu Isadukayon mamakeŋ, luebalas ebe emamei ajarun; kiŋita ŋes ebe," 
Mark12:19 “Ekesisianakinan, abu Musa kiwadikak sio ebe, Arai ketwana onace ketuŋanan, kinyek akeberu emamei ikoku, eyaŋaari onaceke akeberu, tetere edumakini onaceke aur." 
Mark12:20 Kejaas iinacan ikanykaarei: komany losodit aberu, kotwana komam inyeinit aur;" 
Mark12:21 Kirum lokiareit ŋes, kotwana, komam inyeinit aur; ka lokiwuniet da kwape kwaŋin." 
Mark12:22 Kiton lukanykaarei kere komam inyeinito aur. Kokaukec kere kotwana aberu da. 
Mark12:23 Aso kotoma ajarun eraun ŋin aberu nakaŋai kama kaŋul? Naarai kerai aberu naka lukany kaarei kere.” 
Mark12:24 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Mere akirot na ŋes ipaanariata yesi? Naarai mam ijenete nukiwadikatai, karaida apedor naka Edeke." 
Mark12:25 Naarai naejaruniata kotoma okatwak, mam emanyete, karaida amanyio: konye eraas bala imalaikan toma akui," 
Mark12:26 Konye nuka lukatwak ebe itajarunio; mam isiomito kotoma oitabo loka Musa kotoma owai loka Ekiot, kwape kelimokinia Edeke ŋes ebe, ‘Arai eoŋ Edeke loka Aburaam, Edeke loka Isaak, ka Edeke loka Yakob da’?" 
Mark12:27 Mam ŋes erai Edeke loka lukatwak, dimarai loka lukajarak; ipaarete noi.”" 
Mark12:28 Kobu ediopet kokewadikak, kiira kes iŋitanaros, kojenu ebe aboŋoki kotenan, kiŋit ŋes ebe, “Ani aicorakinet nasodit kakere?”" 
Mark12:29 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Nasodit ŋes na ebe, ‘Kiira wu Isirael; Ejakait Ewokodeke, erai Ejakait ediopet." 
Mark12:30 Komina Ejakait Ekonideke kekonitau kere, ka akoniijar kere, ka akonicoa kere, ka akonigogoŋ kere.’" 
Mark12:31 Nakiareit da ŋes na ebe, ‘Komina ikoniidunyet kwape iminar bon.’ Emamei aicorakinet ace nakapolon aitelekarit nu.”" 
Mark12:32 Kotema ekewadikan ŋes atiar, “Abeit, Ekesisianakinan, iner kotenan ebe erai ŋesi ediopet; kwabo emamei ece dimarai ŋes," 
Mark12:33 Amina ŋes ketau kere, ka ajenun kere, ka agogoŋ kere, ka amina ikeidunyet kwape eminar bon, itelekarit noi ainakineta nuicweio kere ka asuban da.”" 
Mark12:34 Nakeanyunia Yesu ebe aboŋoki kapirianut, kotema ŋes atiar, “Mam jo ilwana kajakanut naka Edeke.” Akaulo kaŋun amamei bobo yeniketitiŋikinit aiŋit ŋes akirot." 
Mark12:35 Koboŋok Yesu, nakisisianakinia koyekalu, ebe, “Biai bo ebalatatar ikewadikak nuka Kristo ebe erai okoku loka Daudi?" 
Mark12:36 Abu Daudi elopet kiner kanuka Emoyo Lokalaunan ebe, ‘Abu Ejakait kotema Ekajakait ebe, Kiboikin akanika nakoteten, Aitodol neebwaikinia lukasurupokon kwap kakejenekon.’" 
Mark12:37 Daudi elopet enyarit ŋes Ejakait; aso keraun bo biai ikekoku?” Kopupokinite ekodet loapol kaiyalama," 
Mark12:38 Kinera kaisisianakinike ebe, “Kocoito ikewadikak, luekotosi alosit konapito inapen lueojak, ka aiyogao kagwelanareta," 
Mark12:39 ka iicoloŋo lukapolou katukosia, ka aiboisio nukapolou kopucin." 
Mark12:40 Luecamete itogoi luka apuserun, luijoseete ebe ilipete nukaojak; edumunete ŋul atubokinio naitelekarit.”" 
Mark12:41 Kiboikin koseseni aiŋadis, koany kwape ecakanakinia ekodet apesan toma aiŋadis; luipu keraas ikabarak kocakanakis nuipu." 
Mark12:42 Kobu apuserut nakican kocakak ikapun iarei luerai apesa. 
Mark12:43 Konyarau ikekesisiak, kotema kes atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, acakaki apuserut ŋin nakican luipu adepar kere luecakanakinete aiŋadis," 
Mark12:44 Naarai acakakis ŋul kere kideikina luipu; konye ŋin kotoma ocanike acakaki lukejaatar kere, ŋes aijarake kere.”" 
Mark13:1 Nakelomunia koyekalu, abu ediopet kokesisiakake kolimok ŋes ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, koany amoru nu kwape ejaatar, ka aduketa nu da kwape ejaatar!”" 
Mark13:2 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Iany aduketa nu nuepolok? Mam esalakin amoru adiopet kuju kanace, namam etiyakinio.”" 
Mark13:3 Nakiboioo kotoma omoru loka Iseitunin atereikina eyekalu, kiŋita ŋes Petero ka Yakob ka Yokana ka Anderea kaiyeiyea ebe," 
Mark13:4 “Kolimokinai, ejaunete bo ŋun wori? Anyoin da aanyunet naka apak naeapuuniata ŋun kere aitodolikinio?”" 
Mark13:5 Kogeu Yesu atemar kes atiar, “Kocoito kinyek ituŋanan aitapaar yes." 
Mark13:6 Epote rwaru luipu kokirorika, kobalas ebe, Eoŋ ŋopeŋol; itapaarete kesi luipu." 
Mark13:7 Naiirariata nuka ijiisio ka iemuto luka ijiisio, sirikiyaloŋoŋoto: ibusakinit ŋun ajaun; konye koroko awasia edoluno," 
Mark13:8 Naarai enyoikini ateker asurokin ateker, ka ajakanut da asurokin ajakanut: ejaununete amaraneta nuka akwap kaiboisio nuegelegela; ejaunun da ebel: ŋun ŋes ageunet naka ariebo naka aidoun," 
Mark13:9 “Konye kocoito yesi ikulepek: naarai kiyaŋaarete yes airabisia; kibuŋao katukosia; ibwoete kakonyen nuka ikayaitok ka ikabakan kanukaŋ, araut ikajenak kamakec," 
Mark13:10 Ibusakinit ber Akiro Nukajokak alimonokinio atekerin kere," 
Mark13:11 Nakiyaŋaariata yes aijaikin atubokinio, sirikiliŋa aiyaloŋoŋ nuinerete: konye nukiinakinio kosawa kaŋol kinerata ŋun: naarai mere yes inerasi, dimarai Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
Mark13:12 Ijaikini onac onaceke atwanare, papa da ikekoku; enyoikinete idwe da lukauriakakec, tetere eario." 
Mark13:13 Kiŋarunete yes ituŋa kere kanuka ekakiror: konye yenetitiŋikini kiton awasia, ŋes itajario." 
Mark13:14 Konye naianyuniata etal loemudiari ebwoi nemam ibusakinit (yenesiomi kojenu), ŋes konyet ekeriata ŋul luejaas Yudaya oroŋan," 
Mark13:15 Ituŋanan yenejai kuju togo sirikedoku, karaida alomar ayaŋaar ibore kotogoke." 
Mark13:16 Yenejai mana da sirikeboŋu kau ayaŋaar akenapito. 
Mark13:17 Konye itukwi kes nuepotiete, ka nuitanakete da kapaarasia kaŋun!" 
Mark13:18 Kilipata yesi kinyek apak ŋin adolun kiporo. 
Mark13:19 Naarai eraunos apaarasia ŋun nukican, numam peŋo etakanunito ameun kasubio naasubia Edeke kiton kwana, komam bobo ejaunete cut." 
Mark13:20 Kedim Ejakait aiŋoŋar apaarasia timam kitajari akuan kere; konye kanuka luseuna, luabu ŋesi koseu, eŋoŋa apaarasia." 
Mark13:21 Kapak kaŋin arai kitemari yes ituŋanan ebe, ‘Koany, ejai Kristo ne’; arai bo, ‘Koany, ejai laije’; sirikiyuut." 
Mark13:22 Naarai enyounete luKriston lukeŋalak ka inabin lukeŋalak, itodikinete ŋul aanyuneta ka nukaumokin da, tetere itapaarete luseuna, arai epedoros." 
Mark13:23 Konye kocoito yesi kadau aikwenyar yes eroko akiro nu kere epona," 
Mark13:24 “Konye kapaarasia kaŋun akaulo ka ican ŋul, itumutonorio akoloŋ, mam elap ecauni," 
Mark13:25 ibirununos aacerin kotoma akuj, itamaranio da nukapedor nuejaas toma akuj." 
Mark13:26 Kosodi konyet eanyunete Okoku loka etuŋanan ebuni kodouon, kapedor naepol ka aibuses." 
Mark13:27 Kosodi ijukuni imalaikan, etukonokini luseunake anyoun kokwamin iwoŋon, ameun kosaŋe loka akwap kiton osaŋe loka akuj." 
Mark13:28 Aso kisisiautu akewaragan kama ejai etini; kedaut aketenieik alibun, itolomuni akekui, ijenunete ebe eapie apak naka aidweny." 
Mark13:29 Aso yes da, naianyuniata ŋun edolunete, kojenut ebe eapie ŋesi, kokek," 
Mark13:30 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Mam edaun atur na aitodol naejaunotor akiro ŋun kere." 
Mark13:31 Edaunos akuj ka akwapin, konye akakiro mam edaunos cut." 
Mark13:32 “Konye akiro nuka apaaran kaya ka esawa da emamei yenejeni, karaida imalaikan luejaas toma akuj, karaida Okoku, dimikito Papa bon." 
Mark13:33 Kocoito, kokwenyete, kilipete: naarai mam ijenete naejaikinor apak." 
Mark13:34 Eputos bala etuŋanan ekepejon loiboiororoi kacekwap, kinyeinite eketogo, koinakinite ikebulesin apolou, ŋinituŋanan akeswam, kicorakinite da ekagolon aikweny." 
Mark13:35 Aso kokwenyete: naarai mam ijenete naebunio ejakait loka etogo, arai eboŋ, arai kidiŋ ebai, arai naeruikinioto ikokoroi, arai tupuruc;" 
Mark13:36 kinyek aŋesun atipet kodum yes ijotoete. 
Mark13:37 Ido nukalimokini yes, alimokini kere, ebe Kokwenyete.”" 
Mark14:1 Kosodi esalito apaarasia aarei eroko epucit loka Aleleŋ ka imugatin lumam itubuunitoi kedolo: komoata lusasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak epone lokikamunet kapirianut, ka aiar ŋes," 
Mark14:2 Naarai kobalas ebe, “Mere toma apak naka epucit, kinye diat ecelet ajaun otuŋa.”" 
Mark14:3 Nakejaar ŋesi Betaniya togo loka Simon lokatapon, iboie enyami, kobu aberu nakejai ekube loka akinyet naelai naka etiai loepol naeuru maa: kobwaŋ ekube, kobukok akouke." 
Mark14:4 Konye kojaas ice lukenyunyuras, kotemanaros atiar, “Kanukinyo emadiŋikinor akinyet kopone kaŋol?" 
Mark14:5 Naarai tikepedor agwelar akinyet ŋin adenarin akwat auni ka aitedepar da, kokoranakinai lukican.” Kitorona ya." 
Mark14:6 Konye kotema Yesu atiar, “Kinyekisi; kanukinyo itiyaloŋoŋooto ŋes? Keswamak eoŋ aswam naejok." 
Mark14:7 Naarai apaarasia kere ejaas lukican nepepe kayes, ido naikototor ipedorete aiswamakin kes nuejok: konye eoŋ mam kija kayes apaarasia kere." 
Mark14:8 Eswama nuepedorit: ageik ainyonyoikin akakuan akinyet kanuka aidaare. 
Mark14:9 Ido abeit katemari yes atiar, Neelimonokinio Akiro Nukajokak kotoma akwapin kere, ŋin naeswama aberu na elimorio akiitunitor ŋes.”" 
Mark14:10 Konyou Yuda Isikariot, lokerai ediopet kotomon kaluarei, kolot mama ejaas isasedotin lupeti, tetere ijaikini ŋes mamakec." 
Mark14:11 Kosodete nakiirariata, kiyalamikinos, kisumunoto ainakin ŋes arupian. Komo apak naejokiar aijaikin ŋes mamakec." 
Mark14:12 Kapaaran nasodit naka imugatin lumam itubuunitoi, naearere lukaleleŋ, kotemasi ikekesisiak ŋes atiar, “Ai bo ikoto kaloto ketemokis konyamak lukaleleŋ?”" 
Mark14:13 Kiyakia iarei kokesisiakake kotema kes atiar, “Koloto ore, iriamunos yesi ketuŋanan loibwokit amot naka akipi: kotupasi ŋes." 
Mark14:14 Kere neelomari, kolimokis elopet etogo ebe, ‘Ebala Ekesisianakinan ebe, Ani bo akagola nakipejok, neanyamakini lukaleleŋ nepepe kikakesisiak?’" 
Mark14:15 Kitodikini ŋesi yes agola naepol nakokuiu epesitai itemokino: kitemonokis nen kanuwok.” 
Mark14:16 Konyout ikekesisiak, koloto ore, kodumut kwape kelimokinitor: kitemokis lukaleleŋ." 
Mark14:17 Nakimukoki akwap kobu nepepe kalutomon kaluarei. 
Mark14:18 Napiboiete enyamete, kotema Yesu atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, ediopet kayesi lokimori keoŋ kabilakini nat ebotet.”" 
Mark14:19 Kogeut akadakin, kotemanasi ediopet ediopet atiar, “Eoŋ ca nat ya?”" 
Mark14:20 Kotema kes atiar, “Ediopet kotomon kaluarei, lokicunyi keoŋ atibo," 
Mark14:21 Naarai elosi Okoku loka etuŋanan kwape kiwadikatere kanukeŋ; konye itukwi, etuŋanan ŋol loebilakini Okoku loka etuŋanan ebotet! Tiejok kama ketuŋanan kaŋol arai mam kewuruunitai.”" 
Mark14:22 Napenyamete, kolem emugati, kedau aisirereŋ, kobilibil, koinak kes, kotema atiar, “Kolemutu: lo ŋes akakuan.”" 
Mark14:23 Kolem akoli da, kedau aimal, koinak kes; komatata kere," 
Mark14:24 Kotema kes atiar, “Nu kes akaokot nuka aitutuket, nuebukoros kanuka ikepuak." 
Mark14:25 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Mam amasi bobo cut nuka araito naka emusabibu, kiton apaaran ya naamasia nukitetiak kotoma ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Mark14:26 Nakedauniata ayoore ekosio, koloto moru loka Iseitunin." 
Mark14:27 Kobala Yesu kes ebe, “Iguikinos yesi kere: naarai iwadikatai ebe, ‘Ebuŋai rwaru ekecokon, isiarakinos amerekekin.’" 
Mark14:28 Konye kadau ajarun, keŋarenikinete yes alosit Galilaya.”" 
Mark14:29 Konye kotema Petero ŋes atiar, “Karaida kiguikinos kere, konye eoŋ mam.”" 
Mark14:30 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Abeit katemari jo atiar, Lolo akuare na, eriŋa ekokor eruikino irwan aarei, kiŋeri eoŋ irwan auni.”" 
Mark14:31 Konye kiyatak ŋesi noi kobala ebe, “Karaida kebusakinit atwanare kajo, mam kaŋeri jo cut.” Luce da kere kinerata kwape kwaŋin," 
Mark14:32 Kodolokis aibois ekekiror Getesemane; kobala ŋesi ikekesisiak ebe, “Kiboikinos ne, kelipi ber eoŋ.”" 
Mark14:33 Koyaŋa Petero ka Yakob ka Yokana nepepe kaŋes, kogeu ainoŋanakin noi ka aburun." 
Mark14:34 Kotema kes atiar, “Itururwei noi ekatau aapiar atwanare: kosalata yesi ne, kokwenyete.”" 
Mark14:35 Kikunyak nediokasilon, kibiror ebuburia, kilip ebe arai kepedoros kinac esawa ŋol." 
Mark14:36 Kobala ebe, “Aba, Papa, kere epedoros kamakon: kolemarai akoli na: konye mere nuakoto eoŋ, dimarai nuikoto ijo.”" 
Mark14:37 Koboŋ, kodum kes ejotoete, kotema ŋesi Petero atiar, “Simon, ijotoi ca ijo? Mam ipedori aikweny esawa ediopet?" 
Mark14:38 Kokwenya kilipa, kinyeis alomar acodunio; ekoto bo emoyo, konye ekalanyana akuan.”" 
Mark14:39 Kikunya bobo, kilip, kinera akiro kwapekwa," 
Mark14:40 Koboŋ bobo, kodum kes ejotoete, naarai eluranaros ajo; mam apotu kojenut nueboŋokinete ŋes," 
Mark14:41 Koboŋ bo bo nakiwuniet, kotema kes atiar, “Iroko kereka ijotoete, iyeŋito? Aso do; adolu esawa; koany, einakinio Okoku loka etuŋanan akanin nuka ikadiakanarak," 
Mark14:42 Konyoutu, kaloto; koany, eapie lokabilaki eb otet.”" 
Mark14:43 Atipet napinera, kodolu Yuda, edioper kotomon kaluarei, koupas kekodet lokejaas ikileŋa ka ibelai, epote kama ejaas isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak ka imakio." 
Mark14:44 Koinakinite kes lokebilakini ŋes ebotet aanyunet, kobala ebe, “Loanui eoŋ, ŋes ŋol; kikamutu ŋes, koyaŋaasi ikokito.”" 
Mark14:45 Napekedolu, atipet kolot mama ejai Yesu, kobala ebe, “Rabi”; konu noi." 
Mark14:46 Koriosi akecekanin, kikamut ŋes." 
Mark14:47 Konye ediopet kakesi lukebwoete eapie, kout ekekileŋ, kinom ebulesit loka esasedoti lopeti, kojepa akekit." 
Mark14:48 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Ilomut teni yesi kikileŋa ka ibelai aikamun eoŋ, bala ekaŋatan?" 
Mark14:49 Ajaenena kayes ŋinipaaran toma oyekalu, esisianakini, komam kikamunete; konye ajaut nu tetere edolete Nukiwadikatai.”" 
Mark14:50 Kosodete kojalakis ŋes kere, kokerata." 
Mark14:51 Kotupa etelepat ediopet, lokijelokinit egoe lokebaputa bon. Kikamut ŋes," 
Mark14:52 Konye kinyek egoe lokebaputa, koker imujalal." 
Mark14:53 Koyaŋaasi Yesu mama ejai losasedoti lopeti; kotukonokinotor isasedotin lupeti kere ka imakio ka ikewadikak da. 
Mark14:54 Petero da kotupite kama elwana, kiton toma alaro naka losasedoti lopeti; kiboiete nepepe kikejaanakinak, ipieri akim." 
Mark14:55 Komoata isasedotin lupeti ka aurianet kere ikajenak aluikin Yesu, tetere earete; mam edumuna." 
Mark14:56 Naarai apotu luipu kitejenut nukaiŋal, konye mam emorikikina akeceitejenun." 
Mark14:57 Kobwaata ice, kitejenut nukaiŋal, kobalas ebe," 
Mark14:58 “Kipou isio keirasi ŋes ebala ebe, ‘Akesi eoŋ eyekalu lo lokedukio kakanin, adukuni ece kotoma apaarasia auni lomam edukio kakanin.’”" 
Mark14:59 Karaida kwaŋin mam aitejenunikec emorikikina. 
Mark14:60 Kobwo losasedoti lopeti kokidiŋ, kiŋit Yesu ebe, “Mam cabo iboŋokini akirot? Anyoika ŋun nuetejenut ŋul aluikin jo?”" 
Mark14:61 Konye ŋes kililiŋ, mam eboŋokino akirot, Kiŋit bobo losasedoti lopeti, kotema atiar, “Irai kereka ijo Kristo, Okoku loka Loituritoi?”" 
Mark14:62 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Eoŋ ŋopeŋol; ido ianyunete rwaru Okoku loka etuŋanan iboie kakan nakoteten nakapedor, eupunos kidouon luka akuj.”" 
Mark14:63 Kocil losasedoti lopeti ikenapen, kobala ebe, “Inyo bo kipudar bobo ikajenak?" 
Mark14:64 Iirasi ainyanakinike: iwomitos anu?” Kotubokis kere ebe ibusakinit atwanare. 
Mark14:65 Kogeut ice aimwaanakin aimul, korapakis akekonyen, kodipidipoto, kobalas ebe, “Komurwo.” Ikejaanakinak da lukeyaŋaarete, kibapanasi ŋes." 
Mark14:66 Kosodi nakejaar Petero kwap alaro, kobu adiopet kakejaanakinak nuka losasedoti lopeti;" 
Mark14:67 koany Petero ipieri akim, kosesen ŋes, kobala ebe, “Ijai nan ijo da nepepe ka Enasarayot je Yesu.”" 
Mark14:68 Konye koŋer, kobala ebe, “Mam ajeni, ido mam apupi nuinera ijo.” Koloma kiŋa kiton neelomarere: koruik ekokor." 
Mark14:69 Koany akejaanakinan ya ŋes, kogeu bobo alimokin ŋul lukebwoete kanen ebe, “Erai lo lokec.”" 
Mark14:70 Konye koŋer bobo. Apak edit bobo kolimokis Petero lukebwoete kanen ebe, “Abeit irai ijo lokec; naarai irai ijo Egalilayat.”" 
Mark14:71 Konye kogeu eilam ka aiyapo ebe, “Mam eoŋ ajeni etuŋanan ŋol loilimito yesi.”" 
Mark14:72 Atipet koruik ekokor irwan nakiareit. Kiitu Petero akirot nakelimokini Yesu ŋes ebe, “Eriŋa ekokor keruikino irwan aarei, kiŋeri eoŋ irwan auni.” Komulau eketau, komony." 
Mark15:1 Atipet tupuruc sek kinerut isasedotin lupeti ka imakio ka ikewadikak, ka aurianet kere, koenata Yesu, koyaŋaasi, kijaikis Pilato." 
Mark15:2 Kiŋit Pilato ŋes ebe, “Irai kereka ijo Ekabaka loka Iyudayan?” Koboŋok kotema atiar, “Ijo ibala.”" 
Mark15:3 Kiwosatos ŋes isasedotin lupeti kakiro nuipu. 
Mark15:4 Kiŋit bobo Pilato ŋes ebe, “Mam cabo iboŋokini akirot? Koany akiro nuetia nen nukiwosatere,”" 
Mark15:5 Mam bobo Yesu eboŋokino akirot; koumok Pilato. 
Mark15:6 Kopucit atapit aosikin kes eenat ediopet, loelipete." 
Mark15:7 Kejai etuŋanan lokenyaritai Baraba, lokeenitai nepepe kalukipaliikinete, lukearete ituŋa kotoma aipaliikin ŋin," 
Mark15:8 Kobu ekodet kogeu ailip aiswamakin kes kwape kenaikinitotor. 
Mark15:9 Koboŋok Pilato kes ebe, “Ikotosi kaosikis yes Ekabaka loka Iyudayan?”" 
Mark15:10 Naarai ajeni ŋesi ebe ainakis isasedotin kanuka ekolo. 
Mark15:11 Konye kisidikoto isasedotin lupeti ekodet ebe, koosik gwai Baraba." 
Mark15:12 Koboŋok bobo Pilato, kotema kes atiar, “Aso ekonakini ai ŋol loibalasi yesi ebe erai Ekabaka loka Iyudayan?”" 
Mark15:13 Kiworoto bobo ebe, “Kibubuk ŋes.”" 
Mark15:14 Kotema Pilato kes atiar, “Kanukinyo, naanyoin aronis nakiswamai?” Konye kiyatakisi kesi aiworo noi ebe, “Kibubuk ba.”" 
Mark15:15 Kosodi kokoto Pilato aisiyalamikin ekodet, koosik kes Baraba, ido kedau aida Yesu koinak tetere ibubukinio." 
Mark15:16 Kitolomasi ŋes iserikalei alaro, naerai Epuraitorion, kotukokis erioŋet kere." 
Mark15:17 Kitanapa anapito namuge, kojeata aboko naka ikukwa, kitanapikis akouke." 
Mark15:18 Kogeut ayogan ŋes ebe, “Yoga, ijo Ekabaka loka Iyudayan!”" 
Mark15:19 Kinomonomata akouke kagada, kimwaanakis aimul, kokukonokinos komaata." 
Mark15:20 Kosodete kedaut akienar ŋes, kolacasi anapito namuge, kitanapata akenapito. Kitolomasi kiŋa aibubukin." 
Mark15:21 Kitiŋaasi etuŋanan lokitorit, Simon Lokurenayot lokebuni kamanat, papa loka Alegesanda ka Rupo, tetere erioŋi emusalaba loka Yesu." 
Mark15:22 Koyaŋaasil aitodol aibois naenyaritai Gologota, apolouke ebe, Aibois naka Abelekek naka Akou." 
Mark15:23 Koinakis ebino lokinyalakinitai lukesai; konye mam abu kocam. 
Mark15:24 Kibubukis ŋes, kokorokorata ikenapen, kilamilamata eroet, aanyun lueyaŋaari ŋolituŋanan." 
Mark15:25 Kerai esawa lokiwuniet, kibubukis ŋes." 
Mark15:26 Kojai da ebalua loka nueosatai ŋes loewadikatai kuju ebe, “EKABAKA LOKA IYUDAYAN.”" 
Mark15:27 Kibubukis ikaŋatak iarei nepepe kaŋes; ediopet kakanike nakoteten, ka ediopet da kakanike nakokediany. [" 
Mark15:28 Kosodi kitodolikinoi Nukiwadikatai ebe, “Aponi kimarakinai nepepe kalukepali.”]" 
Mark15:29 Lukitorito nen koinyanakinete ŋes, kimuŋumuŋete da akecekwes, kobalas ebe, “Aso cado! Ijo loikesi eyekalu, ka adukun kotoma apaarasia auni," 
Mark15:30 kitajarun cani, kodoku komusalaba!”" 
Mark15:31 Kikote nen da isasedotin lupeti kokienatar ŋes bonik ka bonik nepepe kikewadikak, kobalas ebe, “Etajar ice; mam epedori aitajarun bon." 
Mark15:32 Kristo, Ekabaka loka Isirael, kodoku komusalaba, kaanyutu, keyuutu da.” Ŋul da lukibubukinitoi nepepe kaŋes kimuasi ŋes." 
Mark15:33 Napekedolo esawa lokikanyet kape, kojau amuton akwap kere kiton osawa lokikanyet kaoŋon." 
Mark15:34 Kosawa lokikanyet kaoŋon kodelo Yesu keporoto loepol kobala ebe, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabakatani?” apolouke ebe, “Ekadeke, Ekadeke, kanukinyo kijalakinia eoŋ?”" 
Mark15:35 Ice kalukebwoete kanen, kiirasi, kobalas ebe, “Koany, enyarit Eliya.”" 
Mark15:36 Koker ediopet, kileleb acago ebino loedwar ria, kibwaik toma agada, kitamat ŋes, kobala ebe, “Kinyeisi; kaanyutu arai cani ebuni Eliya aitodokun ŋes.”" 
Mark15:37 Konye Yesu kodelo keporoto loepol, kiridak." 
Mark15:38 Kocila aigalisit naka eyekalu kaarei ameun kokuju kiton kwap. 
Mark15:39 Keanyu ekapolokiton lokebwoi kanen atereikina, ebe eridaki kwaŋin, kobala ebe, “Abeit etuŋanan lo kerai Okoku loka Edeke.”" 
Mark15:40 Kojaas da aŋor nukesesenete kama elwanikina: kotomakec kejai Mariam Magadalene, ka Mariam toto naka Yakob lodidi ka Yose, ka Salome da," 
Mark15:41 nuaupenenas kaŋes, naajaar Galilaya, ijaanakinete ŋes; ka aŋor ace da nuipu nukedokarete nenipe kaŋes Yerusalem." 
Mark15:42 Kosodi napekitiboŋ, naarai kerai Aitemonokin, ŋes atemar ebe apaaran naeliŋakini nakasabato," 
Mark15:43 kobu Yosep loko Arimataya, esot lokaurianet, lokemunokina ajakanut naka Edeke; kotitiŋior koloma mama ejai Pilato, kilip akuan naka Yesu." 
Mark15:44 Koumok Pilato kwape ketwania atipet: konyarau ekapolokiton, kiŋit arai teni kedau atwanare." 
Mark15:45 Kedau ajenun kama kekapolokiton, kocam ainakin Yosep akuan." 
Mark15:46 Kogwel ŋesi egoe loka ebaputa, kolacu akuan, konunukik ogoe loka ebaputa, kibwaik toma ates nakikeitoi atiiba; kikokorik amor okek loka ates." 
Mark15:47 Kosesenete Mariam Magadalene ka Mariam toto naka Yose aibois naebwaikinio. 
Mark16:1 Kosodi ketubor nakasabato, kogwelut Mariam Magadalene, ka Mariam toto naka Yakob, ka Salome, lueuru maa, tetere elosete ainyonyoanakin ŋes." 
Mark16:2 Kosodi tupuruc sek kapaaran nasodit nakasabato, koloto ates napeŋiuni akoloŋ," 
Mark16:3 Kineranakinos bonik ka bonik ebe, “Iŋai bo kikokorikini oni amoru alemar kokek loka ates?”" 
Mark16:4 Nakiteluoroto, koanyutu amoru ikokorioritai awai; naarai apol noi." 
Mark16:5 Kolomasi ates, koanyutu etelepat iboie kowai lokoteten, enapit anapito nailiacanit; koumokis." 
Mark16:6 Kotema kes atiar, “Sirikiwumokis; imoete yesi Yesu Enasarayot lokibubukinitoi: ajaru; emamei kane; koanyutu aibois kama kibwaikinitai ŋes!" 
Mark16:7 Konye koloto, kolimokis ikekesisiak ka Petero da ebe, Kiŋarenikini ŋesi yes alosit Galilaya; ianyikinete ŋes ŋina, kwape kilimokinitor yes.”" 
Mark16:8 Kolomutu kiŋa, kokerata anyoun kates; naarai apotu komaranata, ka aumokin: mam elimokina imodiotuŋanan akirot; naarai akuriaka. [" 
Mark16:9 Nakedaunia ajarun tupuruc apaaran nasodit nakasabato, kisiau aitakanikin Mariam Magadalene, nakolo kireŋeari ŋesi ajokin akanykaarei." 
Mark16:10 Kolot ŋin kolimok lukejaenenas kaŋes, nakibworotor komonyete." 
Mark16:11 Kes da nakiirariata ebe ejari, aanyu ŋesi, mam apotu kiyuut." 
Mark16:12 Akaulo kaŋun, kitakanik ituŋa iarei kakesi kopone loegelara, napelosete okialo," 
Mark16:13 Koboŋosi kolimokis luce; mam apotu kiyuut ŋul da. 
Mark16:14 Kokau kitakanikin lutomon ka lodiopet iboiete enyamete; kitoron kanumam iyuuniata ka aninik naka ikecetauon, naarai mam apotu kiyuut ŋul lukeanyunete ŋes kedau ajarun okatwak." 
Mark16:15 Kotema kes atiar, “Koloto yesi akwapisinei kere, kolimonokis ŋinisubat kere Akiro Nukajokak." 
Mark16:16 Yeniyuuni kibatisai, itajario; konye yenimam iyuuni itelekarete akiro." 
Mark16:17 Etupanakinete aanyuneta nu ŋul luiyuunete; kokirorika ireŋeanarete ajokin: inerenenas aŋaiepa nukitetiak; 
Mark16:18 ikamununete imunwo, karaida kemata ibore yenikaaran, mam isiriebi kes cut; idokonokinete lukadekak akecekanin, eŋaleunete.”" 
Mark16:19 Kosodi Ejakait Yesu kedau einer kakes, koyaŋaarai toma akuj; kiboikin akan nakoteten naka Edeke." 
Mark16:20 Konyoutu kwi, kolimonokis kotoma aiboisio kere, kiswamai Ejakait nepepe kakes, kitogogoŋ akirot kanuka aanyuneta nuketupanakinete. Amen.]" 
Luke1:1 Naarai apotu luipu kotamakis aiwadik kotenan akiro ŋun nuetodolikinos kamawok," 
Luke1:2 kwape kiilimonokiniata kwi lukeraas ikajenak lukeanyunito ameun kageunet, ido ikejaanakinak luka akirot kaŋin," 
Luke1:3 ketojok eoŋ da, naarai abu kamoote abeit naka akiro ŋun kere ameun kanusodit, kesuduny da, kewadikak jo Teopilo lokaibuses," 
Luke1:4 tetere ijenuni abeit naka akiro nukiisisianakinio. 
Luke1:5 Kapaarasia nuka Kerode ekabaka loka Yudaya, kejai esasedoti ekekiror Sakaria, loka abeanakin naka Abiya: kerai aberuke naka aur naka Aaron, ekekiror Elisabet." 
Luke1:6 Keraas kesi kere luedolito kakonyen nuka Edeke, kolosenenete kaicorakineta ka ikisila da kere luka Ejakait komam aitoronio." 
Luke1:7 Kemamei kes ikoku, naarai arakakit Elisabet, ido kemojoŋito kesi kere." 
Luke1:8 Kosodi kanen, nakiswamaa ŋesi aswam naka esasedoti kakonyen nuka Edeke, kwape kebeikinitor," 
Luke1:9 kwape kejaar epone loka esasedotene, kobeik ŋes eroet alomar aibois nakalaunan naka Ejakait, aisupuruun lukisupurununo." 
Luke1:10 Kilipi ekodet kere loka ituŋa kokiŋa kosawa loka aisupuruun. 
Luke1:11 Kitakanikin ŋes emalaika loka Ejakait ebwoi kowai lokoteten loka etem loka aisupuruun. 
Luke1:12 Nakeanyunia Sakaria ŋes, kiyaloŋoŋ, kokurianar." 
Luke1:13 Konye kotema emalaika ŋes atiar, “Sakaria, sirikikurianar; naarai eirar akoniilip, kiwurikini jo akoniberu Elisabet ikoku yenisapat, imaikini ekekiror Yokana." 
Luke1:14 Ilakar ijo, iyalamikin; ido isiyalamikinete luipu akeurunio." 
Luke1:15 Naarai eraun lokapolon kakonyen nuka Ejakait, kwabo mam emasi ajon karaida nuitemerete; ilelebun Emoyo Lokalaunan, ameun kakoik naka totoke," 
Luke1:16 Ido inyakuni ŋesi luipu kodwe luka Isirael mama ejai Ejakait Ekecedeke. 
Luke1:17 Iŋareni kakonyeneke komoyo ka apedor naka Eliya, ainyakun itauon luka lukapapa mama ejaas idwe, ka lukepali mama ejai acoa naka ikadolitok; aitemonokin Ejakait ituŋa luesikapikinitai.”" 
Luke1:18 Kotema Sakaria emalaika atiar, “Ajenuni biai ŋun? Naarai amojoŋit eoŋ, akaberu da atuboros ikekar.”" 
Luke1:19 Koboŋok emalaika kotema ŋes atiar, “Eoŋ Gaburiel, loabwoi kakonyen nuka Edeke; keyakuunitai einer kajo, ka alimokin jo akiro nu nukajokak." 
Luke1:20 Ido koany, ililiŋi ijo komam ipedori einer, aitodol apaaran naedolioto nu, naarai mam iyuunit akakiro, nuitodolikinio kapakikec.”" 
Luke1:21 Edarito ituŋa Sakaria, koumokis kanu etumoror kaibois nakalaunan." 
Luke1:22 Nakelomunia, mam apedori einer kakes: kojenut ebe aanyunit aitapoet kotoma aibois nakalaunan: kiyatak aitetem kakanin, kosal mam epedori einer." 
Luke1:23 Kosodi kanen, nakitodolikinotor apaarasia nuka aijaanakinike, koboŋo oreke." 
Luke1:24 Akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun kopotuu akeberu Elisabet; koŋop ilapio ikany, kobala ebe," 
Luke1:25 “Kekonak Ejakait kwanata kapaarasia nukasesenia, tape kawoori ikaleic kakonyen nuka ituŋa.”" 
Luke1:26 Kolap lokikanyetekape aponi kijukunai emalaika Gaburiel kama ejai Edeke alosit Galilaya ore Nasaret," 
Luke1:27 mama ejai abekot nakisinerit ekiliokit ekekiror Yosep, lokokek loka Daudi; ekiror loka abekot ŋes Mariam." 
Luke1:28 Koloma emalaika mama ejai, kotema atiar, “Yoga, naisirereŋitoi noi, ejai Ejakait kajo!”" 
Luke1:29 Konye kiyaloŋoŋ ŋesi noi kanuka akiroke, koomoom kotauke ebe ikoni bo ai ayogan na," 
Luke1:30 Kotema emalaika ŋes atiar, “Sirikiyoŋ, Mariam, naarai idum asianut kama ejai Edeke." 
Luke1:31 Ido koany, ipotuuni, idouni ikoku yenitelepat, imaikini ekekiror Yesu." 
Luke1:32 Eraun ŋol lokapolon, enyarao Okoku loka je Ioejai kuju kakuj; Ejakait Edeke einakini ŋes eicoloŋ loka Daudi papaake," 
Luke1:33 irumi ekek loka Yakob ikar kere; akejakanut da mam enaŋi.” 
Luke1:34 Kotema Mariam emalaika atiar, “Ikwaikinete bo ai ŋun, naarai mam ajeni ekiliokit?”" 
Luke1:35 Koboŋok emalaika ŋes ebe, “Kidoikini jo Emoyo Lokalaunan, kirapiari agogoŋ naka Je loejai kuju kakuj; kanuka ŋun yeneuruunio enyarao yenikalaunan, Okoku loka Edeke." 
Luke1:36 Ido koany, Elisabet kinacikon, ŋes da epotiei ikoku yenitelepat kotoma amojoŋuke; elap lo da ŋes lokikanyetekape loka ŋin nakenyaritai arakan." 
Luke1:37 Naarai emamei akirot naikaruni Edeke.” 
Luke1:38 Kobala Mariam ebe, “Koany, arai eoŋ abulesit naka Ejakait; kojaut mamakaŋ kwape kakonikiro.” Kosodi konyou emalaika kamakeŋ." 
Luke1:39 Kapaarasia kaŋun konyou Mariam, kisunya alosit akwap nakiukon, kiton ore ediopet loko Yuda;" 
Luke1:40 koloma togo loka Sakaria kiyoga Elisabet. 
Luke1:41 Kosodi kanen, nakiiraria Elisabet ayogan naka Mariam, kicuru ikoku kakoikike; kilelebai Elisabet Emoyo Lokalaunan;" 
Luke1:42 kodelo jokan, kotema atiar, “Isirereŋitoi jo kotoma aŋor, isirereŋitoi da araito nuka aliligetekon." 
Luke1:43 Kepote bo nu kai, toto naka Ekajakait abunore mamakaŋ?" 
Luke1:44 Naarai koany, napadolunio ayoganikon akiika, kicuru ikoku kakoikika kanuka aiyalama," 
Luke1:45 Isirereŋitoi da ŋin naiyuunit; naarai itodolikinio nualimokinitai ŋes kama ka Ejakait.” 
Luke1:46 Kotema Mariam atiar, “Itopoloori ekatau Ejakait," 
Luke1:47 Elelakinit da ekamoyo Edeke Ekaketaiaran. 
Luke1:48 Naarai aanyu ican luka akebulesit. Naarai koany, amear lolo kanyaritos eoŋ aturio kere naitusulianyitai." 
Luke1:49 Naarai keswamaki Lokapedor nuepolok: Lokalaunan ekekiror. 
Luke1:50 Akeitim ejai kaŋul lueyoŋito ŋes, Anatar aturio kere." 
Luke1:51 Etodia agogoŋ kakekan, Esiarisiar ikewoŋok kaomisio nuka itauonokec." 
Luke1:52 Ereŋea lukapolok koicoloŋokec, Etopolo luitasonos," 
Luke1:53 Esimoniki Iuketeŋei iboro luejok, Epapel ikabarak." 
Luke1:54 Eitu akeitim, Eŋaraki Isirael ekebulesit." 
Luke1:55 Kwape kisumunio lukapapaawok, Aburaam ka aurike apaarasia kere.”" 
Luke1:56 Kosalak Mariam kaŋes bala ilapio iuni, kosodi koboŋo orekec," 
Luke1:57 Kosodi kanen kodol apak naka Elisabet aidoun, kidou ikoku yenitelepat." 
Luke1:58 Kiirasi ikeidunyeta ka ikepajen ebe etopoloo Ejakait akeitim mamakeŋ, kiyalamikinos nenipe kaŋes." 
Luke1:59 Kosodi kapaaran nakikanyetekauni kopotu aikep ikoku; kokotosi amaikin ekiror loka papake Sakaria. 
Luke1:60 Koboŋok totoke kotema atiar, “Mam, konye emaikinio Yokana.”" 
Luke1:61 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Emamei yenikajenakon yenemaikinitai ekiror ŋol.”" 
Luke1:62 Kokwetut papake ajenun ebe ekoto amaikin iŋai. 
Luke1:63 Kilip ibore yenikiwadika, kiwadik ebe, “Ekekiror erai Yokana.” Koumokis kere." 
Luke1:64 Atipet kopukoroi akeituk, kolacarai da akeŋalep, kiner, iturit Edeke," 
Luke1:65 Kokuriakaros ikeceidunyeta kere, Kitisiarakinai akiro ŋun anatar akwap kere nakiukon naka Yudaya;" 
Luke1:66 kere lukiirarete koricata kotauonokec, kobalas ebe, “Aso eraun ikoku yen yenikepone enyoin?” Naarai akan naka Ejakait ajai kaŋes," 
Luke1:67 Kilelebun papake Sakaria Emoyo Lokalaunan, kodwar kobala ebe," 
Luke1:68 “Kituritete Ejakait Edeke loka Isirael, Naarai aanyana iketuŋa alaku da," 
Luke1:69 Etonyoiki oni amumwarat naka aitajar Kokek loka Daudi eketelepat. 
Luke1:70 Kwape enerar kolo kageunet Kaituke nuka inabinoke lukalaunak; 
Luke1:71 Ebe kitaiari oni kama kalukasurupowok, Kakan da naka ŋul kere lukireito;" 
Luke1:72 Itodoli aitim naesumunit lukapapaawok, Ka aiitun akeitutuket nakalaunan," 
Luke1:73 Aitodolikin aiyaposit naeyapoikinit Aburaam papaawok," 
Luke1:74 Ainakin oni ketajarunos kakan naka lukasurupowok, Kejaanakis ŋes komam kikuriaka;" 
Luke1:75 Kotoma alaunit ka adolit kakonyeneke Apaarasia kere nuka aiiarawok," 
Luke1:76 Ŋo da ikoku, kinyarao enabi loka Je loejai kuju kakuj; Naarai iŋareni kakonyen nuka Ejakait aitemokin ikerotin," 
Luke1:77 Kitejen iketuŋa aitajario kotoma aisionio akecediakanareta," 
Luke1:78 Kanuka aitim nakotau loka Edekewok, Kipejok oni Acilakide naabuni kokuju," 
Luke1:79 Acaikin ŋul luiboete kotoma amuton, Kotoribe da lokatwanare, Aiteten awokokeie korot loka ainapakin.”" 
Luke1:80 Kopoloor ikoku, kiyatanakin agogoŋor komoyo; kojai kamodiŋo aitodol apaaran nakitakanikinor Isirael." 
Luke2:1 Kosodi kanen kapaarasia kaŋun, kobu ekisil kama ka Kaisar Augusito ebe ibusakinit ituŋa luka akwapin kere aiwadikao." 
Luke2:2 Ŋin ŋes aiwadikao nasodit nakeraar Kuirinio ekayaiton loka Suria. 
Luke2:3 Koloto ituŋa kere aiwadikao, ŋinituŋanan bukec." 
Luke2:4 Konyou Yosep da koGalilaya, kore Nasaret, kodoka alosit Yudaya, ore loka Daudi, loenyaritai Betelekem, naarai kerai ŋesi lokokek ka ajena naka Daudi;" 
Luke2:5 tetere iwadikao nepepe ka Mariam, nakisinerit ŋesi, epotiei." 
Luke2:6 Kosodi kanen, ejaas ŋina, kodoloto akepaarasia nuka aidoun." 
Luke2:7 Kidou yenikiyaike yenisapat; kimuko kigoen lukimukeru, kiperik atuba nakenyamenenata ibaren, naarai mam adumunito apak kotogo loka ipejok." 
Luke2:8 Kojaas ikecokok kakwap kaŋin lukiboiete kais idarete ekecesipan kuare. 
Luke2:9 Kotakanik kes emalaika loka Ejakait, kocau aŋosibib naka Ejakait airiamar kes: kokuriakaros noi." 
Luke2:10 Kotema emalaika kes atiar, “Sirikikuriakaros; naarai koany, kainunit yes akiro nukajokak nuka aiyalama naepol naejauni mama ejaas ituŋa kere;" 
Luke2:11 naarai auruun lolo kanukus Eketaiaran, ŋes Kristo Ejakait kotoma ore loka Daudi," 
Luke2:12 Na ŋes aanyunet kamakus; idumunete ikoku yenimukeru imukoritai kigoen lukimukeru, eperi kotoma atuba nakenyamenenata ibaren.”" 
Luke2:13 Atipet kojai nepepe kemalaika kaŋol ekodet loka ajore naka akuj ituritos Edeke, ebalasi ebe," 
Luke2:14 “Kojai aibuses mama ejai Edeke kokuju kakuj, Ka ainapakin da kakwapin mama ejaas ituŋa luitoiokit.”" 
Luke2:15 Kosodi kanen, kenyout imalaikan aboŋor toma akui, kotemanaros ikecokok ebe, “Aso kaloto kiton Betelekem, kaanyut ŋun nuiswamatai, nukitejenu Ejakait oni,”" 
Luke2:16 Koloto atipet, kodumutu Mariam ka Yosep, nepepe kimukeru eperi katuba nakenyamenenata ibaren," 
Luke2:17 Keanyutu, kiteienut akirot nakelimokinio kes naka ikoku kaŋin," 
Luke2:18 Koumokis lukiirarete kere akiro nukelimokinete ikecokok. 
Luke2:19 Konye koricite Mariam akiro ŋun kere, koomite kotauke." 
Luke2:20 Koboŋosi ikecokok, itopoloorito ituritos da Edeke kanuka akiro kere nukiirarete, ka nuaanyut da, kwape kelimokinitere." 
Luke2:21 Kedolo apaarasia akanykauni nuka aikep ŋes, komaikis ekekiror Yesu, kwape kemaikinia emalaika eriŋa epotuuno." 
Luke2:22 Kedol apak naka aitesegariokec kwape ejaar ekisil loka Musa, koyaŋaasi ŋes Yerusalem aitodiar mama ejai Ejakait." 
Luke2:23 (Kwape iwadikatere kokisil loka Ejakait ebe, “Ŋinikoku yenikiliokit yenepukori aliliget enyaritai yenikalaunan mama ejai Ejakait.”)" 
Luke2:24 Koinakis da asuban kwape kineritere kokisila luka Ejakait, “Ajeleik aarei arai ilukei iarei ludidik.”" 
Luke2:25 Ido koany, kejai etuŋanan Yerusalem, ekekiror Simeon, kerai etuŋanan loedolit loeyoŋit Edeke, edaret aitalakario naka Isirael, kejai ŋes Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
Luke2:26 Kikwenyarit Emoyo Lokalaunan ŋes ebe mam etwani eroko eanyuna Kristo loka Ejakait. 
Luke2:27 Kobu ŋol toma oyekalu iŋarenikinit Emoyo; ido nakeyauniata ikauriak ikoku Yesu tetere iswamakinete ŋes kwape ejaar epone loka ikisila," 
Luke2:28 kodak ŋes elopet kakaninike, kimal Edeke, kotema atiar," 
Luke2:29 “Ejakait, kotwar kwana ekonibulesit inapakina, Kwape ejaar akonikirot;" 
Luke2:30 Naarai aanyut akakonye akoniitajar," 
Luke2:31 Nakitemonokinit kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere," 
Luke2:32 Aica naapukoo lukaŋekwapin, Araun aibuses naka ikonituŋa Isirael.”" 
Luke2:33 Koumokis papake ka totoke ŋun nukinerai kanukeŋ. 
Luke2:34 Kilipak Simeon kes arereŋ, kotema ŋesi Mariam totoke atiar, “Koany, ibwaikinitai ikoku yen kanuka aibiror ka anyoun da naka luipu kotoma Isirael, Ido araut aanyunet naitepegitai." 
Luke2:35 Ijo da alopet kicumi ekileŋ ekonitau, Tetere epukoros aomisio nukotauon kaluipu.”" 
Luke2:36 Kejai da anabi, ŋes Ana, akoku naka Panuel loka ateker naka Aser; kedaunit ikar luipu, kiboikino kokilenike ikar ikanykaarei ameun kabekonutuke," 
Luke2:37 kerai apuserut ikar akaisakanykauni ka luoŋon, Mam kenyoununei koyekalu, konye komaenenei Edeke paaran ka kuare da kailuŋ ka ailip." 
Luke2:38 Kotakanu ŋin da kapak kaŋin, kimala Edeke, kolimok lukidareto alakunio naka Yerusalem nuka ikoku." 
Luke2:39 Kosodete nakedauniata aitodolikin kere kwape kicorakinitere kotoma okisila luka Ejakait, koboŋosi Galilaya, orekec Nasaret." 
Luke2:40 Kopoloor ikoku, kiyatakin agogoŋ, kileleba acoa; asianut da naka Edeke kojai kaŋes." 
Luke2:41 Kolosenenete ikauriakake ŋolikaru Yerusalem apak naka epucit loka Aleleŋ. 
Luke2:42 Nakedol ŋesi ikar itomon kaarei, koloto kwape kejaar epone loka epucit;" 
Luke2:43 nakedaut aitodolikin apaarasia, apak naka aboŋorikec, kosalak isapat Yesu Yerusalem, komam ikekauriak ejenete." 
Luke2:44 Konye koomitos kesi ebe ejai toma okodet, koloto alosit naka apaaran adiopet; kosodete komoata ŋes opajenakec ka opaperokec da." 
Luke2:45 Nakekurwokis adumun, koboŋosi Yerusalem emootos ŋes." 
Luke2:46 Kosodi kanen, ketuboros apaarasia auni kodumakis ŋes oyekalu, iboie kokidiŋ kikesisianakinak, epupi, kiŋisi da aiŋiseta." 
Luke2:47 Koumokis kere lukiirarete ŋes akeijen ka akeboŋonokin da. 
Luke2:48 Nakeanyuniata, koumokis: kotema totoke ŋes atiar, “Ikakoku, kanukinyo kikonakinia sio kwaŋin? Koany, papakon ka eoŋ da kipou kamootos jo kaiturur.”" 
Luke2:49 Kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo kimoiata eoŋ? Mam kereka yes ijenete ebe kebusakinit aiboi kotogo loka Papaka?”" 
Luke2:50 Mam kes apotu kojenut akirot ŋin nakelimokini kes," 
Luke2:51 Kijesar nepepe kakes, kiton Nasaret; kononokikinite kes. Koricite totoke akiro ŋun kere kotauke." 
Luke2:52 Kiyatanakini Yesu kotoma acoa ka apoloor, ka asianut mama ejai Edeke ka ituŋa da." 
Luke3:1 Kokaru lokitomonet kakany loka airumit naka Kaisar Tiberio, korai Pontio Pilato ekayaiton loko Yudaya, ka Kerode da ekabaka loko Galilaya, ka Pilipo onaceke ŋes ekabaka loka akwap naka Ituraya ka Turakonito, ka Lusania ŋes eka baka loka Abilene," 
Luke3:2 kapak nakeraatar Ana ka Kaiapa lusasedotin lupeti, kobu akirot naka Edeke mama ejai Yokana okoku loka Sakaria kamodiŋ." 
Luke3:3 Kolot akwap kere naidunyasi Yorodan, elimonokini aibatisa naka aitoronikin kanuka alemar adiakanareta." 
Luke3:4 Kwape kiwadikatere koitabo loka akiro nuka enabi Isaia ebe, “Eporoto loka yenikiworoi kamodiŋ ebe, Kitemonokis erot loka Ejakait, Kitetena ikesokono." 
Luke3:5 Itutuo rwaru ŋinidirot, Ikeio ŋoliroŋat ka ŋoliukot; Itetenio neekudukudo, liyaiyakinio nuimugogolito;" 
Luke3:6 Eanyunete kere luejaas awat aitajar naka Edeke.” 
Luke3:7 Aso kolimok ikodeta lukepote mamakeŋ aibatisao ebe, “Yes aur naka imusagan, iŋai bo kiikwenyari yes akerit anyunyura naebunit?" 
Luke3:8 Aso koraata araito nuibusakinito aitoronikin, ido sirikigeut einer kotauonokus ebe, ‘Ejai oni Aburaam papaawok’; naarai kalimokini yes ebe, Epedori Edeke aitonyoikin Aburaam idwe kotoma amor kanu," 
Luke3:9 Nati kwape kwana da ibwaikinitai aep atoromin nuka ikito: asa ŋolikitoi lomam erai araito nuejok ejepario, ka acakakin akim.”" 
Luke3:10 Kiŋita ŋes ikodeta ebe, “Aso keswamara anyoika?”" 
Luke3:11 Koboŋok kes kotema atiar, “Yenejaas ikason iarei, koinak yenemamei; ka yenejaas inyamat da kikon nepenen.”" 
Luke3:12 Kopotu luketelemak esolo da aibatisao, kiŋita ŋes ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, keswamata isio da anyoika?”" 
Luke3:13 Kotema kes atiar, “Siritelemenenete luedeparito lukicorakinitai.”" 
Luke3:14 Kiŋita ŋes iserikalei da ebe, “Ka sio da, keswamata anyoika?” Kotema kes atiar, “Siribenyaka kama ejai ituŋanan, sirisabanakinete; kisiyalamikinito da ekusiropit,”" 
Luke3:15 Kosodete komunos ituŋa, koomoomoete ituŋa kere kotauonokec nuka Yokana, arai diat erai ŋesi Kristo;" 
Luke3:16 Koboŋok Yokana kotema kes kere atiar, “Abeit kebatisai yes kakipi; konye ebunit loketelekarit eoŋ kagogoŋ, lomam eoŋ kebusakinit alacun amuny naka amukake: kibatisai ŋol yes kEmoyo Lokalaunan ka akim," 
Luke3:17 Ejai ekeritei akanike, epiari cut ekepeial, etukonokini akimake odula; konye icwei agugu kakim namam itudeŋio.”" 
Luke3:18 Ido kaicoreta ace nuipu kolimonok ituŋa akiro nukajokak. 
Luke3:19 Konye ekabaka Kerode, kanuetoronia Yokana ŋes kanuka Kerodia aberu naka onaceke, ka nukaronok kere nukiswamat Kerode," 
Luke3:20 kiyatak na da tomakec, kogolok ŋesi Yokana aidaris," 
Luke3:21 Kosodi kanen, kedaut ituŋa kere aibatisao, kibatisauna Yesu da, napilipi ŋesi, koŋaar akuj," 
Luke3:22 kijesun Emoyo Lokalaunan mamakeŋ kakuan bala ajele, kolom eporoto kakuj, ebe, “Irai ijo Okokuka Iominat; kalelakinit jo noi.”" 
Luke3:23 Yesu elopet nakegeunia aisisianakin kerai loka ikar bala akaisauni, koomitete araut okoku loka Yosep, okoku loka Keli," 
Luke3:24 Okoku loka Matat, okoku loka Lebi, okoku loka Meliki, okoku loka Yanai, okoku loka Yosep," 
Luke3:25 okoku loka Matatia, okoku loka Amos, okoku loka Nakum, okoku loka Esili, okoku loka Nagai," 
Luke3:26 okoku loka Maat, okoku loka Matatia, okoku loka Semein, okoku loka Yosek, okoku loka Yoda," 
Luke3:27 okoku loka Yoanan, okoku loka Resa, okoku loka Serubabel, okoku loka Sealutiel, okoku loka Neri," 
Luke3:28 okoku loka Meliki, okoku loka Adi, okoku loka Kosam, okoku loka Elamadam, okoku loka Er," 
Luke3:29 koku loka Yesu, okoku loka Elieser, okoku loka Yorim, okoku loka Matat, okoku loka Lebi," 
Luke3:30 okoku loka Simeon, okoku loka Yuda, okoku loka Yosep, okoku loka Yonam, okoku loka Eliakim," 
Luke3:31 okoku loka Melea, okoku loka Mena, okoku loka Matata, okoku loka Natan, okoku loka Daudi," 
Luke3:32 okoku loka Yese, okoku loka Obed, okoku loka Boas, okoku loka Salumon, okoku loka Nason," 
Luke3:33 okoku loka Aminadab, okoku loka Arani, okoku loka Kesuron, okoku loka Peres, okoku loka Yuda," 
Luke3:34 okoku loka Yakob, okoku loka Isaak, okoku loka Aburaam, okoku loka Tera, okoku loka Nakor," 
Luke3:35 okoku loka Serug, okoku loka Reu, okoku loka Peleg, okoku loka Eber, okoku loka Sela," 
Luke3:36 okoku loka Kainan, okoku loka Arupakasad, okoku loka Sem, okoku loka Noa, okoku loka Lamek," 
Luke3:37 okoku loka Metusela, okoku loka Enok, okoku loka Yared, okoku loka Makalaleel, okoku loka Kainan," 
Luke3:38 okoku loka Enos, okoku loka Set, okoku loka Adam, okoku loka Edeke." 
Luke4:1 Kosodi Yesu, kilelebun Emoyo Lokalaunan, koboŋo koYorodan, kiŋarenik Emoyo Lokalaunan amodiŋ," 
Luke4:2 kodau apaarasia akaisaoŋon, ecoduni Satan ŋes. Kapaarasia kaŋun mam kenyami ibore: kedaunos, korieb eteŋei," 
Luke4:3 Kotema Satan ŋes atiar, “Arai tope irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke kicorak amoru na koraun atap.”" 
Luke4:4 Koboŋok Yesu ŋes ebe, “Iwadikatai ebe, Mam ituŋanan ejari kanuka atap bon.”" 
Luke4:5 Kitodoka kuju, kitodianak ajakanuto kere nuka akwapin, katipet," 
Luke4:6 Kotema Satan atiar, “Kainakini jo apolou na kere, ka aibusesukec; naarai kainakinitai eoŋ; eoŋ da ainakini yenakoto kere." 
Luke4:7 Aso arai kiima eoŋ, eraunete kere nukon.”" 
Luke4:8 Koboŋok Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Iwadikatai ebe, Komaenenei Ejakait Ekonideke, kijaanakinenei ŋes bon.”" 
Luke4:9 Koyaŋa ŋes Yerusalem, kisibwo koswi loka eyekalu, kotema atiar, “Arai tope irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke, kosomari kwap." 
Luke4:10 Naarai iwadikatai ebe, Icorakini ikemalaikan kanukon, kidarata joo" 
Luke4:11 ido, Kidakete jo kakaninikec, Kinyek amoru aiguikin akonikeju.”" 
Luke4:12 Koboŋok Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Ebalai ebe, Sirikodununei Ejakait Ekonideke.”" 
Luke4:13 Nakedaunia Satan ŋinicodunet, kinyek ber ŋes." 
Luke4:14 Koboŋ Yesu kapedor naka Emoyo, kolot Galilaya: kisiarakin ekeemutu anatar akwapin kere nuidunyatar." 
Luke4:15 Kisisianakinenei kotoma atukosiakec, kitopolooritos ituŋa kere." 
Luke4:16 Kobu Nasaret, kama kitopolounere; kapaaran nakasabato koloma toma atukos, kwape kejaar ekepitene, kobwo asoman." 
Luke4:17 Koinakinai eitabo loka enabi Isaia. Kopuko eitabo, kodum aibois mama kiwadikatai ebe," 
Luke4:18 “Emoyo loka Ejakait ejai keoŋ, Naarai abu kenyonyoik akinyet alimonokin lukican akiro nukajokak; Kejuk eoŋ alimor aosikinio mama ejaas luijoreoritai, Ka imudukiok da akwenyun, Alakakin lueridakinitai," 
Luke4:19 Alimor da ekaru loka Ejakait loecamunitai.” 
Luke4:20 Korapak eitabo, kinyakak ekejaanakinan, kiboikin; kosesenata ŋes noi ituŋa kere lukejaas atukos." 
Luke4:21 Kogeu alimokin kes ebe, “Etodolikin lolo nukiwadikatai nu toma akiikus.”" 
Luke4:22 Kitejenut kere, koumokis akiro nukasianut nukelomunete kaitukuke: kobalas ebe, “Mere lo okoku loka Yosep?”" 
Luke4:23 Kotema kes atiar, “Abeit ipote ainerakin eoŋ awaragan na ebe, ‘Emurwon, kitaŋaleun bon: ŋun kere nukiiranari ebe kiswamat Kaparanaum, kiswama kane da kobukus.’ ”" 
Luke4:24 Kotema atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, Emamei enabi loecamunio kobukec." 
Luke4:25 Konye abeit katemari yes atiar, Kojaas kolo apuserun nuipu koIsirael kapaarasia nuka Eliya, apak nakegolitere akuj ikar iuni ka ilapio ikanykape, nakedoikinio ebeli loepol akwap kere;" 
Luke4:26 mam aponi kijukarai Eliya mama ejai adiopet kakesi, dimarai Sarapeta, kakwap naka Sidon, mama ejai aberu nakerai apuserut," 
Luke4:27 Kojaas da lukatapon luipu koIsirael kapaarasia nuka Elisa enabi; mam yenaponi kiswagarai, dimarai Naaman Esuriat.”" 
Luke4:28 Nakiirariata kesi akiro ŋun kotoma atukos, kilelebunos kere anyunyura." 
Luke4:29 Konyoutu, koremosi kiŋa ka ere, koyaŋaasi neetukum koukot loadukokinitai ekecere, tetere eremorete ŋes kwap cut." 
Luke4:30 Konye ŋes kitoro kidiŋikec kolot. 
Luke4:31 Kikokorun kiton Kaparanaum, ore loko Galilaya. Kisisianak kes kapaaran nakasabato," 
Luke4:32 Koumokis noi ituŋa akeisisianakin; naarai kejai akekirot apolou," 
Luke4:33 Kejai etuŋanan atukos lokejai emoyo loka ajokit naerono, kiworo keporoto loepol ebe," 
Luke4:34 “Kinyeinai! Anyoika isio kajo, Yesu loko Nasaret? Ibu kereka amudiar sio? Kajeni jo kwape iraar, Lokalaunan loka Edeke.”" 
Luke4:35 Kiretak Yesu ŋes ebe, “Kobuta, kolom kamakeŋ.” Kibirok ajokit lokadekan kidiŋikec, konyou kamakeŋ, komam imadiŋit," 
Luke4:36 Koumokis kere, kineranakinos bonik ka bonik ebe, “Akirot anyoin na? Naarai icorakini imoyon lueroko kapolou ka apedor, elomunete da.”" 
Luke4:37 Kisiarakin ekeemut anatar aiboisio kere nuidunyatar akwap ŋin. 
Luke4:38 Konyou katukos koloma togo loka Simon. Kedeka toto naka aberu naka Simon ekamidi loepol; kiŋaiŋaata ŋes kanukeŋ. 
Luke4:39 Kobwo kama ejai, kiretak ekamidi; kinyek ŋin: atipet konyou kijaanak kes." 
Luke4:40 Napibiror akoloŋ, ŋul kere lukejaas ituŋa lukedekasi adekesia nuegelegela koinut ŋes; kidokok akekanin ŋinidiopet kaŋul, kitaŋaleu kes." 
Luke4:41 Konyoununut ajokin da kaneejaas luipu, kiworoto ebe, “Irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke.” Kiretak kes, kisimik einer, naarai kejenete ebe ŋes Kristo." 
Luke4:42 Kosodi kiwala akwap, konyou kolot aibois naesil; komoata ŋes ikodeta, kopotu mama ejai, kokotosi aitasal ŋes, kinyek anyoun kamakec," 
Luke4:43 Konye kotema kes atiar, “Kebusakinit alimonokin akiro nukajokak nuka ajakanut naka Edeke koreria ice da: naarai ŋin keyakuunere.”" 
Luke4:44 Kolimonokinenei katukosia nuko Galilaya. 
Luke5:1 Kosodi kanen nakeridakiniata ŋes ikodeta iirarete akirot naka Edeke, kebwoi ŋesi kariri kaŋolol naka Genesaret." 
Luke5:2 Koany atakerin aarei nukeiaas oitolima loka aŋolol; konye kedokunito ikalokak ilosete iboyanakec. 
Luke5:3 Kodoka ataker adiopet, nakerai naka Simon, kilip ŋes aisukunyar nediokasilon anyoun koitolima, Kiboikin kisisianak ikodeta kojai ataker." 
Luke5:4 Nakedau einer, kotema ŋesi Simon atiar, “Koremo ataker kiton ataro, kocakakis iboyanakus aikamia lukecor.”" 
Luke5:5 Koboŋok Simon kotema atiar, “Ejakait, kipou ketaaritos akuare kiya, komam kidumuni idiobore: konye kanuka akonikirot, acakakini bo iboyan.”" 
Luke5:6 Kedaut aswam ŋun, kipokata iboro lukecor luipu noi: kokotosi ikeceboyan aŋed;" 
Luke5:7 kokwetut lukaupakec lukejaas ataker ace aponare aiŋarakin kes. Kopotu, kisilelebata atakerin kere aarei kiton neebuciata alumor." 
Luke5:8 Konye keanyu Simon Petero ŋun, kibirokin kwap akuŋin nuka Yesu, kobala ebe, “Wu Ejakait, kinyeinai, naarai arai eoŋ ekadiakanaran.”" 
Luke5:9 Naarai koumok ŋesi, ka ŋul kere lukejaas kaŋes, kanuka aipues naka lukecor lukikamunete:" 
Luke5:10 koumokis da Yakob ka Yokana, odwe luka Sebedayo, lukemoranara ka Simon. Kotema Yesu Simon atiar, “Sirikikurianar; amear natikwana iraun ekalokan ituŋa.”" 
Luke5:11 Nakedauniata aitodokun atakerinikec oitolima, kinyeis kere, kotupasi ŋes." 
Luke5:12 Kosodi kanen, nakejaar ore ediopet, kojai etuŋanan loelelebikina atapon: nakeanyunia ŋesi Yesu, kibirokin kwap ebuburia, kiŋaiŋa kotema atiar, “Ejakait, arai ikoto, ipedori aiswagar eoŋ.”" 
Luke5:13 Korio Yesu akekan, kotiro ŋes, kotema atiar, “Akoto; kiswagar.” Atipet konyou atapon kamakeŋ." 
Luke5:14 Kicor ŋes sirikelimoki idiotuŋanan; konye ebe, “Kolot, kitodiar mama ejai esasedoti, koinak kanuka aiswagariokon kwape kolo kicorakinitor Musa, araun aitejenunet kamakec.”" 
Luke5:15 Konye kiyatakinos akekiro aisiarar: kotukonokinos ikodeta luipu akiirar, ido aitaŋaleunio adekesiakec." 
Luke5:16 Konye ŋes kogitar kolot amodiŋ, kilip." 
Luke5:17 Kosodi kanen kapaaran adiopet kaŋun, isisianakini ŋesi: ido kiboiete Iparisayon ka ikesisianakinak luka ikisila kanen, lukepote koreria kere luko Galilaya ka Yudaya ka Yerusalem: kojai agogoŋ naka Ejakait kaŋes aitaŋaleun." 
Luke5:18 Ido koany, kibwokut ituŋa etuŋanan loesenyit koitada: kokotos aitolomar ŋes toma, ka aibwaikin akonyeneke," 
Luke5:19 Nakekurwosi aitolomar kanuka ekodet, kodokasi kuju oswi, kijoliliut ŋes aitorunio ametegulan koitadake kokidiŋ, akonyen nuka Yesu," 
Luke5:20 Nakeanyunia ŋesi akeceiyuun kotema atiar, “Ijo ba, esionii akonidiakanareta.”" 
Luke5:21 Kogeut ikewadikak ka Iparisayon epeget kobalas ebe, “Tŋai bo lo loinera nukainyanakin Edeke? Iŋai bo epedori aisioni adiakanareta, dimarai Edeke bon?”" 
Luke5:22 Konye kojeni Yesu ekecepeget, koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo ipegatatar kotauonokus?" 
Luke5:23 Ani bo naepatana, atemar ebe, ‘Esionii akonidiakanareta,’ arai bo atemar ebe, ‘Konyou kolot?’" 
Luke5:24 Konye tetere ijenunete ebe ejai Okoku loka etuŋanan apedor kakwap aisioni adiakanareta,” (kolimok lokasenyan ebe,) “Katemari jo atiar, Konyou, kibwok ekoniitada, kolot orekon.”" 
Luke5:25 Atipet konyou kakonyenekec, kibwok akeperit, kolot oreke, itopoloorit Edeke." 
Luke5:26 Koumokis kere, kitopoloorito Edeke; kilelebunos akurian, kobalas ebe, “Kiany lolo nukaumokin.”" 
Luke5:27 Kokau kaŋun koloma, koany eketeleman esolo, ekekiror Lebi, iboie kaitelemis, kotema ŋes atiar, “Kotupunai.”" 
Luke5:28 Kinyek kere, konyoi: kotupa ŋes," 
Luke5:29 Kipoik Lebi ŋes epucit loepol koreke: kojau ekodet loepol laka iketelemak esolo ka ke lukemorete kakes," 
Luke5:30 Kirurumakis Iparisayon ka ikewadikakakec ikekesisiak kobalas ebe, “Kanukinyo inyamiata imasiata da nepepe ka iketelemak esolo ka ikadiakanarak da?”" 
Luke5:31 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Lukaŋaleok mam ipudas emurwon; dimarai lukadekak." 
Luke5:32 Mam abunit anyarit ikadolitok, dimarai ikadiakanarak tetere itoronikinos.”" 
Luke5:33 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Eluŋete ikesisiak luka Yokana irwan ipu, ka ailip; ikote nen da ikesisiak luka Iparisayon; konye lukon enyamete emasete da.”" 
Luke5:34 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Ipedorete kereka aituluŋ luenyaritai opucit loka eiterane, naejaatar keteran?" 
Luke5:35 Konye eponito apaarasia, nuedemarere eteran, eluŋete do kapaarasia kaŋun.”" 
Luke5:36 Kolimok kes awaragan, ebe, “Emamei yeneciluni atutubet kanapito nakitetet, ka adonyokin ŋes anapito namojoŋ; arai kikonaki nen eciluni nakitetet, atutubet da naecilunio kama kanakitetet, mam ecamanaros kanamoion." 
Luke5:37 Emamei da yenebukokini ebino loitet oriagin lukemukule lumoioŋ; arai kikonaki nen, ecili ebino loitet iriagin, ebukor ebino, imadiŋikinos iriagin da." 
Luke5:38 Konye ebukonokinio ebino loitet oriagin lukitetiak. 
Luke5:39 Kwabo emamei yenemasi ebino loikuniatai, yenekoto loitet; naarai ebala ebe, ‘Ejok loikuniatai.’ ”" 
Luke6:1 Kosodi kanen nakitoritor amanat apaaran nakasabato, kijejeata ikekesisiak aluŋuren nuka akima, koninata kakanin konyama." 
Luke6:2 Konye ice koParisayon kotemasi atiar, “Kanukinyo iswamaata yesi numam ibus kapaaran nakasabato?”" 
Luke6:3 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Mam isiomito na nakiswamai Daudi, nakeriebia eteŋei, ŋes ka ikepaup;" 
Luke6:4 kwape kelomaria togo loka Edeke, kolem imugatin luka aitodikin, konyam, koinak da ikepaup; lumam ibus ainyam dimarai isasedotin bonik?”" 
Luke6:5 Kotema kes atiar, “Okoku loka etuŋanan ŋes ejakait loka asabato.”" 
Luke6:6 Kosodi kanen, kanakasabato ace, koloma toma atukos kisisianak: kojai nen etuŋanan, lokewonit akekan nakoteten." 
Luke6:7 Kiteikinito ikewadikak ka Iparisayon, aanyun arai itaŋaleuni kapaaran nakasabato; tetere edumunete akirot nakiwosaet ŋes." 
Luke6:8 Konye kojeni akeceomisio; kolimok etuŋanan lokejai akan nakewonit ebe, “Konyou, kobwo kokidiŋ.” Konyou ŋesi kobwo." 
Luke6:9 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Keŋisit yes ebe, Ibus kereka aswam nuejok kapaaran nakasabato, arai bo aswam nueroko, aitaiar aijar arai bo amudiar?”" 
Luke6:10 Kosesen kes kere, kolimok je ebe, “Korio akonikan.” Kikonak nen: koŋaleu akekan," 
Luke6:11 Konye kilelebun kes anyunyura, kinerut bonik nuiswamakinete Yesu," 
Luke6:12 Kosodi kanen kapaarasia kaŋun, kolot oroŋat ailip; kilip Edeke akuare kiya," 
Luke6:13 Kiwala akwap, konyarau ikekesisiak; koseu itomon ka luarei kotomakec, luabu komaik ikiyakia;" 
Luke6:14 Simon, loamaikini Petero, ka Anderea onaceke, ka Yakob ka Yokana, ka Pilip ka Batolomayo," 
Luke6:15 ka Matayo ka Tomas, ka Yakob okoku loka Alupayo, ka Simon loenyaritai Selot," 
Luke6:16 ka Yuda okoku loka Yakob, ka Yuda Isikariot, lokebilakini ŋes ebotet." 
Luke6:17 Kikokorun nepepe kakes, kobwo kaibois kanaeriana, ka ekodet loepol loka ikekesisiak, ka ituŋa luipu noi lukepote koYudaya kere ka Yerusalem, ka ariri nakaŋolol nako Turo ka Sidon, lukepote akiirar ŋes, ka aitaŋaleunio akecedekesia:" 
Luke6:18 ŋul da lukiticanete imoyon lueroko aponi kitaŋaleunoi. 
Luke6:19 Kokotos lukokodet kere atiror ŋes; naarai kolom apedor kamakeŋ kitaŋaleu kes kere. 
Luke6:20 Kikeu akekonye kosesen ikekesisiak, kotema atiar, “Isirereŋitoi yes lukican; naarai ajakanut naka Edeke erai nakus," 
Luke6:21 “Isirereŋitoi yes lukiriebi eteŋei kwana; naarai imonikinos. “Isirereŋitoi yes luimonyete kwana: naarai ikieniete. 
Luke6:22 “Isirereŋitoi yes, nakiŋaruniata ituŋa, kigitarete yes, kimoromoroete, ecakarete ekusikiror bala ibore yenerono, kanuka Okoku loka etuŋanan," 
Luke6:23 Kolelakis ka eicur apaaran ŋin: naarai koany, epol ekusiropit kotoma akui: naarai kikonakis, lukapapaakec inabin kwaŋin." 
Luke6:24 “Konye itukwi yes lukabarak! Naarai idaut adumun akusiitaakario," 
Luke6:25 “Itukwi yes, luimonikinos kwana! Naarai ebuni eteŋei airieb yes. “Itukwi yes, luikienasi kwana! Naarai ipote aibworo ka aimony." 
Luke6:26 “Itukwi yes, lukiturete kwana kere! Naarai kikonakis lukapapaakec inabin lukeŋalak kwaŋin." 
Luke6:27 “Konye katemari yes luipupete atiar, Kominasi lukasurupokus, kikonakinete nuejok ŋul lukinaras yes," 
Luke6:28 kilipakis arereŋ ŋul lukilamete, kilipakis da ŋul lukireito yes." 
Luke6:29 Yenikibapi eitinyo, kibelok loce da; yenikidemari ekonilou, sirikimik ekaso da." 
Luke6:30 Koinak ŋinituŋanan kere yenikilipi; yenikidemari jo ikoniboro sirikiburau bobo. 
Luke6:31 Kwape ikototor ituŋa aikonakin yes, kikonakis yesi da kes kwape kwaŋin." 
Luke6:32 “Arai iminasi ŋul lukiminasi yes, kimalao kanuka inyo? Naarai ikadiakanarak da eminasi lueminasi kes." 
Luke6:33 Arai da iswamakinete nuejok ŋul lukiswamakinete yes nuejok, kimalao kanuka inyo? Naarai ikadiakanarak da iswamaete kwape kwaŋin," 
Luke6:34 Arai da iyuunete ŋul luimunos adumun kamakec, kimalao kanuka inyo? Ikadiakanarak da eyuunete ikadiakanarak tetere edumunete ŋupeŋul bobo." 
Luke6:35 Konye kominasi lukasurupokus, kiswamakisi nuejok, koyuut, komam ijuruŋuŋito; epol rwaru ekusiropit, iraunete yesi idwe luka Je kaloejai kuju kakuj: naarai esiana ŋesi mama kalumam imalaete ka lueroko da." 
Luke6:36 Koraas luketimok, kwape eraar Papakus loketimon." 
Luke6:37 “Siritubonokinete, yes da kinyeis atubokinio: sirisitelekanarete, yes da kinyeis aisitelekario; kisioniete, yes da kisionio;" 
Luke6:38 koinakisi, yes da kiinakinio; aitemis naejok, naicikakinitai, naijaŋijaŋitai, kiton abukonor, ŋin ŋes kiinakinete ituŋa atorobusiokus. Naarai aitemis naitemioto, ŋipeŋin kitemere yes da.”" 
Luke6:39 Kolimok kes awaragan ebe, “Epedori kereka emuduki aiŋarenikin emuduki? Mam ibirokinos kere iarei toma aipany?" 
Luke6:40 Mam ekesisian itelekari ekesisianakinanike, konye ŋinituŋanan yenituutooritai cut erianakinos ka ekesisianakinanike." 
Luke6:41 Aso kanukinyo isesenia igugut yenejai akoŋu naka onacekon, komam ipodo akitoi naejai akoŋukon kilopet?" 
Luke6:42 Arai ipedori biai alimokin onacekon ebe, ‘Onaceka, kinyek kalem igugut yeneiai akoŋukon’, komam iseseni akitoi naejai akoŋukon kilopet? Yenikesoswai ijo, kolem ber akitoi naejai akoŋukon, kosodi konyet asesen kotenan alemun igugut kakoŋu naka onacekon." 
Luke6:43 “Naarai emamei ekitoi loejok loerai araito nukaronok; karaida ekitoi loerono loerai araito nuejok. 
Luke6:44 Naarai ejenunio ŋolikitoi kanuka araitoke. Naarai kotoma okukwa mam ituŋa edeŋete itinin, karaida toma okodokodo aideŋ imusabibun." 
Luke6:45 Itolomuni ituŋanan yenejok nuejok kotoma kanuejok nuiŋadakinit otauke; ituŋanan da yenikaronon itolomuni nukaronok kotoma kanueroko nuiŋadakinit: naarai inera akeituk nuilapununos kotauke. 
Luke6:46 Kanukinyo kinyaritotor eoŋ ebe, ‘Ejakait, Ejakait,’ kwabo mam iswamaete nuabala eoŋ?" 
Luke6:47 Ŋinituŋanan kere yenebuni mamakaŋ, kiira da akakiro ka aswam kes, ketodikini yes kwape eputor:" 
Luke6:48 Eputos bala ekadukon etogo, loeboki kwap noi, epesikini apetetait atiida; naeleleunia akalel, naeretonokinotor akip nukecor togo ŋol, mam epedori aijaŋijaŋa: naarai edukitoi ejok." 
Luke6:49 Konye yenepupuni, komam iswamai, eputos bala lokeduki eketogo alup komamei apetetait; koretonokinos akip nukecor togo ŋol, atipet kibiror; kepol da atiyakinike.”" 
Luke7:1 Nakedaunia akekiro kere kopupete ituŋa, koloma Kaparanaum," 
Luke7:2 Keiai ekapolokiton-erioŋet ekebulesit lokemina noi, lokedeka eapikinit airidakin," 
Luke7:3 Nakiiraria ŋol eemut loka Yesu, kiyakia imakio luka Iyudayan ailip ŋes abunore aitaŋaleun ekebulesit." 
Luke7:4 Nakedolioto kesi mama ejai Yesu, kiŋaiŋaata noi, kobalas ebe, “Ibus ŋesi, kiswamaki nu:" 
Luke7:5 naarai emin awokoteker, kidukok sio akositukos.”" 
Luke7:6 Kouparos Yesu kakes, Nakeapikinia etogoke, kiyakik ekapolokiton ikepapero kotema atiar, “Ejakait, sirikitaar: naarai mam eoŋ kebusakinit jo alomun kwap kekaswi." 
Luke7:7 Ŋes mam aomitor aibusakin abunore mamakon: konye kolim akirot bon, eŋaleuni ekatelepat." 
Luke7:8 Naarai eoŋ da arai etuŋanan lokayaitai, ejaas iserikalei luayait eoŋ: ido alimokini ediopet ebe, ‘Kolot’, elosi; ece da ebe, ‘Bia,’ ebuni; ekabulesit da ebe, ‘Kiswama na,’ ido iswamai.”" 
Luke7:9 Nakiiraria Yesu akiro ŋun, koumok kanukeŋ, kibelokin kolimok ekodet loketupit ŋes ebe, “Katemari yes atiar, Mam lem adumunit aiyuun naepol naetia na, karaida toma Isirael kere.”" 
Luke7:10 Nakeboŋoriata lueyakunitai ore, kodumut ebulesit keŋaleu." 
Luke7:11 Kosodi kanen ketubor apak naedit kolot ore loenyaritai Nain, koupas ikekesisiak kaŋes ka ekodet loepol." 
Luke7:12 Nakeapiaria orute loka ere, koany, kibwokunitai lokatwan kiŋa, lokerai loteluna, totoke da kerai apuserut: kejaas ituŋa luipu lukore nenipe kaŋes." 
Luke7:13 Nakeanyunia Ejakait ŋin kitim, kotema ŋes atiar, “Sirikimony.”" 
Luke7:14 Kikunyak kotiro ekirigi lokibwokitere, kobwout lukibwokito. Kotema atiar, “Etelepat, katemari jo atiar, Konyou.”" 
Luke7:15 Kiboikin lokatwan kogeu einer. Koinak ŋes totoke," 
Luke7:16 Kokuriakaros kere; kitopoloosi Edeke, kobalas ebe, “Atakanu cama enabi lokapolon kamawok!” ebe da, “Aanyana Edeke iketuŋol”" 
Luke7:17 Kisiarakinos akiro ŋun toma Yudaya kere, ka akwap kere naidunyatar." 
Luke7:18 Apotu ikesisiak luka Yokana kolimokis ŋes akiro ŋun kere. 
Luke7:19 Kenyarau Yokana iarei kokesisiakake kiyakia mama ejai Ejakait, iŋisit ebe, “Irai kereka ijo ŋol loebunit, arai bo kedarata ece?”" 
Luke7:20 Nakedolioto ituŋa mamakeŋ, kobalas ebe, “Kijukunit Yokana Lokebatisan sio mamakon iŋisit ebe, ‘Irai kereka ijo ŋol Iocbunit, arai bo kedarata ece?’ ”" 
Luke7:21 Kosawa kaŋol kitaŋaleu luipu akecedekesia, ka ican ka imoyon lueroko; koinak imudukiok luipu aanyun." 
Luke7:22 Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Koloto, kolimokis Yokana ŋun nuianyut ka nuiirarito da; ekwenyunete imudukiok, elosete iŋwalasik, iswagio lukatapon, epupete ikimiŋiok, itajario lukatwak, elimonokinio da lukican akiro nukajokak." 
Luke7:23 Isirereŋitoi da ŋol lomam itiguikin kanukaŋ.” 
Luke7:24 Kosodi kedaut ikiyakia luka Yokana alosit, kogeu alimokin ikodeta nuka Yokana ebe, “Kilomarete alosit amodiŋ aanyun inyo? Egada lokijaŋijaŋ! ekwam?" 
Luke7:25 Konye bo kilomarete asesen inyo? Etuŋanan lokenapit anapito naanebek? Koany, luisiritoi kaluibusak, luenyamete da luetaitaete, ejaas toma alaroi nuka ikabakan." 
Luke7:26 Konye kilomarete asesen inyo? Enabi? Eebo, katemari yes atiar, loitelekarit enabi." 
Luke7:27 Ŋol ŋes iwadikatere nu ebe, ‘Koany, ejukari ekakiyakia kakonyenekon, Loitemonokini ekonirot kakonyenekon.’" 
Luke7:28 Katemari yes atiar, Kotoma lukeuriete aŋor emamei yenepol aitelekarit Yokana: konye loedit kotoma ajakanut naka Edeke ŋes epol aitelekarit ŋes.”" 
Luke7:29 (Nakiirariata ituŋa kere, ka iketelemak esolo da, kitogogoŋoto adolit naka Edeke, naarai kibatisauna kaibatisa naka Yokana." 
Luke7:30 Konye koŋeroto Iparisayon ka iricakisila ainerun naka Edeke, naarai mam apotu kibatisaunos kamakeŋ.)" 
Luke7:31 “Aso do etupusi kinyo ituŋa luka atur kana, eputosi kesi kinyo?" 
Luke7:32 Eputosi kidwe luiboiete kagwelanaret, konyaras, kobalas ebe, ‘Kikut alamarun, mam yes esoma; Kibwolol, mam yes emonya.’" 
Luke7:33 Naarai kobu Yokana Lokebatisan komam enyami karaida aimat ebino; ibalasi yesi ebe, ‘Ejai ajokit’." 
Luke7:34 Kobu Okoku loka etuŋanan enyami emasi da; ibalasi yesi ebe, ‘Koany, ekeraŋat lo, ekameran da, epapero loka iketelemak esolo ka ikadiakanarak!’" 
Luke7:35 Konye ikedwe kere kes itojokere Acoa.” 
Luke7:36 Kosodi konyara ediopet koParisayon Yesu aimor kaŋes. Koloma togo loka Eparisayot, kiboikin ainyam." 
Luke7:37 Ido koany, kepupu aberu nakore kaŋol, nakerai nakadiakanaran ebe eboikin togo loka Eparisayot ainyam, koyau ekube loka akinyet;" 
Luke7:38 kobwo kokauke koapie kakejeke, emonyi, kogeu aitodoonokin akiyo akejeke, koninana kitima luka akouke, konu akejeke, kinyonyoanak akinyet." 
Luke7:39 Keanyu Eparisayot lokenyararit, kotema kotauke atiar, “Arai kerai etuŋanan lo enabi, tikejenu aberu ŋin erai iŋai, ido nakepone enyoin, naetironori ŋes, naarai erai nakadiakanaran.”" 
Luke7:40 Koboŋok Yesu kotema atiar, “Simon, ejai akirot naakoto alimokin jo.” Kotema atiar, “Aso, Ekesisianakinan, kiner.”" 
Luke7:41 Kotema atiar, “Kejaas etuŋanan kalukapesen iarei; kiburai ediopet adenarin akwat akany, lokiareit da akaisakany." 
Luke7:42 Amameete kes nutacet, abu kitim kes kere iarei. Kotoma kes luarei, iŋai bo eminuni ŋes aitelekarit?”" 
Luke7:43 Koboŋok Simon ebe, “Aomit ebe je lokisionio nuipu.” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Itub kotenan.”" 
Luke7:44 Kibelokin mama ejai aberu kotema ŋesi Simon atiar, “Iany ijo aberu na? Alom eoŋ togokon, mam jo einakina akipi nuka akejeka, konye na etodoonoki akiyo akejeka ka anina da kitimake." 
Luke7:45 Mam jo ibu konu eoŋ, konye ameun napenan alomunia mam na inyeina ainu noi akakeje." 
Luke7:46 Mam jo ibu kinyonyo akinyet akouka, konye na enyonyo akinyet akejeka," 
Luke7:47 Kanuka ŋun katemari jo atiar, Isionio akediakanareta nuipu, naarai epol akemin; konye yenisionio nuikidioko, edit akemin.”" 
Luke7:48 Kotema ŋesi ŋin atiar, “Esionii akonidiakanareta.”" 
Luke7:49 Kosodete kogeutu lukemorete kaŋes atemanar atiar, “Iŋai ca lo, loisioniei adiakanareta?”" 
Luke7:50 Kotema ŋesi aberu atiar, “Kitajar jo akoniiyuun; kolot inapakina.”" 
Luke8:1 Kosodi kanen ketubor apak naedit, kimaniman ireria kere lukapolok ka luedisiak, elimonokini ka alimor akiro nukajokak nuka ajakanut naka Edeke, kojaas nenipe ka lutomon kaarei," 
Luke8:2 ka aŋor ace nukitaŋaleunitai imoyon lueroko ka adekesia, Mariam naenyaritai Magadalene, nakelomunete ajokin akanykaarei," 
Luke8:3 ka Yoana aberu naka Kusa ekeŋadan loka Kerode, ka Susana, ka ace nuipu nukijaanakinete kiborokec lukejaatar." 
Luke8:4 Naketukokinor ekodet loepol, kopotu da lukepote kaŋolire mamakeŋ, kiner kawaragan atiar," 
Luke8:5 “Abu ekayean koloma aiye ikekinyom; napeyei, kodooto ice ariri kerot; kicakacakai, konyama ikweny luka apak." 
Luke8:6 Kodooto ice aŋaŋam; nakegeuniata abwaŋun, kooko, kanuemameatar akip." 
Luke8:7 Kodooto ice okukwa; kopolooto ikukwa kakes, koridakis," 
Luke8:8 Kodooto ice alup nuejok, kopolooros, koraata araito kiton akwatat.” Nakinerar akiro ŋun, kiworo ebe, “Yenejaas aki nuka akiirar, kiira.”" 
Luke8:9 Kiŋita ŋes ikekesisiak ebe inyo bo apolou kawaragan kaŋin," 
Luke8:10 Kotema atiar, “Kiinakinitai yes ajenun nukaiyeiyea nuka ajakanut naka Edeke; konye ice kawaragasia; tetere eanyunete komam eanyunete, ido iirarete komam ejenunete," 
Luke8:11 Aso apolou naka awaragan ŋes nata: Ekinyomit ŋes akirot naka Edeke. 
Luke8:12 Kwi da lukariri kerot kes lukiirarete; kosodi ebuni Satan, alemar akirot kotauonokec, tetere mam iyuunete ka aitajario da." 
Luke8:13 Kwi da lukaŋaŋam kes lukiirarete kocamut akirot kailel; konye komameete alias, iyuunete nediokasilon, kosodete kapak naka acodunio etiakaros," 
Luke8:14 Kwi da lukedoete okukwa, kes lukiirarete, ido kelototo koridakinos aiyaloŋoŋ, ka abar, ka aiyalama naka aijar, komam ititionete adioraito," 
Luke8:15 Kwi da luka alup nuejok, kes luka itauon luitenara luejok lukiirarete akirot, koricito, koraata araito katitiŋikin," 
Luke8:16 “Emamei ituŋanan yeninokokini atala, kobuburik ibore, arai aibwaikin kwap keitada; konye ibwaikini kuju ocoget, tetere epedorete luelomunete aanyun akeija." 
Luke8:17 Naarai emamei akirot naibwaitai, namam ikujunio, karaida naimunonitai namam ejenunio ka aikujunio." 
Luke8:18 Aso kocoito kwape ipupioto; naarai yenejai ibore, einakinio ice; ka yenemamei ibore, edemunio ŋin da yeneomit ŋesi ebe ejaatar.”" 
Luke8:19 Kopotu do totoke ka ikeinacan, mam apedorete aikunyakin ŋes kanuka ekodet." 
Luke8:20 Kolimokinai ebe, “Ebwoete totokon ka ikoniinacan kokiŋa; ekotosi aanyun jo.”" 
Luke8:21 Konye Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Totoka ka ikainacan kes ŋul luiirarete akirot naka Edeke, kiswamata da.”" 
Luke8:22 Kosodi kanen adiopet kapaarasia kaŋun, kodoka ataker, ŋes ka ikekesisiak; kotema kes atiar, “Aso kekwaŋaros aŋolol juwai”; kogeut alosit." 
Luke8:23 Konye napikwaŋasi kojotoor ŋesi, kokut ekwam loepol kaŋolol; kogeut akipi ailelebun ataker, kojaut toma ationis." 
Luke8:24 Koloto mama ejai kitwekenyut, kobalas ebe, “Ekapolon, ekapolon ba, kitwaka.” Kokweny ŋesi, kiretak ekwam ka agat naka akipi: kopalasi kojaun aiyamakin." 
Luke8:25 Kotema kes atiar, “Ani bo aiyuunikus?” Kokuriakata, koumokis, kotemanaros atiar, “Aso iŋai bo lo, naarai icorakini kiton ikwamin ka akipi da, korimarete?”" 
Luke8:26 Kodolot akwap naka Igerasenin, naetereikina Galilaya," 
Luke8:27 Nakedokunia koitolima, kiriamunos ketuŋanan loka ore kaŋol lokejaas ajokin; apak naepol mam anapit inapen, mam abu kosal togo, konye toma atesin," 
Luke8:28 Nakeanyunia ŋol Yesu, kilala, kibirokin kakonyeneke, kiner keporoto loepol ebe, “Anyoika eoŋ kajo, Yesu, Osoku loka Edeke loejai kuju kakuj? Keŋaiŋait, sirikiitican eoŋ.”" 
Luke8:29 Naarai abu kicorak emoyo loerono alomun kotuŋanan. (Naarai kikamununei ŋes irwan ipu; kidareneno, koenen kirikoi ka iloin; koŋedeŋedei lukeenitere; kokerianara ŋes ajokit amodiŋ.)" 
Luke8:30 Kiŋit Yesu ŋes ebe, “Ekonikiror iŋai?” Kobala ebe, “Ajore,” naarai kelomakinitos ŋes ajokin nuipu." 
Luke8:31 Kiŋaiŋaata ŋes sirikicorak kes alomar aipany. 
Luke8:32 Kejai nen esipan loka ipegei luipu edakasi oroŋat; kiŋaiŋaata ŋes acamakin kes alomar opegei. Kocamak kes," 
Luke8:33 Kolomut ajokin kotuŋanan, kolomasi toma opegei: komotar esipan kaneijululuei, kibirokin aŋolol, kotwakikis akipi." 
Luke8:34 Nakeanyuniata ikecokok nuadoikis, kokerata, kisiarakis akiro toma ore kamanat da." 
Luke8:35 Koloto aanyun nuadoikis; kopotu mama ejai Yesu, kodumut etuŋanan lokelomunete ajokin, iboie kakejen nuka Yesu, enapit igoen, kejokiar adam; kokuriakaros." 
Luke8:36 Ŋul da luapotu koanyut kitejenut kes kwape kitaŋaleunere ŋol lolem ajaas ajokin," 
Luke8:37 Kosodete ituŋa kere luka akwap naka Igerasenin airiamar kilipa ŋes anyoun kamakec; naarai kikam kes akurian naepol; kodoka ataker, koboŋo." 
Luke8:38 Konye kilip etuŋanan lokelomunete ajokin aup kaŋes; konye kotwar, kobala ebe," 
Luke8:39 “Koboŋo orekon, kolimonok nukapolok nukiswamak jo Edeke.” Kolot, kolimonok anatar ere kere nukapolok nukiswamakini ŋes Yesu." 
Luke8:40 Kosodi nakeboŋunio Yesu, kisukunyik ekodet ŋes kaiyalama; naarai kidaritos ŋes kere." 
Luke8:41 Ido koany, kobu etuŋanan ekekiror Yairo, lokerai ekayaiton loka atukos; kibirokin akejen nuka Yesu, kiŋaiŋa ŋes alomar togoke;" 
Luke8:42 Naarai kejai ŋes apese nateluna, naka ikar itomon ka luarei, keapikinit atwanare. Konye napelosi koridakis ikodeta," 
Luke8:43 Kosodi aberu nakedeka alele nakaokot ikar itomon ka luarei, naketacakinit imurwok lukejaatar kere, komam epedori ituŋanan aitaŋaleun," 
Luke8:44 komanu kokauke, kotiro atwele naka anapitoke; atipet kosaŋ alele nakaokotoke." 
Luke8:45 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Iŋai bo katiro?” Kosodete nakeŋerioto ituŋa kere, kobala Petero ebe, “Ekapolon, kilukut jo ikodeta kiridakis da!”" 
Luke8:46 Konye kotema Yesu atiar, “Katiro ma ituŋanan: naarai amisiik ebe alom apedor kamakaŋ.”" 
Luke8:47 Nakeanyunia aberu ebe mam epedori aibwaio, kobu emarani, kibirokin akonyeneke, kitejenu kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere akiro nukeinakinete ŋes atiror, ido kwape kitaŋaleunere atipet." 
Luke8:48 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Akokuka, kitaŋaleu jo akoniiyuun; kolot inapakina.”" 
Luke8:49 Napinera ŋun, kobu etuŋanan kore loka ekayaiton loka atukos, kobala ebe, “Adaun akoonipese; sirikitaar bobo Ekesisianakinan.”" 
Luke8:50 Konye nakiiraria Yesu ŋun koboŋok ebe, “Sirikikurianar; konye kiyuu aiyuun, itaiario.”" 
Luke8:51 Nakedolio togo, mam abu kisunup ituŋanan alomar nepepe kaŋes, dimarai Petero, ka Yokana, ka Yakob, ka papa loka ikoku ka totoke." 
Luke8:52 Emonyete kere kibworos; konye kotema atiar, “Sirikimonya; naarai mam etwanit, konye ejotoi.”" 
Luke8:53 Kokienatar ŋes noi, naarai kejenete ebe adau ikoku atwanare." 
Luke8:54 Konye kitiŋ akekan, kiworo ebe, “Ipese, kokweny.”" 
Luke8:55 Koboŋu ekemoyo, atipet konyou; kicorak ainakin ŋes inyamat," 
Luke8:56 Koumokis ikekauriak; konye kicor kes kinyeis alimokin ituŋanan nukiswamao. 
Luke9:1 Konyarau lutomon ka luarei nepepe, koinak apedor ka apolou kama ejaas ajokin kere, ka aitaŋaleun adekesia." 
Luke9:2 Kiyakia kes alimonokin ajakanut naka Edeke, ka aitaŋaleun da lukadekak," 
Luke9:3 Kotema kes atiar, “Sirikiyaŋaasi ibore kere yenikerot, karaida ebela, karaida ecoe, karaida inyamat, karaida apesan, karaida ajaut kikason iarei." 
Luke9:4 Kaŋolitogo loilomanarete, kosalenenete nen, aitodol nainyounioto alosit." 
Luke9:5 Ŋul lumam kisukunyikinete yes, nainyounioto kotoma ore kaŋol, kilakilakenenete adae nuka akejenekus araut akajenak kamakec.”" 
Luke9:6 Koloto kesi, kiriamas ireria, elimonokinete Akiro Nukajokak, ka aitaŋaleun da kaŋiniibois." 
Luke9:7 Kosodi kiira ekabaka Kerode nukiswamao kere; kiyaloŋoŋ noi, naarai kebalas ituŋa ice ebe, ajaru Yokana kotoma okatwak;" 
Luke9:8 ka ice da ebe, “Atakanu Eliya”; ka ice da ebe, “Ajaru ediopet kotoma onabin lukolo sek.”" 
Luke9:9 Kobala Kerode ebe, “Abu kajepa akou naka Yokana; konye iŋai bo lo loapupi eoŋ akiro nuetia nen?” Kokoto aanyun ŋes." 
Luke9:10 Kosodi keboŋut ikiyakia kitejenut Yesu akiro kere nuapotu kiswamata, Koyaŋa kes, kogita kiton ore loenyaritai Betesaida." 
Luke9:11 Konye nakejenuniata ikodeta kotupasi ŋes; kisukunyik kes kaiyalama kolimok kes nuka ajakanut naka Edeke, kitaŋaleu da lukipudas aitaŋaleunio," 
Luke9:12 Kejotaki akoloŋ; kopotu lutomon kaarei mama ejai, kotemasi atiar, “Kotwar ekodet, tetere elosete toma oreria ka amanat da nuidunyatar, kodumutu neeperete ka inyamat da; naarai kijaa ne amodiŋ.”" 
Luke9:13 Konye kotema kes atiar, “Koinakisi yesi kes lunyaman.” Kotemasi atiar, “Emamei sio ibore yenedeparit imugatin ikany ka agaria aarei; arai mam kilosit agwelakin etuŋat lo kere inyamat.”" 
Luke9:14 Naarai emwaasi ikiliok bala ilukumin ikany. Kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Kisiboikis kes katukon bala akaisakany ŋinitukot.”" 
Luke9:15 Kiswamata kwaŋin, kisiboikis kes kere." 
Luke9:16 Kolem imugatin lukany, ka agaria aarei, kosesen akuj, kisirereŋ kes, kobilibil; koinak ikesisiak akoranakin ekodet." 
Luke9:17 Konyama, kimonikinos kere; kotukonokinai atutubeta nuabilibila nukesalete, iditai itomon ka luarei." 
Luke9:18 Kosodi kanen, napilipi ŋesi kogitara, kojaas ikekesisiak nenipe kaŋes: kiŋit kes ebe, “Ebalas ikodeta ebe arai eoŋ iŋai?”" 
Luke9:19 Koboŋokis ebe, “Yokana Lokebatisan; konye ice Eliya; ice da ebe ajaru ediopet konabin lukolo sek.”" 
Luke9:20 Kotema kes atiar, “Ido bo yes kibalas ebe arai eoŋ iŋai?” Koboŋok Petero ebe, “Ijoŋ Kristo loka Edeke.”" 
Luke9:21 Konye kicor kes, kisimik alimokin idiotuŋanan akirot ŋin." 
Luke9:22 Kobala ebe, “Ibusakinit Okoku loka etuŋanan aiticanio nuipu, egirete da imakio ka isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak, ka aiar, kapaaran da nakiwuniet ejaruni.”" 
Luke9:23 Kolimok kes kere ebe, “Arai ekoto ituŋanan aitup eoŋ, koŋerokin ilopet, korioŋ ekemusalaba ŋinipaaran, katup eoŋ." 
Luke9:24 Naarai ŋin yenekoto aitaiar akeijar etwaniari; konye ŋin yenetwaniari akeijar kanukaŋ, itajari ŋes," 
Luke9:25 Naarai ajokis anyoin arai kedumu ituŋanan akwapin kere, kitoolio arai kotwania akeijar?" 
Luke9:26 Naarai yenirumete ileic kanukaŋ, kanuka akakiro da, irumete ileic Okoku loka etuŋanan da kanukeŋ, naebunio kaibusesuke, ka naka Papa, ka naka imalaikan da lukalaunak." 
Luke9:27 Konye abeit katemari yes atiar, Ejaas ice kaluebwoete kane lumam iirete cut atwanare aitodol neaanyuniata ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Luke9:28 Kosodi kanen akaulo kakiro kaŋun bala apaarasia akanykauni, koyaŋa Petero ka Yokana ka Yakobo, kodoka oroŋat ailip." 
Luke9:29 Napilipi, kogelakin epone loke ereeteke, kiliacanata ikenapen komwekimwekete," 
Luke9:30 Ido koany, kineras ituŋa iarei kaŋes, lukeraas Musa ka Eliya;" 
Luke9:31 luketakanete kaibuses, kineras akiro nuka atwanareke naelosi ŋesi aitodolikin koYerusalem." 
Luke9:32 Kilurunito Petero ka lukejaas kaŋes ajo; konye nakekwenyuniata koanyutu aibusesuke, ka kwi da iarei lukebwoete kaŋes," 
Luke9:33 Kosodi kanen, napetiakas kaŋes, kotema Petero Yesu atiar, “Ekapolon, ejok oni ajaut ne; aso keswamata iswamin iuni; ediopet lokon, ediopet loka Musa, ka ediopet da loka Eliya.” Komam ejeŋi nukinera." 
Luke9:34 Napinera ŋesi ŋun, kobu edou, kiteribo kes; kokuriakaros nakelomariata odou." 
Luke9:35 Kolom eporoto kotoma odou, kobala ebe, “Lo ŋes Okokuka, loseunaka; kiirasi ŋes.”" 
Luke9:36 Napinera eporoto ŋol, kotakan Yesu bon. Kililiŋata kesi, komam elimokinete idiotuŋanan kapaarasia kaŋun adiokirot kanuaanyut." 
Luke9:37 Kosodi kanen apaaran naatupakini nakedokuniata koroŋat, kiriamunos kekodet loepol." 
Luke9:38 Ido koany, kiworo etuŋanan kotoma okodet ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, keŋaiŋait, koany ikakoku; naarai erai ikateluna;" 
Luke9:39 Ido koany, ikamununei ajokit ŋes, atipet isilalai; bobo da kisiilio, kokui ekuetete, mam inyeini dimarai kationis, idecideci ŋes," 
Luke9:40 eŋaiŋa ikonikesisiak aireŋear ŋes, konye mam epedoro.”" 
Luke9:41 Koboŋok Yesu kotema atiar, “Wu okwe yes atur namam iyuunit, naepaarit, etodoli eoŋ ai ajaut kayes, ka atitiŋikinit da yes? Koyau ma ikonikoku ne.”" 
Luke9:42 Napebuni kibirok ajokit kwap, kisiilio. Kiretak Yesu ajokit naerono, kitaŋaleu isapat kinyakak papake." 
Luke9:43 Koumokis kere apolou naka Edeke. Konye napeumokinitos kere akiro kere nueswamai, kotema ŋesi ikekesisiak atiar," 
Luke9:44 “Kitolomasi akiro nu akiikus; naarai einakinio Okoku loka etuŋanan akanin nuka ituŋa.” 
Luke9:45 Konye mam kes apotu kojenut akirot ŋin, kimunonitai kamakec, kinyeis amisiikin; koyoŋata aiŋit apolou naka akirot kaŋin." 
Luke9:46 Kogeut epeget kotomakec ebe iŋai bo kakesi eraun lokapolon. 
Luke9:47 Konye kejen Yesu epeget loka itauonokec, koyau ikoku yenididi, kisibwo kodieke," 
Luke9:48 kotema kes atiar, “Ŋin yenisukunyikini ikoku yen kokirorika kesukunyikinit eoŋ, ŋin da yenikesukunyikini eoŋ, isukunyikinit ŋol lokejukuni; naarai loerai loedit kokidiŋikus kere, ŋol ŋes erai lokapolon.”" 
Luke9:49 Koboŋok Yokana kotema atiar, “Ekapolon, kipou kaanyutu etuŋanan ireŋeari ajokin kokirorikon, kesimika ŋes, naarai mam kiupa kaoni.”" 
Luke9:50 Konye Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Sirikisimika; naarai ŋol lomam erai lokasurupikus, erai lokowaikus.”" 
Luke9:51 Kosodi kanen, keapuut apaarasiake nuka aitodokario, kitogogoŋ akonyeneke alosit Yerusalem." 
Luke9:52 Kijuka ikiyakia aliŋakin ŋes, koloto kolomasi ore loka Isamarian tetere itemokinete kanukeŋ;" 
Luke9:53 konye mam kes apotu kisukunyikis, naarai atereit akekonyen aibe Yerusalem." 
Luke9:54 Keanyut ikekesisiak Yakob ka Yokana ŋun, kobalas ebe, “Ejakait, ikoto kecorakis akim kodoku kokuju komudia kes [kwape kolo eswamaa Eliya]?”" 
Luke9:55 Konye kibelokin, kitoron kes, [kotema atiar, “Mam ijenete epone loka emoyo loejai kayes. Naarai mam abunit Okoku loka etuŋanan amudiar aijar naka ituŋa, dimarai aitaiar.”]" 
Luke9:56 Koloto ore ece. 
Luke9:57 Napelosete kesi korot, kotema etuŋanan atiar, “Katupenenei jo kama ilosi kere.”" 
Luke9:58 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Ejaas ikuwei apanya, akweny da nuka apak ejaas akaisikec; konye Okoku loka etuŋanan emamei nama iperikini akekou.”" 
Luke9:59 Kotema ŋesi ece atiar, “Kotupunai.” Konye kobala ebe, “Ejakait, kisiikinai ber kalot keda papaka.”" 
Luke9:60 Konye kotema ŋes atiar, “Kinye lukatwak kidaata lukarwakakec; konye jo, kolot kolimono ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Luke9:61 Kobala ece da ebe, “Ejakait, katupenenei jo; konye kisiikinai ber katwar ituŋa lukokaleka.”" 
Luke9:62 Konye Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Emamei yenetiŋit emeleku lokimoŋin, kosesen kau, yenibusakinit ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Luke10:1 Kosodi kokau kaŋun koseu Ejakait ice akaisakanykaarei, kiyakia kes iarei iarei aiŋarenikin ŋes alosit ŋolire ka ŋiniibois naekoto ŋesi elopet alosit." 
Luke10:2 Kotema kes atiar, “Ipu idwenyan, konye ikidioko ikeswamak; aso kilipa Ejakait loka aidweny kijuk ikeswamak toma aidwenyeke." 
Luke10:3 Koloto yesi; koany, keyakiari yes kwape idwe luka amerekekin kokidiŋ opeen." 
Luke10:4 Sirikiyata eriagi, karaida ecoe, karaida amuk; sirikiyogata da ituŋanan korot." 
Luke10:5 Ido ŋolitogo loilomanarete, kotemasi ber atiar, ‘Kojau ainapakin togo lo!’" 
Luke10:6 Arai kejaun okoku loka ainapakin kanen, esalakini ŋes ainapakinikus; arai mam, kiboŋokini yes ainapakinikus." 
Luke10:7 Kosalata ber togo ŋopeŋol, inyamete komasete lukiinakinete yes, naarai edolit ekeswaman aropio; siribwosenenete otogoi ice." 
Luke10:8 Ido ŋolire kere loilomanarete kiisukunyikis, konyamata inyamat lukiinakinete yes;" 
Luke10:9 kitaŋaleununete lukadekak luejaas nen, kolimonokinete ebe, ‘Ekunyu ajakanut naka Edeke mamakus.’" 
Luke10:10 Konye ere kere loilomanarete, arai mam kisukunyikinete, kolomutu orotinike, kineras ebe," 
Luke10:11 Kilakilakanakini yes adae nukakejenekosi; konye kojenutu na ebe, ‘Ekunyu ajakanut naka Edeke mamakus.’" 
Luke10:12 Katemari yes atiar, Kapaaran kaya, epatana Sodom atitiŋikin aitelekarit ere ŋol." 
Luke10:13 “Itukwi ijo Korasin! Itukwi ijo Betesaida Naarai arai kiswamatai koTuro ka Sidon nukapedor ŋun nukiswamatai kamakus, tikitoronikinos ŋosek, kibojete kopukoi ka ekurwon." 
Luke10:14 Konye apaaran naka etube epatanikini Turo ka Sidon atitiŋikin aitelekarit yes. 
Luke10:15 Ka jo da Kaparanaum, kitopoloorio kereka kiton akuj? Kijesario do kiton Okatwak." 
Luke10:16 “Yenikiirari yes, keirari eoŋ; yenikipaluni yes, kapaluni eoŋ da; yenikapaluni eoŋ epaluni lokejukuni.”" 
Luke10:17 Kosodete koboŋut kwi akaisakanykaarei kaiyalama, kobalas ebe, “Ejakait, kononokikis sio ajokin da kokirorikon!”" 
Luke10:18 Kotema kes atiar, “Aany Satan ibiruni kokuiu kwape keimilia," 
Luke10:19 Koany, kainakinit yes apedor aicakacak imunwo ka ikiritona, ido kama ejai apedor kere naka lokasurup; emamei da ibore kere yenikikonakini yes erono." 
Luke10:20 Konye sirikiyalamikinos kanu kinonokikiniata yes ajokin; konye kiyalamikinos naarai iwadikatai ikusikiroria kotoma akuj.” 
Luke10:21 Kosawa kaŋol kolakar kOmoyo Lokalaunan, kotema atiar, “Kemalai jo, wu Papa, Ejakait loka akuj ka akwap, naarai ibu kimunonik akiro nu lukacoa ka lukaijen, kopukok da idwe ludidik; eebo, Papa, naarai kwaŋin ibu kitojokia kakonyenekon."
