Luke10:22 Kainak Papaka iboro kere; ido emamei yenejeni Okoku dimarai Papa, kwabo emamei yenejeni Papa dimarai Okoku, ka ŋin da yenekot Okoku apukokin ŋes.”" 
Luke10:23 Kosodi kibelokin mama ejaas ikekesisiak, kiner kakes kaiyeiyea ebe, “Isirereŋitoi akonye nuesesenete nuisesenete yesi." 
Luke10:24 Naarai katemari yes atiar, ‘Apotu kimielas inabin luipu ka ikabakan aanyun nuisesenete yesi, mam eanyuna, ka akiirar da nuiirarete yesi, mam iirara.’ ”" 
Luke10:25 Ido koany, kobwo ericakisil ediopet kokodokod, kobala ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, ekonakini ai tetere erumi aijar naka ikar kere?”" 
Luke10:26 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Iwadikatai bo inyo toma okisila? Isiomi biai?”" 
Luke10:27 Koboŋok ŋes ebe, “Komina Ejakait Ekonideke kekonitau kere, ka akoniiiar kere, ka akonigogoŋ kere, ka akonicoa kere; ka ekoniidunyet da kwape iminari bon.”" 
Luke10:28 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Iboŋok kotenan; kikonaki nen, iiari.”" 
Luke10:29 Konye ŋes ekoto aitoiokikin, kiŋit Yesu ebe, “Iŋai bo ekaidunyet?”" 
Luke10:30 Koboŋok Yesu kobala ebe, “Abu etuŋanan kijesar anyoun koYerusalem alosit Yeriko, kiriamunos kikaŋatak, lukelacarete ŋes inapen, kibuŋata, koloto kinyeis eapie airidakin." 
Luke10:31 Kosodi kanen kitor esasedoti orot ŋol; nakeanyunia ŋes, kinac kotubor," 
Luke10:32 Elebit da kwape kwaŋin, nakedolio aibois ŋin, koany ŋes, kinac kotubor." 
Luke10:33 Konye Esamariat ediopet kalositeke, kedol nen nekejai; nakeanyunia, kitim ŋes," 
Luke10:34 kikunyak koen akemusuŋun, kobukok akinyet ka ebino; kibwanenik otiaŋake koyaŋa kiton togo laka ipejok, kimuke," 
Luke10:35 Apaaran nakiareit kolem adenarin aarei koinak elopet etogo, kobala ebe, ‘Kimuke lo; ibore kere yenitaci aitedepar, katacakini jo naaboŋunio.’" 
Luke10:36 Iŋai kaŋul kaluuni loiwomit ijo araut ekeidunyet kaje kalokiriamunos kikaŋatak” 
Luke10:37 Kotema atiar, “Ŋol lokitimi ŋes.” Kolimok Yesu ŋes ebe, “Kolot ijo da, kikonak nen.”" 
Luke10:38 Kosodete napebeete, koloma ore ediopet; kisukunyik aberu ekekiror Marita togoke," 
Luke10:39 Kejai ŋes kainacike naenyaritai Mariam, nakiboie kakejen nuka Yesu, iirari akekiro," 
Luke10:40 Konye abu Marita kitaaritoi kanuka aijaanakin naapol; kolot mama ejai Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, mam kereka ipodo ebe kenyeinia kinacika aijaanakin bon? Aso kolimok ŋes keŋarak eoŋ.”" 
Luke10:41 Konye Koboŋok Ejakait kotema atiar, “Marita, Marita, iyaloŋoŋoi ilolonyi da kanuka akiro nuipu;" 
Luke10:42 konye ipudai luikidioko, arai bo idiopet bon; naarai aseu Mariam ewai loejok, lomam edemario ŋes.”" 
Luke11:1 Kosodi kanen, nakilipia kaibois adiopet, nakedaunia, kotema ediopet kosesisiakake atiar, “Ejakait, kisisianakinai sio ailip, kwape kisisianakinia Yokana da ikekesisiak.”" 
Luke11:2 Kotema kes atiar, “Nailipiata, kineras ebe, Papakosi loejai toma akuj, ekonikiror kitalaunai. Akonijakanut kobu. Nuikoto kiswamai kakwap, kwape iswamaere kotoma akuj." 
Luke11:3 Koinanakinai sio ikosinyamat luka ŋinipaaran; 
Luke11:4 Kisionioi sio akosidiakanareta; naarai kisioniei isio lukapeseninikosi. Sirikiya sio toma acodunio, konye koyuunai sio kama ejai lokaronon.”" 
Luke11:5 Kotema kes atiar, “Iŋai kayesi yenejai ekepapero, kelot mama ejai kidiŋ kuare, kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Opaperoka, koyuunai ber kimugatin iuni;" 
Luke11:6 naarai adolu ekapapero mamaka ebuni kalosit, emamei eoŋ idiobore yenainakini ŋes ainyam’;" 
Luke11:7 eboŋokini lokotogo ebe, ‘Sirikiitapas eoŋ; egolol ekek, kiperi eoŋ nepepe kikadwe koitada; mam apedori anyoun ainakin jo’?" 
Luke11:8 Katemari yes atiar, Karaida mam enyouni ainakin naarai erai ekepapero, konye kanuka akeiŋaiŋait enyouni einakini ŋes luipuda kere." 
Luke11:9 Katemari yes atiar, Kilipa, kiinakinio; komoata, idumunete; kikuŋukuŋoto, kiŋaikinio," 
Luke11:10 Naarai ŋin yenilipi ijaikinio, yenemoi edumuni, ka yenikuŋukuŋi da enaikinio." 
Luke11:11 Iŋai bo kayesi erai papa, arai kilipi ikokuke emugati, einakini tope amoru? Arai bo agar, ido aibois kagar einakini tope ŋes emun?" 
Luke11:12 Arai kilip abeet, einakini tope ekiriton?" 
Luke11:13 Aso arai yes lukaronok iienete ainakin ikusidwe ainakineta nuejok, mam kereka itelekarit noi Papakus loejai toma akuj ainakin ŋul luilipete ŋes Emoyo Lokalaunan?”" 
Luke11:14 Kosodi kanen ireŋeari ŋesi ajokit nabaŋ, Kelom ajokit, kiner lobaŋ; koumokis ikodeta." 
Luke11:15 Konye kobalas ice kakesi ebe, “Ireŋeari ŋesi ajokin kanuka Beelesebul ekapolon loka ajokin.”" 
Luke11:16 Kocodut ice, kokotosi aanyunet naebuni kotoma akuj." 
Luke11:17 Konye kejeni ŋesi akeceomisio, kotema kes atiar, “Ŋinijakanut naetiakatiakaun asurokin bon emudiar; arai etogo ketogo ibiror." 
Luke11:18 Aso arai etiakatiakaun Satan bon, ikonakini ai akejakanut icasi? Naarai ibalasi yesi ebe ereŋeari eoŋ ajokin kanuka Beelesebul." 
Luke11:19 Aso arai ereŋeari eoŋ ajokin kanuka Beelesebul, ido bo ikusidwe ireŋearete kanuka iŋai? Kanuka ŋun ŋes eraatar ŋul ikusikatubok." 
Luke11:20 Konye arai ereŋeari eoŋ ajokin kebokorit loka Edeke, aso adolu ajakanut naka Edeke mamakus," 
Luke11:21 Etuŋanan lokagogon ekapi lujiisike idari alaroke, inapakina ikeboro:" 
Luke11:22 Konye naebunokinia ekagogoŋon loedeparit ŋes, ipikori edemari lujiisike kere luamunokina ŋesi, ka akorokor iŋatanake," 
Luke11:23 Ituŋanan yenimam ejai keoŋ, ŋes yenikekoloka; ituŋanan da yenimam etukonokini keoŋ, isiarakini." 
Luke11:24 “Kelonu emoyo loerono kotuŋanan, itori aiboisio nuemameete akip, emoot nekiyeŋunet; keoliki, ebala ebe, ‘Aboŋori togoka nekabunio.’" 
Luke11:25 Keboŋu, edumuni epieitai, epesitai da." 
Luke11:26 Kosodi do elosi eupunos kimoyon ice ikanykaarei luitelekarito ŋes aronis; elomarete kesi da esalete nen; ejautene loka ituŋanan kaŋin lokawasia eraun loerono adepar losodit.” 
Luke11:27 Kosodi kanen, napinera akiro ŋun, kiworo adiopeberu kotoma okodet, kotema atiar, “Isirereŋitoi aliliget nakipotiere jo, ka ikisin da lukinaki.”" 
Luke11:28 Konye Yesu kobala ebe, “Konye ca, nuitelekarito, isirereŋitoi luiirarete akirot naka Edeke, koricata da!”" 
Luke11:29 Kosodi naketukokinotor ikodeta mamakeŋ, kogeu atemar kes atiar, “Atur na erai atur nakaronon; emoot aanyunet, kwabo mam einakinio aanyunet, dimarai aanyunet naka Yona." 
Luke11:30 Naarai kwape keraar Yona aanyunet kama ejaas ituŋa luko Ninebe, kwape kwaŋin eraunia Okoku loka etuŋanan kama ejai atur na," 
Luke11:31 Enyouni akabaka naka Eŋalakimak kapaaran naka etube nepepe kituŋa luka atur kana, itetelekari kes akiro; naarai abu ŋesi kobu kosaŋe loka akwap akiirar acoa naka Solomon, ido koany, ejai ne yenitelekarit Solomon." 
Luke11:32 Enyounete ikiliok luka Ninebe kapaaran naka etube nepepe katur na itetelekarete ŋes akiro; naarai apotu kesi kitoronikinos kanuka alimonokin naka Yona, ido koany, ejai ne yenitelekarit Yona," 
Luke11:33 Emamei yeninokokini atala kibwaik aipany arai toma obukit, dimarai ikajakini ocoget, tetere epedorete luelomunete aanyun aica." 
Luke11:34 Atala naka akuan ŋes akonikoŋu; arai oteni akonikoŋu, akonikuan kere ecai; konye arai erono, akonikuan da emutono." 
Luke11:35 Aso kocoite kinye aica nakotomakon araun amuton. 
Luke11:36 Aso arai ecai akonikuan kere, komamei adiotutubet naemutono, ileleba kere aica pas, kwape katala nakinwakakinit jo kaicake.”" 
Luke11:37 Napinera, konyara Eparisayot ediopet oreke aimor kaŋes lukapaaran; koloma kiboikin ainyam." 
Luke11:38 Keanyu Eparisayot ŋol koumok, naarai mam ber kilosit eroko enyama." 
Luke11:39 Kotema Ejakait ŋes atiar, “Kwana yes Iparisayon itesegarete kiŋa kakolin ka asanin, konye kotomakus ileleba aiŋat ka aronis," 
Luke11:40 Ibaŋiok yesi! Lokesubi lukokuiu mere ŋes lokesubi lukotoma da? 
Luke11:41 Konye koinakisi lukotoma araut ainakineta nukaitim; ido koany, elaete kere kamakus." 
Luke11:42 “Konye itukwi yes Iparisayon! Naarai iinanakinete idiopet kotomon yenika alilot ka ecaboi ka ŋinikiyot kere, inyeinete etube ka amin naka Edeke; ibusakinit yes aswam ŋun komam inyeinete kwa da." 
Luke11:43 Itukwi yes Iparisayon! Naarai iminasi iicoloŋo lukapolou katukosia, ka aiyogao kagwelanareta." 
Luke11:44 Itukwi yes! Naarai iputos katesin numam etakanete, nuitorito ituŋa komam ejenete.”" 
Luke11:45 Koboŋok ediopet koricakisila kotema ŋes atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kiner ijo kwaŋin kimoromor sio da.”" 
Luke11:46 Kotema atiar, “Itukwi yes da iricakisila! Naarai isibwokete ituŋa ibwokon lukalaŋirok, konye yes ikulepek mam itirorete ibwokon kediopet kobokorokus." 
Luke11:47 Itukwi yes! Naarai idukete atesin nuka inabin luapotu lukapapaakus koara. 
Luke11:48 Aso iraas ikajenak icamunito da aswamisio nuka lukapapaakus; naarai kes lukearete, yes da idukete atesinakec," 
Luke11:49 Kanuka ŋun inera acoa naka Edeke ebe, ‘Ejukakini kes inabin ka ikiyakia, earete ice kakes, ereete,’" 
Luke11:50 tetere itepesenio atur na aokot nuka inabi; kere, nukebukoros ameun kapetetait naka akwap," 
Luke11:51 ameun kaokot nuka Abel kiton aokot nuka Sakaria, lokearakinio kidiŋ ketem ka aibois nakalaunan. Eebo, katemari yes atiar, Itepesenio kotoma atur kana." 
Luke11:52 Itukwi yes iricakisila! Naarai ilemut alacetait naka aijen; mam yes ilomarito, ido itikokinito luakotos alomar.”" 
Luke11:53 Nakelomunia kanen, kogeut ikewadikak ka Iparisayon aridakin jokan, ka aiŋitiŋit akiro nuipu," 
Luke11:54 kolokata ŋes tetere ipoki kakirot naelomuni kaitukuke. 
Luke12:1 Kapaarasia kaŋun, naketukonokinotor ilukumin luka ikodeta kiton aicakacaka, kogeu alimokin ber ikekesisiak ebe, “Kocoito aitubuunet naka Iparisayon, ŋes aisoswanut." 
Luke12:2 Konye emamei akirot naimunonitai, namam epukorio; karaida naibwaitai, namam ejenunio," 
Luke12:3 Aso nuinerata kamuton iirario kaica; ido nuiyeiyeata kagolai nukotoma elimonokinio kokuju otogoi. 
Luke12:4 “Katemari yes ikapapero atiar, Sirikikuriakaros luearete akuan, kosodi mam bobo nuepedorete aswam." 
Luke12:5 Konye kekwenyari yes loikuriaka: kokuriaka ŋol loejai apedor kedau aiar acakakin Ogeena; eebo, katemari yes ariar, Kokuriaka ŋol." 
Luke12:6 Mam kereka egwelete anyiporin akany apesan aarei? Kwabo mam imurwokinio adiopet kakonyen nuka Edeke. 
Luke12:7 Konye imaritai itima da kere luka akwesikus kere, Sirikuriaka; iraas yesi luketiai adepar anyiporin nuipu." 
Luke12:8 “Katemari yes atiar, ŋinituŋanan yenikalimori eoŋ kakonyen nuka ituŋa, elimori da Okoku loka etuŋanan ŋes kakonyen nuka imalaikan luka Edeke;" 
Luke12:9 Konye ŋin yenikaŋeri eoŋ kakonyen nuka ituŋa, enerio ŋin da kakonyen nuka imalaikan luka Edeke." 
Luke12:10 Ŋinituŋanan da yeninera akirot asurokin Okoku loka etuŋanan isionio; konye yeneinyanakini Emoyo Lokalaunan mam isionio. 
Luke12:11 Nakiyaŋaariata yes akonyen nuka atukosia ka ikayaitok ka lukapolou, sirikiyaloŋoŋoto epone arai akiro nuiboŋokinete arai nuineras;" 
Luke12:12 naarai kisisianakini Emoyo Lokalaunan kosawa kaŋol nuibusakinit einer.” 
Luke12:13 Kotema ediopet kokodet atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kolimok onaceka katiakata keoŋ akosikirumet.”" 
Luke12:14 Konye kotema ŋes atiar, “Ikatunanan, iŋai bo kadakakini eoŋ araut ekatubon arai ekakoran kamakus?”" 
Luke12:15 Kotema kes atiar, “Kocoito, kidaras bonik kama ejai airaŋaanut kere; naarai aijar naka ituŋanan mere iboro luipu luejaatar ŋesi.”" 
Luke12:16 Kolimok kes awaragan ebe, “Kebwaŋunito noi alup nuka etuŋanan lokabaran." 
Luke12:17 Kogeu aomoom kotauke ebe, ‘Kekonak ai, naarai emamei neengadakini ikanyamat?’" 
Luke12:18 Kotema atiar, ‘Ekonakini ne; atiyatiyai idulaaka, ka aje da luitelekarito; eŋadakini nen akakima kere ka ikaboro.’" 
Luke12:19 Atemari akaijar atiar, ‘Aijar, ejaas jo iboro luipu luimonot kanuka ikar luipu; aso kijamam, konyam, komat, kolakara da.’" 
Luke12:20 Konye kotema Edeke ŋes atiar, ‘Ibaŋaana ijo! Ekotoi akoniijar akuare na; iboro da luitemokinit, eraunete lukaŋai?’" 
Luke12:21 Ikoni nen yeniŋadakinit iboro luka akais kanuke elopet, komam ebari mama ejai Edeke.”" 
Luke12:22 Kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Kanuka ŋun katemari yes atiar, Siriyaloŋoŋoete kanuka akusiiiar, luinyamete, karaida kanuka akusiwat luinapete," 
Luke12:23 Naarai aijar itelekarit inyamat, ka akuan da itelekarit anapito." 
Luke12:24 Koomito ikuruka ebe mam eyeete kwabo mam idwenyete, emameete aiŋadisia karaida idulaa; konye itanyami kes Edeke, Itelekarito cama yesi noi akweny!" 
Luke12:25 Iŋai bo kayes kiyaloŋoŋ epedori aiyatakin akeibut? 
Luke12:26 Aso do arai mam ipedorete akirot naedit noi kwaŋin, kanukinyo iyaloŋonooro kanuka ace kere?" 
Luke12:27 Koomito aapecelun, kwape epolooto; mam itaaritos, karaida aoj; konye katemari yes atiar. Ka Solomon da kotoma aibusesuke kere mam esiritoi kojokan kwape adiopet kaŋun." 
Luke12:28 Aso arai itanapi Edeke kwaŋin inya luka ais, Iuejaas lolo, ecakario moi oupa; itelekarit cama noi aitanap yes, okwe yes luedit aiyuun." 
Luke12:29 Sirikimoata luinyamete karaida nuimasete, kwabo sirikibuonokinos." 
Luke12:30 Naarai emooto atekerin kere nuka akwapin ŋun kere: konye ejeŋi Papakus ebe ipudasi yesi ŋun. 
Luke12:31 Konye komoata akejakanut, kiyatakinio da ŋun." 
Luke12:32 “Ijo esipan loedit, sirikikurianar, naarai isiyalamikinit Papakus ainakin yes ajakanut." 
Luke12:33 Kogwelanasi luijaatar, kokora lukaitim; kodonyonokinos iriagin lumam emojoŋete, emono kotoma akuj lomam iŋoŋar, aibois namam eapikini ekokolan, karaida ikajekel amunaun." 
Luke12:34 Naarai nepejai akusibar, nepenen ejaikinos ikusitauon da." 
Luke12:35 “Koenito akusiŋabes, konokete da akusitalai;" 
Luke12:36 yes da ikulepek kosubito bala ituŋa luidarete ejakaitikec naebonunio koiterane tetere naebunio aikuŋukuŋ konaikis atipet. 
Luke12:37 Isirereŋitoi ibulesin ŋul luedumuni ejakaitikec ekwenyete naebunio; abeit, katemari yes atiar, eeni akeŋabet, isukunyikini kes onyamat, ebuni ŋesi elopet ijaanakini kes." 
Luke12:38 Arai kebu kakwenyunet nakiareit, arai nakiwuniet, kodum ikote nen, isirereŋitoi ibulesin ŋul." 
Luke12:39 Konye kojenutu akirot na ebe arai kejeni elopet etogo esawa loebunio ekokolan, tikekweny, kwabo timam kejalaki eketogo abokio." 
Luke12:40 Yes da kokapakina; naarai ebuni Okoku loka etuŋanan kosawa lomam iwomito.” 
Luke12:41 Kotema Petero atiar, “Ejakait, kilimokinit sio bon awaragan ŋin, arai bo ituŋa kere?”" 
Luke12:42 Kotema Ejakait atiar, “Aso iŋai bo erai ekeŋadan lomunot loepiriana, lokedakakini ejakaitike ayait lukokaleke kere akoranakin kes ikecenyamat kapakikec?" 
Luke12:43 Isirereŋitoi ebulesit ŋol, loedumuni ejakaitike iswamai kwaŋin naebunio." 
Luke12:44 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Edakakini ŋes ayait luejaatar kere." 
Luke12:45 Konye arai etemari ebulesit ŋol otauke ebe, ‘Eyap ejakaitika abunore,’ kogeu aibuŋ itelepai ka apesur, ka ainyam ka aimat ka amer da;" 
Luke12:46 ebuni ejakait loka ebulesit kaŋol kapaaran namam eomit, ka esawa da lomam ejeni, etubi ŋes katutubeta aarei, itebei ekewai nepepe kalumam iyuunito." 
Luke12:47 Ebulesit ŋol loeieni nuekoto ejakaitike, komam ekapakin, karaida aswam nuekoto ejakaitike, edaio luipu." 
Luke12:48 Konye ŋol lomam ejeni, kiswama da nuibusakinito adaia, edaio luikidioko. Ŋin da yeneinakinitai nuipu, emoio nuipu kamake; ŋin da yenititiŋito ituŋa nuipu, iburaete nuiyatakina." 
Luke12:49 “Abunit acakakin akim akwap; ti akoto kinokokinitete sek! 
Luke12:50 Ejai aibatis naebusakinit aibatisao; ido aridakina cama eoŋ kiton neitodolikinere! 
Luke12:51 Aso iwomitos kereka ebe abu kabu ayaŋaun ainapakin toma akwap? Katemari yes atiar, Mam; dimarai atiakatiak:" 
Luke12:52 naarai amear kwana ejaikinos ituŋa ikany togo ediopet, etiakas iuni aluikin iarei, ka iarei da aluikin iuni;" 
Luke12:53 etiakas, papa eluikini okokuke, ka okoku da eluikini papake, toto eluikini akokuke, ka akoku da eluikini totoke, tataa eluikini ateranike, ateran da eluikini tataake.”" 
Luke12:54 Kotema ŋesi ikodeta da atiar, “Naianyuniata edou edakun koto, atipet ibalas ebe, ‘Etepi nat akir’; ido ejaun kwaŋin," 
Luke12:55 Naianyuniata ekusi ekwam loka eŋalakimak, ibalas ebe, ‘Ejaun aibuse naepol’; ejaun da kwaŋin," 
Luke12:56 Yes lukesoswai, ijenete aŋicun ejautene loka akwap ka akuj; konye kanukinyo mam ijeniata aŋicun apak na?" 
Luke12:57 “Kanukinyo mam yes ikulepek itubioto nueraas nukabeit? 
Luke12:58 Naarai naiupatarar ka lokiwosat alosit mama ejai ekayaiton, kinyikok ainerun kaŋes korot nuka aipuc, kinyek aidilidilar jo mama ejai ekatubon, ekatubon da kijaikini akanin nuka eketatacan, eketatacan da kieakakini aidaris." 
Luke12:59 Katemari jo atiar, Mam cut ilomuni kanen aitodol naidaunia atacakin apesa nakawasia.”" 
Luke13:1 Kapak kanipe kaŋin kojaas ituŋa lukitejenunete ŋes nuka Igalilayan, lukinyalakini Pilato akeceokot kasubanakec," 
Luke13:2 Koboŋok kotema kes atiar, “Iwomito kereka ebe keroko Igalilayan ŋul aitelekarit Igalilayan ice kere, naarai iticanio ŋun?" 
Luke13:3 Katemari yes atiar, Mam; konye arai mam yes itoronikinos, imudiaros kere kwape kwaŋin," 
Luke13:4 Arai kwi itomon kakanykauni lukibirokin etogo loeoja, koSiloam, koara kes, iwomito kereka ebe ebucarito ŋul aitelekarit ituŋa kere lukiboiete koYerusalem?" 
Luke13:5 Katemari yes atiar, Mam; konye arai mam yes itoronikinos, imudiaros kere kwape kwaŋin.”" 
Luke13:6 Kiner awaragan na ebe, “Kejai etuŋanan ka etini lokiraikinitai manake naka emusabibu; kolot amoot araitoke, mam edumuna." 
Luke13:7 Kotema ŋesi ekeswaman loka amana naka emusabibu atiar, ‘Koany, ikar iuni lu abu amoot araito naka etini kalo, mam adumunit amodio. Kojepa; kanukinyo imadiŋikinia alup?’" 
Luke13:8 Koboŋok kotema atiar, ‘Ejakait, kinyek ber ekaru lo da, kebokibok kewor da." 
Luke13:9 Arai kera do araito okaru je, ejok; konye arai mam, ijepari.’ ”" 
Luke13:10 Kapaaran nakasabato isisianakini kotoma adiopet katukosia. 
Luke13:11 Ido koany, kojai aberu nakejai ajokit nakalany ikar itomon kakanykauni; nakekudokina, komam epedori cut aitenar," 
Luke13:12 Nakeanyunia Yesu ŋes, konyarau, kotema ŋes atiar, “Toto, kilacar kotoma akalanyanutukon.”" 
Luke13:13 Kidokok ŋes akekanin, atipet kitenar, kitopolo Edeke." 
Luke13:14 Konye konyunyura ekayaiton loka atukos naarai etaŋaleun Yesu kapaaran nakasabato, kotema ituŋa atiar, “Ejaas apaarasia akanykape nuejokiar ituŋa aiswamaa aswam; aso kopotu aitaŋaleunio kapaarasia kaŋun, kwabo mere kapaaran nakasabato.”" 
Luke13:15 Konye Ejakait Koboŋok ebe, “Yes lukesoswai! Kapaaran nakasabato mam kereka ilacununete ninidioper kayes ekemoŋ arai akesigiria kotoma auj, koyaŋa aitamat?" 
Luke13:16 Aberu na da, naerai aur naka Aburaam, nakeeni Satan ikar lu itomon kalukanykauni, mam tope kibusakinit alacakinio kaenet kana apaaran nakasabato?”" 
Luke13:17 Nakinerar ŋun, kirumata ileic lukasurupoke kere: kiyalamikin ekodet kere kanuka akiro kere nukaibuses nukiswamai ŋesi." 
Luke13:18 Aso kotema atiar, “Eputos ajakanut naka Edeke kinyo? Etupusi kinyo?" 
Luke13:19 Eputosi kecokat loka ekaradali lokelemari etuŋanan, kocakak toma omanikorike; kobwaŋ, koraun ekitoi; koperenenete akweny nuka apak atenieikike.”" 
Luke13:20 Kotema bobo atiar, “Etupusi kinyo ajakanut naka Edeke?" 
Luke13:21 Eputosi kaitubuunet nakelemari aberu kibwa kotoma aitemisio auni nuka akiria, kiton neabuunioto kere.”" 
Luke13:22 Kiyatak akelosit aitor koreria lukapolok ka ludidik, isisianakini, ebei Yerusalem," 
Luke13:23 Kiŋit ŋes etuŋanan ediopet ebe, “Ejakait, ikidioko ca luitaiario?” Kotema kes atiar," 
Luke13:24 “Kokokito alomar kokek kaloedidiŋ: naarai katemari yes atiar, Ekotokinos luipu alomar kwabo mam epedorete." 
Luke13:25 Apak naanyounio elopet etogo agoloki da ekek, igeunete yesi aibwo kokiŋa, ka aikuŋukuŋ ekek, kobalas ebe, ‘Wu okwe Ejakait, koŋaarai;’ eboŋokini ŋesi etemari atiar, ‘Mam ajeni nekiponiata.’" 
Luke13:26 Kanen igeunete atemar atiar, ‘Kipou kanyama kamata da kakonyenekon, ijo da kisisianakini korotinikosi;’" 
Luke13:27 etemari ŋesi atiar, ‘Katemari yes atiar, Mam ajeni nekiponiata; irwa kamakaŋ, yes kere lukeswamak numam adolit.’" 
Luke13:28 Kanen ejaun aimony ka airiamanakin ikel, naianyuniata Aburaam, ka Isaak, ka Yakob, ka inabin kere, kotoma ajakanut naka Edeke, ka yes da ikulepek kicakario kiŋa." 
Luke13:29 Epote ituŋa anyoun kokide, koto, ka agolitomei ka eŋalakimak da, iboikinos kesi toma ajakanut naka Edeke," 
Luke13:30 Ido koany, ejaas lukawasia lueraunos lusodit, ejaas da lusodit, lueraunos lukawasia.”" 
Luke13:31 Kosawa kaŋol kopotu Iparisayon ice kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Konyou kane kolot nenice; naarai ekoto Kerode aiar jo.”" 
Luke13:32 Kotema kes atiar, “Koloto kolimokis ekuwe ŋol ebe, ‘Koany, ereŋeari ajokin, etaŋaleununei da lolo ka moi, kapaaran nakiwuniet etodolikin." 
Luke13:33 Konye kebusakinit aibe ekarot lolo ka moi, ka apaaran naetupakini da; naarai mam ibusakinit enabi amudiario kokiŋa naka Yerusalem.’" 
Luke13:34 Wu okwe Yerusalem, Yerusalem, loeari inabin ka aibiribir kamor ŋul lukiyakunio mamakon! Irwan imwa ai abu kakotor atukonokin ikonidwe kwape etukonokinia akokor ikemiyoi kwap abebenokake, konye mam yes ekotokino!" 
Luke13:35 Koany, kinyeinere ekusitogo. Katemari yes atiar, Mam kianyunete eoŋ bobo cut, aitodol naitemariata atiar, ‘Isirereŋitoi ŋol loebunit kokiror loka Ejakait!’ ”" 
Luke14:1 Kosodi kanen nakelomaria ainyam togo loka ekayaiton ediopet loka Iparisayon kapaaran nakasabato, kiteikinito," 
Luke14:2 Kosodi koany, kiŋarenike kejai etuŋanan lokedeka eidada." 
Luke14:3 Koboŋok Yesu iricakisila ka Iparisayon kobala ebe, “Ibus kereka aitaŋaleun kapaaran nakasabato arai bo mam?”" 
Luke14:4 Konye kes kililiŋata. Kitim, kitaŋaleu ŋes, kotwar." 
Luke14:5 Kotema kes atiar, “Iŋai bo kayesi, arai kibirokin akeiteŋ arai akesigiria toma aipany, yenimam iriuni ŋes atipet kapaaran nakasabato?”" 
Luke14:6 Kes da mam apotu kopedosi aboŋokin ŋun. 
Luke14:7 Kolimok awaragan ŋul lukenyaraunitai, naaanyunia epone lokeseata kesi iicoloŋo lukapolou, kobala kes ebe," 
Luke14:8 “Arai kinyararit jo ituŋanan opucit loka eiterane, sirikiboikin oicoloŋ lokapolou, kinyek loenyarit ŋesi lokitelekarit jo apolou abunore." 
Luke14:9 Kosodi ŋol lokiinyarari jo ka ŋes alimokin jo ebe, ‘Koosik lo aibois,’ kanen kigeunete ileic airum, ibei da aibois nakokwap." 
Luke14:10 Konye nakinyararere, kolot kiboikin aibois nakokwap, tetere naebunio je lokinyararit jo kolimok ebe, ‘Opapero ba, kikuny ne kuju’; kanen ijaunete kaibuses kakonyen nuka ŋul kere kalukiboiete kajo." 
Luke14:11 Naarai ŋin kere yeniturokin itisilio, ka yenitisilikin iturio.”" 
Luke14:12 Kotema da lokenyarit ŋes atiar, “Naipoio inyamat luka paaran arai luka eboŋ, sirikinyarau ikonipapero karaida ikoniinacan, karaida ikonipajen, karaida iidunyeta lukabarak, kinyeis ŋul anyarar jo bobo, jo da kitacakinio." 
Luke14:13 Konye naipoio epucit, konyaraununei lukican, ka iŋwalasik, ka luicodos, ka imudukiok da," 
Luke14:14 kwaŋin kisirereŋitoi; naarai emameete ŋul lukitacakiniata; naarai kitacakinio kotoma ajarun naka luedolito.” 
Luke14:15 Nakiiraria ŋun ediopet kalukemorete kaŋes, kotema atiar, “Isirereŋitoi ŋin yenenyami atap kotoma ajakanut naka Edekel.”" 
Luke14:16 Konye kotema ŋes atiar, “Kojai etuŋanan loabu kipo epucit loepol, konyarau ituŋa luipu;" 
Luke14:17 kedol apak naka ainyam kiyakia ekebulesit alimonokin kwi luanyaritai ebe, ‘Kopotu; naarai adaun aitemonokin iboro kere.’" 
Luke14:18 Konye kogeutu kere aiyanar kediopetau. Kobala losodit ebe, ‘Agwel emanikor, kebusakinit alosit aanyun; keŋaiŋait kiikinai.’" 
Luke14:19 Kobala ece ebe, ‘Agwel imoŋin ajookon akany, alosi aitetemor; keŋaiŋait, kiikinai.’" 
Luke14:20 Kobala ece ebe, ‘Amany aberu, ŋes mam apedoria abunore.’" 
Luke14:21 Kobu ebulesit kolimok ejakaitike akiro ŋun kere. Kosodi konyunyurikin elopet etogo, kotema ekebulesit atiar, ‘Koloma atipet kolot toma orotin ka isokono da luka ere, koyau ne lukican, ka iŋwalasik ka imudukiok, ka luicodos da.’" 
Luke14:22 Kotema ebulesit atiar, ‘Ejakait, ŋun nukicorak eswamasi, konye ca eriŋa aibois ejai.’ ”" 
Luke14:23 Kotema ejakait ebulesit atiar, “Koloma kolot orotin lukapolok ka asisiarin da, kitiŋau ituŋa alomun, tetere ilelebun ekatogo." 
Luke14:24 Naarai katemari yes atiar, Kotoma kwi kalukenyaritai emamei edio da loiiri ekapueit.”" 
Luke14:25 Kouparos ikodeta luipu kaŋes; kibelokin kotema kes atiar," 
Luke14:26 “Arai ebuni etuŋanan mamaka, komam elai papake, ka totoke, ka nakowaike, ka ikedwe, ka ikeinacan ka ainacan, eebo, kiton akeijar alopet, mam epedori araun ekakesisian." 
Luke14:27 Ŋin yenimam erioŋi ekemusalaba, katup eoŋ, mam epedori araun ikakesisian," 
Luke14:28 Naarai iŋai bo kayesi, arai ekoto aiduk etogo loeoja, mam iboikini ber aimar eketiai, ebe luejaatar edaunete?" 
Luke14:29 Kinyek diat kedau aipet apetetait, komam epedori adaun, egeunete ituŋa kere lueanyunete akienar ŋes," 
Luke14:30 kobalas ebe, ‘Abu etuŋanan ŋol kogeu aiduk, komam epedori adaun.’" 
Luke14:31 Arai bo ekabaka enyoin, arai ekoto alosit ejie kekabaka ece, lomam ber iboikini ainerun arai epedori kilukumin itomon airiamakin kaje loebunit asurokin ŋes kilukumin akaisaarei?" 
Luke14:32 Arai keanyu ebe mam epedori, iyakiari ikiyakia ailip nukainapakin, eriŋa je elwana." 
Luke14:33 Aso kwaŋin ŋinituŋanan kayesi, yenimam epaluni luejaatar kere mam epedori araun ikakesisian." 
Luke14:34 “Ejok abalaŋ; konye arai kepianiar abalaŋ, itemokinio kinyo?" 
Luke14:35 Mam ibusakini alup, karaida etut; ebukorete ituŋa kiŋa, Yenejaas aki nuka akiirar, kiira.”" 
Luke15:1 Kosodete kikunyakis iketelemak esolo ka ikadiakanarak kere akiirar ŋes. 
Luke15:2 Kirurumata Iparisayon ka ikewadikak ebe, “Isukunyikini etuŋanan ŋol ikadiakanarak, emorete da kakes.”" 
Luke15:3 Kolimok kes awaragan na ebe," 
Luke15:4 “Iŋai bo kayes yenejaas amerekekin akwatat, keolio adiopet, mam kereka inyeini akaisakanykaoŋon ka nukanykaonon kamodiŋ, kolot amoot ŋin nakeoliorit aitodol needumunia?" 
Luke15:5 Kedau adumun, erioŋakini okeperinike, kolakara." 
Luke15:6 Naedolio togoke, enyarauni ikepapero ka ikeidunyeta, kolimok ebe, ‘Kolakaros nepepe keoŋ, naarai adum akamerekek naaoliorit.’" 
Luke15:7 Katemari yes atiar, Kwape kwaŋin ŋes ejaunor alakara toma akuj kanuka ikadiakanaran idiopet yenitoronikin itia kanuka ituŋa akaisakanykaoŋon ka lukanykaoŋon lumam ipudasi aitoronikin." 
Luke15:8 “Arai iŋai bo aberu, ejaas karupiyan atomon, arai koolio adiopet, mam inokokini atalake ka aipie etogo ka amoot kainyikokinit kiton needumunia?" 
Luke15:9 Kedau adumun, enyarauni akepapero ka akeidunyeta kolimok ebe, ‘Kolakaros nepepe keoŋ, naarai adum arupiya naaoliorit.’" 
Luke15:10 Katemari yes atiar, Kwape kwaŋin ejai alakara kakonyen nuka imalaikan luka Edeke kanuka ikadiakanaran idiopet yenitoronikin.”" 
Luke15:11 Kobala ebe, “Kojai etuŋanan lokejaas odweke iarei." 
Luke15:12 Kotema lodidi papake atiar, ‘Papa, ae atutubet naka ikoniboro lukabeito eoŋ.’ Kokorak do kes lukejaatar," 
Luke15:13 Ketuboros apaarasia nuikidioko, kotukonok lodidi lukebeito ŋes kere, kolot akwap naelwana, kiweliwel ikeboro kaŋina koponesio luutai." 
Luke15:14 Nakedaunia aitwasam kere, kodo ebeli akwap ya, kogeu ŋesi da aiyarorotoi." 
Luke15:15 Kolot kimorikikinos kediopet kokulepek akwap, kijuka ŋol ŋes oronyike acok ipegei." 
Luke15:16 Konat aimonikin abubuk nukenyamete ipegei; kemamei da ituŋanan yeneinakini ŋes idiobore. 
Luke15:17 Nakiitoki kotauke, kobala ebe, ‘Imwaasi ai ikejaanakinak luka papaka luenyamete inyamat kosala, eoŋ da kane atwani eteŋei." 
Luke15:18 Anyouni do kalot mama ejai papaka, kalimok ŋes ebe, “Papa, adiaka kama ejai akuj, kakonyenekon da;" 
Luke15:19 Mam bobo kebusakinit anyarao okokukon; kikonakinai bala ediopet kokejaanakinakakon.” ’ 
Luke15:20 Konyou kobu mama ejai papake. Konye naperoko elwana, koany papake ŋes, kitim, koker kibirokin omurisiŋike, konu ŋes." 
Luke15:21 Kotema okoku ŋes atiar, ‘Papa, adiaka kama ejai akuj, kakonyenekon da; mam bobo kebusakinit anyarao okokukon.’" 
Luke15:22 Konye kobala papake ikekejaanakinak ebe, ‘Koyaŋautu atipet anapito naitelekarit aibuses, kitanapa ŋes; kitanapikis da egilut obokoritike, ka amuka da akejeke;" 
Luke15:23 koyaŋautu da itaok yenirobok koarata, kanyama kalakaros;" 
Luke15:24 naarai okokuka lo abu kotwana, ajaru bobo; aoliorit, atakanu bobo.’ Kogeut alakar." 
Luke15:25 “Kojai okokuke lokapolon amana; konye napebuni aapikin ere, kiira lueruos ka ekosio." 
Luke15:26 Konyarau ediopet kotelepai kiŋit ebe, ‘Ikote bo ai ŋun?’" 
Luke15:27 Kolimok ebe, ‘Abu onacekon, aaraki papakon itaok yenirobok, naarai abwatu ŋes eŋalei.’" 
Luke15:28 Konye konyunyurikin, mam abu kokoto alomar toma. Kolom papake kiŋa kiŋaiŋa." 
Luke15:29 Konye Koboŋok ŋesi papake ebe, ‘Koany, keiaanak jo ikar lu luipu, kwabo mam adiakit adioicorakinetekon; konye mam kiinakinit eoŋ imodiokalol, kalakarotor kikapapero." 
Luke15:30 Konye napabunio okokukon ŋol, loabu konyam ikoniboro nepepe kanudotea, iarak ŋes itaok yenirobok.’" 
Luke15:31 Kotema papake atiar, ‘Ikakoku, ijai ijo keoŋ apaarasia kere, kere da lukijaar eoŋ eraas lukon." 
Luke15:32 Ibusakinit alakar ka aiyalamikin, naarai onacekon ŋol abu kotwana, ajaru bobo; aoliorit, atakanu bobo.’ ”" 
Luke16:1 Kotema bobo Yesu ikekesisiak atiar, “Kojai etuŋanan ekabaran lokejai ekekeŋadan, kirupeai ŋol kamake ebe eweliwel iboroke." 
Luke16:2 Konyarau kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Akiro nunyoika nu nueirarit kamakon? Kimar iboro luka akoniiŋad, naarai mam ipedori bobo araut ekeŋadan.’" 
Luke16:3 Kotema ekeŋadan je kotauke atiar, ‘Kekonak ai, naarai kadema papaka aiŋad? Emamei eoŋ agogoŋ akor, kerumito da ileic ailipitoi." 
Luke16:4 Ajeni nueswamai, tetere keereŋei kaiŋadakaŋ, kesukunyikis otogoikec.’" 
Luke16:5 Konyarau lukapesenin luka ejakaitike ŋolidiopet, kotema losodit atiar, ‘Inyo bo kiburai ejakaitika jo?’" 
Luke16:6 Kobala ebe, ‘Aitemisio akwatat nuka akinyet.’ Kolimok ebe, ‘Kolem akoniitutuket, kiboikin atipet, kiwadik akaisakany.’" 
Luke16:7 Kosodi atemar ece atiar, ‘Inyo bo kiburao jo?’ Kobala ebe, ‘Aitemisio akwatat nuka akima.’ Kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Kolem akoniitutuket, kiwadik akaisakanykauni.’" 
Luke16:8 Kitojok ejakaitike ekeŋadan lokeŋalan kanuka aswam nukapirianut; naarai idwe luka akwapin kanu kotoma aturikec ejaas kapirianut aitelekarit idwe luka aica. 
Luke16:9 Katemari yes atiar, Koneronosi ipapero kotoma abar naka amamus adolit, tetere naemamuunor, kisukunyikis yes toma aiboisio nuka ikar kere." 
Luke16:10 “Yenimunot kakirot naedit noi, erai yenimunot kakirot naepol; ŋin da yeniŋalai kakirot naedit, erai yeniŋalai da kakirot naepol." 
Luke16:11 Aso arai mam yes iraas lumunon kotoma abar naka aiŋal, iŋai bo kisiŋadikini yes abar nakabeit?" 
Luke16:12 Arai mam iraas lumunon kotoma kaŋul kalueraas luka ice, iŋai bo kiinakini yes lueraas lukus ikulepek?" 
Luke16:13 Emamei ekejaanakinan loepedori aijaanakin ijaka iarei, naarai arai elai ediopet, komina loce, arai bo iketakin kediopet emeni loce. Mam ipedorete aijaanakin Edeke ka aijaanakin abar da.”" 
Luke16:14 Kiirasi Iparisayon lueminas apesan ŋun kere, kimuasi ŋes." 
Luke16:15 Kotema kes atiar, “Iraas yesi luitojokas araut ikadolitok kakonyen nuka ituŋa, konye ejeŋi Edeke ikusitauon; naarai yenitopolooritai kotuŋa erai yeniketal kakonyen nuka Edeke." 
Luke16:16 “Kejaas ikisila ka inabin kiton Yokana; ameun kapak kaŋin elimonokinio akiro nukajokak nuka ajakanut naka Edeke, ebelakini da ŋinituŋanan kagogoŋ." 
Luke16:17 Konye epatana akuj ka akwap adaun itia aicunyakinet adiopet naka ikisila apalunio. 
Luke16:18 “Ŋolituŋanan loereŋeari akeberu komany ace adotear, ŋol da loemanyi nakireŋeari okilenike adotear." 
Luke16:19 “Kojai etuŋanan lokabaran, lokenapenenei egoe lomuge ka ebaputa loejok, kolakanar ŋinipaaran koboro luetaitaete." 
Luke16:20 Kojai da lokican ekekiror Lasaro, loeperionokino oruteke, kojaas kajimii nuipu." 
Luke16:21 Kimiela ŋesi aimonianakin ararasia nukedoenenete komesa loka ekabaran; koponenenete iŋokwo da aime akejimii. 
Luke16:22 Kosodi kanen kotwana lokican, kodakasi imalaikan atorob naka Aburaam. Kotwana ekabaran da, konukai." 
Luke16:23 Kitonyou akekonye kotoma Okatwak, kanekejaar toma aikilianar naepol, koany Aburaam kama elwana ka Lasaro da katorobuke." 
Luke16:24 Kiworo ebe, ‘Aburaam Papa, kitimoi, kijuk Lasaro kidomak kiŋaren kebokoritike akipi ketojonia akaŋajep; naarai arieba noi kotoma akim na.’" 
Luke16:25 Kobala Aburaam ebe, ‘Okokuka, kiitu ebe ibu ijo kodum nukajokakakon kotoma aijarakon, ka Lasaro da kwaŋin kodum nukaronok; konye kwana italakario ŋes kane, ka jo da kisiriebio." 
Luke16:26 Mere ŋun bon, konye kidiŋikosi kayes ejai asoogot naidul, tetere ŋulluekotosi anyoun kane mam epedorete atubun mamakus, emameete da luepedorete anyoun kaŋina ailamun mamakosi.’" 
Luke16:27 Kotema atiar, ‘Aso papa, keŋaiŋait, kijuka ŋes togo loka papaka," 
Luke16:28 naarai ejaas eoŋ iinacan ikany, tetere ikwenyari kes, kinyeis kesi da adolun aibois na nakaikilianar.’" 
Luke16:29 Konye kobala Aburaam ebe, ‘Ejaas kes kaMusa ka inabin, kiirasi ŋul.’" 
Luke16:30 Kotema atiar, ‘Mam, Aburaam Papa; konye arai kelot etuŋanan loenyouni kokatwak, itoronikinos.’" 
Luke16:31 Kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Arai mam iirarete Musa ka inabin, mam ecamunete karaida kejaru ituŋanan kokatwak.’”" 
Luke17:1 Kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Mam eswakete nuitiguikinete abunore; konye itukwi ituŋanan ŋin yeneyaŋauni ŋun!" 
Luke17:2 Tiejok ituŋanan ŋin aenikin akukuse omurisiŋike, kocakakinai aŋolol itia aitiguikin idiopet kaludidik kalu." 
Luke17:3 Kocoito; arai kediak onacekon, kitoron ŋes; arai kitoronikin kisioni." 
Luke17:4 Arai kediak kamakon irwan akanykaarei kapaaran adiopet, koboŋu mamakon irwan akanykaarei, kobala ebe, ‘Etoronikin,’ kisioni ŋes.”" 
Luke17:5 Kotemasi ikiyakia Ejakait atiar, “Kiyatakinai aiyuunikosi!”" 
Luke17:6 Kotema Ejakait atiar, “Arai kijaas kaiyuun naetia ecokat loka ekaradali, tikilimokis esukamin lo ebe, ‘Koukor, kiraikin aŋolol.’ Tikiirimak yes." 
Luke17:7 “Ido iŋai bo kayesi yenejai ekebulesit loekoriei arai loicokiei amerekekin yenelimokini ŋes atipet napeboŋunio kotoma amana ebe, ‘Kobia atipet kiboikin ainyam’." 
Luke17:8 Arai bo elimokini ŋes ebe, ‘Kitemokinoi ikanyamat lukatiboŋ, koen aŋabet, kijaanak eoŋ, kiton neadaunia eoŋ ainyam ka aimat; kosodi konyet inyami ijo da ka aimat’?" 
Luke17:9 Imalai kereka ŋesi ebulesit naarai eswama nuecorakinitai? 
Luke17:10 Kwape kwaŋin yes da, naidauniata aswam kere nukicorakinitai, kineras ebe, ‘Kirai isio ibulesin lumam ajokis; kiswama bon nukibusakinit aswam.’ ”" 
Luke17:11 Kosodi kanen napelosi Yesu Yerusalem, kitor kidiŋ Samaria ka Galilaya." 
Luke17:12 Napelomari ore ediopet, kiriamunos kalukatapon itomon, lukebwoete kama elwana," 
Luke17:13 kiworoto kobalas ebe, “Wu Yesu, Lokapolon, kitimoi sio.”" 
Luke17:14 Nakeanyunia kes kotema atiar, “Koloto, kitodiaros mama ejaas isasedotin.” Ido napelosete kiswagarai." 
Luke17:15 Kosodi ediopet kakesi nakeanyunia ebe aŋaleu, koboŋu, kitopolo Edeke keporoto loepol." 
Luke17:16 Kibirokin ebuburia akejen nuka Yesu, kimala ŋes. Kerai da ŋol Esamariat." 
Luke17:17 Koboŋok Yesu kiner atiar, “Mam eswagara itomon kere? Ai bo do ejaas kwi ikanykaoŋon?" 
Luke17:18 Mam ca etakanunit edio da aboŋun aitopoloor Edeke dimarai emoit lo?” 
Luke17:19 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Konyou, kolot; kitajar jo akoniiyuun.”" 
Luke17:20 Nakiŋisiata Iparisayon ebe ebuni bo wori ajakanut naka Edeke, Koboŋok kes kotema atiar, “Mam ebuni ajakanut naka Edeke iteio;" 
Luke17:21 kwabo mam ineras ebe, ‘Koany, ejai lailo!’ arai, ‘Ejai laije!’ Naarai koany, ejai ajakanut naka Edeke tomakus.”" 
Luke17:22 Kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Epote rwaru apaarasia, nuimielatar aanyun adiopet kotoma apaarasia nuka Okoku loka etuŋanan, komam ianyunete." 
Luke17:23 Kilimokinete ebe, ‘Koany, ejai laije!’ ‘Koany, ejai lailo!’ Sirikiloto, kwabo sirikitupasi da." 
Luke17:24 Naarai kwape imiliaunia eimilia ameun kowai ediopet loka akuj, inwakit kiton owai ece loka akuj, kwape kwaŋin ejaunia Okoku loka etuŋanan kotoma apaaranike." 
Luke17:25 Konye ibusakinit ber ŋes aiticanio nuipu, kogir atur na." 
Luke17:26 Kwape kejaatar kapaarasia nuka Noa, kwape kwaŋin ejauniata kotoma apaarasia nuka Okoku loka etuŋanan," 
Luke17:27 Konyama, komata, komanya, ka amanyio da, kiton apaaran nakelomaria Noa toma ataker, kijesun akalele komudia kere." 
Luke17:28 Kwape kwaŋin kwape kejaatar kapaarasia nuka Lot; konyama, komata, kogwela, kogwelasi, kiraata, koduko da;" 
Luke17:29 konye kapaaran nakelomunia Lot koSodom, kotep akim ka acukuman abunore kakuj, komudia kere." 
Luke17:30 Ikote nen kapaaran naepukorere Okoku loka etuŋanan," 
Luke17:31 Kapaaran kaŋin, yenejai kuju togo, kojaas ikeboro toma togo, sirikijesun alemun; kwape kwaŋin yenejai mana sirikeboŋu kau," 
Luke17:32 Kiitut aberu naka Lot. 
Luke17:33 Inituŋanan yenekoto aitajar akeijar, itooliori; ka ŋin da yenitooliori akeijar itajari." 
Luke17:34 Katemari yes atiar, kakuare kaŋin ejaunos ituŋa iarei oitada ediopet; eyaŋaario ediopet, inyeinio loce." 
Luke17:35 Ejaunos aŋor aarei iricete nepepe; eyaŋaario adiopet, inyeinio nace. [" 
Luke17:36 Ejaunos ituŋa iarei amana; eyaŋaario ediopet, inyeinio loce]”" 
Luke17:37 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Laali bo, Ejakait?” Kotema kes atiar, “Neejai akuan, etukonokinos da atarukon nen.”" 
Luke18:1 Kolimok kes awaragan, aikwenyar ebe ibusakinit kes ailipenen Edeke komam itapalikina." 
Luke18:2 Kotema kes atiar, “Kojai kolo ekatubon ore ece, lomam eyonit Edeke, kwabo mam kepodo ituŋa." 
Luke18:3 Kojai da apuserut ore ŋol; nakicebokinit abunenen mamake, kobala ebe, ‘Kigaŋai kama kalokasurupika.’" 
Luke18:4 Koŋer ber; konye kokau kotema kotauke atiar, ‘Karaida mam ayoŋit Edeke, karaida mam apodo ituŋa," 
Luke18:5 konye naarai kecebokinit apuserut na, egaŋi ŋes, kenye aitapas eoŋ kanuka arim tiritir neajai.’ ”" 
Luke18:6 Kotema Ejakait atiar, “Kiirasi nuenera ekatubon lomam edolit." 
Luke18:7 Mam kereka igaŋi Edeke luseunake, luemonyakinete paaran ka kuare, etitiŋikinit ŋesi kanukec?" 
Luke18:8 Katemari yes atiar, Igaŋi kes atipet. Konye naebunio Okoku loka etuŋanan, edumuni kereka aiyuun kakwap?”" 
Luke18:9 Kolimok da awaragan na ituŋa lukemunokina ebe eraas kesi luedolito komwaŋito luce; 
Luke18:10 “Kodokasi ituŋa iarei oyekalu ailip, ediopet Eparisayot, loce da eketeleman esolo." 
Luke18:11 Kobwo Eparisayot kilip kwana kotauke ebe, ‘Wu Edeke, kemalai jo naarai mam eoŋ kiputo kicetuŋa, ikaŋatak, ikeŋalak, idotea, karaida bala lo eketeleman esolo." 
Luke18:12 Aluŋenenei eoŋ irwan aarei ŋinisabato, ainanakini da yenikitomonet kotoma kaluadumuni kere.’" 
Luke18:13 Konye kobwo eketeleman esolo kama elwana, kwabo mam ketitinikinit aikeun akekonyen akuj, konye kodipidip aketorob, kobala ebe, ‘Wu Edeke, kitimoi eoŋ ekadiakanaran!’" 
Luke18:14 Katemari yes atiar, Abu ŋol kodok alosit oreke imarakinitai adolit aitelekarit je; naarai ŋinituŋanan yeniturokin itisilio, konye yenitisilikin iturio.”" 
Luke18:15 Koinunai idwe ludidik da tetere etirori kes; konye nakeanyuniata ikesisiak, kitorona kes." 
Luke18:16 Konye Yesu konyarau kes kotema atiar, “Kocamutu idwe ludidik abunore mama ajai, kwabo sirikisimika kes; naarai lueputosi kalu ajakanut naka Edeke erai nakec," 
Luke18:17 Abeit katemari yes atiar, ŋin yenimam iyuuni ajakanut naka Edeke kwape kikoku yenididi, mam cut elomari toma.”" 
Luke18:18 Kiŋit ŋes ekayaiton ediopet ebe, “Ekesisianakinan Iokajokan, keswama anyoika tetere erumi aijar naka ikar kere?”" 
Luke18:19 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kanukinyo kinyaraa eoŋ lokaiokan? Emamei yenikajokan dimarai ediopet, ŋes Edeke." 
Luke18:20 Ijeni aicorakineta ebe: ‘Siridote, Siriari, Sirikokoi, Sirisabanakinenei, Koyoŋitenenei papakon ka totokon.’ ”" 
Luke18:21 Kotema atiar, “Aricit ŋun kere ameun keiditeuka.”" 
Luke18:22 Nakiiraria Yesu ŋun, kotema ŋes atiar, “Eriŋa kiwolikit adiopekirot. Kogwela luijaatar kere, kokoranak lukican, ijaunete moolo kabar kotoma akuj; kosodi kobu, kotup eoŋ.”" 
Luke18:23 Konye nakiiraria ŋun kokadak noi, naarai kebarit noi." 
Luke18:24 Nakesesenia Yesu ŋes kotema atiar, “Etiono cama lukabarak alomar ajakanut naka Edeke!" 
Luke18:25 Epatana ekaal aitor apedot naka ekus, itia ekabaran alomar ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Luke18:26 Kotemasi ŋul lukiirarete atiar, “Aso iŋai bo do epedori aitaiario?”" 
Luke18:27 Konye kotema atiar, “Numam epedorio kotuŋa epedorio kama ejai Edeke.”" 
Luke18:28 Kobala Petero ebe, “Koany, kipou isio kenyeis ikosiboro katuputu jo.”" 
Luke18:29 Kotema kes atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, Emamei etuŋanan loenyeinit etogo arai aberu, arai iinacan, arai ikauriak, arai idwe, kanuka ajakanut naka Edeke," 
Luke18:30 lomam edumuni ipu noi aitelekarit kapak kana, ido kokar luepote aijar naka ikar kere.”" 
Luke18:31 Koyaŋa lutomon ka luarei, kotema kes atiar, “Koany, kidokari alosit Yerusalem, itodolikinio akiro kere nukiwadikaete kolo inabin kama ka Okoku loka etuŋanan," 
Luke18:32 Naarai einakinio mama ejaas Imo, eboliatar, iswamakinio nukepali, imwaanakinio aimul:" 
Luke18:33 edaete ka aiar ŋes; kapaaran da nakiwuniet ejaruni.” 
Luke18:34 Konye mam kes apotu kojenut adis kaŋun; naarai kimunonikinitai kes akirot ŋin, kwabo mam ejenuna nukinerai." 
Luke18:35 Kosodi kanen, nakeapiaria Yeriko, kejai etuŋanan emuduk iboie kawai kerot ilipitoi." 
Luke18:36 Nakiiraria ekodet itorit, kiŋit ebe, “Ikote bo ai ŋun?”" 
Luke18:37 Kolimokis ŋes ebe, “Yesu loko Nasaret itorit.”" 
Luke18:38 Kiworo ebe, “Yesu, okoku loka Daudi, kitimoi eoŋ.”" 
Luke18:39 Ŋul da lukiŋarenito kiretakis tetere ililiŋi: konye ŋes kiyatak noi aiworo ebe, “Wu jo okoku loka Daudi, kitimoi eoŋ.”" 
Luke18:40 Kobwou Yesu, kicorak ayaunio mama ejai, Napekeapiki, kiŋit ŋes ebe," 
Luke18:41 “Ikoto keswamak jo inyo?” Kotema atiar, “Ejakait, akoto kakweny.”" 
Luke18:42 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kokweny: kitaŋaleu jo akoniiyuun.”" 
Luke18:43 Atipet kokweny, kotupa ŋes, itopoloorit Edeke. Nakeanyuniata ituŋa da kere, kituritos Edeke." 
Luke19:1 Koloma Yeriko kitorite kidiŋike," 
Luke19:2 Ido koany, kojai etuŋanan ekekiror Sakayo; korai eketeleman esolo lokapolon, kerai da ekabaran," 
Luke19:3 Kemoot ŋol aanyun Yesu kerai loka epone enyoin, mam epedoro kanuka ekodet, naarai kewuriana ŋesi." 
Luke19:4 Koker kiŋaren, kodoka kuju osukamin, tetere eanyuni; naarai itorunit orot ŋol." 
Luke19:5 Nakedolio Yesu aibois ŋin, kosesen okitoi, kotema atiar, “Sakayo, kodoku atipet; naarai kebusakinit lolo aiboikin togokon.”" 
Luke19:6 Kodoku atipet, kisukunyik ŋes kaiyalama," 
Luke19:7 Nakeanyuniata ituŋa kirurumata kere, kobalas ebe, “Aloma aiboikin ketuŋanan lokadiakanaran.”" 
Luke19:8 Kobwo Sakayo, kotema ŋesi Ejakait atiar, “Koany, Ejakait, akorakini lukican atutubet naka ikaboro; arai da arodit ituŋanan idiobore, atacakini irwan aoŋon.”" 
Luke19:9 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Adolu lolo aitaiario togo lo, naarai erai ŋesi da okoku loka Aburaam." 
Luke19:10 Naarai abu Okoku loka etuŋanan amoot ka aitajar yenikeoliorit.” 
Luke19:11 Nakiirariata ŋun, kiyatak alimokin awaragan, naarai keapie ko Yerusalem, ido naarai komunosi ebe etakanuni ajakanut naka Edeke atipet." 
Luke19:12 Aso kobala ebe, “Kojai etuŋanan lokapolon, kolot akwap naelwana, tetere edumuni ajakanut, kosodi konyet aboŋun," 
Luke19:13 Konyarau itomon kobulesinike, koinak kes ŋinituŋanan arupian atomon, kotema kes atiar, ‘Aso kogwelanasi aitodol neaboŋunio.’" 
Luke19:14 Konye kolaata ŋes ituŋa lukoreke, kiyakiasi ikiyakia atupar ŋes, alimokin ebe, ‘Mam kikoto ŋol ayait sio.’" 
Luke19:15 Kosodi kanen nakeboŋunio, kodumunite akejakanut, kicorak anyaraun ibulesin ŋul luainakinit arupian, tetere ejenuni ameda naadumut kanuka agwelanar." 
Luke19:16 Kobu losodit akonyeneke, kobala ebe, ‘Ejakait, akonirupia emedau ace atomon.’" 
Luke19:17 Kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Iswama ejok, ijo ebulesit loejok! Naarai irai lomunot kakirot naedit noi, koyaŋa apolou naka ireria itomon.’" 
Luke19:18 Kobu lokiareit da, kobala ebe, ‘Ejakait, akonirupia emedau ace akany.’" 
Luke19:19 Kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Ijo da koyaŋa ireria ikany.’" 
Luke19:20 Kobu ece da kobala ebe, ‘Ejakait, koany akonirupia na, naeŋadakinit ogoe." 
Luke19:21 Naarai abu kakurianar jo, naarai irai loininik: ilemuni numam ibwaikinit, idwenyi da numam iyeit.’" 
Luke19:22 Kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Katubokini jo kakiro nuka aitukukon, ijo ibulesit loerono! Ibu kojeni ebe aninik eoŋ, alemi numam ebwaikinit, adwenyi da numam ayeit." 
Luke19:23 Aso kanukinyo mam kiinakinia akarupian mama ejaas ikagwelanarak, tetere neabunio kadum nepepe kamedakec?’" 
Luke19:24 Kobala lukebwoete eapias ebe, ‘Kodemut arupia, koinakis je loka arupian atomon.’" 
Luke19:25 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, ‘Ejakait, ejaas ŋes arupian atomon.’" 
Luke19:26 ‘Katemari yes atiar, yenejai ibore einakinio; konye yenemamei ibore, edemunio ŋin da yenejaas kaŋes." 
Luke19:27 Bobo da ŋul lukasurupoka, lumam akotos eoŋ ayait kes, koyaut ne, koarata kakonyeneka.’ ”" 
Luke19:28 Nakedaunia einer ŋun, kiŋarenik kes adokar Yerusalem." 
Luke19:29 Kosodi kanen nakeapiki Betepage ka Betaniya, komoru loenyaritai loka Iseitunin, kijuka iarei kokesisiak," 
Luke19:30 kobala ebe, “Koloto ore loisesenete; nailomariata toma idumunete ikoku yenika asigiria eenitai, yenimam lem ibwanenit idiotuŋanan: kolacut, koinut." 
Luke19:31 Arai kiŋisi ituŋanan ebe, ‘Kanukinyo ilacariata?’ iboŋokinete ebe, ‘Ejakait ipuda ŋes.’ ”" 
Luke19:32 Koloto lukijukario kodumut kwape kelimokinitere. 
Luke19:33 Napelacunete ikoku yenika asigiria, kobalas ikulepek ebe, “Kanukinyo ilacariata isigiria?”" 
Luke19:34 Koboŋokis ebe, “Ejakait ipuda ŋes.”" 
Luke19:35 Koyaŋaut mama ejai Yesu, kopetanakis isigiria ikecenapen, kisibwanenoto Yesu." 
Luke19:36 Napelosi, kopetanakis ikecenapen orot," 
Luke19:37 Nakeapikinia aijesaret naka Emoru loka Iseitunin, kogeu ekodet kere loka ikesisiak ailel ka aiturit Edeke keporoto loepol kanuka aswamisio kere nukapedor nuaanyut." 
Luke19:38 Kobalas ebe, “Isirereŋitoi Ekabaka loebunit kokiror loka Ejakait! Ainapakin kotoma akuj, ka aibuses da kokuju kakui!”" 
Luke19:39 Ice koParisayon lukejaas toma okodet kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, kitoron ikonikesisiak.”" 
Luke19:40 Koboŋok ebe, “Katemari yes atiar, Arai kililiŋata lu, iworoete do amor.”" 
Luke19:41 Nakeapiki koany ere, komonyak," 
Luke19:42 kobala ebe, “Arai kojeni ijo kapaaran kana akiro nukiinakinete ainapakin! Konye kwana ibwaitai kakonyenekon." 
Luke19:43 Naarai epote apaarasia nukidukokiniata lukasurupokon itutio airigaunia, kiridakinete jo airiamar iwaitin kere," 
Luke19:44 kibirokinete jo kwap, ka ikonidwe kotomakon, komam kinyeiniata amoru naidokokino amoru nace; naarai mam ibu kojen apak naka aanyanariokon.”" 
Luke19:45 Koloma toma oyekalu kogeu aireŋear lukagwelanarak. 
Luke19:46 Kobala kes ebe, “Iwadikatai ebe, ‘Ekatogo eraun etogo lokilipet’; konye yes ituluosi abua naka ikaŋatak.”" 
Luke19:47 Kisisianakini ŋinipaaran kotoma oyekalu, Konye komooto isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak ka ikapolok luka ituŋa amudiar ŋes;" 
Luke19:48 konye mam eanyuna nuepedorete aswam, naarai kokotos noi ituŋa kere akiirar ŋes." 
Luke20:1 Kosodi kanen kapaaran adiopet nakisisianakinia ituŋa koyekalu, ka alimonokin da akiro nukajokak, koponikis ŋes isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak nepepe kimakio." 
Luke20:2 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kolimokinai iswamai ijo nu kapolou anyoin, bobo da iŋai bo kiinakini apolou ŋin?”" 
Luke20:3 Koboŋok ebe, “Eoŋ da keŋisi yes akirot adioper; kolimokis;" 
Luke20:4 aibatis naka Yokana kebuni kereka kotoma akuj arai bo kotuŋa?” 
Luke20:5 Kiŋitanakinos bonik ka bonik, kobalas ebe, “Arai kiitema ebe ‘Kebuni kotoma akuj’, etemari ŋesi atiar, ‘Aso kanukinyo mam kiyuuniata ŋes?’" 
Luke20:6 Konye arai kiitema ebe, ‘Kebuni kotuŋa’ kibiribirete oni ituŋa kamor; naarai acamunito ebe kerai Yokana enabi.”" 
Luke20:7 Koboŋokis ebe mam kejenete nekebunio. 
Luke20:8 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Eoŋ da mam kalimokini yes apolou nakeswamaa nu.”" 
Luke20:9 Kogeu alimokin ituŋa awaragan na ebe, “Abu etuŋanan kira amana naka emusabibu, kititiŋ ikakoriok, kolot akwap ace kiboioror apak naeoj," 
Luke20:10 Kapak naka aidweny kiyakia ebulesit mama ejaas ikakoriok, tetere einakinete araito nuka emusabibu; konye kibuŋata ikakoriok ŋol, kireŋeasi titai." 
Luke20:11 Kiyakia ebulesit ece: kibuŋata ŋol da, kisuruma ileic, kireŋeasi titai." 
Luke20:12 Kiyakia lokiwuniet da: kimusunata ŋol da, kocakasi kiŋa," 
Luke20:13 Kobala ejakait loka amana naka emusabibu ebe, ‘Ekonakini ai? Ejukari okokuka lominat: elemuni eyoŋete ŋes.’" 
Luke20:14 Konye nakeanyuniata ikakoriok, kinerut bonik ka bonik, kobalas ebe, ‘Lo ŋes lokeruman: aso kaarata ŋes, tetere eraun airum nawok.’" 
Luke20:15 Kocakasi kiŋa kamana naka emusabibu, koarata. Aso ikonakini kes ai ejakait loka amana naka emusabibu?" 
Luke20:16 Ebuni emudiari ikakoriok ŋul, einakini ice amana naka emusabibu.” Nakiirariata ŋun, kobalas ebe, “Madi akuj!”" 
Luke20:17 Konye kosesen kes, kotema atiar, “Anyoin apolou naka akirot kana naiwadikatai ebe, ‘Amoru nakeŋerete ikadukok, ŋin ŋes keponi kitaraunai amoru nakapolon naka agor?’" 
Luke20:18 Ŋinituŋanan yenibirokini kuju amoru ŋin ebilibiliun; konye ŋin yenibirokin amoru ipicipicari ŋes cut.” 
Luke20:19 Apotu ikewadikak ka isasedotin lupeti komooto aikamun ŋes kosawa kaŋol, konye kokuriaka ituŋa; naarai apotu kojenut ebe inerakinit kes awaragan ŋin." 
Luke20:20 Kiteikinitoi, kijukasi ikarotak, lukijoseete araut lukabeit, tetere ikamunete ŋes kakiroke, kosodete aijaikin ŋes mama ejai ayait ka apolou naka ekayaiton." 
Luke20:21 Kiŋita kobalas ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, kijeni ebe inera, isisianakini da nukabeit, kwabo mam isei ituŋa, konye isisianakini erot loka Edeke kotoma abeit." 
Luke20:22 Ibus kereka sio ainakin Kaisar esolo, arai bo mam?”" 
Luke20:23 Konye kojeni akecepirianut, kotema kes atiar," 
Luke20:24 “Kitodikinai adenarit. Nakaŋai aput na, ka nuiwadikatai?” Koboŋokis ebe, “Nuka Kaisar.”" 
Luke20:25 Kotema kes atiar, “Aso kotacakis Kaisar nueraas nuka Kaisar, ka Edeke da nueraas nuka Edeke.”" 
Luke20:26 Ido mam apedorete aikamun ŋes kakiroke kakonyen nuka ituŋa; koumokis akeboŋokin koŋatakis. 
Luke20:27 Kopotu ice koSadukayon mamakeŋ, luebalas ebe emamei ajarun, kiŋita ŋes ebe," 
Luke20:28 “Ekesisianakinan, abu Musa kiwadikak sio ebe, arai ketwana onace ketuŋanan, loemanyit, komamei ikoku, ibusakinit onaceke ayaŋaar aberu, kodumak onaceke aur." 
Luke20:29 Aso kejaas iinacan ikanykaarei: komany losodit aberu, kotwana komamei ikoku;" 
Luke20:30 ka lokiareit da," 
Luke20:31 Koyaŋa Iokiwuniet da; ka ice da kere ikanykaarei, kotwaka komam inyeinito idwe." 
Luke20:32 Kawasia kotwana aberu da," 
Luke20:33 Aso kotoma ajarun eraun ŋin aberu nakaŋai? Naarai kemanyito ikanykaarei kere.” 
Luke20:34 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Emanyete odwe luka akwapin kanu, emanyario da;" 
Luke20:35 konye ŋul luimaritai araut luibusakinito adolokin akwap ya ka ajarun kokatwak, mam emanyete, karaida amanyio." 
Luke20:36 Naarai mam epedorete atwakare bobo: naarai eriakakinos ka imalaikan; kes da eraas idwe luka Edeke, kanu eraatar idwe luka ajarun." 
Luke20:37 Konye ebe itaiarunio lukatwak, abu Musa da kitodik, kotoma owai laka Ekiyot, nakelimoria Ejakait araut Edeke laka Aburaam, ka Edeke laka Isaak, ka Edeke loka Yakob da." 
Luke20:38 Mam ŋes erai Edeke laka lukatwak, dimarai loka lukajarak; naarai ejarete kere kamakeŋ,”" 
Luke20:39 Koboŋokis ikewadikak ice, kotemasi atiar, “Ekesisianakinan, iner ejok.”" 
Luke20:40 Naarai mam bobo etitiŋikino aiŋit akirot. 
Luke20:41 Kotema kes atiar, “Biai bo ebalatatar ituŋa ebe erai Kristo okoku loka Daudi?" 
Luke20:42 Naarai Daudi elopet inera koitabo loka Isabulin ebe, ‘Abu Ejakait kotema Ekajakait atiar, Kiboikin akanika nakoteten." 
Luke20:43 Aitodol neebwaikinia Iukasurupokon araut iicoloŋ yenika akejekon.’ 
Luke20:44 Aso enyarit Daudi ŋes Ejakait, kikonakini bo ai erai ikekoku?”" 
Luke20:45 Kopupete ituŋa kere, elimokini ikekesisiak ebe," 
Luke20:46 “Kocoito ikewadikak, luekotos alosit konapitos ikason Iueojak, kominasi aiyogao kagwelanareta, ka aiboikin aiboisio nukokuiu katukosia, ka iicoloŋo lukapolou kopucin;" 
Luke20:47 ecamete itogoi luka apuserun, kanuka ejose da ilipete ailipasia nueojak; edumunete ŋul atubokinio naitelekarit.”" 
Luke21:1 Kikeu akekonyen, koany ikabarak icakanakinete ainakinetakec toma aiŋadis," 
Luke21:2 Koany apuserut adiopet nakican ecakakini ikapun iarei. 
Luke21:3 Kotema atiar, “Abeit katemari yes atiar, acakaki apuserut ŋin nakican luipu adepar ice kere:" 
Luke21:4 Naarai acakanakis ŋul kere kotoma luebarara, konye ŋin kotoma ocanike acakaki Iukejaatar kere.”" 
Luke21:5 Nakineratar ice nuka eyekalu, kwape kitubusitere kamor nuejok ka ainakineta, kotema atiar," 
Luke21:6 “Ŋun nuisesenete, epote apaarasia numam esalakinia amoru adiopet kuiu kanace namam etiyakinio.”" 
Luke21:7 Kiŋita ŋes ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, ejaunete bo ŋun wori? Anyoin da aanyunet naeapuuniata ŋun adolun?”" 
Luke21:8 Kotema atiar, “Kocoito kinyein aitapaar yes; naarai epote luipu kokirorika, kobalas ebe, ‘Eoŋ ŋopeŋol!’ Ebe da, ‘Aapuu apak!’ Aso sirikitupasi ŋul." 
Luke21:9 Naiirariata rwaru nuka ijiisio ka iceleta, sirikikuriakaros, naarai ibusakinit ber ŋun ajaun, konye mam awasia edoluni atipet.”" 
Luke21:10 Kosodi kotema kes atiar, “Enyoikini ateker asurokin ateker, ka ajakanut da asurokin ajakanut." 
Luke21:11 Ejaununete amaraneta nuepolok nuka akwap, ejaunun da ebeli, ka atular kaiboisio nuegelegela; ejaunete nuketasuro ka aanyuneta nukos abunore kotoma akui." 
Luke21:12 Konye eriŋa ŋun edoluno, kikamunete yes, kireete, kijaikinete yes kakonyen nuka atukosia ka aidarisia, kiyaŋaario kakonyen nuka ikabakan ka ikayaitok kanuka ekakiror." 
Luke21:13 Eraunete ŋun akajenak kamakus. 
Luke21:14 Aso kibwaikisi otauonokus ebe sirikiwomoomata ber nuiboŋokinete; 
Luke21:15 naarai kainakinete yes aituk ka acoa, numam lukasurupokus kere epedorete aitepeg karaida airebokin." 
Luke21:16 Kijaikinete ikauriakakus, ka iinacanakus, ka lukatekerekus, ka ipaperokus, earete ice kayesi;" 
Luke21:17 kiŋarunete yes ituŋa kere kanuka ekakiror. 
Luke21:18 Konye mam eoliori etimat ediopet loka akwesikus. 
Luke21:19 Kotoma atitiŋikinikus ikucaunete akusiijar. 
Luke21:20 “Konye naianyuniata irimorito ajoresio Yerusalem, aso kojenut ebe aapiki amudiarioke." 
Luke21:21 Ŋes konyet ekeriata ŋul luejaas Yudaya oroŋan, kolomutu ŋul luejaas kotomake kiŋa, sirikelomasi ŋul luejaas amanat;" 
Luke21:22 naarai eraas nu apaarasia nuka einyaŋane, tetere edolete kere nuiwadikatai." 
Luke21:23 Itukwi kes nuepotiete, ka nuitanakete da kapaarasia kaŋun! Naarai ejaun ationus naepol toma akwap, ka anyunyura da asurokin ateker na," 
Luke21:24 Eŋianakinere akwanis naka ekileŋ, ijoreorio toma atekerin kere; icakacakaete Imo Yerusalem, aitodol naedolioto apakio nuka Imo." 
Luke21:25 Ejaunete moolo aanyuneta toma akoloŋ ka elap ka aacer, ido toma akwap aburun naka atekerin, nuebuonokinos kanuka agat naka aŋolol ka akailan;" 
Luke21:26 ipirisiaros itauon luka ituŋa kanuka akurian, ido kanuka aidaret akiro nueponikinito akwap: naarai itamaranio nukapedor nuka akuj." 
Luke21:27 Kosodi konyet eanyunete Okoku loka etuŋanan ebuni kodou kapedor ka aibuses naepol. 
Luke21:28 Konye naegeuniata ŋun atakanun, kikeutu akwesikus, kosesenata kuju, naarai aapu alakuniokus.”" 
Luke21:29 Kolimok kes awaragan ebe, “Koanyutu etini, ka icekito kere." 
Luke21:30 Apak naegeuniata ailib, ianyunete, ijenunete da kanukus ebe aaput apaarasia nuka aidweny," 
Luke21:31 Aso do, yes da, naianyuniata akiro ŋun ketakanut, kojenutu ebe aapu ajakanut naka Edeke." 
Luke21:32 Abeit katemari yes atiar, Mam edaun atur na, aitodol naejaunotor akiro kere." 
Luke21:33 Edaunos akuj ka akwapin; konye akakiro mam edaunos cut. 
Luke21:34 “Konye kocoito yesi kinyek airaŋanut ka emeret ka aiyaloŋoŋ da naka aijar kana aisilaŋirir ikusitauon, konesakin apaaran ŋin kwape ipokia akuluma," 
Luke21:35 Naarai edolokini ituŋa kere luejaas akwapin kere. 
Luke21:36 Konye kokwenya apakio kere, kiŋaiŋaata tetere idumunete agogoŋ aiku kakiro ŋun kere nuedolokinete, ka aibwo da kakonyen nuka Okoku loka etuŋanan.”" 
Luke21:37 Kisisianakinenei ŋinipaaran koyekalu, konye kolosenenei apero kuare moru loenyaritai loka Iseitunin." 
Luke21:38 Kodilenenete ituŋa kere tupuruc sek alosit mama ejai oyekalu akiirar ŋes. 
Luke22:1 Kosodi koapu epucit loka Imugatin lumam itubuunitoi loenyaritai Aleleŋ. 
Luke22:2 Komootos isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak epone loka aiar ŋes; naarai apotu kokuriaka ituŋa," 
Luke22:3 Kolomak Satan Yuda loenyaritai Isikariot, lokerai ediopet kotomon ka luarei;" 
Luke22:4 kolot kinerut ka lusasedotin lupeti, ka ikapolokitok iserikalei, epone loka aijaikin ŋes akaninikec." 
Luke22:5 Kiyalamikinos, kitutukoto ainakin ŋes arupian." 
Luke22:6 Kocam, komo apak naka aijaikin ŋes mamakec, komamei ekodet." 
Luke22:7 Kodol apaaran naka Imugatin lumam itubuunitoi, naibusiar aaria imerekekin lukaleleŋ." 
Luke22:8 Kiyakia Yesu Petero ka Yokana kobala ebe, “Koloto kitemonokis lukaleleŋ kanuwok, tetere kinyami.”" 
Luke22:9 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Ikoto ketemokis lali?”" 
Luke22:10 Kotema kes atiar, “Koany, nailomariata ore, iriamunos ketuŋanan loibwokit amot naka akipi; kotupasi ŋes, kolomasi togo loelomari ŋesi," 
Luke22:11 Ilimokinete elopet etogo ebe, ‘Ebala Ekesisianakinan ebe, Ani bo agola nakipejok, neanyamakini lukaleleŋ nepepe kikakesisiak?’" 
Luke22:12 Kitodikini ŋesi yes agola naepol nakokuju naepesitai; kitemonokis nen.” 
Luke22:13 Koloto, kodumutu kwape kelimokinia; kitemonokis lukaleleŋ," 
Luke22:14 Nakedolio apak, kiboikin ainyam nepepe kikekesisiak." 
Luke22:15 Kotema kes atiar, “Abu kemiela noi aimor kayes lukaleleŋ lu, eriŋa eoŋ kiticana;" 
Luke22:16 naarai katemari yes atiar, Mam anyami bobo Iukaleleŋ kiton naitodolikinere kotoma ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Luke22:17 Kolem akoli, kedau aimal kobala ebe, “Kolemutu na, kijaanakinos:" 
Luke22:18 naarai katemari yes atiar, Amear kwana mam amasi araito nuka emusabibu kiton neebunio ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
Luke22:19 Kolem emugati, kedau aimal, kobilibil, koinak kes, kobala ebe, “Lo ŋes akakuan, nakeinakinio kanukus: kiswamaenenete kwaŋin akiitunitor eoŋ,”" 
Luke22:20 Ka akoli da kwape kwaŋin kedautu ainyam, kobala ebe, “Akoli na erai aitutuket nakitetet kotoma aokotoka, nuebukoros kanukus." 
Luke22:21 Konye koany, akan naka ŋol kalokabilakini ebotet ejai keoŋ omesa." 
Luke22:22 Naarai elosi Okoku loka etuŋanan kwape kelosikinitere; konye itukwi etuŋanan ŋol loebilakini ŋes ebotet!” 
Luke22:23 Kogeutu aiŋitanar bonik ebe Iŋai bo kakesi ekoto aswam akirot ŋin. 
Luke22:24 Kolom epeget kotomakec ebe, Iŋai bo loeomitai araut lokapolon." 
Luke22:25 Kotema kes atiar, “Irumitos ikabakan lukacekwapin ikecetuŋa; ŋul da lukapedor kamakec enyaritai ikeswamak ajokis." 
Luke22:26 Konye yes mam ikote kwaŋin, dimarai lokapolon kamakus koraun bala erai lodidi, ka lokeŋarenikinon da bala ŋol loijaanakini." 
Luke22:27 Naarai iŋai bo lokapolon, ŋol loiboikini ainyam, arai bo ŋol lojaanakini? Mere tope je loiboikini ainyam? Konye ajai eoŋ kokidiŋikus bala ekejaanakinan." 
Luke22:28 “Iraas yesi luipotu kotitiŋikis keoŋ kotoma acodunioka; 
Luke22:29 eoŋ da keŋadakinit yes ajakanut, kwape keŋadakinitor Papaka eoŋ," 
Luke22:30 tetere inyamete ka aimat komesaka kotoma ajakanutuka, ka aiboikin oicoloŋo luka ajakanut, itubokinete atekerin atomon kanuarei nuka Isirael." 
Luke22:31 “Simon, Simon, koany, enit Satan yes, tetere kipiesi kwape kalos," 
Luke22:32 Konye kelipak eoŋ jo kinyek akoniiyuun akurwor; ijo da naibelokinor, kitogogoŋ ikoniinacan.”" 
Luke22:33 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, etemokino aupar kajo aenio, kiton atwanare da.”" 
Luke22:34 Kotema atiar, “Kalimokini jo, Petero, ebe mam lolo ekokor eruikini aitodol nakiŋerio eoŋ irwan auni ebe mam kijeni.”" 
Luke22:35 Kiŋit kes ebe, “Nakejukaritor yes emamei eriagi, karaida ecoe, karaida amuk, ipotu kereka kipudas imodiobore?” Kobalas ebe, “Mam,”" 
Luke22:36 Kotema kes atiar, “Konye kwana, yenejai eriagi koyaŋa, ka yenikecoe da kwape kwaŋin. Yenemamei ekileŋ kogwela ekelou, kogwelunia." 
Luke22:37 Naarai katemari yes atiar, Ibusakinit ŋun nuewadikatai aitodolikinio mamakaŋ ebe, ‘Aponi kimarakinai nepepe ka lukepali’; naarai nukabeito eoŋ ejaas aitodolikiniokec.”" 
Luke22:38 Kobalas ebe, “Ejakait, koany, ejaas ne ikileŋa iarei.” Kobala kes ebe, “Aso do.”" 
Luke22:39 Kolom, kolot Moru loka Iseitunin, kwape atapitor; kotupasi ikekesisiak da." 
Luke22:40 Nakedolio aibois ŋin kotema kes atiar, “Kilipa, kinyeis alomar toma acodunio.”" 
Luke22:41 Kotiakar ŋesi elopet bala apak naetiakara amoru, kokukokin, kilip," 
Luke22:42 ebe, “Wu Papa, arai ikoto, kolema akoli na kamakaŋ; konye mere nuakoto eoŋ, dimarai nuikoto ijo kiswamai.”" 
Luke22:43 Kitakanikin ŋes emalaika loabuni kokuju, kitogogoŋ ŋes." 
Luke22:44 Kosodi kanuka aikilianar kiyatak noi ailip; kosubito ainyinyirake bala imany luka aokot nuedoenenete kwap," 
Luke22:45 Nakenyounio kotoma ailipike, kobu mama ejaas ikesisiak kodum kes ejotoete kanuka aiturur." 
Luke22:46 Kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo ijotooto? Konyoutu kilipa kinyeis alomar toma acodunio.”" 
Luke22:47 Atipet napinera ŋesi, koany, kotakan ekodet, iŋarenikinit etuŋanan loenyaritai Yuda, ediopet kotomon ka luarei. Kikunyak mama ejai Yesu tetere enui." 
Luke22:48 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Yuda, ibilakini kereka ijo Okoku loka etuŋanan ebotet kainu?”" 
Luke22:49 Ŋul da lukejaas die kaŋes, kojenutu nuekotosi adoikin, kobalas ebe, “Ejakait, kajepejepata ca kikileŋa?”" 
Luke22:50 Ediopet kakesi kojepe ebulesit loka losasedoti lopeti kotubo akekit nakoteten," 
Luke22:51 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Kinyeis ŋun!” Kotiro akekit kitaŋaleu." 
Luke22:52 Kosodi kobala Yesu isasedotin lupeti ka ikapolokitok luka eyekalu ka imakio lukeponikinito ŋes ebe, “Ilomutu ca ikapito ikileŋa ka ibelai bala aikamun ekaŋatan?" 
Luke22:53 Apaarasia kere ajaenena eoŋ nenipe kayes toma oyekalu, konye mam ipotu kikamut eoŋ. Konye lo erai ekusisawa, ka apedor naka amuton.”" 
Luke22:54 Kosodete kikamut ŋes, koyaata togo loka losasedoti lopeti, konye kotupite Petero kama elwana." 
Luke22:55 Kedaut ainokokin akim kidiŋ alaro, kiboikinos nepepe, kiboie Petero da kokidiŋikec," 
Luke22:56 Kanen koany apese ŋes, iboie kaneejai akim, kojene, kobala ebe, “Ajaas nan etuŋanan lo nenipe kaŋes.”" 
Luke22:57 Konye koŋer, kobala ebe, “Ŋo ba na, mam eoŋ ajeni ŋes,”" 
Luke22:58 Nediokasilon koany ece ŋes, kobala ebe, “Ijo da irai lokec.” Konye Koboŋok Petero ebe, “Ijo ba lo, mere eoŋ,”" 
Luke22:59 Ketubor bala esawa ediopet kitogogoŋ ece ebe, “Abeit ajai lo nepepe kaŋes; naarai erai ŋesi da Egalilayat.”" 
Luke22:60 Konye kobala Petero ebe, “Ijo ba lo, mam ajeni nuinera ijo.” Atipet napinera ŋesi koruik ekokor." 
Luke22:61 Kibelokin Ejakait kosesen Petero. Kiitu Petero akirot ya naka Ejakait, nakelimokinit ŋes ebe, “Lolo, eriŋa ekokor eruikino, kiŋeri eoŋ irwan auni.”" 
Luke22:62 Koloma kiŋa komony noi. 
Luke22:63 Kosodete ituŋa lukikamunete Yesu koboliatar ŋes, kinomonomata;" 
Luke22:64 korapanakis akekonye kiŋita atiar, “Kodwaru cani! Iŋai bo kinom jo?”" 
Luke22:65 Koinyanakinete da kakiro nuipu nuka amoromor. 
Luke22:66 Kosodi kiwala akwap, kotukonokin atukot naka imakio luka ituŋa, ka isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak; koyautu toma aurianetekec, kobalas ebe," 
Luke22:67 “Arai irai ijo Kristo, kolimokinai.” Kobala ebe, “Karaida kaalimokis yes, mam iyuunete cut;" 
Luke22:68 Arai keeŋit yes, mam iboŋokinete." 
Luke22:69 Konye amear natikwana iboikin Okoku loka etuŋanan akan nakoteten naka apedor naka Edeke.” 
Luke22:70 Kobalas kere ebe, “Aso irai kereka ijo Okoku loka Edeke?” Kobala kes ebe, “Yes ibalas ebe arai eoŋ.”" 
Luke22:71 Kobalas ebe, “Kipudar bo inyo bobo nuitejenunete? Naarai kiira oni ikulepek akiro nuka aitukuke.”" 
Luke23:1 Konyou atukot kere, koyaŋaasi Yesu mama ejai Pilato." 
Luke23:2 Kogeutu aosan, kotemasi atiar, “Kianyu lo itapaari atekerekosi, ka aiteŋer ituŋa ainanakin Kaisar esolo, ebala ebe ŋes elopet erai Kristo ekabaka.”" 
Luke23:3 Kiŋit Pilato ŋes ebe, “Irai kereka ijo ekabaka loka Iyudayan?” Koboŋok ebe, “Ijo ibala.”" 
Luke23:4 Kobala Pilato isasedotin lupeti ka ikodeta ebe, “Mam aanyunit akirot naerono kotuŋanan kalo.”" 
Luke23:5 Konye kiketakis kesi noi, kobalas ebe, “Isidiki ituŋa, isisianakini kotoma Yudaya kere, ameun koGalilaya kiton ne da.”" 
Luke23:6 Kiira Pilato ŋun, kiŋit arai erai etuŋanan ŋol Egalilayat." 
Luke23:7 Nakejenu ebe erai eyaitono loka Kerode, kijuka ŋes mama ejai Kerode, naarai kejai ŋesi da Yerusalem kapaarasia kaŋun," 
Luke23:8 Kosodi napekeanyu Kerode Yesu, kiyalamikin noi, naarai abu kokoto lem aanyun ŋes, naarai abu kiiranar akekiro, komuno aanyun aanyunet naiswamai." 
Luke23:9 Kiŋiriŋit ŋes kakiro nuipu; konye ŋes mam eboŋokino amodiokirot. 
Luke23:10 Kobwaata isasedotin lupeti ka ikewadikak, kiwosata ŋes kakiro nuipu." 
Luke23:11 Kosodete Kerode nepepe kikeserikalei kowena Yesu, koboliatar; kitanapata anapito naibus, kinyakas mama ejai Pilato." 
Luke23:12 Kosodi kapaaran kaŋin kominunos do Kerode ka Pilato, naarai kekolosi lem." 
Luke23:13 Kosodi kotukonok Pilato isasedotin lupeti ka ikayaitok ka ituŋa," 
Luke23:14 kotema kes atiar, “Kiinut etuŋanan lo kwape loitapaari ituŋa, eoŋ da eŋitana ŋes kakonyenekus, ido koany, mam abu kaany amodiodiakaret kotoma akiro ŋun kere nuiwosatotor ŋes." 
Luke23:15 Karaida Kerode, naarai enyaku ŋes mamawok. Aso koany, emamei akirot kere naeswamat naibusakinit atwania;" 
Luke23:16 kanuka ŋun alecori ŋes kasodi aosikin.” [ 
Luke23:17 Kibusakinit ŋes aosikin kes ediopet kopucit.] 
Luke23:18 Konye kiworoto kere nepepe ebe, “Koyaŋa lo, koosik sio Baraba.”" 
Luke23:19 Kerai ŋesi etuŋanan lokeenitai kanuka aipaliikin kotoma ore, ka aiar da," 
Luke23:20 Kosodi kiner Pilato kakes bobo, kokoto aosikin Yesu;" 
Luke23:21 konye kiworoto ebe, “Kibubuk, kibubuk baa!”" 
Luke23:22 Kolimok irwan nakiwuniet ebe, “Kanukinyo, naanyoin aronis naeswamat lo? Mam aanyunit kamakeŋ adiokirot naibusakinit atwania; kanuka ŋun alecori ŋes kasodi aosikin.”" 
Luke23:23 Konye kes kiketakis, kilipa kiporotoi luepolok ebe ibusakinit ŋes aibubukinio. Kipikosi iporotoikec." 
Luke23:24 Kotub Pilato kwape eŋaiŋaitotor. 
Luke23:25 Koosik etuŋanan lokeenitai kanuka aipaliikin ka aiar, lokilipete; konye koinak Yesu aiswamakinio kwape kekototor." 
Luke23:26 Nakeyaŋariata ŋes, kikamut Simon loka Kurene, lokebuni kamanat, kisirioŋa emusalaba, arionit atupitor Yesu," 
Luke23:27 Kotupite ekodet loepol loka ituŋa, ka aŋor da nukedipidipeete atorobusio ibworosi ŋes." 
Luke23:28 Konye kibelokin Yesu kobala ebe, “Yes apesur nuko Yerusalem, sirikiimonyata eoŋ, konye komonya akulepek, ka ikusidwe." 
Luke23:29 Naarai koany, epote apaarasia nuetemariata atiar, ‘Isirereŋitoi arakanin, ka aliligeta numam eurito, ka ikisin da lumam itanakito!’" 
Luke23:30 Kanen egeunete kesi alimokin iroŋan ebe, ‘Kibirunos mamakosi’; ka iukon da ebe, ‘Koraparai’." 
Luke23:31 Naarai arai kiswamata nu kokitoi loepalal, ikonakinete bo do ai kaloeonit?”" 
Luke23:32 Koyaŋaasi ice da iarei, ikeswamak nueroko, aario nenipe kaŋes," 
Luke23:33 Nakedolioto aibois naenyaritai Abelekek naka Akou, kibubukis ŋes nen, ka kwi ikeswamak nueroko, ediopet akanike nakoteten, ka ediopet da akanike nakokediany." 
Luke23:34 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Papa, kisioni kes; naarai mam ejenete nuiswamaete.” Kokorokorata ikenapen kailamilam eroet." 
Luke23:35 Kobwoete ituŋa esesenete; konye ikayaitok koinyanakinete kobalas ebe, “Etajari lem ice; kitaiarun ŋes elopet, arai erai kito Kristo loka Edeke, Loseunake!”" 
Luke23:36 Kokienatar iserikalei da, koloto koinutu ŋes ebino loedwar ria;" 
Luke23:37 kobalas ebe, “Arai irai cani Ekabaka loka lyudayan, kitaiarun jo elopet!”" 
Luke23:38 Kujuke da kojai aiwadikaet ebe, “LO ŊES EKABAKA LOKA IYUAYAN.”" 
Luke23:39 Ediopet ka ikeswamak nueroko lukikajakinitai koluik ŋes kobala ebe, “Mere ijo Kristo? Kitaiarun bon ka sio da!”" 
Luke23:40 Koboŋok loce kitoron ebe, “Mam jo iyonit Edeke, naarai ijai ijo toma atubokinio napena?" 
Luke23:41 Erai na nakabeit kamawok; naarai kitacakinio nukibusakinito kanuka aswamisiowok; konye lo mam iswamat adiokirot naerono.” 
Luke23:42 Kotema atiar, “Wu Yesu, kiitunoi eoŋ nailomaria toma ajakanutukon.”" 
Luke23:43 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Abeit katemari jo atiar, lolo ijaun nepepe keoŋ Paradais.”" 
Luke23:44 Kedol bala esawa lokikanyetekape, komutonor akwap kere kiton osawa lokikanyetekaoŋon." 
Luke23:45 Komamu aica naka akoloŋ; kocila aigalisit naka aibois nakalaunan kaarei. 
Luke23:46 Kodelo Yesu keporoto loepol ebe, “Wu Papa, ebwaikini ekamoyo akaninikon.” Kedau einer ŋun, kiridak." 
Luke23:47 Keanyu ekapolokiton nuadoikis, kitur Edeke, kobala ebe, “Abeit kerai etuŋanan lo loedolit.”" 
Luke23:48 Ikodeta da kere luatukokina aanyun ŋun, keanyutu nuadoikis, koboŋosi ore edipidipeete atorobusio." 
Luke23:49 Kere da lukejenete ŋes, ka aŋor nuketupito ŋes anyoun koGalilaya, kobwoete kama elwanikina, esesenete akiro ŋun." 
Luke23:50 Ido koany, kojai etuŋanan ekekiror Yosep, lokerai lokaurianet, etuŋanan loejok loedolit da." 
Luke23:51 (Mam ŋes acamunit ainerunikec ka aswamisioitikec da.) Kerai ŋesi loka Arimataya, ere ediopet loka Iyudayan, edaret ŋesi ajakanut naka Edeke." 
Luke23:52 Kolot ŋol mama ejai Pilato, kilip akuan naka Yesu." 
Luke23:53 Kolacu, konunukik ogoe loka ebaputa, kiperik ates nakikeitoi atiiba, namam lem kiperikinitoi idiotuŋanan." 
Luke23:54 Kerai apaaran naka Aitemonokin, koapie asabato ageun." 
Luke23:55 Kotupito aŋor nukepote kaŋes koGalilaya, koanyutu ates, ka epone lokiperikinere akekuan." 
Luke23:56 Koboŋosi kitemonokis lueuru maa ka akinyet. 
Luke24:1 Kiyeŋutu kapaaran nakasabato, kwape kejaar aicorakinet. Konye kapaaran nasodit nakasabato, tupuruc sek, koloto ates, koyaŋaasi lueuru maa lukitemokinito." 
Luke24:2 Kodumut amoru kikokorior kates. 
Luke24:3 Kolomasi toma mam eanyuna akuan naka Ejakait Yesu. 
Luke24:4 Kosodi kanen, napebuonokinos kanuka akirot kaŋin, koany, kobwaata ituŋa iarei aapu kakes enapito inapen luimilias;" 
Luke24:5 nakekuriakarotor kesi ka aitulur akonyenekec kwap, kotemasi ŋul atiar, “Kanukinyo imoototor lokajaran mama ejaas lukatwak?" 
Luke24:6 Emamei kane, konye ajaru, Kiitutu kwape enerar kayes eroko ejai Galilaya," 
Luke24:7 ebe ibusakinit Okoku loka etuŋanan ainakinio akanin nuka ikadiakanarak, ka aibubukinio, ka ajarun da kapaaran nakiwuniet.”" 
Luke24:8 Kiitut akiroke," 
Luke24:9 koboŋosi kates, kolimokis lutomon kadiopet ka ice da kere, akiro ŋun kere," 
Luke24:10 Keraas kesi Mariam Magadalene, ka Yoana, ka Mariam toto naka Yakob, ka aŋor ace nuajaas nepepe kakes, nualimokinete ikiyakia akiro ŋun." 
Luke24:11 Kosubito akiro ŋun kakonyenekec bala nukabaŋaanut; mam apotu kiyuut kes. 
Luke24:12 Konye konyou Petero, koker kiton ates; kokukum kireik toma, koany igoen luka ebaputa egitara; koboŋo ore eumokinit nuajaut." 
Luke24:13 Ido koany, kapaaran kaŋin alosete iarei kakesi ore ediopet ekekiror Emao, lokelwanikina ko Yerusalem bala amairon akanykaarei," 
Luke24:14 kineranakinos kesi bonik akiro ŋun kere nuadoikis. 
Luke24:15 Napinerasi epeganakinos, kikunyak Yesu elopet koupakinos kakes." 
Luke24:16 Konye koraparai akecekonye kinyeis ajenun ŋes," 
Luke24:17 Kotema kes atiar, “Akiro anyoika ŋun nuineranakinos ilosete?” Kobwaata ekadakinito." 
Luke24:18 Kosodi ediopet kakes, ekekiror Keleopa, Koboŋok ebe, “Ijo bon ipejonikinit ko Yerusalem tape mam ijeni nuadoikis nen kapaarasia kanu?”" 
Luke24:19 Kotema kes atiar, “Anyoika?” Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Akiro nuka Yesu loko Nasaret, lokerai enabi lokapedor kotoma aswamisio ka akiro kakonyen nuka Edeke ka ituŋa da kere." 
Luke24:20 Bobo da epone loejaikiniata ŋes isasedotin lupeti ka ikayaitokowok toma atubokinio naka atwanare, kibubukis," 
Luke24:21 Konye kipou isio kamunosi ebe ŋes loekoto alakun Isirael. Eebo, keja ŋun da, lolo ŋes apaaran nakiwuniet ameun naeswamatar akiro ŋun." 
Luke24:22 Bobo da, kituwumokis sio ace kaŋor nukokodetekosi, nuadilito sek ates," 
Luke24:23 mam eanyuna akekuan; kopotu ebalas ebe etakanikina kes imalaikan luabalas ebe ejari ŋesi. 
Luke24:24 Ice da lukejaas nenipe kasio apotu koloto ates, koanyut kwape kwaŋin kwape eneratar aŋor kwa; konye mam apotu koanyutu ŋes.”" 
Luke24:25 Kotema kes atiar, “Wu yes luedit aijen, luiyapete da itauon aiyuun kere nukineras inabin!" 
Luke24:26 Mam kereka ebusakinit Kristo aiticanio ŋun, ka alomar da toma aibusesuke?”" 
Luke24:27 Kosodi ageun kama ka Musa ka inabin kere kitejen kotoma kanukiwadikatai kere akiro nuabeito ŋes. 
Luke24:28 Keapikis ere lokelosete, kosubite bala elitor kiŋaren;" 
Luke24:29 konye kitiŋaasi ŋes, kobalas ebe, “Kosalak ne kasio, naarai ekamus akwap, aapu apaaran adaun.” Koloma kosal kakes." 
Luke24:30 Kosodi nakiboioto kakes enyamete, kolem emugati, kisirereŋ, kobilibil koinak kes." 
Luke24:31 Kopukoroi akecekonye kojenut ŋes; koolio kakonyenekec. 
Luke24:32 Kotemanaros bonik atiar, “Mam tope amulaete iwokotauon naenerar kaoni korot, ka aikujonokin oni nukiwadikatai?”" 
Luke24:33 Konyout kosawa kaŋope kaŋol koboŋosi Yerusalem, kodumut lutomon ka lodiopet etukokina, kes ka lukejaas nepepe kakes," 
Luke24:34 ebalas ebe, “Abeit ajaru Ejakait, etakanikin ŋesi Simon,”" 
Luke24:35 Kes da kolimokis akiro kwa nukorot, ka epone lokitejenunor mamakec kotoma abilibil emugati." 
Luke24:36 Napinerasi akiro ŋun kobwo Yesu elopet kokidiŋikec, kotema kes atiar, “Kinapakinos.”" 
Luke24:37 Konye korieŋutu kokuriakata noi, koomitos ebe aanyut etoil." 
Luke24:38 Kotema kes atiar, “Kanukinyo iyaloŋoŋooto, kanukinyo da iŋitanarotor kotauonokus?" 
Luke24:39 Koanyutu akakanin ka akakeje, ebe eoŋ lopelo: kotiroroi, koanyutu; naarai emamei etoil akuan, ka akojo da, kwape ianyuniata ejaas eoŋ.”" 
Luke24:40 Kedau einer ŋun, kitodik kes akekanin ka akekeje," 
Luke24:41 Naarokotor mam iyuuna kanuka aiyalama, koumokis da, kotema kes atiar, “Ejaas yes idisinyamat?”" 
Luke24:42 Koinakis atutubet naka agar naipoo. 
Luke24:43 Kolem, konyam kakonyenekec." 
Luke24:44 Kotema kes atiar, “Nu kes akakiro, nuabu kalimok yes, naariŋar ajai kayes, ebe ibusakinit kitodolikinos akiro kere nuiwadikatai kokisila luka Musa, ka inabin, ka isabulin, nukabeito.”" 
Luke24:45 Kosodi kikujok akececoa ajenun nukiwadikatai. 
Luke24:46 Kotema kes atiar, “Kwaŋin iwadikatai ebe ibusakinit Kristo aiticanio, ka ajarun da kotoma okatwak kapaaran nakiwuniet." 
Luke24:47 Ebe da elimonokinio atekerin kere kokirorike aitoronikin ka aisionio naka adiakanareta, agear ko Yerusalem," 
Luke24:48 iraas yesi da ikajenak luka akiro kaŋun. 
Luke24:49 Ido koany, kejukakini yes aisumunet naka Papaka; konye kiboikinos ore, aitodol nekitanapere yes apedor naebuni kokuiu.”" 
Luke24:50 Kosodi kiŋarenik kes kiton Betaniya, korio akekanin kisirereŋ kes." 
Luke24:51 Kosodi kanen napisirereŋi kes, kotiakar kamakec, koyaŋaarai toma akuj." 
Luke24:52 Komaata ŋes, koboŋosi Yerusalem kailel naepol:" 
Luke24:53 Kojaenenas duc toma oyekalu, ituritos Edeke." 
John1:1 Kageunet ajai Akirot, ajai Akirot mama ejai Edeke, korai Akirot Edeke," 
John1:2 Kojai ŋol kageunet mama ejai Edeke. 
John1:3 Kesubio iboro kere kanukeŋ; kemamei ŋesi mam kesubi ibore kere yenikesubio. 
John1:4 Kojai aijar tomakeŋ; korai aijar ŋin aica naka ituŋa. 
John1:5 Ecai aica kamuton, ido mam amuton ipikorit," 
John1:6 Kobu etuŋanan, lokijukuni Edeke, ekekiror Yokana." 
John1:7 Kobu ŋol araut ekajenan, tetere itejenuni nuka aica kaŋin, tetere iyuunete kere kanukeŋ," 
John1:8 Mam ŋol kerai aica ŋin, dimarai kobu tetere itejenuni nuka aica," 
John1:9 Kejai aica nakabeit naecaikini ŋinituŋanan ebunit toma akwap," 
John1:10 Kejai ŋesi toma akwap, kesubio akwap kanukeŋ, ido mam akwap abu kojenu ŋes," 
John1:11 Abu kobu obukeŋ, ido ŋul lukeraas iketuŋa mam apotu kisukunyut," 
John1:12 Konye ŋul kere lukisukunyunete ŋes, koinak apedor araut idwe luka Edeke, kes ŋul luiyuunito ekekiror:" 
John1:13 lumam keurio kaokot, karaida koipud loka akuan, karaida koipud loka ekiliokit, dimarai kanuka Edeke." 
John1:14 Koraun akirot akuan, kiboiororoi kamawok, (kaanyut oni da akeibuses, aibuses naka eteluna lokebuni kama ka Papa,) ileleba asianut ka abeit." 
John1:15 Etejenuni Yokana nukeŋ, eworoi ebe, “Ŋol ŋes loabu eoŋ kabala ebe, ŋol loebunit kokaukaŋ arau lokageikini; naarai ajai ŋesi sek ageikin eoŋ.”" 
John1:16 Ido kotoma ailelebake kipou kere kadumutu, asianut da itia asianut." 
John1:17 Naarai ikisila etorunere neejai Musa, konye asianut ka abeit etorunere neejai Yesu Kristo." 
John1:18 Emamei ituŋanan yeneanyunit Edeke kapakio kere; Okoku loteluna, loejai atorob naka Papa, ŋol ŋes etejenuni." 
John1:19 Na ŋes aitejenunet naka Yokana, naejukakiniata lyudayan isasedotin ka Ilebin anyoun koYerusalem, aiŋit ŋes ebe, “Iŋai bo ijo?”" 
John1:20 Kolimo, mam abu kogir, konye kolimo ebe, “Mam eoŋ arai Kristo.”" 
John1:21 Kiŋita ŋes ebe, “Inyo bo do? Irai kereka ijo Eliya?” Kotema atiar, “Mam arai,” “Irai kereka ijo enabi je?” Koboŋok ebe, “Mam.”" 
John1:22 Kanuka ŋun kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Iŋai bo do ijo? Kaboŋokisi kwi lukiijukunete. Ibala bo ijo ai kanukon?”" 
John1:23 Kotema atiar, “Arai eoŋ eporoto loka yeniworoi kamodiŋ ebe, ‘Kitetenata erot loka Ejakait,’ kwape kineritor enabi Isaia.”" 
John1:24 Ejukunitai kes kama ejaas Iparisayon. 
John1:25 Kiŋita ŋes, kotemasi atiar, “Kanukinyo ibatisaa, arai mam jo irai Kristo, arai Eliya, karaida enabi je?”" 
John1:26 Koboŋok Yokana kotema atiar, “Ebatisai eoŋ kakip; konye ebwoi kokidiŋikus lomam yes ijenete," 
John1:27 ŋes ŋol loebunit kokaukaŋ, lomam kebusakinit eoŋ ailac arukan naka amukatake.”" 
John1:28 Eswamao ŋun koBetaniya okekwa Yorodan, neajai Yokana ibatisai." 
John1:29 Kapaaran naatupakini koany Yesu ebunit mamake, kotema atiar, “Koany Imerekek yenika Edeke, yenelemari adiakar naka akwapin!" 
John1:30 Ŋol ŋes loabu eoŋ kenerite ebe, ‘Ebunit kokaukaŋ etuŋanan lokageikini, naarai ajai ŋesi sek ageikin eoŋ.’" 
John1:31 Kwabo mam abu kajeni ŋes; konye abu eoŋ kabu ebatisai kakipi tetere itodikinio ŋes Isirael.” 
John1:32 Kitejen Yokana ebe, “Aany Emoyo edokuni kokuju kwape kajele, kosal mamakeŋ." 
John1:33 Kwabo mam abu kajeni ŋes; konye kabala ŋes lokejukuni eoŋ aibatis kakipi ebe, ‘Ŋol loianyuni Emoyo edokuni mamakeŋ kosalak, ŋes ŋol loibatisai kEmoyo Lokalaunan.’" 
John1:34 Aany eoŋ, etejen da ebe erai ŋol Okoku loka Edeke.”" 
John1:35 Bobo da kapaaran naatupakini kobwoi Yokana nepepe kikekesisiak iarei; 
John1:36 kosesen Yesu elosi, kotema atiar, “Koany Imerekek yenika Edeke!”" 
John1:37 Kiirasi ikesisiak ŋul iarei inera ŋesi, kotupasi Yesu." 
John1:38 Kibelokin Yesu koany etupito ŋes, kotema kes atiar, “Imoete inyo?” Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Rabi, (apolouke Ekesisianakinan,) iboie kai?”" 
John1:39 Kotema kes atiar, “Kopotu ianyunete.” Koloto, koanyutu nekiboio; kosalakis mamakeŋ apaaran ŋin, naarai kerai bala esawa lokitomonet." 
John1:40 Anderea, onaceke ka Simon Petero, ŋes arai ediopet kaluarei lueirarete Yokana, kotupasi Yesu." 
John1:41 Kodum ber ŋesi Simon onaceke, kotema ŋes atiar, “Kidumu Mesia,” (apolouke ebe Kristo)," 
John1:42 Koyaŋa ŋes mama ejai Yesu. Kosesen Yesu ŋes, kotema atiar, “Ijo Simon okoku loka Yokana, Kinyarao Kepa” (apolouke ebe Petero, arai Amoru)," 
John1:43 Kapaaran naatupakini kokoto alosit Galilaya, kodum Pilip kotema ŋes atiar, “Kotupunai.”" 
John1:44 Kerai Pilip loko Betesaida, ere loka Anderea ka Petero," 
John1:45 Kodum Pilip Natanael, kotema ŋes atiar, “Kidum ŋol lokiwadikai Musa kotoma okisila, ka inabin da, Yesu loko Nasaret, okoku loka Yosep.”" 
John1:46 Kotema Natanael ŋes atiar, “Epedori tope ibore yenejok alomun koNasaret?” Kotema Pilip atiar, “Bia koany.”" 
John1:47 Koany Yesu Natanael ebunit mamakeŋ, kiner nuke ebe, “Koany, lokIsirael obe, loemamei aimod kotomakeŋ!”" 
John1:48 Kotema Natanael ŋes atiar, “Kikonakini ai kijenuni eoŋ?” Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Eriŋa Pilip kenyarauna jo, naijaar kwap ketini abu kaany jo.”" 
John1:49 Koboŋok Natanael ebe, “Rabi, irai ijo Okoku loka Edeke! Irai ijo Ekabaka loka Isirael!”" 
John1:50 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Naarai kalimok jo ebe abu kaany jo kwap ketini, ŋes iyuunia? Ianyuni akiro nuepolok aitelekarit nu.”" 
John1:51 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Ianyunete akuj eŋaara, ka imalaikan luka Edeke edokarete edokunete da mama ejai Okoku loka etuŋanan.”" 
John2:1 Apaaran nakiwuniet kojai adukokin koKana loka Galilaya; kojai toto naka Yesu da ŋina: 
John2:2 konyararai Yesu da ka ikekesisiak opucit. 
John2:3 Kedaun ebino, kotema totoke Yesu atiar, “Emamei kes ebino.”" 
John2:4 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Toto, anyoika eoŋ ka jo? Eroko akapak edolo.”" 
John2:5 Kolimok totoke ikejaanakinak ebe, “Nukilimokini kere, kiswamata.”" 
John2:6 Aso kejaas nen akaalakanya akanykape nuka amor, kibwaikinitai kes nen kanuka epone loka Iyudayan loka aitesegaar, nuilosikinos akeito aarei arai auni." 
John2:7 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Kilelebata akaalakanya akipi.” Kes da kilelebata kiton atokitoit," 
John2:8 Kotema kes atiar, “Aso do kooko, koinasi ekapolon loka epucit.” Koinasi."
