John2:9 Kosodi kiir ekapolon loka epucit akipi nukeluoros ebino, komam ejeŋi nekebunio, (konye kojenete ikejaanakinak luaokete akipi,) konyarau ekapolon loka epucit eteran," 
John2:10 kotema ŋes atiar, “Ŋinituŋanan itemokini ber ebino loejijim, kosodi kedaut ituŋa aimat noi, eyaunio do loepiana; konye jo iŋadak loejijim kiton kwana,”" 
John2:11 Abu Yesu kiswama aanyunet na nasodit koKana loko Galilaya, kitodia da akeibuses; kiyuutu ikekesisiak ŋes." 
John2:12 Kokau kaŋun kijesar kiton Kaparanaum, ŋes ka totoke, ka ikeinacan ka ikekesisiak da; kosala ŋina apaarasia nuikidioko." 
John2:13 Keapie Aleleŋ naka lyudayan, kodoka Yesu Yerusalem." 
John2:14 Kodum kotoma oyekalu lukegwelanarete imoŋin ka amerekekin ka ajeleik da, ka ikesiecanarak arupian iboiete." 
John2:15 Kosub edaset kaunoi, kireŋea kes kere koyekalu, amerekekin ka imoŋin da; kobuko arupian nuka ikesiecanarak, kobuburiana imesanakec," 
John2:16 Kolimok ŋul lukegwelanarete ajeleik ebe, “Kolemasi ŋun; sirikituluosi etogo loka Papaka araut logwelanaret.”" 
John2:17 Kiitut ikekesisiak ebe iwadikatai ebe, “Kaari ekokote loka ekonitogo.”" 
John2:18 Kosodete koboŋokis Iyudayan kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Aanyunet anyoin nakitodikini ijo sio naarai iswama nu?”" 
John2:19 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Kotiyakisi eyekalu lo, ido adukokini eoŋ apaarasia auni.”" 
John2:20 Kosodete kotemasi Iyudayan atiar, “Eyekalu lo lokedukokinio ikar akaisaoŋon ka lukanykape, iduki tope ijo kotoma apaarasia auni?”" 
John2:21 Konye enera ŋesi nuka eyekalu loka akuanake. 
John2:22 Aso nakejarunia kotoma okatwak, kiitut ikekesisiak ebe enerit ŋun; kiyuut nakiwadikatai ka akirot da nakinera Yesu," 
John2:23 Nakejaar Yerusalem kapak naka epucit loka Aleleŋ, kiyuut ituŋa luipu ekekiror, nakeanyuniata aanyuneta nukiswamai," 
John2:24 Konye Yesu mam abu komunokina kes, naarai kejeni ituŋa kere," 
John2:25 komam ipuda ituŋanan aitejenun ŋes nuka ituŋa; naarai kejeni ŋesi elopet nukejaas otuŋa. 
John3:1 Kojai etuŋanan loka Iparisayon, ekekiror Nikodemo, ekayaiton loka Iyudayan," 
John3:2 Kobu ŋol mama ejai Yesu kuare, kotema ŋes atiar, “Rabi, kijeni ebe irai ijo Ekesisianakinan loibunit kama ejai Edeke; naarai emamei ituŋanan yenepedori aswam aanyuneta nu nuiswamai ijo, dimikito ejai Edeke kaŋes.”" 
John3:3 Koboŋok Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Abeit, abeit, katemari jo atiar, Arai mam ituŋanan eurio nakiareit, mam epedori aanyun ajakanut naka Edeke.”" 
John3:4 Kobala Nikodemo ŋes ebe, “Ikwaikini ai ituŋanan eurio kemojoŋ? Epedori kereka airucakin alomar akoik naka totoke, kouriai?”" 
John3:5 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Abeit, abeit, katemari jo atiar, Arai mam ituŋanan eurio kakipi ka Emoyo, mam epedori alomun ajakanut naka Edeke." 
John3:6 Ibore yeneuriei akuan erai akuan; ka yeneuriei Emoyo erai emoyo," 
John3:7 Sirikiwumok naarai kabala jo ebe, Ibusakinit yes aurio nakiareit." 
John3:8 Ekusi ekwam mama ekot, ipupi airurumake; konye mam ipedori aijen kama kebunio, karaida mama ebei; ikoni nen ŋinituŋanan yeneuriei Emoyo.”" 
John3:9 Koboŋok Nikodemo kotema ŋes atiar, “Ikwaikinete ŋun ai epedoros?”" 
John3:10 Koboŋok Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Irai tope ijo ekesisianakinan loka Isirael, komam ijeni akiro ŋun?" 
John3:11 Abeit, abeit, katemari jo atiar, Kinera nukijeni, kitejenuni da nukianyunit; konye do mam yes icamunito akosiitejenun." 
John3:12 Arai abu kalimok yes akiro nuka akwap komam iyuunete, ikote Iyuunete ai arai kaalimokis akiro nuka akuj?" 
John3:13 Emamei yenabu kodokarite toma akuj, dimarai ŋol lokedokuni kotoma akuj, ŋes Okoku loka etuŋanan." 
John3:14 Kwape kolo kikajakinia Musa emun kamodiŋ, ibusakinit Okoku loka etuŋanan da aikajakinio kwape kwaŋin:" 
John3:15 tetere ŋinituŋanan yeniyuuni ŋes kojaas kaijar naka ikar kere.” 
John3:16 Naarai komina Edeke akwapin kwanata, abu koinak Okokuke loteluna, tetere ŋinituŋanan yeniyuuni ŋes kinye aolior, konye kojaas kaijar naka ikar kere." 
John3:17 Naarai mam Edeke ejukunit Okokuke akwapin tetere itelekarete akwapin akiro, dimarai tetere itajario akwapin kanukeŋ." 
John3:18 Ŋin yeniyuuni ŋes mam itelekarete akiro; yenimam iyuuni ŋes adaut akiro aitelekar, naarai mam abu kiyuu ekiror loka Okoku loteluna loka Edeke," 
John3:19 Lo da ŋes etube, ebe abu aica kobu akwapin, konye kominas ituŋa amuton aitelekarit aica, naarai aroko aswamisiokec." 
John3:20 Naarai ŋinituŋanan yeniswamai nueroko elait aica, kwabo mam ebuni neejai aica, kinyeis akeswamisio aideleleun." 
John3:21 Konye yeniswamai nukabeit ebuni neejai aica, tetere etakanete akeswamisio, ebe iswamatai kotoma Edeke." 
John3:22 Kokau kaŋun kolot Yesu ka ikekesisiak akwap nako Yudaya; kiboie kaŋina nepepe kakes ibatisai. 
John3:23 Kibatisai Yokana da kAenon naeapias ka Salim, naarai kejaas akipi nuipu nen; kolosenenete ituŋa mamakeŋ kibatisai," 
John3:24 Naarai koriŋa Yokana eenikina aidaris. 
John3:25 Aso kojau epeget ikekesisiak luka Yokana ka Eyudayat kanuka aitalaun. 
John3:26 Koloto mama ejai Yokana, kotemasi atiar, “Rabi, ŋol loajai nenipe kajo okekwa Yorodan, lokitejenunit, koany, ibatisai ŋol, ido elosenenete ituŋa kere mamakeŋ.”" 
John3:27 Koboŋok Yokana ebe, “Mam epedori ituŋanan adumun akirot kere dimikito einakinitai abunore kotoma akuj." 
John3:28 Itejenut yesi ikulepek ebe, abu kener ebe, Mam eoŋ arai Kristo, dimarai kejukunitai aiŋarenikin ŋes," 
John3:29 Loejaas kateran ŋes eteran; konye epapero loka eteran, loebwoi iirari ŋes, elelakinit noi eporoto loka eteran; aso adol do akaiyalama ŋin." 
John3:30 Ibusakinit ŋes aiyatakin, konye eoŋ aiŋoŋar.”" 
John3:31 Ŋol loebuni kokuju eyait kere; ŋol loerai loka akwap erai loka akwap, inera nuka akwap; ŋol loebuni kokuju eyait kere." 
John3:32 Itejenuni ŋun nueanyunit ka nuiirarit da, kwabo emamei yeniyuuni akeitejenun." 
John3:33 Yeniyuunit akeitejenun itogogoŋit ebe Edeke ŋes abeit. 
John3:34 Naarai lokijukuni Edeke inera akiro nuka Edeke: naarai mam Edeke einakini Emoyo kaitemis. 
John3:35 Emina Papa Okoku, ititiŋit iboro kere." 
John3:36 Yeniyuuni Okoku ejaas kaijar naka ikar kere; konye yenimam erima Okoku mam eanyuni aijar, konye esalakini ŋes anyunyura naka Edeke." 
John4:1 Aso nakejenunia Ejakait ebe eirasi Iparisayon ebe adum Yesu ikesisiak luipu aitelekar Yokana ka aibatis," 
John4:2 (Kwabo mam Yesu elopet kibatisai, dimarai ikekesisiak,)" 
John4:3 kinye Yudaya kolot bobo Galilaya. 
John4:4 Kibusakinit ŋes aitor kidiŋ Samaria. 
John4:5 Kosodi kodol ore loko Samaria, loenyaritai Sukar, loaapias kamana nakeinakini Yakob okokuke Yosep." 
John4:6 Kejai nen atan naka Yakob, aso naarai kepasit Yesu kanuka alositeke, kiboikin atan. Kerai bala esawa lokikanyetekape." 
John4:7 Kobu aberu naSamariat aiwok akipi. Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Ae akipi kamat.”" 
John4:8 Naarai kelositos ikekesisiak ore agwel inyamat. 
John4:9 Kotema aberu naSamariat ŋes atiar, “Ikonakini ai ijo Eyudayat kilipi eoŋ akipi, eoŋ naarai Asamariat?” Naarai mam Iyudayan imorikikina kIsamarian," 
John4:10 Koboŋok Yesu kotema atiar, “Arai kijeni ainakinet naka Edeke, ka ŋol da lokibala ebe, Ae akipi kamat, tikilipi ŋes, tikiinak jo akipi nukajarak.”" 
John4:11 Kotema aberu ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, emamei jo ibore yeniwokunet, idul atan da; aso idumuni kai akipi ŋun nukajarak?" 
John4:12 Ipol kereka ijo aitelekarit papaakosi Yakob, loabu koinak sio atan na, ŋes da elopet komat akipike, nepepe kikedwe, ka ikebaren da?”" 
John4:13 Koboŋok Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Ŋin yenemasi akipi nu ejaki bobo akur," 
John4:14 konye yenemasi akipi nuainakini eoŋ, mam ejaki akur ikar kere; konye akipi nuainakini eoŋ eraunete kotomake atan naka akipi nuibulubulitos kiton aijar namam edaun.”" 
John4:15 Kobala aberu ŋes ebe, “Ejakait, koinakinai eoŋ akipi ŋun kenyek akur aijak, karaida abunenen ne aiwok akipi.”" 
John4:16 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kolot, konyarau okilenikon, koboŋu ne,”" 
John4:17 Koboŋok aberu ebe, “Emamei eoŋ ekiliokit.” Kotema Yesu atiar, “Inera abeit ebe, Emamei eoŋ ekiliokit;" 
John4:18 naarai kijaas kikiliok ikany, ŋol da loijaatar kwana mam erai okilenikon; inera nu abeit.”" 
John4:19 Kotema aberu atiar, “Ejakait, aanyun ebe irai enabi," 
John4:20 Kemaete lukapapaakosi koroŋat kalo; ibalasi yesi ebe Yerusalem ŋes aibois naibusakinit amaia.” 
John4:21 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Toto, kiyuunai, ebunit esawa lomam imaiata bobo Papa koroŋat kalo karaida Yerusalem," 
John4:22 Imaete yesi yenimam ijenete; kimai isio yenikijeni, naarai ebunit aitajario kotoma oYudayan." 
John4:23 Konye ebunit esawa, ejai da kwana, loemaiata ikamaak lukabeit Papa, kotoma omoyo ka abeit, naarai emoot Papa ituŋa luikote nen aima ŋes." 
John4:24 Erai Edeke Emoyo, ŋul da luemaete ŋes, ibusakinit aima kotoma omoyo ka abeit.”" 
John4:25 Kotema aberu ŋes atiar, “Ajeni ebe ebunit Mesia (ŋol Ioenyaritai Kristo); naebunio ŋesi kipukokini sio akiro kere.”" 
John4:26 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Eoŋ lopelo lokinera kajo.”" 
John4:27 Atipet kopotu ikekesisiak, koumokis naarai kineras kaberu, konye mam loabu kolim ebe, “Ikoto inyo?” Arai ebe, “Kanukinyo ineratar kaŋes?”" 
John4:28 Aso kinyek aberu akemot, kolot ore, kolimok ituŋa ebe," 
John4:29 “Kopotu, koanyut etuŋanan lokalimoki akiro kere nukeswamaenenei. Epedori kereka lo araut Kristo?”" 
John4:30 Kolomutu kesi kore koloto mamakeŋ. 
John4:31 Kapak kaŋin kiŋaiŋaata ikesisiak ebe, “Rabi, konyam.”" 
John4:32 Konye kotema kes atiar, “Ejaas eoŋ inyamat lumam yes ijenete.”" 
John4:33 Kineranakinos ikesisiak ebe, “Eiai ca nat yeneinunit ŋes inyamat?”" 
John4:34 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Ikanyamat kes luta, aswam nuekot lokejukuni, ka aitodol da akeswam." 
John4:35 Mam kereka ibalasi yesi ebe, ‘Eroko esalito ilapio iwoŋon, kodoli aidweny’? Katemari yes atiar, Kikeutu akusikonye, koanyut amanat ebe adaut areŋeun adwenyio," 
John4:36 Eropio ekadwenyan, etukonokini araito kanuka aijar namam edaun, tetere iyalamikinos ekayean ka ekadwenyan nepepe." 
John4:37 Naarai erai akirot nakabeit ebe, ‘Eyei ice, edwenyi da ice.’" 
John4:38 Abu kejuka yes aidweny ŋun numam kitaaritotor; konye kitaaritos ice, ilomakis yesi aitaaritoikec.”" 
John4:39 Kiyuut Isamarian luipu kotoma ore kaŋol kanuka akirot naka aberu, nakitejenunit ebe, “Abu kalimok akiro kere nukeswamaenenei.”" 
John4:40 Aso nakeponiata Isamarian mamakeŋ, kiŋaiŋaata ŋes asalakin kakes; kosalak do nen apaarasia aarei." 
John4:41 Kiyuut ice luipu kanuka akekirot," 
John4:42 Kotemasi aberu atiar, “Kiyuunit kwana, mere kanuka ekoniiner bon, naarai kiira isio ikulepek, kijenu da ebe abeit erai ŋol Eketajaran loka akwapisinei.”" 
John4:43 Akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun aarei konyou kanen kolot Galilaya. 
John4:44 Naarai kitejen Yesu elopet ebe mam enabi eyoŋio kobukec. 
John4:45 Aso nakedolio Galilaya, kisukunyikis Igalilayan, naarai apotu koanyutu akiro kere nukiswamai koYerusalem kopucit, naarai kelosito ŋul da opucit." 
John4:46 Kobu bobo Kana loko Galilaya mama etuluoria akipi ebino. Kojai etuŋanan lokapolou Kaparanaum, lokejai okokuke edeka." 
John4:47 Kiira ŋol ebe ebunit Yesu Galilaya anyoun koYudaya, kolot neejai kiŋaiŋa aijesar aitaŋaleun okokuke, naarai keapikinit atwanare," 
John4:48 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Arai mam ianyunete aanyuneta ka nukaumokin, mam iyuunete cut.”" 
John4:49 Kobala lokapolou ebe, “Ejakait, kijesar eroko ikakoku ketwana.”" 
John4:50 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kolot; ejari okokukon.” Kiyuu etuŋanan akirot nakelimokini Yesu ŋes, kolot," 
John4:51 Kosodi napijesar kiriamakinos kikebulesin, lukebalas ebe ejari okokuke." 
John4:52 Kiŋit kes esawa lokegeunia aitemokin, kolimokis ŋes ebe, “Bian esawa lokikanyetekaarei alakakinia ekamidi ŋes.”" 
John4:53 Kosodi kojen papake ebe ŋes esawa je lokelimokinia Yesu ebe, “Ejari okokukon.” Kiyuu ŋesi ka lukokaleke kere." 
John4:54 Ŋin ŋes aanyunet nakiareit nakiswamai Yesu nakenyounio koYudaya adolore Galilaya. 
John5:1 Akaulo kaŋun kojai epucit loka Iyudayan, kodoka Yesu Yerusalem." 
John5:2 KoYerusalem ejai atapar ariri kerute loka amerekekin, nakenyaritai kAburanian Betesata, naejaas alomareta akany." 
John5:3 Koperenenete lukadekak luipu kanen, imudukiok, ka luicodos, ka lukasenyak da, [lukidarito akulaun naka akipi," 
John5:4 Naarai keiai apak nakedokununia emalaika loka Ejakait atapar, kigur akipi: aso yenikegei alomar kedaun aigur akipi koŋaleuni adeka kere nakikamunit.]" 
John5:5 Kojai nen etuŋanan, lokedeka ikar akaisauni ka lukanykauni." 
John5:6 Nakeanyunia Yesu ŋol eperi kojen ebe kikoni nen ikar luipu, kotema ŋes atiar, “Ikoto aŋaleun?”" 
John5:7 Koboŋok lokadekan ebe, “Ejakait, emamei eoŋ etuŋanan lokebwaikini eoŋ atapar naitukulaunere akipi, konye naalosio, kageikini icetuŋanan adokar.”" 
John5:8 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Konyou, kibwok akonikapet, kolot.”" 
John5:9 Atipet koŋaleu etuŋanan ŋol, kibwok akekapet, kolot. Kerai da apaaran ŋin nakasabato." 
John5:10 Kanuka ŋun kolimokis Iyudayan etuŋanan lokitaŋaleunio ebe, “Erai lolo nakasabato, mam ibus jo aibwok akonikapet.”" 
John5:11 Konye Koboŋok ebe, “Ŋol loketaŋaleuni ŋes kalimokini ebe, ‘Kibwok akonikapet, kolot.’ ”" 
John5:12 Kiŋita ebe, “Iŋai bo ŋol lokilimokini ebe, ‘Kibwok, kolot?’ ”" 
John5:13 Konye etuŋanan lokitaŋaleunio mam kejeni ebe erai iŋai, naarai koekarite Yesu, naarai ajaas ituŋa luipu aibois ŋin," 
John5:14 Kokau kaŋun kodum Yesu ŋes koyekalu, kotema ŋes atiar, “Koany, iŋaleu! Sirikidiaka bobo, kinyek akirot naerono adepar ŋin adoikin jo.”" 
John5:15 Kolot etuŋanan kolimok Iyudayan ebe kerai Yesu lokitaŋaleuni ŋes," 
John5:16 Kanuka ŋun kimanata Iyudayan Yesu, naarai kiswamai ŋun kapaaran nakasabato." 
John5:17 Konye Koboŋok Yesu kes ebe, “Iswamai Papaka kiton kwana, eoŋ da eswamai.”" 
John5:18 Aso kanuka akirot kaŋin kiyatakis Iyudayan amoot aiar Ŋes, naarai mere bon aibil asabato, konye kanu anyaritor Edeke Papake, kitiriana da ka Edeke." 
John5:19 Aso Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Mam Okoku epedori aswam adiokirot elopet, dimarai ŋin naeanyuni ŋesi Papa iswamai; naarai nuiswamai Papa kere, ŋupeŋun iswamai Okoku da." 
John5:20 Naarai emin Papa Okoku, itodikini ŋes kere nuiswamai ŋesi elopet; itodikini da aswamisio nuitelekarito ŋun, tetere yes iwumokinete." 
John5:21 Naarai kwape itajaria Papa lukatwak ka ainakin kes aijar, kwaŋin einakinia Okoku da ŋul luekot aijar." 
John5:22 Mam Papa etubokini idiotuŋanan kere akiro, konye ainak Okoku etube kere," 
John5:23 tetere ituŋa kere itopoloorete Okoku, kwape itopolooritotor Papa. Ŋin yenimam itopoloori Okoku mam itopoloori Papa da lokijukuni." 
John5:24 Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, ŋin yeniirari akakirot ka aiyuun ŋol lokejukuni, ejaas kaijar naka ikar kere; kwabo mam elomari toma atubokinio, konye anyou kotoma atwanare aloma aijar." 
John5:25 “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Ebunit esawa, ejai da kwana, loiirariata lukatwak eporoto loka Okoku loka Edeke, ŋul da luiirarete ejarete," 
John5:26 Naarai kwape ejaatar Papa aijar kotomakeŋ, kwape kwaŋin abu koinak Okoku da ajaut kaijar kotomakeŋ;" 
John5:27 koinak ŋes apedor naka aitub, naarai erai Okoku loka etuŋanan," 
John5:28 Sirikiwumokis akiro nu; naarai ebunit esawa, loiirariata ituŋa kere luejaas toma atesin ekeporoto," 
John5:29 elomunete; ŋul luiswamato nuejok mama ejai ajarun naka aijar; ka ŋul da luiswamato nueroko, mama ejai ajarun naka atubokinio." 
John5:30 “Mam eoŋ apedori aswam adiokirot kanukaŋ elopet; kwape eiraria, kwape kwaŋin atubio: ekatube da erai lokabeit, naarai mam amoot nuakot eoŋ dimarai nuekot ŋol lokejukuni." 
John5:31 Arai ketejenu eoŋ nukaŋ elopet, akaitejenun mam erai nakabeit;" 
John5:32 ejai ece loitejenuni nukaŋ, ajeni eoŋ ebe akeitejenun naitejenunia nukaŋ erai nakabeit." 
John5:33 Ipotu yesi kijukut ituŋa mama ejai Yokana, kitejenu ŋesi abeit." 
John5:34 Konye eoŋ mam adumuni aitejenunio naebuni kotuŋa; konye enera eoŋ nu tetere yes kitajario. 
John5:35 Kerai ŋol atala naenoki kocai, yes da ikotos aisiyalamikin akeica apak naedit." 
John5:36 Konye aitejenun nakijaar eoŋ erai naepol adepar naka Yokana; naarai aswamisio nukainakinit Papa aitodolikin, aswamisio akulepek nueswamai, itejenunito nukaŋ ebe, kejukunit Papa." 
John5:37 Papa da lokejukunit, etejenunit nukaŋ, Mam yes iirarito ekeporoto apaarasia kere, karaida aanyun akeput." 
John5:38 Mam da akekirot esalit tomakus, naarai mam yes iyuunitos lokijukuni ŋesi." 
John5:39 Imoete kotoma nukiwadikatai, naarai iwomito ebe ijaunete kaijar naka ikar kere kotomakec; ŋun da itejenunito nukaŋ;" 
John5:40 kwabo iŋerete aponare mamakaŋ tetere ijaunete kaijar. 
John5:41 Mam eoŋ adumuni aibuses kotuŋa. 
John5:42 Konye kajeni yes, ebe emamei amin naka Edeke kotomakus." 
John5:43 Abu kabu kokiror loka Papaka, mam yes kisukunyikis eoŋ; arai kebu ece kokirorike elopet, isukunyikinete ŋol." 
John5:44 Ipedorete biai aiyuun, yes luidumanakinos aibuses bonik komam imoete aibuses naebuni kama ejai Edeke ediopet bon?" 
John5:45 Siriwomito ebe kewosai yes kama ejai Papa; ejai lokiwosai, ŋes Musa, loimunosi yesi." 
John5:46 Naarai arai kiyuunito Musa, tikiyuut eoŋ da, naarai abu ŋesi kiwadika nukaŋ." 
John5:47 Konye arai mam iyuunito akeiwadikaeta, ikwaikinete ai iyuunete akakiro?”" 
John6:1 Akaulo kaŋun kolot Yesu okekwa juwai loka aŋolol naka Galilaya, naerai naka Tiberia." 
John6:2 Kotupa ekodet loepol, naarai apotu koanyut aanyuneta nukiswamakini lukadekak." 
John6:3 Kodoka Yesu oroŋat, kiboikin nen nepepe kikekesisiak." 
John6:4 Keapie Aleleŋ, epucit loka Iyudayan." 
John6:5 Aso kikeu Yesu akekonye, koany ekodet loepol ebunit mama ejai, kotema ŋesi Pilip atiar, “Kigweli kai inyamat, konyamata lu?”" 
John6:6 Kinera ŋun aitem ŋes: naarai ajeni ŋesi elopet nuelosi aswam. 
John6:7 Koboŋok Pilip ebe, “Inyamat luka adenarin akwat aarei mam ilosikinos kes, arai kenyam ŋinituŋanan idis tai.”" 
John6:8 Ediopet kokesisiakake, ŋes Anderea onace loka Simon Petero, kotema ŋes atiar," 
John6:9 “Ejai ne isapat, yenejaas imugatin ikany lukesairi, ka agaria aarei: konye epedorete inyo ŋul kotuŋa luetia nen?”" 
John6:10 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Kisiboikis ituŋa.” Kejaas anya nuipu aibois ŋin, Aso kiboikinos ikiliok, kwaka ilukumin ikany." 
John6:11 Kosodi kolem Yesu imugatin; kedau aimal, kokorak lukiboiete; kikonak nen agaria, koinak kwape akototor." 
John6:12 Nakimonikinotor, kolimok ikekesisiak ebe, “Kotukonokisi atutubeta nuabilibila nuesalito, sirikedepar imodiobore.”" 
John6:13 Kosodete kotukonokis, kilelebata ibukito itomon ka luarei atutubeta nuabilibila nuka imugatin ikany lukesairi, nukitasalete kwi lukenyamete." 
John6:14 Kosodete nakeanyuniata ituŋa aanyunet naeswamai, kobalas ebe, “Abeit lo ŋes enabi loebunit akwapin.”" 
John6:15 Kosodi kejenu Yesu ebe kekotosi aponare aikamun ŋes tetere itaraunete ekabaka, kogitar kolot bobo oroŋan ŋes elopet bon." 
John6:16 Nakitiboŋia kijesaros ikekesisiak aŋolol," 
John6:17 kodokas ataker, kogeut aikwaŋar alosit Kaparanaum. Komutonor akwap, komam ber Yesu ebunit mamakec." 
John6:18 Kogeu aŋolol akulaun kanuka aikut naka ekwam loepol. 
John6:19 Nakikwaŋarotor bala amairon auni arai aoŋon, koanyut Yesu itorit aŋolol, ikunyunit ataker; kokuriakaros." 
John6:20 Konye kotema kes atiar, “Eoŋ lo: sirikikuriakaros.”" 
John6:21 Aso kokotosi aisukunyuun ŋes ataker; atipet kodol ataker akwap naabeete kesi. 
John6:22 Apaaran naatupakini keany ekodet loabwoi kokekwa kaŋolol ebe emamei acetaker, dimarai adiopet bon, bobo da ebe mam Yesu adokarit ataker ŋin nepepe kikekesisiak, konye alosito ikekesisiak bonik." 
John6:23 (Konye kopotu atakerin ace anyoun koTiberia koapias kaibois nakenyamiata imugatin kedau Ejakait aimal.) 
John6:24 Aso nakeanyunia ekodet ebe emamei Yesu kanen, karaida ikekesisiak, kodokasi kesi ikulepek atakerin, koloto Kaparanaum, emooto Yesu." 
John6:25 Nakedumuniata ŋes kokekwa kaŋolol, kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Rabi, kibuni ijo ne wori?”" 
John6:26 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, kimoete eoŋ, mere kanuianyuniata aanyuneta, konye naarai ipotu konyama imugatin kimonikinos." 
John6:27 Siritaaritos kanuka inyamat luedaunos, konye kanuka inyamat luikuniasi kiton aijar naka ikar kere, lukiinakini Okoku loka etuŋanan; naarai ŋol ŋes loepucakinit Papa.”" 
John6:28 Kosodete kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kikonakini ai tetere kiswamai aswamisio nuka Edeke?”" 
John6:29 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Na Ŋes aswam naka Edeke, kiyuut ŋol lokijukuni ŋesi.”" 
John6:30 Kosodete kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Aso ca iswamai aanyunet anyoin, tetere kianyun keyuutu jo? Iswamai aswam anyoin?" 
John6:31 Apotu lukapapaakosi konyama emanu kamodiŋ; kwape iwadikatere ebe, ‘Koinak kes inyamat lukepote kotoma akuj ainyam.’”" 
John6:32 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Mere Musa kiinakini yes inyamat ŋul lukepote kotoma akuj; konye Papaka ŋes kiinakini yes inyamat lukabeit luepote kotoma akuj." 
John6:33 Naarai inyamat luka Edeke ŋes ŋin yenijesuni kotoma akuj, ka ainakin akwapisinei aijar.”" 
John6:34 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, koinakinai inyamat lu apaarasia kere.”" 
John6:35 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Arai eoŋ inyamat luka aijar; ŋin yenebuni mamakaŋ mam cut eriebi eteŋei, ŋin da yenikeyuuni eoŋ mam cut ejakenenei akur," 
John6:36 Konye katema yes atiar kianyut eoŋ, komam iyuunito," 
John6:37 Kere lukainakini Papa epote mama ajai; ŋin da yenebuni mamakaŋ mam cut ereŋeari," 
John6:38 Naarai ejesuna kotoma akuj, mere aswam nuakoto eoŋ, dimarai nuekot lokejukuni." 
John6:39 Nuekot lokejukuni kes nu ebe, Kotoma kaŋul kere lukainakini siriketoolio idiopet da, konye ketajar kapaaran nakawasia." 
John6:40 Naarai nuekot Papaka kes nu ebe, Yeneanyuni Okoku ka aiyuun ŋes kojaut kaijar naka ikar kere; etajaruni eoŋ ŋes kapaaran nakawasia.”" 
John6:41 Kosodete kirurumakis ŋes Iyudayan, naarai abala ebe, “Arai eoŋ inyamat lukijesunos kotoma akuj.”" 
John6:42 Kobalas ebe, “Mere kereka lo Yesu, okoku loka Yosep, lokijeni papake ka totoke? Ikwaikini ai ebala ebe, Ejesun eoŋ kotoma akuj?”" 
John6:43 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Sirikirurumata bonik ka bonik." 
John6:44 Emamei ituŋanan yenepedori abunore mamakaŋ arai mam eriunit Papa lokeiukuni; eoŋ da etajaruni ŋes kapaaran nakawasia. 
John6:45 Iwadikatai kotoma onabin ebe, ‘Isisianakini Edeke kes kere.’ Ŋin yeniirarit, ka aisisiaun kaneejai Papa, ebuni mamakaŋ." 
John6:46 Mere ebe eanyunit ituŋanan Papa, dimarai ŋol loabuu kama ejai Edeke; ŋol ŋes eanyunit Papa." 
John6:47 Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Yeniyuunit ejaas kaijar naka ikar kere." 
John6:48 Arai eoŋ inyamat luka aijar. 
John6:49 Apotu lukapapaakus konyamata emanu kamodiŋ, kotwaka da." 
John6:50 Lu kes inyamat luijesunos kotoma akuj, tetere enyami ituŋanan kes komam etwani." 
John6:51 Arai eoŋ inyamat lukajarak lukijesunos kotoma akuj; arai kenyam ituŋanan inyamat lu, ebusi ikar kere; inyamat da luainakini eoŋ kanuka aijar naka akwapisinei ŋes akakuan.”" 
John6:52 Kopegasi Iyudayan bonik ebe, “Epedori biai etuŋanan lo ainakin oni akekuan ainyam?”" 
John6:53 Aso kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Arai mam inyamete akuan naka Okoku loka etuŋanan, ka aimat da akeokot, emamei aijar kotomakus." 
John6:54 Yenenyami akakuan ka aimat da akaokot ejaas kaijar naka ikar kere, eoŋ da etajaruni ŋes kapaaran nakawasia." 
John6:55 Naarai akakuan kes inyamat lukabeit, akaokot da kes numatan nukabeit." 
John6:56 Yenenyami akakuan ka aimat da akaokot esalakini tomakaŋ, eoŋ da tomakeŋ," 
John6:57 Kwape kejukunia Papa lokajaran eoŋ, ajari eoŋ da kanuka Papa, kwape kwaŋin yenikanyami eoŋ ejari kanukaŋ," 
John6:58 Lu kes inyamat lukijesunos kotoma akuj, mere kwape kenyamiata lukapapaa kotwaka; yenenyami inyamat lu ejari ikar kere.”" 
John6:59 Enera ŋesi akiro ŋun kotoma atukos, naesisianakinia Kaparanaum." 
John6:60 Nakiirariata ice luipu kokesisiakake kobalas ebe, “Etiono ca akirot na; iŋai bo epedori aiirar?”" 
John6:61 Konye kojeni Yesu kotauke ebe erurumata ikekesisiak kanuka akirot kaŋin, kotema kes atiar, “Kitiguiki ca yes akirot na?" 
John6:62 Ikonakinete bo do ai arai ianyunete Okoku loka etuŋanan edokari nekolo kejai sek? 
John6:63 Emoyo ŋes einakini aijar, mam akuan epedori ibore; akiro nukalimokinit yes eraas emoyo, eraas da aijar." 
John6:64 Konye ejaas ice kotomakus lumam iyuunito.” Naarai kejeni Yesu ameun kageunet lumam iyuunito, ka ŋol da loebilakini ŋes ebotet." 
John6:65 Kobala ebe, “Kanuka ŋun katema yes ebe emamei ituŋanan yenepedori abunore mamakaŋ, dimikito einakinitai kama ka Papa.”" 
John6:66 Kanuka ŋun koboŋosi luipu kokesisiakake, komam bobo eupasi kaŋes." 
John6:67 Aso kotema Yesu lutomon kaarei atiar, “Ikotosi kereka yesi da aboŋor?”" 
John6:68 Koboŋok Simon Petero ebe, “Ejakait, kilosi mama ejai iŋai? Ijaas ijo kakiro nuka aijar naka ikar kere." 
John6:69 Kiyuunit isio, bobo da kijeni ebe irai ijo Lokalaunan loka Edeke.”" 
John6:70 Koboŋok Yesu kes ebe, “Mere kereka eoŋ kaseunit yes lutomon kaarei, ediopet da kayesi erai Satan?”" 
John6:71 Enera nuka Yuda okoku loka Isikariot, naarai ŋol loebilakini ŋes ebotet, ŋes da ediopet kotomon ka luarei." 
John7:1 Akaulo kaŋun kitorite Yesu Galilaya; naarai mam kekoto aitorit Yudaya, naarai kemootos lyudayan aiar ŋes." 
John7:2 Keapie epucit loka lyudayan loka iswamin. 
John7:3 Aso kotemasi ŋes ikeinacan atiar, “Konyou kane kolot Yudaya, tetere eanyunete ikonikesisiak akoniswamisio nuiswamai." 
John7:4 Naarai emamei ituŋanan yeniswamai akiro kaiyeiyea, yenekoto ŋes elopet aitebeun. Arai kiswama nu kitodiar kakwapin.”" 
John7:5 Naarai ikeinacan da mam eyuunito ŋes," 
John7:6 Aso kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Eroko akapak edolo; konye itemokino akusipak apaarasia kere." 
John7:7 Mam akwapin kipedorete aila yes, konye kalaito eoŋ, naarai etejenu eoŋ ebe eroko akeceswamisio." 
John7:8 Kodokasi yesi opucit, mam ber eoŋ edokari opucit ŋol, naarai eroko akapak itodolikino.”" 
John7:9 Nakedaunia alimokin kes ŋun kosalak Galilaya. 
John7:10 Konye nakedauniata ikeinacan adokar opucit, kanen kodoka ŋesi da elopet, mere kaitebeikin konye bala kaiyeiyea." 
John7:11 Aso komoata Iyudayan ŋes kopucit, kobalas ebe, “Ai bo ejai ŋol?”" 
John7:12 Kojau airuruma naepol kokodeta kanukeŋ; kobalas ice ebe, “Erai etuŋanan loejok.” Kobalas ice da ebe, “Mere kwaŋin, konye itapaari ekodet.”" 
John7:13 Konye emamei ituŋanan yeninera kaitebeikin naarai kekuriaka Iyudayan. 
John7:14 Kosodi kanen kokidiŋ kepucit kodoka Yesu, koloma oyekalu, kogeu aisisianakin." 
John7:15 Koumokis Iyudayan, kobalas ebe, “Kikonakini lo ai ecouni komam isisiat?”" 
John7:16 Aso Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Akaisisianakin mere nakaŋ dimarai naka ŋol lokejukuni;" 
John7:17 arai ekoto ituŋanan aswam nuekot ŋol, ejenuni nuka aisisianakin kana, arai kebuni kama ejai Edeke, arai bo enera kanukaŋ bon." 
John7:18 Yeninera kanukeŋ bon emoot akeibuses ilopet; konye yenemoot aibuses naka ŋol kalokijukuni ŋes erai yenikabeit, ido kotomake emamei aiŋalanut." 
John7:19 Mam kereka Musa kiinakinit yes ikisila? Konye emamei idio kayesi yenericit ikisila. Kanukinyo kimoiata aiar eoŋ?” 
John7:20 Koboŋok ekodet ebe, “Ejai jo ajokit! Iŋai bo emoot aiar jo?”" 
John7:21 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Abu keswama aswamisioit adiopet, iwumokinito yesi kere," 
John7:22 Kanuka ŋun abu Musa koinak yes aikep (konye mam abuni kama ka Musa, konye kama ka lukapapaa); ikepete yesi etuŋanan kapaaran nakasabato," 
John7:23 Arai ekepio etuŋanan kanakasabato, tetere mam ekisil loka Musa ebila, kinyunyurikis kereka eoŋ kanu etaŋaleunio cut etuŋanan kapaaran nakasabato?" 
John7:24 Sirikituboto kwape eseseniata akusikonye, konye kotuboto kotoma adolit.”" 
John7:25 Aso kotemasi ice lukoYerusalem atiar, “Mere lo loemootos kesi aiar?" 
John7:26 Konye, koany, inera kaitebeikin, kwabo mam elimokinete adiokirot! Motoko ejenete ikayaitok abeit ebe erai lo Kristo?" 
John7:27 Konye kijeni lo neebunitor; konye naebunio Kristo, emamei yenejeni neebunio.”" 
John7:28 Kiworo Yesu isisianakini koyekalu kobala ebe, “Ijenete eoŋ, ijenete nekabunio da; kwabo mam eoŋ abunit kanukaŋ, konye ŋol lokejukuni erai lokabeit, lomam yes ijenete." 
John7:29 Ajeni eoŋ ŋes; naarai abuni kamakeŋ, ŋes da kejukuni.”" 
John7:30 Kosodete komootos aikamun ŋes; konye mam etuŋanan abu korio akekanin aikamunia, naarai ariŋa edoluno ekesawa," 
John7:31 Konye luipu lukokodet kiyuut ŋes; kobalas ebe, “Naebunio Kristo, iswamai kereka ŋesi aanyuneta nuipu aitelekarit nuiswamat lo?”" 
John7:32 Kiirasi Iparisayon ikodeta irurumaete ŋun kanukeŋ; kosodete isasedotin lupeti ka Iparisayon kijukasi ikejaanakinak aikamun ŋes," 
John7:33 Kosodi Yesu kobala ebe, “Eroko apak edit ajai nenipe kayes, kasodi alosit mama ejai lokejukuni." 
John7:34 Kimoete eoŋ komam kidumunete: neajai eoŋ mam yes ipedorete aponare.” 
John7:35 Kosodete kineranakinos Iyudayan ebe, “Ai bo elosi lo nemam oni kipedori adumunia ŋes? Elosi kereka ŋesi mama ejaas luisiarakina oYonanin, ka aisisianakin da Iyonanin?" 
John7:36 Akirot anyoin na nainerit ebe, ‘Kimoete eoŋ komam kidumunete’, ido, ‘Neajai eoŋ mam ipedorete aponare’?”" 
John7:37 Kosodi kapaaran nakawasia naka epucit, ŋes apaaran nakapolon, kobwo Yesu kiworo ebe, “Arai kejak ituŋanan akur, kobu mamakaŋ komat." 
John7:38 Yenikeyuuni, kwape ineratar nuiwadikatai ebe, ‘Eleleete icorin luka akipi nukajarak kotomakeŋ.’”" 
John7:39 Enerit akirot ŋin kanuka Emoyo, loeinakinio luiyuunito ŋes: naarai ariŋa ber Emoyo einakina, naarai eriŋa Yesu itopolooro." 
John7:40 Aso nakiirariata ice kokodet akiro ŋun, kobalas ebe, “Abeit erai lo enabi je.”" 
John7:41 Ice da kobalas ebe, “Erai lo Kristo.” Konye ice kobalas ebe, “Mam, ebuni tope Kristo koGalilaya?" 
John7:42 Mam kereka ebalas nukiwadikatai ebe ebuni Kristo kaur naka Daudi, kotoma Betelekem, ere lokejai Daudi?”" 
John7:43 Kwaŋin kojai atiakatiakaun kotuŋa kanukeŋ," 
John7:44 Kokotosi ice aikamun ŋes, konye komamei yenikibwaikini ŋes akanin;" 
John7:45 Koboŋosi ikejaanakinak mama ejaas isasedotin lupeti ka Iparisayon, luketemarete kes atiar, “Kanukinyo mam kiyauniata ŋes?”" 
John7:46 Koboŋokis ikejaanakinak ebe, “Mam inerit cut idiotuŋanan kwape inerar etuŋanan lo.”" 
John7:47 Kosodete koboŋokis Iparisayon ebe, “Aso cama kitapaa yes da?" 
John7:48 Iŋai bo kotoma ikayaitok loiyuunit ŋes, arai kotoma oParisayon?" 
John7:49 Konye ikenitoi ekodet ŋol lomam ejeni ikisila.” 
John7:50 Kobala Nikodemo, ŋes lokelosit kolo mama ejai Yesu, lokerai ediopet kakesi ebe," 
John7:51 “Etubokinete kereka ikisilawok etuŋanan, eriŋa ber iirara ŋes ka ajenun nuiswamai?”" 
John7:52 Koboŋokis kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Ibunit kereka ijo da koGalilaya? Koŋic, koany ebe mam enyouni enabi koGalilaya.”" 
John7:53 Koboŋo ŋolituŋanan oreke. 
John8:1 Konye kolot Yesu moru loka Iseitunin. 
John8:2 Koboŋo tupuruc sek oyekalu, kopotu ituŋa kere mamakeŋ; kiboikin kogeu aisisianakin kes." 
John8:3 Koyaut ikewadikak ka Iparisayon aberu naekamunitai kadoteu; kibwaikis kidiŋ," 
John8:4 kobalas ŋes ebe, “Ekesisianakinan, ikamunitai aberu na edotei." 
John8:5 Aso kotoma okisila abu Musa kicorak aibiribir nuikote nen kamor; aso ca ibala bo ijo ai?” 
John8:6 Kinerasi kesi akiro ŋun ekodunete ŋes, tetere edumunete akirot nakiwosaet. Konye kokukum Yesu, kiwadik alup kekebokorit." 
John8:7 Nakiyatanakiniata aiŋit ŋes, kitenar kotema kes atiar, “Yenemamei adiakaret kotomakus, kogeu aibir ŋes kamoru.”" 
John8:8 Kokukum bobo, kiwadik alup kekebokorit." 
John8:9 Kes da, nakiirariata, kilepilepata itauonokec, kolomasi idiopet idiopet, ageun komakio kiton lukawasia; kosalak Yesu bon, ka aberu ebwoi kanen kokidiŋ," 
John8:10 Kitenar Yesu, kotema ŋes atiar, “Toto, alu bo ŋul lukiwosato jo? Emamei kereka yenikitubokini jo?”" 
John8:11 Kotema atiar, “Emamei, Ejakait.” Kotema Yesu atiar, “Eoŋ da mam katubokini jo: kolot; konye sirikidiaka bobo.”" 
John8:12 Kinera Yesu bobo kakes, kotema atiar, “Arai eoŋ aica naka akwapin; yenikatupuni eoŋ mam cut elosi kamuton, konye ejaas kaica naka aijar.”" 
John8:13 Kotemasi Iparisayon ŋes atiar, “Itejenuni ijo elopet boni mam akoniitejenun erai nakabeit.”" 
John8:14 Koboŋok Yesu kotema kes atiar, “Karaida ketejenun eoŋ elopet erai akaitejenun nakabeit; naarai ajeni nekabunio, ka nealosi da; konye yes mam ijenete nekabunio, karaida nealosi." 
John8:15 Itubete yesi kwape ejaar akuan; mam eoŋ atubokini ituŋanan. 
John8:16 Karaida katubi eoŋ, erai ekatube lokabeit; naarai mam eoŋ ajai bon, konye eoŋ ka lokejukuni." 
John8:17 Bobo da kotoma okisilakus iwadikatai ebe aitejenun naka ituŋa iarei erai nakabeit. 
John8:18 Etejenuni eoŋ elopet, ketejenuni Papa da lokejukuni.”" 
John8:19 Kosodi kotemasi atiar, “Ejai bo ai Papakon?” Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Mam kijenete eoŋ karaida Papaka; arai kiijenete eoŋ, tikijenut Papaka da.”" 
John8:20 Kinera akiro ŋun kotoma agola naka aiŋad, nakisisianakinia koyekalu; kwabo amamei etuŋanan loekamuni ŋes; naarai aroko ekesawa edoluno." 
John8:21 Kotema bobo atiar, “Alosi eoŋ, yes da kimoete, itwakete yesi kotoma adiakanaretakus; nealosi eoŋ mam yes ipedorete aponare.”" 
John8:22 Kosodete kotemasi Iyudayan atiar, “Earakin ca, naarai ebala ebe, ‘Nealosi eoŋ mam yes ipedorete aponare’?”" 
John8:23 Kotema kes atiar, “Iraas yesi lukokwap, arai eoŋ lokokuju; iraas yesi luka akwapin kanu; mam eoŋ arai loka akwapin kanu." 
John8:24 Kanuka ŋun kalimokis yes ebe itwakete kotoma adiakanaretakus; naarai arai mam iyuunito ebe arai eoŋ, itwakete kotoma adiakanaretakus.”" 
John8:25 Kosodete kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Irai bo ijo iŋai?” Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Ŋopeŋol lokalimokinit yes ameun kageunet," 
John8:26 Ejaas nuipu einer ka aitub da kanukus: konye ŋol lokejukuni erai abeit; nueirari eoŋ kamake, kes enera kotoma akwapin.”" 
John8:27 Kwabo mam apotu kojenut ebe inerakinit kes nuka Papa," 
John8:28 Aso kotema Yesu atiar, “Naidauniata aikeun Okoku loka etuŋanan, ŋes konyet ijenuniata ebe eoŋ ŋopeŋol, ebe da mam eswamai akirot kanukaŋ bon, dimarai kwape kesisianakinia Papa, enera kwaŋin." 
John8:29 Ejai ŋol lokejukuni nenipe keoŋ; mam kenyeinit eoŋ bon; naarai eswamaenenei nuekot ŋesi apaarasia kere.” 
John8:30 Nakinerar ŋesi ŋun, kiyuut luipu." 
John8:31 Aso kotema Yesu lyudayan lukiyuunito ŋes atiar, “Arai kisalakis toma akirotoka, abeit iraas ikakesisiak;" 
John8:32 ijenunete da abeit, abeit da kiwosikini yes.”" 
John8:33 Koboŋokis ŋes ebe, “Kirai isio aur naka Aburaam, kwabo mam kiraunit ibulesin luka idiotuŋanan kere apakio kere: ikwaikini ijo ibala ai ebe, Kiwosikinio yes?”" 
John8:34 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Ŋinituŋanan yenediakanari erai ibulesit yenika adiakar." 
John8:35 Mam ibulesit iboie kotogo ikar kere; konye iboie okoku ikar kere. 
John8:36 Aso arai kiiwosik Okoku, iraas lukiwosikinitai cut." 
John8:37 Ajeni ebe iraas yesi aur naka Aburaam; konye kimootos aiar eoŋ, naarai emamei akakirot aibois kotomakus." 
John8:38 Nuaanyunit kaneejai Papa kes nuenera eoŋ: yes da iswamaete akiro nukiirarito kaneejai papakus.” 
John8:39 Koboŋokis kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Papakosi ŋes Aburaam.” Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Arai kiraas idwe luka Aburaam, tikiswamata aswamisio nuka Aburaam," 
John8:40 Konye kwana kimootos aiar eoŋ, lokalimoki yes abeit, naeirarit kama ejai Edeke: mam Aburaam abu kiswama kwaŋin." 
John8:41 Iswamaete yesi aswamisio nuka papakus.” Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Mam sio kiwuritai kadoteu; ejai sio Papa ediopet, ŋes Edeke.”" 
John8:42 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Arai kerai Edeke Papakus, tikiminas eoŋ; naarai abu kalom kama ka Edeke kabu; naarai mam kabuni kanukaŋ bon, konye ŋes kejukunit." 
John8:43 Kanukinyo mam ijenuniata ŋun nuenera eoŋ? Naarai mam ipedorete aiirar akakirot. 
John8:44 Iraas yesi luka Satan papakus, ikotosi da aswam airaŋaanut naka papakus. Kerai ŋesi ekaaran ameun kageunet, mam icasit kotoma abeit, naarai emamei abeit kotomakeŋ. Nainerar nukaiŋal, inera nueraas nukeŋ elopet; naarai erai ekeŋalan, papa da loka aiŋalanut." 
John8:45 Konye naarai enera eoŋ abeit mam kiyuunito eoŋ. 
John8:46 Iŋai kayes kelepilepi nukaronok? Arai enera eoŋ abeit, kanukinyo mam yes iyuuniata?" 
John8:47 Yenerai yenika Edeke iirari akiro nuka Edeke; kanuka ŋun mam yes iirarete, naarai mam iraas luka Edeke.”" 
John8:48 Koboŋokis Iyudayan kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Aso ca ma mam teni sio kinerit ejok ebe irai Esamariat, ido ejai jo ajokit?”" 
John8:49 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Emamei eoŋ ajokit; konye ayoŋit eoŋ Papaka, konye yes kimwaŋito eoŋ." 
John8:50 Kwabo eoŋ mam amoot akaibuses; ejai loemoot ka aitub da. 
John8:51 Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Arai keric ituŋanan akakirot, mam egipari atwanare ikar kere.”" 
John8:52 Kobalas Iyudayan ebe, “Kwana do kijeni ebe ejai jo ajokit, Kotwana Aburaam, ka inabin da; ibala ijo ebe, ‘Arai keric ituŋanan akakirot, mam iiri atwanare ikar kere.’" 
John8:53 Itelekarit tope ijo kapolou papaakosi Aburaam loketwani? Inabin da luketwakete; ituluori ijo elopet iŋai?” 
John8:54 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Arai ketopoloor eoŋ elopet, akaibuses mam erai ibore; loketopoloorit eoŋ ŋes Papaka; ŋol loibakasi yesi ebe erai Ekusideke;" 
John8:55 kwabo mam ipotu kojenut ŋes; konye eoŋ ajeni ŋes; arai kener ebe, ‘Mam ajeni ŋes,’ tikaraun ekeŋalan kwape kayesi; konye ajeni ŋes, aricit da akekirot." 
John8:56 Abu papaakus Aburaam kolelakinite aanyun akapaaran; ŋes da koany, kiyalamikin.”" 
John8:57 Kosodete kotemasi lyudayan atiar, “Eroko jo edolo ikar akaisakany, ianyunit tope ijo Aburaam?”" 
John8:58 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Eroko Aburaam ejauna, ajai eoŋ.”" 
John8:59 Kosodete kirarata amor tetere ibiribirete; konye Yesu koŋop, koloma koyekalu." 
John9:1 Nakitoritor, koany etuŋanan emuduki ameun kaurioke," 
John9:2 Kiŋita ŋes ikekesisiak ebe, “Rabi, iŋai bo kediakarit, etuŋanan lo arai bo ikekauriak, tape eurio emudukana?”" 
John9:3 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Mam lo ediakarit, karaida ikekauriak; konye tetere itodiaros aswamisio nuka Edeke kotomakeŋ." 
John9:4 Kibusakinit aswam aswamisio nuka ŋol lokejukuni, eroko apaaran; ebuni akuar, namam epedoria ituŋanan aswam." 
John9:5 Naajaar eoŋ akwapin, arai eoŋ aica naka akwapin.”" 
John9:6 Nakedaunia einer ŋun, kimuik aimul kwap, kosubunia elupe, kinyonyo akonye nuka etuŋanan kelupe," 
John9:7 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Kolot kilota katapar naka Siloam” (apolouke ebe Loiyakiaritai), Kosodi kolot, kilota, koboŋu eseseni," 
John9:8 Kosodete ikeidunyeta ka lukeanyununete lem erai ekelipan kotemasi atiar, “Mere kereka lo lolem iboienenei ilipitoi?”" 
John9:9 Kobalas ice ebe, “Ŋes ŋol”; ka ice da ebe, “Mam, konye eputosi kaŋes.” Kobala ŋesi ebe, “Eoŋ lopelo.”" 
John9:10 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kekwenyunete biai akonikonye?”" 
John9:11 Koboŋok ebe, “Etuŋanan loenyaritai Yesu kosub elupe kenyonyoik akakonye katema atiar, ‘Kolot Siloam kilota’; kasodi kalot, kelota, kakweny.”" 
John9:12 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Ai bo ejai ŋol?” Kotema atiar, “Mam eoŋ ajeni.”" 
John9:13 Koyaŋaasi lokerai lem emuduki mama ejaas Iparisayon. 
John9:14 Kerai apaaran nakasabato nakesubia Yesu elupe ka aitwekenyun da akekonye. 
John9:15 Aso kiŋita ŋes bobo Iparisayon da epone lokekwenyunia, Kotema kes atiar, “Abu kibwaik elupe akonyeka, kelota, kwana do aseseni.”" 
John9:16 Kobalas ice koParisayon ebe, “Mam etuŋanan ŋol ebunit kama ejai Edeke, naarai mam ericit nakasabato.” Konye kobalas ice ebe, “Epedori biai ekadiakanaran aswam aanyuneta nuikote nen?” Kojaun atiakatiakaun kamakec." 
John9:17 Kobalas bobo emuduki ebe, “Ido bo jo ibala biai kanukeŋ, naarai abu kitwekeny akonikonyen?” Kobala ebe, “Erai enabi.”" 
John9:18 Aso mam Iyudayan apotu kiyuut akekiro ebe kerai lem emuduki, kosodi akwenyun, kiton neanyarauniata ikauriak luka lokitwekenyunio," 
John9:19 kiŋita kes ebe, “Erai kereka lo okokukus? Loibalasi aurio emudukana? Ikwaikini bo ai ekwenyi kwana?”" 
John9:20 Koboŋokis ikekauriak ebe, “Kijeni ebe lo ŋes okokukosi, ebe da aurio emudukana;" 
John9:21 konye epone loekwenyia kwana mam kijeni; mam kijeni da yenikitwekenyuni ŋes akonye. Kiŋita ŋes; epol ŋesi, ineri elopet kanukeŋ.”" 
John9:22 Enerasi ikekauriak kwaŋin naarai akuriaka Iyudayan; naarai enerunitos Iyudayan ebe arai elimori ituŋanan ŋes araut Kristo, ireŋeario katukos." 
John9:23 Kanuka ŋun ŋes eneratar ikekauriak ebe, “Epol ŋesi; kiŋita ŋes.”" 
John9:24 Konyaraut nakiareit etuŋanan loamudukana, kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kitopolo Edeke; kijeni isio ebe erai etuŋanan ŋol ekadiakanaran.”" 
John9:25 Koboŋok ebe, “Arai ca erai ekadiakanaran, mam eoŋ ajeni; ajeni adiopekirot ebe karai eoŋ emuduki, kwana do akwenyi.”" 
John9:26 Kosodete kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kiikonakini ai? Kiitwekenyuni biai akonikonye?”" 
John9:27 Koboŋok kes ebe, “Kadau alimokin yesi komam iirarete. Kanukinyo bobo ikototor akiirar? Ikotosi yesi da araun ikekesisiak?”" 
John9:28 Komoromoroto, kobalas ebe, “Ijo irai ekekesisian; konye kirai isio ikesisiak luka Musa." 
John9:29 Kijeni isio ebe abu Edeke kinera ka Musa; konye ŋol mam kijeni nekebunio.” 
John9:30 Koboŋok etuŋanan kotema atiar, “Eraas nu nukaumokin, ebe mam yes ijenete nekebunio, konye abu ketwekeny akakonye." 
John9:31 Kijeni ebe mam Edeke iirari ikadiakanarak; konye arai emai ituŋanan Edeke, iswamai da nuekoto ŋesi, iirari ŋol." 
John9:32 Ameun kageunet naka akwapin mam lem iiraritai ebe itwekenyunit ituŋanan akonye nuka yeneuritai emudukana," 
John9:33 Arai kemam ŋol ebunit kama ejai Edeke, ti mam kepedo aswam akirot kere.”" 
John9:34 Koboŋokis kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kiwuritai cut jo kotoma adiakar, kisisianakini kereka ijo da sio?” Kireŋeasi ŋes kiŋa," 
John9:35 Kiira Yesu ebe ereŋeasi kiŋa, kodum ŋes kotema atiar, “Iyuunit kereka ijo Okoku loka etuŋanan”" 
John9:36 Koboŋok ŋesi kotema atiar, “Ŋes bo iŋai, Ejakait, keyuu ŋes?”" 
John9:37 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Iany ŋes, ŋes ŋol loineras kajo.”" 
John9:38 Kotema atiar, “Ejakait, eyuunit.” Komaa ŋes," 
John9:39 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Abu kabu toma akwapin nu kanuka etube, tetere eanyunete lumam eanyunete, koraut da lueanyunete imudukiok.”" 
John9:40 Nakiirariata ice koParisayon lukejaas nepepe kaŋes, kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kirai kereka isio da imudukiok?”" 
John9:41 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Arai kiraas imudukiok, timam ijaas kadiakar; konye kwana ibalasi ebe ‘Kikwenyi,’ aso esalit adiakarikus.”" 
John10:1 “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, yenimam itori orute elomari anuk naka amerekekin konye kodoka kamace, erai ŋin ikokolan ka ikaŋatan da;" 
John10:2 konye yenitori orute ŋes erai ekecokon loka amerekekin. 
John10:3 Eŋaikini ekagolon ŋes; iirarete amerekekin ekeporoto, enyarai ŋesi akemerekekin kikiroriakec, itolomari kes kiŋa," 
John10:4 Kedau aitolomar nukeŋ kere, iŋarenikini kes, etupakinete amerekekin, naarai ejenete ekeporoto." 
John10:5 Mam etuparete cut eloŋwau, konye ekerete kama ejai, naarai mam ejenete eporoto loka iloŋwau.”" 
John10:6 Abu Yesu kolimok kes awaragan ŋin, konye mam ejenuna akiro nualimokini kes." 
John10:7 Kolimok Yesu kes bobo ebe, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, arai eoŋ erute loka amerekekin." 
John10:8 Kere lukageikinete keraas ikokolak ka ikaŋatak; konye mam apotu amerekekin kiirasi kes. 
John10:9 Arai eoŋ erute; arai kitoro ituŋanan mamakaŋ, itajario, elomari ka alomun, edumuni da erony." 
John10:10 Mam ekokolan ebuni atai dimarai akoko, ka aiar, ka amunaar da; abu eoŋ kabu tetere ejaunete kaijar, ejaunete da kanaedeparit." 
John10:11 Arai eoŋ ekecokon lokajokan. Einakini ekecokon lokajokan akeijar kanuka amerekekin. 
John10:12 Etuŋanan loeropio, lomam erai ekecokon, amerekekin da mam eraas nuke, eanyuni epeet ebuni, inyeini amerekekin, ekeri; ikami do epeet kes, isiarakini." 
John10:13 Ekeri ŋol naarai erai loeropio, mam epodo amerekekin." 
John10:14 Arai eoŋ ekecokon lokajokan; ajeni ŋun nueraas nukaŋ, nukaŋ da kajenete eoŋ," 
John10:15 kwape kajenia Papa, eoŋ da ajeni Papa; ainakini akaijar kanuka amerekekin." 
John10:16 Ido ejaas eoŋ amerekekin ace, numam eraas nuka anuk kana; kebusakinit ayaun ŋun da, iirarete ekaporoto; kosodete araun esipan ediopet, ka ekecokon ediopet." 
John10:17 Kanuka na kamina Papa, naarai ejaikini akaijar, tetere alemuni bobo." 
John10:18 Emamei ituŋanan yenikademari, konye ejaikini eoŋ elopet. Ejai eoŋ apedor naka aijaikin, ejai da apedor alemun bobo; adumunit aicorakinet na kama ejai Papaka.”" 
John10:19 Kojau bobo atiakatiak koYudayan kanuka akiro kaŋun," 
John10:20 Luipu kakes kobalas ebe, “Ejai lo ajokit, ekerepiki; kanukinyo iirariata ŋes?”" 
John10:21 Kobalas ice ebe, “Akiro ŋun mam eraas nuka ituŋanan yenejai ajokit. Epedori kereka ajokit aitwekenyun akonye nuka imudukiok?”" 
John10:22 Kerai epucit loka Atiakunio koYerusalem; kapak naka aterot; 
John10:23 kitorit Yesu oyekalu alomaret naka Solomon. 
John10:24 Kosodete kolukut ŋes Iyudayan kotemasi atiar, “Itodoli ai isibuonokini ikositauon? Arai irai Kristo, kolimokinai kaitebeikin.”" 
John10:25 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Abu kalimok yes, konye mam iyuunito. Aswamisio nueswamai eoŋ kokiror loka Papaka, kes ketejenunito." 
John10:26 Konye yes mam iyuunito, naarai mam iraas lukotoma amerekekinika." 
John10:27 Iirarete akamerekekin ekaporoto, ajeni kes, kes da katupito eoŋ;" 
John10:28 ainakini kes aijar naka ikar kere, mam cut eoliorete, kwabo emamei ituŋanan yeneurupoori kes kakanika." 
John10:29 Papaka lokainakini ŋun erai lokapolon aitelekarit kere, kwabo emamei ituŋanan yenepedori aurupoor kes kakan naka Papaka." 
John10:30 Kirai eoŋ ka Papa ipe.” 
John10:31 Kosodete kirarata bobo Iyudayan amor aibiribirio ŋes. 
John10:32 Koboŋok Yesu kes ebe, “Ketodik yes aswamisio nuipu nuejok nuepote kama ejai Papa; kanuka aswamisioit anyoin kaŋun kibiribirioto eoŋ kamor?”" 
John10:33 Koboŋokis Iyudayan ebe, “Mam kibiribiri jo kanuka aswamisioit naejok, konye kanuka ainyanakin Edeke; naarai jo etuŋanan, ituluori bon Edeke.”" 
John10:34 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Mam kereka iwadikatai kokisilakus ebe, ‘Kabala iraas yesi idekesio’?" 
John10:35 Arai abu konyara kes idekesio ŋul lukebunokini akirot naka Edeke (ido mam epedorete nukiwadikatai abilio)," 
John10:36 ibalasi kereka yesi lokitalauni Papa kijuk akwapin ebe, ‘Iinyanakini Edeke’; kanu abalar ebe, ‘Arai eoŋ Okoku loka Edeke’?" 
John10:37 Arai mam eswamai aswamisio nuka Papaka, sirikiyuut." 
John10:38 Konye arai eswamai, karaida mam kiyuunito eoŋ, kiyuutu aswamisio; tetere ijenunete ipiirikinete da ebe ejai Papa tomaka, eoŋ da toma Papa.”" 
John10:39 Komoata bobo aikamun ŋes; konye koku kakanikec. 
John10:40 Kolot bobo okekwa Yorodan aibois nakegeunia Yokana aibatis; kosalak ŋina. 
John10:41 Kopotu luipu mamakeŋ; kobalas ebe, “Abeit mam Yokana eswamat aanyunet kere: konye nukinera Yokana kere kanuka ŋol keraas abeit.”" 
John10:42 Kiyuut luipu kaŋina. 
John11:1 Kodeka etuŋanan, ekekiror Lasaro loko Betaniya, lokorekec loka Mariam ka Marita kinacike." 
John11:2 Ŋes Mariam nakinyonyoanakini Ejakait akinyet, konina akekeje kitimake, ŋipeŋin nakedeka onaceke Lasaro." 
John11:3 Aso kiyakiasi ainacan ŋun mama ejai Yesu ebe, “Ejakait, edeka ŋol loimina ijo.”" 
John11:4 Konye nakiiraria Yesu kobala ebe, “Adeka na mam erai nakatwanare; konye kanuka aibuses naka Edeke, tetere itopoloorio Okoku loka Edeke kanuka ŋun.”" 
John11:5 Komina Yesu Marita ka inacike, ka Lasaro da." 
John11:6 Aso nakiiraria ebe edek, kosalak nekejai apaarasia aarei," 
John11:7 Kosodi kokau kaŋun kotema ikekesisiak atiar, “Kaloto bobo Yudaya.”" 
John11:8 Kotemasi ŋes ikekesisiak atiar, “Rabi, koloje kwape kwana kikotos Iyudayan aibiribir kamor, ilosi teni bobo ŋipeŋina?”" 
John11:9 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Mam kereka eraas isawan luka paaran itomon ka luarei? Arai elosi ituŋanan paaran mam iguikini, naarai eanyuni aica naka akwapin kanu." 
John11:10 Konye arai kelot kuare, iguikini, naarai emamei aica kotomakeŋ.”" 
John11:11 Kinera ŋun, kosodi kotema kes atiar, “Opaperowok Lasaro ejotoi, konye alosi eoŋ ketwekeny.”" 
John11:12 Kotemasi ikekesisiak ebe, “Ejakait, arai eiotoi, eŋaleuni.”" 
John11:13 Konye kinera Yesu nuka atwanareke, koomitos kesi ebe enera akiro nuka ajo." 
John11:14 Kosodi kolimok Yesu kes kaitebeikin ebe, “Atwana Lasaro." 
John11:15 Ido eyalamikin eoŋ kanukus naarai amamei eoŋ kaŋina, tetere iyuunete. Konye kaloto do mamakeŋ.”" 
John11:16 Kosodi Tomas loenyaritai Didumo kobala ikepaup ikesisiak ebe, “Kaloto oni da, katwaka nepepe kaŋes.”" 
John11:17 Kosodi nakedolio Yesu kodum edaunit ŋesi apaarasia aoŋon kates," 
John11:18 Keapias Betaniya ka Yerusalem, bala amairon aarei," 
John11:19 keponitos ituŋa luipu ko Yudayan mama ejai Marita ka Mariam aipudun kes kanuka onacekec. 
John11:20 Kosodi nakiiraria Marita ebe ebunit Yesu, kolot aisiriam ŋes; kosalakinite Mariam togo." 
John11:21 Kosodi kotema Marita Yesu atiar, “Ejakait, arai kijai ijo ne, timam onaceka ketwana." 
John11:22 Konye kwana da ajeni ebe kere nuilipi ijo Edeke kiinakini Edeke.” 
John11:23 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Ejaruni onacekon.”" 
John11:24 Kotema Marita ŋes atiar, “Ajeni ebe ejaruni kotoma ajarun naka apaaran nakawasia.”" 
John11:25 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Arai eoŋ ajarun ka aijar da; ŋin yenikeyuuni eoŋ, karaida ketwana, ejari." 
John11:26 Ŋin da yenejari yenikeyuuni eoŋ mam etwani ikar kere. Iyuunit kereka ijo ŋun?” 
John11:27 Kotema ŋes atiar, “Eebo, Ejakait; eyuunit eoŋ ebe irai ijo Kristo, Okoku loka Edeke, loebunit akwapin.”" 
John11:28 Nakedaunia einer ŋun, kolot, konyarau kinacike Mariam kaiyeiyea, kobala ebe, “Ejai Ekesisianakinan ne, kinyarit jo.”" 
John11:29 Nakiiraria ŋesi ŋun, kodetun atipet, kolot mamakeŋ," 
John11:30 Aroko Yesu edoluno ore, konye aroko ejai aibois naesiriamia Marita." 
John11:31 Kosodete Iyudayan luajaas ka Mariam togo ipudunete, nakeanyuniata edetun atipet ka alomar kiŋa, kotupasi ŋes, koomito ebe elosi ates aimony ŋina." 
John11:32 Kosodi nakedolio Mariam nekejai Yesu, koany ŋes, kibirokin akejeke, kotema atiar, “Ejakait, arai kijai ijo ne timam onaceka ketwana.”" 
John11:33 Nakeanyunia Yesu ŋes emonyi, ka Iyudayan da lukeupas kaŋes emonyete, komulau eketau, kokadak," 
John11:34 kotema atiar, “Ibwaikinito ai?” Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, bia koany.”" 
John11:35 Komony Yesu," 
John11:36 Kosodete kotemasi Iyudayan atiar, “Koany, kwape lem keminar ŋes!”" 
John11:37 Konye kobalasi ice kakesi ebe, “Ŋol lokitwekenyuni akonye nuka emuduki mam tikepedo aisimik ŋol atwanare?”" 
John11:38 Kosodi Yesu, komulau bobo eketau, kodol ates; kerai abua, kerapakinitai amoru," 
John11:39 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Kolemasi amoru.” Kobala Marita inac naka lokatwan ebe, “Ejakait, eur kwana, naarai edaunit apaarasia aoŋon etwanit.”" 
John11:40 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Mam kereka kalimokinit jo ebe arai iyuunit, ianyuni aibuses naka Edeke?”" 
John11:41 Kosodete kolemasi amoru. Kikeu Yesu akekonye akuj, kotema atiar, “Kemalai jo Papa, naarai kiira eoŋ." 
John11:42 Kajen ebe kiiranari eoŋ apaarasia kere, konye kener nu kanuka ekodet kalo loejai ne, tetere iyuunete ebe jo kijukunit eoŋ.”" 
John11:43 Nakedaunia einer ŋun, kiworo keporoto loepol ebe, “Lasaro, kolom.”" 
John11:44 Kolom lokatwan, eenitai akanin ka akeje kigoen luka aida; eenitai akekonye da keitabala. Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Kolacasi ŋes, koosikis kolot.”" 
John11:45 Kosodete kiyuutu ŋes luipu kotoma oYudayan lukeponito mama ejai Mariam, lukeanyunito nueswamat Yesu." 
John11:46 Konye ice kakesi koloto mama ejaas Iparisayon, kolimokis nukiswamai Yesu." 
John11:47 Kosodete isasedotin lupeti ka Iparisayon kotukokis aurianet, kobalas ebe, “Kikwaikini ai? Naarai iswamai etuŋanan ŋol aanyuneta nuipu." 
John11:48 Arai kiinyei, iyuunete ŋes ituŋa kere: epote Iromayon kidemarete oni aiboisiwok ka awokoteker da.”" 
John11:49 Konye ediopet kakesi, ŋes Kaiapa, lokerai losasedoti lopeti kokaru kaŋol, kotema kes atiar, “Mam iienete adiokirot kere." 
John11:50 Kwabo mam iwomito ebe ibusakinit ediopetuŋanan atwanare kanuka ituŋa, kinye ateker kere amudiar.”" 
John11:51 Mam ŋes kinera akirot ŋin kanukeŋ bon; konye naarai kerai losasedoti lopeti kokaru kaŋol, abu kodwar ebe etwani Yesu kanuka ateker;" 
John11:52 kwabo mere kanuka ateker kaŋin bon, konye tetere etukokini nepepe idwe luka Edeke lukisiarakinos araut ipe," 
John11:53 Ameun kapaaran kaŋin kinerut nuka aiar ŋes. 
John11:54 Kanuka ŋun mam bobo Yesu alosi kaitebeikin kotoma oYudayan, konye konyou kaŋina kolot aibois naeapias kamodiŋ, kiton ore loenyaritai Epuraim; kosal ŋina nenipe kikekesisiak." 
John11:55 Keapie Aleleŋ naka Iyudayan; kodokasi luipu Yerusalem anyoun kamanat aliŋakin Aleleŋ, tetere italaunos." 
John11:56 Kosodete komoata Yesu, kineranakinos ebwoete koyekalu ebe, “Iwomito inyo? Mam kereka ŋes ebuni opucit lo?”" 
John11:57 Kicorakinito isasedotin lupeti ka Iparisayon ebe arai kejenu ituŋanan neejai, kitejenu kes, tetere ikamunete." 
John12:1 Kosodi esalito apaarasia akanykape eriŋa edoluno Aleleŋ, kobu Yesu Betaniya, nekejai Lasaro, lokitajaruni Yesu kotoma okatwak." 
John12:2 Kitemokinoi epucit kanen; kijaanak Marita, konye kerai Lasaro ediopet kalukemorete kaŋes." 
John12:3 Kosodi kolem Mariam elatiri loka akinyet naelai naka etiai loepol, kinyonyoanak akeje nuka Yesu, konina akekeje kitimake; kilelebun aures naka akinyet etogo kere," 
John12:4 Konye kobala Yuda Isikariot, ediopet kokesisiakake, loekoto abilakin ŋes ebotet, ebe," 
John12:5 “Kanukinyo mam egwelarere akinyet na adenarin akwat auni, koinakinai lukican?”" 
John12:6 Kinera nu mere kanu etimitor lukican; konye naarai kerai ekokolan, ŋes etiŋenenei eriagi koyaŋanar nukibwaanakinio toma." 
John12:7 Kosodi kotema Yesu atiar, “Kinyeisi ŋes, kiŋadak kanuka apaaran naka aidaioka," 
John12:8 Naarai ejaas lukican nenipe kayes apaarasia kere, konye eoŋ mam kija kayes apaarasia kere.”" 
John12:9 Kosodete kejenut luipu koYudayan ebe ejai ŋina; kopotu kesi, mere kanuka Yesu bon, dimarai aanyun Lasaro da, lokitajaruni ŋesi kotoma okatwak." 
John12:10 Konye kinerut isasedotin lupeti aiar Lasaro da; 
John12:11 naarai kanukeŋ apotu luipu koYudayan kotiakas, kiyuut Yesu." 
John12:12 Apaaran naatupakini kiira ekodet loepol loabunit kanuka epucit ebe ebuni Yesu Yerusalem. 
John12:13 Kogweununut atenieik nuka amusogon, kolomasi aisiriam ŋes, kiworoto ebe, “Kosana! Isirereŋitoi ŋol loebunit kokiror loka Ejakait, Ekabaka loka Isirael!”" 
John12:14 Adumunit Yesu ikoku yenika asigiria, kibwanen; kwape iwadikatere ebe," 
John12:15 “Sirikikurianar, ijo akoku naka Sion; Koany ebunit Ekonikabaka, Ibwanenit ikoku yenika asigiria.”" 
John12:16 Mam ber ikekesisiak apotu kojenut ŋun: konye kedau Yesu aitopoloorio, ŋes konyet kiitunioto ebe iwadikatai ŋun kanukeŋ, eswamakis da ŋes ŋun." 
John12:17 Kitejen ekodet lokejai kaŋes nakenyaraunia Lasaro alomun kates, kitajaru da ŋes kokatwak." 
John12:18 Kanuka ŋun kolot ekodet aisiriam ŋes naarai apotu kiirasi ebe eswamat aanyunet ŋin," 
John12:19 Kineranakinos Iparisayon bonik ebe, “Koanyutu mam ipedorete ibore; koany, atupasi ŋes lukakwapin kere.”" 
John12:20 Kejaas Iyonanin ice kotoma kalukedokarito aima kopucit," 
John12:21 Aso koloto ŋul mama ejai Pilip, etuŋanan loko Betesaida loko Galilaya, kilipata ŋes ebe, “Ejakait, kikoto isio aanyun Yesu.”" 
John12:22 Kolot Pilip kolimok Anderea; kouparos Anderea ka Pilip, kolimokis Yesu." 
John12:23 Koboŋok Yesu kes ebe, “Adol esawa kitopolooroi Okoku loka etuŋanan," 
John12:24 Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Arai mam ecokat loka akimait edoi kwap kotwani, esalit ikoni nepenen; konye arai ketwana, erai araito nuipu." 
John12:25 Yenemina akeijar itooliori; ka yenelait akeijar kakwapin kanu idari kiton aijar naka ikar kere. 
John12:26 Arai kejaanakini ituŋanan eoŋ, katup; neajai eoŋ ejauni ikakejaanakinan da nepenen; arai kejaanakini ituŋanan eoŋ, itopoloori Papa ŋes." 
John12:27 “Kwana ekadakinit ekatau; atemari ai? Papa, koyuunai kosawa kalo. Konye kanuka ŋun abu kadol osawa lo." 
John12:28 Papa, kitopoloo ekonikiror.” Kosodi kobu eporoto kotoma akuj ebe, “Etopolo, ido etopoloori bobo.”" 
John12:29 Nakiiraria ekodet lokebwoi kanen kobalas ebe Eretu akuj; kobalas ice ebe, “Emalaika enerata kaŋes.”" 
John12:30 Koboŋok Yesu kotema atiar, “Mam ebunit eporoto lo kanukaŋ, konye kanukus." 
John12:31 Atubokin kwana akwapin nu akiro: ereŋear kwana ekapolon loka akwapin kanu. 
John12:32 Eoŋ da arai keekiar kakwap, eriari ituŋa kere mamakaŋ.”" 
John12:33 Konye kinera nu itodikini aketwanare naetwani. 
John12:34 Koboŋok ekodet kotema ŋes atiar, “Kiirarit isio kotoma okisila ebe ebusi Kristo ikar kere: ikwaikini ai ijo inera ebe ibusakinit Okoku loka etuŋanan aikiario? Iŋai bo ŋol erai Okoku loka etuŋanan?”" 
John12:35 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Eroko aica ejai kayes apak naedit. Koloto yesi eroko aica ejai kayes, kinye amuton adolokin yes; ŋin yenelosi kamuton mam ejeni neelosi." 
John12:36 Eroko aica ejai kayes, kiyuutu aica ŋin, tetere iraunete idwe luka aica.” Kiner Yesu ŋun, konyou kamakec koŋop." 
John12:37 Karaida abu kiswama aanyuneta nuipu noi kakonyenekec mam apotu kiyuut ŋes; 
John12:38 tetere edoli akirot naka enabi Isaia nakinerit ebe, “Ejakait, iŋai eyuunit akosikirot? Iŋai da epukokinitai akan naka Ejakait?”" 
John12:39 Kanuka ŋun ŋes mam kiyuuniata naarai enerit bobo Isaia ebe," 
John12:40 “Etumudak akecekonye, etininik ikecetauon, Kinyeis aanyun kakecekonye, kojenut kotauonokec, Ka aibelokin, ketaŋaleu kes.”" 
John12:41 Kinera Isaia akiro ŋun naarai abu koany aibusesuke, kolimo akiroke." 
John12:42 Konye kiton ikayaitok da kiyuut ŋes luipu; konye kanuka Iparisayon mam apotu kolimosi, kinyeis aireŋeario katukos:" 
John12:43 naarai keminasi aibuses naka ituŋa aitelekarit aibuses naka Edeke. 
John12:44 Kiworo Yesu kobala ebe, “Ŋin yenikeyuunit eoŋ, mam keyuunit eoŋ, dimarai je lokejukuni." 
John12:45 Yenikaanyuni eoŋ, eanyuni je lokejukuni," 
John12:46 Abu eoŋ kabu araun aica toma akwapin, tetere ŋin yenikeyuunit mam esalakini amuton," 
John12:47 Arai kiira ituŋanan akakiro, komam erici, mam eoŋ atubokini ŋes; naarai mam eoŋ abunit atubokin akwapin, dimarai aitajar akwapin." 
John12:48 Yenikaŋeri eoŋ, yenimam ecamuni akakiro, ejai ekatubokinanike: akirot naenerit, ŋes etubokini kapaaran nakawasia." 
John12:49 Naarai mam eoŋ enerit kanukaŋ bon; konye Papa lokejukuni kainakinit aicorakinet, nuatemari ka nuenera da." 
John12:50 Ajeni ebe akeicorakinet erai aijar naka ikar kere: aso akiro nuenera eoŋ, kwape kalimokinitor Papa, kwape kwaŋin enerar.”" 
John13:1 Kosodi eriŋa edolo epucit loka Aleleŋ, kejeni Yesu ebe adolu ekesawa loenyounio kakwapin kanu alosit mama ejai Papa, kemina ŋesi iketuŋa lukejaas akwapin, komina kes aitodol awasia," 
John13:2 Napenyamete lukatiboŋ, kodaunite Satan aibwaikin Yuda Isikariot, okoku loka Simon, etau lokabilakin ebotet," 
John13:3 kejeni Yesu ebe ainaki Papa akiro kere akaninike, ebe da alomu kama ejai Edeke, elosi da mama ejai Edeke," 
John13:4 konyou konyamat, kolaca ikenapen; kolem aninaet, koenik aŋabeteke." 
John13:5 Kosodi kobukok akipi atuba, kogeu ailot ikekesisiak akeje, ka anina kes kaninaet nakenapit." 
John13:6 Kodolok do Simon Petero. Kotema Petero ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, ilosi ijo akakeje?”" 
John13:7 Koboŋok Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Nueswamai eoŋ mam ijeni kwana, konye ijenuni kokau.”" 
John13:8 Kotema Petero atiar, “Mam jo ilosi akakeje cut kiton ikar kere.” Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Arai mam kelosi jo, mam imorikikina keoŋ.”" 
John13:9 Kotema Simon Petero ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, mere akakeje bon, konye akakanin ka akakou da.”" 
John13:10 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Yenedauni ailoŋ emamei eipud dimarai ailot akeje, konye elai akuan kere: ilaete yesi da, konye mere kere.”" 
John13:11 Naarai ajeni ŋesi loekoto abilakin ŋes ebotet; ŋes abalar ebe, “Mam ilaete kere.”" 
John13:12 Kosodi nakedaunia ailot akejekec, ka alemun ikenapen, ka aiboikin bobo, kotema kes atiar, “Ijenut kereka nukeswamak eoŋ yes?" 
John13:13 Kinyarito eoŋ Ekesisianakinan ka Ejakait da; inerasi yesi kotenan, naarai arai eoŋ kwaŋin." 
John13:14 Aso arai eoŋ, Ekusijakait ka Ekusikesisianakinan da, kelot yes akeje, ibusakinit yes da ailot akeje nuka lucekus." 
John13:15 Naarai kainak yes aitodikinet, tetere iswamaete yesi da kwape keswamakinia yes." 
John13:16 Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Mam ebulesit itelekarit ejakaitike; karaida ekiyakia aitelekarit lokiyakiari." 
John13:17 Arai kijenutu ŋun, isirereŋitoi yes arai kiswamata," 
John13:18 Mam enera nukus kere: ajeni luaseunit; konye kodol naiwadikatai ebe, ‘Lokenyami ikanyamat, ŋes ketonyoik aketitibat.’" 
John13:19 Amear kwana kalimokini eriŋa edoluno, tetere naedolunioto, kiyuut ebe eoŋ ŋopeŋol," 
John13:20 Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Yenisukunyikini ŋin yeneyakiari, kesukunyik eoŋ; yenikesukunyikini eoŋ isukunyikinit je lokejukuni.”" 
John13:21 Kedau Yesu einer ŋun, kokadak kotauke, kitejenu kobala ebe, “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, ediopet kayesi kabilakini ebotet.”" 
John13:22 Koŋoleanakinos ikesisiak, kobuonokinos iŋai bo ŋol loelimit ŋesi," 
John13:23 Kejai ediopet kokesisiakake lokegoŋakina atorob naka Yesu, lokemina Yesu." 
John13:24 Aso kokwet Simon Petero ŋes, kobala ebe, “Kiŋitu cani loelimit ŋesi.”" 
John13:25 Aso egoŋakina ŋesi kwape kwaŋin atorob naka Yesu, kotema atiar, “Ejakait, ŋes bo iŋai?”" 
John13:26 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Loecunyakini aodunet kainak, ŋes ŋol.” Kosodi kedau aicunyakin aodunet, kolem koinak Yuda okoku loka Simon Isikariot." 
John13:27 Kokau kaodokinet, kolomak Satan ŋes, Kosodi kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Nuiswamai, kisunyite aswam.”" 
John13:28 Kwabo emamei etuŋanan kalukemorete kaŋes lokejeni akirot nakelimokinia ŋes ŋun. 
John13:29 Naarai koomitos ice ebe naarai itiŋit Yuda eriagi, abu Yesu kolimok ŋes ebe, “Kogwel lukipuda kanuka epucit,” arai ebe kijaik lukican ibore." 
John13:30 Kosodi kedau ŋol aijaar aodokinet, atipet koloma: kerai da kuare." 
John13:31 Kosodi nakedaunia ŋol alomar, kotema Yesu atiar, “Kwana itopolooritai Okoku loka etuŋanan; Edeke da itopolooritai kotomakeŋ," 
John13:32 Itopoloori Edeke ŋes kotomakeŋ, itopoloori da atipet." 
John13:33 Yes idwe ludidik, eroko apak naedit ajai nepepe kayes. Kimoete eoŋ; kwape abu kalimokinitor Iyudayan ebe, ‘Nealosi eoŋ, mam yes ipedorete abunore’; kwana da kalimokini yes kwape kwaŋin," 
John13:34 Kainakini yes aicorakinet nakitetet ebe, Kominanaros; kwape abu kaminar yes, kominanaros yesi da kwape kwaŋin." 
John13:35 Kanuka ŋun ejenunete ituŋa kere ebe iraas yesi ikakesisiak, arai iminanaros bonik.”" 
John13:36 Kotema Simon Petero ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, ilosi bo ai?” Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Nealosi eoŋ, mam kipedori atupun kwana; konye kitupuni kokau.”" 
John13:37 Kotema Petero ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, kanukinyo mam eoŋ apedoria atupar jo kwana? Ainakini akaijar kanukon.”" 
John13:38 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Iinakini kereka ijo akoniijar kanukaŋ? Abeit, abeit, katemari jo atiar, Mam ekokor eruikini, aitodol nakiŋerio eoŋ irwan auni." 
John14:1 “Sirikiyaloŋoŋoto ikusitauon; kiyuutu Edeke, eoŋ da kiyuunai." 
John14:2 Togo loka Papaka ejaas aiboisio nuipu; arai mere kwaŋin tikalimokis kereka yes ebe alosi aitemokin yes aibois? 
John14:3 Arai kalot eoŋ aitemokin yes aibois, aboŋuni bobo kesukunyu yes mamakaŋ, tetere neajai eoŋ ijaikinos yesi da nen." 
John14:4 Ijenete yesi erot loalosi eoŋ,”" 
John14:5 Kotema Tomas atiar, “Ejakait, mam sio kijeni neilosi ijo; kijenuni biai erot?”" 
John14:6 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Arai eoŋ erot, ka abeit, ka aijar da; emamei yenebuni mama ejai Papa, dimikito itorit tomakaŋ." 
John14:7 Arai kiijenete eoŋ, tikijenutu Papaka da; amear kwana ijenete ŋes, ianyut da.”" 
John14:8 Kotema Pilip atiar, “Ejakait, kitodikinai Papa, kidauni.”" 
John14:9 Kotema Yesu atiar, “Ajai lem eoŋ kayes apak naetia nen kere, mam jo da kijeni eoŋ, Pilip? Yenikaanyunit eoŋ, eanyunit Papa; aso biai bo ibalar ijo ebe, ‘Kitodikinai Papa’?" 
John14:10 Mam kereka jo iyuunit ebe ajai eoŋ toma Papa, Papa da tomakaŋ? Akiro nuabala yes mam enera kanukaŋ bon; konye Papa loiboie tomakaŋ iswamai akeswamisio." 
John14:11 Kiyuunai ebe ajai eoŋ toma Papa, Papa da tomakaŋ; arai mere kwaŋin, kiyuunai kanuka aswamisio akulepek." 
John14:12 “Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Yenikeyuuni eoŋ, iswamai ŋesi da aswamisio nueswamai eoŋ; iswamai da aswamisio nuitelekarito ŋun, naarai alosi neejai Papa." 
John14:13 Akirot kere nailipete kokirorika, eswamai ŋin, tetere itopoloorio Papa kotoma Okoku;" 
John14:14 Arai kilipa akirot kere kokirorika, eswamai ŋin," 
John14:15 “Arai kiminas eoŋ, iricete akaicorakineta." 
John14:16 Eoŋ da elipi Papa, kiinakini ŋesi yes Ekayuunan ece, tetere ejaenena kayes ikar kere," 
John14:17 ŋes Emoyo lokabeit, lomam epedorete akwapin adumun; naarai mam eanyunete ŋes karaida ajenun; ijenete yesi ŋes; naarai esalit mamakus, ejaenena da tomakus." 
John14:18 “Mam kenyeinete yes iraas ikokiok; abuni mama ijaas. 
John14:19 Apak edit mam kaanyunete bobo akwapin; konye yes kianyunete; naarai ajari eoŋ, yes da ijarete." 
John14:20 Kapaaran kaŋin ijenunete ebe ajai eoŋ toma Papaka, yes da tomakaŋ, eoŋ da tomakus." 
John14:21 Ŋin yenejaas kakaicorakineta, koricite da kes, ŋin ŋes kamina eoŋ: ŋin da yenikamina eoŋ, eminuni Papaka, eoŋ da aminuni ŋes ka aitakanikin mamake.”" 
John14:22 Kotema Yuda (mere Isikariot) atiar, “Ejakait, ikwaikini ai ikoto aitakanikin mamakosi, kwabo mere akwapin?”" 
John14:23 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Arai kamina ituŋanan, erici da akakirot, eminuni Papaka, sio da kiponi mamakeŋ kitarauni ŋes ekosire." 
John14:24 Ŋin yenimam kamina eoŋ, mam erici akakiro; akirot da naiirarete mam erai nakaŋ dimarai naka Papa lokejukuni." 
John14:25 “Kalimokis yes akiro ŋun, naariŋar ajai kayes." 
John14:26 Konye Ekayuunan, ŋes Emoyo Lokalaunan, loijukuni Papa kokirorika, kisisianakini ŋol yes akiro kere, kisiituni da kere nukalimokinit yes." 
John14:27 Kenyeiniata ainapakin; kainak yes akainapakin; mere kwape einakiniata akwapin, kainakinia eoŋ yes. Sirikiyaloŋoŋoto ikusitauon, kinyeis da akurian." 
John14:28 Ipuput eoŋ abala ebe, Alosi eoŋ, abuni da bobo mama ijaas. Arai kiiminasi eoŋ, tikilakaros, naarai alosi mama ejai Papa; naarai Papa ŋes lokapolon adepar eoŋ." 
John14:29 Kwana da kalimok yes eriŋa edoluno, tetere naedolunio, kiyuut." 
John14:30 Mam bobo kinera kayes akiro nuipu, naarai ebunit ekapolon loka akwapin kanu. Konye emamei ŋes adiokirot kotomakaŋ;" 
John14:31 konye eswamai eoŋ kwape kecorakinitor Papa, tetere ejenunete akwapin ebe amina eoŋ Papa. Konyoutu do, kaloto kane." 
John15:1 “Arai eoŋ emusabibu lokabeit, Papaka da ŋes lokeswaman." 
John15:2 Ŋinitenu kotomakaŋ namam erai araito, elemari ŋesi, ka ŋinitenu da naerai araito igweri, tetere iyatakini aira araito." 
John15:3 Idaut yesi araut luilaete kanuka akirot nakalimokinit. 
John15:4 Kosalakis tomakaŋ, eoŋ da tomakus. Kwape mam epedoria atenu aira araito alopet bon, arai mam esalit toma omusabibu, kwape kwaŋin yes da mam ipedorete, arai mam isalito tomakaŋ." 
John15:5 Arai eoŋ emusabibu, iraas yesi atenun. Yenesalit tomakaŋ, eoŋ da tomakeŋ, erai ŋin araito nuipu, naarai neamamea eoŋ mam ipedorete ibore." 
John15:6 Ituŋanan arai mam esali tomakaŋ, ecakario kiŋa kwape katenu, erinyori; etukokinio atenuna, ecakakinio akim, kidoposi." 
John15:7 Arai isalito tomakaŋ, akakiro da esalito tomakus, kilipata nuikotosi kere, kiswamakinio." 
John15:8 Itopolooritai Papaka kotoma nu arai iraete yesi araito nuipu, iraunos da ikakesisiak," 
John15:9 Kwape kaminar Papa, eoŋ da kamina yes kwape kwaŋin; kosalata toma aminaka." 
John15:10 Arai iricete akaicorakineta, isalete toma aminaka, kwape aricitor eoŋ aicorakineta nuka Papaka, asalit da toma aminake." 
John15:11 Kalimokis yes akiro ŋun tetere ejaun aiyalamaka tomakus, kitodolikinoi da aiyalamakus." 
John15:12 “Na ŋes akaicorakinet ebe Kominanaros, kwape abu kaminar yes," 
John15:13 Emamei yenejaas kamin naepol aitelekarit na, ituŋanan ainakin akeijar kanuka ipaperoke." 
John15:14 Iraas yesi ikapapero arai iswamaete nukecorakini yes. 
John15:15 Mam kanyarit bobo ibulesin, naarai ebulesit mam ejeni nuiswamai ejakaitike, konye kanyara yes ikapapero, naarai ketejenu yes kere nueirarit kama ejai Papaka." 
John15:16 Mere yes kiseunete eoŋ, dimarai eoŋ kaseu yes, kadakak yes tetere ilosete koraata araito, araitokus da kosalito; tetere nuilipete Papa kere kokirorika, kiinakini." 
John15:17 Kecorakini yes ŋun tetere iminanaros. 
John15:18 “Arai kilai yes akwap, kojenutu ebe abu kala eoŋ eriŋa elaa yes." 
John15:19 Arai kiraas lukakwap, tiemina akwap yenerai yenikeŋ; konye naarai mam iraas lukakwap, konye abu kaseu yes kotoma akwap, kanuka ŋun ŋes kilaia yes akwap." 
John15:20 Kiitunito akirot nakalimokinit yes ebe, Mam ebulesit itelekarit ejakaitike kapolou. Arai kareito eoŋ, kireete yes da; arai kericito akakirot, ericete nakus da." 
John15:21 Konye kiswamakinete yes ŋun kere kanuka ekakiror, naarai mam ejenete lokejukunit," 
John15:22 Arai kemam abunit einer kakes, timam ejaas karonis; konye kwana mam eiyaros karonisikec." 
John15:23 Yenikaŋara eoŋ eŋara Papaka da. 
John15:24 Arai mam keswamat kamakec aswamisio numam icetuŋanan iswamat, timam ejaas karonis, konye kwana kaanyut kaŋarut eoŋ ka Papaka da." 
John15:25 Konye itodolikinio akirot naewadikatai kotoma okisilakec ebe, ‘Apotu kalaata atitai.’" 
John15:26 Konye kebu Ekayuunan, lokejukakini yes anyoun kama ejai Papa, ŋes Emoyo Lokabeit, loebuni kama ejai Papa, itejenuni ŋol nukaŋ;" 
John15:27 Yes da itejenunete, naarai ijaas keoŋ ameun kageunet." 
John16:1 “Abu kalimok yes akiro nu, kinyeis aitiguikinio," 
John16:2 Kireŋeanario katukosia; eebo, ebunit esawa loeomitor ŋinituŋanan yenikiari yes ebe iiaanakini Edeke." 
John16:3 Iswamaete ŋun da naarai mam ejenunito Papa, karaida eoŋ." 
John16:4 Konye abu kalimok yes ŋun tetere naedolio esawakec, kiitunete ebe abu kalimokinite yes." 
John16:5 Mam abu kalimok yes nu ameun kageunet, naarai ajai nepepe kayes. “Konye kwana alosi mama ejai je lokejukunit; emamei edio kayesi lokeŋisi ebe, ‘Ilosi bo ai?’" 
John16:6 Konye naarai kalimokis yes akiro nu, elelebunos ican otauonokus," 
John16:7 Konye eoŋ kalimokini yes abeit; ejok kamakus arai kalot eoŋ, naarai arai mam alosi mam ebuni Ekayuunan mama ijaas; konye arai alosi ejukuni ŋes mamakus." 
John16:8 Kebu ŋol, ilepilepi ŋesi akwapin kanuka aronis ka adolit, ka etube da," 
John16:9 Aronis, naarai mam keyuunito eoŋ;" 
John16:10 adolit, naarai alosi mama ejai Papa, mam bobo kianyunete;" 
John16:11 ka etube da, naarai adaun lokapolon loka akwapin kanu atubokinio." 
John16:12 “Eroko ejaas eoŋ nuipu alimokin yes, konye mam ipedorete atitiŋikin kwana." 
John16:13 Kebu je, Emoyo loka abeit, kiŋarenikini yes kabeit kere; naarai mam inera nuke bon, konye inera kere nuepupuni, kitejenuni da yes akiro nuepote." 
John16:14 Ketopoloori ŋesi eoŋ, naarai elemuni nueraas nukaŋ kitejenuni yes," 
John16:15 Nuejaatar Papa kere eraas nukaŋ; kanuka ŋun ŋes abalar ebe elemuni nueraas nukaŋ ka aitejenun yes. 
John16:16 “Apak naedit, mam kianyunete eoŋ; bobo da apak naedit, kianyunete.”" 
John16:17 Kineranakinos ice kokesisiakake atiar, “Anyoika bo nu nuebala ŋesi oni ebe, ‘Apak naedit, mam kianyunete eoŋ, bobo da apak naedit, kianyunete’; ido ebe, ‘Naarai alosi mama ejai Papa’?”" 
John16:18 Kobalas ebe, “Anyoika bo nu nuebala ebe, ‘Apak naedit’? Mam kijeni nuinera.”" 
John16:19 Kojeni Yesu ebe ekotosi aiŋit ŋes; kotema kes atiar, “Nupenu kereka nuiŋitanaros yesi nuabala eoŋ ebe, ‘Apak naedit, mam kianyunete eoŋ, bobo da apak naedit kianyunete’?" 
John16:20 Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Imonyete yesi, ka aibworo, konye iyalamikinos akwapin; itururwete yesi, konye akusiiturur eraun ailel." 
John16:21 Naeriebar aberu aidoun eanyuni ican, naarai adolu ekesawa; konye kedau auruun ikoku, mam bobo iituni ariebo ŋin, kanuka ailel! naarai aurii ituŋanan kotoma akwapin," 
John16:22 Yes da, kwape kwaŋin ianyunete ican kwana, konye eoŋ kaanyuni yes bobo, elelete ikusitauon, emamei yenikidemari akusiilel." 
John16:23 Kapaaran kaŋin mam kiŋisete eoŋ adiokirot. Abeit, abeit, katemari yes atiar, Arai kilipa Papa akirot kere kiinakini kokirorika." 
John16:24 Kiton kwana mam ipotu kilipata akirot kokirorika; kilipa, idumunete tetere itodolikin akusiilel." 
John16:25 “Enera eoŋ ŋun kayes kawaragasia; konye ebunit esawa lomam kinerar bobo kayes kawaragasia, konye kalimokinete kaitebeikin nuka Papa." 
John16:26 Kapaaran kaŋin ilipete kokirorika; kwabo mam kabala ebe eoŋ kelipakini yes kama ejai Papa; 
John16:27 naarai Papa elopet kimina yes, naarai kiminasi yesi eoŋ, ido iyuunito ebe abu kabu kama ejai Papa." 
John16:28 Abu kabu kama ejai Papa, kabu toma akwapin; bobo da enyeini akwapin, alosi mama ejai Papa.”" 
John16:29 Kotemasi ikekesisiak atiar, “Kwana do inera kaitebeikin, kwabo mam bobo inera kawaragan." 
John16:30 Kijeni do kwana ebe ijeni akiro kere, mam bobo ipuda ituŋanan aiŋit jo; kanuka ŋun kiyuunit ebe ibu kobu kama ejai Edeke.”" 
John16:31 Koboŋok Yesu kes ebe, “Aso iyuunito do kwana?" 
John16:32 Koany, ebunit esawa, eebo, adau adolun, naisiarakinotor ŋolituŋanan oreke, ka ajalakin eoŋ kasilikinit, Konye mam eoŋ kasilikini, naarai ejai Papa keoŋ." 
John16:33 Kalimokis yes akiro ŋun tetere ijaunete kainapakin tomakaŋ, Toma akwapin ejaas yes ican; konye kotitiŋikis, epiko eoŋ akwapin.”" 
John17:1 Kinera Yesu ŋun; kikeu akekonye akuj, kobala ebe, “Papa, adol esawa; kitopolo Okokukon, tetere Okokukon da kitopoloori jo." 
John17:2 Kwape ibu koinakinia apedor kama kaluejaas awat kere, tetere einakini kere lukiinakini ŋes aijar namam edaun." 
John17:3 Aijar namam edaun ŋes na ebe, kojenutu jo Edeke ediopet lokabeit, ka Yesu Kristo Iokijukuni." 
John17:4 Ketopolo eoŋ jo kakwap, naarai etodolik aswam naibu koinak eoŋ aswam." 
John17:5 Kwana da, wu Papa, kitopolooroi eoŋ kamakon kaibuses nakijaar eoŋ kajo eroko akwapin ejauna." 
John17:6 “Etodia ekonikiror mama ejaas ituŋa lukiinakinit kakwapin; araas lukon kosodi ainakin eoŋ: aricata da akonikirot. 
John17:7 Kwana ejenete ebe kere lukiinak apote kamakon: 
John17:8 naarai akiro nukiinakinit eoŋ ainak kes; acamut, ajenut da abeit ebe abu kalom kamakon, eyuut ebe ijo kijukuni eoŋ." 
John17:9 Elipakini eoŋ ŋul: mam elipakini akwapin, konye ŋul lukiinak; naarai eraas lukon." 
John17:10 Ŋul da kere lueraas lukaŋ eraas lukon, lueraas lukon da lukaŋ; ketopolooritai eoŋ tomakec." 
John17:11 Mam eoŋ aroko bobo ajai toma akwapin, konye lu ejaas toma akwapin, abuni eoŋ mamakon. Papa Lokalaunan, kidar kotoma okirorikon lukiinakinit eoŋ, tetere eraunete ipe, kwape kiraar oni ipe." 
John17:12 Naariŋar ajai kakes, abu kedar kes kotoma okirorikon lokiinakinit; kegalikinite kes, kwabo emamei ediopet kakesi loeoliorit dimarai okoku loka aolior; tetere edoli nakiwadikatai." 
John17:13 Konye kwana abuni mamakon; enera akiro nu toma akwapin, tetere ejaunete kaiyalamaka naedolit kotomakec." 
John17:14 Ainak eoŋ kes akonikirot; alaata akwapin kes naarai mam eraas luka akwapin, kwape mam eoŋ araar loka akwapin." 
John17:15 Mam eoŋ elipi ebe kolema kes kakwapin, konye kidar kes kama ejai lokaronon," 
John17:16 Mam kes eraas luka akwapin, kwape mam eoŋ araar loka akwapin," 
John17:17 Kitalau kes kotoma abeit; akonikirot ŋes abeit. 
John17:18 Kwape ibu kijukunia eoŋ toma akwapin, ejuka eoŋ da kes kwape kwaŋin." 
John17:19 Etalauna kanukec, tetere italaunio kes da kotoma abeit." 
John17:20 “Mam elipakini lu bon, konye ŋul da lukeyuunete kanuka akecekirot;" 
John17:21 tetere eraunete kere ipe; kwape ijo Papa ijaar tomakaŋ, eoŋ da tomakon, ŋul da kojaut tomawok: tetere iyuunete akwapin ebe ijo ŋes kijukunit," 
John17:22 Eoŋ da ainak kes aibuses nakiinakinit eoŋ; tetere eraunete ipe, kwape kiraar oni ipe:" 
John17:23 eoŋ tomakec, ijo da tomakaŋ, tetere edolete aitekoro naka eipeone; tetere ejenunete akwapin ebe ijo ŋes kijukunit, komina kes kwape ibu kominar eoŋ." 
John17:24 Papa, akoto kes lukiinakinit ajaut nenipe keoŋ kere neajai; koanyutu akaibuses nakiinakinit; naarai ibu komina eoŋ eriŋa epesikina apetetait naka akwapin." 
John17:25 Wu Papa Ekadoliton, mam akwapin kijenete, konye kajeni jo; ejenete lu ebe ijo ŋes kijukunit." 
John17:26 Etejenu eoŋ kes ekonikiror, ido etejenuni, tetere amina nakiminar eoŋ ejaun tomakec, eoŋ da tomakec.”" 
John18:1 Nakedaunia Yesu einer akiro ŋun, koloma nepepe kikekesisiak kodoka aguurut Kidiron, nekejai emanikor, koloma ŋesi ka ikekesisiak." 
John18:2 Kejeni Yuda da loakoto abilakin ŋes ebotet aibois ŋin; naarai kelosenenei Yesu ŋina irwan ipu nenipe kikekesisiak. 
John18:3 Kosodi kedau Yuda ainakinio erioŋet loka iserikalei, ka ikejaanakinak kama kisasedotin lupeti ka Iparisayon, kolot ŋina katalai ka akalasia ka lujiis," 
John18:4 Kosodi Yesu, kojeni kere nuedoikinete, kolom kotema kes atiar, “Iŋai bo imootos?”" 
John18:5 Koboŋokis ebe, “Yesu loko Nasaret.” Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Eoŋ lo.” Kebwoi Yuda da lokebilakini ŋes ebotet nenipe kakes." 
John18:6 Nakelimokinia kes ebe, “Eoŋ lo,” koboŋosi kau, kibirokinos kwap." 
John18:7 Kosodi kiŋit bobo ebe, “Iŋai bo imootos?” Kotemasi atiar, “Yesu loko Nasaret.”" 
John18:8 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Kadau alimokin yes ebe eoŋ lo: aso arai kimootos eoŋ, kinyeis lu koloto.”" 
John18:9 Tetere edoli akirot naenerit ebe, “Lukiinakinit eoŋ mam etooliorit ediopet.”" 
John18:10 Kosodi Simon Petero, kejai ekileŋ, kout kinom ebulesit loka losasedoti lopeti, kotub akekit nakoteten. Kerai ekiror loka ebulesit Malako." 
John18:11 Kotema Yesu Petero atiar, “Kinyakak ekileŋikon akuraruke; mam kereka eoŋ amasi akoli nakainakinit Papa?”" 
John18:12 Kosodete iserikalei ka ekapolokiton ka ikejaanakinak luka Iyudayan kikamut Yesu, koena," 
John18:13 Koyaŋaasi ber mama ejai Anas; naarai kerai ekamuran loka Kaiapa lokerai esasedoti lopeti okaru ŋol. 
John18:14 Kaiapa ŋol lokeinakin Iyudayan aomisioit ebe ejok etuŋanan ediopet atwanikin ituŋa," 
John18:15 Kotupa Simon Petero Yesu, ka ekesisian ece da. Kejenikina ekesisian ŋol kama ka losasedoti lopeti, koloma ŋesi nepepe ka Yesu alaro naka losasedoti lopeti;" 
John18:16 konye kobwoi Petero korute kokiŋa. Kosodi kolom ekesisian ece lokejenikina kama ka losasedoti lopeti, kinerata ka akagolon, kitolom Petero." 
John18:17 Kosodi kotema apese nakagolon Petero atiar, “Irai kereka ijo da ediopet kokesisiak luka etuŋanan kaŋol?” Konye ŋes kobala ebe, “Mere eoŋ.”" 
John18:18 Kebwoete ibulesin ka ikejaanakinak inokokinito akim naka atotol; naarai kededen aaterot; ipierete akim; kejai Petero da nenipe kakes ebwoi ipieri. 
John18:19 Kiŋit losasedoti lopeti Yesu nuka ikekesisiak ka nuka akeisisianakin da. 
John18:20 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Enerit eoŋ kakwapin kaitebeikin; esisianakinenei apaarasia kere katukosia ka oyekalu da, neatukonokinos Iyudayan kere; kwabo mam eoŋ enerit akirot kere kaiyeiyea." 
John18:21 Kanukinyo kiŋisitor eoŋ? Kiŋit lukeirarito anyoika nukalimokinit kes; koany, ejenete ŋul nuenerit eoŋ.”" 
John18:22 Nakedaunia einer ŋun, abu ekejaanakinan lokebwoi aapu kaŋes kibapa Yesu, kobala ebe, “Iboŋokini kwaŋin esasedoti lopeti?”" 
John18:23 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Arai enerit nukaronok kitejen nukaronok; konye arai enerit nuejok, kanukinyo kibapia?”" 
John18:24 Kosodi kijuka Anas ŋes eenitai mama ejai Kaiapa losasedoti lopeti. 
John18:25 Kebwoi Simon Petero ipieri akim. Kosodete kobalas ŋes ebe, “Irai kereka ijo da ediopet kokesisiakake?” Koŋer kobala ebe, “Mere eoŋ.”" 
John18:26 Kobala ediopet kobulesin luka losasedoti lopeti, lokerai lokajen naka je loketubi Petero akekit ebe, “Mam kereka kaanyunit jo komanikor nepepe kaŋesi”" 
John18:27 Kosodi koŋer bobo Petero: atipet koruik ekokor. 
John18:28 Kosodete koyaŋaasi Yesu anyoun kama ka Kaiapa kiton ore loka ekayaiton: kerai napetupuruc sek: konye mam kes elomara toma ore loka ekayaiton, kinyeis amunaar, konye kopedosi ainyam lukaleleŋ," 
John18:29 Kosodi kolom Pilato kiŋa mamakec, kobala ebe, “Nunyoika iwosatere etuŋanan lo?”" 
John18:30 Koboŋokis kotemasi atiar, “Arai mam etuŋanan lo iswamat nueroko, timam kiyau mamakon.”" 
John18:31 Kotema Pilato kes atiar, “Aso koyaŋaasi yesi, kotubokis kokisilikus.” Kotemasi Iyudayan ŋes atiar, “Emamei sio apedor aiar ituŋanan.”" 
John18:32 Tetere edoli akirot naka Yesu nakinerit, itodikini atwanare naekoto atwanare." 
John18:33 Kosodi koloma Pilato bobo toma ore loka ekayaiton, konyarau Yesu, kotema ŋes atiar, “Irai kereka ijo Ekabaka loka Iyudayan?”" 
John18:34 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Inera kereka ijo nu kanukon bon, arai bo kilimokis ituŋa ice nukaŋ?”" 
John18:35 Koboŋok Pilato ebe, “Arai tope eoŋ Eyudayat? Akoniteker ka isasedotin lupeti kes kijaikinete mamakaŋ, Iswamat anyoika?”" 
John18:36 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Akajakanut mere naka akwapin kanu: arai kerai akajakanut naka akwapin kanu, tikejioto ikakejaanakinak, kenyek aijaikin mama ejaas Iyudayan; konye akaiakanut mere naka ne.”" 
John18:37 Kotema Pilato ŋes atiar, “Irai kereka ijo ekabaka?” Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Ijo ibala ebe arai eoŋ ekabaka. Kauritai eoŋ kanuka ŋun, kanuka ŋun da abu kabu akwapin, tetere etejenuni abeit. Yenerai yenikabeit iirari ekaporoto.”" 
John18:38 Kotema Pilato atiar, “Inyo bo abeit?” Kedau einer ŋun, koloma bobo mama ejaas Iyudayan, kotema kes atiar, “Mam eoŋ aanyunit adioronis kamakeŋ."
