John18:39 Konye ejai yes epone, eoŋ aosikin yes ediopet apak naka Aleleŋ: aso ikotosi kereka kaosikis Ekabaka loka Iyudayan?”" 
John18:40 Kiworoto bobo ebe, “Mere lo, dimarai Baraba.” Kerai Baraba ŋol ekaŋatan." 
John19:1 Kosodi Pilato koyaŋa Yesu, koda ŋes." 
John19:2 Kojeata iserikalei aboko naka ikukwa, kitanapikis akouke, kitanapata da anapito naamuge;" 
John19:3 koponenenete mama ejai, kobalas ebe, “Yoga, Ekabaka loka Iyudayan!” Kibapanasi ŋes." 
John19:4 Kosodi kolom bobo Pilato kiŋa, kotema kes atiar, “Koany ayaŋauni ŋes kiŋa mama ijaas, tetere ijenunete ebe mam eoŋ aanyunit adioronis kamakeŋ.”" 
John19:5 Kolom do Yesu, enapit aboko naka ikukwa ka anapito naamuge, Kotema Pilato kes atiar, “Koany etuŋanan!”" 
John19:6 Kosodete keanyutu isasedotin lupeti ka ikapolokitok, kiworoto ebe, “Kibubuk, kibubuk ba!” Kotema Pilato kes atiar, “Koyaŋaasi yesi, kibubukis, naarai mam eoŋ aanyunit adioronis kamakeŋ.”" 
John19:7 Koboŋokis Iyudayan ebe, “Ejai sio ekisil, ido kanuka ekisil kaŋol ibusakinit ŋes atwanare, naarai abu kitarauna bon Okoku loka Edeke.”" 
John19:8 Kosodi nakiiraria Pilato akirot ŋin, kiyatak akurianar;" 
John19:9 koloma bobo oPuraitorion kotema Yesu atiar, “Laali bo kibunio?” Konye mam Yesu eboŋokino." 
John19:10 Kanuka ŋun kotema Pilato ŋes atiar, “Mam inera keoŋ? Mam ijeni ebe ejai eoŋ apedor aosikin jo, ejai da apedor aibubukin?”" 
John19:11 Koboŋok Yesu ebe, “Ti mam jo ijaas kapedor kere mamakaŋ, arai mam kidumunit abunore kokuju; kanuka ŋun ŋol lokejaikini eoŋ akaninikon ŋes erono adepar.”" 
John19:12 Ageun kapak kaŋin komoote Pilato aosikin ŋes, konye kiworoto Iyudayan ebe, “Arai kiwosik lo, mam irai epapero loka Kaisar; ŋolituŋanan loedakakini bon araun ekabaka itokokoli Kaisar.”" 
John19:13 Nakiiraria Pilato akiro ŋun, kitolom Yesu kiŋa, kiboikin oicoloŋ loka aitub, aibois naenyaritai Amor Nuepesitai, konye kAburanian enyaritai Gabata." 
John19:14 Kerai da apaaran naka Aitemokin Aleleŋ; kerai bala esawa lokikanyetekape. Kotema Pilato Iyudayan atiar, “Koany, Ekabakakus!”" 
John19:15 Kanuka ŋun kiworoto ŋul ebe, “Kolema, kolema, kibubuk!” Pilato kotema kes atiar, “Ebubukini kereka Ekabakakus?” Koboŋokis isasedotin lupeti ebe, “Emamei sio ekabaka ece dimarai Kaisar.”" 
John19:16 Kosodi kijaik ŋes akaninikec aibubukinio. 
John19:17 Koyata Yesu, koloma, erioŋit ekemusalaba kiton aibois naenyaritai Abelekek naka Akou, kAburanian ebe Gologota." 
John19:18 Kibubukis nen, ka ice iarei nenipe kaŋes, ediopet epuai ka ece da epuai, ka Yesu kidiŋikec." 
John19:19 Kiwadik Pilato aitejenunet, kikajak omusalaba; ewadikatai ebe, “YESU LOKO NASARET, EKABAKA LOKA IYUDAYAN.”" 
John19:20 Kosioma luipu koYudayan aitejenunet ŋin, naarai keapie aibois nakibubukinitoi Yesu kore; kiwadikatai kAburanian, ka Aromayon, ka Ayonanin da." 
John19:21 Kosodete isasedotin lupeti luka Iyudayan kotemasi Pilato atiar, “Sirikiwadika ebe, ‘Ekabaka loka lyudayan’, dimarai ebe, ‘Abala ŋesi ebe Eoŋ ekabaka loka Iyudayan.’”" 
John19:22 Koboŋok Pilato ebe, “Nuewadik, ewadik.”" 
John19:23 Nakedauniata iserikalei aibubukin Yesu, koyaŋaasi akenapito kokora katutubeta aoŋon, ŋoliserikalet nakeŋ, ka ekaso da. Konye ekasoke kemamei airiamasit, naarai kejeitai ameun kokuju kiton kwap;" 
John19:24 Kotemanaros bonik atiar, “Sirikiicil, konye kelamilamakisi eroet aanyun iŋai ebeikini.” Tetere edolete nukiwadikatai ebe, “Akorokorata anapitoka, Kilamilamata kanuka ekasoka.” Kiswamata iserikalei kwaŋin." 
John19:25 Konye kobwoete totoke ka inaci naka totoke, ŋes Mariam aberu naka Kelopa, ka Mariam Magadalene, eapiete kemusalaba loka Yesu." 
John19:26 Kosodi keanyu Yesu totoke, ka ekesisian lokemina ebwoi kodie, kotema totoke atiar, “Toto, koany okokukon!”" 
John19:27 Kosodi kotema ŋesi ekesisian atiar, “Koany totokon!” Ameun kosawa kaŋol koyaŋa ekesisian ŋin oreke." 
John19:28 Kokau kaŋun, kojeni Yesu ebe aŋetakinos kere, tetere itodolikini nakiwadikatai kobala ebe, “Kajak akur.”" 
John19:29 Kejai nen amot naeleleba ebino loedwar; kibwaikis acago naileleba ebino ŋol loedwar kuju akwara, kikiasi kiton aitukuke." 
John19:30 Kedau Yesu aijaikinio ebino loedwar, kobala ebe, “Aŋetakinos.” Kitulur akekou, kijaik ekemoyo." 
John19:31 Aso naarai kerai apaaran naka Aitemonokin, kinyeis awat asalakin omusalaba apaaran nakasabato (naarai kerai nakasabato ŋin apaaran nakapolon), ŋes kilipiata Iyudayan Pilato akejekec abilio, tetere elemunio." 
John19:32 Kopotu do iserikalei kobilata akeje nuka losodit, ka nuka lokiareit lokibubukinitoi nenipe kaŋes;" 
John19:33 konye kedolokis Yesu koanyut ebe kedau nan atwanare, mam ebila akejeke," 
John19:34 Konye ediopet koserikalei kicum amaranake kakwara, atipet kolomutu aokot ka akipi." 
John19:35 Ŋol da lokeanyuni iteienunit, ido akeitejenunet erai nakabeit, ŋes da ejeni ebe inera abeit, tetere yes da iyuunete." 
John19:36 Naarai kedoikinete ŋun tetere edoli nakiwadikatai ebe, “Mam ebilio akekoit.”" 
John19:37 Ka nakiwadikatai ace da ebala ebe, “Esesenete moolo ŋol lokicumete.”" 
John19:38 Kokau kaŋun abu Yosep loka Arimataya lokerai ekesisian loka Yesu, konye kaiyeiyea kanuka akurian Iyudayan, kilip Pilato apedor alemar akuan naka Yesu: kisiik Pilato. Kosodi kolot, kolema akuanake." 
John19:39 Kolot Nikodemo da, lokelosit ber mama ejai ŋesi kuare, koyaŋa lukesaete ka icicikwa luinyalal, bala alaŋir naka ilatirin akwatat." 
John19:40 Kosodete kolemut akuan naka Yesu, konunukikis ogoen luka ebaputa nepepe kalukesai, kwape ejaar epone loka Iyudayan loka aida." 
John19:41 Nepenen nekibubukinitoi kejai emanikor; ido toma omanikor kejai ates nakitetet namam lem kibwaikinitai idiotuŋanan. 
John19:42 Kosodi kanuka Aitemonokin naka Iyudayan, kibwaikis Yesu nen, naarai aapie ates." 
John20:1 Apaaran nasodit nakasabato kodil Mariam Magadalene alosit ates, eroko emutono akwap, koany amoru ikokororitai awai kates." 
John20:2 Koker, kolot mama ejai Simon Petero ka ekesisian ŋol lokemina Yesu, kolimok kes ebe, “Kelemar Ejakait kates, mam kijeni neibwaikinitai.”" 
John20:3 Kosodi konyou Petero ka ekesisian ece, koloto ates," 
John20:4 Kokerata kere iarei, konye kilany ekesisian ŋol Petero, koliŋ adolore ates;" 
John20:5 kokukum, kireik toma, koany igoen lukebaputa ejaas nen, konye mam abu koloma." 
John20:6 Kosodi kodolu Simon Petero da, etupakinit ŋes, koloma toma ates; koany igoen lukebaputa ejaas nen," 
John20:7 ka eitabala, lokejai akouke, mam kejaas kigoen lukebaputa konye kenunukitoi kaiboisike bon." 
John20:8 Kosodi koloma da ekesisian ece, lokeliŋi adolore ates, koany ŋesi kiyuu da;" 
John20:9 naarai mam ber kes aienunito nakiwadikatai ebe ibusakinit ŋes ajarun," 
John20:10 Kosodete koboŋosi bobo ikesisiak oreriakec. 
John20:11 Konye kebwoi Mariam kokiŋa eapie kates emonyi, napemonyi kokukum kireik toma ates;" 
John20:12 koany imalaikan iarei lukenapito luakwaŋak, iboiete, ediopet kakou, ediopet da kakejen kanekiperikinitoi akuan naka Yesu." 
John20:13 Kes da kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Imonyi inyo, toto?” Kotema kes atiar, “Naarai kelemar Ekajakait, mam ajeni neibwaikinitai.”" 
John20:14 Kedau einer ŋun kibelokin kau koany Yesu ebwoi, komam ejeni ebe ŋes Yesu," 
John20:15 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Imonyi inyo, toto? Imoi iŋai?” Konye ŋin koomite ŋes araut ekeswaman emanikor, kotema atiar, “Ejakait, arai ilemarit ijo ŋes, kolimokinai neibwaikinit, eoŋ da ayaŋaari.”" 
John20:16 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Mariam,” Kibelokin ŋesi kotema kAburanian atiar, “Raboni!” (Ŋes atemar ebe, “Ekesisianakinan,”)" 
John20:17 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Sirikitiŋ eoŋ, naarai eriŋa edokara mama ejai Papa; konye kolot mama ejaas ikainacan kolimok kes ebe, Adokari alosit mama ejai Papaka, ŋes Papakus da, mama ejai Ekadeke, ŋes Ekusideke da.”" 
John20:18 Kolot Mariam Magadalene kolimok ikesisiak ebe, “Aanyu eoŋ Ejakait.” Kolimok da kes nuabu kinera kaŋes." 
John20:19 Kosodi kikamus apaaran ŋin nasodit naka asabato, kegolol ikekia kaneajaas ikesisiak kanuka akurian Iyudayan, kobu Yesu kobwo kokidiŋikec, kotema kes atiar, “Kinapakinos,”" 
John20:20 Kedau einer ŋun, kitodik kes akekanin ka akemarana. Kosodete kiyalamikinos ikesisiak nakeanyuniata Ejakait," 
John20:21 Kotema Yesu kes bobo atiar, “Kinapakinos. Kwape keyakuunia Papa, eoŋ da keyakiari yes kwape kwaŋin.”" 
John20:22 Kosodi kedau einer ŋun, kiyeŋak kes, kotema atiar, “Kijautu Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
John20:23 Arai isioniete adiakanareta nuka ituŋanan kere, isionio; arai da ienete adiakanareta nuka ituŋanan kere, eenio.”" 
John20:24 Konye ediopet ka lutomon kaarei, ŋes Tomas lokenyaritai Didumo mam kejaas kakes nakebunio Yesu." 
John20:25 Aso kolimokis ikesisiak ice ŋes ebe, “Kianyu Ejakait.” Konye kotema atiar, “Arai mam eoŋ aanyunit apoorei nuka aseito kakaninike, ka aibwaikin da ikabokor apedon nuka aseito, ka aibwaikin akakan toma amaranake, mam eoŋ eyuuni nepetai da.”" 
John20:26 Ketuboros apaarasia akanykauni kojaas bobo ikekesisiak togo, kojai Tomas da nepepe kakes. Kegolol ikekia konye kobu Yesu kobwo kokidiŋikec, kotema atiar, “Kinapakinos,”" 
John20:27 Kosodi kotema ŋesi Tomas atiar, “Koyau ne ekonibokorit, koany akakanin; koyau da akonikan, kibwaik toma amaranaka; kwabo sirikiraun lomam iyuunit, dimarai loiyuunit.”" 
John20:28 Koboŋok Tomas ebe, “Ekajakait, Ekadeke da!”" 
John20:29 Yesu kotema ŋes atiar, “Naarai kiany eoŋ ŋes konyet iyuunia? Isirereŋitoi luiyuunete komam eanyunito.”" 
John20:30 Kiswama Yesu aanyuneta ace nuipu kakonyen nuka ikesisiak, numam iwadikatai oitabo lo;" 
John20:31 konye iwadikatai nu tetere iyuunete yesi ebe Yesu ŋes Kristo, Okoku loka Edeke, ido kanuka aiyuun ŋin kojaut kaijar kokirorikeŋ." 
John21:1 Akaulo kaŋun kitakanikin bobo Yesu ikesisiak kaŋolol naka Tiberia; kitakanikin kwanata: 
John21:2 kejaas nepepe Simon Petero, ka Tomas loenyaritai Didumo, ka Natanael, loko Kana loko Galilaya, ka odwe luka Sebedayo, ka ice iarei kokesisiakake." 
John21:3 Kotema Simon Petero kes atiar, “Alosi ailok.” Kotemasi atiar, “Isio da kiupari kajo.” Kolomasi, kodokasi ataker; konye kakuar kaŋin mam ikamuna ibore." 
John21:4 Napiwalari akwap kobwo Yesu koitolima; konye mam ikesisiak ajenete ebe erai ŋesi Yesu. 
John21:5 Kosodi kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Idwe, ejaas yes idinyaman?” Koboŋokis ebe, “Mam.”" 
John21:6 Kotema kes atiar, “Kocakakisi eboi kowai lokoteten loka ataker, idumunete yesi.” Kosodete kocakakis, kwana do mam epedorete airiun kanuka aipues naka lukecor." 
John21:7 Kosodi ekesisian lokemina Yesu kotema Petero atiar, “Ŋes Ejakait.” Nakiiraria Simon Petero ebe ŋes Ejakait, konap akenapito (naarai kimujalal), kibirokin aŋolol," 
John21:8 Konye kopotu ikesisiak ice kotoma ataker, iriitos eboi ileleba lukecor, naarai mam kelwanikina kaneeonit, konye bala iyadin akwatat." 
John21:9 Kosodi nakedokuniata oitolima koanyut kanen akim naka atotol, ibwaikinitai yenikecor ka emugati da." 
John21:10 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Koyaut lukecor ice luikamunito.”" 
John21:11 Kosodi kodoka Simon Petero ataker kiriu eboi oitolima, ileleba lukecor luepolok, akwatat ka akaisakany ka luuni: karaida kipu kwaŋin, mam eboi eŋeda," 
John21:12 Kotema Yesu kes atiar, “Kopotu konyama.” Kwabo emamei ediopet kokesisiak loketitiŋikini aiŋit ŋes ebe, “Iŋai bo ijo?” Kojenut ebe kerai Ejakait." 
John21:13 Kobu Yesu, kolem emugati koinak kes, ka yenikecor da kwape kwaŋin." 
John21:14 Ŋin ŋes irwan nakiwuniet nakitakanikinor Yesu ikekesisiak kedau ajarun kokatwak. 
John21:15 Nakedauniata ainyam, kotema Yesu Simon Petero atiar, “Simon, okoku loka Yona, kimina eoŋ aitelekarit lu?” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Eebo, Ejakait, ijo ijeni ebe kamina.” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Kitadakenenei idwe luka amerekekinika.”" 
John21:16 Kolimok bobo nakiareit ebe, “Simon, okoku loka Yona, kimina eoŋ?” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Eebo, Ejakait, ijo ijeni ebe kamina,” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Kipisenenei akamerekekin.”" 
John21:17 Kolimok irwan nakiwuniet ebe, “Simon okoku loka Yona, kimina eoŋ?” Kokadak Petero naarai abu kolimok irwan nakiwuniet ebe, “Kimina eoŋ?” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Ejakait, ijeni akiro kere; ijeni kamina.” Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Kitadakenenei akamerekekin." 
John21:18 Abeit, abeit, katemari jo atiar, Nairaar kolo ikatumunan ikapakini bon, ilosi neikoto: konye naimojoŋia iriori akonikanin, kisikapi ece, kiyaŋaari nemam ikoto.”" 
John21:19 Kinera ŋun itodikini atwanare naetopolooria Edeke. Nakedaunia einer ŋun, kotema atiar, “Kotupunai.”" 
John21:20 Kibelokin Petero, koany ekesisian lokemina Yesu etupit, ŋes ŋol lokegoŋakina katorob naka Yesu kapak kaya naka inyamat lukatiboŋ, loabala ebe, “Ejakait, iŋai bo kibilakini ebotet?”" 
John21:21 Aso keanyu Petero ŋol, kotema ŋesi Yesu atiar, “Ejakait, ido bo lo ikwaikinio ai?”" 
John21:22 Kotema Yesu ŋes atiar, “Arai akoto ŋol aidarit aitodol neabunio, ipodo bo ijo inyo? Kotupunai ijo eoŋ.”" 
John21:23 Kisiarakin akirot ŋin oinacan, ebe mam ekesisian ŋol etwani, konye mam kebala Yesu ebe mam etwani; konye ebe, “Arai akoto ŋol aidarit aitodol neabunio, ipodo bo ijo inyo?”" 
John21:24 Ŋol ŋes ekesisian ŋol loitejenuni akiro ŋun, loewadikai ŋun; kijeni oni ebe akeitejenun erai nakabeit." 
John21:25 Ejaas da akiro ace nuipu nueswamat Yesu, arai kiwadikatai ŋinidiopet, aomit ti mam akwapin ilosikinos iitabon lutikiwadikai." 
Acts1:1 Abu kewadik eitabo losodit, wu Teopilo, kotoma akiro kere nukegeuni Yesu aswam ka aisisianakin da," 
Acts1:2 kiton apaaran naayaŋarere ŋes toma akuj, naadaunitor aicorakin ikiyakia luaseunit kanuka Emoyo Lokalaunan," 
Acts1:3 Nakedaunia aiticanio kitodikin kes ejari kanuka nuitogogoŋete nuipu, kitakananakin kes apak naka apaarasia akaisaoŋon, ka ainerenen akiro nuebeito ajakanut naka Edeke." 
Acts1:4 Nakiriamunotor kakes kicorak kinyeis anyoun koYerusalem, konye kidarata aisumunet naka Papa. Kobala ebe, “Ipotu kiirasi ŋun kamakaŋ;" 
Acts1:5 naarai abu Yokana kibatis kakip, konye yes kibatisao kEmoyo Lokalaunan eriŋa etuboro apaarasia nuipu.”" 
Acts1:6 Kosodi naketukokinotor, kiŋita ŋes ebe, “Ejakait, apak na ŋes kereka nainyakakinia Isirael ajakanut?”" 
Acts1:7 Kotema kes atiar, “Mere nakus ajenun apakio karaida ikar luabu Papa kitemok kapedorike." 
Acts1:8 Konye idumunete agogoŋ kedau Emoyo Lokalaunan adoikin yes; iraunete yesi ikakajenak kotoma Yerusalem, ka Yudaya kere, ka Samaria, kiton osaŋe da loka akwap.”" 
Acts1:9 Kedau einer ŋun, naperoko esesenete, kodakarai, kiteribo edou kakonyenekec," 
Acts1:10 Napesesenete noi akuj naalosio ŋesi, koany kobwaata ikiliok iarei aapu kakes enapito lukakwaŋak," 
Acts1:11 kobalas ebe, “Yes ikiliok luko Galilaya, kanukinyo ibwoiata kosesenete akuj? Yesu ŋol, loayaŋaar kamakus alosit toma akuj, eboŋuni kopone kaŋope kaŋol loianyuniata ŋes elosi toma akuj.”" 
Acts1:12 Kosodete koboŋosi Yerusalem anyoun komoru loenyaritai loka Iseitunin, loeapias ka Yerusalem, alosit bala naka apaaran nakasabato." 
Acts1:13 Nakelomariata kodokasi agola nakokuju, nakiboienenoto; Petero ka Yokana, ka Yakob, ka Anderea, Pilip ka Tomas, Batolomayo ka Matayo, Yakob okoku loka Alipayo, ka Simon Selot, ka Yuda okoku loka Yakob." 
Acts1:14 Ŋul kere kinyikokinito ailip ketau ediopet, nepepe kaŋor ka Mariam toto naka Yesu, ka ikeinacan." 
Acts1:15 Kapaarasia kaŋun kobwo Petero kokidiŋ kiinacan, (etiai loka ekodet kerai bala akwatat ka akaisaarei) kobala ebe," 
Acts1:16 “Iinacan, ibusakinit kodolo nakiwadikatai, nakinerit kolo Emoyo Lokalaunan kaituk naka Daudi, nuka Yuda lokiŋarenikinit ŋul lukikamunete Yesu." 
Acts1:17 Naarai kimaritai nepepe kaoni, kodum ekewai kotoma aijaanakin kana." 
Acts1:18 (Naarai kogwelia etuŋanan ŋol amana keropit loka aronisike; kibiror keŋeso kocila, kolomut amoetenake kere." 
Acts1:19 Kojenunos kotuŋa kere luibojete koYerusalem, konyarai amana ŋin kaŋajepakec Akeledama, apolouke ebe Amana naka Aokot.)" 
Acts1:20 Naarai iwadikatai kotoma oitabo loka Isabulin ebe, ‘Kosilior ekere, Komamuun ituŋanan yeniboie kanen.’ Bobo da ebe, ‘Kirum ece akepolou,’" 
Acts1:21 Aso kotoma otuŋa luaupenenas kaoni kapakio kere nukelomanaria Ejakait Yesu kolomununei da mamawok," 
Acts1:22 ameun kaibatis naka Yokana, kiton apaaran naayaŋarere kamawok alosit toma akuj, ibusakinit ediopet kakesi araun ekajenan loka ajarunike nepepe kaoni.”" 
Acts1:23 Koseut iarei, Yosep loenyaritai Barasaba, lokerai ekekiror Yusito, ka Matiya." 
Acts1:24 Kilipa, kotemasi atiar, “Ijo Ejakait loijeni itauon luka ituŋa kere, kitodikinai loiseunit ijo kotoma kalu luarei," 
Acts1:25 kirum aibois kotoma aijaanakin kana ka aiyakianut na, naebuci Yuda kolot akeibois elopet.”" 
Acts1:26 Kilamilamata eroet, kobeik eroet Matiya; kimarakinai nepepe kikiyakia itomon kalodiopet." 
Acts2:1 Nakedolio apaaran naka Pentekosit, kejaas kere nepepe aibois adiopet," 
Acts2:2 Koŋesun airuruma kokuju bala airuruma naka ekwam loekusi ka gogoŋ, kilelebun etogo kere lokiboioto." 
Acts2:3 Kotakanut aŋajepa nuketiakatiaka bala nuka akim; kodoik ŋinidiopet kakesi. 
Acts2:4 Kilelebai kere Emoyo Lokalaunan, kogeut einer aŋajepa ace, kwape keinakinia Emoyo kes einer." 
Acts2:5 Kejaas Iyudayan lukiboiete koYerusalem, ituŋa luiyapaarito lukepote kaŋiniteker nakokwap kakui." 
Acts2:6 Kosodi nakiirarere airuruma ŋin, kotukokinos ikodeta, kitirirata, naarai abu ŋinituŋanan kiira kes inerasi aŋajepeke." 
Acts2:7 Koumokis kere noi noi, kobalas ebe, “Koany, mam kereka lu kere luinerasi eraas Igalilayan?" 
Acts2:8 Inyo bo ainaki oni aiirar, ŋinituŋanan aŋajepewok nakiwuriere?" 
Acts2:9 Iparatian, ka Imedin, ka Iyelamin, ka luibolete koMesopotamia, ko Yudaya da, ka Kapadokia, koPonto ka Asia," 
Acts2:10 ko Purugia, ka Pampulia, ko Misiri ka atutubeta nuka Libua aapu ka Kurene, ka ice lukepote ko Rome, Iyudayan ka ikebelokinok," 
Acts2:11 Ikuretan, ka Iyarabun, kiira kes inerasi aŋajepawok aswamisio nuepolok nuka Edeke.”" 
Acts2:12 Koumokis kere, kobuonokinos, kotemanaros atiar, “Inyo bo apolou kanu?”" 
Acts2:13 Konye kokienatar ice kobalas ebe, “Emeras ajon nuwinyiwiny,”" 
Acts2:14 Konye kobwo Petero nepepe ka lutomon ka lodiopet, kikeseu ekeporoto kolimok kes ebe, “Yes ikiliok luko Yudaya, ka yes da kere luibojete koYerusalem, kojenut akirot na, kopuputu akakiro." 
Acts2:15 Mam ituŋa lu Emerasi, kwape iwomitotor yesi, naarai eraas isawan iuni luka apaaran;" 
Acts2:16 konye erai na naenerit enabi Yoel ebe: 
Acts2:17 ‘Ebala Edeke ebe, Ejaun kapaarasia nukawasia, Abukokini awat kere Ekamoyo, Edwarete rwaru ikusidwe lusap ka lupesur, Eanyunete ikusikatumunak aitapoeta, Irujaete ikusimakio airujasia." 
Acts2:18 Eebo apaarasia ŋun abukokini ikabulesin ka akabulesin Ekamoyo, edwarete kesi." 
Acts2:19 Etodikini nukaumokin kokuju toma akuj, Ka aanyuneta kakwap kokwap, Aokot, ka akim, ka euria loka apuru;" 
Acts2:20 Ituluorio akoloŋ amuton, Elap da araun aokot, Eroko edoluno apaaran naka Ejakait, Nakapolon naejenikina," 
Acts2:21 Kosodi kanen, ŋin yeniwonei ekiror loka Ejakait itajario.’" 
Acts2:22 “Yes ikiliok luka Isirael, kopuputu akiro nu: Yesu loko Nasaret, ekiliokit lokitodiar Edeke mamakus kanuka aswamisio nukapedor, ka nukaumokin ka aanyuneta da nukiswamai Edeke kotomakeŋ kokidiŋikus, kwape ijeniata yesi ikulepek," 
Acts2:23 Yesu ŋol, lokijaikinio kanuka ainerun ka aijen naka Edeke ameun apeŋo, ipotu yesi kibubukis, koarata kakanin nuka ituŋa lukaronok." 
Acts2:24 Konye kitajaru ŋes Edeke, kolaca ariebo naka atwanare; naarai mam epedoro aikamunit ŋes," 
Acts2:25 Naarai inerit Daudi kanukeŋ ebe, ‘Abu kaanyununei Ejakait kakonyeneka, Naarai ejaenena akanika nakoteten, Kenyek airiaŋiriaŋa." 
Acts2:26 Ŋes iyalamikinor ekatau, elakanari da akaŋajep; Bobo da iboie akakuan kotoma amun." 
Acts2:27 Naarai mam jo inyeini ekatau kokatwak, Karaida aijaikin Lokalaunanikon aibos." 
Acts2:28 Kitejenik eoŋ irotin luka aijar; Kilelebikini eoŋ aiyalama kakonyenekon.’ 
Acts2:29 “Ikiliok iinacan, apedori atitiŋikin alimokin yes nuka papaawok Daudi ebe abu kotwana konukai, ejai da atesike mamawok kiton lolo." 
Acts2:30 Aso kanu keraar enabi, kojeni ebe iyapoikinit Edeke aiyaposit ebe, kotoma aurike edakakini ediopet oicoloŋoke," 
Acts2:31 abu ŋesi kogeik aanyun kinera da nuka ajarun naka Kristo ebe, mam aponi kinyeinai Okatwak, karaida akekuan aibos." 
Acts2:32 Yesu ŋol abu Edeke kitajaru, kirai isio kere ikajenakake." 
Acts2:33 Aso kedaun aitodokaar kiton akan nakoteten naka Edeke, ka ainakinio kama ejai Papa aisumunet naka Emoyo Lokalaunan, abuku lo loianyunete loipupete da." 
Acts2:34 Naarai mam Daudi abu kodoka toma akuj; konye ebala ŋesi elopet ebe, ‘Abu Ejakait kotema Ekajakait ebe, Kiboikin akanika nakoteten," 
Acts2:35 Aitodol naebwaikinia lukasurupokon kere Araut iicoloŋ yenika akejekon.’ 
Acts2:36 Aso kojen ekek kere loka Isirael kabeit ebe etarau Edeke ŋes Ejakait ka Kristo da, ŋes Yesu loipotu kibubukis.”" 
Acts2:37 Nakiirariata ŋun koditasi ikecetauon, kobalas Petero ka ikiyakia ice ebe, “Kekonakis ai, iinacan?”" 
Acts2:38 Kotema Petero atiar, “Kitoronikinos, kibatisaunos, ŋinituŋanan kayesi, kokiror loka Yesu Kristo, kanuka aisionio naka adiakanaretakus; kiinakinio ainakinet naka Emoyo Lokalaunan," 
Acts2:39 Naarai aisumunet erai kanukus ka ikusidwe da, ka ituŋa kere luelwaka, kere luenyarauni Ejakait Edekewok mamakeŋ.”" 
Acts2:40 Kitejenu kes kakiro ace nuipu ka aicor da ebe, “Kitajarunos katur kana namagul.”" 
Acts2:41 Aponi kibatisai ŋul lukecamunete akekirot, kiyatakinos ituŋa kapaaran kaŋin bala ilukumin iuni." 
Acts2:42 Kinyikokinito kaisisianakin naka ikiyakia, ka eidicane, ka aibil emugati, ka ailipasia da." 
Acts2:43 Kokurianari ŋinituŋanan; kitwasamai ikiyakia aswam nukaumokin nuipu ka aanyuneta da. 
Acts2:44 Kojaas luiyuunito kere nepepe, kimorikikina koboro kere;" 
Acts2:45 Kogwelanasi luebeito ka iborokec ka akoranakin ituŋa kere, kwape kipudar ŋinituŋanan." 
Acts2:46 Kinyikokinito ŋinipaaran ketau ediopet kotoma oyekalu, ebilete emugati kore, komorete kalakara ka etau loelai," 
Acts2:47 ituritos Edeke kitojokito ituŋa kere. Kiyatanakini Ejakait otiaikec ŋinipaaran lukitajario. 
Acts3:1 Kosodete edokarete Petero ka Yokana alosit oyekalu esawa loka ailip, ŋes lokikanyetekaoŋon." 
Acts3:2 Ido adakitai etuŋanan Ioeŋwalit ameun kaurioke, lokibwaanakinio ŋinipaaran orute loka eyakalu loenyaritai Lokajokan, tetere ilipitoi nukaitim kama ejaas ituŋa luelomanarete toma oyekalu," 
Acts3:3 Keanyu ŋol Petero ka Yokana elomarete oyekalu, kilip kes nukaitim." 
Acts3:4 Kosodi Petero kosesen ŋes nepepe ka Yokana, kotema atiar, “Kiteoi sio.”" 
Acts3:5 Koŋolia kes, komun adumun ibore kamakec." 
Acts3:6 Konye Petero kotema atiar, “Emamei eoŋ epuesa karaida esabu; konye yenikija keoŋ, kainakini ŋin, Kokiror loka Yesu Kristo loko Nasaret, kosakasak.”" 
Acts3:7 Kitiŋ akekan nakoteten, kitonyou ŋes: atipet kodomut akekeje ka ikekurunya agogoŋ." 
Acts3:8 Kodetu, kobwo, kogeu alosit; koloma oyekalu nepepe kakes, elosi, esomanari, iturit Edeke," 
Acts3:9 Koanyut ituŋa kere elosi iturit Edeke. 
Acts3:10 Kojenata ebe kerai ŋesi ŋopeŋol lokiboie ilipitoi nukaitim korute Lokajokan loka eyekalu: koumokis noi ŋin naedoikinit ŋes. 
Acts3:11 Naperiŋa ŋesi itiŋit Petero ka Yokana, kokerut ituŋa kere mama ejaas toma alomaret naenyaritai naka Solomon, eumokinitos noi." 
Acts3:12 Nakeanyunia Petero, Koboŋok ituŋa ebe, “Yes ikiliok luka Isirael, kanukinyo iwumokinitotor nu, kanukinyo da kiseseniata sio, bala Iem kitolosi ŋes kakosipedor arai bo kakosiyoŋit Edeke?" 
Acts3:13 Edeke loka Aburaam, ka loka Isaak, ka loka Yakob, Edeke loka lukapapaawok etopoloo Eketelepat Yesu; loipotu yesi kijaikis, ka aiŋer kakonyen nuka Pilato, nakekotor aosikin ŋes." 
Acts3:14 Konye yes ipotu koŋeroto Lokalaunan Lokadoliton, kilipa ainakinio ekaaran," 
Acts3:15 koarata Ekapolon loka aijar; lokitajaruni Edeke kotoma okatwak, Kirai isio ikekajenak." 
Acts3:16 Kanuka aiyuun ekekiror ainak ekekiror etuŋanan lo agogoŋ, loianyunete loijenete da; eebo, aiyuun ŋin naejai mamakeŋ ainak lo aŋaleu naeleleba kakonyenekus kere." 
Acts3:17 “Kwana da iinacan, ajeni ebe iswamato ŋun kanu mam ijeniata, kwape eswamaata ikayaitokokus da." 
Acts3:18 Konye akiro kwa nukelimonokini Edeke ameun apeŋo kaituk nuka inabin kere ebe ibusakinit Kristoke aiticanio, etodoliki kwaŋin," 
Acts3:19 Aso do kitoronikinos, kibelokinos, komwatarai akusidiakanareta, tetere edolete apakio nuka aisikwarunio nuepote kama ejai Ejakait," 
Acts3:20 Ido tetere ijukuni Kristo lokiseikinitai apeŋo, ŋes Yesu:" 
Acts3:21 loibusakinit akuj aisukunyikin aitodol apakio nuiteteunere akiro kere nukinerit Edeke kaituke nuka inabinoke lukalaunak ameun kageunet naka akwapin. 
Acts3:22 Naarai enerit teni Musa ebe, ‘Kitonyoikini yes Ejakait Edeke enabi kotoma oinacanakus loeputos keoŋ. Ŋol ŋes iirarete kotoma akiro kere nukilimokini yes." 
Acts3:23 Kosodi kanen, ŋinituŋanan yenimam iirari enabi ŋol emudiario kotuŋa.’" 
Acts3:24 Eebo, inabin kere ameun ka Samuel ka luketupakinete ŋes, kere lukineras, kelimonokinete nuka apaarasia kanu." 
Acts3:25 Iraas yesi idwe luka inabin ka aitutuket ŋin nakitutuki Edeke kalukapapaakus, elimokini Aburaam ebe, ‘Isirereŋio atekerin kere nuka akwapin kotoma aurikon.’" 
Acts3:26 Kedau Edeke aitaiarun eketelepat Yesu, kijuku ber mamakus, tetere kisirereni yes aibelokin ŋinidiopet kayesi kotoma nukaronokokus.”" 
Acts4:1 Napineras kituŋa, koponikis isasedotin ka ekapolokiton loka eyekalu ka Isadukayon," 
Acts4:2 ekadakinito noi naarai isisianakinete ituŋa, ka alimono kin ajarun naka Iukatwak kotoma Yesu." 
Acts4:3 Kikamut kogolokis aidaris kiton tupuruc: naarai kitiboŋit akwap," 
Acts4:4 Konye kiyuunito luipu luapotu kiirasi akirot; etiai da loka ikiliok kodol kwaka ilukumin ikany. 
Acts4:5 Kosodi kanen tupuruc, kotukonokinos ikayaitokokec ka imakio ka ikewadikak Yerusalem;" 
Acts4:6 ka Anas losasedoti lopeti, ka Kaiapa, ka Yokana, ka Alegesanda da, ka ŋul lukeraas luka ekek loka losasedoti lopeti." 
Acts4:7 Kedautu aisibwo kes kokidiŋ, kiŋita ebe, “Kanuka apedor anyoin, ka okiror enyoin, iswamaata yesi nu?”" 
Acts4:8 Kosodi Petero, kilelebun Emoyo Lokalaunan, kotema kes atiar, “Yes ikayaitok luka ituŋa, ka imakio," 
Acts4:9 arai kiiŋisi lolo akiro nukajokak nueswamakinio loŋwalas, epone lokitanaleunere," 
Acts4:10 kojenutu yesi kere, ka ituŋa kere luka Isirael ebe, Kokiror loka Yesu Kristo loko Nasaret, lokibubukinete yesi, lokitajaruni Edeke kokatwak, kanuka ŋol ebwoi etuŋanan lo kakonyenekus eŋalei," 
Acts4:11 ŋol ŋes amoru nakinerete yesi ikadukok, naebwaikin araut amoru nati naka agor." 
Acts4:12 Kwabo emamei aitajar kotoma ece kere: naarai emamei ecekiror kokwap kakuj loeinakinitai ituŋa, loibusakinitor oni aitajario.”" 
Acts4:13 Kosodi keanyutu atitiŋ naka Petero ka Yokana, komisiikis da ebe eraas ituŋa lumam isisianakinitai, luemamei aijen, koumokis; kojenut da ebe kejaas kaYesu." 
Acts4:14 Nakeanyuniata da lokitaŋaleunio ebwoi nepepe kakes, komamuut nueboŋokinete," 
Acts4:15 Konye kicorakis kes alomar kaurianet, kineranakinos ebe," 
Acts4:16 “Kikonakini ai ituŋa lu? Naarai idelelei kotuŋa kere luibojete koYerusalem ebe eswamai aanyunet naejenio kamakec; kwabo mam kipedori aiŋer. 
Acts4:17 Konye kinye akirot na aiyatakin aisiarakin otuŋa, ketukuriana kes, sirikinerata bobo kediotunanan kere kokiror kaŋol.”" 
Acts4:18 Konyaraut kes, kicorakis kinyeis einer cut karaida aisisianakin kokiror loka Yesu." 
Acts4:19 Konye koboŋokis Petero ka Yokana kotemasi kes atiar, “Arai edolit kakonyen nuka Edeke aiirar yes aitelekarit Edeke, kotuboto yesi:" 
Acts4:20 naarai mam kipedori ainyein einer akiro nukianyunit ka nukiirarit da.” 
Acts4:21 Nakedauniata aitukurian bobo, koosikis, mam apedorete aitican kes kanuka ituŋa; naarai kitopolooritos ituŋa kere Edeke kanuka ŋun nukiswamao." 
Acts4:22 Naarai keraas ikar luka etuŋanan lokiswamakinio naanyunet ŋin naka aitaŋaleun luedeparito akaisaoŋon," 
Acts4:23 Nakeosikinere koloto neejaas ikecetuŋa, kitatamikis kes akiro kere nukelimokinete isasedotin lupeti ka imakio," 
Acts4:24 Nakiirariata, kikeut ikeceporotoi nepepe mama ejai Edeke, kotemasi atiar, “Wu Ejakait, lokisubi akuj, ka akwap, ka aŋolol, ka kere da luejaas tomakec:" 
Acts4:25 ibu kiner kotoma Emoyo Lokalaunan kaituk naka papaakosi Daudi ekonitelepat ebe, ‘Kanukinyo enyunyuratatar lukacekwapin, Ka ituŋa da itetemonoroto aamameak?" 
Acts4:26 Etemonokinos ikabakan luka akwapin, Etukonokinos ikayaitok nepepe, Asurokin Ejakait, ka Lokinyonyoikitonoke akinyet.’" 
Acts4:27 Naarai abeit etukonokinos Kerode ka Pontio Pilato, nepepe ka Imo ka ituŋa luka Isirael ore lo asurokin ekonitelepat lokalaunan Yesu, loinyonyoikinit akinyet," 
Acts4:28 tetere iswamaete kere nuelosikinit akonikan, ka nuinerunit ŋol ajaun." 
Acts4:29 Kwana da, wu Ejakait, kosesen aitukurianakec: koinak ikonibulesin einer akirot katitiŋ kere," 
Acts4:30 nairioria akonikan aitaŋaleun; kiswamai da aanyuneta ka nukaumokin kanuka ekiror loka ekonitelepat lokalaunan Yesu.” 
Acts4:31 Nakedauniata ailip, kitamaranai aibois kama ketukonokina; kilelebunos kere Emoyo Lokalaunan, kinerata akirot naka Edeke katitiŋ." 
Acts4:32 Kejaas ekodet kere loka luiyuunito ketau ediopet ka aijar adiopet: kwabo emamei idiopet yenikebala ebe ibore kere yenejaatar erai yenike; dimarai emorikikinito iboro kere. 
Acts4:33 Kitejenut ikiyakia ajarun naka Ejakait Yesu kapedor naepol, kojai asianut naepol mamakec kere." 
Acts4:34 Amamei yenilwaritoi kotomakec, naarai ituŋa kere lukejaas amanat arai itogoi, apotu kogwelanasi, koyaata etiai loka iboro lukegwelunete" 
Acts4:35 kibwaikis akejen nuka ikiyakia: kokorakinai ŋinituŋanan kwape kipudar. 
Acts4:36 Yosep da, lokenyaraete ikiyakia Baranaba, (apolouke Okoku loka aitalakaar) Elebit, lokeurikinio Kupuro," 
Acts4:37 kejai ŋes amana kogwela, koyau apesan kibwaik akejen nuka ikiyakia." 
Acts5:1 Konye ekiliokit ediopet, ekekiror Anania, ka akeberu Sapira, abu kogwela ibore yenajaatar," 
Acts5:2 kiŋadak acepesan kotiai, kojeni akeberu da, koyau ace, kibwaik akejen nuka ikiyakia." 
Acts5:3 Konye kotema Petero atiar, “Anania, kanukinyo kisilelebia Satan etaukon aimod Emoyo Lokalaunan, ka aiŋadakin da acepesan kotiai loka amana?" 
Acts5:4 Arai kesalakinit mam egwelara, mam kereka kesalit erai nakon? Nakedaunere agwelar, mam kerai nakakonipedor? Kikonakini bo ai ibwaikin akirot ŋin otaukon? Mam imodit ituŋa konye Edeke.”" 
Acts5:5 Nakiiraria Anania akiro ŋun, kibiror kotwana. Kokuriakaros ituŋa kere noi lukiirarete ŋun." 
Acts5:6 Konyout ikatumunak konunukoto, kodakasi kiŋa, kidaata." 
Acts5:7 Ketuboros bala isawan iuni kolom akeberu da komam ejeni nukedoikinete. 
Acts5:8 Kotema Petero atiar, “Kolimokinai, ipotu kereka kogwelasi amana kotiai kaŋol” Kotema atiar, “Eebo, kotiai kaŋol.”" 
Acts5:9 Kotema Petero atiar, “Kanukinyo ineruniata akodun Emoyo loka Ejakait? Koany, akejen nuka luedaete okilenikon ejaas okek, kidakarete jo da.”" 
Acts5:10 Atipet kibirokin akejeke kotwana. Kolomut ikatumunak kodumut ketwana, kodakasi kiŋa, kidaata kidunyas kokilenike." 
Acts5:11 Kokurianar Ekanisa kere, ka ituŋa kere lukiirarete ŋun," 
Acts5:12 Kiswamai aanyuneta ka nukaumokin nuipu kotuŋa kakanin nuka ikiyakia. Kojaenenas kere nepepe kediopetau alomaret naka Solomon. 
Acts5:13 Ice da mam apotu kotitiŋikis aimorikikin kakes, konye ituŋa kitopoloorito kes." 
Acts5:14 Kiyatanakinos lukiyuunito mama ejai Ejakait, ikepuak, ikiliok ka aŋor;" 
Acts5:15 kodakununete lukadekak orotin, ka aiperionokin ojam ka opalisin, tetere naitorio Petero kodolokini etoribeke ice kakesi." 
Acts5:16 Kotukonokinos da ituŋa lukoreria lukeapias ko Yerusalem, koyaununete lukadekak ka ŋul lukiticanenete ajokin nueroko; kitaŋaleunoi kes kere." 
Acts5:17 Konye konyou losasedoti lopeti ka lukejaas nepepe kaŋes kere, ŋes erioŋet loka Isadukayon, ileleba ekolo," 
Acts5:18 Kikamut ikiyakia koenikis aidaris naka ituŋa kere. 
Acts5:19 Konye kuare koŋaa emalaika loka Ejakait ikekia luka aidaris, kitolom kes kotema atiar," 
Acts5:20 “Koloto, kobwaata koyekalu kolimokis ituŋa akiro kere nuka Aijar kana.”" 
Acts5:21 Nakiirariata kesi, kolomasi oyekalu tupuruc sek, kisisianakis. Konye kobu losasedoti lopeti, ka ŋul lukejaas nepepe kaŋes, konyaraut aurianet, ka imakio kere luka idwe luka Isirael, kiyakiasi ituŋa aidaris tetere eyaunete kes." 
Acts5:22 Konye nakedolioto ikejaanakinak mam eanyuna kesi kaidaris; koboŋut kolimokis kes ebe," 
Acts5:23 “Kidum aidaris eenen ejok, ebwoete ikedarak da kokekia; konye nakiŋaaria mam edumuna idiotuŋanan kotoma.”" 
Acts5:24 Nakiiraria ekapolokiton loka eyekalu ka isasedotin lupeti akiro ŋun, kobuonokinos noi kanukec ebe, “Ikonakini bo do akirot na ai?”" 
Acts5:25 Kobu etuŋanan kolimok kes ebe, “Ituŋa ŋul lukienikinito yesi aidaris ejaas toma oyekalu, ebwoete isisianakinete ituŋa.”" 
Acts5:26 Kosodi kolot ekapolokiton nepepe ka ikejaanakinak koomata kes, konye mere kagogoŋ, naarai kekuriaka ituŋa kinyeis aibiribir kes kamor." 
Acts5:27 Nakeyauniata, kibwaikis akonyen nuka aurianet. Kiŋit losasedoti lopeti ebe," 
Acts5:28 “Kipou kecorakis yes kagogoŋ ebe Sirikisisianakis kokiror kalo; ido koany, ilelebata Yerusalem kaisisianakinikus, ikotosi ayaŋaun aokot nuka etuŋanan kaŋol mamakosi.”" 
Acts5:29 Konye koboŋokis Petero ka ikiyakia ebe, “Kibusakinit arimarit Edeke aitelekarit ituŋa." 
Acts5:30 Abu Edeke loka lukapapaawok kitaiaru Yesu, lokiarete kaikajakin okitoi." 
Acts5:31 Etopoloo Edeke ŋes kakanike nakoteten korau Lokapolon ka Eketaiaran, koinak Isirael aitoronokin ka aisionio adiakanareta." 
Acts5:32 Kirai isio ikajenak luka akiro kaŋun, nepepe ka Emoyo Lokalaunan, loainak Edeke kere luerimasi ŋes.”" 
Acts5:33 Nakiirariata ŋun, konomos noi ikecetauon, kinerut aiar kes." 
Acts5:34 Konye etuŋanan ediopet, Eparisayot ekekiror Gamaliel, ekesisianakinan loka ikisila, lokeyonito ituŋa kere, kobwo kaurianet, kicorak kitolomarai ber ikiyakia kiŋa." 
Acts5:35 Kotema kes atiar, “Yes ikiliok luka Isirael, kocoito nuiswamakinete ituŋa ŋul." 
Acts5:36 Naarai eroko apaarasia nu edoluno abu Teudas konyou, kituro ebe erai lokapolon; kimorikikinos ŋes kituŋa bala akwat aoŋon; konye koarai ŋes, kere da lukerimarete ŋes kisiarakinos, mam eraun ibore." 
Acts5:37 Akaulo kaŋol konyou Yuda Egalilayat, kapaarasia nuka aibil akwes, kiria ice kotuŋa atupar ŋes; ŋes da abu koolio; kere da lukerimarete ŋes kisiarakinos." 
Acts5:38 Kwana da katemari yes atiar, Kinaca ituŋa ŋul, kinyeisi kes; naarai akirot na arai aswam na, arai erai naka ituŋa, eoliori;" 
Acts5:39 konye arai erai naka Edeke, mam ipedorete aitoolior kes; kinyeis diat atakanun bala itijiete Edeke.”" 
Acts5:40 Kocamut akekiro; nakenyarauniata ikiyakia, kodaata, kicorakis kes kinyeis einer kokiror loka Yesu, koosikis." 
Acts5:41 Aso kolomut kesi kaurianet, iyalamasi naarai imaritai luibusakinit aiticanio kanuka Ekiror kaŋol," 
Acts5:42 Ido ŋinipaaran, koyekalu ka oreria da mam inyeina aisisianakin ka alimonokin nuka Yesu ebe ŋes Kristo." 
Acts6:1 Kapaarasia kaŋun nakiyatakinor etiai loka ikesisiak, kojau aŋuurian naka Iyonanin aluikin Iburanian naarai aponi kopalunai apuserunukec kotoma aijaanakin naka ŋinipaaran." 
Acts6:2 Konyaraut lutomon ka luarei ekodet ŋol loka ikesisiak, kotemasi atiar, “Mam ibusakinit sio ainyein akirot naka Edeke aijaanakin komesan." 
Acts6:3 Aso do, iinacan, koseutu ituŋa ikanykaarei kokidiŋikus, luijenete ebe ejokuka, luileleba Emoyo ka acoa, lukipedori adakakin oswam na." 
Acts6:4 Konye sio kinyikokini kotoma ailip ka aijaanakin naka akirot.” 
Acts6:5 Kitojokai akirot na kokodet kere, koseut Sitepan etuŋanan loileleba aiyuun ka Emoyo Lokalaunan, ka Pilip, ka Porokoro, ka Nikanor, ka Timon, ka Pamena, ka Nikolao, ekebelokinon loko Antiokia." 
Acts6:6 Kibwaikis ŋul akonyen nuka ikiyakia, kosodete nakedauniata ailip, kidokokis kes akecekanin." 
Acts6:7 Konyanyaar akirot naka Edeke; kiyatakin noi etiai loka ikesisiak ko Yerusalem, korimasi luipu lukosasedotin aiyuun ŋin." 
Acts6:8 Kilelebun Sitepan asianut ka apedor, kiswama nukaumokin nukos ka aanyuneta kotuŋa," 
Acts6:9 Konye ice kotuŋa lukatukos naanyaritai atukos naka Luaosikinitai, ka luko Kurene, ka luko Alegesanderia, ice da lukoKilikia ka Asia, konyoutu kopegata ka Sitepan," 
Acts6:10 Konye mam apedorete abwoikin acoa ka Emoyo lokinerar. 
Acts6:11 Kosodete kicora ituŋa, lukebalas ebe, “Kipou keirasi ŋol inera akiro nukainyanakin Musa ka Edeke.”" 
Acts6:12 Kisidiko ituŋa ka imakio ka ikewadikak, koponikis ŋes, kikamut, koyaŋaasi aurianet," 
Acts6:13 kisibwaata ikaienak lukeŋalak luabalas ebe, “Etuŋanan lo mam inyeinit einer akiro nuka asurokin aibois na nakalaunan ka ikisila da;" 
Acts6:14 naarai kipou keirasi ŋes inera ebe ebuni Yesu ŋol Enasarayot amudiar aibois na, ka ailocokin iponesio lukiinakini Musa oni.”" 
Acts6:15 Koŋanyakis ituŋa kere lukiboiete kaurianet ŋes akonyen, koanyut ekereet eputosi bala loka emalaika." 
Acts7:1 Kotema losasedoti lopeti atiar, “Ikote kereka akiro ŋun nen?”" 
Acts7:2 Kosodi Sitepan ebe, “Iinacan ka lukapapa da, kiirarai. Abu Edeke loka aibuses kotakanik papaawok Aburaam, nakejaar Mesopotamia, eroko iboikino Karan," 
Acts7:3 kotema ŋes atiar, ‘Konyou kotoma akwapukon, ka ajenakon, kolot akwap naketodikini.’" 
Acts7:4 Kosodi konyou kakwap naka Ikaludean, kiboikin Karan. Ketwana papake kitonyou Edeke ŋes kanen kiton akwap na naiboito yesi kwana;" 
Acts7:5 kwabo mam keinakinit adioirumet, karaida nekicakakina akeju, konye kisumun ainakin ŋes airum, ka aurike naetupanakini, nakerokor ŋes ikoku emamei," 
Acts7:6 Kinera Edeke nuikote nen ebe eraun akeur apeionon kotoma akwap naka ituŋa ice, luitubulesenete kes, ikonakinete kes erono apak naka ikar akwat aoŋon." 
Acts7:7 Kobala Edeke ebe, ‘Atubokini eoŋ ateker ŋin naitubulesene kes; akaulo kaŋun elomunete, kamaete eoŋ kaibois kana.’" 
Acts7:8 Koinak ŋes aitutuket naka aikep. Kouri do Aburaam Isaak, kokep kapaaran nakikanyetekauni; Isaak kouri Yakob, Yakob da kouri lukapapaawok lutomon ka luarei." 
Acts7:9 “Koreata lukapapaawok Yosep, kogwelasi Misiri. Kojai Edeke nenipe kaŋes," 
Acts7:10 Kolem ŋes kotoma aiticanioke kere, koinak aminunio ka acoa kakonyen nuka Parao, ekabaka loko Misiri, kitarau ŋes ekayaiton loko Misiri kere, ka eketogo da kere." 
Acts7:11 Kosodi koiau ebeli akwap kere nako Misiri ka Kanaan da, ka aiticanio naepol, lukapapaawok da mam edumuna inyamat lukedaunito." 
Acts7:12 Konye nakiiraria Yakob ebe ejaas akima Misiri, kijuka lukapapaawok irwan nasodit," 
Acts7:13 Kiton alosit nakiareit kitejenikin Yosep ikeinacan, kojenun do ateker naka Yosep kama ka Parao," 
Acts7:14 Kijuka Yosep, konyarau Yakob papake, ka akejena kere, ituŋa akaisakanykaarei ka lukany." 
Acts7:15 Kijesar Yakob Misiri, Kotwana, ŋes ka lukapapaawok;" 
Acts7:16 koyaŋaarai kiton Sekem, kidaikinai toma ates ya nakegwelit Aburaam kotiai loka epuesa kama ejaas odwe luka Kamor koSekem." 
Acts7:17 “Konye nakeapuunia apak naka aisumunet naabu Edeke koinak Aburaam, kipuaros ituŋa, kiyatakinos noi koMisiri," 
Acts7:18 aitodol naanyounio ekabaka ece koMisiri, lomam ajeni Yosep." 
Acts7:19 Koŋopik ŋol atekerewok, kikonak lukapapaawok erono, kicorak acakanar ikecemukerun tetere mam ejarete." 
Acts7:20 Kouriai Musa kapak kaŋin, kerai ŋesi yenikejok noi kama ejai Edeke. Kosaai ilapio iuni kotogo loka papake;" 
Acts7:21 kiton neacakarere, kiraru akoku naka Parao, kitan ŋes kwape ikekoku." 
Acts7:22 Kituutooroi Musa kacoa kere nako Misiri, kogogoŋor kotoma akiro ka aswamisio da." 
Acts7:23 “Kedolo ikekaru bala akaisaoŋon, kineru kotauke alosit aanyun ikeinacan idwe luka Isirael." 
Acts7:24 Koany ediopet ikonakinio erono, koyu ŋol lokereitai kinyaŋak kinom Emisiriat:" 
Acts7:25 koomit ebe ejenunete iinacanake ebe ainak Edeke aitajario kakanike; konye mam apotu kojenut. 
Acts7:26 Kapaaran naatupakini kitakanikin kes nakecelatar, kokoto aidiek kes, kobala ebe, ‘Ikatuŋa, iraas yesi iinacan, kanukinyo ikonanakinotor erono?’" 
Acts7:27 Konye lokikonakini onaceke erono koremo ŋes, kobala ebe, ‘Iŋai bo kiidakakini jo araut ekayaiton ka ekatubon kamakosi?" 
Acts7:28 Ikoto kereka aiar eoŋ da, kwape bian iaria Emisiriat?’" 
Acts7:29 Koker Musa kakirot kaŋin, korau epejonon kakwap nako Midian, kouru kaŋina idwe iarei." 
Acts7:30 “Kosodi ketuboros ikar akaisaoŋon, kitakanikin emalaika loka Ejakait kotoma amodiŋ naka Emoru Sinai, kaipelonoreta nuka akim kotoma okiot." 
Acts7:31 Nakeanyunia Musa, koumok nuaanyu; nakikunyakinia aanyun, kobu eporoto loka Ejakait ebe," 
Acts7:32 ‘Arai eoŋ Edeke loka lukapapaakon, Edeke loka Aburaam, ka loka Isaak, ka loka Yakob da.’ Komaran Musa, komam etitiŋikini asesen." 
Acts7:33 Kotema Ejakait ŋes atiar, ‘Kolaca amuk kakejenekon, naarai aibois naibwoia erai akwap nakalaunan," 
Acts7:34 Abeit aany aiticanio naka ikatuŋa luejaas Misiri, eira da eidinyikec, ejesun eoŋ ayuun kes. Aso kwana, kejukari jo Misiri.’" 
Acts7:35 “Musa ŋol lokegirete kobalas ebe, ‘Iŋai bo kiidakakini jo araut ekayaiton ka ekatubon da?’ ŋes kijukari Edeke araut ekayaiton ka ekayuunan kakan naka emalaika lokitakanikin kotoma okiot." 
Acts7:36 Ŋol ŋes kitolomuni kes, kedau aswam nukaumokin ka aanyuneta koMisiri ka Aŋolol Nakareŋan, kamodiŋ da apak naka ikar akaisaoŋon," 
Acts7:37 Ŋes Musa ŋol lokelimokini Isiraelin ebe, ‘Kitonyoikini Edeke yes enabi kotoma oinacanakus kwape kaeoŋ.’" 
Acts7:38 Ŋol ŋol loajai okanisa toma amodiŋ nepepe ka emalaika Iokineras kaŋes kotoma Moru Sinai, ido kalukapapaawok; ŋes lokedumuni akiro nuka aijar ainakin oni." 
Acts7:39 Kogiroto lukapapaawok arimar ŋes, konye koremosi, kinyakasi ikecetauon Misiri," 
Acts7:40 kolimokis Aaron ebe, ‘Kosubakinai sio idekesio lukiŋarenikinete; naarai mam kijeni nuadoikis Musa ŋol, lokiitolomuni kotoma akwap nako Misiri.’" 
Acts7:41 Kapaarasia kaŋun kosubut itaok, koinakis asuban mama ejai aput ŋin, kolelakis aswam naka akaninikec." 
Acts7:42 Konye kibelokin Edeke, kojalak tetere emaete ajore naka akuj; kwape kiwadikatere oitabo loka inabin ebe, ‘Ipotu kereka koinakis eoŋ itiaŋ luearitai ka asuban, Ŋo ekek loka Isirael, ikar akaisaoŋon kamodiŋ?" 
Acts7:43 Ipotu kodakasi ewema loka Molok, Ka aacerit naka edeke Repan, Aputosia nuiswamata tetere imaete: Ketwobosi yes koloto neelwana adepar Babulon.’" 
Acts7:44 “Kejaas lukapapaawok ewema loka aitejenunet kamodiŋ, kwape kicorakinia lokineras ka Musa, aswam koriakas kaput nakeanyuni." 
Acts7:45 Apotu lukapapaawok, kabeikinikec kitolomut ŋes nepepe ka Yosua, nakebeata airumet naka atekerin, nuereŋear Edeke kakonyen nuka lukapapaawok, kiton apaarasia nuka Daudi;" 
Acts7:46 lokedumun asianut kakonyen nuka Edeke, kilip adumakin Edeke loka Yakob eyekalu." 
Acts7:47 Konye abu Solomon kodukok ŋes etogo. 
Acts7:48 Kwabo Loejai kuju kakuj mam iboie kotogoi luiswamao kakanin; kwape inerar enabi ebe," 
Acts7:49 ‘Akuj ŋes ekaicolon, Ka akwapin da iicoloŋ yenika akakeie, Ebala Ejakait ebe, Etogo enyoin kidukokinete eoŋ? Arai aibois anyoin naebworaria?" 
Acts7:50 Mere kereka akakan iswamat ŋun kere?’ 
Acts7:51 “Yes lueninik imurisiŋa, lumam ekepitai itauon ka aki, irebirebete tiritir Emoyo Lokalaunan. Kwape eswamaata lukapapaakus, yes da iswamaete kwape kwaŋin," 
Acts7:52 Enabi ali lomam lukapapaakus areito? Apotu koarata lukedwarete akiro nuka abunore naka Ekadoliton; lokwana ibilakis yesi ebotet, koarata da," 
Acts7:53 yes luipotu kodumut ikisila kwape icorakinitotor imalaikan, komam iricito.”" 
Acts7:54 Kosodi nakiirariata akiro ŋun, konomos noi itauonokec, kiriamanakis ikel asurokinia ŋes." 
Acts7:55 Konye Sitepan kileleba Emoyo Lokalaunan, kosesen toma akuj, koany aibuses naka Edeke, ka Yesu da ebwoi kakan nakoteten naka Edeke;" 
Acts7:56 kotema atiar, “Koany, aanyuni akuj eŋaara, ka Okoku loka etuŋanan ebwoi kakan nakoteten naka Edeke.”" 
Acts7:57 Konye koresiaros keporoto loepol, kisikakis akeceki, kosomakinos ketau ediopet," 
Acts7:58 Kireŋeasi kore, kibiribiroto kamor; kibwaikis ikajenak ikecenapen akeje nuka ekatumunan loanyaritai Saul." 
Acts7:59 Kibiribiroto Sitepan kamor, kilip ŋesi ebe, “Ejakait Yesu, kiira ekamoyo.”" 
Acts7:60 Kokukokin kiworo keporoto loepol ebe, “Ejakait, sirikimarak kes aronis na.” Kedau einer ŋun, kojotoor." 
Acts8:1 Kitojokit Saul da akeario. Kapaaran kaŋin kodakun aimanit naepol aluikin ekanisa lokejai Yerusalem; kisiarakinos kere akwap nako Yudaya ka Samaria, dimarai ikiyakia." 
Acts8:2 Apotu ituŋa lueyoŋito Edeke kidaata Sitepan, kokuudianata da ŋes noi." 
Acts8:3 Konye komuna Saul ekanisa, kolomanari ŋolitogo, kidilidiliununei ikiliok ka aŋor da, kibwaik aidaris." 
Acts8:4 Kosodete ŋul lukisiarakinio koloto elimonokinete akirot," 
Acts8:5 Kijesar Pilip ore loko Samaria, kolimonok Kristo." 
Acts8:6 Kopupokis ikodeta kacoit ketau ediopet nukinera Pilip, naiirariata ka aanyun da aanyuneta nukiswamai." 
Acts8:7 Naarai apotu ajokin nuipu nueroko kolomut kama kaŋul lukikamunito, kiworoto keporoto loepol: luipu da lukasenyak ka iŋwalasik kitaŋaleunoi." 
Acts8:8 Kojau aiyalama naepol ore ŋol. 
Acts8:9 Konye koiai etuŋanan ekekiror Simon, lolem eswamaenenei nukecudet kore kaŋol, kisiwumok ituŋa luko Samaria, kobala ebe ŋes lokapolon." 
Acts8:10 Kopupokito kesi kere kacoit, ameun ka yenididi kiton yenikapolon kobalas ebe, “Etuŋanan lo erai apedor naka Edeke naenyaritai Nakapolon.”" 
Acts8:11 Kopupokito kacoit, naarai abu kisiwumok kes apak naepol kanuka ecudeteke," 
Acts8:12 Konye nakiyuuniata Pilip elimonokin akiro nukaiokak nuka ajakanut naka Edeke, ka ekiror da loka Yesu Kristo, kibatisai, ikiliok ka aŋor da." 
Acts8:13 Simon da elopet abu kiyu; kedau aibatisao koupakinos ka Pilip. Koumok nakeanyunia aanyuneta ka nukapedor nukapolok nukiswamai Pilip. 
Acts8:14 Kosodete nakiirariata ikiyakia lukejaas Yerusalem ebe eyuu Samaria akirot naka Edeke, kiyakiasi Petero ka Yokana mama ejaas," 
Acts8:15 lukijesaros kilipakis kes, tetere edumunete Emoyo Lokalaunan:" 
Acts8:16 naarai mam ber kedoikinit idio kakesi, konye ebatisatai ber kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu," 
Acts8:17 Kosodete kidokokis kes akecekanin, kodumut do Emoyo Lokalaunan," 
Acts8:18 Konye nakeanyunia Simon ebe einakinio Emoyo Lokalaunan kanuka aidokokin akanin nuka ikiyakia, kokoto ainakin kes arupian," 
Acts8:19 kobala ebe, “Koinakinai eoŋ da apedor na, tetere ŋinituŋanan yenedokokini akakanin kodumun Emoyo Lokalaunan.”" 
Acts8:20 Konye kotema Petero atiar, “Koolio epuesakon nepepe kajo; naarai iwomit ebe idumuni ainakinet naka Edeke kanuka arupian," 
Acts8:21 Emamei jo akorakinet karaida ewai kotoma akirot kana; naarai mam itenara ekonitau kakonyen nuka Edeke. 
Acts8:22 Aso kitoronikin aronisikon na, kilip Ejakait, elemuni kisionii aomisioit na naketaukon," 
Acts8:23 Naarai kaanyu jo ileleba adwaris kwape kepiu, ido da kienit elomorut loka amamus adolit.”" 
Acts8:24 Koboŋok Simon ebe, “Kilipakinai yesi eoŋ kama ejai Ejakait, kenyeis akiro ŋun nuinerata adolokin eoŋ.”" 
Acts8:25 Kosodi nakedauniata aitejenun ka alimonokin akirot naka Ejakait, koboŋos! Yerusalem, elimonokinete Akiro Nukajokak oreria luipu luka Isamarian." 
Acts8:26 Konye kinerata emalaika loka Ejakait ka Pilip, kotema atiar, “Konyou kobe ari naka eŋalakimak kiton orot loijesar anyoun ko Yerusalem alosit Gasa.” Ŋes amodiŋ." 
Acts8:27 Konyou kolot. Ido koany, etuŋanan loko Etiopia, ebwacit, ejakait loka Kadake akabaka naka Etiopia, loapolokinit abarake kere, kelosit ŋesi Yerusalem aima;" 
Acts8:28 eboŋuni ŋesi iboie kagalike, esiomi eitabo loka enabi Isaia." 
Acts8:29 Kotema Emoyo Pilip atiar, “Kikunyak agali ŋin, koupakinos kaŋes.”" 
Acts8:30 Aso koker Pilip mama ejai, kiira ŋes esiomi eitabo loka enabi Isaia, kiŋit ebe, “Ijeni kereka ijo ŋun nuisiomi?”" 
Acts8:31 Kobala ebe, “Ekonakini ai ajenuni, arai mam keŋarenikinit ituŋanan?” Kiŋaiŋa ŋesi Pilip adokar aiboikin kaŋes." 
Acts8:32 Ewai loka nukiwadikatai lokisiomi ŋesi ŋes lota ebe: “Koyaŋaarai aario kwape kamerekek; Ido kwape ililiŋia ikoku yenika amerekek kama kekatubon ajul, Kwape kwaŋin mam ŋes eoŋari akeituk;" 
Acts8:33 Kaitisilioke aponi kolemarai aketubokinio; Iŋai bo epedori aitejenikin aketur? Naarai alemar akeijar kakwap.” 
Acts8:34 Kotema ebwacit Pilip atiar, “Keŋaiŋait, kinera enabi akiro ŋun kanuka ŋai? Eraas kereka akekiro, arai bo nuka ece?”" 
Acts8:35 Kooŋ Pilip akeituk, kogeu kanakiwadikatai kaŋin kolimok ŋes akiro nukajokak nuka Yesu." 
Acts8:36 Napelosete korot, kodoloto neajaas akip; kotema ebwacit atiar, “Koany, akipi nu; inyo ca kesimikit eoŋ aibatisao?” [" 
Acts8:37 Kotema Pilip atiar, “Arai iyuunit kekonitau kere, epedoros.” Koboŋok ebe, “Eyuunit ebe Erai Yesu Kristo Okoku loka Edeke.”]" 
Acts8:38 Kicorak agali aibwo; kijesaros kesi iarei akipi, Pilip ka ebwacit, kibatisa ŋes," 
Acts8:39 Kedaut adokun kakipi abu Emoyo loka Ejakait kourupo Pilip; mam bobo ebwacit eanyuna, konye kiyatak akelosit iyalama." 
Acts8:40 Konye kotakanu Pilip kotoma Asoto, nakitoritor kolimonok akiro nukajokak koreria kere, kiton adolore Kaisarea." 
Acts9:1 Konye Saul, kiyatakinite nukaitukurian ka nukaiar ikesisiak luka Ejakait, kolot mama ejai losasedoti lopeti," 
Acts9:2 kilip ibaluan lulosit Damasiko lukiwadikakinitai atukosia, tetere arai kedum ituŋa luka Erot kalo, ikiliok ka aŋor da, koeni ka ayaun Yerusalem." 
Acts9:3 Ido napelosi eapikinit Damasiko, atipet kimiliau aica nakebuni kokuju airiamar ŋes." 
Acts9:4 Kibirokin kwap, kiira eporoto lokelimokini ŋes ebe, “Saul, Saul, kanukinyo kimanitor eoŋ?”" 
Acts9:5 Kobala ebe, “Ijo iŋai, Ejakait?” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Eoŋ Yesu loimanit ijo." 
Acts9:6 Konye konyou, koloma ore, kilimokinio nuibusakinit aswam.”" 
Acts9:7 Ituŋa da lukeupas kaŋes, kobwaata ililiŋete, iirarete eporoto, komam eanyunete etuŋanan," 
Acts9:8 Konyou Saul kokwap; komudukaka akekonyen, komam eanyuni ibore; kitiŋata akan, korikosi ŋes kiton Damasiko," 
Acts9:9 Kodau apaarasia auni komam eseseni, komam enyami da karaida aimat." 
Acts9:10 Kojai ekesisian Damasiko, ekekiror Anania, Kolimok Ejakait ŋol kaitapoet ebe, “Anania,” Kobala ebe, “Eoŋ lo, Ejakait.”" 
Acts9:11 Kotema Ejakait ŋes atiar, “Konyou, kolot orot loenyaritai Loitenara, kiŋitu kotogo loka Yuda etuŋanan loenyaritai Saul loko Taruso; naarai koany, ilipi," 
Acts9:12 eanyunit da etuŋanan ekekiror Anania, elomari ka aidokokin ŋes akanin, tetere ekwenyuni bobo.”" 
Acts9:13 Konye Koboŋok Anania ebe, “Ejakait, abu keira akiro nuka etuŋanan kaŋol kotuŋa luipu, nukaronok nuipu nuabu kiswamak lukalaunakakon, koYerusalem;" 
Acts9:14 kiton ne da ejai ŋes apolou naebuni kaneejaas lusasedotin lupeti ajen kere lukiwoneete ekonikiror.” 
Acts9:15 Konye kotema Ejakait ŋes atiar, “Kolot, naarai erai ŋol ibore yeneseunitai kamakaŋ adakar ekakiror kakonyen nuka atekerin ka ikabakan ka idwe luka Isirael;" 
Acts9:16 naarai etodikini ŋes nuipu nuibusakinit ŋes aiticanio kanuka ekakiror.” 
Acts9:17 Kolot do Anania koloma togo. Kidokok akanin, kotema atiar, “Onac Saul, keyaku Ejakait, ŋes Yesu lokiitakanikini jo korot lokibunio, tetere ikwenyuni bobo, kilelebi Emoyo Lokalaunan.”" 
Acts9:18 Atipet kodooto iboro kakonyeneke bala aabel, kokweny. Konyou kibatisai," 
Acts9:19 konyam inyamat, kodum agogoŋ. Kiboioto apaarasia ace ka ikesisiak luajaas Damasiko." 
Acts9:20 Atipet kolimonok Yesu katukosia ebe, “Ŋes Okoku loka Edeke.”" 
Acts9:21 Koumokis lukiirarete kere, kotemasi atiar, “Mere lo etuŋanan loabu komuna ŋul lukiwoneete ekiror ŋol koYerusalem? Ne da abu kobunite kanuka akirot kaŋin ajen kes ka ayaŋaar mama ejaas isasedotin lupeti.”" 
Acts9:22 Konye kiyatak Saul agogoŋoor, kisitirira Iyudayan lukejaas Damasiko, itogogoŋit ebe erai ŋol Kristo," 
Acts9:23 Kosodi ketuboros apaarasia nuipu, kinerut Iyudayan aiar ŋes," 
Acts9:24 konye kojenu Saul ekecebotet. Kidarata korutei paaran ka kuare da tetere earete ŋes," 
Acts9:25 Konye koyaŋaasi ikekesisiak ŋes kuare, kitodokasi karwatat, kijoliliosi kobukit." 
Acts9:26 Kosodi kedol ŋesi Yerusalem, abu kotam aimorikikin kikesisiak; kokuriakaros ŋes kere, naarai mam eyuunito ebe kerai ekesisian," 
Acts9:27 Konye Baranaba koyaŋa ŋes, kitoloma mama ejaas ikiyakia, kitejen kes kwape keanyunia Ejakait koroto, ebe da kinera kaŋes, ido kwape kelimonokinia katitiŋ kokiror loka Yesu koDamasiko." 
Acts9:28 Kojau kakes kolomanari kolomununei da koYerusalem," 
Acts9:29 elimonokini katitiŋ kokiror loka Ejakait; inera ka apeg ka Iyonanin; konye komootos kesi aiar ŋes," 
Acts9:30 Konye nakejenuniata iinacan, koyaŋaasi ŋes Kaisarea, kijukasi alosit Taruso." 
Acts9:31 Kwaŋin kinapakina ekanisa anatar Yudaya kere ka Galilaya ka Samaria da, kodukoi; ido kiyatanakin kolosenenei kayoŋit Ejakait, ka aitalakar naka Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
Acts9:32 Kosodi kanen nakimanimania Petero owaitin kere, kijesar mama ejaas lukalaunak lukiboiete koLuda." 
Acts9:33 Kanen kodum etuŋanan ekekiror Aenea, eperi koitada adaun ikar ikanykauni, naarai kesenyit." 
Acts9:34 Kotema Petero ŋes atiar, “Aenea, kitaŋaleu jo Yesu Kristo; konyou, kopet ekoniitada.” Atipet konyou." 
Acts9:35 Koanyutu ŋes ituŋa kere lukiboiete koLuda, ka Saron, kibelokinos mama ejai Ejakait." 
Acts9:36 Kojai akesisian koYopa, ekekiror Tabita, apolouke ebe Dorokas arai Amiam. Eleleba aberu ŋin aswamisio nuejok ka nukaitim nuakorenenei." 
Acts9:37 Kosodi kanen kapaarasia kaŋun kodekakin, kotwana; nakedauniata ailoŋ, kiperikis agola nakokuju." 
Acts9:38 Kosodi kanueapiatar Luda ka Yopa, kiirarito ikesisiak ebe ejai Petero ŋina, kiyakiasi ituŋa iarei mamakeŋ, kiŋaiŋaata ebe, “Sirikiyap abunore mamakosi.”" 
Acts9:39 Konyou do Petero kouparos kakes. Nakedolio, koyaŋaasi agola nakokuju. Kobwaata apuserun kere aapu kaŋes emonyete, ka aitodikin ikootin ka inapen lukedonyenenei Dorokas apak nakejaar kakes." 
Acts9:40 Konye kitoloma Petero kes kere kiŋa, kokukokin, kilip; kedau, kibelokin neejai akuan, kotema atiar, “Tabita, konyou.” Kokwenyu ŋesi; nakeanyunia Petero, konyou kiboikin." 
Acts9:41 Koinak ŋes akekan kitonyou; kosodi konyarau lukalaunak ka apuserun, kitodia ŋes ejari." 
Acts9:42 Kojenunai kore kere loko Yopa, kiyuutu da ituŋa luipu Ejakait." 
Acts9:43 Kosodi kosalak Petero Yopa apaarasia nuipu togo loka etuŋanan ekekiror Simon, ekekisikisan imukulen." 
Acts10:1 Kojai etuŋanan koKaisarea ekekiror Korunelio, ekapolokiton loka erioŋet loenyaritai Italian," 
Acts10:2 etuŋanan loeyoŋit Edeke, nepepe ka lukokaleke kere, lokekorenenei nukaitim nuipu otuŋa, ka ailipenen da Edeke tir." 
Acts10:3 Kosawa lokikanyetekaoŋon loka apaaran koany kaitapoet kaitebeikin emalaika loka Edeke ebunit neejai ŋesi, lokinera ebe, “Korunelio.”" 
Acts10:4 Kosesen noi, kokurianar, kobala ebe, “Anyoika, Ejakait?” Kotema ŋes atiar, “Adokasi ailipikon ka aikorokon araun aisitunet akonyen nuka Edeke." 
Acts10:5 Aso kwana kiyakia ituŋa Yopa, konyarau Simon loenyaritai Petero:" 
Acts10:6 Ipejokinit ŋesi Simon, ekekisikisan imukulen, loejai eketogo ariri kaŋolol.”" 
Acts10:7 Nakelosio emalaika loeneras kaŋes, konyarau iarei kokejaanakinakake lukotogo, ka eserikalet ediopet loeyoŋit Edeke kotoma kaŋul kalukijaanakinete ŋes tiritir;" 
Acts10:8 nakedaunia aitatamikin akiro kere, kijuka kes Yopa." 
Acts10:9 Kapaaran naatupakini, nakelosioto, ka aapikin ere, kodoka Petero kuju oswi loketogo ailip, kosawan ikanykape luka paaran." 
Acts10:10 Korieb noi eteŋei, kokoto ainyam: konye napitemonokinio, kogelakin ekemoyo," 
Acts10:11 koany akuj eŋaara, ka ibore yenejesunitai, bala aisuka naepol, ijoliliunitoi kwap kowaitin iwoŋon," 
Acts10:12 Nakejaas iponesio kere luka itiaŋ, ka lueliatos kakwap, ka ikweny luka apak," 
Acts10:13 Kobu eporoto ebe, “Petero, konyou; koar, konyam.”" 
Acts10:14 Konye kotema Petero atiar, “Mam cut, Ejakait; naarai mam anyamenenei ibore yeniketal, karaida yenimam elai.”" 
Acts10:15 Kobu eporoto irwan nakiareit ebe, “Luitalaunit Edeke, sirikinyara ijo luketal.”" 
Acts10:16 Kiswama akirot ŋin irwan auni, atipet kinyakarai ibore ii toma akuj." 
Acts10:17 Napebuonokin Petero kotauke apolou naka aitapoet naanyunit, koany, kobwoete ituŋa lukiyakuunit Korunelio kokek, kedaut aiŋitun etogo loka Simon," 
Acts10:18 Konyarata kiŋita arai ipejot Simon loenyaritai Petero nen. 
Acts10:19 Napeomoomoi Petero aitapoet, kotema Emoyo ŋes atiar, “Koany, ejaas ituŋa iuni lukimooto jo." 
Acts10:20 Aso konyou, kijesar kwap, koupakinos kakes komam ibuonokin; naarai eoŋ ejukunit kes.”" 
Acts10:21 Kijesun Petero mama ejaas ituŋa, kobala ebe, “Eoŋ lo lokimooto; iponitos kanuka akiro anyoika?”" 
Acts10:22 Kotemasi atiar, “Korunelio, ekapolokiton, etuŋanan loedolit Ioeyoŋit Edeke, loitojokitai kotoma ateker kere naka Iyudayan, abu emalaika lokalaunan kikwenya ŋes anyaraun jo alosit togoke, tetere iirari akiro kamakon.”" 
Acts10:23 Kisukunyik kes araut ikepejok. Kapaaran naatupakini konyou kolot kakes, koupakinos da ice koinacan luko Yopa kaŋes." 
Acts10:24 Kapaaran naatupakini kolomasi Kaisarea. Kidaret kes Korunelio, kotukokinite lukajenake ka ikepadic da." 
Acts10:25 Napelomari Petero, kisiriam Korunelio ŋes, kibirokin akejeke, koma ŋes." 
Acts10:26 Konye Petero kitonyou ŋes, kobala ebe, “Kobwo; arai eoŋ da etuŋanan.”" 
Acts10:27 Napinera, koloma kodum ituŋa luipu etukokina;" 
Acts10:28 kotema kes atiar, “Ijenete yesi ikulepek kwape eraar naketal Eyudayat aimorikikina arai aipejokin etuŋanan kere loka ateker ace; konye abu Edeke ketodik eoŋ ebe mam ebusakinit anyara idiotuŋanan yeniketal arai yenimam elai." 
Acts10:29 Kanuka ŋun nakanyaraunere, abu komam aŋeri, Aso keŋisit anyoin akirot nakinyaritotor eoŋ.”" 
Acts10:30 Kotema Korunelio atiar, “Eraas apaarasia aoŋon atuboros, kwape esawa lo, abu karicite esawa lokikanyetekaoŋon loka ailip kotogoka; ido koany, kobwo etuŋanan kakonyeneka enapit luimiliasi," 
Acts10:31 kabala ebe, ‘Korunelio, eirar akoniilip, akoniikor da eitun kakonyen nuka Edeke." 
Acts10:32 Aso kiyakia ituŋa Yopa, konyarau Simon loenyaritai Petero; ipejokinit ŋesi togo loka Simon, ekekisikisan imukulen, kariri naka aŋolol.’" 
Acts10:33 Aso abu kanyarau jo atipet, iswama ejok abunore. Aso kwana kija ne kere akonyen nuka Edeke, keirasi kere nukicorakinit Ejakait jo.”" 
Acts10:34 Kosodi kooŋ Petero akeituk, kotema atiar, “Abeit ajenu ebe mam Edeke etiakatiakai ituŋa," 
Acts10:35 konye kotoma ŋiniteker yeneyoŋit, kiswama da nuedolito, ecamuni ŋesi." 
Acts10:36 Akirot nakijukakini idwe luka Isirael, elimonokini akiro nukajokak nuka ainapakin kotoma Yesu Kristo, (ŋes Ejakait loka kere,)" 
Acts10:37 ijenete yesi akirot naalimoritai anatar Yudaya kere, ageun koGalilaya, akaulo ka aibatisa naalimonokini Yokana;" 
Acts10:38 Kwape kinyonyoikinia Edeke Yesu loko Nasaret akinyet naka Emoyo Lokalaunan ka apedor; lokelosenenei iswamai nuejok, itaŋaleununei kere lukiticani Satan, naarai kejai Edeke nenipe kaŋes." 
Acts10:39 Kirai isio ikajenak luka akiro kere nukiswamai ŋesi kakwap naka Iyudayan, koYerusalem da; koarata ŋol kaikajakin okitoi," 
Acts10:40 Abu Edeke kitajaru ŋes kapaaran nakiwuniet, koinak ŋes aitodiario;" 
Acts10:41 mere kotuŋa kere, konye mamakosi luabu Edeke koseu sek araut ikajenak, lukinyami ka aimat da nepepe kaŋes kedau ajarun kokatwak," 
Acts10:42 Kicorak sio kalimonokis ituŋa, ka aiteienun da ebe ŋol ŋes lekedakakini Edeke araut ekatubon loka ikajarak ka ikatwak da." 
Acts10:43 Ŋol ŋes itejenunitos inabin kere ebe kanuka ekekiror ŋinituŋanan yeniyuuni ŋes edumuni aisionio naka adiakanareta.” 
Acts10:44 Naperiŋa Petero inera ŋun, kodoik Emoyo Lokalaunan kere lukiirarete akirot." 
Acts10:45 Koumokis lukiyuunito lukekepitai lukeupunos ka Petero, naarai abukokin Imo da ainakinet naka Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
Acts10:46 Naarai kiirasi kes ineras kaŋajepa ka aitopoloor Edeke. Kosodi Koboŋok Petero ebe," 
Acts10:47 “Epedori kereka ituŋanan aisimik akipi nuka aibatis ituŋa lu, luainakin Emoyo Lokalaunan kwape kaoni?”" 
Acts10:48 Kicorak kes aibatisao kokiror loka Yesu Kristo. Kosodete kilipata ŋes asalakin apaarasia nuipupuuto. 
Acts11:1 Kosodete kiirasi ikiyakia ka iinacan luajaas Yudaya ebe eyuut Imo da akirot naka Edeke. 
Acts11:2 Kosodi nakedolunio Petero Yerusalem, ko pegata lukekepitai nepepe kaŋes," 
Acts11:3 kobalas ebe, “Ibu kolot otuŋa lumam ekepitai, komorata kakes.”" 
Acts11:4 Konye kogeu Petero aitejenun kaisudunyit, kotema atiar," 
Acts11:5 “Abu kajai ore loka Yopa elipi; kogelakin ekamoyo kaany aitapoet, ijesun ibore, bala aisuka naepol, ijoliliunio kokuju kowaitin iwoŋon; kadolok." 
Acts11:6 Kerere, kaŋic, ido kaany itiaŋ luka akwap, ka itiaŋ luededeŋ, ka lueliatos, ka akweny nuka apak." 
Acts11:7 Keira eporoto ebala ebe, ‘Petero, konyou; koar, konyam.’" 
Acts11:8 Konye katema atiar, ‘Mam cut, Ejakait; naarai ibore yenerai yeniketal karaida yenimam elai mam elomarit cut aitukuka.’" 
Acts11:9 Konye Koboŋok eporoto irwan nakiareit ebuni kokuju ebe, ‘Lukitalauni Edeke mam ibusakinit jo anyarit luketal.’" 
Acts11:10 Kiswama akirot na irwan auni, kosodi kiriarai bobo kere toma akuj." 
Acts11:11 Atipet ŋipeŋin, kobwaata ituŋa iuni koiŋaren ketogo lokija, lukiyakuunio mama ajai koKaisarea." 
Acts11:12 Kalimok Emoyo aupar kakes komam abuonokin. Koloto iinacan lu ikanykape nepepe keoŋ, kalomasi togo loka etuŋanan kaje." 
Acts11:13 Kitejenik epone lokeanyunia emalaika lokebwoi kotogoke ka atemar ebe, ‘Kiyakia ituŋa Yopa, konyarau Simon loenyaritai Petero;" 
Acts11:14 lokilimokini akiro nukitaiarete, ijo ka lukokalekon kere.’" 
Acts11:15 Konye napageari einer, kodoik kes Emoyo Lokalaunan kwape kiidoikinio oni kageunet," 
Acts11:16 Keitu do akirot naka Ejakait, kwape kinerar ebe, ‘Abu Yokana kibatis kakip, konye yes kibatisao kEmoyo Lokalaunan.’" 
Acts11:17 Aso arai ainaki Edeke kes ainakinet ŋin nakiinakinit oni nakiyuunia Ejakait Yesu Kristo, eoŋ bo iŋai lotiapedori airebokin Edeke?”" 
Acts11:18 Nakiirariata akirot ŋin kililiŋata. Kitopoloosi Edeke, kobalas ebe, “Ainak Edeke kiton Imo da aitoronikin naeyauni ajiar.”" 
Acts11:19 Kosodete lukisiarakinos kanuka aimanit nakedoikini kanuka akiro nuka Sitepan, koloto kiton Poenike ka Kupuro ka Antiokia, komam elimonokinete akirot dimarai oYudayan bon," 
Acts11:20 Konye ice kaŋul luko Kupuro ka Kurene, nakedolioto Antiokia, kinerata ka Iyonanin da elimonokinete akiro nukajokak nuka Ejakait Yesu." 
Acts11:21 Kojai akan naka Ejakait nenipe kakes, kiyuut ituŋa luipu kibelokinos neejai Ejakait." 
Acts11:22 Kodol eemut loka ituŋa kaŋul aki nuka ekanisa lokejai toma Yerusalem, kiyakiasi Baranaba Antiokia." 
Acts11:23 Nakedolio koany da asianut naka Edeke, kiyalamikin; kicor kes kere aikokoikin aimorikikina ka Ejakait kikecetauon kere;" 
Acts11:24 naarai kerai etuŋanan loejok, loeleleba Emoyo Lokalaunan ka aiyuun. Kiyatakinos ituŋa luipu mama ejai Ejakait." 
Acts11:25 Kosodi kolot Baranaba Taruso amoot Saul," 
Acts11:26 Nakedumunia koyau ŋes Antiokia. Kosodi kanen kotukonokinos nenipe kekanisa adaun ekaru kere, kisisianakis ituŋa luipu; ido kotoma Antiokia Ŋes ageunere amaikin ikesisiak Ikristayon." 
Acts11:27 Kapaarasia kaŋun kijesaros inabin anyoun koYerusalem kiton Antiokia. 
Acts11:28 Kobwo ediopet kakesi ekekiror Agabo, kodwar kanuka Emoyo ebe, ebuni ebeli loepol anatar akwapin kere; kojau da kapaarasia nuka Kulaudia." 
Acts11:29 Kinerut ikesisiak, ŋinituŋanan kwape epedoria, aijukakin iinacan lueboiete ko Yudaya iboro luiŋarakinete;" 
Acts11:30 Kiswamata kwaŋin, kijukakis imakio kakanin nuka Baranaba ka Saul." 
Acts12:1 Kapak kaŋin korio Kerode ekabaka akekanin aikonakin erono ice lukokanisa. 
Acts12:2 Koar Yakob onace loka Yokana kekileŋ; 
Acts12:3 nakeanyunia ebe itojokito Iyudayan, kiyatak aikamun Petero da. Keraas apaarasia ŋun nuka Imugatin lumam itubuunitoi." 
Acts12:4 Nakedaunia aikamun, kogolok aidaris, kibwaik akanin nuka irioŋeta iwoŋon luka iserikalei iwoŋon iwoŋon, tetere idarete; kokoto aitolomun ŋes neejaas ituŋa kedaun Aleleŋ." 
Acts12:5 Aso kidarai Petero kaidaris; konye kinyikokis noi lukokanisa ailip Edeke kanukeŋ. 
Acts12:6 Kakuar kaŋin naakotor Kerode aitolomun ŋes, kojotoi Petero kokidiŋ kiserikalei iarei, eenitai kirikoi iarei, kojaas ikedarak okek idarete aidaris;" 
Acts12:7 ido koany, kobwo emalaika loka Ejakait aapu kaŋes, kocau aica kagola; kinom Petero osiep kitwekeny, kobala ebe, “Konyou atipet.” Kodooto irikoi kakaninike." 
Acts12:8 Kotema emalaika ŋes atiar, “Konap, kirupak da akonimuk.” Kiswama kwaŋin, Kotema ŋes atiar, “Kimukok ekonilou, kotupunai.”" 
Acts12:9 Koloma kotup ŋes; mam abu kojen ebe nueswamai emalaika eraas nukabeit, konye aomit ŋesi ebe aanyu aitapoet." 
Acts12:10 Naketuborotor kaidaret nasodit ka nakiareit, kodoloto okek lokasua lolomaret kiŋa toma ore; koŋaari bon, kolomasi kiŋa kitoroto orot ediopet; atipet kinye ŋes emalaika." 
Acts12:11 Kosodi nakejenunia kotema atiar, “Kwana ajeni abeit ebe ejuku Ejakait ekemalaika alemun eoŋ kakan naka Kerode ka kere nuemuno ateker naka Iyudayan.”" 
Acts12:12 Nakedaunia aomoom ŋun, kolot togo loka Mariam, toto naka Yokana ŋol loerai ekekiror lokiareit Marako; ketukokina ituŋa luipu nen, ilipete." 
Acts12:13 Nakikuŋukuŋio ekek loka erute, kobu apese ekekiror Roda ajaar." 
Acts12:14 Nakejenunia eporoto loka Petero, mam eŋaara ekek kanuka aiyalama, konye koker koloma toma, kobala ebe, “Ebwoi Petero kokek.”" 
Acts12:15 Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Kikerepiki ca ijo.” Konye kitogogoŋ noi ebe ikote nen. Kotemasi atiar, “Erai ekemalaika.”" 
Acts12:16 Konye kiyatak Petero aikuŋukuŋ; kiton neaŋaariata, koanyutu ŋes, koumokis." 
Acts12:17 Konye kisililin kes kakekan, kitatamik kes kwape kelemunia ŋes Ejakait kotoma aidaris. Kotema atiar, “Kolimokis Yakob ka iinacan da akiro ŋun.” Kosodi konyou kolot aibois ace." 
Acts12:18 Nakiwalaria akwap, kobur iserikalei kanuadoikis Petero," 
Acts12:19 Nakemoia Kerode komam edumuni, kiŋitiŋit ikedarak, kicorak aario. Kosodi kijesar anyoun koYudaya alosit Kaisarea, kosalak nen." 
Acts12:20 Konyunyurik Kerode ituŋa luko Turo ka Sidon, kolosikis Ŋes ketau ediopet, ido kedaut aipaperikin ka Bulasito, lokedaran agola naperot naka ekabaka, kilipa ainapakin, naarai kedumunit akwapukec inyamat kakwap naka ekabaka." 
Acts12:21 Kapaaran naaseunitai konap Kerode ikenapen luka ekabakane, kiboikin oicoloŋ loka ekabakane, kiner akiro kamakec." 
Acts12:22 Kocelut ituŋa kobalas ebe, “Ŋes eporoto loka edeke, mere loka etuŋanan!”" 
Acts12:23 Atipet kinom emalaika loka Ejakait, naarai mam kitubusikinit Edeke; konyamata ŋes ikur, kotwana." 
Acts12:24 Konye kiyatakin akirot naka Ejakait, konyanyaar." 
Acts12:25 Koboŋosi Baranaba ka Saul koYerusalem, kedaut aijaanakinikec, kouparos Yokana loenyaritai Marako kakes." 
Acts13:1 Ko Antiokia, kokanisa lokejai kanen koiaas inabin ka ikesisianakinak, kes Baranaba, ka Simeon loenyaritai Niger, ka Lukio loko Kurene, ka Manaen Lokitanakio nepepe ka Kerode ekabaka, ka Saul da." 
Acts13:2 Kosodi napijaanakinete Ejakait, ka ailuŋ, kotema Emoyo Lokalaunan atiar, “Kogitakinai Baranaba ka Saul kanuka aswam naanyarakinit kes.”" 
Acts13:3 Kosodi kedaut ailuŋ ka ailip, kidokokis kes akecekanin kotwarata." 
Acts13:4 Kosodi kijuka Emoyo Lokalaunan kijesaros Seleukia; kenyoutu kanen kikwaŋaros kiton Kupuro. 
Acts13:5 Nakedolioto Salamis, kolimonokis akirot naka Edeke katukosia nuka Iyudayan. Kojaas ka Yokana ijaanakini kes." 
Acts13:6 Nakedauniata aitor apujan kere kiton Papo, kodumut ekacudan, enabi lokeŋalan, Eyudayat, ekekiror Bar-Yesu;" 
Acts13:7 kejaas etuŋanan ŋol nepepe ka ekayaiton, Serugio Paul, etuŋanan loka acoa. Konyara ekayaiton Baranaba ka Saul, kokoto aiirar akirot naka Edeke." 
Acts13:8 Konye Elumayo ekacudan (ŋes apolou naka ekekiror) kopegata kakes, kokoto aitapaar ekayaiton ainyein aiyuun." 
Acts13:9 Konye Saul, ŋes Paul, kilelebun Emoyo Lokalaunan, koŋanyak ŋes akonye," 
Acts13:10 kobala ebe, “Ijo loileleba aimod ka aronis kere, ijo okoku loka Satan, lokasurup loka adolit kere, mam kereka inyeini aitapaar irotin luitenara luka Ejakait?" 
Acts13:11 Kwana da, koany, ejai akan naka Ejakait mamakon, imudukanar ijo, komam ianyuni akoloŋ adaun apak.” Atipet kodoik ŋes elisina ka amuton, koturiaitoi ka amoot luerikete kakan." 
Acts13:12 Kosodi kiyu ekayaiton, nakeanyunia nukiswamao, naarai koumok aisisianakin naka Ejakait." 
Acts13:13 Kosodete kikwaŋaros Paul ka ikepaup anyoun koPapo, kodoloto Peruga toma Pampulia. Kinye kes Yokana kanen koboŋo Yerusalem." 
Acts13:14 Konye kes, konyout koPeruga kitoroto akwap kodoloto Antiokia ere loka Pisidia. Kolomas atukos kapaaran nakasabato, kiboikinos." 
Acts13:15 Kedaut asoman ikisila ka inabin, kiyakiasi ikayaitok luka atukos mamakec ebe, “Iinacan, arai ijaas kakirot nakaicor ituŋa, kolimut.”" 
Acts13:16 Kobwo Paul kokwet kakan kobala ebe, “Ikiliok luka Isirael, ka yes da luiyoŋito Edeke, kiirasi." 
Acts13:17 Edeke loka ituŋa kalu luka Isirael abu koseu lukapapaawok, kitopoloo ituŋa nakiboiororoto kakwap nako Misiri, kitolom kakan naerioro." 
Acts13:18 Apak bala naka ikar akaisaoŋon kotitiŋik kes kamodiŋ," 
Acts13:19 Nakedaunia amudiar atekerin akanykaarei kotoma akwap nako Kanaan, koinak kes akecekwap araut airumet, apak naka ikar bala akwat aoŋon ka akaisakany." 
Acts13:20 Akaulo kaŋun koinak kes ikatubok kiton Samuel enabi. 
Acts13:21 Kosodete kilipa ekabaka; koinak Edeke Saul okoku loka Kis, lokateker naka Benyamin, apak naka ikar akaisaoŋon," 
Acts13:22 Nakelemaria ŋol, kodakak Daudi araut ekabakakec; lokitejenuni ŋesi ebe, ‘Adum Daudi okoku loka Yese etuŋanan loitalakarit ekatau, loebuni aswam nuakoto eoŋ kere.’" 
Acts13:23 Kotoma aur naka etuŋanan kaŋol ainu Edeke Isirael Eketaiaran, ŋes Yesu, kwape esumunitor." 
Acts13:24 Eriŋa ŋesi ebuno abu Yokana koliŋak alimonokin ituŋa kere luka Isirael aibatis naka aitoronikin," 
Acts13:25 Napedauni Yokana akelosit, kobala ebe, ‘Kiwomito eoŋ araut iŋai? Mam arai ŋol. Konye koany, ebunit kokaukaŋ lomam kebusakinit eoŋ alacar amuk nuka akejeke.’" 
Acts13:26 “Iinacan, idwe luka aur naka Aburaam, ka luiyoŋito Edeke da kotomakus, ejukun akirot naka aitaiario mamawok." 
Acts13:27 Naarai luiboiete koYerusalem, ka ikayaitokokec, kanu mam ajenuniata ŋes, karaida akiro nuka inabin nuesiomenenoo ŋinisabato, etodolikis kanuka atubokin ŋes," 
Acts13:28 Karaida mam eanyunitos akirot naibusakinitor atwanare, konye kilipata Pilato koarai," 
Acts13:29 Nakedauniata aitodolikin kere nukiwadikatai kanukeŋ, kijesut kokitoi, kibwaikis ates," 
Acts13:30 Konye kitajaru ŋes Edeke kokatwak. 
Acts13:31 Apaarasia nuipu kitakanikin ŋul lukedokarete nepepe kaŋes anyoun koGalilaya kiton Yerusalem, lueraas kwana ikajenakake mama ejaas ituŋa." 
Acts13:32 Kiinunit isio yes akiro nukajokak nuka aisumunet nakeinakinio lukapapaawok," 
Acts13:33 ebe etodolik Edeke oni ikecedwe aisumunet ŋin, kanuka aitajarun Yesu; kwape iwadikatere kotoma osabuli lokiareit ebe, ‘Irai ijo Okokuka, Lolo kawuru jo.’" 
Acts13:34 Ido kanuka akirot kaŋin ebe etajaru ŋes kokatwak, kinye bobo aboŋor aibos, inera kwanata ebe, ‘Kainakini yes arereŋesio nukalaunak ka nuicasito nuka Daudi.’" 
Acts13:35 Kanuka ŋun inera kosabuli ece ebe, ‘Mam icamuni Ekalaunanikon aibos.’" 
Acts13:36 Naarai Daudi, kedau aijaanakin ainerun naka Edeke katurike, abu kojotoor, kibwaikinai nepepe ka lukapapaake, kobos;" 
Acts13:37 konye ŋol lokitajaruni Edeke mam abu kobos," 
Acts13:38 Aso do iinacan, kojenutu ebe, kotoma otuŋanan kaŋol elimonokinio yes aisionio naka adiakanareta;" 
Acts13:39 ido kotomakeŋ ŋin yeniyuuni imarakinio adolit kakiro kere, numam epedorere aimarakin adolit kokisila luka Musa," 
Acts13:40 Aso kocoito, kinye akirot adoikin yes, nainerito inabin ebe:" 
Acts13:41 ‘Koanyutu, yes ikamenak, koumokis, kooliosi; Naarai eswamai eoŋ aswam kapaarasiakus, Aswam namam iyuunete cut, karaida kiilimonok ituŋanan yes.’ ”" 
Acts13:42 Napelomarete, kiŋaiŋaata alimokin akiro ŋun kasabato naatupakini." 
Acts13:43 Nakisiarakinor atukokin naka atukos, apotu Iyudayan luipu ka ikebelokinok lueyoŋito Edeke kotupasi Paul ka Baranaba, lukinerasi kakes, kisicerededata aiyatakin kotoma asianut naka Edeke." 
Acts13:44 Kosodi kasabato naatupakini kotukokinos ituŋa luipu, aapie ere kere, aiirar akirot naka Edeke." 
Acts13:45 Konye nakeanyuniata Iyudayan ikodeta, kilelebun ekolo, kitepega nuenera Paul, komoromoroto da." 
Acts13:46 Kinerata Paul ka Baranaba katitiŋikin ebe, “Ibusakinit akirot naka Edeke ainerio ber kamakus. Konye naarai igaguarete kamakus, itubokinos bonik araut lumam ibusakinito aijar namam edaun, koany, kibelokin do mama ejaas Imo," 
Acts13:47 Naarai abu Ejakait kicorak sio kwaŋin ebe, ‘Kebwaik jo araut aica naka Imo, Tetere iyauni aitajario kiton osaŋeta luka akwapin.’ ”" 
Acts13:48 Nakiirariata Imo ŋun, kiyalamikinos, kitopoloos akirot naka Ejakait; ŋul da lukelosikinito aijar namam edaun kiyuut do." 
Acts13:49 Kisiarakin akirot naka Ejakait akwap ŋin kere. 
Acts13:50 Konye kicecemoto Iyudayan aŋor nueyoŋito nukapolou ka ikeŋarenikinok luka ere, kisidikoto aimanit Paul ka Baranaba, kireŋeasi koikorunokec." 
Acts13:51 Konye kilakilakata adai nuka akejekec, koloto Ikonium." 
Acts13:52 Kilelebunos ikesisiak aiyalama ka Emoyo Lokalaunan. 
Acts14:1 Kosodi kanen kotoma Ikonium, kolomasi nepepe toma atukos naka Iyudayan, ido kanuka ŋun nuenerasi kiyu ekodet loapol loka Iyudayan ka Iyonanin." 
Acts14:2 Konye Iyudayan lumam kiyuunito kisidikoto Imo kitolomikis etau loerono asurokin iinacan. 
Acts14:3 Kosodete kosala nen apak naepol, inerasi katitiŋ kotoma Ejakait, lokitejenuni akirot naka akesianut, kocamak aanyuneta ka nukaumokin aiswamao kakaninikec," 
Acts14:4 Konye kotiakas ituŋa lukore; ice owai loka lyudayan, ice da owai loka ikiyakia," 
Acts14:5 Kiton neatakanunia asurokin naka Imo ka Iyudayan, nepepe kikayaitokokec, aiswamakin kes erono, ka aibiribir kamor." 
Acts14:6 Kejenut kes ŋun, kokereasi Lusitura ka Derube, ireria luka Lukaonia, ka akwapin nuedunyatar;" 
Acts14:7 kanen da kolimonokis akiro nukajokak. 
Acts14:8 Kanen koLusitura kojai etuŋanan iboie, ilejekekas akekeje, eŋwalas ameun kakoik naka totoke, lomam alosi cut." 
Acts14:9 Abu ŋol kiira Paul inera; kosesen Paul ŋes, koany ebe ejai aiyuun naitanaleuni," 
Acts14:10 kolimok keporoto loepol ebe, “Kobwo kotenan kakonikeje.” Kodetun atipet, kosakasak." 
Acts14:11 Nakeanyuniata ikodeta nukiswamai Paul, kikeseut iporotoikec, kobalas kaŋajep naka Lukaonia ebe, “Kijesakinos oni idekesio kaput naka ituŋa.”" 
Acts14:12 Komaikis Baranaba Seu, ka Paul da Kereme, naarai kerai ŋesi lokiŋarenikinit einer." 
Acts14:13 Koyau esasedoti loka Seu, lokejai eyekaluke kiŋaren naka ere, imoŋin ka abokoi nuka atur kiton okek, kokoto ainakin asuban nepepe kikodeta." 
Acts14:14 Konye nakejenuniata ikiyakia Baranaba ka Paul, kocilata ikecenapen, kokerata kolomasi okodet, kiworoto ebe," 
Acts14:15 “Ikatuŋa, kanukinyo iswamaata nu? Kirai isio da ituŋa lukepone kwape kayesi, kiinunit yes akiro nukaiokak, tetere ibelokinos ainyein akiro nu nukamameak kosesena Edeke lokajaran lokesubi akuj ka akwap ka aŋolol ka iboro da kere luejaas tomakec," 
Acts14:16 Katurio nuatuboros abu kojalak atekerin kere alosit kotoma orotinikec; 
Acts14:17 konye mam kinyein komamei aitejenunet, naarai kiswama nuejok, koinak yes akiru abunore kakuj, ka apakio nuka amio, isimonikini ikusitauon kinyamat ka aiyalama.”" 
Acts14:18 Kakiro kaŋun, kitikokis ikodeta kationis ainakin kes asuban." 
Acts14:19 Konye kodolut Iyudayan luapote koAntiokia ka Ikonium; kisidikoto ikodeta, kibiribiroto Paul kamor, kiriasi kiŋa naka ere, koomito ebe atwana," 
Acts14:20 Konye napelukunito ikesisiak, konyou, koloma ore; kapaaran naatupakini kolot Derube nepepe ka Baranaba." 
Acts14:21 Kosodi nakedauniata alimonokin akiro nukajokak toma ore ŋol, ka adumun ikesisiak luipu, koboŋosi Lusitura ka Ikonium ka Antiokia," 
Acts14:22 kitogogoŋo itauon luka ikesisiak, ka aikwenyar kes kosalito toma aiyuun ŋin, ebe da kibusakinit alomar toma ajakanut naka Edeke kotoma aiticanio nuipu." 
Acts14:23 Nakedauniata aseikin kes imakio kotoma ŋolikanisa, kailip, ka ailuŋ, kibwaikis kes akanin nuka Ejakait lokiyuunito." 
Acts14:24 Kitoro Pisidia, kodolot Pampulia." 
Acts14:25 Kedaut alimonokin akirot toma Peruga, kijesaros kiton Atalia;" 
Acts14:26 konyout kanen kikwaŋaros kiton Antiokia nekolo elipakinere kes asianut naka Edeke kanuka aswam naadaut aitodol. 
Acts14:27 Nakedolioto, kotukokis ekanisa, kitatamikis akiro kere nukiswamai Edeke nepepe kakes, ebe da aŋaik Imo ekek loka aiyuun," 
Acts14:28 Kiboioto kanen apak namam edit nepepe kikesisiak. 
Acts15:1 Konye kijesunos icetuŋa anyoun koYudaya, kisisianakis iinacan ebe, “Arai mam kikepio kwape ejaar epone loka Musa, mam ipedorete aitajario.”" 
Acts15:2 Kosodi kedaut Paul ka Baranaba epeget kituŋa kaŋul ka aibakibak noi, kicorakis iinacan Paul ka Baranaba ka ice kakesi adokar Yerusalem mama ejaas ikiyakia ka imakio kanuka akirot kaŋin." 
Acts15:3 Aso kotwar ekanisa kes kitoro akwapin nuko Poinike ka Samaria, itatamete aibelokin naka Imo, kisiyalamikis noi iinacan," 
Acts15:4 Nakedolioto Yerusalem, kisukunyik ekanisa, ka ikiyakia ka imakio, kitejenut akiro kere nukiswamai Edeke nepepe kakes." 
Acts15:5 Konye konyout lukiyuunito ice lukorioŋet loka Iparisayon, kobalas ebe, “Ibusakinit aikep kes, ka aicorakin da airic ikisila luka Musa.”" 
Acts15:6 Kotukokinos ikiyakia ka imakio tetere eomoomoete akirot ŋin," 
Acts15:7 Kedaut aibakibak noi, kobwo Petero kotema kes atiar, “Iinacan, ijenete ebe kapaarasia nugeet, abu Edeke koseu kokidiŋikus, tetere iirarete Imo akirot naka Akiro Nukajokak kaitukuka, kiyuut." 
Acts15:8 Edeke da loejeni itauon luka ituŋa kitejenik kes, koinak Emoyo Lokalaunan kwape kiinakinia oni;" 
Acts15:9 kwabo mam etiakit oni ka kes, konye itesegaari itauonokec kaiyuun." 
Acts15:10 Aso kanukinyo ikoduniata Edeke kanuka aibwaikin aiookot omurisiŋa luka ikesisiak, namam lukapapaawok karaida oni kipedorit airioŋ?" 
Acts15:11 Konye kiyuunit ebe kitajario kanuka asianut naka Ejakait Yesu, kwape kakesi.”" 
Acts15:12 Kosodi kililiŋ atukot kere; kopupokis Baranaba ka Paul itatamete aanyuneta ka nukaumokin nukiswamai Edeke kotomakec komo," 
Acts15:13 Nakedauniata aililiŋ koboŋok Yakob ebe, “Iinacan, kiirarai." 
Acts15:14 Kitejenu oni Simeon kwape kisiaunia Edeke aanyanar Imo, alemun kotomakec ituŋa kanuka ekekiror." 
Acts15:15 Ecamanara nu kakiro nuka inabin, kwape iwadikatere ebe," 
Acts15:16 ‘Akaulo kaŋun aboŋuni, Aduki bobo ewema loka Daudi lokibiror; Aduki bobo amejeke, Eticasi ŋes," 
Acts15:17 Tetere luesalito luka ituŋa emoete Ejakait, Ka Imo kere luenyaritai ekakiror," 
Acts15:18 Ebala Ejakait nu, loitejenunit akiro nu ameun apeŋo.’" 
Acts15:19 Kanuka ŋun atubi eoŋ kwanata ebe, Mam kiticani ŋul luibelokinos mama ejai Edeke kotoma Imo," 
Acts15:20 konye kewadikakisi kes kinaca nuesiliaka nuka aputosia, ka adoteu, ka itiaŋ luemiedio ka aokot." 
Acts15:21 Naarai ameun katurio nupeŋo ajaas lualimonokinete akiro nuka Musa kaŋolire, naarai esiomio ŋinisabato kotoma atukosia.”" 
Acts15:22 Kosodete kitojoka ikiyakia ka imakio ka ekanisa kere, aseun ituŋa lukotomakec, aiyakiar Antiokia nepepe ka Paul ka Baranaba; kes luta, Yuda loenyaritai Barasaba, ka Sila, lukeraas ikeŋarenikinok koinacan:" 
Acts15:23 kiwadikata kwanata kijukasi kakaninikec ebe: “Iinacan ikiyakia ka imakio mama ejaas iinacan lueraas Imo kotoma Antiokia ka Suria ka Kilikia, ayogan," 
Acts15:24 Naarai kipupu ebe ituŋa ice lukepote kamakosi kiticanata yes kakirokec, isibuonokinete itauonokus, numam sio kicorakinit," 
Acts15:25 kitojok sio, kemorikikina ketau ediopet, aseun ituŋa aiyakuun mama ijaas nepepe ka Baranaba ka Paul luminanawok," 
Acts15:26 ituŋa luijaikinito aijarakec kanuka ekiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo," 
Acts15:27 aso kijuku Yuda ka Sila, lukilimokinete akiro nupenu kaitukekec." 
Acts15:28 Naarai itojokit Emoyo Lokalaunan ka sio da kenyeis aisibwok yes abwokon naitelekarit akiro nu nuibusakinito: 
Acts15:29 Kes nuta ebe, Kinaca iboro lueinakinio aputosia araut asuban, ka aokot, ka itiaŋ luemiedio, ka adoteu da. Arai kitikokinos kaŋun, iswamaete ejok, Yoga do,”" 
Acts15:30 Kosodi ketwar, kijesaros Antiokia; kotukokis ekodet kere, koinakis ebalua." 
Acts15:31 Nakesiomiata, kiyalamikinos kanuka aitalakario kaŋin," 
Acts15:32 Yuda ka Sila da, lukeraas inabin, kitalakasi iinacan kakiro nuipu, kitogogoŋo kes." 
Acts15:33 Kosalakis ŋina adaun apak, kotwara kes iinacan aboŋor kainapakin mama ejaas lukiyakuunete. [" 
Acts15:34 Konye kitojok Sila asalakin nen.] 
Acts15:35 Konye kosalakis Paul ka Baranaba Antiokia, isisianakinete ka alimonokin akirot naka Ejakait, nepepe ka icetuŋa da luipu." 
Acts15:36 Ketuboros apaarasia adis, kotema Paul Baranaba atiar, “Aso kabonosi kwana kaanyanasi iinacan kaŋolire nekiilimonokinit akirot naka Ejakait, kaanyutu kwape ejaatar.”" 
Acts15:37 Kokoto Baranaba ayaŋaar Yokana loenyaritai Marako aupar kakes," 
Acts15:38 Konye mam kitojokit Paul ayaŋaar ŋol lokinyeini kes koPampulia, komam elosete kakes aswam." 
Acts15:39 Kosodi kojau epeget loepol kidiŋikec kiton neatiakatar, koyaŋa Baranaba Marako kikwaŋaros Kupuro," 
Acts15:40 konye Paul koseu Sila konyou, ilipakinete iinacan tetere einakinio asianut naka Ejakait." 
Acts15:41 Kitor Suria ka Kilikia, itogogoŋi ikanisan."
