Acts16:1 Ido kodol Derube ka Lusitura: nekejai ekesisian ekekiror Timoteo, okoku loka aberu Ayudayat nakiyuunit; konye papake kerai Eyonanit." 
Acts16:2 Kitejenut iinacan lukiboiete koLusitura ka Ikonium kwape ejokiar ŋesi," 
Acts16:3 Kokotokin Paul ŋol aupakin kaŋes; koyaŋa kokep ŋes kanuka Iyudayan lukejaas atutubeta ŋun, naarai kejenete kere ebe kerai papake Eyonanit." 
Acts16:4 Kosodete nakitoritotor oreria, koinakis kes aicorakineta nukicorakinete ikiyakia ka imakio luko Yerusalem tetere ericete." 
Acts16:5 Kwaŋin kitogogoŋoi ikanisan kotoma aiyuun ŋin, kiyatanakin etiaikec ŋinipaaran." 
Acts16:6 Kitoroto akwap naka Pirugia ka Galatia, kisimik kes Emoyo Lokalaunan alimonokin akirot toma Asia." 
Acts16:7 Nakedolioto atereikina Musia, kotama alosit Bitunia, konye mam Emoyo loka Yesu abu kocamak kes," 
Acts16:8 Aso kinaca Musia kijesaros Tiroa. 
Acts16:9 Koany Paul aitapoet kuare: bala ebwoi etuŋanan loko Makedonia iŋaiŋait kobala ebe, “Kikwaŋun Makedonia, kiŋarak sio.”" 
Acts16:10 Nakedaunia aanyun aitapoet, atipet kakotos alosit Makedonia, naarai kiwomit cut ebe kinyarit Edeke sio alimonokin kes akiro nukajokak." 
Acts16:11 Aso kekwaŋaros anyoun koTiroa, karasasi Samoturake, kapaaran da naatupakini kadoloto Neapoli." 
Acts16:12 Kanyoutu kanen kadoloto Pilipi, ere lokapolon loka akwap nako Makedonia, akwap nakebwotunito ice ko Romayon. Keboioto kore kaŋol apaarasia adis." 
Acts16:13 Kosodi kapaaran nakasabato kalomutu korute kaloto ariri kecor, nekiwomit ebe kejai aibois nakilipet; keboikinos kenerata kaŋor nukidumuni kanen." 
Acts16:14 Aberu, ekekiror Ludia, nakegwelanari iboro lumugeik, naka ere loka Tuatira, naeyoŋit Edeke, kopup sio: nakepukorit Ejakait eketau tetere ecoit akiro nuenera Paul." 
Acts16:15 Kosodi kedau aibatisao, ŋes ka lukokaleke, kiŋaiŋa sio, kobala ebe, “Arai ianyunito eoŋ arai naiyuunit Ejakait, kolomutu togoka kipejoto.” Kitiŋa sio." 
Acts16:16 Napekilosi aibois naka ailip, keriamata kapese naejai aiokit naka aidwar, nakedumanakini ikejaka ameda naepol naka aidwar." 
Acts16:17 Kotupu ŋin Paul ka sio iworoi ebe, “Ituŋa lu eraas ikejaanakinak luka Edeke loejai kuju kakuj, lukilimonokinete yes erot loka aitajario.”" 
Acts16:18 Kikoni nen apaarasia nuipu. Konye koŋoiar Paul, kibelokin kotema ajokit atiar, “Kecorakini jo kokiror loka Yesu Kristo kolom kamakeŋ.” Kolom kosawa kaŋope kaŋol," 
Acts16:19 Konye nakeanyuniata ijakake ebe atwakiasi ameda naamunos, kikamutu Paul ka Sila, kidilidilasi kiton agwelanaret akonyen nuka ikayaitok;" 
Acts16:20 koyaŋaasi mama ejaas ikatubok kotemasi atiar, “Ituŋa lu eraas Iyudayan, amunaasi erewok," 
Acts16:21 bobo da elimonokinete iponesio lueraas luketal kamawok Iromayon acamun karaida aswam.” 
Acts16:22 Konyou ekodet kere asurokin kes: kolacasi ikatubok inapenekec kagogoŋ, kicorakis kes aleio kisureta." 
Acts16:23 Nakedauniata aile noi, kogolokis aidaris, kicorakis ekedaran aidar kes kacoit," 
Acts16:24 Kedau adumun aicorakinet ŋin, kibwaik kes toma aidaris nakotoma, koen akejekec oloin." 
Acts16:25 Konye kidiŋebai ilipete Paul ka Sila, eyeikinete Edeke ikososio luka aiturit, kopupete ienan da ice;" 
Acts16:26 atipet kojau amaran naepol naka akwap, komaranata apeteta nuka aidaris; atipet koŋaaros ikekia kere, kolacaros da aeneta nuka ituŋa kere," 
Acts16:27 Kokweny ekedaran, nakeanyunia ebe eŋaara ikekia luka aidaris, kout ekekileŋ, kokoto aarakin, koomit ebe asiata ienan." 
Acts16:28 Konye kiworo Paul keporoto loepol ebe, “Sirikimusuŋikin, naarai kija isio ne kere.”" 
Acts16:29 Konyarau atalai, komotar toma, emarani kanuka akurian, kibirokin akonyen nuka Paul ka Sila," 
Acts16:30 kitolom kiŋa, kotema atiar, “Ikajaka, kekonak ai tetere ketajario?”" 
Acts16:31 Kobalasi ebe, “Kiyuu Ejakait Yesu, kitaiario jo ka lukokalekon kere.”" 
Acts16:32 Kolimokis ŋes ka ituŋa kere luajaas togoke akirot naka Ejakait," 
Acts16:33 Kisukunyik kes kosawa kaŋol loka akuare, kilot ikecemacarin, atipet kibatisai ŋes ka iketuŋa kere." 
Acts16:34 Kosodi koyau kes togoke, koinak kes inyamat, kolakara noi, ŋes ka ekekale kere, naarai iyuunit Edeke." 
Acts16:35 Konye kiwala akwap, kiyakiasi ikatubok ikapolok luka iserikalei, kobalas ebe, “Koosikis ituŋa ŋul koloto.”" 
Acts16:36 Kitejen ekedaran Paul akiro ŋun ebe, “Eyakuut ikatubok aosikin yes: aso do kolomutu, koloto inapakina.”" 
Acts16:37 Konye kotema Paul kes atiar, “Apotu koleata sio kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere, komam etubokina, kwabo kirai isio Iromayon, bobo da kigolokis aidaris; kwana da ekotosi cabo alacakin kaiyeiyea? Mam cut; konye kopotu kesi ikulepek kolacakis sio.”" 
Acts16:38 Kolimokis ikapolok luka iserikalei ikatubok akiro ŋun; kokuriakaros nakiirariata ebe eraas ŋul Iromayon; 
Acts16:39 kopotu, kiŋaiŋaata; nakedauniata aitolomun, kilipa kes anyoun kore kaŋol." 
Acts16:40 Konyoutu do kaidaris kolomasi togo loka Ludia: ido kedaut aanyun iinacan, kitalakasi kes, koloto." 
Acts17:1 Nakedauniata aitor Amipipoli ka Apolonia, kodoloto Sesalonika, nekejai atukos naka Iyudayan," 
Acts17:2 Kosodi koloma Paul mama ejaas, kwape kejaar ekepone, kopeta kakes nukiwadikatai asabaton auni." 
Acts17:3 Kikujok kitogogoŋ da ebe ebusakinit Kristo aiticanio ka ajarun kotoma okatwak, ebe da, “Yesu ŋol lokalimonokini yes, ŋes Kristo.”" 
Acts17:4 Kiyuut ice kakesi, kimorikikinos ka Paul ka Sila; ka Iyonanin lukiyaparito luipu noi, ka aŋor da nukapolok numam ikidioko," 
Acts17:5 Konye kilelebun Iyudayan ekolo, koyaŋas ituŋa lueroko luutai, kotukokis ekodet, kigurut ere, kosurokis etogo loka Yason, kokotos aitolomun kes otuŋa," 
Acts17:6 Nakekurwokis adumun kes, kiriasi Yason ka ice koinacan mama ejaas ikapolokitok ere, kiworoto ebe, “Ituŋa lu luabuburiasi akwap adolutu ne da," 
Acts17:7 esukunyiki Yason kes; iswamaete ŋul kere nuesurokinete ikisila luka Kaisar, kobalas ebe, ejai ekabaka ece, loenyaritai Yesu.”" 
Acts17:8 Kiyaloŋoŋoto ekodet ka ikapolokitok ere nakiirariata ŋun," 
Acts17:9 Kosodete nakedauniata aitelemun Yason ka ikepaup aititiŋet, koosikis kes alosit." 
Acts17:10 Atipet kijukasi iinacan Paul ka Sila Beroea kuare; nakedolioto ŋina kolomasi atukos naka lyudayan. 
Acts17:11 Konye kejokuka lu aitelekarit luko Sesalonika, naarai apotu kocamut akirot kitauon luekapakina, koŋicenenata nuiwadikatai ŋinipaaran ajenun arai ikote akiro ŋun nen," 
Acts17:12 Kanuka ŋun kiyuut luipu kakesi, ka aŋor nuYonanin nusotia ka ikiliok da lumam ikidioko." 
Acts17:13 Konye kejenut Iyudayan luko Sesalonika ebe elimonokini Paul akirot naka Edeke koBeroea da, kopotu nen da kisidikoto kigurut ikodeta." 
Acts17:14 Kosodi atipet kijukasi iinacan Paul alosit adolore aŋolol, konye kosalata Sila ka Timoteo nen." 
Acts17:15 Konye lukinyamakinete Paul koyaŋaasi kiton Asene; kosodete kicorakinai alimokin Sila ka Timoteo abunore mama ejai atipet kwape epedoriata, koloto." 
Acts17:16 Kosodi nakejaar Paul Asene idaret kes, koriebakin eketau nakeanyunia ere ileleba aputosia." 
Acts17:17 Kwaŋin kopetanak lyudayan ka Iukeyoŋito Edeke akiro kotoma atukos, ido ŋinipaaran kagwelanaret kaŋul lukiriamununos kaŋes." 
Acts17:18 Ice luka ikaminak acoa luka Ipikurean ka Isitoikin kiriamunos kaŋes, Kobalas ice ebe, “Ekoto kereka ekenerat lo einer anyoika?” Kobalas ice ebe, “Etakani bala elimonokini akiro nuka idekesio lumo.” Naarai kelimonokini Yesu ka ajarun." 
Acts17:19 Kikamut ŋes koyaŋaasi Areopago, kobalas ebe, “Kipedori kereka isio ajenun anyoin aisisianakin na nakitetet nainera ijo?" 
Acts17:20 Naarai iyaŋaut akiro numo akiikosi; asa do kikoto ajenun apolou naka akiro kanu,”" 
Acts17:21 Naarai kemameete luka Asene ka imo lukiboienenete kanen aceswam dimarai aitatam arai aiirar akiro nukitetiak. 
Acts17:22 Kobwo Paul kokidiŋ Areopago, kobala ebe, “Yes ituŋa luka Asene, amisiiki ebe iraas luka edini kakiro kere." 
Acts17:23 Naarai naketoritor, ka aanyun iboro luimaete, abu kadum etem lokiwadikatai akiro nu ebe, ‘LOKA EDEKE LOMAM EJENA.’ Aso kalimonokini yes ŋol loimaete komam ijenete." 
Acts17:24 Edeke lokesubi akwapisinei ka iboro kere luejaas toma, naarai erai ŋesi Ejakait loka akuj ka akwap, mam iboie kabilai nuedukio kakanin," 
Acts17:25 kwabo mam ijaanakinio kakanin nuka ituŋa, bala ipuda idiobore; naarai ŋes elopet einakini kere aijar ka eiyeŋane ka iboro da kere," 
Acts17:26 Kojautene ediopet kosub atekerin kere nuka ituŋa aiboi kakwapin kere, nakedaunia aibwaikin apakio ka iikorun luka aiboisiokec," 
Acts17:27 tetere emoete Edeke, moto erarapete ka adumun ŋes; karaida mam elwana kaneejai ŋinidiopet kaoni," 
Acts17:28 ‘Naarai kotomakeŋ, kijari, kilosi, kijai da’; kwape abalatar ice kokapwakunakakus ebe, ‘Naarai kirai oni aurike.’" 
Acts17:29 Aso naarai kirai oni aur naka Edeke, mam kibusakinit aomit ebe eput Edeke ka esabu, karaida epuesa, karaida amor, iboro luegerio kanuka apirianut ka acoa naka ituŋa." 
Acts17:30 Mam abu Edeke kosesenenei apakio nuka aolit, konye kwana icorakini ituŋa kere luejaas aiboisio kere aisilar:" 
Acts17:31 naarai abu kibwaik apaaran naebunio atubokin akwapin kadolit, kotuŋanan loaseunit; ido itogogoŋit ŋun mama ejaas ituŋa kere, kanuka aitajarun ŋes kokatwak.”" 
Acts17:32 Kosodi nakiirariata nuka ajarun naka ikatwak, kokienatar ice; konye kobalas ice ebe, “Kiirari bobo jo kakiro kaŋun.”" 
Acts17:33 Kosodi konyou Paul kinye kes. 
Acts17:34 Konye kimorikikinos icetuŋa kaŋes, kiyuut; kotomakec kojai Dionusio Eareopagot, ka aberu naenyaritai Damaris, ka icetuŋa da nepepe kaŋul." 
Acts18:1 Kokau kaŋun konyou ko Asene kodol Korinto. 
Acts18:2 Kodum Eyudayat ekekiror Akuila, euriat koPonto, kerai ŋesi abunore ŋipeŋin koItalia nepepe kakeberu Pirisikila, naarai abu Kulaudio kicorakinite Iyudayan kere anyoun koRome. Kodol Paul mama ejaas;" 
Acts18:3 naarai kerai akeceswam adiopet, kosal mamakec, kiswamata nepepe, naarai keraas ikasubak iweman." 
Acts18:4 Kopetanak akiro katukos ŋinisabato, kotam aimaumaun Iyudayan ka Iyonanin." 
Acts18:5 Konye nakijesunotor Sila ka Timoteo koMakedonia, kitiŋaik akirot Paul, kitejenanak lyudayan ebe Yesu ŋes Kristo." 
Acts18:6 Nakitepegiata ka ainyanakin Edeke, kilakilak inapeneke, kotema kes atiar, “Kojaas aokotokus akwesikus; alai eoŋ; amear kwana alosi mama ejaas Imo.”" 
Acts18:7 Konyou kanen, koloma togo loka etuŋanan ekekiror Tito Yusito, loemai Edeke, lokeapias eketogo katukos." 
Acts18:8 Abu Kirisipo ekayaiton loka atukos kiyuu Ejakait, nepepe ka lukokaleke kere; nakiirariata Ikorinton luipu Paul kiyuut, kibatisai." 
Acts18:9 Kolimok Ejakait Paul kaitapoet kuare ebe, “Sirikikurianar, konye kiner, sirikililiŋ;" 
Acts18:10 naarai ajai eoŋ nenipe kajo, kwabo emamei ituŋanan yenikisurokini aitican; naarai ejaas eoŋ ituŋa luipu ore lo.”" 
Acts18:11 Kosalak nen apak naka ekaru ediopet ka ilapio ikanykape, isisianakini kes akirot naka Edeke." 
Acts18:12 Konye nakeraar Galio ekayaiton loko Akaia, konyoikis Iyudayan Paul ketau ediopet, koyaata airabis." 
Acts18:13 Kobalas ebe, “Ijodijodi ekesa lo ituŋa aima Edeke asurokin ikisila.”" 
Acts18:14 Konye nakekotor Paul aooŋ akeituk, kotema Galio Iyudayan atiar, “Wu yes Iyudayan, arai erai akirot naka aswam aronis arai naka adiakaret naerono, tikebusakinit atitiŋikin kayes;" 
Acts18:15 konye arai erai akirot naka aiŋiseta nuka akiro ka ikiroria ka ikisilakus, nukus bo ŋun; mam eoŋ akoto araut ekatubon kaŋun.”" 
Acts18:16 Kireŋea kes kairabis. 
Acts18:17 Kikamutu kere Sosetene, ekayaiton loka atukos, koleata kairabis. Konye mam Galio apodo ŋun." 
Acts18:18 Kokau kaŋun kosalak Paul apaarasia nuipu, kosodi kotwar iinacan, kikwaŋar alosit Suria, kouparos ka Pirisikila ka Akuila. Kobaren akekou koKenekerea, naarai kiyapot." 
Acts18:19 Kodoloto Epeso, kinye kes kaŋina; konye koloma ŋesi elopet atukos, kopeta ka Iyudayan akiro." 
Acts18:20 Nakilipiata ŋes asalakin apak naepol, koŋer;" 
Acts18:21 konye kotwaras kakes kobala ebe, “Aboŋuni bobo mama ijaas arai itoiokit Edeke.” Kikwaŋa anyoun ko Epeso." 
Acts18:22 Nakedokunia Kaisarea, kodoka kiyoga ekanisa, kijesar Antiokia." 
Acts18:23 Kosalak nen adiopak, kosodi konyou, kitor anatar akwapin nuka Galatia, ka Pirugia, itogogoŋi ikesisiak kere." 
Acts18:24 Kobu Eyudayat Epeso, ekekiror Apolo, euriat loka Alegesanderia, etuŋanan loisisianakinitai; kerai lokapedor kotoma nukiwadikatai." 
Acts18:25 Aponi kituutooritete korot loka Ejakait; kodunyakinite komoyo, kinera kisisianakini kacoit akiro nuka Yesu, konye kojeni aibatis naka Yokana bon." 
Acts18:26 Kogeu einer katitiŋ katukos; konye nakiirariata Pirisikila ka Akuila, koyaŋaasi ŋes, kiyatakis aitejenun kacoit erot loka Edeke." 
Acts18:27 Nakekotor aikwaŋar alosit Akaia, kisicerededata iinacan, kiwadikakis ikesisiak aisukunyikin ŋes, Nakedolio, kiŋarak noi ŋul lukiyuunito kanuka asianut," 
Acts18:28 naarai kiteleka Iyudayan kagogoŋ, kaitebeikin, itodikini kakiro nukiwadikatai ebe Yesu ŋes Kristo." 
Acts19:1 Nakejaar Apolo Korinto, kitor Paul akwap naimukurur, kodol Epeso. Kodum ikesisiak ice kaŋina," 
Acts19:2 Kiŋit kes atiar, “Ipotu kereka ko dumut Emoyo Lokalaunan nakiyuuniata?” Kobalas ebe, “Mam, karaida aiirarit ebe ejai Emoyo Lokalaunan.”" 
Acts19:3 Kotema atiar, “Aso kibatisatai yes aibatis anyoin?” Kotemasi atiar, “Aibatis naka Yokana.”" 
Acts19:4 Kotema Paul atiar, “Abu Yokana kibatis kaibatis naka aitoronikin, elimonokin ituŋa aiyuun loebunit kokaukeŋ ŋes Yesu.”" 
Acts19:5 Nakiirariata ŋun, kibatisaunos kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu." 
Acts19:6 Kosodi nakedaunia Paul aidokokin kes akekanin, kodoik kes Emoyo Lokalaunan; kinerata kaŋajepa, ka aidwar." 
Acts19:7 Keraas kere bala ituŋa itomon ka luarei. 
Acts19:8 Koloma Paul atukos, kinerenena katitiŋ ilapio iuni, epesi akiro kituŋa kiyamuyam kes toma akiro nuka ajakanut naka Edeke." 
Acts19:9 Konye ice lueninik kogiroto aiyuun, kinerasi nueroko nuka Erot kakonyen nuka ekodet, kosodi kinyek kes, kogita ikesisiak, kopegenenas ka ituŋa ŋinipaaran kosomero loka Turano." 
Acts19:10 Kiyatanakinos akiro ŋun apak naka ikar iarei; kiton lukiboiete kere koAsia aiirar akirot naka Ejakait, Iyudayan ka Iyonanin da." 
Acts19:11 Kiswama Edeke nukaumokin nuedeparito kakanin nuka Paul," 
Acts19:12 kiton ayaŋaar iitabalan ka inapen kakuanake mama ejaas ikadekak, konyout adekesia kamakec, kolomut da ajokin nueroko kamakec." 
Acts19:13 Konye koŋasikinos ice koYudayan lukerimok, ikereŋeak ajokin, alimor ekiror loka Yesu mama ejaas lukejaas aiokin nueroko, kobalas ebe, “Kecorak yes kanuka Yesu loelimonokini Paul.”" 
Acts19:14 Kosodi kojaas idwe ikanykaarei luka Sekeba esasedoti lopeti loYudayat, lukiswamaenenete ŋun." 
Acts19:15 Konye Koboŋok kes ajokit naerono ebe, “Ajeni Yesu, ajeni Paul da; konye yes lukaŋai?”" 
Acts19:16 Kosomakin kes etuŋanan lokejai ajokit naerono, kiteleka kes kere, kipiko, tape ekerete kotogo kaŋol imujalalas, imusuŋitai," 
Acts19:17 Kojenut ŋun kere Iyudayan ka Iyonanin lukiboiete ko Epeso; kirum akurian kes kere; kitopolooroi da ekiror loka Ejakait Yesu. 
Acts19:18 Kopotu luipu da kaŋul luiyuunito, kolimosi, kilepilepata da akeceswamisio." 
Acts19:19 Ka ituŋa luipu kaŋul lukiswamaete nukamurwonut, kotukonokis ikeceitabon, kicweata kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere; kimarata etiaikec, kodumut ebe edolit atutubeta alukumin akaisakany nuka epuesa." 
Acts19:20 Kwaŋin kopoloor akirot naka Ejakait, kitelekarit kagogoŋ." 
Acts19:21 Kedaunos akiro ŋun kolosik Paul Komoyo aitor Makedonia ka Akaia alosit Yerusalem, kobala ebe, “Kadau ajaut ŋina, kebusakinit aanyun Rome da.”" 
Acts19:22 Kiyakia iarei kokejaanakinakake alosit Makedonia, kes Timoteo ka Erasito, kosalak ŋes elopet Asia apak." 
Acts19:23 Kapak kaŋin kodakun aigurun namere naedit kanuka Erot. 
Acts19:24 Naarai etuŋanan ekekiror Demeterio ekatatan epuesa, lokesubenenei abilai nuka epuesa nuka Aratemi, lokedumanakini ikeswamak luepiriaka ameda naepol;" 
Acts19:25 kotukonoki ŋul nepepe ka ikeswamak ice luka aswam kaŋin, kobala kes ebe, “Ikatuŋa, iienete yesi ebe kidumuni abarawok kotoma aswam kana." 
Acts19:26 Bobo da ianyut, iirarete da ebe, mere koEpeso bon, konye eapie toma Asia kere, ejodijod Paul lo ituŋa luipu ka aijulakin akeceomisio, ebala ebe ŋulluiswamao kakanin mam eraas idekesio:" 
Acts19:27 mere atemar ebe aswamuwok na bon emwaŋio, konye eyekalu da loka adeke nakapolon Aratemi mam imario araut ibore, ebuni aitisilio kapolouke, ŋin naemaete luko Asia kere ka akwapisinei da.”" 
Acts19:28 Nakiirariata ŋun konyunyurikinos, kiworoto kobalas ebe, “Aratemi naka Ipeson ŋes nakapolon!”" 
Acts19:29 Kilelebun ere ecelet; komotaros ketau ediopet alomar alaro naka aboliasio, kedaut aikamun Gaio ka Arisitariko, ituŋa luko Makedonia, lukeupas ka Paul kalositeke." 
Acts19:30 Kokoto Paul alomar otuŋa, kisimika ikesisiak." 
Acts19:31 Ikapolok ice da luka Asia, lukeraas ikepapero kiyakiasi mamakeŋ, kiŋaiŋaata ŋes kinyek alomar alaro naka aboliasio," 
Acts19:32 Aso kiworoto ice ace, ka ice da ace; naarai kitolutoluno ekodet; naarai luipu kakesi mam kejenete akirot naeinakinit kes atukokin." 
Acts19:33 Kolemut Alegesanda kotoma okodet, lokisibwoete Iyudayan kakonyen nuka ituŋa. Kokwetu Alegesanda kakanike, kokoto apurokin kakonyen nuka ituŋa." 
Acts19:34 Konye nakejenuniata ebe erai ŋesi Eyudayat, kiworoto kere keporoto ediopet bala apak naka isawan iarei ebe, “Aratemi naka Ipeson ŋes nakapolon!”" 
Acts19:35 Nakedaunia ekewadikan loka ere aisiyamikin ekodet, kobala ebe, “Okwe ikatuŋa luko Epeso, iŋai bo ituŋanan yenimam ejeni ebe, erai ere loka Epeso ekedaran loka eyekalu loka Aratemi nakapolon, ka loka aput nakedouni kokuju?" 
Acts19:36 Aso naarai mam epedorio aiŋer akiro ŋun, ibusakinit yes aiyamakin, komam isunyito akirot," 
Acts19:37 Naarai iyaut ituŋa lu ne lumam ekokoto iboro luka eyekalu, karaida ainyanakin adekewok." 
Acts19:38 Aso arai ejaas Demeterio ka ikeswamak ice ipaupake akiro nuiwosaete kituŋanan, ejai airabet, ejaas da ikayaitok; kiwosakinos." 
Acts19:39 Konye arai imootos acekirot, itemonokinio katukot naduc." 
Acts19:40 Naarai kija toma aronis aiwosao kanuka ecelet loka lolo, loemamei akirot; ido kotoma akirot kana mam kipedori aitojok atukokin na.”" 
Acts19:41 Kedau einer ŋun kotwar atukot. 
Acts20:1 Kinapakin ailoŋiloŋa, konyarau Paul ikesisiak, kicor, kotwar kes, konyou kolot Makedonia," 
Acts20:2 Nakedaunia aitor atutubeta ŋun, ka aitalakar kakiro nuipu, kodol Yonan." 
Acts20:3 Kosalak nen ilapio iuni, ido nakineruniata Iyudayan asurokin ŋes edwar aikwaŋar alosit Suria, kopeleik aboŋor korot loko Makedonia." 
Acts20:4 Kouparos kituŋa kalu, Sopater loka Beroea, okoku loka Puro, ka Arisitariko ka Sekundo Isesalonikan; ka Gaio loka Derube, ka Timoteo; ka Tukiko ka Toropimo luko Asia." 
Acts20:5 Konye keliŋara ituŋa ŋul, kidareut sio koTiroa," 
Acts20:6 kekwaŋaros isio anyoun koPilipi akaulo kapaarasia nuka imugatin lumam itubuunitoi, kadolokis kes koTiroa kalosit naka apaarasia akany; kasalakis nen apaarasia akanykaarei." 
Acts20:7 Kapaaran nasodit nakasabato, nakiriamunor tetere kibili emugati, kiner Paul kakes, apele alosit apaaran naatupakini; kiyatak einerike kiton kidiŋebai." 
Acts20:8 Kojaas atalai nuipu kagola nakokuju kama kitukokina. 
Acts20:9 Iboie etelepat ekekiror Eutuko kadirisa; kilurutu noi ajo; kiyatakinit Paul noi alimonokin, kipikosi ajo, kibiror kwap kagola nakiwuniet, kodakunai etwanit." 
Acts20:10 Konye kodoka Paul kokukum kamake, kotun, kobala ebe, “Sirikiyaloŋoŋoto; naarai eroko ŋesi ejari.”" 
Acts20:11 Kodoka bobo kuju, kobil emugati, konyam, kiyatak einer kakes apak naepol, kiton tupuruc, kosodi kolot." 
Acts20:12 Koyaut etelepat ejari, kolakara alakara naepol." 
Acts20:13 Konye sio kaliŋa alosit ataker, kekwaŋaros kiton Assos, kamunos aitodokun Paul ataker kaŋina; naarai kitemokinit ŋesi kwaŋin, komuno ŋes; aitorit neeonit," 
Acts20:14 Nakiriamunor Assos, ketodokutu ŋes ataker, kasodete kadoloto Mitulene," 
Acts20:15 Kekwaŋaros anyoun kaŋina kadolo apaaran nakiareit aibois naetereikina ka Kios; apaaran da naatupakini kabwoutu koSamos, ka naatupakini ŋin kadoloto Mileto." 
Acts20:16 Naarai abu Paul kitojokite ainac Epeso tetere mam itumor kotoma Asia; naarai kemarani arai epedori adolore Yerusalem eroko apaaran naka Pentekote edolo," 
Acts20:17 Nakejaar Mileto kiyakik anyaraun imakio luka ekanisa koEpeso," 
Acts20:18 Nakedolunioto mamakeŋ, kotema kes atiar, “Ijenete yesi kwape keboienenoo kayes apak kere ageun kapaaran kanasodit naadolio Asia," 
Acts20:19 ejaanakinenei Ejakait kaitasono kere, ka akiyo, ka acoduneta nukadoikinete kobotei luka Iyudayan," 
Acts20:20 mam abu kenac alimonokin yes akirot kere naeyaun aiokis, kesisianakinenei yes kaitebeikin, ido kaŋolitog," 
Acts20:21 etejenuni lyudayan ka Iyonanin da nuka aitoronikin mama ejai Edeke ka aiyuun da Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo," 
Acts20:22 Aso kwana, koany, alosi Yerusalem, kaenitai komoyo, mam ajeni akiro nukadoikinete kaŋina," 
Acts20:23 dimarai ketejenuni Emoyo Lokalaunan kaŋolire ebe kedareto aeneta ka areio. 
Acts20:24 Konye mam apodo akaijar araun naketiai kamakaŋ, dimikito kaŋetak akaigerosit ka aijaanakin nakadumuni kama ejai Ejakait Yesu, aitejenun Akiro Nukajokak nuka asianut naka Edeke." 
Acts20:25 Aso kwana, koany, ajeni eoŋ ebe yes kere lukerimorit alimonokin ajakanut naka Edeke mam bobo ianyunete akakonyen," 
Acts20:26 Kanuka ŋun ketejenuni yes lolo ebe mam akusiwokot kabeikinete eoŋ," 
Acts20:27 naarai mam abu kenac alimonokin yes ainerun kere naka Edeke. 
Acts20:28 Kocoito yesi, ka esipan da kere loadakaki Emoyo Lokalaunan yes araut ikaanyanarak, tetere icokiete ekanisa loka Edeke, lokikurauni kakeokot elopet." 
Acts20:29 Ajeni ebe kanyou eoŋ epote ipeen luededeŋ mamakus, mam itimete esipan;" 
Acts20:30 bobo da enyounete kotomakus ikiliok luineras nuitapaarete airiar ikesisiak atupar kes. 
Acts20:31 Asokokwenyete, kiitunitos ebe ikar iuni mam abu kenyek aicor ŋinituŋanan paaran ka kuar kakiyo." 
Acts20:32 Kwana da ketitiŋ yes Edeke, ka akirot naka akesianut naepedori aiduk yes ka ainakin da airumet nepepe kaŋul kere luitalaunitai." 
Acts20:33 Mam abu kemiela epuesa karaida esabu karaida inapen luka ituŋanan. 
Acts20:34 Ijenete yesi ebe akakanin nu apotu kiswamata nukeipudika, ka loka ŋul kalukija nepepe keoŋ." 
Acts20:35 Kotoma akiro kere ketodik yes ebe kaitaaritoi naikoni nen ibusakinit aiŋarakin luekalanyaka, kaiitunite akiro nuka Ejakait Yesu, nukebala ebe, ‘Ainakin erai nakarereŋ adepar adumun.’ ”" 
Acts20:36 Nakedaunia einer ŋun kokukokin kilip nepepe kakes kere. 
Acts20:37 Komonyata noi kere, kotunata Paul konuata," 
Acts20:38 Ekadakinitos noi kanuka akirot ŋin nakinera ebe mam bobo eanyunete akekonyen. Kinyamakis do kiton ataker. 
Acts21:1 Kosodi kanen nakidaunia atwarakin, kekwaŋaros kiderit kadoloto Kos, apaaran da naatupakini kadoloto Rodo, kanyout kanen kadolo Patara." 
Acts21:2 Kadumutu ataker naekoto aikwaŋar kiton Poenike, kadokasi, kekwaŋaros." 
Acts21:3 Nakianyunia Kupuro kipou kenyeisi ŋes kakan nakokediany, kediata kiton Suria, kadokutu koTuro; naarai nen kekotor ataker alemario iboro lueleleba." 
Acts21:4 Kiidau amoun ikesisiak, kasalakis nen apaarasia akanykaarei. Kolimokis kesi Paul kanuka Emoyo ebe sirikedoka Yerusalem." 
Acts21:5 Kosodi kedaunos apaarasiakosi kanen, kanyoutu kasodokinete; apotu ituŋa kere, nepepe kaŋorokec ka idwekec kinyamakis sio kiton kiŋa naka ere; kakukokinos oitolima kelipa kasodete katwarakinos." 
Acts21:6 Kadokas isio ataker, koboŋosi do kesi orekec." 
Acts21:7 Kasodete nakidaunia alositekosi anyoun koTuro, kadoloto Pitolomai; keyogata iinacan kasalata mamakec apaaran adiopet." 
Acts21:8 Tupuruc kanyoutu kadoloto Kaisarea; kalomasi togo loka Pilipo ekalimonokinan, lokerai ediopet kokanykaarei, kasalata mamake." 
Acts21:9 Kejaas ŋol apesur aoŋon abekon, nukeraas akadwarak." 
Acts21:10 Nakisalitor nen apaarasia nuipu, kodoku enabi ekekiror Agabo anyoun koYudaya." 
Acts21:11 Nakedolunio mamakosi kolem amuny naka Paul, koen elopet akekeje ka akekanin, kotema atiar, “Ebala Emoyo Lokalaunan kwanata ebe, Kwape kwaŋin eeniata Iyudayan luko Yerusalem elopet amuny na, ijaikinete da akanin nuka Imo.”" 
Acts21:12 Nakiiraria ŋun, isio ka ituŋa luka aibois kaŋin, keŋaiŋaata ŋes sirikedoka Yerusalem." 
Acts21:13 Kosodi Koboŋok Paul ebe, “Anyoika iswamaete yesi, aimony ka aibil ekatau? Naarai akapakina mere aenio bon, konye atwanare da kotoma Yerusalem, kanuka ekiror loka Ejakait Yesu.”" 
Acts21:14 Nakegirio akosiiŋaiŋa, kapalutu do kabalas ebe, “Nuekoto Ejakait kiswamai.”" 
Acts21:15 Akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun, ketemokisi ikosiboro kadokasi kiton Yerusalem." 
Acts21:16 Kouparos ice kokesisiak luko Kaisarea kasio, koyaŋaasi sio ore loka Menason loko Kupuro, ekesisian lokolo sek, lokipejoi mamakeŋ." 
Acts21:17 Nakidolio Yerusalem kisukunyikis iinacan sio kaiyalama. 
Acts21:18 Kapaaran naatupakini koloma Paul nepepe kasio mama ka Yakob; kojaas da imakio kere. 
Acts21:19 Akaulo kayogan kes, kitatam kisudunyite akiro kere nukiswamai Edeke kama ka Imo kotoma aijaanakinike." 
Acts21:20 Nakiirariata, kituroto Edeke. Kotemasi ŋes atiar, “Onacekosi, iany kwape imwaatar ilukumin luka Iyudayan luiyuunito, irumit kes kere ekokote kanuka ikisila," 
Acts21:21 elimonokinitai kes nukon ebe isisianakini Iyudayan kere luejaas Omo ainyein Musa, ilimonokini kes ebe sirikekepata ikecedwe karaida atupit iponesio." 
Acts21:22 Aso ikwaikinio bo do ai? Abeit epupunete ebe ibu ijo. 
Acts21:23 Aso kiswama nukilimokini jo, Ejaas sio ikiliok iwoŋon lueenit aiyaposit;" 
Acts21:24 koyaŋa ituŋa lu, kitalaun nepepe kakes, kotacak kes tetere ebarenete akwesikec. Kojenut ituŋa kere ebe akiro kwa nukelimonokinitai kanukon mam ebeito, konye jo elopet iricit aitodol ikisila." 
Acts21:25 Konye kanuka Imo luiyuunito, kipou kewadikata ebalua katubito ebe kinaca kesi iboro lueinakinio aputosia araut asuban, ka aokot, ka itiaŋ luemiedio, ka adoteu.”" 
Acts21:26 Kosodi Paul ayaŋaar ikiliok ŋul, kitalaun elopet nepepe kakes apaaran naatupakini, koloma oyekalu, aitejenun apak naitodolikinere apaarasia nuka aitesegaario naeinakinere asubanit kanuka ŋolidiopet kakesi." 
Acts21:27 Keapuut apaarasia akanykaarei aŋetakin, koanyut lyudayan lukepote koAsia ŋes koyekalu, kisidikoto ekodet kere, kikamutu ŋes," 
Acts21:28 kocelut ebe, “Yes ikiliok luka Isirael, kiŋarakinai sio! Lo ŋes etuŋanan loisisianakini ituŋa kere kaiboisio kere asurokin atekerewok ka ikisila ka aibois na da; ido da ayau ŋesi Iyonanin toma oyekalu, amunaa aibois na nakalaunan.”" 
Acts21:29 Naarai keanyunitos Toropimo Epesot nepepe kaŋes kore, koomitos da ebe ayau Paul ŋes toma oyekalu." 
Acts21:30 Kosodi kibwaa ere kere, kokerut ituŋa; kikamutu Paul kibwosasi kiŋa keyekalu, atipet kogolokinoi ikekia." 
Acts21:31 Nakemoototor epone loaret, kodolokis akiro ekapolon loka erioŋet ebe enyalinyalun Yerusalem kere." 
Acts21:32 Atipet kolem iserikalei ka ikapolokitokokec, koker mamakec; kosodete nakeanyuniata ekapolon ka iserikalei kinyeis aibuŋa Paul." 
Acts21:33 Kosodi koapik ekapolon kikam ŋes, kicorak aenio kirikoi iarei, Kiŋit ebe, “Iŋai bo lo?” ido ebe, “Anyoika eswama?”" 
Acts21:34 Kocelas ice kokodet ace, ka ice da ace; namam kepedoria ajenun akiro kanuka ecelet, kicorak ayaŋaario ore loka iserikalei." 
Acts21:35 Nakedolio adoketa kodakasi ŋes iserikalei kanuka agogoŋ naka ekodet; 
Acts21:36 naarai ketupit ekodet loka ituŋa luipu, ecelasi, kobalas ebe, “Kicutasi ŋes!”" 
Acts21:37 Konye napedwar kes aitolomar ŋes orekec, kiŋit Paul ekapolon ebe, “Ibus kereka eoŋ alimokin jo akirot?” Kobala ŋesi ebe, “Ijeni tope ijo Ayonanin?" 
Acts21:38 Mere kereka ijo Emisiriat je, loitonyounit pac ituŋa ilukumin iwoŋon lukenyaritai Ikaarak, kiŋarenik amodiŋ?”" 
Acts21:39 Koboŋok Paul ebe, “Arai eoŋ Eyudayat, loko Taruso kotoma Kilikia, lokore lomere loedit; keŋaiŋait, kisiikinai kener kituŋa kalu.”" 
Acts21:40 Kisiik ŋes, kosodi kobwo Paul kadoketa, kokwet ituŋa; kojau aililiŋ tiiti, kiner kakes kaŋajep nAburaniat, ebe:" 
Acts22:1 “Yes ikiliok iinacan ka lukapapaka, kiirarai kwana nuenera aiiyaror.”" 
Acts22:2 Nakiirariata ebe inera kakes kaŋajep nAburaniat, kiyatakis aililiŋ tii. Kobala ebe:" 
Acts22:3 “Arai eoŋ Eyudayat, kaurikinio Taruso, koKilikia, konye kasaunio kore kalo kakeje nuka Gamaliel, kesisianakinio kainyikokin kokisila luka lukapapaawok, abu kerumite ekokote kanuka Edeke kwape ijaatar yesi kere lolo." 
Acts22:4 Kareite ituŋa luka Erot kala kiton atwanare, kaenenei karemonokin aidaris ikiliok ka aŋor da," 
Acts22:5 kwape itejenikina esasedoti lopeti ka imakio kere luka aurianet, Abu kadum ibaluan kamakec ainar iinacan, kalot Damasiko tetere ekamuni luejaas ŋina da, ka ayaun kes Yerusalem eenitai tetere iticanio." 
Acts22:6 “Kosodi kanen napalosi, aapikin Damasiko, kidiŋ paaran, atipet kemiliaik aica naepol naabuni kokuju." 
Acts22:7 Kebirokin kwap, keira eporoto lokabala eoŋ ebe, ‘Saul, Saul, kanukinyo kireitor eoŋ?’" 
Acts22:8 Kaboŋok ebe, ‘Ijoŋo iŋai, Ejakait?’ Kabala ebe, ‘Arai eoŋ Yesu Enasarayot, loireit ijo.’" 
Acts22:9 Ŋul da lukejaas keoŋ apotu koanyut aica ŋin, konye mam apotu kiiras eporoto loka ŋol kalokinera keoŋ." 
Acts22:10 Kabala ebe, ‘Keswama anyoika, Ejakait?’ Katema Ejakait eoŋ atiar, ‘Konyou, koloma Damasiko, kanen kilimokinio kere nuitemokinitoi jo aswam.’" 
Acts22:11 Konye namam apedoritor aanyun kanuka amwekimwek naka aica kaŋin, karikosi eoŋ ŋul lukejaas keoŋ, kaloma Damasiko." 
Acts22:12 Kanen Anania, etuŋanan loeyoŋit Edeke kwape ejaatar ikisila, loetojokitai koYudayan kere lukiboiete kanen," 
Acts22:13 kobu mamakaŋ, kobwo kodiekaŋ kabala ebe, ‘Onaceka Saul, kokweny.’ Ido kosawa kaŋol abu kakweny kaany ŋes." 
Acts22:14 Kobala ŋesi ebe, ‘Kiseu jo Edeke loka lukapapaawok tetere ijenuni nuekoto ŋesi, ka aanyun da Ekadoliton, apupun eporoto loelomuni kaitukuke;" 
Acts22:15 naarai iraun ekekajenan kotuŋa kere kakiro kaŋun nuiany ka nuiiraa da. 
Acts22:16 Aso kwana idaret inyo? Konyou, kibatisai, kilota akonidiakanareta, kiwonete ekekiror.’" 
Acts22:17 “Kosodi kanen nakadaunia aboŋun Yerusalem, elipi koyekalu, kogelakin ekamoyo," 
Acts22:18 Abu kaany ŋes, katema eoŋ atiar, ‘Kisunyite, konyou atipet koYerusalem, naarai mam ecamunete akoniitejenun kamakaŋ.’" 
Acts22:19 Kabala ebe, ‘Ejakait, ejenete kesi ebe abu eoŋ kaenenenei ka aibuŋ da ŋul lukiyuunito jo kaŋinitukos kere." 
Acts22:20 Naabukorere da aokot nuka Sitepan ekajenanikon, ajai eoŋ da abwoi eapie, ketojokite, kedari inapen luka lukearete ŋes.’" 
Acts22:21 Katema eoŋ atiar, ‘Ape; naarai keyakiari jo neelwana mama ejaas Imo.’ ”" 
Acts22:22 Apotu kopupokis ŋes kiton akirot ŋin; kosodete kodelosi kiworoto ebe, “Kicutasi oloŋai ŋol kakwap. Naarai mam ibus ŋes aijar.”" 
Acts22:23 Napecelasi, ka acakanar ikecenapen ka aiwelanar da apua kuju," 
Acts22:24 kicorak ekapolon aitolomar ŋes ore loka iserikalei, kotema ŋes aŋicio kadaio, tetere ejenuni nuainakinit kes ecelas kwaŋin kanukeŋ," 
Acts22:25 Nakedauniata aien ŋes kaunoi, kobala Paul ekapolokiton lokebwoi eapie ebe, “Ibus kereka yes aida etuŋanan loerai Eromayot komam etubokinitai?”" 
Acts22:26 Nakiiraria ekapolokiton kolot kitejen ekapolon kobala ebe, “Nunyoika ikoto ijo aswam? Naarai erai etuŋanan ŋol Eromayot.”" 
Acts22:27 Kobu ekapolon kiŋit ŋes ebe, “Kolimokinai, irai teni ijo Eromayot?” Kobala ebe, “Eebo.”" 
Acts22:28 Koboŋok ekapolon ebe, “Abu eoŋ kagwel araut Eromayot karupian nuipu.” Kobala Paul ebe, “Konye eoŋ euriat.”" 
Acts22:29 Atipet kobwata lukekapakina aiŋit ŋes; kokuriana ekapolon da, naarai ajenu ebe erai Eromayot ido abu koen ŋes." 
Acts22:30 Apaaran naatupakini, kokoto ajenun abeit nuainakinete Iyudayan aosan ŋes, kolacak, kicorak isasedotin lupeti ka aurianet kere atukokin, koyanau Paul da kisibwo ŋes kakonyenekec." 
Acts23:1 Kikesite Paul akonye kaurianet, kobala ebe, “Ikiliok iinacan, abu kajar kakonyen nuka Edeke ketau kaloejok kiton lolo.”" 
Acts23:2 Kicorak Anania losasedoti lopeti lukebwoete aapu kaŋes aibap ŋes akeituk. 
Acts23:3 Kosodi Paul atemar ŋes atiar, “Kibapi jo Edeke, ijo arwatat naiworiworitai kakwanis! Iboikin kereka ijo atubokin eoŋ kwape ejaatar ikisila, kwabo icorak eoŋ aibapio aitegelikin ikisila?”" 
Acts23:4 Kobalas lukebwoete aapu kaŋes ebe, “Ijo ba, imoromoroi kereka esasedoti lopeti loka Edeke?”" 
Acts23:5 Kotema Paul atiar, “Iinacan, mam ajeni ebe erai esasedoti lopeti; naarai iwadikatai ebe, ‘Sirikiner erono mama ejai ekayaiton loka ikonituŋa.’”" 
Acts23:6 Konye nakejenunia Paul ebe atutubet adiopet kerai naka Isadukayon, ka nace da naka Iparisayon, kiworo kaurianet ebe, “Ikiliok iinacan, arai eoŋ Eparisayot, okoku loka Iparisayon; katubokinitai eoŋ kanuka amun naka ajarun naka ikatwak.”" 
Acts23:7 Nakedaunia einer ŋun, kojau epeget kidiŋ Iparisayon ka Isadukayon; kotiaka atukot," 
Acts23:8 Naarai ebalas Isadukayon ebe emamei ajarun, karaida emalaika, karaida emoyo; konye ecamunito Iparisayon ŋun kere." 
Acts23:9 Kojau ecelet loepol; kobwaata ikewadikak ice owai loka Iparisayon, koutasi kobalas ebe, “Mam sio kidumuni adiokirot naerono kotuŋanan kalo. Arai bo emoyo inera kaŋes, arai bo emalaika?”" 
Acts23:10 Kiyatakin ecelet apoloor, kokurianar ekapolon ebe enyilinyiliete kesi Paul, kicorak iserikalei adokun ka alemun ŋes kagogoŋ kakaninikec, ainyakar da ore loka iserikalei." 
Acts23:11 Kakuare kaŋin kobwo Ejakait aapu kaŋes, kobala ebe, “Kotitiŋior, naarai kwape itejenunia nukaŋ koYerusalem, kwape kwaŋin ibusakinit ijo aitejenun ko Rome da.”" 
Acts23:12 Nakiwala akwap, kitutuko Iyudayan, koenikinos kaiyaposit ebe mam enyamete karaida aimat kiton neaariata Paul." 
Acts23:13 Lukiyapoikinete kwaŋin emwaasi ituŋa akaisaoŋon ka adepar da. 
Acts23:14 Koloto kesi mama ejaas isasedotin lupeti ka imakio, kotemasi atiar, “Kienikin noi kaiyaposit ebe mam kiiri ibore kiton nekiaria Paul." 
Acts23:15 Aso do kwana, kikwenyasi yesi ka aurianet ekapolon ayaŋaun Paul mama ijaas, bala ikotosi ajenun kotenan akekiro, Kikapakina isio da aiar ŋes eriŋa eekuna die.”" 
Acts23:16 Kiira ecen loka Paul nuka aperunikec; kolot koloma ore loka iserikalei, kolimok Paul." 
Acts23:17 Konyarau Paul ekapolokiton ediopet kotemaatiar, “Koyaŋa etelepat lo mama ejai ekapolon; naarai ejai akirot naelimokini ŋes.”" 
Acts23:18 Kanuka ŋun koyaŋa ŋes, kitoloma neejai ekapolon, kobala ebe, “Abu Paul ŋol eenat kanyara eoŋ, kelip aitolomun etelepat lo mamakon, naarai ejai akirot naineras kajo.”" 
Acts23:19 Kitiŋ ekapolon akekan kogitaros kaŋes, kiŋit kaiyeiyea ebe, “Anyoin akirot naikoto ijo alimokin eoŋ?”" 
Acts23:20 Kobala ebe, “Enerut Iyudayan aiŋitun jo aitodokar Paul moi toma aurianet, bala ekotos aiŋitiŋit kotenan akekiro." 
Acts23:21 Aso siri jo kicam; naarai eperunito ŋes ituŋa luedeparito akaisaoŋon kakesi, luaenikinos kaiyaposit ebe mam enyamete karaida aimat kiton neaariata ŋes; aso kwana ekapakina kesi, idaretos akoniisumunet.”" 
Acts23:22 Kosodi kotwar ekapolon etelepat, kicoro ebe, “Sirikilimok idiotuŋanan ebe kikwenyarit eoŋ.”" 
Acts23:23 Kosodi konyarau ikapolokitok iarei, kobala ebe, “Kitemokis iserikalei akwat aarei, ka ikebwanenok akaisakanykaarei, ka lukakwaras da akwat aarei, alosit kiton Kaisarea, osawa lokiwuniet loka akuar." 
Acts23:24 Kitemokis itiaŋ lukisibwaneno Paul da, koyaŋaasi ŋes mama ejai Pelikis ekayaiton eiyara.”" 
Acts23:25 Kiwadik ebalua kepone kalota: 
Acts23:26 “Kulaudio Lusia mama ejai ekayaiton lokaibuses Pelikis, ayogan." 
Acts23:27 Ikamunito Iyudayan etuŋanan lo, aapikinito aiar ŋes, kabunok kes nepepe ka iserikalei, kayu, kajenu ebe erai Eromayot." 
Acts23:28 Kakoto ajenun akirot naeosatotor, ketodoka aurianetekec." 
Acts23:29 Kadum ebe kiwosatai kanuka aiŋiseta nuka ikisilakec, kwabo mam kiwosatai adiokirot kere naibusakinitor aaria karaida aenia." 
Acts23:30 Kosodi nakapukokinere ebe ejaun ebotet loebilakinete ekiliokit lo, atipet kejuku mamakon, kecoraki da lukewosatok einer akecekiro kakonyenekon.”" 
Acts23:31 Kosodete koyaŋaasi iserikalei Paul kwape kicorakinitere kinyamasi kuare kiton Antipaturi. 
Acts23:32 Tupuruc do koboŋosi kesi ore loka iserikalei kinyeis ikebwanenok aiyatakin alosit kaŋes," 
Acts23:33 Kedolo ŋul Kaisarea, ka ainakin ekayairon ebalua, kisibwaata da Paul kakonyeneke," 
Acts23:34 Ŋes da nakedaunia asoman, kiŋit ebe, “Erai ŋesi loko buku ali?” Nakejenunia ebe erai loko Kilikia," 
Acts23:35 kotema atiar, “Keirari jo naeponiata lukiwosato.” Kicorak aidario kotogo lokapolou loka Kerode." 
Acts24:1 Kosodi ketuboros apaarasia akany, kijesar Anania esasedoti lopeti nepepe kice komakio, ka ekeneranikec, Teratulo. Kikujokis kesi ekayaiton nuesurokinitotor Paul." 
Acts24:2 Kenyaraun ŋes, kogeu Teratulo aosan ebe: “Naarai kidumunit ainapakin naepol kanukon, wu Pelikis lokaibuses, kanuka apiirikinikon da eteteun akiro nuka ateker kana," 
Acts24:3 kicamunit da kaimal naepol koponesio kere kaiboisio da kere. 
Acts24:4 Konye kenyek aitapas jo noi, keŋaiŋait jo kopupok sio kasianutukon kanuesupaaka." 
Acts24:5 Naarai kidum isio ekesa lo erai ekamunaaran, ekesidikon da loka ecelet koYudayan kere anatar akwapin kere, ekeŋarenon da loka erioŋet loka Inasarayon." 
Acts24:6 Bobo da abu kotam amunaar eyekalu, kekamut, [kakotos atubokin kwape ejaatar ikisilakosi." 
Acts24:7 Konye kobu ekapolon Lusias kolema ŋes kagogoŋ naepol kakaninikosi,]" 
Acts24:8 kicorak da ikewosatokoke aponare akonyenekon. Ijo elopet kaiŋitiŋitikon ipedori adumun akiro nukiwosat isio ŋes.” 
Acts24:9 Kiwosata Iyudayan da kobalas ebe, “Ikote nepenen.”" 
Acts24:10 Kosodi kokwet ekayaiton Paul einer, Koboŋok ebe: “Naarai ajeni ebe irai ijo ekatubon loka ateker kana ikar luipu, atubo elop ketau kaloelakara," 
Acts24:11 naarai ipedori ajenun ebe eroko apaarasia edepara atomon kanuarei ageun naadokaria eoŋ Yerusalem aima; 
Acts24:12 mam ituŋa lu apotu kadumut koyekalu kipega kidiotunanan, karaida aituwutaar atukot, karaida katukosia, karaida kore." 
Acts24:13 Kwabo mam epedorete aitogogoŋ akiro ŋun nuiwosaete kwana. 
Acts24:14 Konye alimori kamakon nu ebe kwape ejaar Erot, loenyarito kesi erioŋet, kwaŋin amaia Edeke loka lukapapaakosi, eyuunit kere nuelimito ikisila, ka nuiwadikatai oitabon luka inabin," 
Acts24:15 amunokina Edeke, ŋol loecamunito kesi da ikulepek, ebe ejaun ajarun naka luedolito ka lumam edolito da." 
Acts24:16 Kanuka ŋun enyikokinit ajaut ketau lomam itoronio mama ejai Edeke ka ituŋa da apaarasia kere. 
Acts24:17 Akaulo naka ikar luipu abu kabu ainun atekereka nukaitim ka ainakineta da. 
Acts24:18 Kaŋun kadumut eoŋ koyekalu etesegaara, komamei ekodet karaida autar. Konye Iyudayan ice lukepote ko Asia—" 
Acts24:19 lutiebusakinit ajaut ne akonyenekon aosan eoŋ, arai ejai adiokirot keoŋ," 
Acts24:20 Arai bo kolimut lupelu aibucaret naeanyunitos kamakaŋ naabwoia kaurianet," 
Acts24:21 dimarai akirot na adiopet bon nakeworoi kabwoi kokidiŋikec ebe, ‘Kanuka ajarun naka ikatwak katubokinio lolo kakonyenekus.’ ”" 
Acts24:22 Konye kisiyap Pelikis kes, naarai kejeni ace nuka Erot, kobala ebe, “Naijesunor Lusias ekapolon atubi akirokus.”" 
Acts24:23 Kosodi kicorak ekapolokiton aidar Paul konye kajalakinit, komam isimiki idio kopaperoke aijaanakin ŋes." 
Acts24:24 Kosodi ketuboros apaarasia kodol Pelikis nepepe ka Durusila akeberu, nakerai Ayudayat, kiyakia anyaraun Paul, kiira ŋes inera nuka aiyuun naejai toma Kristo Yesu." 
Acts24:25 Kopesik Paul ŋes akiro nuka adolit, ka nuka ayaikina, ka atubokinio naebunit, kokurianar Pelikis, Koboŋok ebe, “Kolot do kwana; kadum eoŋ apak, keworouni.”" 
Acts24:26 Komuno da ebe einakini ŋes Paul arupian, Kanuka ŋun konyaraunun eyala kaŋes," 
Acts24:27 Kosodi ketuboros ikar iarei, kodakakinai Porukio Pesito airum aibois naka Pelikis; kekoto Pelikis aitojokio kama ka Iyudayan, kwaŋin kinyek Paul kaidaris." 
Acts25:1 Kosodi nakedolio Pesito obuku, ketuboros apaarasia auni kodoka Yerusalem anyoun koKaisarea." 
Acts25:2 Kikujokis ŋes isasedotin lupeti ka ikeŋarenok luka Iyudayan nuka Paul, kiŋaiŋaata ŋes," 
Acts25:3 kilipata kasianutuke ayaun Paul Yerusalem, tetere eperunete ka aarakin orot," 
Acts25:4 Konye Koboŋok Pesito ebe idario Paul koKaisarea, eapie ŋes da alosit ŋina." 
Acts25:5 Kobala ebe, “Aso ŋulluejai apedor kayesi kauparos kaeoŋ, arai kito ejai akirot naerono kotuŋanan kaŋol, kiwosata do.”" 
Acts25:6 Nakesalitor kakes apaarasia numam edeparito akanykauni arai atomon, kijesar Kaisarea; apaaran naetupakini kiboikin oicoloŋ loka etube, kicorak Paul ayaunio." 
Acts25:7 Nakedolunio Paul, kobwaata Iyudayan lukijesunos koYerusalem airimor ŋes, kiwosata ŋes akiro nuipu nuelaŋir, numam apedorete aitogogoŋ," 
Acts25:8 Kobala Paul eiyar ebe, “Mam eoŋ adiakit akirot karaida kokisila luka Iyudayan, karaida oyekalu, karaida mama ejai Kaisar.”" 
Acts25:9 Konye Pesito kekoto aitojokio kama ka Iyudayan, Koboŋok Paul ebe, “Ikoto kereka ijo alosit Yerusalem atubokinio kaŋina kakonyeneka kakiro kanu?”" 
Acts25:10 Konye kobala Paul ebe, “Abwoi eoŋ kane koiŋaren keicoloŋ loka etube loka Kaisar, nekebusakinitor atubokinio; mam adiakit akirot koYudayan, kwape ijenia ijo kotenan." 
Acts25:11 Aso arai adiakit, arai eswamat akirot naibusakinitor atwania, mam aŋeri atwanare; konye arai emamei abeit kanukewosatotor, emamei yenepedori aijaikin eoŋ akaninikec. Eyatakinit mama ejai Kaisar.”" 
Acts25:12 Kosodi nakedaunia Pesito einer kituŋa luka aurianet Koboŋok ebe, “Iyatakinit ijo mama ejai Kaisar; ilosi do mama ejai Kaisar.”" 
Acts25:13 Ketuboros apaarasia, kodol Agiripa ekabaka, ka Berenike Kaisarea ayogan Pesito." 
Acts25:14 Nakesalitotor nen apaarasia nuipu, kitatamik Pesito ekabaka akiro nuka Paul ebe, “Ejai ne etuŋanan lokinyeini Pelikis eenitai;" 
Acts25:15 lokekujokinete isasedotin lupeti ka imakio luka Iyudayan akiroke nakajaar Yerusalem, kokotosi ŋes atubokinio." 
Acts25:16 Abu kaboŋok kes ebe mam erai epone loka Iromayon aijaikin etuŋanan kere eroko yeniwosatai etereikina ka luiwosato, ka adumun apak naka aiyar kotoma kanuiwosatai." 
Acts25:17 Aso naketukonokinotor ne, mam abu keyap, konye apaaran naatupakini keboikin oicoloŋ loka etube, kecorak etuŋanan ŋol ayaunio." 
Acts25:18 Kosodi nakebwoiata lukiwosato ŋes mam eyauna akirot naerono kwape abu kaomitor; 
Acts25:19 konye ejaas aiŋiseta ace nuka edinikec, ido nuka etuŋanan ece Yesu loabu kotwana, konye loitogogoŋit Paul ebe ejari." 
Acts25:20 Kaoliki eoŋ aiŋic aiŋiseta ŋun, abu keŋit arai ekoto alosit Yerusalem atubokinio kaŋina kakiro kaŋun." 
Acts25:21 Konye Paul kiyatak aidario tetere etubokini Kaisar, kecorak ŋes aidario kiton neejukaria ŋes mama ejai Kaisar.”" 
Acts25:22 Kotema Agiripa Pesito atiar, “Eoŋ da elopet abu kakoto apupun etuŋanan ŋol.” Kobala ebe, “Ipupuni ŋes moi.”" 
Acts25:23 Kosodi kapaaran naatupakini kobu Agiripa nepepe ka Berenike kaibuses naepol, kolomasi aibois naka aipup akiro nepepe ka ikapolok luka iserikalei ka ikiliok luejenikina lukore. Kicorak Pesito Paul ayaunio." 
Acts25:24 Kotema Pesito atiar, “Ekabaka Agiripa, ka yes kere luijaas ne nepepe kasio, ianyut etuŋanan lo lokelipito eoŋ Iyudayan kere luko Yerusalem ka ne da, kiworoete ebe mam bobo ebusakinit ŋes aijar." 
Acts25:25 Konye abu kaany ebe mam iswamat akirot naibusakinitor atwanare; ŋes da elopet iyatakinit mama ejai Kaisar, abu kaomite aijukar." 
Acts25:26 Eoŋ da emamei akirot nakabeit naewadikakini ejakait. Kanuka ŋun ayau ŋes ne akonyenekus, aitelekarit akonyenekon, wu Ekabaka Agiripa, tetere kidau aiŋitiŋit kadum akirot naewadikai." 
Acts25:27 Naarai aomit eoŋ ebe mam ejok aijukar eenat komam itodiara nuiwosatere ŋes.” 
Acts26:1 Kobala Agiripa Paul ebe, “Kinup jo einer kanukon.” Kosodi korio Paul akekan, koiyar, kobala ebe:" 
Acts26:2 “Wu Ekabaka Agiripa, kekemer naarai kaiyar lolokakonyenekon kanuka akiro kere nukewosatotor Iyudayan," 
Acts26:3 aitelekarit naarai ijeni ijo iponesio kere ka aiŋiseta da kere nuejaas oYudayan. Kanuka ŋun kemaimait kopupok eoŋ katitiŋikinit. 
Acts26:4 Naarai ejenete Iyudayan kere ekajautene ameun keitelepane, lokejai kageunet kotoma atekereka, ido ko Yerusalem da." 
Acts26:5 Apotu kajenut ameun apeŋo, arai ekotosi aitejenun, ebe abu karai Eparisayot lokorioŋet loetokit noi kotoma odinikosi." 
Acts26:6 Kwana da abwoi kane atubokinio kanuka amun aisumunet nakisumunit Edeke lukapapaakosi," 
Acts26:7 naemunosi atekerinikosi atomon ka nuarei adolokin, emaenenete Edeke kainyikokinit paaran ka kuare da." 
Acts26:8 Kanukinyo eomitere kamakus araut akirot namam ecamuna ebe itaiari Edeke ikatwak? 
Acts26:9 “Abeit abu eoŋ elopet kaomite ebe kebusakinit aswam nuipu airebokin ekiror loka Yesu Enasarayot. 
Acts26:10 Abu keswama ŋun ko Yerusalem; abu kaen ice kalukalaunak aidaris, kadau ainakinio apedor kaneejaas isasedotin lupeti, ido da abu kekeik akan luaario." 
Acts26:11 Ido irwan ipu abu keticanenenei kes katukosia kere, ketiŋaikinite ainyanakin Edeke; kareite kes kaibworit kiton oreria Iukokiŋa da." 
Acts26:12 “Kasodi alosit Damasiko kanuka aswam kaŋin, kija kapedor ka anupakinio naka isasedotin lupeti." 
Acts26:13 Kosodi kidiŋ paaran, wu ekabaka, abu kaany aica nakebuni kokuju, nakedeparit ailiya naka akoloŋ, kacaikin eoŋ ka ŋul lukija nenipe keoŋ." 
Acts26:14 Kebirokinos isio kere kwap, keira eporoto lokinera keoŋ kaŋajep naka Aburanian ebe, ‘Saul, Saul, kanukinyo kireitor eoŋ? Kitionikinit ijo aipet iketetin.’" 
Acts26:15 Kabala ebe, ‘Iŋai bo ijo, Ejakait?’ Katema eoŋ Ejakait atiar, ‘Eoŋ Yesu loireit ijo." 
Acts26:16 Konye konyou, kobwo kakejekon; naarai ketakanikin jo kanuka nu, adakakin jo araun ekejaanakinan ka ekajenan loka akiro nuibu koanyunia eoŋ, ido kaŋun nuketakanikinor," 
Acts26:17 kayuuni jo kama kituŋakon ka Imo da-lukeyakiari mamakec," 
Acts26:18 aitwekenyun akecekonye, tetere ibelokinos ainyein amuton kesesenata aica, ainyein da apedor naka Satan kosesenata Edeke, kosodete adumun aisionio adiakanareta, ka airumet kokidiŋ; kaŋul kaluitalaunitai kanuka aiyuun naejai tomakaŋ.’" 
Acts26:19 “Kanuka ŋun, wu Ekabaka Agiripa, mam abu kepaliik aitapoet nakakuj," 
Acts26:20 konye abu kageu alimonokin luko Damasiko, kosodi koYerusalem, kotoma akwap kere da naka Iyudayan, ka Imo da, ebe kitoronikinos, kibelokinos mama ejai Edeke, iswamaete aswamisio nuibusakinito aitoronikin." 
Acts26:21 Kanuka ŋun ŋes kekamuniata Iyudayan kotoma oyekalu, katamakis aiar da." 
Acts26:22 Aso kiton lolo adum aisigalikinio naebuni kama ejai Edeke, abwoi aitejenun ludidik ka lukapolok da, kwabo mam eneri akirot dimarai ŋun nukinerasi Musa ka inabin ebe ejaunete:" 
Acts26:23 ebe ibusakinit Kristo aiticanio, ido da korau ŋesi losodit ajarun kokatwak, elimonokini aica mama ejaas ituŋakosi ka Imo da.”" 
Acts26:24 Kosodi nakeiyaror kwaŋin, kotema Pesito keporoto loepol atiar, “Kikerepiki cama ijo, Paul, kijulaki jo aisisiakon naepol.”" 
Acts26:25 Konye kobala Paul ebe, “Mam kekerepikinit, wu Pesito lokaibuses, dimarai enera akiro nukabeit ka nukapirianut da obe." 
Acts26:26 Naarai ejeŋi ekabaka nuka akiro kaŋun, eoŋ da enera kaŋes katitiŋ; naarai etogogoŋit ebe emamei akirot kotoma kaŋun naimunonikinitai ŋes, naarai mam nu eswamas kagor." 
Acts26:27 Ekabaka Agiripa, iyuunit tope ijo inabin? Ajeni ebe iyuunit.”" 
Acts26:28 Kotema Agiripa Paul atiar, “Kanaesupaana ikoto aituluor eoŋ da Ekristayot!”" 
Acts26:29 Koboŋok Paul ebe, “Arai kanaesupaana, arai kanaepol elipi Edeke mere ijo bon, konye kaŋul da kere lukapupete lolo, koraut kwape keoŋ-dimarai aeneta nu.”" 
Acts26:30 Kosodi kobwo ekabaka, ka ekayaiton ka Berenike, ka ŋul lukiboiete kakes;" 
Acts26:31 napenyounete, kineranakinos ebe, “Mam etuŋanan lo iswamat akirot naibusakinitor atwanare karaida aenio.”" 
Acts26:32 Kobala Agiripa Pesito ebe, “Arai kedim etuŋanan ŋol aiyatakinit mama ejai Kaisar ti kelacakin.”" 
Acts27:1 Kosodi nakicorakinere sio aikwaŋar kiton Italia, kijaikis Paul ka ienan ice mama ejai ekapolokiton erioŋet loka Augusito, ekekiror Yulio." 
Acts27:2 Kadokas ataker naka Aduramutio, nakekapakina alosit kiton oreria luka oitolima luka Asia, kekwaŋasi, kauparos ka Arisitariko Emakedoniat loko Sesalonika." 
Acts27:3 Apaaran naatupakini kadolo Sidon; kikonak Yulio Paul asianut, kocamak ŋes alosit mama ejaas ipaperoke tetere imukeo." 
Acts27:4 Kanyoutu kanen kekwaŋaros kediata keririto Kupuro, naarai kemeunito ikwamin kakonyen." 
Acts27:5 Ketoro aŋolol naka Kilikia ka Pampulia, kadolo Mura nako Lukia." 
Acts27:6 Kanen kodum ekapolokiton ataker naka Alegesanderia idiai Italia, kadokikis ŋin," 
Acts27:7 Kekwaŋaros motimot apaarasia nuipu, kadolo Kinido kationis, ido naarai kitikokinit ekwam, keririata Kurete katereikina Salumone," 
Acts27:8 Ketoroto kationis aapu koitolima, kadolo aibois naenyaritai Odoketa Lukajokak naidunyas ka ere Lasea." 
Acts27:9 Kiilonya apaarasia, kojau aronis alosit naarai atuboros apaarasia nuka Ailuŋ, kidelu Paul," 
Acts27:10 kobala kes ebe, “Lukipa, aanyunit eoŋ ebe ejaun amunaar ka atwaniar alosit na, mere iboro bon ka ataker, konye aijarawok da.”" 
Acts27:11 Konye abu ekapolokiton kopupok ekekwaŋan lokapolon ka elopet ataker aitelekarit ŋun nuenera Paul. 
Acts27:12 Ido da mam ebusakinit edoket ŋol aiboio apak naka aaterot, kidelut luipu kakesi aikwaŋar anyoun kanen, tetere elemuni edolete Poenike, edoket loka Kurete, loetereikina agolitome nakokide, ka egalakimak nakokide, kasala nen kapak naka aaterot." 
Acts27:13 Kosodi napekusi ekwam lokeŋalakimak kiyamakina, koomitos ebe adumutu nukekotos, kibwosut edobo lokitapaikinet, kikwaŋaros aapu koitolima loka Kurete." 
Acts27:14 Ketubor apak naedit kokut ekwam lokagogon, loenyaritai Eurakulon ebuni kaneonit," 
Acts27:15 Kokutar ataker, mam epedoro atereikina ekwam, kajalakisi kikutario," 
Acts27:16 Kanen ketoro atipet ariri naka apujan naedit naenyaritai Kulauda, kekurautu ajen itaker." 
Acts27:17 Kekiasi ŋes, kitwasamata aisigalikineta, koenikis kwap ataker; ido naarai kokuriaka aipok koSuritis, kijoliliosi iboro, kwaŋin kokutarai." 
Acts27:18 Naarai kiiliilit ekwam, apaaran naatupakini kogeut acakar iboro aŋolol;" 
Acts27:19 apaaran nakiwuniet da kocakanasi kakaninikec ikulepek iboro luka ataker. 
Acts27:20 Mam atakani akoloŋ karaida aacer apaarasia nuipu, kokuta sio ekwam loededeŋ, kokau kodaun amun kere naka aitajario." 
Acts27:21 Nakiboioto apak naapol mam enyamete, kosodi kobwo Paul kokidiŋikec, kotema atiar, “Lukipa, ti ebusakinit yes aiirar eoŋ, amamus aikwaŋar anyoun koKurete, adumun amunaar ka atwaniar na." 
Acts27:22 Aso kwana kecori yes kolakaros; naarai emameun yenetwaniari akeijar, dimarai ataker bon." 
Acts27:23 Naarai kakuar kana abu emalaika loka Edeke, loarai eoŋ lokeŋ, loamaenenei da, kobwo aapu keoŋ," 
Acts27:24 kalimok eoŋ ebe, ‘Paul, sirikikurianar; ibusakinit ijo aibwo kakonyen nuka Kaisar; ido koany, kiinak Edeke ituŋa lu kere luiupatar.’" 
Acts27:25 Aso, lukipa, kolakaros, naarai eyuunit eoŋ Edeke, ebe ejaun kwape kalimokinitere." 
Acts27:26 Konye ibusakinit aipok kapujan.” 
Acts27:27 Kosodi kedol apaaran nakitomonet kaoŋon, nakikaleleor aŋolol naka Adiria, bala kidiŋ ebai koomitos ikekwaŋak ebe aapikis neeonit." 
Acts27:28 Kitemo, kodumut aidules akaisaarei; kiyatakis edit kitemo bobo, kodumut aidules atomon kakany." 
Acts27:29 Kokuriakaros aipok katiban, koosikis idoboi iwoŋon lukitapaikinet kokori, kilipa akwap aiwalar." 
Acts27:30 Nakekototor ikekwaŋak aisii kataker, apotu kijoliliosi itaker toma aŋolol, kijoseikinito bala eosikinete idoboi lukitapaikinet kokume." 
Acts27:31 Kolimok Paul ekapolokiton ka iserikalei ebe, “Dimikito esalete ituŋa lu ataker, mam ipedorete aitajario.”" 
Acts27:32 Kosodete iserikalei aitub aunoi nuka itaker, kojalakis kodo." 
Acts27:33 Napiwalari, kiŋaiŋa Paul kes kere ainyam inyamat, kobala ebe, “Lolo ŋes apaaran nakitomonet kaoŋon aidaret kailuŋ, komam inyamete ibore." 
Acts27:34 Aso keŋaiŋait, konyamata; naarai eraun mamakus aitaiario, naarai emamei karaida etimat loka akwesikus loeoliori.”" 
Acts27:35 Kedau einer ŋun, kolem emugati, kimala Edeke kakonyenekec kere, kobil, kogeu ainyam." 
Acts27:36 Kosodete kolakaros kere, konyama kesi da." 
Acts27:37 Isio lukija toma ataker kimwa ituŋa kere akwat aarei ka akaisakanykaarei, ka lukanykape." 
Acts27:38 Kedaut aimonikin, kitebebenata ataker, kocakakis akima aŋolol." 
Acts27:39 Kiwala akwap, mam ejenuna akwap ŋin, dimarai apotu koanyutu agule naejai oitolima, kinerut aisukunyar ataker ŋina arai epedor." 
Acts27:40 Kocakasi idoboi lukitapaikinet, kinyeis kes kaŋolol, nepepe kaijarijar aunoi nueenis aiteteneta; kikeut egoe tetere ekutari ekwam kobeasi oitolima." 
Acts27:41 Konye kodoloto neiriamata akailan kipok ataker kokwap, kiminaikin ekume, kosalak komam ijaŋijaŋa, konye kobila akailan ekori." 
Acts27:42 Kinerut iserikalei aiar ienan, kinye idiokakesi aiduor ka aisi;" 
Acts27:43 konye kokoto ekapolokiton aituku Paul, kitikok kinyeis aswam nuenerunitotor. Kicorak luapedorete aidu kisiaut aibironokin aŋolol kobeata neeonit," 
Acts27:44 lukesalete da kabaoi ka oboro ke luka ataker. Kwaŋin kokuasi ituŋa kere neeonit. 
Acts28:1 Nakidaunia aiku, kajenut ebe apujan ŋin kenyaritai Melita." 
Acts28:2 Kiswamakis sio ikulepek akwap asianut namam etapit, naarai apotu kinokokis akim, kisukunyikis sio, kanuka edou loketepi, ido kanuka aterot da." 
Acts28:3 Nakeraraa Paul ekesit loka akito, kibwaik akim, kolom emusaga kanuka amwanis, kidolakin akanike." 
Acts28:4 Nakeanyuniata ikulepek akwap emun edelideli kakanike, kotemanaros ebe, “Abeit erai etuŋanan lo ekaaran, Karaida kekuit kaŋolol, mam Etube isiikit ŋes aijar.”" 
Acts28:5 Konye ŋes kilakilakak emun akim komam edumunit amusuŋut," 
Acts28:6 Kidarito, komunosi ŋes abuun arai aibiror atwanare eŋeso; konye kedaut aidar apak naepol koanyut ebe amamei adiomusuŋut kere, kibelokinos kotemasi ebe erai edeke." 
Acts28:7 Aapu kaibois kaŋin kejaas amanat nuka ekapolon loka apujan, ekekiror Publio, kisukunyik ŋol sio ketau loka eipaperone apaarasia auni." 
Acts28:8 Kosodi kanen kedeka papa loka Publio ekamidi ka aleporit aokot, koloma Paul mamakeŋ, kilip, kidokok ŋes akekanin, kitaŋaleu," 
Acts28:9 Akaulo kaŋun, kopotu ice lukedekas kapujan kaŋin kitaŋaleunoi." 
Acts28:10 Kosodete kitubusikis sio kainakineta nuipu; ido nakikwaŋaror kibwaikis iboro kere lukipuda ataker," 
Acts28:11 Akaulo naka ilapio iuni, kediata kataker naka Alegesanderia, nakesalakinit apujan apakio nuka aterot, aanyuneteke kerai Iinacan Imwatok," 
Acts28:12 Kadolo Surakusa, kasalakis nen apaarasia auni." 
Acts28:13 Anyoun kanen kerimosi kadolo Regium; ketubor apaaran adiopet kokut ekwam lokeŋalakimak, kadolo Puteoli apaaran nakiareit." 
Acts28:14 Kanen kadumut iinacan, kiŋaiŋaata sio asalakin mamakec apaarasia akanykaarei. Kwaŋin kadolo do Rome." 
Acts28:15 Kiirasi iinacan lukaŋina nukosi, kopotu kiton Agwelanaret naka Apius ka Iswamin Iuni aisiriam sio. Nakeanyunia Paul kes, kimal Edeke, kotitiŋior." 
Acts28:16 Nakilomaria Rome, kocamakinai Paul aiboi bon nepepe ka eserikalet loidari ŋes." 
Acts28:17 Akaulo kapaarasia auni konyarau lukeraas ikapolok koYudayan; kedaut atukokin, kotema kes atiar, “Iinacan, karaida mam eswamat aronis kotuŋa karaida koponesio luka lukapapaawok, aponi kejaikin ko Yerusalem toma akanin nuka Iromayon aenio." 
Acts28:18 Kaadaut aiŋitanar, kakotosi alacakin, naarai kemamei adiokirot kamakaŋ naaret," 
Acts28:19 Konye nakepegatar Iyudayan, ketiŋaikin aiyatakin mama ejai Kaisar-kwabo amamei nakiwosaet ituŋa luka atekereka." 
Acts28:20 Aso kanuka ŋun kanyarautu yes aponare aanyun eoŋ keiner keoŋ, naarai kanuka amun naka Isirael ŋes kaenitere korikot kalo.”" 
Acts28:21 Kotemasi kesi ŋes atiar, “Mam sio kidumunit ebalua anyoun koYerusalem kakirokon, ido emamei onace edio da loebunit ne loelimorit ka ainerit akirot naerono kanukon." 
Acts28:22 Konye kikoto apupun kamakon nuiwomit; naarai kanuka akiro nuka erioŋet kalo ejenikina kamakosi ebe ereitai noi kaŋinikibois.” 
Acts28:23 Kedaut aseikin ŋes apaaran kopotu luipu noi mamakeŋ togo lokiboio. Kitetemik kes ka aitejenun ameun tupuruc kiton eboŋ nuka ajakanut naka Edeke, ikujokini akiro nuka Yesu kanuka ikisila luka Musa ka inabin da." 
Acts28:24 Apotu ice kiyuut nuenerai, kwabo ice mam iyuuna." 
Acts28:25 Namam kecamanarotor, koloto do, kedau Paul einer akirot adiopet na ebe: “Abu Emoyo Lokalaunan kinera kotenan kama ka enabi Isaia mama ka lukapapaakus ebe:" 
Acts28:26 ‘Kolot mama ejaas ituŋa lu, kolimok kes ebe: Kiiranarete konye mam ijenunete, Koanyununete da konye mam imisiikinete," 
Acts28:27 Abaŋaakata itauon luka ituŋa kalu, Ijikititas akiikec, Itumudakito akecekonyen, Kinyeis aanyun kakonyenekec, Ka aiirar kakeceki, Kojenut kotauonokec, Kibelokinos ketaŋaleu kes.’" 
Acts28:28 Aso kojenutu ebe ejukakin aitaiario na naka Edeke Omo: iirarete kesi da.” [ 
Acts28:29 Kedau einer ŋun koloto Iyudayan, epeganakinos noi.]" 
Acts28:30 Kodau Paul ikar iarei kotogoke loketacanakini, kisukunyanakinenei kere lukeponenenete mamakeŋ," 
Acts28:31 elimonokini ajakanut naka Edeke, ido ka aisisianakin katitiŋ akiro nuka Ejakait Yesu Kristo, komam itikokinio." 
Romans1:1 Paul ebulesit loka Kristo Yesu, Iokenyaraunio araun: ekiyakia, Iokegitakinio alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke," 
Romans1:2 nuesumunit Edeke kolo kama ka inabinoke kotoma nukiwadikatai nukalaunak," 
Romans1:3 kes akiro nuka okokuke Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok, lokeurio kaur naka Daudi kwape ejaar akuan," 
Romans1:4 loedakakinitai araut Okoku loka Edeke kapedor kwape ejaar Emoyo loka Alaunit, kanuka ajarun kokatwak," 
Romans1:5 kotomakeŋ ŋes kipou kadumuniata asianut ka eiyakiane tetere erimarete lukatekerin kere aiyuun kanuka ekekiror," 
Romans1:6 kotomakec yes da kinyaritai araut luka Yesu Kristo; 
Romans1:7 Mama ejaas ŋul kere luejaas Rome luminan luka Edeke luenyaritai araut ikalaunak: Asianut kojai mamakus ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo. 
Romans1:8 Esiauni aimal Ekadeke kotoma Yesu Kristo kanukus kere, naarai elimonokinio akusiiyuun anatar akwapin kere." 
Romans1:9 Naarai Edeke, loamai komoyoka kotoma Akiro Nukajokak nuka Okokuke, ŋes ekajenanika ebe alimununei yes kailipika komam apalari." 
Romans1:10 Ecebokinit ailip arai motoko kanuka akoteke kesipedori Edeke arurukun mama ijaas. 
Romans1:11 Naarai kemuit aanyun yes tetere kekopakin yes adioinakinet naka emoyo nakiticasi yes," 
Romans1:12 ŋes atemar ebe aitalakanario bonik ka bonik kanuka aiyuunikus, ka nakaŋ da." 
Romans1:13 Konye iinacan, akoto yes ajenun ebe irwan ipu alosikinit abunore mamakus, tetere adumuni adioraito kamakus kwape kama kImo ice, konye ketikokinitai kiton kwana." 
Romans1:14 Keburaete Iyonanin ka lukacekwapin da, keburaete lukacoa ka lueolito da:" 
Romans1:15 kanuka ŋun akapakina eoŋ kowaika alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak kiton mamakus da luijaas Rome. 
Romans1:16 Naarai mam Akiro Nukajokak kesurumito ileic: naarai erai apedor naka Edeke ainun aitajario mama ejai ŋinituŋanan yeniyuuni, mama ejai Eyudayat ber, ka Eyonanit da." 
Romans1:17 Naarai tomakec epukoritai adolit naka Edeke, anyoun kaiyuun kiton aiyuun; kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Ebusi ikadoliton kanuka aiyuun.”" 
Romans1:18 Naarai epukoritai anyunyura naka Edeke abunore kokuju mama ejai epali kere ka amamus adolit naka ituŋa luitikokinete abeit kanuka amamus adolitekec," 
Romans1:19 Naarai ejenas akiro nuka Edeke ideleleete kotomakec, naarai abu Edeke kisideleleu mamakec." 
Romans1:20 Naarai ameun kaisub akwap, atakanut iboroke lumam etakanete, ŋes atemar akepedor namam enaŋi, ka Eidekeoneke, kotoma oboro lukesubi. Aso emamei kes aiyar:" 
Romans1:21 naarai apotu kojenut Edeke, mam kes itubusikinito ŋes kwape Edeke, karaida aima ŋes, dimarai kooliosi kotoma aomisiokec, kitumutoroi ikecetauon luemamei ajenun." 
Romans1:22 Kineras ebe eraas lukacoa, kobaŋaakaros," 
Romans1:23 kisiecata aibuses naka Edeke lomam etwani aituputoor aputosia nuka ituŋa kaluetwakete, arai nuka akweny, arai nuka itiaŋ, arai nuka lueliatos." 
Romans1:24 Kanuka ŋun abu Edeke kojalak kes toma oraŋasia luka itauonokec mama ejai amamus aila, ka aitisilio da naka awatekec bonik ka bonik," 
Romans1:25 naarai apotu kisiecata abeit naka Edeke araun aiŋal, koyoŋito komaata da isubat itia Ekasuban loituritoi ikar kere! Amen." 
Romans1:26 Kanuka ŋun abu Edeke kojalak kes ainekit naka ileic, naarai apotu aŋorokec da kilocokis einono lokaurunet aituluor lomere lokaurunet," 
Romans1:27 ikiliok da kwape kwaŋin kinyeis einono lokaurunet loka aberu kibworo kotoma oraŋakec ŋolituŋanan mama ejai locekeŋ, ikiliok kiswamanakis ikiliok nukileic, ido koinanakinos eropit loebusakinit apaarikec." 
Romans1:28 Ido kwape mam apotu kocamuniata ajenun Edeke, abu Edeke kojalak kes aomisio numam ajokis, kiswamata numam ibusakinito." 
Romans1:29 Ileleba amamus adolit kere, nukaronok, airaŋaanut, ameŋeranut; ileleba ekokote, earit, aŋolopa, aiŋal, aomisio nueroko, ikedeideok," 
Romans1:30 ikasiomak, luelaito Edeke, lukepali, luepogaka, luituros, ikapwakak nueroko, luiulakinito ikauriakakec," 
Romans1:31 luemamei acoa, luejalete aitutuket, lumam eminanara, luemamei aitim," 
Romans1:32 luejenete aitepesenit naka Edeke, ebe luiswamaete nuikote nen ibusakinit atwanare, mam bon iswamaete ŋun, konye itojokito da ŋul lukiswamaete ŋun." 
Romans2:1 Aso emamei jo aiyar, ijo ituŋanan yenitubokini yenice; naarai ŋun nuitubokini yenice, itubokin ilopet aitelekar, naarai jo yenitubi, iswamai da ŋupeŋun," 
Romans2:2 Kijeni oni ebe aitub naka Edeke erai nakabeit mama ejaas ŋul luiswamaete nuikote nen. 
Romans2:3 Ijo ituŋanan, yenitubokini luiswamaete nuikote nen, iswamai ijo da ŋupeŋun, iwomit ebe ikui tope kaitub naka Edeke?" 
Romans2:4 Imwaŋit kereka ijo abar naka ajokisike, ka aŋirikin, ka atitiŋikinitike da? Mam kereka ijeni ebe ajokis naka Edeke kiriuni jo aitoronikin?" 
Romans2:5 Konye kanuka aninikukon, ka etaukon loemamei aitoronikin, iŋadakin bon anyunyura kapaaran naka anyunyura ka apukorio naka etube loedolit loka Edeke," 
Romans2:6 loetacakini ŋinituŋanan kwape ejaatar aswamisioke; 
Romans2:7 mama ejaas ŋul luemoete aibuses ka ayoŋio, ka aibut, kotoma atitiŋ naka aswamisio nuejok einakini aijar naka ikar kere." 
Romans2:8 Ido kaŋul kalueŋolopaka, luiulakinito abeit, luerimasi amamus adolit, edumunete anyunyura ka adedeŋ." 
Romans2:9 Ejaunete ican ka aridakinio toma aijar naka ŋinituŋanan yeniswamai nueroko, aisiaun lyudayat, ka Iyonanit da," 
Romans2:10 konye aibuses ka ayoŋio ka ainapakin mama ejai ŋinituŋanan yeniswamai nuejok, aisiaun Iyudayat, ka Iyonanit da." 
Romans2:11 Naarai emamei aitiak ituŋa kama ejai Edeke. 
Romans2:12 Naarai lukediakarete kere komameete ikisila, emudiaros da komameete ikisila, ŋul da kere lukediakarete kojaas kikisila, etubokinio kokisila." 
Romans2:13 Naarai mere ŋul luiirarete ikisila kes eraas ikadolitok kakonyen nuka Edeke, konye ikeswamak ikisila kes luitojokio araut ikadolitok." 
Romans2:14 Naarai naiswamaata Imo luemameete ikisila koinono loka ikisila, karaida emameete ikisila eraas kesi ikulepek ikisila." 
Romans2:15 Itodikinete ebe iwadikatai aswam naka ikisila toma otauonokec itejenikini da etaukec, iwosaete akeceomisio nuepegasi bonik ka bonik, arai bo eiyaros;" 
Romans2:16 kapaaran naetubokinia Edeke nukaiyeiyea nuka ituŋa kama ka Yesu Kristo kwape ejaatar Akiro Nukajokak nuketitiŋitai eoŋ. 
Romans2:17 Konye jo, arai kinyaritai Eyudayat kogoŋakina okisila, iwoloboboi kama ejai Edeke," 
Romans2:18 kojeni nuekoto ŋesi, icamuni da nuitelekarito ajokis, kituutooritai kotoma okisila," 
Romans2:19 itogogoŋit bon araut ekeŋarenon loka imudukiok, aica da naka ŋul kaluejaas amuton," 
Romans2:20 eketetenan loka ibaŋiok, ekesisianakinan loka imukerun, ijai kaput naka aijen ka abeit toma okisila," 
Romans2:21 aso jo loisisianakini loce, mam tope isisianakini bon? Jo loilimonokini ebe Sirikokoi, ikokoi kereka ijo?" 
Romans2:22 Jo loibala ebe Siridote, idotei ijo? Jo loisacit aputosia, iŋasi ijo abilai?" 
Romans2:23 Jo loiwolobobot kotoma okisila, itisili kereka Edeke kanuka apaar kokisila?" 
Romans2:24 Naarai kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Einyanakinio ekiror loka Edeke katekerin kanukus.”" 
Romans2:25 Naarai ejai akepio ajokis arai iswamai ikisila; konye arai irai ijo loipaarit kokisila, arau akonikepio amamus akepio." 
Romans2:26 Aso arai erici lomam ekepep aicorakineta nuka ikisila, mam kereka amamus akepioke imarakinio araut akepio?" 
Romans2:27 Ŋol da lomam ekepitai koinono loerici ikisila, mam kereka kitubokini jo loijaas kaiwadikaet ka akepio da, loipaari kokisila?" 
Romans2:28 Naarai ŋol loerai Eyudayat kokuju mere ŋol Eyudayat cut, karaida akepio nakokuju toma akuan;" 
Romans2:29 dimarai ŋol loerai Eyudayat kotoma, ka akepio nakotau kotoma omoyo kwabo mere aiwadikaet. Akeiturio mam ebuni kotuŋa dimarai kama ejai Edeke." 
Romans3:1 Itelekarit kereka Eyudayat kinyo? Arai anyoin bo ajokis naka akepio? 
Romans3:2 Itelekarit noi kaŋolipone. Nasodit, naarai isiŋadikinitai Iyudayan akiro nuka Edeke." 
Romans3:3 Anyoika bo arai ice kakesi araas lumere lumunon? Amamus amunonutukec itapalauni tope amunonut naka Edeke? 
Romans3:4 Madi akuj! Korai Edeke lokabeit, ŋinituŋanan da ikeŋalan, kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Tetere itojokio araut loedolit kakirokon, Ipikori da kotoma atubokiniokon.”" 
Romans3:5 Konye arai amamus adolitewok iticasi adolit naka Edeke, kenera anu? Ebe Mam Edeke erai loedolit aitican oni kanyunyura? (Enera kopone loka etuŋanan.)" 
Romans3:6 Madi akuj! Kanuka ŋun ikonakini ai Edeke etubokini akwapin? 
Romans3:7 Konye arai kanuka aiŋalaka iyatanakini abeit naka Edeke aitodiar akeibuses, kanukinyo eriŋa katubokinitere eoŋ kwape ekadiakanaran?" 
Romans3:8 Ido kanukinyo mam kibalar ebe, “Keswamata nukaronok tetere epote nukajokak”? kwape kisabanakiniata icetuŋa sio ebe kinera isio kwaŋin, Edolit atubokiniokec." 
Romans3:9 Biai bo do? Kijokuka oni aitelekarit ice? Mam cut, nepepec da; naarai kidau aosan Iyudayan ka Iyonanin da kere ebe eyait adiakanar kes," 
Romans3:10 kwape iwadikatere ebe: “Emamei ikadoliton, karaida idiopet;" 
Romans3:11 Emamei yenejenuni, emamei da yenemoot Edeke." 
Romans3:12 Apaasi kere, emamei kes kere ajokis; Emamei yeniswamai nuejok, emamei karaida idiopet.”" 
Romans3:13 “Elogorotokec ŋes ailit naeŋaara; Ijodijodete kaŋajepakec, Eiai aisorit naka emusaga kwap kaŋajepakec.”" 
Romans3:14 “Ileleba aitukekec elamit ka adwaris.” 
Romans3:15 “Erurukito akejenekec abukor aokot," 
Romans3:16 Ejai amudiar ka aburun orotinikec," 
Romans3:17 Mam apotu kojenut erot loka ainapakin.” 
Romans3:18 “Emamei ayoŋit Edeke kakonyenekec.” 
Romans3:19 Aso kijeni ebe akiro kere nuelimito ikisila, inerasi mama ejaas ŋul lueyaito ikisila, tetere itubutario ŋiniituk, akwap kere da kojau otube loka Edeke." 
Romans3:20 Kanuka ŋun emamei yenejai akuan yenitojokio araut yenedolit kakonyeneke kanuka aswamisio nuka ikisila, naarai kanuka ikisila ŋes ejenunor adiakar." 
Romans3:21 Konye kwana edeleleu adolit naka Edeke komameete ikisila, itejenunitai kokisila ka inabin da," 
Romans3:22 ŋes adolit naka Edeke naejai kanuka aiyuun Yesu Kristo, mama ejaas kere luiyuunito. Naarai emamei atiaketait;" 
Romans3:23 naarai adiakasi kere, komam edolokinito aibuses naka Edeke," 
Romans3:24 akesianut naeinakini atitai ŋes itojokit kes araut luedolito, kanuka alakunio naejai toma Kristo Yesu," 
Romans3:25 loibwaikinit Edeke araut aitupucet kanuka aiyuun akeokot, tetere itodikini akedolit kanuka ajalakin adiakanareta nukolo nueŋirikinit Edeke;" 
Romans3:26 kosodi kitodik adoliteke kapak kana, tetere eraun loedolit ka loitojoki da ŋin yeniyuuni Yesu araut loedolit." 
Romans3:27 Aso ai bo ejai aolobobot? Agolor kiŋa, Kanuka ikisila inyoika tope? Luka aswamisio? Mam cut, konye kanuka ikisila luka aiyuun." 
Romans3:28 Naarai kitogogoŋit ebe itojokio ituŋanan araut yenedolit kanuka aiyuun, komameete aswamisio nuka ikisila." 
Romans3:29 Erai kereka Edeke loka Iyudayan bon? Mam kereka erai loka Imo da? Eebo, loka Imo da," 
Romans3:30 naarai erai Edeke ediopet; loitojoki luekepitai kotoma aiyuun, ka lumam ekepitai da kanuka aiyuun ŋipeŋin." 
Romans3:31 Aso kitapalauni kereka ikisila kanuka aiyuun ŋin? Madi akuj! Konye kiticasi ikisila. 
Romans4:1 Aso kinera anyoika nuka Aburaam papaakosi kwape ejaar akuan? 
Romans4:2 Naarai arai kitojokitai Aburaam kanuka aswamisioke, ejai naeolobobaa, konye mere kakonyen nuka Edeke." 
Romans4:3 Naarai inerasi biai nuiwadikatai? Ebe, “Abu Aburaam kiyu Edeke, kimarakinai ŋes araun adolit.”" 
Romans4:4 Konye mama ejai ekeswaman, mam ekeropit imarakinio kanuka asianut, dimarai iburao." 
Romans4:5 Kwabo mama ejai yenimam iswamai, konye iyuuni ŋol loitojoki luetumaaka, imarakinio akeiyuun araun adolit." 
Romans4:6 Kwape inerar Daudi ebe isirereŋitoi ituŋanan yenimarakinit Edeke araun ikadoliton komameete aswamisio; 
Romans4:7 Ebe, “Isirereŋitoi luisionio aronisio, ka luerapitai da adiakanareta;" 
Romans4:8 Isirereŋitoi etuŋanan lomam Ejakait imarakinit adiakar.” 
Romans4:9 Aso ca isirereŋitoi ŋol loekepitai arai bo ŋol lomam ekepitai da? Naarai kinera ebe, Kimarakinai aiyuun naka Aburaam araun adolit." 
Romans4:10 Kimarakinio biai? Kedaun aikep, arai bo eroko kekepa? Mere kedaun aikep, dimarai eroko ekepa," 
Romans4:11 Abu ŋesi kodum akepio araun aanyunet arai nakaipucakinet naka adolit naka akeiyuun eroko ekepa, tetere eraun papa loka lukeyuunak kere karaida mam ekepitai, tetere imarakinio kes adolit." 
Romans4:12 Eraun da papa loka akepio mere mama ejaas ŋul luekepitai bon, konye mama ejaas ŋul da luetupito ikukut luka aiyuun naka papaakosi Aburaam nakejaatar eriŋa ekepa." 
Romans4:13 Naarai aisumunet ŋin mama ejai Aburaam ka aurike da ebe eraun ekeruman loka akwapin, mam kebuni kokisila, dimarai kanuka adolit naka aiyuun," 
Romans4:14 Naarai arai luka ikisila kes ikerumak, eraun aiyuun atitai, aisumunet da itapalaunio." 
Romans4:15 Naarai eyaŋaunete ikisila anyunyura, konye naemameatar ikisila emamei apaar." 
Romans4:16 Kanuka ŋun ebuni aisumunet kotoma aiyuun, tetere egoŋakina aisumunet asianut, kitogogoŋoi da mama ejai aur kere, mere mama ejaas ŋul luka ikisila bon, dimarai mama ejaas ŋul luka aiyuun naka Aburaam, (loerai papaawok kere," 
Romans4:17 kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Kadakaki jo araun papa loka atekerin nuipu,”) kakonyen nuka Edeke loiyuunit ŋesi, loeinakini lukatwak aijar, loenyarauni da iboro luemameete bala luejaas." 
Romans4:18 Kemamei amun abu kiyuu kotoma amun, tetere eraun papa loka atekerin nuipu; kwape kelimokinere ebe, “Kwape kwaŋin ejaun akoniwur.”" 
Romans4:19 Mam abu akeiyuun kononokiar, naaomitor ejautene loka akuanake naketwanit, nakeraar loka ikar bala akwatat, ka akoik da naka Sara nakerakakinit," 
Romans4:20 konye mam abu kobuonokin kanuka aisumunet naka Edeke kamamus aiyuun, dimarai kogogoŋor kaiyuun, kitopoloo Edeke," 
Romans4:21 kojeni cut ebe epedori Edeke aswam nuisumunit. 
Romans4:22 Kanuka ŋun, “kimarakinai ŋes adolit.”" 
Romans4:23 Konye mam kiwadikatai kanukeŋ bon ebe, “Kimarakinai ŋes”," 
Romans4:24 dimarai kanuwok da, Kiponio aimarakin oni da lukiyuunit ŋol lokitajaruni Yesu Ejakaitiwok kokatwak," 
Romans4:25 lokeinakinio kanuka aibucanaretawok, kitajarunai da aitojok oni araun luedolito." 
Romans5:1 Aso naarai kitojokitai araun luedolito kanuka aiyuun, kajaut kainapakin mama ejai Edeke kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo." 
Romans5:2 Kanukeŋ kidumu erot loka aiyuun lokitodoli asianut ŋin nakibwoia, kiwoloboboi da kotoma amun aibuses naka Edeke." 
Romans5:3 Kwabo mere ŋun bon, dimarai kiwoloboboi da kotoma aiticanio, kajenete ebe aiticanio eyaŋauni atitiŋikin," 
Romans5:4 atitiŋikin da eyaŋauni aitogogoŋio, aitogogoŋio da eyaŋauni amun," 
Romans5:5 amun da mam itisili, naarai ekwamakinitai amin naka Edeke otauonowok kanuka Emoyo Lokalaunan lokiinakinitai oni." 
Romans5:6 Naarai nakirokor kikalanyaka, kedol apak abu Kristo kotwanik luetumaaka," 
Romans5:7 Naarai etiono ituŋanan atwanikin ikadoliton, konye diat eluŋakin ituŋanan aŋirikin atwanikin yenejok." 
Romans5:8 Konye iturit Edeke akemin mamawok, naarai nakirokor kirai ikadiakanarak abu Kristo kotwanik oni." 
Romans5:9 Aso aitelekarit noi kiidau kwana aitojokio kotoma akeokot, kitajario da kanukeŋ alemunio kama ejai anyunyura." 
Romans5:10 Naarai arai nakiraar kolo lukasurup kitupucitoi kEdeke kanuka atwanare naka Okokuke, aitelekarit noi kiidau aitupucio, kitajario kotoma aijarake." 
Romans5:11 Kwabo mere ŋun bon, konye kiwoloboboi da kotoma Edeke, kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, lokidumunia kwana aitupuciowok." 
Romans5:12 Kanuka ŋun kwape kelomunia adiakanar akwapin kanuka etuŋanan ediopet, kolom da atwanare kanuka adiakar, kwaŋin kodolok atwanare otuŋa kere, naarai apotu kere kodiakasi—" 
Romans5:13 naarai ajai adiakar toma akwap aliŋakin ikisila, konye mam emaritai adiakar naemameatar ikisila," 
Romans5:14 Konye erumit atwanare ameun ka Adam kiton Musa, erumit da ŋesi lumam apotu kodiakasi kopone loka apaar naka Adam, loerai aput naka ŋol kaloebunit." 
Romans5:15 Konye ainakinet mam eputos kaibucaret. Naarai arai apotu luipu kotwaka kanuka aibucaret naka ediopet, aitelekarit noi epoloor asianut naka Edeke ka ainakinet naejai toma asianut naka etuŋanan ediopet Yesu Kristo, kanuka luipu." 
Romans5:16 Ido ainakinet mam eputos kanaayau loadiakaa. Naarai etube loabu kobu kanuka ediopetuŋanan abu koyau atubokinio, konye ainakinet naabu kobu kanuka aibucanareta nuipu ayau aitojokio." 
Romans5:17 Aso, arai kanuka aibucar naka ediopetuŋanan abu atwanare kirum kanuka etuŋanan ŋol, aitelekarit noi ŋul luedumunete aipadara naka asianut ka ainakinet naka adolit irumete toma aijar kanuka etuŋanan ŋol ediopet, Yesu Kristo." 
Romans5:18 Aso ca kwape iriaria aibucaret adiopet ituŋa kere atubokinio, kwape kwaŋin iriaria aswamisioit adiopet nakadolit ituŋa kere aitojokio ka aiiar da." 
Romans5:19 Naarai kwape keraunotor luipu ikadiakanarak kanuka epali loka ediopetuŋanan, kwape kwaŋin itaraunio luipu ikadolitok kanuka arima naka etuŋanan ediopet," 
Romans5:20 Apotu ikisila kolomut tetere iyatanakin aibucar; konye nekiyatakinor adiakar, abu asianut kodepa noi noi," 
Romans5:21 tetere kwape erumitor adiakar kotoma atwanare, kwape kwaŋin irumi asianut kanuka adolit kiton aijar naka ikar kere kanuka Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok." 
Romans6:1 Aso do kinera anu? Kasalakis kereka adiakanar, tetere iyatakin asianut?" 
Romans6:2 Madi akuj! Oni lukitwaka kama kadiakar kikwaikini ai kirina kibusi kotomakeŋ? 
Romans6:3 Arai bo mam ijenete ebe oni kere lukibatisatai kotoma Kristo Yesu, aponi kibatisai kotoma atwanareke?" 
Romans6:4 Aso aponi kidaai nepepe kaŋes kanuka aibatis kotoma atwanare, tetere kwape kitajarunere Kristo kokatwak kanuka aibuses naka Papa, kwape kwaŋin oni da kilosenenei kaijar nakitetet." 
Romans6:5 Naarai arai kirotakinitai kaŋes kotoma aput naka atwanareke, kwape kwaŋin kirotakinio kotoma aput naka ajarunike." 
Romans6:6 Kijeni na ebe aponi etuŋananiwok lokolo kibubukinoi kaŋes, tetere itapalaunio akuan nakadiakanar, komam bobo adiakanar kitubuleseni oni." 
Romans6:7 Naarai yenatwana eosikinitai anyoun kadiakar," 
Romans6:8 Konye arai kipou katwaka nepepe ka Kristo, kiyuunit ebe kijari da nepepe kaŋes." 
Romans6:9 Kijeni ebe kedau Kristo ajarun kokatwak, mam etwani bobo, mam bobo atwanare eyait ŋes." 
Romans6:10 Naarai atwanare naketwani, abu kotwanik adiakar irwan atipet bon, konye aijar naejari, ejari mama ejai Edeke." 
Romans6:11 Yes da kwape kwaŋin koomito bonik araut lukatwak kama ejai adiakar, konye ikajarak mama ejai Edeke kotoma Kristo Yesu." 
Romans6:12 Aso kinye adiakar airum awatekus nuetwakete, yes arimar aiŋobelekec," 
Romans6:13 Kwabo sirijaikinete akusitutubeta mama ejai adiakar aitwasamaa amamus adolit, dimarai kijaikis bonik mama ejai Edeke, kwape ikajarak luanyout kokatwak, akusitutubeta da mama ejai Edeke aitwasamaa adolit;" 
Romans6:14 naarai mam adiakar kiyait yes, naarai mere ikisila kiyaito yes, dimarai asianut." 
Romans6:15 Biai bo do? Kadiakasi, naarai mam ikisila kiyaito oni, dimarai asianut? Madi akuj!" 
Romans6:16 Mam kereka ijenete ebe loijaikinos bonik arimar kwape ibulesin, iraas do ibulesin luka ŋol kaloirimarito, arai adiakar naeyauni atwanare, arai bo arima naeyauni adolit?" 
Romans6:17 Konye kimalai Edeke, naarai iraas kolo ibulesin luka adiakar, konye ipotu korimasi kotauonokus aput naka aisisianakin nakiinakinio yes," 
Romans6:18 ido nakiwosikinere anyoun kadiakar koraut ibulesin luka adolit. 
Romans6:19 Enera eoŋ kopone loka etuŋanan kanuka akalanyanut naka awatekus. Naarai kwape kijaikiniata kolo atutubetakus aitwasamao kotoma amodokok, ka epali loeyauni epali, kwape kwaŋin kijaikis do kwana atutubetakus aitwasamao kotoma adolit naeyauni aitalaunio." 
Romans6:20 Naarai nakiraatar ibulesin luka adiakar, kiwosikinitai anyoun kadolit." 
Romans6:21 Anyoika kereka araito nuipotu kodumut kapaarasia kaŋun, kakiro kaŋun nukisurumito kwana ileic? Naarai awasia naka akiro kaŋun ŋes atwanare." 
Romans6:22 Konye kwana kidaut aosikinio anyoun kadiakar iraut ibulesin luka Edeke, idumut araito nueyaunete alaunit, awasiakec da ŋes aijar naka ikar kere." 
Romans6:23 Naarai eropit loka adiakar ŋes atwanare, konye ainakinet naka Edeke erai aijar naka ikar kere kotoma Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok." 
Romans7:1 Iinacan, mam kereka ijenete-naarai enera kaŋul kaluejenete ikisila ebe eyaito ikisila etuŋanan eroko ejari?" 
Romans7:2 Naarai eenito ikisila aberu naemanyitai eroko okilenike ejari; konye ketwana ekiliokit, eosikinitai ŋin kokisila luka okilenike." 
Romans7:3 Kanuka ŋun enyarao naadote arai kedumun kecekiliokit, apak naeriŋar okilenike ejari. Konye arai ketwana okilenike, eosikinitai anyoun kokisila, mam da erai naadote arai kemany ekiliokit ece." 
Romans7:4 Ikainacan, yes da kwape kwaŋin ipotu kotwakata kama kikisila, kanuka akuan naka Kristo, tetere iraunos luka ece, ŋes ŋol loitajarunitai kokatwak, tetere kidumakini Edeke araito." 
Romans7:5 Naarai nakiraar kolo luka akuan, abu airaŋaanut naka adiakar kiswama kotoma atutubetawok kanuka ikisila, kasodete adumakin atwanare araito." 
Romans7:6 Konye kwana kiwosikinitai anyoun kokisila, kitwaka kama ejai ŋin nakijoreorit, kasodete kejaanakis komoyo lokitetet kwabo mere kaiwadikaet namojoŋ." 
Romans7:7 Aso do kinera anu? Eraas kereka ikisila adiakar? Madi akuj! Konye timam kajenu adiakar kedim ikisila. Naarai timam kajenu aiŋobel kedim ikisila atemar ebe, “Siriŋobelei.”" 
Romans7:8 Konye adiakar, naabu kodum apak kanuka aicorakinet, kiswama kotomakaŋ ŋolipone loka aiŋobel, Naarai etwanit adiakar emameete ikisila." 
Romans7:9 Abu eoŋ karai kolo loajari komameete ikisila, konye nakebunio aicorakinet kojaru adiakar, katwana do eoŋ." 
Romans7:10 Kerai aicorakinet naeyauni aijar kosubite ŋin kamakaŋ naeyauni atwanare. 
Romans7:11 Naarai abu adiakar, naabu kodum apak kanuka aicorakinet, keŋala eoŋ, kaaria da." 
Romans7:12 Kwaŋin eraas ikisila lukalaunak, ka aicorakinet da nakalaunan, ka naedolit ka naejok da." 
Romans7:13 Aso do koraun kereka ajokis atwanare kamakaŋ? Madi akuj! Konye adiakar, tetere etakanuni araut adiakar, abu kiswama atwanare kotomakaŋ kanuka ajokis, tetere iyatakin adiakar araut adiakar naerono noi kanuka aicorakinet," 
Romans7:14 Naarai kijeni ebe eraas ikisila luka emoyo; konye eoŋ arai lokakuan, kagwelaritai ayait naka adiakar." 
Romans7:15 Naarai mam ajeni nueswamai, Naarai nuakoto, mere kes nueswamai, konye eswamai nualait." 
Romans7:16 Konye arai eswamai numam akoto, acamunit ebe ejokuka ikisila." 
Romans7:17 Aso kwana mere eoŋ eswamai ŋun dimarai adiakar naiboie kotomakaŋ," 
Romans7:18 Naarai ajeni ebe emamei ibore yenejok yeniboie kotomakaŋ, ŋes atemar ebe toma akuanaka. Naarai ejai akote diekaŋ, konye aswam ajokis be." 
Romans7:19 Naarai mam eswamai ajokis naakoto, konye aronis namam akoto, ŋes eswamai." 
Romans7:20 Konye arai eswamai numam akoto, mam bobo eoŋ eswamai dimarai adiakar naiboie kotomakaŋ." 
Romans7:21 Kwaŋin adumuni ekisil ebe naakotor eoŋ aswam nuejok, kaapikin aronis." 
Romans7:22 Naarai alelakinit ikisila luka Edeke kotoma otuŋanan lokotoma," 
Romans7:23 Konye aanyuni ekisil ece kotoma atutubetaka ejiosi kekisil loka aomisioka, ka aituluor eŋatara loka ekisil loka adiakar loejai toma atutubetaka." 
Romans7:24 Itukwi eoŋ lokican! Iŋai bo kayuuni eoŋ kakuan kana nakatwanare? 
Romans7:25 Emalai Edeke kanuka Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok! Aso do eoŋ elopet ejaanakini ekisil loka Edeke kaomisioka, kwabo ekisil loka adiakar kakuanaka." 
Romans8:1 Aso do kwana emamei ŋul luejaas toma Kristo Yesu atubokinio. 
Romans8:2 Naarai kaosikis eoŋ ikisila luka Emoyo loka aijar loejai toma Kristo Yesu anyoun kokisila luka adiakar ka atwanare. 
Romans8:3 Naarai ŋun numam apedorito ikisila, kanuka akalanyanut naka akuan, abu Edeke, naejukunia Okokuke elopet kaput naka akuan nakadiakaran ido kanuka adiakar, kotubok adiakar kotoma akuan," 
Romans8:4 tetere aicorakineta nuka ikisila itodolikinio kotomawok, lumam kilosenenei atupar akuan dimarai atupar Emoyo." 
Romans8:5 Naarai ŋul luetuparete akuan eomitos nuka akuan, konye ŋul luetuparete Emoyo, eomitos nuka Emoyo." 
Romans8:6 Naarai aomit naka akuan ŋes atwanare, konye aomit naka Emoyo ŋes aijar ka ainapakin."
