Romans8:7 Kanuka ŋun aomit naka akuan ŋes aitusurup Edeke; naarai mam enonokikinit ikisila luka Edeke, kwabo mam epedori anonokikin;" 
Romans8:8 kes da luejaas toma akuan mam epedorete aisiyalamikin Edeke. 
Romans8:9 Konye arai iboie Emoyo loka Edeke kotomakus, mam ijaas toma akuan dimarai toma Omoyo. Arai da emamei ituŋanan Emoyo loka Kristo, mam ŋin erai yenike." 
Romans8:10 Konye arai ejai Kristo kotomakus, atwakata awatekus kanuka adiakar, konye ejarete ikusimoyon kanuka adolit." 
Romans8:11 Konye arai iboie Emoyo loka ŋol lokitajaruni Yesu kokatwak kotomakus, ŋol lokitajaruni Kristo Yesu kokatwak einakini da akusiwat nuetwakete aijar kanuka Ekemoyo loiboie kotomakus." 
Romans8:12 Aso do, iinacan, kija kapesen, mere mama ejai akuan atupar aijar naka akuan," 
Romans8:13 naarai arai ijarete atupar akuan, ikotosi atwakare, konye arai kitwataniasi aswamisio nuka akuan kanuka Emoyo, ijarete do." 
Romans8:14 Naarai kere luiŋarenikinit Emoyo loka Edeke, ŋul kes odwe luka Edeke," 
Romans8:15 Naarai mam idumunito emoyo loka ebulesene aboŋor bobo akurian, dimarai idumunito emoyo loka araun odwe. Kanuka ŋol kimonya ebe, “Abba! Papa!”" 
Romans8:16 Emoyo elopet itejenikini imoyonowok ebe kirai idwe luka Edeke," 
Romans8:17 arai kirai idwe, kirai da ikerumak, ikerumak luka Edeke, luirumete nepepe ka Kristo, arai ca kiiticani nepepe kaŋes, tetere kitubusikinio da kaŋes." 
Romans8:18 Aomit eoŋ ebe aiticanio naka apak kana mam ibusakinit aitiirianio kaibuses naekoto apukokinio oni. 
Romans8:19 Naarai idarete isuban keimiel noi apukokinio naka odwe luka Edeke; 
Romans8:20 naarai kitononokikinai isuban aamameak, mere kanuka eipudikec, dimarai kanuka ŋol lokitononokikini kotoma amun;" 
Romans8:21 naarai eosikinio isuban da anyoun kobulesene loka aibos, alomar aosikinio naka aibuses naka idwe luka Edeke." 
Romans8:22 Naarai kijeni ebe idinyasi isuban kere, eriebasi da nepepe kiton tinenikwana;" 
Romans8:23 kwabo mere ŋul bon, dimarai oni da ikulepek luejaas araito nugeet nuka Emoyo, kidinya oni da kotomawok, kedareto araut odwe, ŋes atemar ebe alakun naka awatewok" 
Romans8:24 Naarai kiponi kitajari kanuka amun. Konye ketakanu ibore yenikemunoi emamei bobo amun. Naarai iŋai tope emunokina ibore yenetakani? 
Romans8:25 Konye arai kimunokina yenimam etakani, kidaret katitiŋikin." 
Romans8:26 Kwape kwaŋin da isigalikini Emoyo akalanyanutuwok; naarai mam kijeni kwape ibusakinitor ailip, konye kinainaanakin Emoyo oni keidiny lomam inerio," 
Romans8:27 Ŋol da loirerei itauon ejeni aomisio nuka Emoyo, kwape ejaatar, naarai iŋaiŋaaŋakini lukalaunak kwape ekotor Edeke," 
Romans8:28 Kijeni ebe iswamaete iboro kere nepepe kanuka ajokis mama ejaas ŋul lueminasi Edeke, ŋes atemar ŋul lukenyaraunio kanuka alosikiniteke." 
Romans8:29 Naarai ŋul luabu kojenu sek, abu koseu da sek aituput kes aput naka Okokuke, tetere erauni ŋesi ekiyai kotoma oinacan luipu." 
Romans8:30 Ŋul da luabu koseu sek, konyarau da kes; ŋul da luabu konyarau, kitojok da kes; ŋul da luabu kitojok, kitubusik da kes." 
Romans8:31 Aso do kinera anu kaŋun? Arai ejai Edeke kanuwok iŋai tope kisurokini oni? 
Romans8:32 Ŋol lomam abu kimik Okokuke elopet, konye koinak ŋes kanuwok kere, mam kereka kikorakini iboro kere da nepepe kaŋes?" 
Romans8:33 Iŋai bo iwosai luseuna luka Edeke? Edeke itojokit; 
Romans8:34 iŋai bo etubokini? Kristo Yesu loketwani, konye aitelekarit lokitajarunio, loejai akan nakoteten naka Edeke, loiŋaiŋaanakini oni." 
Romans8:35 Iŋai bo kitiaki oni kamin naka Kristo? Arai bo ican, arai aridakinio, arai areio, arai ebeli, arai amujalal, arai aronis, arai ekileŋ?" 
Romans8:36 Kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Kanukon kiario aitiwar akwap, Kimario bala amerekekin nutubutubo.”" 
Romans8:37 Konye kotoma ŋun kere kipikori noi kanuka ŋol lokimina oni. 
Romans8:38 Naarai etogogoŋi ebe karaida atwanare, karaida aiiar, karaida imalaikan, karaida lueyaito, karaida nuejaas, karaida nuejaunete, karaida lukapedor," 
Romans8:39 karaida amukurur, karaida aidules, karaida isubat kere, mam kipedorete aitiak oni kamin naka Edeke naejai toma Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok." 
Romans9:1 Enera abeit kotoma Kristo, mam eŋalai; itejenunete akaomisio kotoma Emoyo Lokalaunan," 
Romans9:2 ebe kakadakinit noi ka ariebo da namam enaŋi kotauka. 
Romans9:3 Naarai tikapedo ailip eoŋ elopet aikenio atiakario kama ka Kristo kanuka ikainacan, lukatekerika kwape ejaar akuan," 
Romans9:4 kes luka Isirael, lukeinakinio araut odwe, ka aibuses, ka aitutuketa, ka ainakinio ikisila, ka aijaanakin Edeke, ka aisumuneta da;" 
Romans9:5 eraas lukapapaa lukec, ido kotomakec alomunia Kristo kwape ejaar akuan. Kituritete Edeke loeyait kere ikar ka ikar. Amen." 
Romans9:6 Kwabo mere ebe ekarun akirot naka Edeke. Naarai luelomunete kotoma Isirael, mere kere luka Isirael obe," 
Romans9:7 karaida keraas lukaur naka Aburaam, mam kere eraas idwe; konye “toma Isaak ŋes enyaritere akoniwur.”" 
Romans9:8 Ŋes atemar ebe idwe luka akuan mere ŋul idwe luka Edeke, dimarai idwe luka aisumunet imaritai araut akeur." 
Romans9:9 Naarai akirot na ŋes ebalar aisumunet ebe, “Kedol apak, aboŋuni, ido ejaunete Sara da kikoku.”" 
Romans9:10 Kwabo mere ŋin bon, konye Rebeka da kedum akoik kokiliokit ediopet, ŋes Isaak papaawok," 
Romans9:11 karaida mam ber euruunitai idwe ŋul, komam iswamato adiokirot naejok arai naerono, tetere icasit alosikinit naka Edeke naka aseun, mere kanuka aswamisio, dimarai kanuka anyariteke," 
Romans9:12 aponi kolimokinai ŋin ebe, “Ijaanakini lokapolon lodidi.”" 
Romans9:13 Kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Abu kamina Yakob, konye kala Esau.”" 
Romans9:14 Aso kinera anu? Ejai kereka amamus adolit kaneejai Edeke? Madi akuj! 
Romans9:15 Naarai ebala ŋesi Musa ebe, “Etimi yenakoto aitim, ido ekonakini asianut yenakoto aikonakin asianut.”" 
Romans9:16 Aso do mere kanuka loekot karaida loekeri, dimarai kanuka aitim naka Edeke." 
Romans9:17 Naarai ebala nakiwadikatai Parao ebe, “Kanuka nu ŋes ketonyounio jo tetere etodikini akapedor mamakon, ido tetere elimorio ekakiror kakwapin kere.”" 
Romans9:18 Aso do itimi loekot, ido itininiki loekot." 
Romans9:19 Aso kitemari eoŋ ebe, “Kanukinyo eriŋar ŋesi itoronitor? Naarai iŋai kereka enyoikini nuelosikinit ŋesi?”" 
Romans9:20 Ijo ba ituŋanan, iŋai bo ijo yeniboŋokini Edeke? Epedori kereka ibore yenisubuna alimokin yenikesubuni ebe, “Kanukinyo kiisubia eoŋ kwana?”" 
Romans9:21 Emamei kereka ekajean apedor kama kelupe, asubun ibore yenibus ka ibore da yenesil kaluŋuret ŋipeŋin?" 
Romans9:22 Konye anyoika bo arai ekoto Edeke aitodikin anyunyura ka aitejenun da akepedor, abu kotitiŋikin katitiŋ kanaepol iboro luka anyunyura luasubitai amudiario," 
Romans9:23 tetere itejenuni abarara naka akeibuses kotoma oboro luka aitim, luetemonokinit apeŋo kodumut aibuses," 
Romans9:24 kes oni lukiinyarauni mere Iyudayan bonik, dimarai Imo da?" 
Romans9:25 Kwape kineritor da kama ka Kosea ebe, “Ŋul lumam araas ikatuŋa, anyarai ikatuŋa, ŋin da namam kerai naminataka, anyarai naminat.”" 
Romans9:26 “Bobo da toma aibois ŋin nakelimokinitere kes ebe, ‘Mam yes iraas ikatuŋa,’ Nepenen enyaraere idwe luka Edeke lokajaran.”" 
Romans9:27 Kiworo Isaia da nuka Isirael ebe, “Karaida kerai etiai loka odwe luka Isirael kwape asiŋe naka aŋolol, aatoŋotokec bon itajario;" 
Romans9:28 naarai iswamai Ejakait akekirot kakwap aitodol ka atubutub da.” 
Romans9:29 Ido kwape kegeunia Isaia einer ebe: “Arai kemam Ejakait loka ajoresio kinyeinitor oni aur, Ti kiirau bala Sodom, ti kiiputokin ka Gomora.”" 
Romans9:30 Aso do kinera anu? Ebe Imo lumam atupito adolit apotu kodumut adolit, ŋes adolit naelomuni kaiyuun." 
Romans9:31 Konye do luka Isirael luetupito ikisila luka adolit, mam edolokinito ikisila ŋul." 
Romans9:32 Kanukinyo? Naarai mam apotu kotupata korot loka aiyuun, dimarai korot loka aswamisio. Kitiguikinos kamoru naketiguikinan," 
Romans9:33 kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Koany, ebwaikini toma Sion amoru naketiguikinan ka atiiba nakebiroron; Yeniyuuni ŋes mam isurumio ileic.”" 
Romans10:1 Ikainacan, nuemiela kotauka, ido nuelipi Edeke kanukec ŋes aitajariokec." 
Romans10:2 Naarai etejenuni kanukec ebe edunyaka kanuka Edeke, konye mere kotoma aijen," 
Romans10:3 Naarai kanumam ejeniata adolit naka Edeke, kokotos aitogogoŋ adolitekec kikulepek, mam apotu korimasi adolit naka Edeke." 
Romans10:4 Naarai Kristo ŋes aŋetakinet naka ikisila, tetere ŋin yeniyuuni itojokio araut ikadoliton." 
Romans10:5 Naarai abu Musa kiwadik ebe ituŋanan yeniswamai adolit naelomuni kokisila ejari kotoma ŋin. 
Romans10:6 Konye adolit naelomuni kaiyuun inera kwanata ebe, Sirikiner kotaukon ebe, “Iŋai bo yenekot adokari toma akuj?” (Ŋes atemar ebe, ayaun Kristo kwap.)" 
Romans10:7 Arai bo ebe, “Iŋai bo yenekot aijesar toma aipany?” (Ŋes atemar ebe, ayaun Kristo kuju anyoun kokatwak.)" 
Romans10:8 Konye inera anu? Ebe, Eapie akirot kamakon, kaitukukon, kotaukon da, (ŋes atemar ebe akirot naka aiyuun nakilimonokini isio)." 
Romans10:9 Naarai arai ilimori kaitukukon ebe Yesu ŋes Ejakait, iyuuni da kotaukon ebe abu Edeke kitajar ŋes kokatwak, kitajario." 
Romans10:10 Naarai iyuuni ituŋanan kotauke kiton adumun adolit, elimori da kaitukuke kiton adumun aitajario," 
Romans10:11 Naarai ineras nuiwadikatai ebe, “Ŋin yeniyuuni ŋes mam irumete ileic.”" 
Romans10:12 Naarai emamei atiaketait, Eyudayat ka Eyonanit; naarai erai ŋesi Ejakait loka kere, ekabaran mama ejaas kere luiwoneete ŋes." 
Romans10:13 Naarai “Ŋin yeniwonei ekiror loka Ejakait itajario.” 
Romans10:14 Aso iwoneete biai ŋol lomam iyuunito? Ido da iyuunete biai ŋol lomam iirarito? Iirarete da biai komamei ekalimonokinan? 
Romans10:15 Elimonokinete biai komam iyakiaritai? Kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Ejokuka cama akeje nuka ŋul kaluelimonokinete Akiro Nukajokak!”" 
Romans10:16 Konye mam kes kere apotu korimasi akiro nukajokak. Naarai inera Isaia ebe, “Ejakait, iŋai bo iyuunit akiro nueirarit kamakosi?”" 
Romans10:17 Aso aiyuun elomuni kotoma aiirar, aiirar da kanuka akirot naka Kristo." 
Romans10:18 Konye abala eoŋ ebe, mam kereka apotu kiirasi? Eebo, eirasi; “Anata ekeceporoto akwap kere, Akecekiro da kiton osaŋeta luka akwapin.”" 
Romans10:19 Konye abala eoŋ ebe, mam kereka luka Isirael ajenunito? Nugeet inera Musa ebe, “Kesurumi yes ekokote kama kaŋul lumam eraas ateker; Ketunyunyurikini do yes kanuka ateker naemamei aijen.”" 
Romans10:20 Isaia da etitiŋ noi einer ebe, “Abu kadumun kama kaŋul lumam kamooto; Abu ketejenun mama kaŋul lumam keŋisito.”" 
Romans10:21 Konye nuka Isirael ebala ebe, “Abu kariorite akakanin aitiwar akwap mama ejaas ituŋa lukepali ka luirebirebete.”" 
Romans11:1 Aso abala ebe, Aŋer kereka Edeke iketuŋa? Madi akuj! Naarai arai eoŋ da loka Isirael, loka aur naka Aburaam, loka ateker naka Benyamin." 
Romans11:2 Mam Edeke enerit iketuŋa luabu kogeu ajenun, Mam kereka ijenete nuineras nuiwadikatai kanuka Eliya, kwape iwosaa luka Isirael kakonyen nuka Edeke?" 
Romans11:3 Ebe, “Ejakait, aarata inabinokon, atiyanakis da itemwanakon, eoŋ bon asal, ido emoete akaijar.”" 
Romans11:4 Konye aboŋokinet naka Edeke ebala biai? Ebe, “Etasalit kanukaŋ ikiliok ilukumin ikanykaarei, lumam ekukokinos Baal.”" 
Romans11:5 Aso kwape kwaŋin apak na, naka kwana, ejai aatoŋot naeseunitai kanuka asianut." 
Romans11:6 Konye arai erai kanuka asianut, mam bobo elomuni kanuka aswamisio; arai timam asianut eroko erai asianut." 
Romans11:7 Biai bo do? Ibore ŋin yenikemoot Isirael, mam edumuna. Luseuna apotu kodumut, konye ice kere aponi kitininikai," 
Romans11:8 kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Abu Edeke koinak kes emoyo loka ajo, Akonye numam eanyunete, Aki da numam iirarete, Kiton apaaran naka lolo.”" 
Romans11:9 Ebala Daudi da ebe, “Korau emesakec eic ka akuluma, Ka ibore yenikitiguikinet, ka yenikitegelet kes," 
Romans11:10 Kitumudakai akonyekec, tetere mam esesenete, Kitukukum ipuranakec apaarasia kere.”" 
Romans11:11 Aso abala ebe, eguikis kereka kiton aibiror cut? Madi akuj! Konye kanuka aibucarikec adolok aitajario Imo, tetere isurumio luka Isirael ekokote." 
Romans11:12 Aso arai eraun aibucarikec abar naka akwapin, atwaniarikec da araun abar naka Imo, itelekarit cama aitodolikiniokec!" 
Romans11:13 Konye enera kayes Imo. Aso naarai arai eoŋ ekiyakia loka imo, etopoloori aijaanakinika," 
Romans11:14 tetere esurumi lukatekerika ekokote, ka aitajar da ice kakesi." 
Romans11:15 Naarai arai acakariokec ayau aipuc naka akwapin, anyoin aisukunyuniokec dimarai aijar anyoun kokatwak?" 
Romans11:16 Arai araito nageet erai nakalaunan, kwape kwaŋin aluŋuret da; arai da aliasit erai nakalaunan, kwape kwaŋin atenieik da." 
Romans11:17 Konye arai epakanaritai ace katenieik, ijo da, eseitun loka ais kiraikinitai kidiŋikec, korau ikamoran yenika ajokis naka aliasit," 
Romans11:18 sirikiwolobob katenieik kaŋun. Arai kiwolobob, mere jo idakit aliasit dimarai aliasit kidakit jo:" 
Romans11:19 Aso itemari atiar, “Kepakario atenieik ŋun tetere keraikinio eoŋ.”" 
Romans11:20 Abeit ŋun. Epakanaritai kes kanuka amamus aiyuunikec, ido da icasi kanuka aiyuunikon. Sirikiturokin, konye koyoŋ." 
Romans11:21 Naarai arai mam Edeke itimit atenieik akulepek, mam kitimi jo da." 
Romans11:22 Aso koany ajokis ka adedeŋ naka Edeke; adedeŋ mama ejaas luibiroros, konye aiokis naka Edeke mamakon, arai kisalak ajokis ŋin; arai mere kwaŋin jo da kijepario." 
Romans11:23 Ka ŋul da, arai mam esalito toma amamus aiyuun, iraikinio, naarai epedori Edeke airaikin kes bobo." 
Romans11:24 Naarai arai kijepunitai jo katorom naka eseitun loka ais, kiraikinitai oseitun lokoriot lomam erai einono, itelekarito cama atenieik akulepek airaikinio ainyakakin oseitunikec." 
Romans11:25 Naarai iinacan, akoto yes ajenun aiyeiyea na kinyeis aomit bonik araut lukacoa; ebe, aninikiar atutubet naka Isirael aitodol naelomunia etiai kere loka Imo," 
Romans11:26 kwaŋin itaiario luka Isirael kere; kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Ebuni Ekalakunan koSion, Isiyekari amamus ayoŋit Edeke kotoma Yakob”;" 
Romans11:27 “Na da ŋes akaitutuket kakes, Naalemaria adiakanaretakec.”" 
Romans11:28 Aso kotoma Akiro Nukajokak araut lukasurup luka Edeke kanukus; konye kotoma aseunio araut lueminai kanuka lukapapaakec. 
Romans11:29 Naarai mam Edeke iitokini ainakinetake ka anyariteke da. 
Romans11:30 Naarai kwape kolo kipaliikinioto yesi Edeke, konye kwana idumut aitimio kanuka aipaliikinikec," 
Romans11:31 kwape kwaŋin epaliikinioto kesi kwape kwana tetere edumunete aitimio kanuka aitim naipotu yesi kodumut. 
Romans11:32 Naarai agoloki Edeke kere nepepe toma aipaliikin, tetere itimi kere." 
Romans11:33 Eiliili cama abar ka acoa ka aijen naka Edeke Mam ireikinos itubesiake, irotinike da mam ibwapunos!" 
Romans11:34 “Naarai iŋai tope ejeni aomisio nuka Ejakait, Arai iŋai bo kerai ekapetan akiroke?”" 
Romans11:35 “Arai iŋai bo keinakinit ber ŋes ainakinet, Etacakinio ŋes bobo?”" 
Romans11:36 Naarai epote iboro kere kamakeŋ, ejaas da kanukeŋ, ido eboŋorete mamakeŋ. Kojai aibuses mamakeŋ ikar kere. Amen." 
Romans12:1 Kanuka ŋun, iinacan, keŋaiŋait yes, kanuka aitimeta nuka Edeke, kijaikis akusiwat koraut asubanit naejari, nakalaunan, naisiyalamikinit Edeke, ŋes erai aimakus naibus." 
Romans12:2 Kwabo sirikiputo nuka ikar kalu, konye kanuka aisiteteunio naka aomisiokus kijulakinos, tetere igimorete nuekoto Edeke, nuejok, ka nuisiyalamikinito, ka nuedolito da." 
Romans12:3 Naarai kanuka asianut nakainakinitai alimokini ŋinituŋanan kayesi ebe siriwomiara adepar naibusakinit aomit, konye koomito kacoit, kwape ekorakinitor Edeke aitemis naka aiyuun." 
Romans12:4 Naarai kwape kijaar katutubeta nuipu toma akuan adiopet, kwabo mam atutubeta kere iswamaete aswam adiopet," 
Romans12:5 kwape kwaŋin oni da lukipu, kirai akuan adiopet kotoma Kristo, ka atutubeta da nuka lucewok bonik ka bonik." 
Romans12:6 Aso naarai kija kainakineta nuegelegela kwape ejaar asianut nakiinakinitai, ketwasamata kes; arai adwaranut, kwape ejaar aiyuuniwok;" 
Romans12:7 arai aijaanakin, kotoma aijaanakiniwok; yenisisianakini, kotoma aisisianakinike;" 
Romans12:8 yenicori, kotoma aicoroke; yenekori, kotau loliogot; yeniŋarakini, kadunyanut; yenitimi da, kaiyalama." 
Romans12:9 Korau amina naemamei aisoswanut. Kolaata aronis, kiketakinos kotoma kanuejok." 
Romans12:10 Kotoma amin naka einacane, kominanaros bonik ka bonik; kotoma aibuses kitopoloorite ŋinituŋanan aupake." 
Romans12:11 Kotoma adunyanut sirikalanyaka, kokokito komoyo, kijaanakis Ejakait." 
Romans12:12 Kolelakinito amun kotitiŋioto koean, kicebokinito ailip." 
Romans12:13 Kokoranakisi lukalaunak nuipudasi, kisukunyanakisi ipejok." 
Romans12:14 Kilipanakisi arereŋ lukimanito yes; kilipanakisi arereŋ kwabo sirikilamata. 
Romans12:15 Kolelata kaluelelete, komonyata kaluemonyete." 
Romans12:16 Koomito adiopekirot bonik ka bonik. Siridakara, konye koupanaros kaluitasonos. Siriraas lukacoa kakonyenekus ikulepek." 
Romans12:17 Siritacakis aronis kanuka aronis, kocoito nuejok kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere." 
Romans12:18 Arai epedoros kowaikus, kinapakina kituŋa kere." 
Romans12:19 Luminan, sirinyaŋanakinos, konye kinac anyunyura; naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Ebala Ejakait ebe, Enyaŋit ekaŋ, eoŋ atacakini.”" 
Romans12:20 Konye “arai eriebi lokasurupikon eteŋei, kitanyam, arai ejakit akur, kitamat ŋes; naarai naiswamaa kwaŋin inokokini atotole akouke.”" 
Romans12:21 Sirikiipiko aronis, konye kipiko aronis kanuka ajokis." 
Romans13:1 Kononokikinite ŋinituŋanan ikapolok lueyaito, naarai emamei apolou dimarai naebuni kama ejai Edeke, ka ŋin da naejai icorakinit Edeke." 
Romans13:2 Kanuka ŋun yenitepegi apolou etepeg aicorakinet naka Edeke, ido luitepegete itudumikinos etube," 
Romans13:3 Naarai ikayaitok mere luitukurianete kotoma aswamisioit naejok, dimarai kotoma naerono. Ikoto kereka ijo kinyek akurian apolou? Kiswama do nuejok, kituri ŋesi joo" 
Romans13:4 Naarai erai ŋesi ekejaanakinan loka Edeke kamakon kanuka ajokis, Konye arai kiswama naerono, kokuriana, naarai mam edakit ekileŋ atai; erai ŋesi ekejaanakinan loka Edeke, loinyaŋi kanyunyura yeniswamai nueroko." 
Romans13:5 Kanuka ŋun ibusakinit anonokikin, mere kanuka anyunyura bon, dimarai kanuka aomisio nuilepilepete." 
Romans13:6 Naarai kanuka ŋun itacete da esolo, naarai eraas kesi ikejaanakinak luka Edeke, icebokinito ŋipeŋin." 
Romans13:7 Kotacanakisi kere nuebeito, loitelemi esolo loka ituŋa, esolo loka ituŋa; loitelemi esolo da loka iboro, esolo loka iboro; kotacanakisi ayoŋit luebeito ayoŋit, aibuses da mama ejaas lukaibuses." 
Romans13:8 Sirijaas kapesen mama ejai ituŋanan kere, dimikito aminanara; naarai yenemina aupake etodol ikisila." 
Romans13:9 Naarai na ebe, “Siridote, Siriari, Sirikokoi, Siriŋobelei,” ka aceicorakinet kere, imorikikinitai toma akirot na ebe, “Komina ikoniidunyet kwape iminar bon.”" 
Romans13:10 Amin mam ikonakini iidunyet erono; kwaŋin amin ŋes aitodolikinet naka ikisila. 
Romans13:11 Ka ŋun da, ijenete apak, ebe adol esawa yes akwenyun kajoo. Naarai kwana eapie aitajariowok aitelekarit nakigeunia aiyuun;" 
Romans13:12 aeka akuar, eapie da apaaran. Aso kalacasi aswamisio nuka amuton, kanapa lujiis luka aica," 
Romans13:13 Kalosenenete kebusak kwape paaran, mere kotoma aboliasio ka emeret, mere kotoma adoteu ka abenyanut, mere kotoma aŋolopa ka ekokote," 
Romans13:14 konye konapa Ejakait Yesu Kristo, kwabo siribuakinito akuan aitodol nuimiela." 
Romans14:1 Kisukunyut yenekalanyana kaiyuun, kwabo mere atubokin abuonokinike." 
Romans14:2 Ituŋanan yeniyuunit enyami kere, konye yenekalanyana enyami ikui." 
Romans14:3 Kinyek yenenyami aimen yenimam enyami, karaida yenimam enyami siriketuboki yenenyami; naarai isukunyikinit Edeke ŋes," 
Romans14:4 Iŋai bo jo yenitubokini ebulesit loka yenice? Ebwoi ŋesi arai ibirori kama kejakaitike elopet. Eebo, isibwoio naarai epedori Ejakait aisibwo ŋes." 
Romans14:5 Eomit ice apaaran adiopet adepar apaaran ace, eomit ice apaarasia kere araut nueriakanara. Kitogogoŋite ŋinituŋanan kaomisioke ilopet." 
Romans14:6 Yenericit apaaran, ericit kanuka Ejakait. Yenenyami da, enyami kanuka Ejakait, naarai imalai Edeke. Yenimam enyami da, mam enyami kanuka Ejakait, imalai da Edeke." 
Romans14:7 Naarai emamei ituŋanan kotomawok yenejari kanuke bon, emamei da yenetwani kanuke bon." 
Romans14:8 Aso arai kijari, kijari kanuka Ejakait, arai kitwaki da, kitwaki kanuka Ejakait. Aso arai kiiari, arai kitwaki da, kirai luka Ejakait." 
Romans14:9 Naarai abu Kristo kotwana kojaru da tetere eraun Ejakait loka lukatwak ka lukajarak da. 
Romans14:10 Konye jo, kanukinyo itubokinia onacekon? Ijo da, kanukinyo imenitor onacekon? Naarai kibwoi rwaru kere kakonyen nuka eicoloŋ loka aitub loka Edeke," 
Romans14:11 Naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Ebala Ejakait ebe, Kwape ajaria, ekukokini ŋinikuŋ mamakaŋ, Elimori da ŋiniŋajep Edeke.”" 
Romans14:12 Aso do inera ŋinituŋanan kaoni akekiro ilopet kakonyen nuka Edeke. 
Romans14:13 Kanuka ŋun kenyeis bobo atubonokin bonik ka bonik, konye aitelekarit kitogogoŋoto na ebe sirikibwaikis ekomio karaida aitiguikinet orot loka onacekon" 
Romans14:14 Ajeni eoŋ bobo da etogogoŋit noi kotoma Ejakait Yesu ebe emamei ibore yeniketal kotoma oinonoke. Konye ŋin yeneomit ibore araut yeniketal, erai yeniketal kamakeŋ." 
Romans14:15 Naarai arai ekadakinit onacekon kanuka inyamatakon, mam bobo ilosi kwape ejaar amin. Sirikimudia yenabu Kristo kotwanik kanuka inyamatakon." 
Romans14:16 Aso kinyek yenejok kamakus ainyanakinio. 
Romans14:17 Naarai ajakanut naka Edeke mere ainyam ka aimat, dimarai adolit ka ainapakin ka aiyalama da kOmoyo Lokalaunan;" 
Romans14:18 naarai ŋin yenijaanakini Kristo kotoma akiro kaŋun, isiyalamikinit Edeke, ecamunito da ituŋa." 
Romans14:19 Aso do katupasi akiro nuka ainapakin ka nuka adukonor bonik ka bonik. 
Romans14:20 Sirikimuna aswam naka Edeke kanuka inyamat. Abeit elaete kere, dimarai erono ituŋanan yenenyami kitiguikinia ice;" 
Romans14:21 ejok ainyein ainyam karaida aimat ebino, karaida aswam akirot kere naitiguikini onacekon," 
Romans14:22 Aiyuun naijaatar, kojaut kaŋin ijo elopet kakonyen nuka Edeke. Isirereŋitoi ŋin yenimam etubokin ilopet kotoma akirot naceamunit." 
Romans14:23 Konye yenebuonokin arai enyami etubokinio aitelekar, naarai mam enyamit kaiyuun; naarai ŋiniswamisioit namam elomuni kaiyuun erai adiakar," 
Romans15:1 Kibusakinit oni lukagogoŋok aibwok akalanyanut naka luemamei agogoŋ, kwabo mere aisiyalamikina bonik." 
Romans15:2 Kesiyalamikisi oni ŋinituŋanan ikeidunyet kodum ajokis kodukoi da. 
Romans15:3 Naarai Kristo da mam esiyalamikina elopet bon; dimarai kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Amorosito nuka lukimoromoroete jo, apotu kadoikis eoŋ.”" 
Romans15:4 Naarai nuewadikatai sek, ewadikatai kanuka aisisianakinia oni, tetere kanuka atitiŋikin ka aitalakara naka nukiwadikatai kidumuni amun." 
Romans15:5 Edeke da loka atitiŋikin ka aitalakara koinak yes aomit adiopet bonik ka bonik koidicane loka Kristo Yesu," 
Romans15:6 tetere itopoloorete Edeke Papa da loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, ketau ediopet ka eporoto da ediopet." 
Romans15:7 Kanuka ŋun, kisukunyanakinos bonik ka bonik, kwape kiisukunyikinia Kristo oni, tetere itopoloorio Edeke." 
Romans15:8 Naarai kalimokini ebe araun Kristo ebulesit loka aitutuket naka akepio kanuka abeit naka Edeke, tetere itogogoŋi aisumuneta nuka lukapapaakosi," 
Romans15:9 bobo da tetere Imo itopoloorete Edeke kanuka akeitim, Kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Kanuka ŋun ŋes kalimonoria jo kotoma atekerin, Ayeikinenei ekonikiror.”" 
Romans15:10 Bobo da ebe, “Kolelata, yes atekerin, nepepe kiketuŋa.”" 
Romans15:11 Bobo da ebe, “Yes atekerin kere, kituroto Ejakait, Kituroto da ŋes Ituŋa kere.”" 
Romans15:12 Bobo da ebala Isaia ebe, “Ejaun aliasit naka Yese, Ŋes loenyouni ayait atekerin; Emunokinos ŋol atekerin.”" 
Romans15:13 Edeke da loka amun kilelebik yes aiyalama kere ka ainapakin kotoma aiyuun, kiyatanakinos noi ajaut kamun kotoma apedor naka Emoyo Lokalaunan." 
Romans15:14 Ikainacan, etogogoŋit eoŋ elopet kanukus ebe ileleba yes da ajokis, isilelebitai acoa kere, bobo da ipedorete aikwenyanar bonik ka bonik." 
Romans15:15 Konye kewadikakinit yes katitiŋ naepol katutubeta ace, aisiitun, kanuka asianut nakainakinit Edeke," 
Romans15:16 tetere araun ebulesit loka Kristo Yesu mama ejaas atekerin, keswamak Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke aswam naka esasedoti, tetere eraunete atekerin asubanit naecamunitai, naitalaunit Emoyo Lokalaunan," 
Romans15:17 Aso ejai akirot naaolobobotor kotoma Kristo Yesu kakonyen nuka Edeke. 
Romans15:18 Naarai mam atitiŋikini einer akirot namam Kristo iswamat kotomakaŋ, tetere erimarete atekerin, kanuka akirot arai aswamisioit," 
Romans15:19 kotoma apedor naka aanyuneta ka nukaumokin, kotoma apedor naka Emoyo Lokalaunan, kwaŋin ameun ka Yerusalem, kiton da airiamar Iliriko etodol alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo," 
Romans15:20 kwabo alosikinit alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak, mere neelimoritere ekiror loka Kristo, kenyek adukokin apetetait naka icetuŋanan," 
Romans15:21 konye kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Eanyunete ŋul lumam alimonokinitai akekiro, Ejenunete da ŋul lumam iirarito.”" 
Romans15:22 Kanuka ŋun ŋes ketikokinitere irwan ipu kenyek abunore mamakus," 
Romans15:23 konye kwana, naarai emamei bobo eoŋ aibois katutubeta kanu, bobo da ameun ikar luipu emiela abunore mamakus," 
Romans15:24 amuno aanyun yes naetorio alosit Sipain, yes da kinyamakinete eoŋ korotoka, kadau ber aipejokin yes adaun aimue." 
Romans15:25 Konye kwana alosi Yerusalem, ejaanakini lukalaunak." 
Romans15:26 Naarai isiyalamikinito luko Makedonia ka Akaia atukonokin iboro akorakin lukican lukotoma lukalaunak luejaas Yerusalem. 
Romans15:27 Naarai isiyalamikinito kesi, ido da ejai kes apesen kamakec, naarai arai imorikikinete Imo arereŋesiokec nuka emoyo, ibusakinit da kes aijaanakin ŋul karereŋesiokec nuka akuan." 
Romans15:28 Aso kadau eoŋ ŋun, kepucak kes araito ŋin, etori mamakus alosit Sipain;" 
Romans15:29 ido ajeni ebe naabunio mamakus, abuni kaileleba naka arereŋ naka Kristo." 
Romans15:30 Keŋaiŋait yes, iinacan, kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, kanuka amin da naka Emoyo, koutas nepepe keoŋ kotoma ailipikus kanukaŋ mama ejai Edeke," 
Romans15:31 ebe ketajari kama ejaas lukepali kotoma Yudaya, bobo da akaijaanakin nakijaar ŋina Yerusalem korau naisiyalamikinit lukalaunak;" 
Romans15:32 tetere adoluni mamakus kaiyalama, kanuka akote naka Edeke, keyeŋ nepepe kayes." 
Romans15:33 Edeke loka ainapakin kojai nepepe kayes kere. Amen. 
Romans16:1 Eturit Poibe kinaciwok kamakus, naerai akejaanakinan naka ekanisa loka Kenekerea," 
Romans16:2 tetere isukunyikinete ŋes kotoma Ejakait kwape ibusakinitor lukalaunak, kisigalikis ŋes kotoma akirot kere naipuda kamakus, naarai arau ŋesi akeŋarakinan naka ituŋa luipu, ka eoŋ da elopet." 
Romans16:3 Kiyogata Pirisika ka Akuila ikeswamak lukaupaka kotoma Kristo Yesu," 
Romans16:4 luakapakina cut ajepario akwesikec kanuka aijaraka, luemalai, kwabo mere eoŋ bon konye ikanisan kere luka Imo," 
Romans16:5 kiyogata da ekanisa loejai togokec. Kiyogata Epaineto lominataka, loerai losodit loko Asia kotoma Kristo." 
Romans16:6 Kiyogata Mariam, nakitaaritoi noi kanukus." 
Romans16:7 Kiyogata Anderoniko ka Yunia ipajenaka ka ikijoreoritono nepepe keoŋ; luejenikina kokiyakia, lukageikinete eoŋ toma Kristo." 
Romans16:8 Kiyogata Amupiliato lominataka toma Ejakait. 
Romans16:9 Kiyogata Urubano ekeswaman aupawok toma Kristo, ka Sitakus lominatakaŋ." 
Romans16:10 Kiyogata Apele, loecamunitai toma Kristo. Kiyogata lukokale loka Arisitobolo." 
Romans16:11 Kiyogata Kerodion epajenaka, Kiyogata lukokale loka Narakiso luejaas toma Ejakait." 
Romans16:12 Kiyogata Turupaina, ka Turuposa nuitaaritos toma Ejakait. Kiyogata Perisida naminat, naitaaritoi noi toma Ejakait." 
Romans16:13 Kiyogata Rupo loseuna toma Ejakait, ka totoke ka nakaŋ da." 
Romans16:14 Kiyogata Asunikirito, ka Pelegon, ka Kereme, ka Pataroba, ka Kerema, ka iinacan luejaas nenipe kakes." 
Romans16:15 Kiyogata Pilologo ka Yulia, ka Nerea ka inacike, ka Olumupa, ka lukalaunak kere luejaas kakes." 
Romans16:16 Kiyoganakinos bonik ka bonik kainu nakalaunan. Kiyogaete yes ikanisan kere luka Kristo. 
Romans16:17 Keŋaiŋait yes iinacan, kocoito ŋul lueyaunete atiaketa ka nuitiguikinete, asurokin aisisianakin naipotu yesi kisisiata; kinacata kes." 
Romans16:18 Naarai luikote kwaŋin mam ijaanakinete Ejakaitiwok Kristo, dimarai akecekoikes; iŋalaarete itauon luka luemamei akirot kanuka akecekiro nuejijim nuijodijodete." 
Romans16:19 Naarai adolok akusirima ituŋa kere. Aso aleli kanukus, konye akoto yes koraas lukacoa kotoma akiro kanuejok, ka luiyapaara kotoma akiro kanueroko." 
Romans16:20 Edeke da loka ainapakin idecideci Satan atipet kwap kakejenekus. Asianut naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kojai kayes. 
Romans16:21 Kiyogai yes Timoteo ekeswaman aupaka; ka Lukio ka Yason ka Sosipater, ipajenaka." 
Romans16:22 Eoŋ Teretio, ekewadikan ebalua lo, keyogai yes toma Ejakait." 
Romans16:23 Kiyogai da Gaio lokesipejo eoŋ ka ekanisa kere. Erasito, ekeŋadan loka ere, ka Kuarito onacewok, kiyogaete. [" 
Romans16:24 Asianut naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kojai kayes kere.] 
Romans16:25 Mama ejai ŋol loepedori aitogogoŋ yes kwape ejaatar Akakiro Nukajokak, ka alimonokinio naka Yesu Kristo, kwape ejaar apukokinio naka aiyeiyea naimunonitai ameun ikar lupeŋo," 
Romans16:26 konye kwana itakanunitai, ido kanuka aiwadikaeta nuka inabin itejenunitai mama ejaas atekerin kere kwape kicorakinitor Edeke loka ikar kere tetere erimarete aiyuun—" 
Romans16:27 Mama ejai Edeke bon lokacoa kojai aibuses kotoma Yesu Kristo ikar ka ikar. Amen. 
1Corinthians1:1 Paul, lokenyarao araut ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kanuka akot naka Edeke, ka Sosetene onace," 
1Corinthians1:2 Mama ejai ekanisa loka Edeke loejai Korinto, ŋul lukitalaunio kotoma Kristo Yesu, lukenyarao koraut lukalaunak, nepepe kaŋul kere luiwoneto ekiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kaŋiniibois, loerai Ejakaitikec ka lowok da:" 
1Corinthians1:3 Kojai asianut mama ijaas, ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians1:4 Emalaenenei Edeke tiritir kanukus, kanuka asianut naka Edeke nakiinakinio yes, kotoma Kristo Yesu." 
1Corinthians1:5 Naarai aponi kitabari yes kaŋolipone kotomakeŋ, kotoma akiro kere ka aijen da kere" 
1Corinthians1:6 kwape kitogogoŋere aitejenunet naka Kristo kotomakus," 
1Corinthians1:7 tetere mam itwakiarete amodioinakinet kere, idarete apukorio naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo;" 
1Corinthians1:8 loitogogoŋi yes kiton awasia, komamei aitoronio kapaaran naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians1:9 Erai Edeke lomunot, lokinyarauni yes alomun oidicane loka Okokuke, Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok." 
1Corinthians1:10 Aso iinacan, keŋaiŋait yes, kokiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, ebe kinerata kere adiopekirot, kinye atiakatiakaun ajaun kidiŋikus, konye kidicakina ketau ediopet ka ainerun da adiopet." 
1Corinthians1:11 Naarai, ikainacan, kalimokis eoŋ lukokale loka Kloe, ebe ejai aŋolopa kidiŋikus." 
1Corinthians1:12 Aso naabala nata ebe, ebala ŋinidiopet kayesi ebe, “Arai eoŋ yenika Paul,” ice da ebe, “Konye eoŋ yenika Apolo,” ka ice da ebe, “Arai eoŋ yenika Kepa,” ka ice da ebe, “Arai eoŋ yenika Kristo.”" 
1Corinthians1:13 Okwe, etiakatiaka kereka Kristo? Ibubukinitoi kereka Paul kanukus? Arai bo iponi kibatisai kokiror loka Paul?" 
1Corinthians1:14 Emalai naarai mam ebatisat idio kayesi dimarai Keresipo ka Gaio; 
1Corinthians1:15 kinyek idiotuŋanan atemar ebe aponi kibatisai kokirorikaŋ. 
1Corinthians1:16 (Abu kebatis da lukokale loka Sitepan, Alemar ŋul mam ajeni arai abu kebatis ice kere.)" 
1Corinthians1:17 Naarai mam Kristo keyakit aibatis, dimarai alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak, kwabo mere kacoa naka akirot, kinyek emusalaba loka Kristo araun aamameak." 
1Corinthians1:18 Naarai akirot naka emusalaba erai abaŋaanut kama ejaas lueoliorete, konye mama kija oni lukitajario erai apedor naka Edeke," 
1Corinthians1:19 Naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Amudiari acoa naka lukacoa, Etapalauni da apirianut naka luepiriaka.”" 
1Corinthians1:20 Ai bo ejai lokacoa? Ai bo ejai ekewadikan? Ai bo ejai eketepegan loka ikar kalu? Mam kereka Edeke abu kitababaŋ acoa naka akwap? 
1Corinthians1:21 Naarai kotoma acoa naka Edeke, mam akwap abu kojen Edeke kanuka acoa, abu kisiyalamik Edeke aitajar luiyuunito kotoma abaŋaanut naka akirot naelimonokinio," 
1Corinthians1:22 Naarai ekotosi Iyudayan aanyuneta, Iyonanin da emootos acoa," 
1Corinthians1:23 konye sio kilimonokini Kristo loebubukinitoi, loerai aitiguikinet mama ejaas Iyudayan, abaŋaanut da mama ejaas Imo," 
1Corinthians1:24 konye mama ejaas ŋul luenyaritai, Iyudayan ka Iyonanin da, erai Kristo apedor naka Edeke, ka acoa da naka Edeke." 
1Corinthians1:25 Naarai abaŋaanut naka Edeke erai acoa aitelekarit naka ituŋa, akalanyanut da naka Edeke egogoŋ aitelekarit naka ituŋa." 
1Corinthians1:26 Naarai, iinacan, koomito anyarauniokus, ebe mam luipu kayesi keraas lukacoa kwape ejaar aitemis naka akwap, mam ipu lukapedor, mam ipu lukapolou da luenyaraunitai," 
1Corinthians1:27 konye abu Edeke koseu lukabaŋaanut luka akwap tetere isurumi lukacoa ileic; bobo da abu Edeke koseu luekalanyaka luka akwap tetere isurumi lukagogoŋok ileic; 
1Corinthians1:28 bobo da abu Edeke koseu imukopin, ka luemwaŋitai kotoma akwap, eebo, ka iboro da luemameete, tetere itamamauni ŋul luejaas," 
1Corinthians1:29 kinyek idiotuŋanan aolobobot kakonyen nuka Edeke. 
1Corinthians1:30 Konye kanukeŋ ijaut yes toma Kristo Yesu, loabu Edeke kituluo awokocoa, ka adolit, ka aitalaunio, ka alakunio da;" 
1Corinthians1:31 kanuka ŋun kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Yeneolobobot, koolobobote kotoma Ejakait.”" 
1Corinthians2:1 Eoŋ da, iinacan, naabunio mamakus, mam abunit alimonokin yes nukaiyeiyea nuka Edeke kakiro nuejijim karaida kacoa." 
1Corinthians2:2 Naarai abu kenerunite ainyein ajenun adiokirot kokidiŋikus, dimarai Yesu Kristo loebubukinitoi." 
1Corinthians2:3 Eoŋ da naajaar mamakus, akalanyana, kakurian ka amaran naepol;" 
1Corinthians2:4 akakirot ka akalimonokin da mam keraas akiro nukacoa nuijodoete, dimarai nuitodiarito Emoyo ka apedor," 
1Corinthians2:5 tetere akusiiyuun mam egoŋakina acoa naka ituŋa dimarai toma apedor naka Edeke. 
1Corinthians2:6 Konye ejai acoa nakinera kama kaluapolokoto konye mam erai acoa naka ikar kalu, karaida naka ikayaitok luka ikar kalu, luepote amameun," 
1Corinthians2:7 konye kinera acoa naka Edeke kotoma nukaiyeiyea, acoa naibwaitai, nakicorakinit Edeke eriŋa ikar ejauna, kanuka aibusesuwok." 
1Corinthians2:8 Mam ikayaitok luka ikar kalu apotu kojenut ŋin; naarai arai kejenete timam kibubukis Ejakait lokaibuses. 
1Corinthians2:9 Konye kwape kiwadikatere ebe, “Numam keanyunit akoŋu, karaida akit aibiun, Numam kelomarito da otau loka ituŋanan Nuetia nen nukitemokinit Edeke lueminasi ŋes.”" 
1Corinthians2:10 Konye kipukok Edeke oni kanuka Emoyo. Naarai irerei Emoyo kere, kiton nuidulok nuka Edeke." 
1Corinthians2:11 Naarai iŋai tope kotuŋa yenejeni aomisio nuka ituŋa, dimarai emoyo loka ituŋanan loejai kotomakeŋ? Kwape kwaŋin emamei yenejeni aomisio nuka Edeke dimarai Emoyo loka Edeke," 
1Corinthians2:12 Konye oni, mam kidumunit emoyo loka akwap, dimarai Emoyo loebuni kama ejai Edeke, tetere kijenuni ainakineta nukiinakini Edeke oni atitai." 
1Corinthians2:13 Kinera ŋun mere kakiro nuisisianakini acoa naka etuŋanane, dimarai nuisisianakini Emoyo, kitiiriani nuka emoyo kanuka emoyo." 
1Corinthians2:14 Ituŋanan kauruuneteke mam ecamuni akiro nuka Emoyo loka Edeke, naarai eraas nukabaŋaanut mamakeŋ, kwabo mam epedori ajenun kes naarai emisiikinio kanuka emoyo." 
1Corinthians2:15 Konye ituŋanan yenika emoyo emisiikini kere, kwabo emamei yenemisiikini ŋes." 
1Corinthians2:16 “Naarai iŋai kereka ejenunit aomisio nuka Ejakait, tetere ituutoori ŋes?” Konye kijaa oni kaomisio nuka Kristo." 
1Corinthians3:1 Eoŋ da, iinacan, mam apedorit einer kayes kwape luka emoyo, dimarai luka akuan, kwape imukerun kotoma Kristo." 
1Corinthians3:2 Abu ketamata yes akile, kwabo mere inyamat; naarai mam ipedorito; eebo, kiton kwana da mam ipedorito," 
1Corinthians3:3 naarai iriŋa iraas luka akuan. Naarai naejaar ekokote ka aŋolopa, mam kereka iraas ituŋa luka akuan, ilosenenete kwape ituŋa atai?" 
1Corinthians3:4 Naarai naebalar idiopet ebe, “Arai eoŋ yenika Paul,” ice da ebe, “Arai eoŋ yenika Apolo,” mam kereka iraas ituŋa atai?" 
1Corinthians3:5 Aso iŋai bo Apolo? Iŋai bo da Paul? Kes ikejaanakinak lukiyuunete yesi kamakec, ka ŋin diopet da kwape keinakinia Ejakait." 
1Corinthians3:6 Abu eoŋ kera, kicoco Apolo, konye kitopolo Edeke." 
1Corinthians3:7 Kwaŋin ekeraan mam erai ibore, karaida ekecocoan, dimarai Edeke loitopoloi." 
1Corinthians3:8 Aso loirai ka loicocoi eraas ipe, ido edumuni ŋinituŋanan ekeropit kwape ajaar akeitaaritoi." 
1Corinthians3:9 Naarai kirai isio ikeswamak nepepe ka Edeke; iraas yesi amana naka Edeke, aduket naka Edeke." 
1Corinthians3:10 Kwape ejaar asianut naka Edeke nakainakinitai eoŋ, abu kapesik apetetait kwape ekadukon lokapolon lokacoa, konye eduki ece. Konye kocoite ŋinidiopet kwape edukio." 
1Corinthians3:11 Naarai emamei yenepedori apesikin apetetait ace, dimarai ŋin naedaunitai apesikin, ŋes Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians3:12 Konye arai keduk ituŋanan toma apetetait ŋin esabu, arai epuesa, arai amor nuketiai, arai akito, arai anya, arai ariaŋ da," 
1Corinthians3:13 etakanuni aswam naka ŋinituŋanan; naarai isideleleuni Apaaran, naarai epukorio kotoma akim, itemi da akim aswam naka ŋinituŋanan kwape ejaar." 
1Corinthians3:14 Arai esalit aswam naedukit ituŋanan toma apetetait, edumuni ŋesi eropit." 
1Corinthians3:15 Arai kidopoo aswam naka ituŋanan, etwaniari, kwabo itajario ŋes, konye bala kotoma akim." 
1Corinthians3:16 Mam kereka ijenete ebe iraas yesi eyekalu loka Edeke, ebe da iboie Emoyo loka Edeke kotomakus?" 
1Corinthians3:17 Arai kemuna ituŋanan eyekalu loka Edeke, emunaari Edeke ituŋanan ŋin. Naarai erai eyekalu loka Edeke lokalaunan, ŋes yesi." 
1Corinthians3:18 Sirikemodakin ituŋanan. Arai ejai kotomakus ituŋanan yeneomit ilopet araut yenikacoa kokar kalu, korau ŋesi yenibaŋ, tetere eraun yenikacoa." 
1Corinthians3:19 Naarai acoa naka akwap kana ŋes abaŋaanut kama ka Edeke. Naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Ikamuni ŋesi lukacoa koboteikec.”" 
1Corinthians3:20 Bobo da ebe, “Ejeni Ejakait aomisio nuka lukacoa, ebe eraas aamameak.”" 
1Corinthians3:21 Kwaŋin kinyek ituŋanan aolobobot kotoma otuŋa. Naarai eraas kere lukus," 
1Corinthians3:22 arai Paul, arai Apolo, arai Kepa, arai akwap, arai aijar, arai atwanare, arai nuejaas kwana, arai nuepote, kere eraas nukus," 
1Corinthians3:23 iraas yesi da luka Kristo, Kristo da loka Edeke." 
1Corinthians4:1 Koomit ituŋanan sio kwanata, kwape ikejaanakinak luka Kristo, ka ikeŋadak da luka nukaiyeiyea nuka Edeke." 
1Corinthians4:2 Bobo da iburao ikeŋadak atakan eraas lumunon. 
1Corinthians4:3 Konye kamakaŋ erai akirot naedit noi yes, arai airabet kere naka etuŋanan, atubokin eoŋ. Mam da atubokin bon." 
1Corinthians4:4 Naarai mam ajeni nuewosakin bon, konye mam kemarakinio adolit kanuka ŋun, konye Ejakait ŋes katubokini." 
1Corinthians4:5 Aso sirikitubo akirot eroko apak, aitodol naebunio Ejakait, loitacauni nuibwaitai nuka amuton, ido isideleleuni ainerun naka itauon. Kosodi edumuni ŋinituŋanan akeiturio kama ejai Edeke." 
1Corinthians4:6 Aso iinacan, etuputoo ŋun aputokaŋ ka Apolo da kanukus, tetere kanukosi isisiaete ainyein adepar nuiwadikatai, kinye idio kayesi adakanun kanuka ediopet aitelekarit loce." 
1Corinthians4:7 Naarai iŋai kitegelikinit jo kama kaluce? Inyoin kereka ejai jo yenimam kiinakinitai? Konye arai kiinakinitai, kanukinyo iwolobobotor bala mam kiinakinitai?" 
1Corinthians4:8 Idaut aimonikin! Idaut adumun abar! Iyaitos kamameete isio! Eebo, arai tiiyaito, tetere kimori ayait kayes!" 
1Corinthians4:9 Naarai aomit ebe etodia Edeke sio ikiyakia awasia, kwape ituŋa luetubokinitai aario: naarai kiraun isio ibore yenisesena kakwap, kama ka imalaikan ka ituŋa da." 
1Corinthians4:10 Kirai isio ibaŋiok kanuka Kristo, konye iraas yesi lukacoa kotoma Kristo, Kikalanyaka isio, konye igogoŋ yesi. Kitubusikinitai yes, konye sio kitisilitoi," 
1Corinthians4:11 Kiton osawa lo da, kiriebi eteŋei ka akure da, kimujalal, kibuŋao, bobo da emameete sio ireria," 
1Corinthians4:12 kitaaritoi aswam kakaninikosi. Nakimoromoroere, kilipanakini arereŋ; nakiticanere, kititiŋikinit;" 
1Corinthians4:13 nakisabanakinere, kiŋaiŋai; kitusubi bala asusuj nuka akwap, ediirit da loka iboro kere, kiton kwana." 
1Corinthians4:14 Mam ewadikai nu aisurumia yes ileic, konye aikwenyar yes kwape idweka luminan." 
1Corinthians4:15 Karaida kejaas yes ikesisianakinak ilukumin itomon kotoma Kristo, konye emameete lukapapa luipu. Naarai eoŋ ŋes kaurit yes kotoma Kristo Yesu kanuka alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak." 
1Corinthians4:16 Aso keŋaiŋait yes koputoorito eoŋ. 
1Corinthians4:17 Kanuka ŋun ejuk Timoteo mamakus, loerai okokuka lominat, lomunot da kotoma Ejakait, lokisiituni yes irotinika luejaas toma Kristo, kwape esisianakinia kaŋiniibois kotoma ŋolikanisa." 
1Corinthians4:18 Konye edakanunos ice kayesi ebe mam abuni mamakus. 
1Corinthians4:19 Konye abuni atipet mamakus, arai ekot Ejakait, abuni eoŋ ajenun mere akiro nuka ŋul kaluedakanunos dimarai apedorikec." 
1Corinthians4:20 Naarai mam ajakanut naka Edeke ejai toma akirot, dimarai toma apedor." 
1Corinthians4:21 Ikotosi anyoika? Kabu kereka mamakus kebela, arai bo kabu kamin komoyo loiyapepera?" 
1Corinthians5:1 Isiarakina eemut ebe ejai adoteu kotomakus, adoteu da namam ejauna kotoma atekerin; ebe etuŋanan ajaut kaberu naka papake." 
1Corinthians5:2 Yes da idakanunos, kwabo mam kikadakinit, tetere elemario kokidiŋikus ŋol lokiswamai akirot ŋin." 
1Corinthians5:3 Naarai, karaida amamei kakuan, konye ajai komoyo, adau eoŋ elopet atubokin ŋol lokiswamai akirot ŋin kwape tikajaar," 
1Corinthians5:4 kotoma okiror loka Ejakait Yesu, naitukonokinotor nepepe ka ekamoyo, ka apedor da naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu," 
1Corinthians5:5 kijaikis ŋol Satan tetere emudiario akuanake, tetere itajario emoyoke kotoma apaaran naka Ejakait Yesu." 
1Corinthians5:6 Mam aolobobokus ejok. Mam kereka ijenete ebe aitubuunet naedit itubuuni aluŋuret kere? 
1Corinthians5:7 Kitesegaaros do kaitubuunet namojoŋ, tetere iraunos aluŋuret nakitetet, kwape iraatar lumam itubuuno. Naarai aponi Kristo Aleleŋewok koinakinai araut asubanit." 
1Corinthians5:8 Aso karicata epucit, mere kaitubuunet namojoŋ, karaida kaitubuunet naka ameŋeranut ka aronis, dimarai ka namam itubuuno naka aipioror naka emoyo ka abeit." 
1Corinthians5:9 Abu kewadikak yes kotoma obaluaka ebe sirikimorianakinos kidotea; 
1Corinthians5:10 mam abala ebe kinacata cut idotea luka akwapin kanu, arai ikeraŋak, arai ikaŋatak, karaida ŋul luemaete aputosia, naarai arai kerai kwaŋin ti ibusakinit anyoun kakwapin kanu." 
1Corinthians5:11 Konye kwana kewadikakini yes ebe sirikimorianakinos kaloenyaritai onac arai erai edote, arai ekeraŋan, arai loemai aputosia, arai ekamoromoron, arai ekameran, arai ekaŋatan; etuŋanan loikoni kwaŋin mam acamunit yes karaida aimor kaŋes." 
1Corinthians5:12 Naarai anyoin ajokis kamakaŋ atubokin luejaas kiŋa? Mam kereka yes itubokinito luejaas toma okanisa? 
1Corinthians5:13 Konye etubokini Edeke ŋul luejaas kiŋa, Kireŋeasi yesi ekaronon ŋol loejai kidiŋikus." 
1Corinthians6:1 Arai ejai edio kayesi akirot kama ka onaceke, ijecekini kereka ŋesi aosan ŋes kakonyen nuka lumam edolito, kwabo mere kakonyen nuka ikalaunak?" 
1Corinthians6:2 Arai bo mam ijenete ebe etubokinete ikalaunak akwapin? Aso arai itubokinete yesi akwapin, mam kereka ipedorete aitub akiro nuedisiak noi?" 
1Corinthians6:3 Mam kereka ijenete ebe kitubokini imalaikan? Kikurwokinito biai akiro nuka aijar kana! 
1Corinthians6:4 Aso arai ijaas kaitub akiro nuka aijar kana, idakakinete kereka lumam eomitai kokanisa araut ikatubok?" 
1Corinthians6:5 Enera ŋun aisurumia yes ileic. Emamei kereka kotomakus lokacoa ediopet, loepedori aitub akiro nuka iinacanake," 
1Corinthians6:6 konye iwosanakinos iinacan bonik, bobo da kakonyen nuka lumam iyuunito." 
1Corinthians6:7 Aso kwana ejai aŋwal kotomakus, naarai iwosanakinos bonik, Kanukinyo gwai mam kikonakinere erono? Kanukinyo gwai mam kinasere iborokus." 
1Corinthians6:8 Konye yes ikonakinete erono, ido iŋasete, kiton iinacanakus da." 
1Corinthians6:9 Mam kereka ijenete ebe lumam edolito mam irumete ajakanut naka Edeke? Sirikiŋalas; karaida idotea, karaida luemaete aputosia, karaida lueeloko, karaida ikiliok luituluoros bala aŋor, karaida iketepak ikiliok," 
1Corinthians6:10 karaida ikokolak, karaida ikeraŋak, karaida ikamerak, karaida ikamoromorok, karaida ikaŋatak, mam irumete ajakanut naka Edeke." 
1Corinthians6:11 Ice kayesi da ipotu koraas kwaŋin; konye aponi kilotar, konye aponi kitalaun, konye aponi kitojoki araut luidolito, kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu Kristo, kotoma Emoyo da loka Edekewok." 
1Corinthians6:12 “Ibus iboro kere kamakaŋ”; konye mam iboro kere isigalikinete. “Ibus iboro kere kamakaŋ”; konye mam ketubulesene idiobore. 
1Corinthians6:13 “Eraas inyamat luka akoik, akoik da naka inyamat” itapalauni Edeke kere, ŋin ka ŋul da. Mam akuan erai naka adoteu, dimarai naka Ejakait, Ejakait da loka akuan." 
1Corinthians6:14 Konye abu Edeke kitajar Ejakait, kitajari oni da kapedorike." 
1Corinthians6:15 Mam kereka ijenete ebe eraas awatekus atutubeta nuka Kristo? Aso kalema kereka atutubeta nuka Kristo, ketaraut atutubeta nuka naadote? Madi akuj!" 
1Corinthians6:16 Arai mam kereka ijenete ebe lokirotakinos kanaadote eraas adiopetekuan? Naarai ebala ebe, “Ŋul luarei eraunos adiopetekuan.”" 
1Corinthians6:17 Konye ŋol lokirotakinos ka Ejakait, erai emoyo ediopet kaŋes," 
1Corinthians6:18 Kinacata adoteu, ŋinidiakaret naiswamai ituŋanan erai nakokiŋa akuanake; konye ŋin yenedotei adiaka kotoma akuanake alopet." 
1Corinthians6:19 Mam kereka ijenete ebe awatekus kes eyekalu loka Emoyo Lokalaunan loejai tomakus, lokiinakini Edeke? Mam iraas kanukus;" 
1Corinthians6:20 naarai kigwelitai kakais nuipu. Aso kitopolooritos Edeke kotoma awatekus. 
1Corinthians7:1 Konye nuka akiro nuipotu kiwadikakis eoŋ. Ejok kama kekiliokit kinyek atiror aberu. 
1Corinthians7:2 Konye kanuka adoteu, kojau ŋolikiliokit kakeberu, ŋiniberu da kokilenike." 
1Corinthians7:3 Kotacak ŋolikiliokit akeberu nuibusakinito ŋes, kwape kwaŋin da kotacak ŋiniberu nuibusakinito okilenike." 
1Corinthians7:4 Mam aberu alopet eyait akekuan, dimarai okilenike; kwape kwaŋin da mam ekiliokit elopet eyait akekuan, dimarai akeberu." 
1Corinthians7:5 Sirimikanaros bonik, alemar diat icamanaros adaun apak, tetere iluŋakinos ailip; kosodete konyet aimorikikin bobo, kinyek Satan acodun yes kanuka amamus ayaikina." 
1Corinthians7:6 Enera ŋun kacamun, kwabo mere kaicorakinet." 
1Corinthians7:7 Konye emiela ituŋa kere araut kwape kaeoŋ elopet. Konye ejai ŋinidiopet ainakineteke naebuni kama ejai Edeke, idiopet kopone ece, idiopet da kopone ece." 
1Corinthians7:8 Konye alimokini lumam edukokina ka apuserun da, ebe ejok kamakec arai esalito kwape kaeoŋ." 
1Corinthians7:9 Konye arai mam epedorete ayaikina bonik, kodukokinos. Naarai ejok adukokin itia ainok." 
1Corinthians7:10 Ecorakini luedukokina, kwabo mere eoŋ, dimarai Ejakait, ebe, kinyek aberu aisac okilenike." 
1Corinthians7:11 Konye arai esaci, kosal mam edukokina, arai bo kopuco kokilenike. Bobo da kinyek ekiliokit aireŋear akeberu." 
1Corinthians7:12 Alimokini ice, eoŋ mere Ejakait, ebe, arai ejaas onace kaberu namam iyuunit, ecamuni ŋin da aiboienen kaŋes, kinyek aireŋear ŋin." 
1Corinthians7:13 Arai da ejaas aberu kekiliokit lomam iyuunit, ŋes da ecamuni aiboienen kaŋin, kinyek anyoun kama kokilenike." 
1Corinthians7:14 Naarai italaunitai ekiliokit lomam iyuunit kanuka akeberu, aberu da namam iyuunit italaunitai kanuka okilenike. Arai mere kwaŋin tieraas ikusidwe lumam elaete, konye kwana eraas lukalaunak" 
1Corinthians7:15 Konye arai enyouni lomam iyuunit, konyou do ŋesi; kakiro nuikote nen mam onac arai kinac eenitai. Naarai abu Edeke konyarau oni toma ainapakin." 
1Corinthians7:16 Ijo aberu, ijenuni biai, wolo bo itajari okilenikon? Ijo da ekiliokit, ijenuni biai, wolo bo itajari akoniberu?" 
1Corinthians7:17 Konye na bon, kolosenenei ŋinidiopet kwape kekorakinitor Ejakait, ŋinidiopet da kwape kenyaraunitor Edeke. Ecoranakini kwaŋin kotoma okanisan kere." 
1Corinthians7:18 Kenyaraunitai kereka etuŋanan ekepitai? Kinyek araun lomam ekepitai. Kenyaraunitai kereka etuŋanan lomam ekepitai? Kinyek akepio. 
1Corinthians7:19 Naarai akepio mam erai ibore, amamus akepio da mam erai ibore, dimarai aricit aicorakineta nuka Edeke." 
1Corinthians7:20 Kosalak ŋolituŋanan kanyaraunio nakenyaraunere. 
1Corinthians7:21 Irai kereka ebulesit nakinyaraunere? Siripodo ŋun, Konye arai ipedori araun loeosikinitai, kitwasama gwai kwaŋin." 
1Corinthians7:22 Naarai lokenyaraunio erai ebulesit, erai loeosikinitai loka Ejakait; kwape kwaŋin da lokenyaraunio erai loeosikinitai erai ebulesit loka Kristo." 
1Corinthians7:23 Aponi kogweli yes kakais nuipu; sirikiraut ibulesin luka ituŋa. 
1Corinthians7:24 Aso iinacan, kosal ŋinidiopet nepepe ka Edeke kwape kenyaraunere," 
1Corinthians7:25 Nuka abekon emamei eoŋ aicorakinet naka Ejakait, konye kapesikis yes akiro kwape etuŋanan lomunot kanuka aitim naka Ejakait." 
1Corinthians7:26 Aomit eoŋ ebe kanuka ican luka tinenikwana ejok arai kesal ituŋanan kwape ejaar. 
1Corinthians7:27 Kirotakinitai kereka jo kaberu? Sirimoot alacakinio, Emamei kereka jo aberu? Sirimoot aberu." 
1Corinthians7:28 Konye arai imanyi, mam idiakit, arai da edukokin apese, mam ŋin ediakit. Konye luikote nen eanyunete ican luka akuan, ido akoto aiyar yes ŋul." 
1Corinthians7:29 Enera na, iinacan, ebe eŋoŋar apak; kanuka ŋun koraut luejaas kaŋor kwape kaluemameete," 
1Corinthians7:30 luemonyete da kwape kalumam emonyete, ka luiyalamasi kwape kalumam iyalamasi, luegwelete da kwape kaluemameete iboro," 
1Corinthians7:31 luitwasamaete akwap koraut kwape kalumam itwasamaete, Naarai etubor epone loka akwapin kanu." 
1Corinthians7:32 Akoto yes koraut lumam iyaloŋoŋoete. Lomam emanyi iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka Ejakait, kwape epedoria aitelel Ejakait;" 
1Corinthians7:33 konye loamanyit iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka akwapin, kwape epedoria aitelel akeberu," 
1Corinthians7:34 ido ejai atiaket. Aberu namam edukokinitai, arai bo apese, iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka Ejakait, tetere eraun nakalaunan toma akuanake ka omoyoke da. Kwabo naedukokina iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka akwapin, kwape epedoria aitelel okilenike." 
1Corinthians7:35 Enera ŋun kodumut yes ajokis, mam akoto ailok yes koic, dimarai aitetemikin nuibusakinito, kijaanakinete Ejakait komamei yenitapaari aomisiokus." 
1Corinthians7:36 Arai eomit etuŋanan ebe mam ikonakinit ejok naisinerit, arai imiela noi, ido ibusakinit, aso kiswama ŋesi kwape ekotor, komany ŋes, mam ediaki." 
1Corinthians7:37 Konye loicasit kotauke, komamei ibore yenitinaikinit, loepedori ayait akoteke, itogogoŋit da kotauke aricit naisinerit, iswamai ejok." 
1Corinthians7:38 Kwaŋin loemanyi naisinerit, iswamai ejok; lomam emanyi da iswamai ejok aitelekarit." 
1Corinthians7:39 Irotakinio aberu kokilenike apak kere naejaria ŋol. Konye arai ketwana okilenike, eosikinitai adukokin loekot, konye toma Ejakait." 
1Corinthians7:40 Konye aomit eoŋ ebe iyalama aitelekarit arai esali kwaŋin, Ido aomit ebe ajai kEmoyo loka Ejakait." 
1Corinthians8:1 Nuka asuban nueinakinitai aputosia; kijeni ebe, “Ejai sio kere aijen.” Edakunun aijen, konye do eduki amin." 
1Corinthians8:2 Arai eomit ituŋanan ebe ejeni akirot, eriŋa ejenuna kwape ibusakinitor ajenun," 
1Corinthians8:3 Konye arai emina ituŋanan Edeke, ejeni Edeke ŋin." 
1Corinthians8:4 Aso nuka inyamat lueinakinitai aputosia, kijeni ebe, “Aput mam erai ibore kakwap,” ido ebe, “Emamei Edeke dimarai ediopet.”" 
1Corinthians8:5 Ido karaida ejaas luemaikinitai idekesio arai toma akuj arai toma akwap, kwape ejaatar “idekesio” luipu ka “ijaka” luipu," 
1Corinthians8:6 konye kamawok ejai Edeke ediopet bon, ŋes Papa, loeponiata iboro kere kamakeŋ, oni da kirai lukeŋ, ejai da Ejakait ediopet, Yesu Kristo, lokejauniata iboro kere, oni da kirai kanukeŋ." 
1Corinthians8:7 Konye ajenun ŋin mam ejai otuŋa kere. Konye ice luenaikinito aputosia kiton kwana, enyamete bala iboro lueinakinio araut asuban mama ejaas aputosia; ido naarai ekalanyaka aomisiokec, emunaaros." 
1Corinthians8:8 Mam inyamat kitojokaarete oni kakonyen nuka Edeke, Arai mam kinyami, mam kitwaniari, arai kinyami da mam kiyatakinio." 
1Corinthians8:9 Konye kocoito kinyek akusipedor araun aitiguikinet mama ejaas luekalanyaka. 
1Corinthians8:10 Naarai arai keanyu ituŋanan jo loijai kaijen, iboikin ainyam toma abila naka aput, mam kereka aomisio nuka ŋol nuekalanyaka etitiŋikinete ainyam lueinakinio aputosia?" 
1Corinthians8:11 Kwaŋin eoliori loekalanyana kanuka akoniijen, ŋope ŋol onace loabu Kristo kotwanik." 
1Corinthians8:12 Ido kwaŋin naidiakanariata kama ejaas iinacanakus, ka aimusuŋ akeceomisio nuekalanyaka, idiakanaretc kama ejai Kristo," 
1Corinthians8:13 Kanuka ŋun arai itiguikinete inyamat onaceka, abeit mam anyami akiriŋ ikar kere, kenyek aitiguikin onaceka." 
1Corinthians9:1 Mam kereka eoŋ ejakakai? Mam kereka arai ekiyakia? Mam kereka eoŋ abu kaany Yesu Ejakaitiwok? Mam kereka yes iraas akaswam toma Ejakait? 
1Corinthians9:2 Naarai arai mam eoŋ arai ekiyakia kama ka ice, konye arai ekiyakia kamakus; naarai iraas yesi aipucakinet naka ekiyakianekaŋ kotoma Ejakait." 
1Corinthians9:3 Ŋin ŋes aboŋokineteka mama ejaas ŋul lukeŋisete," 
1Corinthians9:4 Emamei kereka sio apedor ainyam ka aimat? 
1Corinthians9:5 Emamei kereka sio apedor aup kaberu naerai inac, kwape kikiyakia ice, ka iinacan luka Ejakait, ka Kepa da?" 
1Corinthians9:6 Arai bo eoŋ bon ka Baranaba emamei apedor ainyein aswam? 
1Corinthians9:7 Eserikalet enyoin elosi ejie kotacakin ŋes elopet? Iŋai tope irai emusabibu komam enyami araitoke? Iŋai tope icokiei esipan komam emasi akile nuka esipan? 
1Corinthians9:8 Okwe enera kereka ŋun kotuŋanane? Arai bo mam inerasi ikisila ŋupe ŋun? 
1Corinthians9:9 Naarai iwadikatai toma okisila luka Musa ebe, “Sirikien emoŋ loipudapudai aicom akima.” Epodo kereka Edeke imoŋin?" 
1Corinthians9:10 Arai bo inera ŋun kanuwok? Eebo, iwadikatai kanuwok, naarai ibusakinit ekakorion akor kamun, ekecoman da aicom kamun ebe edumuni ewaike." 
1Corinthians9:11 Aso arai kiraikinit yes akiro nuka emoyo, erai ca akirot naepol arai kiidweny nukakuan kamakus?" 
1Corinthians9:12 Arai emorete ice apedor ŋin kamakus, mam kereka sio kitelekarit? Konye mam kitwasamata apedor ŋin, dimarai kiŋirikinit akiro kere, kenyeis aitikokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo." 
1Corinthians9:13 Mam kereka ijenete ebe luiswamaete aswam naka eyekalu enyamete koboro luka eyekalu, ka ŋul da luijaanakinete kotem ejaas kewaikec kotoma oboro luka etem?" 
1Corinthians9:14 Kwape kwaŋin icorakinit Ejakait ebe ŋul luelimonokinete Akiro Nukajokak, ejarete kanuka Akiro Nukajokak." 
1Corinthians9:15 Konye mam eoŋ etwasamat akiro ŋun karaida adiopet. Kwabo mam ewadikat ŋun tetere ejaunete kwaŋin kamakaŋ. Naarai ejok eoŋ atwanare itia idiotuŋanan aitapalaun aoloboboteka. 
1Corinthians9:16 Naarai arai alimonokini Akiro Nukajokak, emamei eoŋ naaolobobotor. Naarai ketiŋaikinitai. Itukwi eoŋ arai mam eoŋ alimonokini Akiro Nukajokak!" 
1Corinthians9:17 Naarai arai eswamai ŋun kakoteka, ejai aropio, konye arai mere akoteka, kamunoi kotoma ajokon." 
1Corinthians9:18 Aso enyoin kereka ekaropit? Ŋes lota, ebe, kalimonok Akiro Nukajokak atai, komam etwasamai akapedor kere nakijaar kotoma Akiro Nukajokak," 
1Corinthians9:19 Naarai karaida kaosikinitai kotuŋa kere, etuluoro ebulesit loka kere, tetere eriuni luipu aitelekarit." 
1Corinthians9:20 Abu karau bala Eyudayat kama ejaas lyudayan, tetere eriuni Iyudayan; kama kaŋul kalueyaito ikisila, abu karau loeyaito ikisila-karaida mam eoŋ elopet kayaito ikisila-tetere eriuni lueyaito ikisila." 
1Corinthians9:21 Kama kaŋul kaluemameete ikisila abu karau loemameete ikisila-mere ŋes amamuut kikisila kama ejai Edeke, konye aricit ikisila luka Kristo-tetere eriuni ŋul luemameete ikisila." 
1Corinthians9:22 Abu karau ekalany kama ka luekalanyaka, tetere eriuni luekalanyaka. Karau lokiponesio kere kotuŋa kere, tetere korotin kere ketajar ice." 
1Corinthians9:23 Eswamai ŋun kere kanuka Akiro Nukajokak, tetere kimori ka ice kotomakec." 
1Corinthians9:24 Mam kereka ijenete ebe lueboloboloete, eboloboloete kere, konye ediopet edumuni ainakinet? Aso koboloboloete tetere idumunete." 
1Corinthians9:25 Yenepega kabolobol eyaikina kakiro kere. Iswamaete ŋul kwaŋin tetere edumunete aboko naemunaar, konye oni namam emunaar." 
1Corinthians9:26 Eoŋ da mam aboloboloi atitai, mam anaŋi da bala loenaŋi apak;" 
1Corinthians9:27 konye eticani akakuan, ketubulesen ŋes, kenyek kadau alimonokin ice, araun eoŋ elopet loeneritoi." 
1Corinthians10:1 Naarai iinacan, akoto yes ajenun ebe abu edou kiteriborite lukapapaakos kere, kitoroto kere aŋolol," 
1Corinthians10:2 aponi kibatisai da kere kama ka Musa kotoma odou kotoma aŋolol da," 
1Corinthians10:3 konyamata da kere inyamat luka emoyo," 
1Corinthians10:4 ido komata kere numatan nuka emoyo. Naarai apotu komata kAtiiba naka emoyo naatupit kes, Atiiba ŋin da kerai Kristo." 
1Corinthians10:5 Konye mam Edeke abu kolelakinite luipu kakesi; naarai aponi komudiarai kamodiŋ. 
1Corinthians10:6 Aso keraas akiro ŋun aput mamawok, tetere mam kiraŋai nueroko, kwape kiraŋaata ŋul." 
1Corinthians10:7 Sirikiraut luimaete aputosia, kwape ice kakesi; kwape kiwadikatere ebe, “Kiboikinos ituŋa ainyam ka aimat, kosodete konyout abolia.”" 
1Corinthians10:8 Kwabo sirikidoteata, kwape ice kakesi, kibiroros da ituŋa ilukumin akaisaarei ka luuni kapaaran adiopet." 
1Corinthians10:9 Kwabo sirikikodut Ejakait, kwape kekoduniata ice kakesi, komudiasi imunwo." 
1Corinthians10:10 Kwabo sirikirurumakis, kwape ice kakesi, komudia kes Ekamudiaran." 
1Corinthians10:11 Aso akiro ŋun apotu kodoikis ŋul aikwenyar, iwadikatai aituutooria oni, lukidoloki awasia naka ikar." 
1Corinthians10:12 Kanuka ŋun kocoite ŋin yeneomit ebe ebwoi, kinyek aibiror." 
1Corinthians10:13 Emamei acodunet nakidoikini yes, namam erai naka ituŋa kere. Konye erai Edeke lomunot, mam ejalakini yes acodunio adepar nuipedorete, konye nenipe kacodunet itemokini neekuianara, tetere ipedorete atitiŋikin." 
1Corinthians10:14 Kanuka ŋun, luminanaka, kinacata aima aputosia." 
1Corinthians10:15 Enera kayes kwape lukacoa; kotuboto yesi nuenera eoŋ," 
1Corinthians10:16 Aikopo ŋin nakarereŋ nakilipakini arereŋ, mere kereka ŋes aimor kaokot nuka Kristo? Emugati ŋol lokibili, mere kereka ŋes aimor kakuan naka Kristo?" 
1Corinthians10:17 Naarai erai emugati ediopet, oni da lukipu, kirai akuan adiopet, naarai kimori oni kere emugati ediopet." 
1Corinthians10:18 Koanyutu kwape kiswamaa Isirael; mam kereka eraas luenyamete asuban ikamorak luka etem? 
1Corinthians10:19 Aso do enera anu? Luainakinitai aputosia eraas kereka ibore? Arai bo ebe erai aput ibore? 
1Corinthians10:20 Mam, konye lueinakinete ikapirin, einakinete mama ejaas ajokin, kwabo mere Edeke. Eoŋ da mam akoto yes aimor kajokin." 
1Corinthians10:21 Mam ipedorete aimat aikopo naka Ejakait, ka aimat da aikopo naka ajokin. Mam ipedorete aimor komesa loka Ejakait, komesa da loka ajokin." 
1Corinthians10:22 Kisurumikereka oni Ejakait ekokote? Ejai tope oni agogoŋ aitelekarit nakeŋ? 
1Corinthians10:23 “Ibusak akiro kere,” konye mam kere isigalikinete. “Ibusak akiro kere,” konye mam kere edukete." 
1Corinthians10:24 Sirikemo ituŋanan akejokis bon, konye naka lucekeŋ," 
1Corinthians10:25 Konyam ŋinibore kere yenegwelario kagwelaret naka akiriŋ, komam iŋisete kanuka abuonokin." 
1Corinthians10:26 Naarai “erai akwap naka Ejakait, ka ailelebake.”" 
1Corinthians10:27 Arai kiinyara yes lomam iyuunit, ikotosi da alosit, konyamata ŋinibore yenibwaikinio kakonyenekus, komam iŋisete kanuka abuonokin." 
1Corinthians10:28 Konye arai kiilimok ituŋanan ebe, “Ibore ŋin ainakinitai araut asubanit,” sirikinyama, kanuka ŋin yenikiitodikini yes, kanuka abuonokin da—" 
1Corinthians10:29 abala eoŋ ebe kanuka abuonokin, mere nakus, konye nakeŋ. Naarai kanukinyo etubokinere akaosikinio kanuka abuonokin naka ice?" 
1Corinthians10:30 Arai amori kaimal, kanukinyo kamoromoroere kanuka ŋin yenemalai?" 
1Corinthians10:31 Aso arai inyamete arai imasete, arai iswamaete adiokirot kere, kiswamata kere kanuka aibuses naka Edeke." 
1Corinthians10:32 Sirikitiguikis Iyudayan, karaida Iyonanin, karaida ekanisa loka Edeke," 
1Corinthians10:33 kwape etalakaritor eoŋ kere kakiro kere, komam amoot akajokis dimarai naka luipu, tetere itajario." 
1Corinthians11:1 Koputoorito eoŋ, kwape eoŋ da aputoritor Kristo." 
1Corinthians11:2 Keturit yes naarai kiitunito eoŋ kakiro kere, ido iricito iponesio kwape kejaikinitor yes." 
1Corinthians11:3 Konye akoto yes ajenun ebe erai Kristo akou naka ŋolikiliokit, ekiliokit da erai akou naka aberu, akou da naka Kristo ŋes Edeke." 
1Corinthians11:4 Ŋolikiliokit loilipi arai loedwari kimukorite akouke, itisili akouke," 
1Corinthians11:5 Konye ŋiniberu nailipi arai naedwari komam akekou imukoro, itisili akouke. Naarai esubit bala ebarenitoi akouke." 
1Corinthians11:6 Naarai arai mam imukoro aberu, koŋera do itimake, Konye arai irumete aberu ileic abarenio arai aŋerio, kimukori do," 
1Corinthians11:7 Naarai mam ibusakinit ekiliokit aimukorit akouke, naarai erai aput ka aibuses naka Edeke; konye aberu ŋes aibuses naka ekiliokit." 
1Corinthians11:8 Naarai ekiliokit mam elomunit kama ka aberu, dimarai aberu kama kekiliokit." 
1Corinthians11:9 Ido mam aponi kosubai ekiliokit kanuka aberu, dimarai aberu kanuka ekiliokit." 
1Corinthians11:10 Kanuka ŋun ibusakinit aberu ajaut kaimukoret akouke kanuka imalaikan. 
1Corinthians11:11 Kwabo toma Ejakait emamei aberu komamei ekiliokit, karaida ekiliokit komamei aberu." 
1Corinthians11:12 Naarai kwape kelomunia aberu kotoma okiliokit, kwape kwaŋin da euruunio ekiliokit kama ka aberu. Epote da iboro kere kama ejai Edeke." 
1Corinthians11:13 Kotuboto kanukus; ibus kereka aberu ailip Edeke komam imukoro? 
1Corinthians11:14 Mam kereka einono elopet kisisianak yes ebe, arai ipisi ekiliokit itimake eraas nukileic kamakeŋ?" 
1Corinthians11:15 Konye arai eojak itima luka aberu, ŋes aibuses kamakeŋ? Naarai einakinitai itimake araparia." 
1Corinthians11:16 Konye arai ekot ituŋanan aitepeg, emamei sio epone loikoni nen, karaida ikanisan luka Edeke." 
1Corinthians11:17 Konye kaicorakinet kana mam keturit yes, naarai naitukonokinotor mam erai ajokis, dimarai aronis." 
1Corinthians11:18 Nasodit, naarai naitukonokinotor okanisa, eira ebe ejaas atiaketa kidiŋikus, eyuunit da ace." 
1Corinthians11:19 Naarai ibusakinit irioŋeta ajaut kotomakus, tetere etakanunete lukabeit kotomakus." 
1Corinthians11:20 Naitukonokinotor yesi mam erai tetere inyamete inyamat luka Ejakait," 
1Corinthians11:21 Naarai kotoma ainyamakus, eyaŋaari ŋinidiopet ikenyamat, kogei ainyam, idiopet da eriebi eteŋei, ice da emerikin." 
1Corinthians11:22 Okwe emameete kereka yes itogoi neinyamiata, ka aimat? Arai bo imenete ekanisa loka Edeke, itisilete da luemameete iboro? Enera anu kayes? Keturit gwai yes? Mam keturit yes kanuka ŋun." 
1Corinthians11:23 Naarai abu kadum kama ka Ejakait, ŋun nukejaikinit yes ebe, kakuare kaya nakebilakinere ebotet, abu Ejakait Yesu kolem emugati," 
1Corinthians11:24 kedau aimal, kobilibil; kotema atiar, “Lo ŋes akakuan naerai kanukus. Kiswamaenenete ŋun aiitunitor eoŋ.”" 
1Corinthians11:25 Kwape kwaŋin da kedaut ainyam, kirum akoli, kobala ebe, “Akoli na erai aitutuket nakitetet kotoma akaokot. Kiswamaenenete ŋun naimasiananata kere, aiitunitor eoŋ.”" 
1Corinthians11:26 Aso irwan kere nuinyamenenata emugati ŋol, arai imasenenata akoli ŋin, ilimorete atwanare naka Ejakait, aitodol naebunio ŋesi." 
1Corinthians11:27 Kwaŋin ŋin yenenyami emugati arai yenemasi akoli naka Ejakait komam ibusakinit, egwaunit akiro nuka akuan ka aokot nuka Ejakait." 
1Corinthians11:28 Konye koŋica ituŋanan ilopet, kosodi konyam nuka emugati, komat da nuka akoli." 
1Corinthians11:29 Naarai yenenyami ka aimat komam imisiikini akuan, enyami emasi da atubokinio." 
1Corinthians11:30 Kanuka ŋun ipu kayesi luekalanyaka, ka luedekasi, ice da ajotooros." 
1Corinthians11:31 Konye arai kimisiikina bonik, mam kitubokinio." 
1Corinthians11:32 Konye nakitubokini oni Ejakait, kilecorio, kenyeis aitelekario nepepe kakwapin." 
1Corinthians11:33 Aso do ikainacan, naitukonokinotor ainyam, kidareununos," 
1Corinthians11:34 arai ejai yeneriebi eteŋei, konyam korekeŋ; kinyek atukonokinikus atubokinio. Etetemi acekiro kere naabunio." 
1Corinthians12:1 Nuka ainakineta nuka emoyo, iinacan, mam akoto yes koolik aijen." 
1Corinthians12:2 Ijenete ebe nairaatar ikapirin kitapaaritai mama ejaas aputosia numam ineras, kwape kiŋarenikinitere." 
1Corinthians12:3 Kanuka ŋun ketejenuni yes ebe emamei ituŋanan yeninera kOmoyo loka Edeke ebe, “Kikenoi Yesu!” kwabo mam epedori ituŋanan atemar ebe, “Yesu ŋes Ejakait,” dimarai kOmoyo Lokalaunan." 
1Corinthians12:4 Aso ejaas ainakineta nuegelegela, konye Emoyo ediopet;" 
1Corinthians12:5 ejaas da iponesio luegelegela luka aijaanakin, konye Ejakait ediopet;" 
1Corinthians12:6 ejaas da iponesio luegelegela luka aswam, konye Edeke ediopet, loiswamai aswamisio kere toma kere." 
1Corinthians12:7 Konye einakinio ŋinituŋanan apukokinio naka Emoyo akerianaror. 
1Corinthians12:8 Naarai einakinio idiopet akirot naka acoa kanuka Emoyo, ice da akirot naka aijen kanuka Emoyo ŋol," 
1Corinthians12:9 ice da aiyuun kanuka Emoyo ŋopeŋol, ice da ainakineta nuka aitaŋaleun kanuka Emoyo ŋol ediopet," 
1Corinthians12:10 ice da aswamisio nuka apedor, ice da aidwar, ice da aitiak komoyon, ice da iponesio luka aŋajepa, ice da aijul aŋajepa," 
1Corinthians12:11 Konye iswamai Emoyo ediopet aswamisio ŋun kere, ŋes ŋol loekorakini ŋinituŋanan kwape ekotor." 
1Corinthians12:12 Naarai kwape eraar akuan adiopet, ejaas da atutubeta nuipu, kwabo atutubeta kere nuka akuan kaŋin, karaida kipu, eraas akuan adiopet, kwape kwaŋin Kristo da." 
1Corinthians12:13 Naarai aponi kibatisai oni kere kotoma emoyo ediopet araun akuan adiopet, karaida Iyudayan, karaida Iyonanin, karaida ibulesin, karaida luijakakaete-aponi oni kere kitamasi Emoyo ediopet." 
1Corinthians12:14 Naarai mam akuan erai atutubet adiopet dimarai nuipu. 
1Corinthians12:15 Arai ketema akeju ebe, “Naarai mam eoŋ arai akan, mam eoŋ arai naka akuan,” mam ŋun itamamaunete ŋes kakuan." 
1Corinthians12:16 Ido arai ketema akit ebe, “Naarai mam eoŋ arai akoŋu, mam eoŋ arai naka akuan,” mam ŋun itamamaunete ŋes kakuan," 
1Corinthians12:17 Arai kerai akuan kere akoŋu, ti kereka aiirar ejai bo ai? Arai kerai akuan kere akit, ti kereka aiŋuun ejai bo ai?" 
1Corinthians12:18 Konye do kwana ibwaikinit Edeke atutubeta, ŋinidiopet kakesi toma akuan kwape akotor." 
1Corinthians12:19 Arai keraas kere atutubet adiopet, ti kereka akuan ejai bo ai?" 
1Corinthians12:20 Konye kwana ejaas atutubeta nuipu, konye akuan adiopet." 
1Corinthians12:21 Mam epedori akoŋu alimokin akan ebe, “Mam eoŋ kepuda jo,” karaida akou alimokin akeje ebe, “Mam eoŋ kepuda yes.”" 
1Corinthians12:22 Konye aitelekarit noi, atutubeta nuka akuan nueomitai araut nuekalanyaka aitelekarit, ipudai noi," 
1Corinthians12:23 atutubeta da nuka akuan nueomitai araut numam ibusak, ŋupeŋun kiinakinit aibuses noi, atutubetawok da nuemamei ajokis, ejai ajokis aitelekarit," 
1Corinthians12:24 namam atutubetawok nuejaas ajokis ipudasi. Konye abu Edeke kimorikik akuan, kaitubusikin noi atutubet naiŋoŋara," 
1Corinthians12:25 tetere mam ejaun atiaketait kakuan, konye kiŋaranakinos atutubeta bonik ka bonik." 
1Corinthians12:26 Arai keriebakin atutubet adiopet, koriebakinos nuce kere kaŋes; arai kitopoloor atutubet, kolakaros atutubeta kere kaŋes." 
1Corinthians12:27 Aso iraas yesi akuan naka Kristo, ka atutubetake, ŋinituŋanan kanukeŋ," 
1Corinthians12:28 Ido ebwaik Edeke ice toma oKanisa, lusodit ikiyakia, lukiareit inabin, lukiwuniet ikesisianakinak, kosodete ikeswamak nukapedor, kosodete lueinakinitai aitaŋaleun, ikeŋarakinak, ikayaitok, ka iponesio luka aŋajepa da." 
1Corinthians12:29 Eraas kereka kere ikiyakia? Eraas kereka kere inabin? Eraas kereka kere ikesisianakinak? Iswamaete kereka kere nukapedor? 
1Corinthians12:30 Ejaas kereka kere ainakineta nuka aitaŋaleun? Inerasi kereka kere aŋajepa? Ijulete kereka kere? 
1Corinthians12:31 Kimielas noi ainakineta nukapolok. Ido ketodikinete yes erot loitelekarit noi ajokis. 
1Corinthians13:1 Arai kener kaŋajepa nuka ituŋa ka nuka imalaikan, kwabo emamei eoŋ amin, arai ibore yeneruo arai aisinin nueruos tai." 
1Corinthians13:2 Bobo da arai ajai kaidwar, ajenuni da nukaiyeiyea kere, ka aijen kere, arai da ajai kaiyuun kere naepedori aitwobot iroŋan, komamei eoŋ amin, mam arai ibore." 
1Corinthians13:3 Bobo da arai kakorak ikaboro kere aitanyamia lukican, bobo da arai kainak akakuan aicweikinio, komamei eoŋ amin, emamei adiojokis," 
1Corinthians13:4 Eŋirikinit amin, esiana amin; mam amin ikokoteono, mam epogana, mam edakunun," 
1Corinthians13:5 mam iswamai numam ibusakinito, mam emoot nuke bon, mam itunyunyurikinio, mam eliliei," 
1Corinthians13:6 mam elelakinit numam edolito, konye elelakinit abeit." 
1Corinthians13:7 Etitiŋikinit amin kere, iyuunit kere, emuno kere, ikanyi kere." 
1Corinthians13:8 Mam amin enaŋi cut; konye kejai aidwar itapalaunio; kejaas aŋajepa, enaŋete; kejai aijen, itapalaunio." 
1Corinthians13:9 Naarai kijeni nuikidioko, kidwari da nuikidioko," 
1Corinthians13:10 konye naejaunia naitekoro, itapalaunio do nuikidioko ŋun." 
1Corinthians13:11 Naaraar ikoku, abu kenera bala ikoku, kajeni bala ikoku, kaomoomoi bala ikoku; naapolooror ketapalau nukeiditeu." 
1Corinthians13:12 Naarai kwana kiseseni karoet kowariwari, konye kapak kaŋin kisesena kakonyen; kwana ajeni nuikidioko, konye kapak kaŋin ajenuni noi kwape kajenunere noi." 
1Corinthians13:13 Aso kwana esalete aiyuun, ka amun, ka amin, ŋun auni; konye naepol aitelekarit kaŋun ŋes amin." 
1Corinthians14:1 Kotupasi amin, kimielasi noi ainakineta nuka emoyo, konye aitelekarit tetere ilimonokinete," 
1Corinthians14:2 Naarai yeninera kaŋajepa mam ineras kituŋa dimarai ka Edeke, naarai emamei yenepupuni konye inera nukaiyeiyea kotoma Omoyo." 
1Corinthians14:3 Konye ŋin yenelimonokini ineras kituŋa nuedukete ka nuitalakarete, ka nuisicerededete da." 
1Corinthians14:4 Yeninera kaŋajep eduko bon, konye yenelimonokini eduki ekanisa." 
1Corinthians14:5 Akoto yes kere einer kaŋajepa, konye aitelekarit noi tetere ilimonokinete. Naarai yenelimonokini epol adepar yeninera kaŋajepa, alemar ejai yenijuli, tetere epedorio aiduk ekanisa." 
1Corinthians14:6 Aso iinacan, arai kabu mama ijaas, kener kaŋajepa, ketudumikini yes ajokis anyoin, dimarai kinera kayes kotoma apukokinio, arai korot loka aijen, arai kalimonokin, arai kaisisianakin?" 
1Corinthians14:7 Iboro luemamei aijar lueruos, bala alamaru arai adeudeu, arai tope mam eruosi kiporotoi luegelegela, ikonakinio ai etiakunio yenekusio arai yeneramio?" 
1Corinthians14:8 Arai da itorokok eporoto loka arupepe, iŋai bo ekapakin kanuka ejie?" 
1Corinthians14:9 Kwape kwaŋin yes da; arai ineras kaŋajep akiro numam ideleleete, ikonakini ai akirot nainerasi ejenun kama ejaas luepupete? Naarai inerasi apak atai," 
1Corinthians14:10 Motoko ejaas iporotoi luka iponesio luipu akwapin, konye emamei loemamei apolou," 
1Corinthians14:11 Aso arai mam ajeni apolou naka eporoto kaŋol, araun bala emoit kama ejai yeninera, ka yeninera da eraun imoit kamakaŋ," 
1Corinthians14:12 Kwape kwaŋin yes da; naarai imielasi noi araut luka ainakineta nuka emoyo, komoata araut luitekoro kotoma aiduk ekanisa." 
1Corinthians14:13 Kanuka ŋun yeninera kaŋajep kilip aijul. 
1Corinthians14:14 Naarai arai kelip kaŋajep, ilipi ekamoyo, konye emameete akaomisio araito." 
1Corinthians14:15 Aso anyoika bo do? Elipi kemoyo, elipi da kaomisio; ayei kemoyo, ayei da kaomisio." 
1Corinthians14:16 Arai imalai kemoyo, eboŋokini biai yeniboie kaibois naka yenemamei ainakineta ebe, “Amen,” naidaunia aimal, arai mam ejeni nuinera ijo?" 
1Corinthians14:17 Naarai elemuni imalai ijo ejok, konye mam yenice edukio." 
1Corinthians14:18 Emalai eoŋ Edeke, naarai enera kaŋajepa adepar yes kere;" 
1Corinthians14:19 konye kotoma okanisa akoto einer akiro akany kaomisioka, tetere esisianakini ice, itia einer akiro alukumin atomon kaŋajep." 
1Corinthians14:20 Iinacan, sirikiraut idwe kotoma aomisiokus; konye kotoma aronis koraut imukerun, konye kotoma aomisiokus koraut luipolok." 
1Corinthians14:21 Iwadikatai kotoma okisila ebe, “Ebala Ejakait ebe, Abuni einer kituŋa kalu kotuŋa luka aŋajepa ace, kaituke da nuka imo, karaida kwaŋin, mam keirarete eoŋ.”" 
1Corinthians14:22 Aso eraas aŋajepa aanyunet mere mama ejaas luiyuunito, dimarai lumam iyuunito, konye alimonokin mam erai kanuka ŋul lumam iyuunito dimarai kanuka luiyuunito." 
1Corinthians14:23 Aso arai etukokina ekanisa kere, kinerasi kere kaŋajepa, arai kelomasi luemameete ainakineta, arai lumam iyuunito, mam kereka ebalasi ebe kikerepiki yes?" 
1Corinthians14:24 Konye arai elimonokinete kere, kolom yenimam iyuunit, arai yenemamei ainakineta, itoronete ŋes kere, etubokinete ŋes kere," 
1Corinthians14:25 ilepilepio nukaiyeiyea nukotauke; kwaŋin ibirori ebuburia, emai ŋesi Edeke, elimori ebe, “Abeit ejai Edeke kayes.”" 
1Corinthians14:26 Aso iinacan, anyoika bo? Nakitukokinotor, ejai ŋinidiopet ekosio, arai aisisianakin, ejai apukokinio, arai aŋajep, arai aijul. Kiswamas akiro kere kanuka aiduk." 
1Corinthians14:27 Arai inera ituŋanan kaŋajep, kinerata iarei arai iuni, mere adepar, bobo da kabeanakin; kijul da idiopet." 
1Corinthians14:28 Konye arai emamei yenikejulan, kililiŋ kotoma okanisa, kinerakin ilopet ka Edeke," 
1Corinthians14:29 Kinerata da inabin iarei arai iuni, komisiikis luce." 
1Corinthians14:30 Konye arai kepukokin yeniboie akirot, kililiŋ yenisodit." 
1Corinthians14:31 Naarai ipedorete yesi kere alimonokin idiopet idiopet, tetere isisiaunete kere, kitalakarai da kere;" 
1Corinthians14:32 korima emoyo loka inabin inabin. 
1Corinthians14:33 Naarai mam Edeke erai Edeke loka ecelet, dimarai loka ainapakin. Kwape ejaar kokanisan kere luka lukalaunak," 
1Corinthians14:34 kililiŋete aŋor kotoma okanisan. Naarai mam ecamakinitai einer, dimarai korimasi, kwape ebalatar ikisila da." 
1Corinthians14:35 Arai ekotos aisisiaun akirot kere, kiŋita ikiliokokec koreriakec, Naarai mam ibus aberu einer kokanisa." 
1Corinthians14:36 Kebuni kereka akirot naka Edeke kamakus, arai bo kidolokinit yes bonik?" 
1Corinthians14:37 Arai eomit ituŋanan ebe erai enabi, arai bo yenikemoyo, koŋic ŋun nuewadikakinit yes, ebe, eraas aicorakinet naka Ejakait." 
1Corinthians14:38 Konye arai emamei ituŋanan aijen, kojau kwaŋin." 
1Corinthians14:39 Aso ikainacan, kimielas alimonokin, sirikitikokinos einer kaŋajepa;" 
1Corinthians14:40 konye kiswamas akiro kere kwape ibusakinitor, ido kopone kaloejok." 
1Corinthians15:1 Iinacan, ketejenik yes Akiro Nukajokak nuabu kalimonok yes, nuipotu yesi kijaut, nuicasitotor da," 
1Corinthians15:2 kanuka ŋun da kitajario, arai kiricata noi akirot naabu kalimonok yes-dimikito iyuunito atai." 
1Corinthians15:3 Naarai abu kejaik yes nusodit nuabu eoŋ da kejau, ebe abu Kristo kotwana kanuka adiakanaretawok, kwape ejaatar nuiwadikatai," 
1Corinthians15:4 ebe da aponi konukai, ebe da aponi kitajarunai kapaaran kanakiwuniet, kwape ejaatar nuiwadikatai," 
1Corinthians15:5 ebe da kitakanikin Kepa, kosodi lutomon kaluarei." 
1Corinthians15:6 Kosodi kitakanikin irwan atipet iinacan luadeparito akwat akany, luipu kotomakec ejarete kiton kwana, konye ajotooros ice." 
1Corinthians15:7 Kosodi kitakanikin Yakob, kosodi ikiyakia kere." 
1Corinthians15:8 Awasia naka ituŋa kere, abu ketakanikin eoŋ da, kwape ikoku yenikijecuna." 
1Corinthians15:9 Naarai arai eoŋ loadit noi kokiyakia kere, lomam kebusakinit anyarao ekiyakia, naarai abu kemanite ekanisa loka Edeke." 
1Corinthians15:10 Konye kanuka asianut naka Edeke arai kwape araar kwana, akesianut da mamakaŋ mam kerai naatitai; dimarai abu keyatak noi aswam adepar kes kere, kwabo mere eoŋ, dimarai asianut naka Edeke nakijaar." 
1Corinthians15:11 Aso arai kerai eoŋ, arai kes, kilimonokini kwaŋin, kwaŋin da ŋes ipotu kiyuuniata." 
1Corinthians15:12 Konye arai elimonokinio Kristo ebe aponi kitajarunai kokatwak, inerasi biai ice kayesi ebe emamei ajarun naka ikatwak?" 
1Corinthians15:13 Konye arai emamei ajarun naka ikatwak, mam Kristo da itajarunitai." 
1Corinthians15:14 Konye arai mam Kristo itajarunitai, aso erai akosilimonokin atitai, akusiiyuun da atitai." 
1Corinthians15:15 Ido kitakani kirai ikajenak luka Edeke lukeŋalak, naarai kitejenunit nuka Edeke ebe abu kitajar Kristo, lomam abu kitajar arai mam ikatwak itajarunio." 
1Corinthians15:16 Naarai arai mam ikatwak itajarunio, Kristo da mam itajarunitai." 
1Corinthians15:17 Ido arai mam Kristo itajarunitai, erai akusiiyuun atitai, isalakinito toma adiakanaretakus." 
1Corinthians15:18 Ido ŋul da lukejotooros kotoma Kristo aoliosi. 
1Corinthians15:19 Arai kimunokina Kristo kotoma aijar kana bon, kirai lukitimitoi adepar ituŋa kere." 
1Corinthians15:20 Konye kwana adau Kristo aitajarunio kokatwak, ŋes araito nugeet nuka ŋul kaluejotooros." 
1Corinthians15:21 Naarai kwape ajaunia atwanare kanuka etuŋanan, kwape kwaŋin ajau da ajarun naka lukatwak kanuka etuŋanan," 
1Corinthians15:22 Naarai kwape etwakiata kere kotoma Adam, kwape kwaŋin ejarete da kere kotoma Kristo." 
1Corinthians15:23 Konye ŋinituŋanan kwape ebeikinia: Kristo ŋes araito nugeet; kosodete naebunio ŋesi ŋul lueraas luka Kristo. 
1Corinthians15:24 Kosodi edoluni esaŋe, naijaikinia ŋesi Edeke Papa ajakanut; naedaunia aitapalaun airumit kere, ka apolou kere ka apedor da," 
1Corinthians15:25 Naarai ibusakinit ŋes airumit aitodol naicakakinia lukasurupoke kere kwap kakejeneke. 
1Corinthians15:26 Lokasurup lokawasia amudiario ŋes atwanare. 
1Corinthians15:27 “Naarai itononokikini Edeke iboro kere kwap kakejeneke.” Konye naetemaria ebe itononokikinio iboro kere, idelelei ebe mam elimunitoi ŋol lokitononokikini iboro kere." 
1Corinthians15:28 Naitononokikinitere iboro kere, ŋes konyet itononokikinitere Okoku da elopet mama ejai ŋol lokitononokikini iboro kere, tetere eraun Edeke loka kere kotoma kere." 
1Corinthians15:29 Ikonakinete bo do ai luibatisauna kanuka lukatwak? Arai mam cut itajarunio ikatwak, kanukinyo kibatisaere kes kanukec?" 
1Corinthians15:30 Kanukinyo do kijaar sio ationis ŋolisawa? 
1Corinthians15:31 Iinacan, etogogoŋit kanuka aoloboboteka kanukus nakijaar toma Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok, ebe, atwani ŋinipaaran" 
1Corinthians15:32 Arai apotu kajioto kitiaŋ kotoma Epeso, kwape etuŋanan, ajokis anyoin? Arai mam itajarunio ikatwak, aso, “Kanyama, kamata, naarai kitwaki moi.”" 
1Corinthians15:33 Sirikiŋalas; “Aup kalueroko emunaari iponesio luejok.” 
1Corinthians15:34 Kikwarut kadolit, ido siridiakanarete, Naarai ejaas ice lumam ejenete Edeke. Enera ŋun aisurumia yes ileic," 
1Corinthians15:35 Konye etemari ituŋanan atiar, “Ikwaikini ai itajarunio lukatwak? Ido epote kakuan anyoin?”" 
1Corinthians15:36 Ibaŋaana ijo, ŋin yeniyei mam ejari dimikito ketwana." 
1Corinthians15:37 Ŋin da yeniyei, mam iyei akuan naejauni, nabarai ikinyomit bon, motoko akimait, arai yenika epone ece." 
1Corinthians15:38 Konye Edeke einakini ŋes akuan kwape akotor, einakini ŋolikinyomit akuanake bon." 
1Corinthians15:39 Naarai akiriŋ kere mam eputonoro; konye ejai akiriŋ naka ituŋa, ace naka itiaŋ, ace da naka ikweny, ace da naka lukecor." 
1Corinthians15:40 Ejaas da awat nuka akuj, ka awat nuka akwap; konye aibuses nakokuju erai ace, aibuses da nakokwap erai ace." 
1Corinthians15:41 Ejai aibuses naka akoloŋ, aibuses ace naka elap, ka aibuses ace da naka aacer: naarai egelegela aacerit adiopet kaacerit ace kotoma aibuses." 
1Corinthians15:42 Ikoni nen ajarun naka Iukatwak," 
1Corinthians15:43 Eyeio komamei aibuses; itajarunio kaibuses; eyeio kakalanyanut; itajarunio kapedor. 
1Corinthians15:44 Eyeio akuan naka akiriŋ; itajarunio akuan naka emoyo. 
1Corinthians15:45 Iwadikatai kwanata ebe, “Korau etuŋanan losodit Adam ekesa loejari.” Korau Adam lokawasia emoyo loeinakini aijar," 
1Corinthians15:46 Konye lokemoyo mam kerai losodit, dimarai lokakiriŋ; kosodi konyet ŋol lokemoyo." 
1Corinthians15:47 Abuni etuŋanan losodit kotoma alup, ŋes lokapua; etuŋanan lokiareit abuni kotoma akuj." 
1Corinthians15:48 Kwape ejaar etuŋanan loka apua, ikote nen luka apua; kwape ejaar da loka akui, ikote nen luka akui." 
1Corinthians15:49 Kwape kiputooro etuŋanan loka apua, kiputoori da lokokuju,"
