1Corinthians15:50 Konye iinacan, enera nu ebe, mam epedorete akiriŋ ka aokot airum ajakanut naka Edeke; ido aibos mam irumi amamus aibos." 
1Corinthians15:51 Koany, kalimokinete nakaiyeiyea ebe: Mam oni kere kijotoor, konye kilocokinio kere," 
1Corinthians15:52 katipet, bala arwakakin akoŋu, keruiki arupepe nakawasia; naarai erui arupepe, itajarunio lukatwak kamamus aibos, kilocokinio oni da." 
1Corinthians15:53 Naarai ibusakinit naebosi na ainap amamus aibos, ibusakinit da naetwani na ainap amamus atwanare." 
1Corinthians15:54 Naebosi na naenapia amamus aibos, naetwani na da naenapia amamus atwanare, ŋes konyet itodolikinor akirot naiwadikatai ebe: “Ejwenyario atwanare kotoma aipikor.”" 
1Corinthians15:55 “Wu jo atwanare, ai bo ejai akoniipikor? Wu jo atwanare, ai bo ejai ekonitidot?”" 
1Corinthians15:56 Etidot loka atwanare ŋes aronis; apedor da naka aronis kes ikisila. 
1Corinthians15:57 Konye kimalai Edeke lokiisipikori oni kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo. 
1Corinthians15:58 Aso do ikainacan luminan, kicata, komam iriaŋiriaŋas, kiyatanakis ŋinipaaran aswam naka Ejakait, naarai ijenete ebe mam itaaritos atai kotoma Ejakait." 
1Corinthians16:1 Konye nuka atukonokin iboro kanuka lukalaunak; kwape ekorakinitor ikanisan luka Galatia, kiswamata yesi da kwape kwaŋin." 
1Corinthians16:2 Apaaran nasodit naka asabato kiŋadak ŋinituŋanan kayesi kidiat, kwape ekerianar, kinyeinai atukonokin naabunio eoŋ," 
1Corinthians16:3 Konye naadolunio, luitojokete yesi kobalua, ŋul eyakiari ayaŋaar akusiinakineta Yerusalem." 
1Corinthians16:4 Arai ibusakinit eoŋ da alosit, kiupari kesi keoŋ." 
1Corinthians16:5 Konye abuni mamakus naadaunia aitor Makedonia, naarai etori Makedonia," 
1Corinthians16:6 Konye motoko asalakin mamakus, arai adaun apak naka aterot kayes, tetere kinyamakinete eoŋ nealosi kere." 
1Corinthians16:7 Naarai mam akoto aanyun yes kwana etori aitor; naarai amuno asalakin kayes apak arai keesiiki Ejakait," 
1Corinthians16:8 Konye asalakini Epeso kiton naka Pentekote," 
1Corinthians16:9 naarai kaŋaikinitai ekek loepol kanuka aswam, ido ejaas luipu luirebirebete." 
1Corinthians16:10 Arai kebu Timoteo, kocoito ebe ejai kayes komamei akurian, naarai iswamai aswam naka Ejakait, kwape kaeoŋ." 
1Corinthians16:11 Kinyek ituŋanan kere aimen ŋes. Konye kinyamakisi ŋes kainapakin, tetere ebuni mamakaŋ; naarai edaret ŋes nepepe kiinacan." 
1Corinthians16:12 Nuka onac Apolo, abu keŋaiŋa ŋes noi abunore mamakus nenipe kiinacan, kwabo mam erai akoteke nepepec da abunore kwana. Konye ebuni naedumunia apak." 
1Corinthians16:13 Kokwenyete, kicata kotoma aiyuun, kiswamata ekiliokone, kogogoŋoto" 
1Corinthians16:14 Kiswamata akusikiro kere kotoma amin. 
1Corinthians16:15 Aso iinacan, ijenete lukokale luka Sitepan, ebe eraas lugeet luka Akaia ido ejaikinos aswam naka aijaanakin lukalaunak; keŋaiŋait yes," 
1Corinthians16:16 kononokikisi yesi da ituŋa luikote nen, ka ŋinituŋanan yenikeswaman nenipe kakes ka yenitaaritoi da," 
1Corinthians16:17 Alakara kanuka abunore naka Sitepan ka Porutunato ka Akaiko, naarai apotu kelelebikis eoŋ nueŋoŋara kamakus;" 
1Corinthians16:18 naara esiyeŋut ekamoyo, ka imoyonokus da. Aso kojenete noi ituŋa luikote nen." 
1Corinthians16:19 Kiyogaete ikanisan luka Asia yes. Kiyogaete da Akuila ka Pirisika noi kotoma Ejakait, ka ekanisa da loejai orekec." 
1Corinthians16:20 Kiyogaete iinacan kere yes. Kiyoganakinos kainu nakalaunan. 
1Corinthians16:21 Eoŋ Paul ŋes ewadikat ayogan na kakanika elopet. 
1Corinthians16:22 Arai ejai yenimam emina Ejakait, korau yenikenitoi. Ebunit Ejakait!" 
1Corinthians16:23 Asianut naka Ejakait kojai kayes. 
1Corinthians16:24 Kojai akamina kayes kere toma Kristo Yesu Amen. 
2Corinthians1:1 Paul ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kanuka akot naka Edeke, ka Timoteo onacewok, Mama ejai ekanisa loka Edeke loejai Korinto, nenipe ka lukalaunak kere luejaas Akaia kere:" 
2Corinthians1:2 Kojai asianut mama ijaas ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo. 
2Corinthians1:3 Kituritete Edeke Papa loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, Papa loka aitim, Edeke da loka aitalakar kere," 
2Corinthians1:4 lokitalakarit oni kotoma aiticanitoiwok kere, tetere oni da kipedori aitalakar ŋul luejaas toma aiticanitoi kere, kaitalakar ŋin nakitalakaria Edeke oni." 
2Corinthians1:5 Naarai kwape iyatanakinor ariebo naka Kristo kamawok, kwape kwaŋin da iyatanakinor aitalakariowok kanuka Kristo." 
2Corinthians1:6 Arai kiticanitoi sio, erai kanuka aitalakariokus ka aitajariokus da; ido arai kitalakario sio, erai kanuka aitalakariokus naeyauni atitiŋikin kariebo ŋin nakisiriebio sio da." 
2Corinthians1:7 Icasit amunokosi kanukus; naarai kijeni ebe kwape imoriata ariebokosi, imorete kwape kwaŋin aitalakariokosi da." 
2Corinthians1:8 Naarai, iinacan, mam kikoto yes kinyeis ajenun aiticanitoi nakidoikinit sio ko Asia, ebe kinuaritai noi noi adepar apedorikosi, komam kiwomit aijar." 
2Corinthians1:9 Kwabo kipou isio kapuput atwanare kotomakosi, kenyeis amunokina bonik, dimarai Edeke loitajaruni lukatwak;" 
2Corinthians1:10 ŋ es abu koyuu sio kotoma atwanare naetia nen, ido kiyuuni, lokimunokina ebe iyatanakini ayuun," 
2Corinthians1:11 Yes da kiŋarakinos ailipanakin sio, tetere imalaete luipu kanukosi, kanuka ainakinet nakiinakinitai sio kanuka ailip naka ituŋa luipu." 
2Corinthians1:12 Naarai aolobobotekosi ŋes nata, ajenanut naka aomisiokosi ebe kipou kalosenenete kotoma akwapin aitelekarit mamakus, kotoma alaunit ka aipioror naka emoyo loebuni kama ejai Edeke, mere kanuka acoa naka akuan, dimarai kanuka asianut naka Edeke," 
2Corinthians1:13 Naarai mam kiwadikakinit yes akirot dimarai nuipedorete asoman ka ajenun, ido amuno ebe ijenunete ŋun kiton awasia," 
2Corinthians1:14 kwape ipotu kojenuniata ace kamakosi, ebe kirai isio aolobobotekus, kwape irauniata yesi da nakosi, kapaaran naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu." 
2Corinthians1:15 Kotoma amun ŋin abu kakoto ailiŋ abunore mama ijaas, tetere idumunete asianut nakiareit;" 
2Corinthians1:16 aitor mamakus alosit Makedonia, ka aboŋun bobo mama ijaas anyoun ko Makedonia, ka yes da ainyamakin eoŋ alosit Yudaya." 
2Corinthians1:17 Aso naakotor ŋun, apotu kereka akaomisio kijulanakinos? Arai bo abu kenerunite ŋun kopone loka akuan, tetere ikote nen kamakaŋ, “Eebo, eebo,” ka “Mam, Mam”?" 
2Corinthians1:18 Konye kwape eraar Edeke lomunot, akosikirot mamakus mere Eebo ka Mam." 
2Corinthians1:19 Naarai Kristo Yesu Okoku loka Edeke, lokipou isio kalimonokis yes, eoŋ ka Silibano ka Timoteo, mam kerai Eebo, ka Mam; dimarai tomakeŋ eraenena Eebo." 
2Corinthians1:20 Naarai aisumuneta kere nuka Edeke eraas Eebo kotomakeŋ, ido kanuka ŋol ŋes kibalar ebe Amen tetere itopoloorio Edeke." 
2Corinthians1:21 Aso ŋol lokiticasi sio nenipe kayes kotoma Kristo, loinyonyoikinit da oni akinyet, ŋes Edeke." 
2Corinthians1:22 Ŋes kipucakini oni aipucet, ka ainakin da Emoyo toma otauonowok araun aititiŋet," 
2Corinthians1:23 Konye eoŋ ewonet Edeke araut ekajenan loka aijaraka, ebe kanuka aitimit yes, mam abu kabu Korinto," 
2Corinthians1:24 Mere ŋes atemar ebe kiyait aiyuunikus, dimarai kirai ikegaŋak luka alakarakus, naarai icasitos kanuka aiyuunikus." 
2Corinthians2:1 Konye alosikinit na ebe mam bobo abuni mamakus kotoma akadakinit. 
2Corinthians2:2 Naarai arai keetakadik yes, aso iŋai bo ketalakari eoŋ, dimarai ŋol loetakadikinit eoŋ?" 
2Corinthians2:3 Abu kewadikak ŋupeŋun kenyek naabunio akadakin kanuka ŋul lutiketalakasi eoŋ, naamunokinor yes kere ebe alakaraka ŋes nakus da kere." 
2Corinthians2:4 Naarai abu kewadikak yes kotoma aiticanio naepol ka aburun naka etau, ka akiyo da nuipu, mere aitakadikin yes, dimarai tetere ijenunete kwape edeparitor noi aminaka mamakus." 
2Corinthians2:5 Konye arai itakadikinit ituŋanan, mam ketakadikinit eoŋ bon, dimarai yes kere nepetai, kenyek ainuar." 
2Corinthians2:6 Ilosikino aiticanet ŋin yenikoni nen naedumuni kama ejaas luipu; 
2Corinthians2:7 ŋes ibusakinitor yes gwai aitim ka aitalakar ituŋanan yenikoni nen, kinyek diat yenikoni nen ailikorio kotoma akadakinike naedeparit." 
2Corinthians2:8 Kanuka ŋun keŋaiŋait yes aitogogoŋ amin kamakeŋ. 
2Corinthians2:9 Naarai abu kewadik kanuka ŋun, tetere ketemi yes, wolo bo irimasi kotoma akiro kere." 
2Corinthians2:10 Konye arai isioniete ituŋanan akirot kere, eoŋ da esioniei ŋes. Naarai arai esionit ituŋanan akirot, esionit kanukus, kakonyen nuka Kristo," 
2Corinthians2:11 kinye Satan aipikor oni; naarai mam kiswakit aijen iboteike. 
2Corinthians2:12 Naadolio Teroa alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo, aponi kaŋaikin ekek kotoma Ejakait;" 
2Corinthians2:13 konye mam ekamoyo eyeŋunit naarai mam adumunit Tito onaceka. Konye abu katwar kes, kalot Makedonia." 
2Corinthians2:14 Konye kimalai Edeke lokisipikonori tir kotoma Kristo, ido loitodiari aures naka aijen ŋes kaŋiniibois kotomakosi." 
2Corinthians2:15 Naarai kirai isio asakat naka Kristo kama ejai Edeke, kotoma kaŋul kaluitaiario, kaŋul da lueoliorito," 
2Corinthians2:16 mama ejaas lukiareit, aures naka atwanare naeyauni atwanare, konye mama ejaas ŋul lusodit aures naka aijar naeyauni aijar. Iŋai kereka ilosikino ŋun?" 
2Corinthians2:17 Naarai mam kirai kwape luipu luegwelanarete akirot naka Edeke, konye kinera kotoma Kristo kwape luipiororoete itauon, kwape luepote kama ka Edeke, akonyen nuka Edeke." 
2Corinthians3:1 Kigeuni kereka aiturokina bobo? Arai bo kwape kicetuŋa kipuda tope ibaluan luka aiturit mamakus, arai kamakus?" 
2Corinthians3:2 Iraas yesi ebaluakosi, iwadikatai otauonokus, ejena esiomete da ituŋa kere." 
2Corinthians3:3 Itakanete ebe iraas yesi ebalua loka Kristo, lokijaanakini isio, iwadikatai mere kebuino dimarai kEmoyo loka Edeke lokajaran, mere amor, dimarai otauon luka awat." 
2Corinthians3:4 Kimunokina Edeke kwaŋin kanuka Kristo," 
2Corinthians3:5 Mam sio kilosikino aomit bonik araut ibore kanukosi; kwabo ebuni aisilosikiniokosi kama ka Edeke," 
2Corinthians3:6 lokisilosikini sio araut ikejaanakinak luka aitutuket nakitetet, mere luka enyukuta, dimarai luka Emoyo; naarai eari enyukuta, konye Emoyo einakini aijar." 
2Corinthians3:7 Aso arai aijaanakin naka atwanare naigirigiritai kinyukutan kamoru, abu kobu kaibuses, tetere mam idwe luka Isirael apedorete asesen akonyen nuka Musa kanuka aibuses naka akonyeneke, aibuses ŋin naitapalaunio," 
2Corinthians3:8 mam kereka aijaanakin naka Emoyo itelekarit kaibuses? 
2Corinthians3:9 Naarai arai kejai aijaanakin naka atubokinio kaibuses, itelekarit noi aijaanakin naka adolit ajaun kaibuses." 
2Corinthians3:10 Naarai naitubusikinitai mam kitubusikinitai kakirot kana, kanuka aibuses naedepari noi noi." 
2Corinthians3:11 Naarai arai naitapalaunio kejai kaibuses, itelekarit noi naesalenenei ajaun kaibuses." 
2Corinthians3:12 Aso kija kamun naetia nen kitwasamai atitiŋ;, naepol," 
2Corinthians3:13 kwabo mere kwape Musa loemukorit akekonyen, kinyeis idwe luka Isirael asesen awasia naka naitapalaunio." 
2Corinthians3:14 Konye kitininikitai ikecetauon. Naarai kiton lolo naesiomenenere aitutuket namojoŋ eriŋa esalit aimukoret ŋipeŋin mam epukoritai; naarai toma Kristo itapalaunitai," 
2Corinthians3:15 Konye kiton lolo naesiomenenere nuka Musa epesikina aimukoret otauonokec; 
2Corinthians3:16 konye naibelonokinor tuŋanan mama ejai Ejakait, elemario aimukoret," 
2Corinthians3:17 Konye erai Ejakait Emoyo, ido neejai Emoyo loka Ejakait, nepenen da ejaikin aosikinio." 
2Corinthians3:18 Konye oni kere kiseseni aibuses naka Ejakait kwape toma aroet, kakonyen numam imukoritai, kiloconokinio aputor ŋes, anyoun kaibuses kiton aibuses, naarai epote ŋun kama ka Ejakait, loerai Emoyo." 
2Corinthians4:1 Kanuka ŋun, kija kaijaanakin na kwape kidumunitor aitimio, mam kitapalikina," 
2Corinthians4:2 konye kiŋer nuibwaitai nuka ileic; kwabo mam kilosenenei ketute karaida aipurujaun akirot naka Edeke kaiŋal, konye kaitodiar naka abeit kitubusikina mama ejaas aomisio kere nuka ituŋa kakonyen nuka Edeke." 
2Corinthians4:3 Ido arai imukoritai Akosikiro Nukajokak, imukoritai kama kalueoliorito." 
2Corinthians4:4 Abu edeke loka ikar kalu kitumudak acoa naka lumam iyuunito kinyeis aanyun ailiya naka Akiro Nukajokak nuka aibuses naka Kristo, loerai aput naka Edeke." 
2Corinthians4:5 Naarai mam kilimonokini bonik dimarai Kristo Yesu Ejakait, ka sio da ikusibulesin kanuka Yesu." 
2Corinthians4:6 Naarai ŋes Edeke loabu kobala ebe, “Kocai aica kotoma amuton,” loecaikinit itauonowok tetere iliyai aijen naka aibuses naka Edeke kakonyen nuka Kristo." 
2Corinthians4:7 Konye kija kabar kana oboro lukelupe, tetere ebuni aidiles naka apedor kama ejai Edeke, kwabo mere kamakosi." 
2Corinthians4:8 Kiticanitoi koponesio kere, konye mam kiridakinio; kibuonokin, konye mam kitapalikina;" 
2Corinthians4:9 kimanio, konye mam kijalakinitai; kicakario, konye mam kimudiario;" 
2Corinthians4:10 kidakenenei tir kawatekosi atwanare naka Yesu itetere etakani da aijar naka Yesu kawatekosi. 
2Corinthians4:11 Naarai nakijaria kijaikinio tir atwanare kanuka Yesu, tetere etakani da aijar naka Yesu kawatekosi nuetwakete." 
2Corinthians4:12 Kwaŋin iswamai atwanare tomakosi, konye aijar tomakus." 
2Corinthians4:13 Konye kija kemoyo ediopet loka aiyuun, kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Abu keyuu, ŋes enerar.” Isio da kiyuunit, kanuka ŋun da kinera." 
2Corinthians4:14 Kijeni ebe ŋol lokitajaruni Ejakait Yesu, itajaruni sio da nepepe ka Yesu, ka aisibwo sio nenipe kayes kakonyeneke." 
2Corinthians4:15 Naarai eraas kere kanukus, tetere kwape iyatanakinor asianut kanuka luipu, iyatanakini da aimal, kitopolooritete Edeke." 
2Corinthians4:16 Kanuka ŋun mam kitapalikina. Karaida emunauna etuŋananekosi Iokokiŋa, konye iteteo lokotoma ŋinipaaran." 
2Corinthians4:17 Naarai ican lu luebenen luka apak naedit, kiswamakinete oni alaŋir naedepari noi noi naka aibuses," 
2Corinthians4:18 naarai mam kiseseni iboro lueanyuna, dimarai lumam eanyuna; naarai lueanyuna eraas luka apak naedit, kwabo lumam eanyuna eraas luka ikar kere." 
2Corinthians5:1 Naarai kijeni ebe arai emunauna iswamuwok yenika akwap kana yenikiboiororor, kija kaduket naebuni kama ejai Edeke, ŋes etogo lomam iswamatai kakanin, loka ikar kere kotoma akuj," 
2Corinthians5:2 Naarai kane kidinya kabeit, kemielas noi aitanapio etogowok loebuni kokuju," 
2Corinthians5:3 kosodi nakitanapere, kenyeis atakanun kimujalal." 
2Corinthians5:4 Naarai kidinya oni lukija toma oswam yen, naarai kilaŋirikinito; mam kikoto alacar, konye aitanapio, tetere ejwenyari aijar yenetwani." 
2Corinthians5:5 Konye ŋol lokiswamakinit oni akirot ŋin ŋes Edeke, lokiinakinit oni Emoyo araun aititiŋet." 
2Corinthians5:6 Aso kititiŋikini oni apaarasia kere, naarai kijeni ebe nakijaar toma akuan, kilwaniar kama ejai Ejakait," 
2Corinthians5:7 naarai kilosi kanuka aiyuun mere kanuka aanyun. 
2Corinthians5:8 Kanuka ŋun kititiŋikini, kikoto alwaniar kakuan, kajaut die ka Ejakait." 
2Corinthians5:9 Aso kigipari aisiyalamikin Ejakait, arai kija die arai kilwaka da." 
2Corinthians5:10 Naarai kibusakinit kere atakanun koiŋaren keicoloŋ loka aitub loka Kristo; kodum ŋinituŋanan nukiswamai akuanake, kwape eswamator, arai nuejok arai nueroko." 
2Corinthians5:11 Aso naarai kijeni ayoŋit Ejakait, kijodouni ituŋa; konye kitakanunitai sio kakonyen nuka Edeke, ido amuno ebe kitakanunitai kotoma aomisiokus da." 
2Corinthians5:12 Mam kiturokina bobo kamakus, dimarai ainakin yes nuiwolobobototor kanukosi, tetere ipedorete aboŋokin ŋul luewoloboboto kakiro nukokuiu bon, kwabo mere nukotauon." 
2Corinthians5:13 Naarai arai kemamu sio acoa, erai kanuka Edeke; arai da kijau isio acoa, erai kanukus." 
2Corinthians5:14 Naarai kitiŋaikinit sio amin naka Kristo, naarai kitogogoŋit ebe abu ediopet kotwanik ituŋa kere; kanuka ŋun apotu kere kotwaka." 
2Corinthians5:15 Ido abu ŋesi kotwanik ituŋa kere, tetere luejarete mam ejarete bobo kanukec bonik, dimarai kanuka ŋol loabu kotwana, kojaru da kanukec." 
2Corinthians5:16 Ŋes mam kitenunia ituŋanan kere kwape ejaar akuan amear lolo, karaida kipou kajenutu Kristo kwape eiaar akuan, konye kwana mam bobo kijeni ŋes kopone kaŋol," 
2Corinthians5:17 Kanuka ŋun, arai ejai ituŋanan kotoma Kristo, arau isubat yenikitetet; atuboros nukolo; koany, araut nukitetiak." 
2Corinthians5:18 Epote kere kama ejai Edeke, loabu kitupuc oni kanukeŋ kotoma Kristo, abu koinak da sio aijaanakin naka aitupuc;" 
2Corinthians5:19 ŋes atemar ebe kejai Edeke toma Kristo itupuci akwap kanukeŋ, komam imarakini kes aibucanaretakec, ebwaiki da tomakosi akirot naka aitupuc." 
2Corinthians5:20 Ŋes kiraar ikiyakia kanuka Kristo, kosubit bala iŋaiŋai Edeke kotomakosi. Kiŋaiŋait yes, kanuka Kristo, kopucoto ka Edeke." 
2Corinthians5:21 Lomam ajeni adiakar kitarau adiakar kanuwok, tetere kiraun oni adolit naka Edeke kotomakeŋ," 
2Corinthians6:1 Aso kiswamai nepepe kaŋes, kiŋaiŋait yes sirikicamut asianut naka Edeke atitai." 
2Corinthians6:2 Naarai inera ebe, “Apak naka acamunio abu keira yes, Kapaaran naka aitajario abu keŋarak yes.” Koany, kwape kwana ŋes apak naka acamunio; koany, kwape kwana ŋes apaaran naka aitajario." 
2Corinthians6:3 Mam kiyaun aiguikinet kere kotoma akirot kere, kinyek akosiijaanakin aitoronio," 
2Corinthians6:4 konye kotoma akiro kere kituro kwape ikejaanakinak luka Edeke; kotoma atitiŋikin naepol, kotoma ocan, kotoma oipud, kotoma aridakinio," 
2Corinthians6:5 kotoma aleconorio, kotoma aenio, kotoma iceleta, kotoma aitaaritoi, kotoma aikolerit, kotoma ailuŋ," 
2Corinthians6:6 kotoma alaunit, kotoma aijen, kotoma aikany, kotoma asianut, kotoma Omoyo Lokalaunan, kotoma amin namam esoswai," 
2Corinthians6:7 kotoma akirot naka abeit, kotoma apedor naka Edeke, kanuka lujiis luka adolit luka akan nakoteten, ka luka akan nakokediany;" 
2Corinthians6:8 kanuka aitopoloorio ka amwaŋio da, kanuka amoromoroo ka aitojokio da, kwape ikeŋalak konye lukabeit," 
2Corinthians6:9 kwape lumam ejenunio, konye luejenunio noi; kwape luetwakete, konye koany, kijari; kwape luiticanio, konye mam kiario," 
2Corinthians6:10 kwape luitururuete konye luelelete tir; kwape luicanas, konye luitabarete ikepuak; kwape luemamei ibore, konye ejaas iboro kere," 
2Corinthians6:11 Wu yes Ikorinton, itooŋaaritai akosiituk mamakus; italalaaritai da ekositau." 
2Corinthians6:12 Mam yes iridakina tomakosi, dimarai iridakina kotauonokus," 
2Corinthians6:13 Konye tetere kitacakinete kotiai lokidumuniata, enera kayes kwape ikadwe, kitalalai da itauonokus." 
2Corinthians6:14 Sirikienikinos ajookot nepepe kalumam iyuunito. Naarai emorete biai adolit ka amamus adolit? Arai ejai eidicane enyoin kidiŋ kaica ka amuton? 
2Corinthians6:15 Anyoin da acamanara naka Kristo ka Belial? Arai bo anyoin akorakinet naka yeniyuunit ka yenimam iyuunit? 
2Corinthians6:16 Anyoin aitutuket kidiŋ ka eyekalu loka Edeke ka aputosia? Naarai kirai oni eyekalu loka Edeke lokajaran; kwape abalar Edeke ebe, “Eboikini tomakec alosenenei da kokidiŋikec, Araun eoŋ da Edekekec, kes da eraunos ikatuŋa," 
2Corinthians6:17 Kanuka ŋun ebala Ejakait ebe, Konyoutu kokidiŋikec, kotiakas kakes, Sirikitirosi ibore yenimam elai; Kesukunyuni eoŋ da yes." 
2Corinthians6:18 Ebala Ejakait Lokapedor kere ebe, Araun eoŋ Papa kamakus, Yes da iraunos ikadwe lusap ka lupesur.”" 
2Corinthians7:1 Aso luminan, naarai kija kaisumuneta ŋun, ketesegaaros kotoma asilianut kere naka akuan ka naka emoyo da, ketodoloto alaunit kotoma ayoŋit Edeke." 
2Corinthians7:2 Koinakinai apak kotauonokus; mam kikonakinit idiotuŋanan erono, karaida amunaar idiotuŋanan, mam da kirodit idiotuŋanan." 
2Corinthians7:3 Mam enera akirot ŋin tetere atubokini yes, naarai abu kenerite sek ebe ijaas yes otauonokosi, kiton atwanare nepepe ka aijar da nepepe." 
2Corinthians7:4 Kija katitiŋ naepol mamakus; kija kaolobob naepol kanukus; ileleba eoŋ alakara. Ilapara noi aileleka kotoma aiticaniokos kere. 
2Corinthians7:5 Naarai nakidolio Makedonia da mam awatekosi iyeŋuna, konye kiticani kowaitin kere-kiŋa kejai ejie, toma da akurian." 
2Corinthians7:6 Konye Edeke, loitalakari luitisilitoi, abu kitalaka sio kanuka abunore naka Tito;" 
2Corinthians7:7 kwabo mere kanuka abunoreke bon, konye kanuka aitalakario nakitalakario ŋes kamakus, kolimonok sio akiro nuka eimielikus, nuka akuudianakus, ka adunyanutukus kanukaŋ, ŋes eyatakinia alakar." 
2Corinthians7:8 Naarai karaida abu kesiturur yes kanuka ebaluaka, mam eitokina, (karaida abu keitok,) naarai aany ebe abu ebalua ŋol kisiturur yes, karaida adaun apak naedit." 
2Corinthians7:9 Konye kwana aleli, mere naarai kitururuoto, dimarai naarai kitururuoto kiton aitoronikin; naarai ipotu kitururuoto mama ejai Edeke, kinyeis atwakiar akirot kere kamakosi." 
2Corinthians7:10 Naarai aiturur mama ejai Edeke iswamai aitoronikin, kiton aitajario namam iitokin, konye aiturur naka akwap iswamai atwanare." 
2Corinthians7:11 Naarai koany aiturur ŋin mama ejai Edeke abu kiswamak yes adunyanut naetia nen, aiyara da, ka anyunyura, ka akurian, ka eimiel, ka akukuranut, ka ainyaŋ da. Kaŋinikirot itodiara yesi araut luilaete kotoma aswamisioit kaŋin," 
2Corinthians7:12 Aso karaida kewadikakinit yes, mere kanuka yenekonit erono, karaida kanuka ŋin yenikikonakinitai erono, dimarai kitoduunai adunyanutukus kanukosi mamakus kakonyen nuka Edeke." 
2Corinthians7:13 Kanuka ŋun kitalakaritai. Bobo da kotoma aitalakariokosi kipou kalelata noi jokan kanuka aile! naka Tito, naarai ipotu yesi kere kisiyenut ekemoyo," 
2Corinthians7:14 Naarai arai abu kaolobobote kamakeŋ kotoma akirot kere kanukus, mam kesurumitai ileic; konye kwape kiilimonokinitor yes akiro kere kabeit, kwape kwaŋin da aolobobotekosi kama ka Tito kerai nakabeit." 
2Corinthians7:15 Ido iyatanakin aminake mamakus, naiitunio kwape irimatar kere, kwape kisukunyikiniata ŋes kakurian ka amaran." 
2Corinthians7:16 Aleli naarai kotoma ŋinikirot icasit amunoka kanukus. 
2Corinthians8:1 Konye iinacan, kikoto yes ajenun asianut naka Edeke nakeinakinio kotoma okanisan luko Makedonia." 
2Corinthians8:2 Naarai nakitemere kes kaiticanio naepol, abu ailelekec nailapara, ka aiyarorotoikec naepol kiyatanak kiton abarara naka aikorokec." 
2Corinthians8:3 Naarai etejenun ebe kwape ejaar apedorikec, ka adepar apedorikec, apotu koseut akorakin iborokec." 
2Corinthians8:4 Apotu kilipata kaiŋaiŋa naepol, kanuka asianut ŋin ka eidicane loka ajiaanakin lukalaunak." 
2Corinthians8:5 Apotu kiswamata kwaŋin, mere kwape kimunor isio, dimarai apotu kogeut ainakin bonik mama ejai Ejakait, ido mamakosi da kanuka akote naka Edeke." 
2Corinthians8:6 Kanuka ŋun kipou kecorata Tito ebe kwape abu kogeunia, koŋetak da kwape kwaŋin asianut ŋin kotomakus." 
2Corinthians8:7 Konye kwape itelekaritotor yesi kakiro kere, kaiyuun, ka einer, ka aijen, ka adunyanut kere, ka akusimina da mamakosi, kitelekarito da kasianut ŋin," 
2Corinthians8:8 Mam enera ŋun kaicorakinet, dimarai kanuka adunyanut naka ituŋa ice aitemio ebe erai akusimin nakabeit." 
2Corinthians8:9 Naarai ijenete asianut naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, karaida kerai lokabaran, konye korau lokican kanukus, tetere kitabari yes kanu ka icanike." 
2Corinthians8:10 Ido kakiro kaŋun ketetemik yes; ejok na kamakus luipotu kogeikis ekaru je, mere bon aswam, dimarai akot da," 
2Corinthians8:11 konye kwana koŋetakis kaswam, tetere kwape ipotu kokapakinotor akot, kwape kwaŋin da koŋetakis kotoma kaluijaatar yesi," 
2Corinthians8:12 Naarai arai ekapakina ituŋanan aikor, ecamunitai kwape ejaatar luejaatar ŋesi, kwabo mere kwape ejaatar luemameete ŋes," 
2Corinthians8:13 Naarai mam enera ŋun tetere isiyeŋunio ice, ka yes da aiticanio," 
2Corinthians8:14 konye aitirian, luidilasi yes kapaarasia kanu itodolete luetwakiarito kesi, kosodete luidilasi kes da itodolete luitwakiarito yesi, kwaŋin ejaun ariakanara," 
2Corinthians8:15 Kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Yeniketukonokini loepol mam edeuni, yeniketukonokini loedit, mam epuda bobo.”" 
2Corinthians8:16 Konye kimalai Edeke loibwaikinit adunyanut ŋipeŋin kanukus otau loka Tito. 
2Corinthians8:17 Naarai abu kocam aicorokosi, kwabo erai loedunyana noi ebuni mama ijaas kakoteke bon." 
2Corinthians8:18 Kijuku nenipe kaŋes onac loituritoi anatar ikanisan kere kanuka alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak," 
2Corinthians8:19 ido mere ŋun bon, konye apotu ikanisan koseutu ŋes aupun kasio kakirot naka asianut kana nakijaanakini isio aitopolooria Ejakait, ka aitodiar da akapakinakosi," 
2Corinthians8:20 Kicoikinit kinyek idiotuŋanan aitoron sio kanuka ainakinet kana naepol nakijaanakini isio," 
2Corinthians8:21 naarai kipodo nuejok mere bon kakonyen nuka Ejakait, konye kakonyen nuka ituŋa da." 
2Corinthians8:22 Nepepe ka ŋul da kijuku onacewok lokipou ketemoto irwan ipu kakiro nuipu araut loedunyana, konye kwana loedunyana aitelekarit kanuka amunoke naepol mamakus." 
2Corinthians8:23 Nuka Tito da, erai epadicika ka ekeswaman da nepepe keoŋ kanukus; nuka iinacanawok, eraas ikiyakia luka ikanisan, aibuses naka Kristo," 
2Corinthians8:24 Aso kitodikisi kes kakonyen nuka ikanisan aitodikinet naka aminakus, ka aolobobotekosi da kanukus." 
2Corinthians9:1 Mam epuda aiwadikakin yes nuka aijaanakin lukalaunak. 
2Corinthians9:2 Naarai ajeni akusikapakina naaolobobotor kanukus mama ejaas Imakedonian, ebe etemokino Akaia ameun kokaru kaje; abu akukuranutukus da kisidik luipu." 
2Corinthians9:3 Konye ejuku iinacan kinyek aolobobotekosi kanukus araun atitai kakirot kaŋin, tetere itemokino yesi, kwape abu kenerar;" 
2Corinthians9:4 kosodete arai epote Imakedonian nepepe keoŋ kodumut da yes mam itemokino, kinyeis ilek airum sio, komam kinera yes da, kamuno kaŋin," 
2Corinthians9:5 Aso abu kaomit ebe kebusakinit aicor iinacan koliŋa aponare mamakus, kogeut kesi aitemokin arereŋ ŋin naipotu kisumunoto, tetere etemokin, mere kwape naitelemunitai kwabo nakarereŋ," 
2Corinthians9:6 Konye enera nata ebe, yeneyei luikidioko, esaki da luikidioko, yeneyei da karereŋ, esaki da karereŋ." 
2Corinthians9:7 Kiswama ŋinituŋanan kwape inerunitor kotauke, mere kaiturur karaida kaitiŋaikin, naarai emina Edeke yenekori kalakara." 
2Corinthians9:8 Konye epedori Edeke ainakin yes asianut kere naidila; tetere yes da itekoro apaarasia kere kakiro kere, idilas aswamisio kere nuejok." 
2Corinthians9:9 Kwape iwadikatere ebe, “Akoro ŋesi, ainaki Iuilwaritos, Ejaenena akedolit ikar kere.”" 
2Corinthians9:10 Konye ŋol loeinakini ikayean ikinyom, lunyaman da ainyam, einakini ka aitupuu ikinyomokus, iyatakini da araito nuka adolitekus." 
2Corinthians9:11 Kitabario yes kakiro kere kiton abar naka aikor kere, naeyauni aimal Edeke kanukosi." 
2Corinthians9:12 Naarai aswam naka aijaanakin na mam bon itodoli nuetwakiarito lukalaunak, konye idila da kanuka aimalaesia nuipu mama ejai Edeke." 
2Corinthians9:13 Kanuka aitem naka aijaanakin na itopoloorete Edeke kanuka arimanutukus alimor Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo, ka abararakus naka eidicane mamakec ka ituŋa da kere;" 
2Corinthians9:14 kes da ilipanakinete yes, imielas yes kanuka asianut naka Edeke naedeparit mamakus." 
2Corinthians9:15 Kimalai Edeke kanuka ainakineteke namam epedorio aitejenun! 
2Corinthians10:1 Eoŋ Paul keŋaiŋait yes, kanuka aiyapepera ka aiyamara naka Kristo, eoŋ loarai loitasono nakijaar kayes, konye naamamear loacerededet kamakus," 
2Corinthians10:2 konye elipi ebe nakijaar kayes kenyek aeereded kamuno kaŋin naaomit atitiŋikin kama ka icetuŋa lueomito ebe kilosenenei isio kwape ejaar akuan. 
2Corinthians10:3 Naarai karaida kilosenenei toma akuan, mam kijio kwape ejaar akuan," 
2Corinthians10:4 naarai lujiis luka ejiewok mam eraas luka akuan, dimarai luka apedor mama ejai Edeke, amudiar aiboisio nuegogon," 
2Corinthians10:5 Kimudiari ipegeta, ka ŋiniirebokinet naikiaritai asurokinia aijen naka Edeke, kijoreori da ŋiniwomisioit arimar Kristo," 
2Corinthians10:6 kitemokin da ainyaŋ amamus arimar kere, naitodolere arimanutukus." 
2Corinthians10:7 Kosesenete nuejaas akonyenekus, Arai itogogoŋit ituŋanan ebe erai yenika Kristo, koomoom bobo na kanuke ebe, kwape eraar ŋesi yenika Kristo, kirai isio da kwape kwaŋin," 
2Corinthians10:8 Naarai arai aoloboboi adepar nuka apoloukosi, naabu Ejakait koinak aiduk yes kwabo mere amudiar, mam kesurumio ilek." 
2Corinthians10:9 Tetere mam asubit bala etukuriani yes kanuka ibaluanaka. 
2Corinthians10:10 Naarai ebalasi kesi ebe, “Elaŋir ikebaluan, egogoŋ da, konye naejaar ŋesi kasio ekalanyana akekuan, akekirot da mam epodoi.”" 
2Corinthians10:11 Kojenut luikote nen ebe nukinera kibaluan nakimamear, ŋupeŋun kiswamai da nakijaar," 
2Corinthians10:12 Naarai mam kineikina atubokina arai aitiriana bonik ka icetuŋa luiturokina, Konye kes itemos bonik ka bonik, itirianas da bonik ka bonik, emamei kes ajenun." 
2Corinthians10:13 Konye mam sio kiwoloboboi adepar aitemis, konye kwape ejaar aitemis naka aikor loekorakinit Edeke sio kwape aitemis, adolokin kiton yes da," 
2Corinthians10:14 Naarai mam kinyaara bonik, bala mam kidolokinit yes; naarai kigeik isio adolokin yes toma Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo." 
2Corinthians10:15 Mam kiwoloboboi adepar aitemis kotoma aitaaritoi naka icetuŋa; konye kimuno ebe naiyatanakinor aiyuunikus, kitopoloorio sio kotomakus kwape ejaar eikorukos kiton adepar da," 
2Corinthians10:16 tetere kilimonokini Akiro Nukajokak aiboisio nuelitoro kamakus, komam kiwoloboboi oikor loitemokino loka icetuŋanan," 
2Corinthians10:17 Konye “Yeneolobobot, koolobobote kotoma Ejakait.”" 
2Corinthians10:18 Naarai yeniturokina, mere ŋin yenecamunitai, dimarai yeniturit Ejakait." 
2Corinthians11:1 Arai koŋirikinito eoŋ kotoma abaŋaanut naedit; eebo, koŋirikinito eoŋ!" 
2Corinthians11:2 Naarai ekokotikinit yes kekokote loka Edeke, naarai abu kesinerik yes ekiliokit ediopet, tetere ketodiari kwape abekot naelai mama ejai Kristo," 
2Corinthians11:3 Konye acoit kinyeis akusiwomisio aitapaario kama ka aipioror ka alaunit nuka Kristo, kwape ejodijodio emun Keba kotoma apirianutuke." 
2Corinthians11:4 Naarai arai ebuni ituŋanan elimonokini Yesu ece lomam sio kilimonokinit, arai bo idumunete emoyo ece lomam idumunito, arai bo icamunito Akiro Nukajokak nuegelara kanuipotu kocamut, iŋirikinete ejok," 
2Corinthians11:5 Naarai aomit ebe mam eoŋ eŋoŋara kadiokirot nakejaatar ikiyakia lukapolok noi. 
2Corinthians11:6 Konye karaida arai eoŋ lomam ajeni einer, mere kwaŋin kotoma acoa; konye koponesio kere kitodia ŋin kakiro kere mamakus," 
2Corinthians11:7 Adiakarit kereka eoŋ aitasonikin tetere yes kitopoloorio, naarai abu kalimonok yes Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke, komam eropit?" 
2Corinthians11:8 Abu kaŋat ikanisan ice adumunio aropio kamakec tetere kejaanakini yes. 
2Corinthians11:9 Ido nakijaar kayes, elwaritoi da, mam abu kalaŋirik ituŋanan, naarai apotu iinacan lukepote koMakedonia kainakis lukepuda. Bon da kotoma akiro kere abu kedarakina kenyek alaŋirikin yes, ido edarakina," 
2Corinthians11:10 Kwape ejaar abeit naka Kristo tomakaŋ, emamei ituŋanan yeniketubutaari kotoma aolobobot ŋin kotoma atutubeta nuka Akaia." 
2Corinthians11:11 Kanukinyo? Naarai mam kamina yes? Ejeŋi Edeke. 
2Corinthians11:12 Konye nueswamai, eyatakini aswam, tetere egaliori einer loka ŋul kaluekotosi einer, tetere kotoma kaŋin naeolobobototor kotakanete araut kwape kasio," 
2Corinthians11:13 Naarai luikote nen eraas ikiyakia lukeŋalak, ikeswamak aimod, luituluoros bonik bala ikiyakia luka Kristo." 
2Corinthians11:14 Mam erai nakaumokin, naarai Satan da ituluonor bon bala emalaika loka aica." 
2Corinthians11:15 Aso mam erai naepol arai ikekeiaanakinak da ituluoros bonik kwape ikejaanakinak luka abeit. Eraun awasiakec kwape akeceswamisio. 
2Corinthians11:16 Enera bobo ebe kinyek ituŋanan aomit eoŋ araut ebaŋ; konye arai kiwomito eoŋ kwaŋin, kocamunitos eoŋ kwape ebaŋ, tetere eoŋ da aoloboboi nuikidioko." 
2Corinthians11:17 Naenera, mam enera kaicorakinet naka Ejakait, konye kwape toma abaŋaanut, kotoma atitiŋ na naka aolobobot." 
2Corinthians11:18 Naarai eolobobotos luipu kopone loka akuan, eoŋ da aoloboboi." 
2Corinthians11:19 Naarai iŋirikinitos luebaŋaka kaiyalama, iraas yesi lukacoal" 
2Corinthians11:20 Naarai iŋirikinitos arai kiitubulesen yes ituŋanan, arai kiiliko yes, arai kiiŋata, arai kedakunun, arai kiibapana yes akonyen." 
2Corinthians11:21 Enera kanuka aitisilikin, ebe kirai isio lukalanyak. Konye arai etitiŋikini ituŋanan akirot kere,—enera kabaŋaanut,—eoŋ da atitiŋ." 
2Corinthians11:22 Eraas kereka kesi Iburanian? Eoŋ da. Eraas kereka kesi Isiraelin? Eoŋ da, Eraas kereka kesi aur naka Aburaam? Eoŋ da." 
2Corinthians11:23 Eraas kereka kesi ikejaanakinak luka Kristo? Enera bala loikerepikinit-eoŋ adeparit-kotoma aitaaritoi naedeparit noi, kotoma aenio naedeparit noi, kotoma aleconorio numam imarunos, irwan ipu kotoma atwanare." 
2Corinthians11:24 Irwan akany aponi kaleconor koYudayan idas akais aoŋon alemar idiopet. 
2Corinthians11:25 Irwan auni aponi kaleconor kasureta; irwan atipet aponi kebiribirii kamor. Irwan auni abu ataker kobwaŋa; ajai ataro akuare ka apaaran; 
2Corinthians11:26 irwanipu kotoma alosit, karonis naka icorin, karonis naka ikaŋatak, karonis naka Iukatekereka, karonis naka Imo, karonis kotoma oreria luepolok, karonis nakotoma amodiŋ, karonis nakotoma aŋolol, karonis naka iinacan lukeŋalak;" 
2Corinthians11:27 kaitaaritoi ka ailolony, irwan ipu kotoma aikoler, kotoma eteŋei ka akure, irwan ipu kotoma ailuŋ, kaaterot ka amujalal da." 
2Corinthians11:28 Komam imarakinit nukokiŋa, ejai nakalanirikinit tiritir, ŋes aiyaloŋoŋ kanuka ikanisan kere." 
2Corinthians11:29 Iŋai bo ekalanyana, komam eoŋ da akalanyana? Iŋai bo kitiguikinitai, komam eoŋ da anoki?" 
2Corinthians11:30 Arai kebusakinit aolobob, aoloboboi kanuka akiro nuka akalanyanutuka." 
2Corinthians11:31 Edeke Papa loka Ejakait Yesu loituritoi ikar kere ejeŋi ebe mam eŋalai," 
2Corinthians11:32 Ko Damasiko, abu ekayaiton loka Areta ekabaka kidar ere loka Damasiko tetere kekamuni," 
2Corinthians11:33 konye kejoluluun kotoma obukit kadirisa naka arwatat, kakuu kotoma akaninike." 
2Corinthians12:1 Kebusakinit aolobob, karaida mam eyauni ajokis; konye adolokini aitegelikineta nuka emoyo, ka apukoreta nuka Ejakait," 
2Corinthians12:2 Ajeni etuŋanan kotoma Kristo, atuboros kwana ikar itomon kaluoŋon,—arai kejai toma akuan, arai kejai kiŋa kakuan, mam ajeni, ejeni Edeke, kowuruporoi loikoni nen kiton akuj nakiwuniet," 
2Corinthians12:3 Ido ajeni etuŋanan loikoni nen-arai kotoma akuan, arai komamei akuan, mam ajeni, ejeŋi Edeke,–" 
2Corinthians12:4 ebe kowuruporoi kiton Paradais, kiira akiro numam inerunos, numam ibus etuŋanan einer." 
2Corinthians12:5 Aoloboboi kanuka loikoni nen, kwabo mam aoloboboi kanukaŋ, dimarai nuka akalanyanurukaŋ." 
2Corinthians12:6 Naarai arai kakoto aolobob, timam arai lobaŋ, naarai enera abeit. Konye etikokina, kinyek ituŋanan aomit kamakaŋ nuedeparito nueseseni ka nuiirari kamakaŋ," 
2Corinthians12:7 Ido kenyek aiturokina kanuka apukoreta nuidilas noi, aponi kainakin ekukwai kotoma akuan, ekiyakia loka Satan, tetere kebuŋai, kenyek aiturokina adepar." 
2Corinthians12:8 Abu keŋaiŋa Ejakait irwan auni kanuka ibore kaŋin, tetere elemario kamakaŋ." 
2Corinthians12:9 Konye abu katema eoŋ atiar, “Akasianut kidaunit jo, naarai itodolitoi akapedor kotoma akalanyanut.” Aso aoloboboi kaiyalama naepol kanuka akalanyanutukaŋ, tetere karapari apedor naka Kristo." 
2Corinthians12:10 Ŋes esiyalamikinitor akalanyanut, aikonakinio nukepali, ailwaritoi, areio, ka aridakinio da, kanuka Kristo; naarai naakalanyanar, nepenen agogoŋoror," 
2Corinthians12:11 Abu karau ebaŋ! Yes kitiŋaikinito. Naarai yes tiibusakinit aiturit eoŋ. Naarai mam eoŋ eŋoŋara kadiokirot nakejaatar ikiyakia lukapolok noi, karaida mam arai ibore." 
2Corinthians12:12 Abeit aponi kiswamai aanyuneta nuka ekiyakia kokidiŋikus, kotoma aŋirikin kere, kanuka aanyuneta, ka nukaumokin ka nukapedor." 
2Corinthians12:13 Naarai inyo kereka ibore yeniŋoŋara kamakus itia ikanisan ice, dimarai mam eoŋ abu kalaŋirik yes? Kitimoi eoŋ aibucaret ŋin!" 
2Corinthians12:14 Koany na ŋes irwan nakiwuniet naakapakina abunore mamakus. Ido mam kalaŋirikinete, naarai mam amoot iborokus, dimarai yes; naarai mam tiibusakinit idwe aiŋadanakin kanuka ikauriakakec, dimarai ikauriak kanuka idwekec." 
2Corinthians12:15 Konye akori ido kakorakinio kaiyalama naepol kanuka aijarakus. Arai kamina yes aitelekarit, eŋoŋar kereka eoŋ aminunio?" 
2Corinthians12:16 Konye kikona nen, mam kalaŋirikinit yes, konye karai loepiriana, abu kalok yes kaimod." 
2Corinthians12:17 Abu kereka kadum ameda kamakus kotoma edio kaŋul lukeiukakinit yes? 
2Corinthians12:18 Abu kecor Tito, kejuk da onac ŋol nenipe kaŋes, Abu kereka Tito kodum ameda kamakus? Mam kereka kilosenenei kOmoyo ediopet? Mam kereka kitupit ikukut ŋupeŋul?" 
2Corinthians12:19 Iwomitos kereka apak na kere ebe kiiyari bonik kamakus? Kakonyen nuka Edeke kinera isio toma Kristo. Konye luminan, eraas kere adukio yes." 
2Corinthians12:20 Naarai acoikina ebe motoko abuni kadum yes ijaas kwape mam akotor, yes da kidumunete eoŋ ajai kwape mam ikototor; kinyeis ipegeta ajaut, ka ekokote, ka anyunyura, ka aŋolopa, ka esiomit, ka aideideonokin, ka adakunun, ka iceleta da." 
2Corinthians12:21 Kinyek Ekadeke aitisil eoŋ kakonyenekus, naabunio bobo, kakuudian luipu luadiakasi sek, komam itoronikinos kanuka amamus ailakec, ka adoteu, ka abenyanut, naapotu kiswamata." 
2Corinthians13:1 Na ŋes irwan nakiwuniet naabunio mamakus. Itogogoŋio ŋinikirot kaituke nuka ikajenak iarei arai iuni. 
2Corinthians13:2 Abu kekwenya ŋul kere luadiakasi sek, ka luce kere da, ido ekwenyari kes kwana naamamear, kwape nakijaar kayes nakiareit, ebe arai abuni bobo mam etimi kes," 
2Corinthians13:3 naarai imootos naitogogoŋi ebe inera Kristo kotomakaŋ. Mam ŋes ekalanyana, konye lokapedor kotomakus." 
2Corinthians13:4 Naarai aponi kibubukinoi kotoma akalanyanut, konye ejari kotoma apedor naka Edeke, Naarai kikalanyaka isio kotomakeŋ, konye kijari nepepe kaŋes toma apedor naka Edeke mamakus." 
2Corinthians13:5 Koŋicas arai ijaas toma aiyuun; kitemos. Arai bo mam ijenete ebe ejai Yesu Kristo kotomakus? Dimarai iraas lumam icamunitai. 
2Corinthians13:6 Konye amuno ebe ijenunete ebe mam sio kirai lumam ecamunitai. 
2Corinthians13:7 Konye kilipi Edeke ebe mam iswamaete adioronis, mere tetere kitakani isio kirai lukicamunitai, dimarai tetere iswamaete yesi aiokis, karaida kirai isio kwape kalumam ecamunitai." 
2Corinthians13:8 Naarai mam kipedori ibore asurokinia abeit, dimarai kanuka abeit," 
2Corinthians13:9 Naarai kileli nakikalanyakar, konye yes igogoŋoros. Kilipi na da ebe yes aitodolikinio," 
2Corinthians13:10 Kanuka ŋun ewadikai nu naamamear, kenyek adedeniar naabunio, kwape ejaar apolou nakainakinit Ejakait adukio, kwabo mere amudiar." 
2Corinthians13:11 Nukawasia, iinacan, yoga do. Kitodolikinos, kitalakanaros, koomitos adiopekirot, kinapakinos, kosodi ejaun Edeke loka amin ka ainapakin kayes." 
2Corinthians13:12 Kiyoganakinos kainu nakalaunan. 
2Corinthians13:13 Kiyogaete yes Iukalaunak kere. 
2Corinthians13:14 Asianut naka Ejakait Yesu Kristo, ka amin naka Edeke, ka eidicane loka Emoyo Lokalaunan, kojai kayes kere." 
Galatians1:1 Paul ekiyakia-mere kama kituŋa, karaida kanuka ituŋanan, dimarai kanuka Yesu Kristo ka Edeke Papa lokitajaruni ŋes kokatwak—" 
Galatians1:2 ka iinacan kere luejaas nepepe keoŋ, Mama ejaas ikanisan luka Galatia:" 
Galatians1:3 Asianut kojai mama ijaas ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok, ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo," 
Galatians1:4 loabu koinakin kanuka adiakanaretawok, tetere kiyuuni oni kama kikar kalu lueroko kwape ejaar akot naka Edekewok ka Papa;" 
Galatians1:5 kojai aibuses mama ejai ikar ka ikar, Amen." 
Galatians1:6 Aumok eoŋ ebe isunyito yesi kwaŋin aibwot kama kaŋol lokinyaraunit yes kotoma asianut naka Kristo, mama ejaas Akiro Nukajokak ace—" 
Galatians1:7 numam eraas ace, konye ejaas icetuŋa luiticanete yes, luekotosi aibelokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo," 
Galatians1:8 Konye arai sio da arai emalaika loebuni kotoma akuj, kilimonok yes Akiro Nukajokak nuegelara ka ŋun nukipou kalimonokisi yes, korau loikenitoi." 
Galatians1:9 Kwape kipou kalimokiniata sek, kwana da alimokini bobo, arai kilimonokini yes ituŋanan Akiro Nukajokak nuegelara kaŋun nuipotu kocamut, korau yenikenitoi." 
Galatians1:10 Naarai ejodouni kereka eoŋ ituŋa, arai bo Edeke? Arai bo amoot kereka eoŋ aisiyalamikin ituŋa? Arai ariŋa esiyalamikinit ituŋa timam karau ebulesit loka Kristo." 
Galatians1:11 Naarai iinacan, akoto yes ajenun ebe Akiro Nukajokak nuabu eoŋ kalimonok, mam keraas kopone loka ituŋanan," 
Galatians1:12 Naarai mam abu kadum kes kama kituŋanan, kwabo mam kesisianakinitai, dimarai kotoma apukokinio naka Yesu Kristo." 
Galatians1:13 Naarai ipotu kiirasi kwape kekonitor sek kodini loka Iyudayan, kwape kareitor noi noi ekanisa loka Edeke, kamuna da ŋes." 
Galatians1:14 Ido abu keyatakin kodini loka lyudayan adepar luatumunete nepepe keoŋ luka atekereka, kekokotikinite noi jokan iponesio luka lukapapaaka." 
Galatians1:15 Konye Edeke loabu katiaku eoŋ ameun kakoik naka totoka, kanyaraun da kanuka akesianut," 
Galatians1:16 nakisiyalamikinitor apukokin eoŋ Okokuke, tetere alimonokini ŋes mama ejaas Imo; atipet mam enerunit kakuan ka aokot," 
Galatians1:17 karaida adokar Yerusalem mama ejaas ŋul lukageikinito eoŋ araun ikiyakia, konye abu kalot Arabia, kasodi konyet aboŋor Damasiko." 
Galatians1:18 Kosodi akaulo naka ikar iuni abu kadoka Yerusalem, aipejokin Kepa, abu kasal kaŋes apaarasia atomon kanukany." 
Galatians1:19 Konye mam abu kaany ice kokiyakia, dimarai Yakob onac loka Ejakait," 
Galatians1:20 (Nukewadikak yes, koany, kakonyen nuka Edeke mam eŋalai!)" 
Galatians1:21 Kasodi alosit atutubena nuka Suria ka Kilikia," 
Galatians1:22 Ido komam ejenuna akakonyen kokanisan luko Yudaya lukejaas toma Kristo," 
Galatians1:23 konye apotu kiirasi bon ebe, “ŋol lokireit oni sek, elimonokini kwana aiyuun ŋin nalem emunaarit,”" 
Galatians1:24 Kitopoloosi da Edeke kanukaŋ. 
Galatians2:1 Kosodi akaulo naka ikar itomon kaluoŋon abu kadoka bobo Yerusalem, nepepe ka Baranaba, kayaŋaasi da Tito nenipe kasio," 
Galatians2:2 Konye abu kadoka kanuka apukokinio; ido abu kapesik kes Akiro Nukajokak nualimonokinit Imo, konye kaiyeiyea kakonyen nuka ŋul kaluecamunitai, kenyek asubit bala akeri, arai bo abu kaker atitai." 
Galatians2:3 Konye Tito da lokijaa keoŋ, karaida erai Eyonanit, mam kitiŋaikinitai akepio." 
Galatians2:4 Konye kanuka iinacan lukeŋalak lukitolomunitai kaiyeiyea, lualomunito airot aosikiniowok nakijaar kotoma Kristo Yesu, tetere kitubulesenete oni," 
Galatians2:5 mam kipou kacamut anonokikin kes nepecep da, tetere kisalakini yes abeit naka Akiro Nukajokak." 
Galatians2:6 Konye kama kaŋul kaluecamunitai araut lukapolok, (kwape ejaatar kesi, mam eoŋ apodo; mam Edeke etiaki kotuŋa), mam ŋul luecamunitai apotu keyatakis eoŋ adiokirot," 
Galatians2:7 konye kepuwai nakeanyuniata ebe aponi ketitiŋi Akiro Nukajokak alimonokin lumam ekepitai, kwape Petero da luekepitai," 
Galatians2:8 (naarai ŋol loiswamakinit Petero ekiyakiane mama ejaas luekepitai, ŋes keswamakinit eoŋ da mama ejaas Imo,)" 
Galatians2:9 nakejenuniata da asianut nakainakinitai eoŋ, apotu Yakob, ka Kepa, ka Yokana, luecamunitai araut ipirin, kainakis eoŋ ka Baranaba akan nakoteten naka eidicane, tetere kilosi isio mama ejaas Imo, konye kes mama ejaas luekepitai." 
Galatians2:10 Konye kokotosi sio aiitunite, lukican, akirot ŋin da nakadunyakinit aswam." 
Galatians2:11 Konye nakebunio Kepa Antiokia, abu kerebok ŋes atereikina, naarai kitelekarito ŋes akiro." 
Galatians2:12 Naarai eriŋa ituŋa ice epona kama ka Yakob, abu komor ainyam nepepe ka Imo; konye nakedolunioto kesi, abu kikunya kogitar bon, ekuriana luekepitai." 
Galatians2:13 Kijoseikis da lyudayan ice kere nepepe kaŋes, kiton Baranaba da ayaŋaario kesoswaikec." 
Galatians2:14 Konye naabu kaanyunia ebe mam kes etenete kabeit naka Akiro Nukajokak, abu kalimok Kepa kakonyenekec kere ebe, “Arai jo loirai Eyudayat, itupi iponesio luka Imo, kwabo mam itupi luka Iyudayan, ikwaikini ai itiŋaikini Imo atupar iponesio luka Iyudayan?”" 
Galatians2:15 Isio lukirai Iyudayan kauruunet kwabo mere Imo lukadiakanarak," 
Galatians2:16 konye kijeni ebe mam ituŋanan itojokio araun yenedolit kanuka aswamisio nuka ikisila, dimarai kanuka aiyuun Kristo Yesu, isio da kipou keyuut Kristo Yesu, tetere kitojokio araut luedolito kanuka aiyuun Kristo, kwabo mere kanuka aswamisio nuka ikisila; naarai kanuka aswamisio nuka ikisila emamei yenejai akuan yenitojokio araun yenedolit." 
Galatians2:17 Konye arai nakimootor aitojokio araun lukidolit kotoma Kristo, kitakanuni kirai ikadiakanarak, erai kereka Kristo ekejaanakinan loka adiakar? Madi akuj!" 
Galatians2:18 Naarai arai aduki bobo ŋun nuabu kamudia, etogogoŋi ebe arai ekebucaran." 
Galatians2:19 Naarai kanuka ikisila abu eoŋ katwana mama ejaas ikisila, tetere ajari mama ejai Edeke," 
Galatians2:20 Aponi kebubukin nepepe ka Kristo; konye ajari, kwabo mere bobo eoŋ, konye ejari Kristo kotomakaŋ; aijar da naajaria kwana toma akuan, ajari toma aiyuun Okoku loka Edeke lokamina eoŋ, lokijaikin bon da kanukaŋ." 
Galatians2:21 Mam etapalauni asianut naka Edeke; naarai arai ejai adolit kanuka ikisila, aso atwana Kristo atitai." 
Galatians3:1 Okwe yes Igalatian luemamei acoa! Iŋai bo kilemelem yes, luaponi Yesu Kristo kolimonokinai kaitebeikin kakonyenekus?" 
Galatians3:2 Akoto aisisia akirot na bon kamakus; Idumut kereka Emoyo kanuka aswamisio nuka ikisila, arai bo kanuka aiirar kaiyuun?" 
Galatians3:3 Iraas kereka luemamei acoa kwaŋin? Naigeuniata ka Emoyo, iŋetakinete kereka kwana kakuan?" 
Galatians3:4 Iriebas nuetia nen atitai?—arai bo erai atitai. 
Galatians3:5 Ŋol lokiinakini yes Emoyo, loiswamai da nukapedor kotomakus, iswamai kereka kanuka aswamisio nuka ikisila, arai bo kanuka aiirar naka aiyuun?" 
Galatians3:6 Kwape kiyuunitor Aburaam Edeke, ido kimarakinai ŋes araun adolit." 
Galatians3:7 Aso kojenutu ebe ŋul Iuka aiyuun, kes eraas odwe luka Aburaam." 
Galatians3:8 Kwabo naki wadikatai naeanyunia sek ebe itojoki Edeke Imo araun luedolito kanuka aiyuun, abu kolo kolimonok Aburaam Akiro Nukajokak ebe, “Isirereŋio atekerin kere kotomakon.”" 
Galatians3:9 Aso ŋul luka aiyuun isirereŋitoi nepepe ka Aburaam lokerai ekeyuunan. 
Galatians3:10 Naarai kere lueraas luka aswamisio nuka ikisila ikenitoi; naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Kikenoi ŋin kere yenimam ericenenei akiro kere nuiwadikatai oitabo loka ikisila, aiswamaenen kes.”" 
Galatians3:11 Aso idelelei ebe emamei ituŋanan yenitojokio kakonyen nuka Edeke kotoma okisila; naarai ebe, “Ejari ikadoliton kanuka aiyuun.”" 
Galatians3:12 Konye ikisila mam eraas kanuka aiyuun, konye ebe, “Yeniswamai kes ejari kanukec.”" 
Galatians3:13 Abu Kristo kolaku oni kama kekenit loka ikisila, nakeraunia ekenit kanuwok, naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Kikenoi ŋin kere yenikajakinitai okitoi.”" 
Galatians3:14 Tetere edoikini Imo arereŋ naka Aburaam toma Yesu Kristo, tetere kidumuni aisumunet naka Emoyo kanuka aiyuun." 
Galatians3:15 Iinacan, enera kopone loka etuŋanan; emamei yenitapalauni aitutuket naka ituŋanan naitogogoŋitere, karaida aiyat akiro." 
Galatians3:16 Aponi kolimokinai Aburaam aisumuneta, ka aurike da. Mam inera ebe, Auriarikon, bala keraas luipu, dimarai bala kerai ediopet, “Aurikon”, ŋes Kristo." 
Galatians3:17 Konye naenera nata ebe, mam ikisila itapalaunito aitutuket naitogogoŋit Edeke sek ikaru akwat aoŋon ka akaisauni eriŋa ikisila ejauna, ŋes mam itamamauniata da aisumunet." 
Galatians3:18 Naarai arai kerai airumet kanuka ikisila, mam bobo erai kanuka aisumunet; konye abu Edeke koinak Aburaam airumet kanuka aisumunet." 
Galatians3:19 Aso inyo bo ikisila? Aponi kiyatakinai kanuka aibucanareta, kiton naebunio aur nakisumunitere; kicorakinitai kanuka imalaikan kakan naka ekadiekan," 
Galatians3:20 Konye ekadiekan mam erai kanuka ediopet, kwabo erai Edeke ediopet." 
Galatians3:21 Aso esurokinete kereka ikisila aisumuneta nuka Edeke? Madi akuj! Naarai arai keinakinitai ikisila luepedorete ainakin aijar, abeit tikerai adolit kanuka ikisila." 
Galatians3:22 Konye agoloki naiwadikatai iboro kere toma adiakar, tetere einakinio luiyuunito aisumunet kanuka aiyuun Yesu Kristo." 
Galatians3:23 Aso eriŋa aiyuun kebuno kiyaito ikisila kigolokinitoi kiton naepukorere aiyuun," 
Galatians3:24 ŋes eraatar ikisila ekeŋarenikinoniwok mama ejai Kristo, tetere kitojokio araun luedolito kanuka aiyuun." 
Galatians3:25 Konye kwana adolu aiyuun mam bobo kiyait ekeŋarenikinon," 
Galatians3:26 Naarai iraas kere odwe luka Edeke kanuka aiyuun kotoma Kristo Yesu. 
Galatians3:27 Naarai yes kere lukibatisatai kotoma Kristo, inapata Kristo." 
Galatians3:28 Emamei Eyudayat karaida Eyonanit, emamei ebulesit karaida loijakakai, emamei lokiliokit karaida naberu, naarai iraas yesi kere idiopet kotoma Kristo Yesu." 
Galatians3:29 Ido arai iraas luka Kristo, aso iraas aur naka Aburaam, ikerumak da kwape ejaar aisumunet." 
Galatians4:1 Konye abala ebe ekeruman naeriŋar erai ikoku, emamei atiaketait ka ebulesit, karaida kerai ejakait loka kere;" 
Galatians4:2 konye eyaito ŋes ikedarak ka ikeŋadak aitodol apak naetetemit papake. 
Galatians4:3 Oni da kwape kwaŋin, nakirokor kirai idwe, karaas ibulesin luka kanugeet nuka akwapin." 
Galatians4:4 Konye naadolio apak naabeit, abu Edeke kijuk Okokuke, lokewuruuni aberu, lokewuruunio koyaito ikisila," 
Galatians4:5 tetere elakuni ŋul lukeyaito ikisila, tetere oni kitaraunio odwe," 
Galatians4:6 Ido naarai iraas odwe, abu Edeke kijuk Emoyo loka Okokuke otauonowok, loiworoi ebe, “Abba, Papa!”" 
Galatians4:7 Kanuka ŋun mam bobo irai ebulesit dimarai okoku, ido arai irai okoku, aso irai ekeruman kanuka Edeke," 
Galatians4:8 Konye apak ya namam ijeniata Edeke, ipotu koraas ibulesin luka ŋul lumam eraas idekesio kauruunet;" 
Galatians4:9 konye kwana ijenut Edeke, konye aitelekarit ajenu Edeke yes, ikonakinete ai iboŋorete bobo mama ejaas nugeet nuekalanyaka ka nukibakor nuikotosi yesi kitubulesenoto bobo?" 
Galatians4:10 Iricito apaarasia, ka ilapio, ka apakio ka ikar da!" 
Galatians4:11 Acoikinit akaitaaritoi kamakus kinyek araun natitai. 
Galatians4:12 Iinacan, keŋaiŋair yes, koraut kwape kaeoŋ, naarai arau eoŋ da kwape kayesi. Mam ipotu kikonakis erono kakirot kere;" 
Galatians4:13 konye ijenete ebe abu kalimonok yes Akiro Nukajokak irwan nasodit kanuka akalanyanut naka akuan; 
Galatians4:14 ido karaida akakuan kerai acodunet kamakus, mam ipotu komwaŋata, karaida aiŋer eoŋ, konye ipotu kisukunyikis eoŋ kwape emalaika loka Edeke, kwape Kristo Yesu." 
Galatians4:15 Aso ani bo akusiisirereŋikino? Naarai etogogoŋit nukus ebe, arai kepedor tikigorununut akusikonyen, koinakis eoŋ." 
Galatians4:16 Arau kereka lokasurup kamakus kanuka alimonokin yes nukabeit? 
Galatians4:17 Kikokotikinitos yes konye mere kotoma ajokis, dimarai kikotos agolor yes kiŋa, tetere yes ikokotikinete kes." 
Galatians4:18 Konye ejok aikokotikinio duc kanuka akirot naejok, kwabo mere apak nakijaar eoŋ kayes bon." 
Galatians4:19 Ikadwe, luariebar bobo bala nakedounon, aitodol naesubunere Kristo kotomakus," 
Galatians4:20 konye tikemuit ajaut kayes kwana, aijulakin ekaporoto, naarai abuonokin kanukus." 
Galatians4:21 Kolimokinai, yes luikotos koyaito ikisila, mam kereka ipupete ikisila?" 
Galatians4:22 Naarai iwadikatai ebe ajaas Aburaam odweke iarei, ediopet loka abulesit, ediopet da loka naijakakai." 
Galatians4:23 Konye ŋol loka abulesit keurio kwape ejaar akuan, konye loka naijakakai kanuka aisumunet." 
Galatians4:24 Akiro ŋun eraas aput: naarai eraas aŋor ŋun aitutuketa aarei. Ebuni adiopet komoru Sinai, naeuriei kanuka ebulesene, ŋin ŋes Kagar." 
Galatians4:25 Kwabo Kagar na ŋes erai emoru Sinai kotoma Arabia; erianas ka Yerusalem loka tinenikwana; naarai erai ŋesi abulesit nenipe kikedwe da. 
Galatians4:26 Konye Yerusalem lokokuju ŋes naijakakai, ŋes ŋin totowok." 
Galatians4:27 Naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Kolakar ijo arakan namam iwuriei, Kodelo, kiworo ijo namam irieba aidoun, Naarai ipu idwe luka naejalakinitai aitelekarit luka ŋin naejai ekiliokit.”" 
Galatians4:28 Konye iinacan, kirai oni idwe luka aisumunet, kwape ka Isaak." 
Galatians4:29 Konye kwape kolo abu ŋol loawurio kwape ejaar akuan koreitor lokeurio kwape eiaar Emoyo, kwape kwaŋin kwana da." 
Galatians4:30 Konye ebala ai naiwadikatai? Ebe, “Kireŋea abulesit ka okokuke, naarai mam okoku loka abulesit irumete kikoku loka naijakakai.”" 
Galatians4:31 Aso iinacan mam kirai idwe luka abulesit, dimarai luka naijakakai." 
Galatians5:1 Kotoma aosikin ŋin abu Kristo koosik oni; kanuka ŋun kicata, kwabo sirikilomasi bobo ajookot naka ebulesene." 
Galatians5:2 Koany, eoŋ Paul kalimokini yes ebe arai kiikepi, mam Kristo kitudumikini yes ajokis." 
Galatians5:3 Konye etogogoŋi bobo ebe ŋinituŋanan yenekepitai itepesenitai aitodol ikisila kere. 
Galatians5:4 Kitiakar kama ejai Kristo, yes luikotosi aitojokio kanuka ikisila; ibiroros ainyein asianut." 
Galatians5:5 Naarai oni kotoma Omoyo kidarete amun naka adolit kanuka aiyuun. 
Galatians5:6 Naarai kotoma Kristo Yesu mam akepio epedori ibore, karaida amamus akepio, dimarai aiyuun naiswamai kanuka amin." 
Galatians5:7 Ikerete lem ejok, iŋai bo kitikokinit yes arimar abeit?" 
Galatians5:8 Aijodijod ŋin mam kebuni kama kaŋol lokinyarit yes. 
Galatians5:9 Aitubuunet naedit itubuuni aluŋuret kere. 
Galatians5:10 Ejai eoŋ amun mamakus kotoma Ejakait ebe mam ijaunete kaomisio ace, konye ŋin kere yenikisiyaloŋoŋoi yes, ebeikini aketubokinio," 
Galatians5:11 Eoŋ da, iinacan, arai eriŋa alimonokini akepio, kanukinyo eriŋar kareitere? Kwaŋin alemar ekomio loka emusalaba." 
Galatians5:12 Arai kepedor ŋul lukiticanete yes tikegitaros! 
Galatians5:13 Naarai iinacan, aponi konyaraun aosikinio; konye aosikiniokus kinyek araun naisigalikini akuan, konye kijaanakinos kanuka amin." 
Galatians5:14 Naarai itodolikinio ikisila kere kotoma akirot adiopet, ŋes nata ebe, “Komina iidunyetekon kwape iminar bon.”" 
Galatians5:15 Konye arai ikonyokonyas, inyamas, kocoito kinyeis amudianar bonik." 
Galatians5:16 Konye abala nata ebe, Kolosenenete kotoma Omoyo, kwabo siritodolete nuimiela akuan." 
Galatians5:17 Naarai imiela akuan asurokin Emoyo, Emoyo da asurokin akuan; naarai eutasi bonik; kanuka ŋun mam ipedorete aswam nuikotosi." 
Galatians5:18 Konye arai kiŋarenikinit Emoyo, mam kiyaito ikisila." 
Galatians5:19 Aso ideleleete aswamisio nuka akuan, kes nupenu: adoteu, asilianut, abenyanut," 
Galatians5:20 aima aputosia, ecudet, asurup, epeget, ekokote, anyunyura, aŋolopa, atiakara, irioŋeta," 
Galatians5:21 alilit, emeret, eraŋa, ka nuikote nen da. Kotoma kaŋun kekwenya yes kwape abu kekwenyaritor ebe, luiswamaete nuikote nen mam irumete ajakanut naka Edeke." 
Galatians5:22 Konye araito nuka Emoyo kes nupenu: amin, aiyalama, ainapakin, atitiŋikin, asianut, ajokis, aiyuun," 
Galatians5:23 aiyapepera, aitikokina; emamei ekisil loisimiki nuikote nen." 
Galatians5:24 Ŋul da lueraas luka Kristo Yesu apotu kibubukis akuan nepepe ka aiŋobeleke ka eimielike da," 
Galatians5:25 Arai kijari kotoma Omoyo, kalosenenete da kotoma Omoyo," 
Galatians5:26 Sirikiiturokin atai, sirikiitunyunyuranakin, sirikiijau da kalilit bonik ka bonik." 
Galatians6:1 Iinacan, arai kedumun ituŋanan ibucarit, yes luiraas luka Emoyo kiteteut yenikoni nen komoyo lokaiyapepera. Koŋica bon, kinyek Ijo da acodunio." 
Galatians6:2 Kodakenenete nuelaŋirikinito ice, kwaŋin itodolete ikisila luka Kristo." 
Galatians6:3 Naarai arai ewomit idiotuŋanan ebe erai ibore, kwabo mam erai ibore, iŋala bon." 
Galatians6:4 Konye kitem ŋinidiopet akeswam, kosodi konyet ejai naeoloboboo kanukeŋ, kwabo mere kanuka yenice." 
Galatians6:5 Naarai edaki ŋinidiopet abwokonike. 
Galatians6:6 Konye komorata yenisisianakinio akirot nepepe ka yenisisianakini kajokisio kere," 
Galatians6:7 Sirikiŋalas; mam Edeke isekelio, naarai lueyei ituŋanan, ŋupeŋul esaki da." 
Galatians6:8 Naarai yeneyeikini akuanake, esaki aibos; konye yeneyeikini Emoyo, esaki aijar naka ikar kere." 
Galatians6:9 Kenyeis aitapalikina aswam nuejok, naarai kedol apakike kisaki, arai mam kiilor." 
Galatians6:10 Aso naeriŋar oni apak ejai, keswamanakisi ituŋa kere ajokis, ido aitelekarit ŋul lukokal loka aiyuun," 
Galatians6:11 Koanyutu kewadikak yes inyukuta luepolok luetia nen kakanika. 
Galatians6:12 Ŋul luekotosi atakan ejok toma akuan, ŋupeŋul kitiŋaikinete yes akepio, konye kinyeis areio kanuka emusalaba loka Kristo." 
Galatians6:13 Naarai luekepitai mam ikulepek ericete ikisila, konye ekotosi yes akepio tetere eoloboboete kotoma awatekus." 
Galatians6:14 Konye eoŋ madi akuj eoŋ aolobob, dimarai kotoma emusalaba loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, lokotomakeŋ kibubukinio akwap kamakaŋ, eoŋ da kama kakwap." 
Galatians6:15 Naarai akepio mam erai ibore, karaida amamus akepio, dimarai yenisubat yenikitetet." 
Galatians6:16 Ido ŋul kere luelosenenete koikor kalo, kojai ainapakin ka aitim mamakec, ido mama ejai Isirael loka Edeke." 
Galatians6:17 Ameari kwana kinyek idiotuŋanan aitican eoŋ; naarai adakit eoŋ imacarin luka Yesu kotoma akuanaka. 
Galatians6:18 Iinacan, kojai asianut naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kimoyonokus. Amen." 
Ephesians1:1 Paul ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kanuka akot naka Edeke, Mama ejaas lukalaunak luejaas Epeso, ka luiyuunito lukotoma Kristo Yesu:" 
Ephesians1:2 Kojai asianut mama ijaas ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo. 
Ephesians1:3 Kituritete Edeke, Papa da loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, lokisirereŋit oni karereŋ kere naka emoyo kotoma Kristo, toma aiboisio nuka akuj." 
Ephesians1:4 Kwape abu koseunia oni kotomakeŋ eriŋa kepesikina akwap, tetere kirauni oni lukalaunak, luemamei aitoronet da, kakonyeneke kotoma amin," 
Ephesians1:5 Abu kineru sek oni araut idwe mamakeŋ kanuka Yesu Kristo, kwape itojokitor akoteke," 
Ephesians1:6 tetere itopoloorio aibuses naka akesianut, nakikwamak oni kotoma Lominat." 
Ephesians1:7 Kotomakeŋ ŋes kidumunia alakunio kanuka akeokot, isioniei aibucanaretawok, kwape ejaar abar naka akesianut," 
Ephesians1:8 nakidilakini mamawok kotoma acoa kere ka acoit," 
Ephesians1:9 nakitejenikinia oni aiyeiyea naka akoteke. Abu kolo kitojok kwaŋin alosikinit kotomakeŋ," 
Ephesians1:10 kanuka aijokokinio nakokar naedolioto, aisimorikikin iboro kere toma Kristo, luejaas toma akuj, ka luejaas toma akwapin da." 
Ephesians1:11 Kotomakeŋ kiseunitai sek araut ikerumak kwape ejaar alosikinit naka ŋol loiswamai kere kwape inerunia akoteke," 
Ephesians1:12 tetere kitopoloori aibusesuke lukigeikini amunokin Kristo," 
Ephesians1:13 Kotomakeŋ yes da luiirarito akirot naka abeit, Akiro Nukajokak nuka aitajariokus, luiyuunito kotomakeŋ, abu Emoyo Lokalaunan lokisumunitoi kipucak yes da aipucet." 
Ephesians1:14 Erai Emoyo ŋol aitogogoŋet naka airumetewok, kiton nealakunere lueraas luka Edeke, kitopolooroi akeibuses." 
Ephesians1:15 Kanuka ŋun eoŋ da, naapupunitor nuka akusiiyuun kotoma Ejakait Yesu, ka akusimin da mama ejaas lukalaunak kere," 
Ephesians1:16 mam enyeini aimal kanukus, eitununei yes kailipika," 
Ephesians1:17 ebe Edeke loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, Papa loka aibuses, koinak yes emoyo loka acoa ka apukokinia ajenun ŋes," 
Ephesians1:18 kinwakenenai akonyen nuka itauonokus, tetere ijenunete amun kwape ejaar naka anyariteke, abar da kwape ejaar naka aibuses naka airumeteke kotoma kalukalaunak," 
Ephesians1:19 apolou da kwape ejaar naedeparit naka akepedor mamawok lukiyuunit, kwape ejaar aswam naka ailerit naka akegogoŋ," 
Ephesians1:20 nakiswamak Kristo nakitajarunia ŋes kokatwak, kisiboik da kakekan nakoteten kotoma aiboisio nuka akuj," 
Ephesians1:21 kuju noi adepar ayait kere, ka apolou, ka apedor, ka ejakaene, ka ekiror da kere loelimitoi, mere bon kokar kalu konye kaluepote da;" 
Ephesians1:22 ido kitononokik iboro kere kwap kakejeneke, koinak da ŋes araun akou ayait iboro kere kama ka ekanisa," 
Ephesians1:23 loerai akekuan, aitekoro naka ŋol loitekori kere toma kere." 
Ephesians2:1 Ido kitajaru yes da, lukolo itwakito kanuka akusiibucanareta ka adiakanareta da," 
Ephesians2:2 nukolo kilosenenete kotoma, kwape ejaar epone loka akwapin kanu, kwape ejaar ekapolon loka apolou naka apak, emoyo loiswamakini kwana odwe luiulaka." 
Ephesians2:3 Kipou isio da kere kekonenenete nen kolo kotoma aiŋobel naka awatekosi, keswamaenenete nuekoto akuan ka aomisio, kirai koinono idwe luka anyunyura kwape kaluce da kere." 
Ephesians2:4 Konye Edeke loebarit aitim, kanuka akemin naepol nakiminaar oni," 
Ephesians2:5 nakitwakitor kanuka aibucanaretawok, abu kituluo oni ikajarak nepepe ka Kristo, (itajarunitai kanuka asianut,)" 
Ephesians2:6 kitonyou oni nepepe kaŋes, kisiboik oni nepepe kaŋes aiboisio nuka akuj kotoma Kristo Yesu," 
Ephesians2:7 tetere kokar luepote itodikini abar naedeparit naka akesianut kotoma ajokis naejai mamawok kotoma Kristo Yesu. 
Ephesians2:8 Naarai asianut ŋes kitajari yes kanuka aiyuun; kwabo mam kebuni kamakus, ŋes ainakinet naka Edeke," 
Ephesians2:9 mam kebuni kanuka aswamisio, kinyek ituŋanan kere aolobobotor." 
Ephesians2:10 Naarai kirai oni akeswamisio, nuesubunitai kotoma Kristo Yesu aswam aswamisio nuejok nukegeunia Edeke aitemonokin tetere kilosenenei kotomakec." 
Ephesians2:11 Kanuka ŋun kiitunito ebe iraas kolo Imo kotoma akuan, luenyarito ŋul luenyarakina bonik luekepitai, lumam ekepitai, ŋes atemar ebe, akepio naka akuan nakiswamaete akanin,—" 
Ephesians2:12 kiitunito ebe kapak kaŋin amamei yes Kristo, igelara kajena naka Isirael, imo luamameete aitutuketa nuka aisumunet, amamei yes amun, amamei da yes Edeke kotoma akwapin." 
Ephesians2:13 Konye kwana kotoma Kristo Yesu yes lukolo kilwaka, kisukunyunitai die kotoma aokot nuka Kristo." 
Ephesians2:14 Naarai erai ŋesi ainapakiniwok, lokiituluorit oni kere ediopet, kotiyaik arwatat nakokidin nakitiakit oni," 
Ephesians2:15 kitamamau asurup kotoma akuanake, ikisila luka aicorakineta kotoma apucuneta, tetere esubuni kotomakeŋ luarei araut etuŋanan ediopet lokitetet, kiswama ainapakin," 
Ephesians2:16 tetere itupuci da luarei kere mama ejai Edeke kotoma akuan adiopet kanuka emusalaba, nakearia ŋes elopet asurup." 
Ephesians2:17 Kosodi kobu kolimonok Akiro Nukajokak nuka ainapakin yes lukilwaka, ainapakin da lueapiete;" 
Ephesians2:18 naarai kanukeŋ oni kere iarei kikunyakini Papa kotoma Omoyo ediopet. 
Ephesians2:19 Aso do mam bobo iraas Imo ka luiboiororos, konye iraas lukajen naka lukalaunak, ka lukokal da loka Edeke," 
Ephesians2:20 naarai aponi kodukokin apetetait naka ikiyakia ka inabin, kerai Kristo Yesu elopet amor nakapolon naka agor," 
Ephesians2:21 kotoma ŋol imorianakino aduketa kere, epoloor araun eyekalu lokalaunan kotoma Ejakait;" 
Ephesians2:22 kotoma ŋol yes da kidukio nepepe araut aibois naiboio Edeke kotoma Omoyo. 
Ephesians3:1 Kanuka ŋun eoŋ Paul, eenat loka Kristo Yesu kanukus kImo,—" 
Ephesians3:2 arai ipotu kiirasi nuka aijokokinio naka asianut naka. Edeke nakainakinio kanukus," 
Ephesians3:3 kwape ketejenikinere kapukokinio aiyeiyea kwape abu kewadikaa sek kanuesupaaka. 
Ephesians3:4 Naisiomiata nu ipedorete ajenun akamisianut nakotoma aiyeiyea naka Kristo," 
Ephesians3:5 namam apotu odwe luka ituŋa kojenut katurio ace, kwape apukorere kwana mama ejaas ikekiyakia lukalaunak ka inabin da kotoma Omoyo;" 
Ephesians3:6 ŋes atemar ebe eraas Imo ikerumak nepepe kasio, atutubeta nuka akuan adiopet, ka ikamorak da luka aisumunet kotoma Kristo Yesu kanuka Akiro Nukajokak." 
Ephesians3:7 Abu eoŋ karau ekejaanakinan loka ŋun, kwape ejaar ainakinet naka asianut naka Edeke nakainakinitai eoŋ, kwape ejaar aswam naka akepedor," 
Ephesians3:8 Kainakinitai eoŋ asianut na, loarai loadit noi adepar lukalaunak kere alimonokin Imo Akiro Nukajokak nuka abar namam imarun naka Kristo," 
Ephesians3:9 ka aitacaikin da ituŋa kere tetere eanyunete aijokokinio kwape ejaar nakaiyeiyea nakibwaitai ameun apeŋo kotoma Edeke lokesubi iboro kere; 
Ephesians3:10 tetere ejenunete ikayaitok ka lukapolou lukotoma aiboisio nuka akuj, acoa naka Edeke nakiponesio luipu, kotoma okanisa;" 
Ephesians3:11 kwape ejaar alosikinit naka ikar kere nakelosikinit kotoma Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok," 
Ephesians3:12 Kotomakeŋ kija katitiŋ, kikunyakini da kamun, kanuka aiyuun ŋes." 
Ephesians3:13 Kanuka ŋun kelipit yes sirikitapalikinos kanuka aiticanioka kanukus, naerai aibusesukus." 
Ephesians3:14 Kanuka ŋun akukonokin Papa kakuninika," 
Ephesians3:15 kama emaikinere eipapaene kere loka akuj ka loka akwap da," 
Ephesians3:16 ebe koinak yes kwape ejaar abar naka akeibuses, aitogogoŋio kapedor kotoma Omoyoke toma otuŋanane lokotoma," 
Ephesians3:17 kiboienenei Kristo kotoma otauonokus kanuka aiyuun; tetere yes, icasete aliasiokus, iketakina da apetetaitikus, kotoma amin," 
Ephesians3:18 kogogoŋoros ajenun nepepe kalukalaunak kere kwape ejaar alalau, ka aojau, ka amukurur, ka aidules," 
Ephesians3:19 ka ajenun da amin naka Kristo naedeparit ajenunio, tetere itekoro kiton aitekoro kere naka Edeke." 
Ephesians3:20 Aso mama ejai ŋol loepedori aswam noi noi adepar kere nukilipi arai nukiwomit, kwape ejaar akepedor naiswamai kotomawok," 
Ephesians3:21 kojai aibuses kotoma okanisa, kotoma Kristo Yesu da, kiton aturio kere ikar ka ikar. Amen." 
Ephesians4:1 Aso eoŋ eenat kotoma Ejakait, keŋaiŋait yes alosenen kwape ibusakinitor anyaraunio nakinyaraunere," 
Ephesians4:2 kaitasono kere ka aiyapepera da, katitiŋikin, koŋirionokinos kotoma amin," 
Ephesians4:3 kodunyakinito aricit eipeone loka Emoyo kotoma olomorut loka ainapakin. 
Ephesians4:4 Ejai akuan adiopet, ka Emoyo ediopet, kwape kolo kinyaraunere kotoma amun adiopet naka anyarauniokus," 
Ephesians4:5 Ejakait ediopet, aiyuun adiopet, aibatis adiopet," 
Ephesians4:6 Edeke ediopet, ŋes Papa loka kere, loeyait kere, loitorit toma kere, loejai da toma kere." 
Ephesians4:7 Konye aponi koinakinai ŋinidiopet kaoni asianut kwape ejaar aitemis naka ainakinet naka Kristo. 
Ephesians4:8 Ŋes ebalar ebe, “Naadokaria kuju abu kijoreo ikijoreoro, Koinak da ituŋa ainakineta.”" 
Ephesians4:9 Akirot ŋin ebe, “Abu kodoka”, ŋes atemar ai dimarai ebe abu kijesar da ariino nukokwap noi nuka akwap?" 
Ephesians4:10 Ŋol loabu kijesar ŋes ŋopeŋol loabu kodoka kuju noi adepar akuj kere, tetere itekori iboro kere." 
Ephesians4:11 Ŋol da abu koinak ice araun ikiyakia, ka ice inabin, ka ice ikalimonokinak Akiro Nukajokak, ka ice ikecokok, ka ice da ikesisianakinak," 
Ephesians4:12 aitodolikinio lukalaunak kanuka aswam naka aijaanakin, kosodi akuan naka Kristo adukio;" 
Ephesians4:13 kiton nepekidolio oni kere oipeone loka aiyuun, ka ajenun da Okoku loka Edeke, kiton nekidolio okiliokone loibecokino, kiton aitemis naka apolou naka aitekoro naka Kristo;" 
Ephesians4:14 tetere mam kirai bobo imukerun luiriaŋiriaŋas, lukiyaŋanari ŋolikwam loka aisisianakin kotoma aimod naka ituŋa, kotute lokibotei luitapaarete." 
Ephesians4:15 Konye karicata abeit kotoma amin, kapolooros da adolore tomakeŋ kakiro kere, loerai akou, ŋes Kristo." 
Ephesians4:16 Tomakeŋ akuan kere kerucokin ka ainicakinio ejok kanuka aisigalikin naka ŋinikilenyasit, kwape ejaar aswam kotoma aitemis naka ŋinitutubet, kiyatanakini akuan apoloor kanuka aiduk kotoma aminanar." 
Ephesians4:17 Aso enera na etejenun da kotoma Ejakait, ebe, sirilosenenete bobo kwape elosenenoto Imo, kotoma aamameak nuka aomisiokec;" 
Ephesians4:18 itumutonitai akececoa, egelara kotoma aijar naka Edeke kanuka aolit naejai tomakec, kanuka aninik naka itauonokec." 
Ephesians4:19 Erum kes esumerededek, aluŋakinos kes ikulepek toma abenyanut aswam nukasilianut kere kotoma airaŋaanut," 
Ephesians4:20 Konye mam yes isisiato Kristo kwaŋin," 
Ephesians4:21 arai ipotu kiirasi ŋes, ka aisisianakinio da kotomakeŋ, kwape ejaar abeit toma Yesu." 
Ephesians4:22 Kotoma akiro nuka iponesiokus lusodit, kolacasi etuŋanane lokolo, loebosi kanuka aiŋobel naka aiŋal," 
Ephesians4:23 ido kiteteunos kotoma omoyo loka aomisiokus," 
Ephesians4:24 konapata da etuŋanane lokitetet, lokesubio toma aput naka Edeke, toma adolit ka alaunit da naka abeit." 
Ephesians4:25 Kanuka ŋun kolacasi asabanut kinerenenasi abeit, ŋinituŋanan kikeidunyet, naarai kirai atutubeta ŋinidiopet kayenice." 
Ephesians4:26 Konyunyurasi, kwabo sirikidiakasi; kinyek akoloŋ alomar koriŋa inyunyurasi," 
Ephesians4:27 kwabo sirikiinakis Satana apak. 
Ephesians4:28 Kinyek ekokolan akoko bobo, konye gwai kokokak aswam ejok kakaninike, tetere edumuni lueinakini yeniyarorotoi." 
Ephesians4:29 Sirikelomu adiokirot kere naebosit kaitukekus, dimarai naejok naeduki kwape ipudar, kosodi ainakin asianut ŋul luepupunete." 
Ephesians4:30 Ido sirikitakadikis Emoyo Lokalaunan loka Edeke, lokolo kipucakini yes aipucet kiton apaaran naka alakuniokus," 
Ephesians4:31 Kolemaros kamakus adwaris kere, ka anyunyura, ka adedeŋ, ka ecelet, ka ainyanakin, nepepe ka ameŋeranut kere," 
Ephesians4:32 koraas luisiaka bonik ka bonik, luitimonoros, ido kisionionoros, kwape kisionio Edeke da yes kotoma Kristo." 
Ephesians5:1 Aso koputorito Edeke kwape idwe luminan. 
Ephesians5:2 Kolosenenete da kotoma amin, kwape Kristo da kiminar yes koinakin elopet kanuwok, ainakinet ka asubanit da naeuru maa mama ejai Edeke." 
Ephesians5:3 Konye adoteu ka asilianut kere ka airaŋaanut sirielimitoi cut kotomakus, kwape ibusakinitor lukalaunak." 
Ephesians5:4 Kinyeis nukileic, ka eyala nukabaŋaanut, karaida aboliar akiro, numam ibusakinito; konye gwai aimalaenen." 
Ephesians5:5 Naarai ijenete yesi kabeit ebe emamei yenedote, karaida yenesiliana, karaida yeniranaana, ŋes yenemai aputosia, yenejaas kairumet toma ajakanut naka Kristo ka Edeke," 
Ephesians5:6 Kinyek ituŋanan aiŋalaŋal yes kakiro nuemameete, naarai kanuka ŋun ŋes ebunokinia anyunyura naka Edeke odwe luiulaka." 
Ephesians5:7 Aso sirikimorianakinos kakes," 
Ephesians5:8 naarai iraas kolo amuton, konye kwana iraut aica kotoma Ejakait; kolosenenete do kwape idwe luka aica." 
Ephesians5:9 Naarai araito nuka aica ejaas ajokis kere ka adolit ka abeit da. 
Ephesians5:10 Kitemete nuitojokit Ejakait. 
Ephesians5:11 Kwabo siridicasi kaswamisio numam eraete, nuka amuton, konye kitoronata kes." 
Ephesians5:12 Naarai erai nakileic alimit ŋun nuiswamaete kesi kaiyeiyea; 
Ephesians5:13 konye nuitoronit aica kere, etakanunete, naarai ŋinikirot kere naetakanunitai, ŋes aica." 
Ephesians5:14 Ŋes ebalar ebe, “Kokweny, ijo yenijotoi, kojaru kokatwak, Kicaikini Kristo.”" 
Ephesians5:15 Aso kocoito noi kwape ilosenenoto, mere kwape luemamei acoa, dimarai kwape luejai acoa," 
Ephesians5:16 koyuununete apak, naarai eroko apaarasia nu." 
Ephesians5:17 Kanuka ŋun siriraas ibaŋiok, konye kojenut nuekot Ejakait kwape ejaatar," 
Ephesians5:18 Kwabo sirimeranakinos ajon, naarai eyaunete iceleta; konye kilelebununos Emoyo," 
Ephesians5:19 kinerenenas kotoma osabulin, ka ikososinei, ka nupwakan nuka emoyo, koyeenenete, kituruonokinete Ejakait lueruos kotauonokus," 
Ephesians5:20 kimalaenenete Edeke Papa apaarasia kere, kanuka kere, kokiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo." 
Ephesians5:21 Kononokianakinos bonik kotoma ayoŋit Kristo. 
Ephesians5:22 Yes aŋor, kononokikis ikiliokokus kwape inonokikiniata Ejakait," 
Ephesians5:23 naarai ekiliokit ŋes akou naka aberu, kwape Kristo da eraar akou naka ekanisa, ŋes Eketajaran loka akuan." 
Ephesians5:24 Konye kwape enonokikinitor ekanisa Kristo, kwape kwaŋin aŋor da kononokikis ikiliokokec kaŋinikirot," 
Ephesians5:25 Yes ikiliok, kominasi aŋorokus, kwape Kristo da keminar ekanisa koinakin kanukeŋ," 
Ephesians5:26 tetere italauni ŋes, kedau aitesegaar kailotar kakipi toma akirot," 
Ephesians5:27 tetere ijaikini ŋes elopet ekanisa lokaibuses, komamei akemer, karaida asukokinet, karaida ibore kere yenikoni nen, konye korai lokalaunan, loemamei aitoronet," 
Ephesians5:28 Kwape kwaŋin da ibusakinit ikiliok aminenena aŋorokec kwape awatekec kikulepek. Loemina akeberu eminakina bon. 
Ephesians5:29 Naarai emamei etuŋanan loelait akekuan elopet, konye itani ka aricit, kwape Kristo da iswamakinitor ekanisa," 
Ephesians5:30 naarai kirai atutubeta nuka akuanake. 
Ephesians5:31 “Kanuka ŋun ŋes inyeinia etuŋanan papake ka totoke da, kirotakinos kakeberu, kes da iarei eraunos adiopekuan.”" 
Ephesians5:32 Epol aiyeiyea ŋin, konye enera nuka Kristo ka ekanisa." 
Ephesians5:33 Konye ŋolituŋanan kayesi kominenena akeberu, kwape eminar bon, koyoŋitenenei aberu da okilenike." 
Ephesians6:1 Yes idwe, korimasi ikauriakakus kotoma Ejakait, naarai ibus ŋin." 
Ephesians6:2 “Koyoŋite papakon ka totokon” ŋes aicorakinet nasodit naejai aisumunet," 
Ephesians6:3 “tetere ijai ejok ido ibusi kakwap.” 
Ephesians6:4 Yes da lukapapa, sirikitunyunyuranakis ikusidwe, konye kosaenenete kes kariemiriem ka aituutoor naka Ejakait." 
Ephesians6:5 Yes ibulesin, korimasi ŋul lueraas ijakakus kwape ejaar akuan, kakurian ka amaran kaipioror naka itauonokus, kwape irimatar Kristo;" 
Ephesians6:6 mere bala kaijaanakin nakokuju kwape luitoiokito ituŋa, konye kwape ibulesin luka Kristo iswamaenenete nuekot Edeke kotauon," 
Ephesians6:7 ijaanakinete kaiyalama, bala ijaanakinete Ejakait, kwabo mere ituŋa," 
Ephesians6:8 kojenete ebe nuejok nuiswamai ituŋanan, ŋes einakinio bobo kama ejai Ejakait, arai erai ebulesit, arai bo erai loijakakai." 
Ephesians6:9 Yes da ijaka, kiswamanakinete kes kwape kwaŋin, kinyeis aitukurian, naarai ijenete ebe ejai Ejakaitikec ka lokus toma akuj, kwabo emamei atiakit ituŋa kamakeŋ." 
Ephesians6:10 Nukawasia, kojaas kagogoŋ toma Ejakait, kotoma ailerit naka agogoŋuke." 
Ephesians6:11 Konapata lujiis kere luka Edeke, tetere ipedorete abwoikin ibotei luka Satana." 
Ephesians6:12 Naarai mam kiwuta kaokot ka akuan, dimarai ka ikayaitok, ka lukapolou, ka lueyaito akwap naka amuton kana, ka ajoresio nuka imoyon luka aronis, luejaas toma aiboisio nuka akuj." 
Ephesians6:13 Kanuka ŋun kolemutu luiiis kere luka Edeke tetere ipedorete abwoikin kapaaran nakaronis, ido kidau aswam kere, aibwo." 
Ephesians6:14 Aso kobwaata, koenito akusiŋabes kabeit, konapito yenikatorob yenika adolit," 
Ephesians6:15 konapito da amuk nuka akapakina naka Akiro Nukajokak nuka ainapakin; 
Ephesians6:16 aitelekarit kere, kolemutu ebuku loka aiyuun, loipedoriata aitudeŋ imalia kere luenokete luka lokaronon." 
Ephesians6:17 Kijautu da akopira naka aitajario, ka ekileŋ loka Emoyo, ŋes akirot naka Edeke." 
Ephesians6:18 Kilipenenete apakio kere kOmoyo, kailip kere ka aiŋaiŋa. Kanuka ŋun kokwenyenenete kainyikokin kotoma aiŋaiŋaanakin lukalaunak kere," 
Ephesians6:19 ido kanukaŋ da, tetere kainakinio aoŋaar akaituk einer, aitejenikin katitiŋ aiyeiyea naka Akiro Nukajokak," 
Ephesians6:20 nuaraar ekiyakia kotoma orikoi; tetere enera katitiŋ kotoma kaŋun, kwape kebusakinitor einer." 
Ephesians6:21 Konye tetere ijenunete kwape ajaar eoŋ, ka nueswamai, ebuni Tukiko onac lominat, ekejaanakinan da lomunot kotoma Ejakait aitejenikin yes akiro kere." 
Ephesians6:22 Ejuk ŋes mamakus kanuka ŋun, tetere iienunete kwape kijaar, ŋes da italakari itauonokus." 
Ephesians6:23 Kojai ainapakin mama ejaas iinacan, ka amin, nepepe kaiyuun, nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papa, ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo." 
Ephesians6:24 Kojai asianut mama ejaas ŋul kere lueminasi Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kamina namam iŋoŋar. 
Philippians1:1 Paul ka Timoteo, ibulesin luka Kristo Yesu, Mama ejaas lukalaunak kere lukotoma Kristo Yesu luejaas Pilipi, nepepe kikaanyanarak ka ikejaanakinak;" 
Philippians1:2 Asianut kojai mama ijaas ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo. 
Philippians1:3 Emalaenenei Ekadeke nakeitununoo yes," 
Philippians1:4 nakelipanakinia yes kere tir, eŋaiŋaenenei kaiyalama," 
Philippians1:5 kanuka eidicanekus aisilosikin Akiro Nukajokak ameun kapaaran nasodit kiton kwana. 
Philippians1:6 Eoŋ da etogogoŋit ebe ŋol loabu kogeu aswam naejok kotomakus, itodoli kiton apaaran naka Yesu Kristo," 
Philippians1:7 kwape eraar naedolit eoŋ aomit ŋin kanukus kere, naarai ijaas yesi otauka, naarai iraas yesi kere luidicakina keoŋ kotoma asianut, kotoma aenioka, ka aiyar kaitogogoŋ da Akiro Nukajokak." 
Philippians1:8 Naarai erai Edeke ekajenanika, kwape kemuitor yes kere kotoma otau loka Kristo Yesu." 
Philippians1:9 Na da ŋes ailipasitika ebe, kiyatanakin akusimin ailapanar kotoma aijen ka amisiikin kere," 
Philippians1:10 tetere icamunete nuejok, iraunos luliogot, komamei aitoronet kiton apaaran naka Kristo," 
Philippians1:11 kilelebi araito nuka adolit nuepote kama ejai Yesu Kristo kanuka aibuses ka aitopoloorio naka Edeke. 
Philippians1:12 Konye iinacan, akoto yes ajenun ebe nukadoikinete apotu kisilosikis Akiro Nukaiokak," 
Philippians1:13 kiton akaenio atakanun ebe ejai kotoma Kristo, kokidiŋ oserikalei kere, ka ice da kere;" 
Philippians1:14 luipu da luka iinacan agogonoros kotoma Ejakait kanuka aenioka, etitiŋikinete aitelekarit einer akirot naka Edeke komam ekuriaka." 
Philippians1:15 Elimonokinete ice Kristo kanuka ekokote ka epeget, konye ice ketau kaloejok," 
Philippians1:16 Elimonokinete lu kanuka amin, kojenete kwape kebwaikinere ne kanuka aiyar naka Akiro Nukajokak," 
Philippians1:17 konye kwi elimonokinete Kristo kanuka aŋolopa, mere kotoma abeit, koomito aitican eoŋ kotoma aenioka." 
Philippians1:18 Aso anyoika bo? Dimarai kotoma oponesio kere, arai kotoma ojose, arai kotoma abeit, elimonokinio Kristo; ido alelakinit ŋin." 
Philippians1:19 Eebo, alelakini do. Naarai ajeni ebe kainunete eoŋ ŋun aitaiario kanuka ainainakus ka ainakinio naka Emoyo loka Yesu Kristo," 
Philippians1:20 kwape emielar noi kamuno da ebe mam kerumete ileic kakirot kere, dimarai katitiŋ kere, kwana, kwape kapaarasia kere, kitopolooroi Kristo kotoma akuanaka, arai kotoma aijar, arai bo kotoma atwanare." 
Philippians1:21 Naarai kamakaŋ aijar ŋes Kristo, atwanare da erai ameda." 
Philippians1:22 Konye arai aijar toma akuan ŋes araito naka aswam kamakaŋ, aso mam ajeni nuaseuni." 
Philippians1:23 Karidakinito akiro ŋun aarei, emiela alosit ajaut ka Kristo, naarai ŋes ejok aitelekarit." 
Philippians1:24 Konye asalit toma akuan ibusakinit aitelekarit kanukus," 
Philippians1:25 Ido naarai etogogoŋit kwaŋin, ajeni ebe asali, ido asalenenei nepepe kayes kere, tetere iyatanakinos yesi kaiyalama kotoma aiyuun," 
Philippians1:26 tetere ilapar akusiwolobobot kanukaŋ kotoma Kristo Yesu, kanuka ajaun kayes bobo." 
Philippians1:27 Konye ejautenekus korai loibusakinit Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo, tetere arai abuni aanyun yes, arai bo amamei, apupuni nukus ebe icasitos kotoma omoyo ediopet, iutas nepepe, ketau ediopet kanuka aiyuun naka Akiro Nukajokak," 
Philippians1:28 kwabo mam ikuriaka lukasurupokus kotoma akirot kere. Kowaikec ŋes aanyunet naka aolior, konye kowaikus ŋes aanyunet naka aitajario, naebuni kama ejai Edeke." 
Philippians1:29 Naarai kiinakinitai yes, kanuka Kristo, mere bon aiyuun ŋes, dimarai aisiriebio da kanukeŋ," 
Philippians1:30 kojaas kauta kaŋin nakianyunete kotomakaŋ, ido naipupete kwana ejai tomakaŋ." 
Philippians2:1 Aso arai ejai aitalakar kotoma Kristo, arai aiyamakina naka amin, arai eidicane loka Emoyo, arai aisioni ka aitim," 
Philippians2:2 kitodolete akaiyalama, tetere iwomitos adiopekirot, ijaas kamin adiopet, luka emoyo ediopet, iwomitos nepepe." 
Philippians2:3 Sirikiswamata akirot kere kanuka aŋolopa, karaida eitur atai, dimarai kaitasono ŋinituŋanan kitopoloorite aupake, itia ŋes ilopet." 
Philippians2:4 Kinyek ŋinituŋanan asesen nuke bon, konye nuka luce da." 
Philippians2:5 Koomitos yesi kotomakus, kwape aomitor Kristo Yesu," 
Philippians2:6 lokejai einono loka Edeke, komam imarakina arianakin ka Edeke araun ibore yenimariauna," 
Philippians2:7 konye kitisilikin, koyaŋaa einono loka ebulesit, kouriai toma aput naka etuŋanan." 
Philippians2:8 Abu kotakan ejaas kasubunet bala naka etuŋanan, kitasonikin, korima kiton atwanare, atwanare da naka emusalaba." 
Philippians2:9 Ŋes etopolooria noi Edeke ŋes, koinak ŋes ekiror ŋol loitelekarit ikiroria kere," 
Philippians2:10 tetere ekukonokini ŋinikuŋ ekiror loka Yesu, nuka akuj, ka nuka akwap, ka nukokwap kakwap da;" 
Philippians2:11 ido kolimonori ŋiniŋajep ebe Yesu Kristo ŋes Ejakait, kitopolooritete Edeke Papa." 
Philippians2:12 Aso, luminanaka, kwape ipotu korimanariata apaarasia kere, mere naajaar eoŋ bon, konye aitelekarit noi kwana naamamea eoŋ, kitodolenenete aitajariokus, kayoŋite ka amaran da," 
Philippians2:13 naarai Edeke ŋes iswamai kotomakus, ainakin yes akot ka aswam da nuitoiokit ŋesi." 
Philippians2:14 Kiswamaenenete kere komamei aŋurian ka epeget," 
Philippians2:15 tetere iraas idwe luka Edeke luemamei aitoronet, luiyapaara, luemamei akemer kokidiŋ katur kanamagul, ka naepaarit, naitakaniata bala aica kotoma akwapin," 
Philippians2:16 itodiarete akirot naka aijar, kasodi aolobob kapaaran naka Kristo, ebe mam abu kaker atai, karaida aitaaritoi atai,"
