Philippians2:17 Konye karaida kaabukokinio asubanit ka aijaanakin naka aiyuunikus, eyalama, ido eyalama nepepe kayes kere." 
Philippians2:18 Kiyalamas yesi da kwaŋin, kiyalamikinos da nepepe keoŋ." 
Philippians2:19 Konye amuno kotoma Ejakait Yesu aijukakin yes atipet Timoteo, kasodi atitiŋior kadau ajenun akirokus." 
Philippians2:20 Naarai emamei eoŋ icetuŋanan yeneriakasi kaŋes, loepodo noi ejautenekus." 
Philippians2:21 Naarai ŋul kere emootos nukec bonik, kwabo mere nuka Yesu Kristo." 
Philippians2:22 Konye ijenete akeiturio, ebe kwape ikoku kapapake abu kijaanakini Akiro Nukajokak nepepe keoŋ," 
Philippians2:23 Aso amuno aijukun ŋes atipet kadau ber aanyun nukadoikinete; 
Philippians2:24 konye amuno kotoma Ejakait ebe eoŋ da abuni atipet. 
Philippians2:25 Konye abu kaomit ebe kebusakinit aijukakin yes Epapurodito onaceka, loiswamai ka ejie da nepepe keoŋ, konye ŋes ekiyakiakus, ekejaanakinan da loka eipudika." 
Philippians2:26 Naarai abu kimuite yes kere, kokadakinite noi, naarai ipotu kiirasi ebe edek." 
Philippians2:27 Naarai abu kodekakin noi nepetai atwanare, Konye abu Edeke kitim ŋes, kwabo mere ŋes bon, konye eoŋ da, kinyek aiturur aiyatakin toma aitururuka." 
Philippians2:28 Ŋes akokakinia noi aijukun ŋes, tetere naianyuniata ŋes bobo, kiyalamikinos, eoŋ da iŋoŋar akaiturur." 
Philippians2:29 Aso kisukunyikisi ŋes kotoma Ejakait, kaiyalama kere; ido kitubusikis luikote kwaka ŋol," 
Philippians2:30 naarai aapiarit nepetai atwanare kanuka aswam naka Kristo, abu koluŋak akeijar tetere itodolikini nuemameete kotoma aijaanakinikus kamakaŋ." 
Philippians3:1 Nuesalito, ikainacan, kiyalamas kotoma Ejakait. Mam ketapasi eoŋ aiwadikakin yes ŋupeŋun, konye kiticasete yes." 
Philippians3:2 Kocoito iŋokwo, kocoito ikeswamak nueroko, kocoito luegeras." 
Philippians3:3 Naarai kirai oni luka akepio nakabeit, lukimai kOmoyo loka Edeke, lukiwolobobot kotoma Kristo Yesu, ido lumam kimunokina akuan." 
Philippians3:4 Karaida kapedori eoŋ amunokina akuan. Arai eomit etuŋanan ece kere amunokina akuan eoŋ etelekarit: 
Philippians3:5 aponi kakepi kapaaran nakikanyetekauni, loka ajena naka Isirael, loka ateker naka Benyamin, Eburaniat obe loka Iburanian; kakiro nuka ikisila, Eparisayot," 
Philippians3:6 kakiro nuka adunyanut, kareite ekanisa, kakiro nuka adolit naejai toma okisila, mam abu kajai kaitoronet." 
Philippians3:7 Konye kere nukeraas ameda kamakaŋ, abu kaomit atwaniar kanuka Kristo." 
Philippians3:8 Konye abu kaomite cut iboro kere araut atwaniar kanuka ajokis naepol noi naka ajenun Kristo Yesu Ejakaitika, Abu katwania iboro kere kanukeŋ, kaomite da araut acin, tetere adumuni Kristo," 
Philippians3:9 kasodi adumunio kotomakeŋ, komamei adoliteka, naebuni kotoma okisila, dimarai ŋin naebuni kanuka aiyuun Kristo, adolit naebuni kama ejai Edeke kotoma aiyuun," 
Philippians3:10 tetere ajenuni ŋes, ka apedor naka ajarunike, ka aimor kaŋes arieboke, ketuputoritere katwanareke," 
Philippians3:11 tetere arai apedori, adolokini ajarun nakokatwak," 
Philippians3:12 Mere ebe adau adumun karaida aitodolikinio; konye ebwapit tetere ekamuni, naarai kekamunit Kristo Yesu eoŋ." 
Philippians3:13 Iinacan, mam aomit ebe adau aikamun, konye eswamai adiopekirot, kemurwokinete nukokau, kewopei nuejaas kiŋaren," 
Philippians3:14 ebwapit adolore neepegare, neejai ainakinet naka anyarit nakokuju naka Edeke toma Kristo Yesu." 
Philippians3:15 Aso oni kere lukipoloor, kaomitos ŋun; ido arai iwomitos yesi nuegelara, kipukokini da Edeke yes ŋin." 
Philippians3:16 Konye ca nukidoloki, kalosenenete kaŋun," 
Philippians3:17 Iinacan, koputorito eoŋ nepepe, ido kosesenete ŋul luelosete kwape ejaar yes aanyunet kamakosi." 
Philippians3:18 Naarai elosete luipu, luabu kalimonok yes irwan ipu, kwana da kalimokini kamonyi, ebe kes lukasurupo luka emusalaba loka Kristo," 
Philippians3:19 Esaŋekec ŋes amudiar, edekekec ŋes akoik, aibusesukec da ejai toma oleic, eomitos nuka akwap." 
Philippians3:20 Naarai obuwok ejai toma akuj, ŋina da kidareo Eketaiaran, Ejakait Yesu Kristo," 
Philippians3:21 loilocokini awatewok nuesilok, aputoor akekuan nakaibuses, kwape ejaar aswam naka akepedor aitononokikin iboro kere kwapukeŋ." 
Philippians4:1 Aso iinacanaka luminan, lukemuit da, akaiyalama ka akaboko da, kobwaata kwaŋin kicasito kotoma Ejakait, luminan," 
Philippians4:2 Eŋaiŋait Euodia, eŋaiŋait da Suntuke, koiaas kaomit adiopet, kotoma Ejakait." 
Philippians4:3 Eebo, kelipit jo da, ekiŋariŋaret ajookot lokabeit, kiŋarak aŋor ŋun, nuetaaritos nenipe keoŋ toma Akiro Nukajokak, ka Kelement da, ka ikeswamak ice da lukaupaka, luejaas ikiroriakec toma oitabo loka aijar." 
Philippians4:4 Kiyalamas kotoma Ejakait apaarasia kere; abala bobo ebe kiyalamas. 
Philippians4:5 Kojenun akusiiyapaara kotuŋa kere. Eapie Ejakait. 
Philippians4:6 Siriyaloŋoŋoete akirot kere, konye kotoma akiro kere toma ailip ka aiŋaiŋa nepepe kaimal, kitejenut Edeke nuikotosi." 
Philippians4:7 Ainapakin da naka Edeke naedeparit ajenun kere, kidarenenei itauonokus ka aomisiokus kotoma Kristo Yesu." 
Philippians4:8 Nuesalito iinacan, nueraas nukabeit kere, nuibusakinito kere, nuedolito kere, nukalaunak kere, nutemela kere, nuisupete kere, arai ejai ajokis kere, ido arai ejai aiturit, koomoomoete ŋun." 
Philippians4:9 Akiro da nuipotu kisisiata kamakaŋ, kodumutu da, kopuputu da, koanyutu da kamakaŋ, kiswamaenenete ŋun; ejaenena da Edeke loka ainapakin kayes." 
Philippians4:10 Konye eyalama noi kotoma Ejakait, naarai kwana atubor apak ekwarutu da akusiwomisio kanukaŋ, kwabo ipotu koomitos ŋun konye kemamei yes apak," 
Philippians4:11 Mere ebe enera kanuka eipud; naarai abu kesisia adauna kwape ajaar kere. 
Philippians4:12 Ajeni aitisilio, ajeni da alitoro; kaŋinikirot, ido kotoma akiro kere, ketuutooritai aiyeiyea naka aimonikin ka ariebo eteŋei da, alitoro ka aiŋonara da." 
Philippians4:13 Apedorit kere kotoma kaŋol kaloketogogoni. 
Philippians4:14 Konye ipotu kiswamata ejok naimorikikinotor kaiticaniokaŋ," 
Philippians4:15 Ijenete yesi da Ipilipin ebe, kotoma ageunet naka Akiro Nukajokak, naanyounio koMakedonia, amamei ekanisa loemorikikina keoŋ kotoma akirot naka aikor ka aijaun, dimarai yes bonik," 
Philippians4:16 naarai koSesalonika da ipotu kijukakis eoŋ irwan atipet ka nakiareit kanuka eipudika. 
Philippians4:17 Mere naarai amoot ainakinet, konye amoot araito nuiyatanakinos otiaikus." 
Philippians4:18 Konye ajai kiboro kere, alitoro da; etekoro, kadau aijaun lukijukunete kama ka Epapurodito, aures naeuru maa, asubanit naecamunitai naitoiokit Edeke." 
Philippians4:19 Ekadeke da itekori luipudasi kere kwape ejaar akebar kotoma aibuses toma Kristo Yesu. 
Philippians4:20 Kojai aibuses mama ejai Edeke Papawok ikar ka ikar. Amen. 
Philippians4:21 Kiyogaete ŋinikalaunan kere kotoma Kristo Yesu. Kiyogaete yes iinacan luejaas keoŋ," 
Philippians4:22 Kiyogaete yes lukalaunak kere, aitelekarit ŋul lukokal loka Kaisar." 
Philippians4:23 Asianut naka Ejakait Yesu Kristo kojai kimoyonokus. 
Colossians1:1 Paul ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kanuka akot naka Edeke, ka Timoteo onacewok," 
Colossians1:2 Mama ejaas lukalaunak ka iinacan luiyuunito lukotoma Kristo luejaas Kolosai: Asianut ka ainapakin kojaas mama ijaas nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok. 
Colossians1:3 Kimalaenenei Edeke Papa loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo apaarasia kere nakilipanakinia yes," 
Colossians1:4 naarai kipou keirasi nuka aiyuunikus kotoma Kristo Yesu, ka aminakus mama ejaas lukalaunak kere," 
Colossians1:5 naejai kanuka amun naiŋadakinio toma akuj kanukus. Ipotu kiirasi ŋin kolo toma akirot naka abeit naka Akiro Nukajokak," 
Colossians1:6 nuadolokis yes; ido kwape eraiata araito, iyatanakinos da kotoma akwapin kere, kwape kwaŋin kotomakus da, ameun kapaaran naipupioto, kojenut da asianut naka Edeke kabeit," 
Colossians1:7 kwape isisiaata kama ka Epapurasi ebulesit aupawok lominat. Erai ŋesi ekejaanakinan lomunot loka Kristo kanukosi," 
Colossians1:8 lokitejenik da sio akusimin kotoma Omoyo. 
Colossians1:9 Kanuka ŋun sio da, ameun kapaaran nakipupunio, mam kinyeinenei ailipanakin yes kaiŋaiŋa ebe, kilelebikin ajenun nuekoto Edeke, kacoa kere, ka acoit naka emoyo," 
Colossians1:10 kolosenenete kwape luibusakinito Ejakait aisiyalamikin ŋes kakiro kere, koraete araito kotoma kaŋiniswam kere naejok, kiyatanakinos da ajenun Edeke." 
Colossians1:11 Kitogogoŋoi kapedor kere, kwape ejaar agogoŋ naka aibusesuke, kiton atitiŋikinit kere, ka aikany da nepepe kaiyalama," 
Colossians1:12 kimalaenenete Papa lokitubusikinit oni aimor kairumet naka lukalaunak kotoma aica. 
Colossians1:13 Abu ŋesi kolaku oni alemar kapolou naka amuton, kisibwot alomar ajakanut naka Okokuke lominat." 
Colossians1:14 Kija kalakunio kotomakeŋ, ŋes aisionio naka adiakanareta." 
Colossians1:15 Erai ŋesi aput naka Edeke lomam etakani, ekiyai loka isuban kere;" 
Colossians1:16 naarai kotomakeŋ ŋes kesubere iboro kere, luejaas toma akuj, ka luejaas toma akwap, luetakanete ka lumam etakanete, arai iicoloŋo lukajakanuto, arai ijaka, arai ikayaitok, arai lukapolou, kesubio iboro kere kotomakeŋ ido kanukeŋ." 
Colossians1:17 Egeikinit ŋesi iboro kere, icasito da iboro kere nepepe kotomakeŋ." 
Colossians1:18 Erai ŋesi da akou naka akuan, ŋes ekanisa; erai ŋesi ageunet, ekiyai kotoma okatwak, tetere eraun ŋesi elopet losodit kotoma kere." 
Colossians1:19 Naarai kotomakeŋ kitojokit aitekoro naka Edeke aiboienen," 
Colossians1:20 kotomakeŋ da aitupuc iboro kere mamakeŋ, arai luejaas akwap, arai da luejaas akuj, kisinapik kanuka aokot nuka emusalabake." 
Colossians1:21 Ka yes da lukolo igelara, lukasurup da kaomisiokus, kaswamisio nueroko, konye kwana abu ŋesi kitupuc yes" 
Colossians1:22 kotoma akekuan naka etuŋanan, kanuka aketwanare, tetere kitodiari yes lukalaunak, luemamei akemer ka luemamei aitoronet da kakonyeneke," 
Colossians1:23 arai bo isalenenete kotoma aiyuun, iketakina apetetaitikus, icasito komam iriaŋiriaŋas, ainyein amun naka Akiro Nukajokak nuipotu kopuput, nuaponi kolimonokin ŋinisubat kere yenejai kwap kakuj, nuabu karaunor eoŋ, Paul, ekejaanakinanikec." 
Colossians1:24 Kwana eyalamikin arieboka kanukus, etodoli da nuikadidio nuka aiticanio naka Kristo toma akuanaka kanuka akuanake, ŋes ekanisa," 
Colossians1:25 lokaraunor eoŋ ekekejaanakinan kwape ejaar aijokokinet naka Edeke nakainakinitai kanukus, aitodolikin akirot naka Edeke," 
Colossians1:26 aiyeiyea nakibwaitai ameun kikar ka aturio da, konye kwana ikujokinitai mama ejaas lukalaunakake." 
Colossians1:27 Abu Edeke kokoto kes aitejenikin Imo abar kwape ejaar naka aibuses naka aiyeiyea kaŋin, naerai Kristo kotomakus, amun naka aibuses." 
Colossians1:28 Kilimonokini ŋes, kekwenya ŋinituŋanan, kisisianakini da ŋinituŋanan kacoa kere, tetere kitodiari ŋinituŋanan epol kotoma Kristo." 
Colossians1:29 Kanuka ŋun ŋes etaaritor aut kwape ejaar akegogoŋ naiswamai kotomakaŋ kapedor. 
Colossians2:1 Naarai akoto yes ajenun aut naetia nen naauta kanukus, kanuka ŋul da luejaas Laodikia, ka ŋul kere lumam eanyunito akakonyen toma akuan;" 
Colossians2:2 tetere italakario ikecetauon, inicakina kotoma amin, koanyut abar kere naka acoit naitogogoŋitoi, kojenut cut aiyeiyea naka Edeke, ŋes Kristo," 
Colossians2:3 loibwaitai kotomakeŋ iboro kere luketiai loepol luka acoa ka ajenun da. 
Colossians2:4 Enera ŋun kinyek idiotuŋanan aitapaar yes kakiro nuka aijodijod. 
Colossians2:5 Naarai karaida amamei eoŋ kotoma akuan, konye ajai kayes kotoma omoyo, eyalama da aanyun ekusipone loeteni ka aicasit naka aiyuunikus kotoma Kristo." 
Colossians2:6 Aso kwape ijauniata Kristo Yesu Ejakait, kolosenenete kwaŋin kotomakeŋ;" 
Colossians2:7 kicasito aliasiokus, kodukokina kotomakeŋ, ido kitogogoŋitete kotoma aiyuun, kwape kisisianakinere, kilapara kaimal." 
Colossians2:8 Kocoito kinyek idiotuŋanan aŋatar yes kanuka aminacoa ka aiŋal naatai, kwape ejaatar iponesio luka ituŋa, kwape ejaatar nugeet nuka akwapin, kwabo mere kwape ejaar Kristo," 
Colossians2:9 Naarai kotomakeŋ iboie aitekoro kere naka Eidekeone kakuan," 
Colossians2:10 yes da itekoro kotomakeŋ, loerai akou naka ayait kere ka apolou da." 
Colossians2:11 Kotomakeŋ da kikepitai yes kakepio namam iswamatai kakanin, ilacata akuan naka etuŋanan kotoma akepio naka Kristo;" 
Colossians2:12 kinukio nepepe kaŋes kaibatis, kaŋin da aponi kitajarun nepepe kaŋes, kanuka aiyuun aswam naka Edeke lokitajaruni ŋes kokatwak," 
Colossians2:13 Yes da lukitwakito kotoma aibucanareta, ka amamus akepio naka awatekus, abu Edeke koinak yes aijar nepepe kaŋes, kedau ŋesi aisioni oni aibucanaretawok kere," 
Colossians2:14 kedau aimwatar aitutuket naewadikatai toma okisila nakitusurupi oni; abu kolema awai, kibubuk omusalaba." 
Colossians2:15 Kolaca ŋesi ikayaitok ka lukapolou kitodia kes katitiŋ, kipiko kes komusalaba." 
Colossians2:16 Aso kinyek idiotuŋanan atubokin yes kakiro nuka inyamat, arai numatan, arai bo kakiro nuka epucit, karaida ailamun naka elap, karaida nuka apaaran nakasabato." 
Colossians2:17 Eraas nu etoribe loka nuepote; konye akuan ŋes naka Kristo. 
Colossians2:18 Kinyek idio ademar ainakinetekus, yenekoto aitisilikin, ka aima imalaikan, kitogogoŋooro kaitapoeta, iturokina atai kanuka aomisioke nuka akuan," 
Colossians2:19 kwabo mam iketakina Akou, lokotomakeŋ akuan kere isigalikinio ka ainicakinio kanuka ailenyeta ka amoori, iyatanakin keiyas loka Edeke." 
Colossians2:20 Arai ipotu kotwaka nepepe ka Kristo ainyein nugeet nuka akwapin, kanukinyo inonokikinitotor ikisila bala iroko ijarete kotoma akwapin," 
Colossians2:21 ebe, “Sirikitiŋ, Sirikiir, Sirikitiro”," 
Colossians2:22 (ŋul kere eoliorete toma aitwasamao) atupar aicorakineta ka aisisianakin naka ituŋa? 
Colossians2:23 Akiro ŋun kere ejai aput naka acoa kotoma aima naepwakunete ituŋa bonik, ka aitisilikin, ka aitican akuan; emamei ŋun ajokis nepetai da aitikokinia aiŋobel naka akuan." 
Colossians3:1 Aso arai kitajarunitai nepepe ka Kristo, komoenenete nuejaas kuju, neejai Kristo, iboie kakan nakoteten naka Edeke." 
Colossians3:2 Koomoomoete nuejaas kuju, kwabo mere nuejaas akwap." 
Colossians3:3 Naarai ipotu kotwaka, ibwaitai da akusiijar nepepe ka Kristo, toma Edeke." 
Colossians3:4 Naetakanunia Kristo, ŋes aijarawok, kosodete yesi da itakanunete nepepe kaŋes kotoma aibuses." 
Colossians3:5 Aso kitwataniasi akusitutubeta nuejaas akwap; adoteu, asilianut, ainekit, eimiel loerono, ka airaŋaanut, ŋes aima aputosia." 
Colossians3:6 Kanuka ŋun ŋes ebunokinia anyunyura naka Edeke odwe luiulaka. 
Colossians3:7 Ipotu yesi da kolosenenete kolo kaŋun, naijariata kotomakec." 
Colossians3:8 Konye yes da kwana kolemasi ŋun kere awai; anyunyura, adedeŋ, aronis, ainyanakin, einer nukileic kaitukekus." 
Colossians3:9 Siriŋalaŋalas, naarai ipotu kolacasi etuŋanan lokolo nepepe kaswamisioke," 
Colossians3:10 konapa da etuŋanan lokitetet loisiteteununio kiton ajenun kwape ejaar aput naka ŋol lokesubi ŋes," 
Colossians3:11 Emamei kanen Eyonanit, karaida Eyudayat, akepio ka amamus akepio, imoit, Esukusit, ibulesit, karaida yenijakakai, konye Kristo ŋes kere, ejai da kotoma kere," 
Colossians3:12 Aso konapenenete etau loka aitim, asianut, aitasono, aiyapepera, atitiŋikin, kwape luseuna luka Edeke, lukalaunak ka luminan da;" 
Colossians3:13 koŋirionokinos, kisionionoros, arai ejai ituŋanan kere aŋurian kayenice, ido kwape kisionio yes Ejakait, yes da kisioniete kwape kwaŋin." 
Colossians3:14 Ido aitelekarit ŋun kere konapa amin, naerai elomorut loka adolior." 
Colossians3:15 Kodiekenenei ainapakin naka Kristo kotoma otauonokus, nakinyarakinio da toma akuan adiopet, kimalaenenete da." 
Colossians3:16 Kiboienenei akirot naka Kristo kabarara kotomakus, kacoa kere: kisisianakinete ido kikwenyanaros kisabulin, ka ikososio, ka nupwakan nuka emoyo; iyeonokinete Edeke kasianut kotoma otauonokus." 
Colossians3:17 Ido nuiswamaenenete kere kakirot arai kaswam, kiswamaenenete kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu, kimalaenenete Edeke Papa kotomakeŋ." 
Colossians3:18 Yes aŋor, kononokikis ikusikiliok, kwape ibusakinitor kotoma Ejakait," 
Colossians3:19 Yes ikiliok, kominas akusiŋor, siridedeŋanakinete kes." 
Colossians3:20 Yes idwe, korimasi ikusikauriak kotoma akiro kere, naarai ŋin itojokit Ejakait." 
Colossians3:21 Yes lukapapa, sirikitunyunyuranakis ikusidwe, kinyeis ajuruŋuŋ." 
Colossians3:22 Yes ibulesin, korimasi ikusijaka luka akuan kotoma akiro kere; mere kaijaanakin nakokuju kwape luitoiokito ituŋa, dimarai kaipioror nakotau, koyoŋito Ejakait," 
Colossians3:23 Yeniswamaete kere, kiswamaenenete kaijar kere, bala iswamanakinete Ejakait kwabo mere ituŋa," 
Colossians3:24 Kojenete ebe kiinakini Ejakait eropit loka airumet; ijaanakinete Ejakait Kristo. 
Colossians3:25 Naarai yeniswamai erono, etacakinio bobo kwape ejaar akeronis, ido emamei atiakit ituŋa." 
Colossians4:1 Yes ijaka, kokorakis ikusibulesin nukadolit ka aitiirian, kojenete ebe ejai yes da Ejakait toma akuj." 
Colossians4:2 Kicebokinito kotoma ailip, kokwenyenenete kotomake kaimal." 
Colossians4:3 Kilipanakinete sio da, ebe koŋaik Edeke sio ekek kanuka akirot, einer aiyeiyea naka Kristo, nakaenitere eoŋ kanukeŋ;" 
Colossians4:4 tetere etodiari kwape kebusakinitor einer," 
Colossians4:5 Kolosenenete kacoa mama ejaas ŋul lukokiŋa, koyuununete apak." 
Colossians4:6 Kinerenenasi apaarasia kere kasianut, kokonyite abalaŋ, tetere ijenete kwape ibusakinitor aboŋonokin ŋinituŋanan," 
Colossians4:7 Kitejenikini yes Tukiko nukadoikis kere; erai ŋesi onace lominat ka ekejaanakinan lomunot, ido ebulesit aupakosi kotoma Ejakait." 
Colossians4:8 Ejuk ŋes mamakus kanuka akirot kana, tetere ijenunete nukidoikis sio, ido kitalaka ŋesi ikusitauon," 
Colossians4:9 nepepe ka Onesimo, onace lomunot ka lominat da, lokobukus. Kitejenikinete kesi yes akiro kere nukane." 
Colossians4:10 Kiyogai yes Arisitariko, ekijoreoritono aupaka, ka Marako ecen loka Baranaba, (Ioaponi kicorakin yes kanukeŋ; arai ebuni mamakus, kisukunyikis ŋes)," 
Colossians4:11 ka Yesu loenyaritai Yusito, Eraas lu lukotoma luekepitai, kes bonik ikeswamak lukaupaka kanuka ajakanut naka Edeke, luapotu ketalakasi eoŋ noi." 
Colossians4:12 Kiyogai yes Epapurasi, loerai lokobukus, ebulesit loka Kristo Yesu, euta apaarasia kere kanukus kotoma ailipike, tetere ibwoenenete kopolok, kitogogoŋito da kere nuekot Edeke." 
Colossians4:13 Naarai etejenaara kanukeŋ ebe itaaritoi ŋesi noi kanukus, kanuka luko Laodikia da, kanuka luko Kierapoli da." 
Colossians4:14 Kiyogai yes Luka emurwon lominat, ka Dema da." 
Colossians4:15 Kiyogaete iinacan luejaas Laodikia, Numpa da ka ekanisa loejai togoke." 
Colossians4:16 Ido naidauniata yesi asoman ebalua lo, kosiomata da kotoma okanisa loka Laodikia; kosiomata yesi da loebuni koLaodikia." 
Colossians4:17 Kolimokis da Arikipo ebe, “Kocoite aijaanakin naibu kodum kotoma Ejakait, tetere itodoli.”" 
Colossians4:18 Eoŋ Paul ewadikai ayogan na kakakan elopet. Kiitununete akaenio. Asianut kojai mama ijaas. 
1Thessalonians1:1 Paul ka Siluano ka Timoteo, mama ejai ekanisa loka Isesalonikan kotoma Edeke Papa ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo: Asianut kojai mama ijaas ka ainapakin," 
1Thessalonians1:2 Kimalaenenei Edeke kanukus kere apaarasia kere, kilimununei yes kotoma ailipikosi," 
1Thessalonians1:3 komam kinyeinenei aiitunun kakonyen nuka Edeke Papawok aswamukus naka aiyuun, ka aitaaritoi naka amin, ka atitiŋikin da naka amuno naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo," 
1Thessalonians1:4 Naarai iinacan luemina Edeke, kijeni aseuniokus;" 
1Thessalonians1:5 naarai Akosikiro Nukajokak mam apotu kodolokis yes kotoma akirot bon, dimarai kotoma apedor, ido kotoma Omoyo Lokalaunan, ido kaitogogoŋio naepol, kwape ijeniata epone lokitodiaror tomakus kanukus." 
1Thessalonians1:6 Ido ipotu koputosi sio ka Ejakait, naarai ijaut akirot kotoma aiticanio naepol, kaiyalama naka Emoyo Lokalaunan;" 
1Thessalonians1:7 kosodete araun aanyunet mama ejaas luiyuunito kere kotoma Makedonia ka Akaia da," 
1Thessalonians1:8 Naarai anyoun kamakus epup akirot naka Edeke, mere kotoma Makedonia ka Akaia bon, dimarai isiarakina akusiiyuun kotoma Edeke ŋiniibois kere, emamei bobo sio eipud einer akirot kere." 
1Thessalonians1:9 Naarai alimosi kesi ikulepek akirokosi kwape kiilomunia mamakus, ido kwape ibelokinotor mama ejai Edeke, kinyeis aputosia, tetere ijaanakinete Edeke lokajaran lokabeit," 
1Thessalonians1:10 ka aidareun Okokuke abunore kokuju, lokitajaruni ŋesi kokatwak, ŋes Yesu lokiyuuni oni kotoma anyunyura naebunit." 
1Thessalonians2:1 Naarai ijenete yesi iinacan, ebe akosilomun mamakus mam kerai atai;" 
1Thessalonians2:2 konye karaida kiiticanitai ka aiswamakinio da nukepali koPilipi, kwape ijeniata, kipou katitiŋikisi kotoma Edekewok, alimonokin yes Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke kauta naepol." 
1Thessalonians2:3 Naarai alimonokinikosi mam erai naka aiŋal, karaida naka asilianut, karaida kotoma aimod," 
1Thessalonians2:4 konye kwape kicamakinia Edeke isio araut lukimunoi kotoma Akiro Nukajokak, kwape kwaŋin kinerar, mere aitalakar ituŋa, dimarai aitalakar Edeke loiteteni itauonokosi," 
1Thessalonians2:5 Naarai mam kijaa kakiro nuisupete apakio kere, kwape ijeniata, karaida nuerapete airaŋaanut, erai Edeke ekajenan;" 
1Thessalonians2:6 mam kipou kamootos aibuses kama kituŋa, karaida kamakus, karaida kama kice, nakipedoria alaŋirikinit yes, kwape ikiyakia luka Kristo." 
1Thessalonians2:7 Konye kipou keyapeperas kokidiŋikus, kwape akasaan naitani ikedwe alopet." 
1Thessalonians2:8 Kwaŋin kipodori yes, ketojokata akorakin yes mere Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke bon, konye akosiijar da, naarai iraas iminanakosi noi." 
1Thessalonians2:9 Naarai, iinacan, iitunito yesi akosiitaaritoi ka ailolony; nakiswamaenena akuare ka apaaran da, kenyeis alaŋirikin ituŋanan kere kayesi, kalimonokinete yes Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke." 
1Thessalonians2:10 Iraas yesi ikajenak, ka Edeke da, kwape kijaar kamakus luiyuunito kalaunit, ka adolit, komamei aitoronet;" 
1Thessalonians2:11 kwape ijeniata yesi ebe, kwape icoria papa ikedwe, kipou kecorata ŋinidiopet kayesi, kesinyikokito, ka aitejenun da," 
1Thessalonians2:12 tetere ilosenenete kwape luibusakinito Edeke, lokinyarit yes alomar toma ajakanutuke ka aibuses da." 
1Thessalonians2:13 Kanuka ŋun da kimalaenenei Edeke tiritir, naarai naijauniata akirot naka Edeke naipupunete kamakosi, ipotu kocamut, mere kwape akirot naka ituŋa, konye kwape eraar abeit akirot naka Edeke, naiswamai da kotomakus kaluiyuunito," 
1Thessalonians2:14 Naarai, iinacan, ipotu koputosi ikanisan luka Edeke Iukotoma Kristo Yesu, Iuejaas Yudaya; naarai apotu ikusituŋa kiticanata yes da, kwape eticaniata Iyudayan lukec;" 
1Thessalonians2:15 luapotu koarata Ejakait Yesu ka inabin da, ido kireŋeto sio, kwabo mam kes isiyalamikinito Edeke, isuruposi kituŋa kere," 
1Thessalonians2:16 kirebokinito da sio alimonokin Imo tetere itajario, kosodete aitodolikin adiakanaretakec apaarasia kere. Konye ekokoikin kes cut anyunyura naka Edeke." 
1Thessalonians2:17 Konye iinacan, kipou isio katiakasi kayes apak naedit, kakonyen, kwabo mere kotauon, kipou kadunyakis noi noi aanyun akusikonyen kaimue naepol;" 
1Thessalonians2:18 naarai kipou kakotosi aponare mamakus, eoŋ Paul, irwan nasodit ka nakiareit da, konye kitikok Satan sio." 
1Thessalonians2:19 Naarai inyo bo amunokosi, arai aiyalama, arai aboko naka aolobob kakonyen nuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu kotoma abunoreke? Mere yes?" 
1Thessalonians2:20 Naarai iraas yesi akosiibuses ka aiyalama da. 
1Thessalonians3:1 Kanuka ŋun namam bobo kipedoria atitiŋikin, kipou ketojokata ainyeinio bon ko Asene," 
1Thessalonians3:2 kejukas Timoteo onacekosi ido ekejaanakinan loka Edeke toma Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo, tetere iticasi yes ka uitalakar da kotoma aiyuunikus," 
1Thessalonians3:3 kinyek ituŋanan kere airiaŋiriaŋa kotoma aiticanio kana. Naarai ijenete yesi ebe kitebeitai ŋin. 
1Thessalonians3:4 Naarai nakijaar kayes, kipou kekwenyasi yes ebe kidumuni aiticanio; kwape kedounio da, ido kwape ijeniata." 
1Thessalonians3:5 Kanuka ŋun namam bobo apedoria atitiŋikin, abu kejuk kasodi ajenun aiyuunikus, kinyek ekacodan acodun yes, aitaaritoikosi da koraun natitai." 
1Thessalonians3:6 Konye kwana naadolunio Timoteo mamakosi ebuni kamakus, abu koinu sio akiro nukajokak nuka aiyuunikus ka aminakus, ebe da kiitununete yesi sio ejok apaarasia kere, kimuito aanyun sio, kwape sio da yes,—" 
1Thessalonians3:7 kanuka ŋun, iinacan, kitalakaritai kanukus kotoma aridakiniokos kere ka aiticanio, kanuka aiyuunikus," 
1Thessalonians3:8 naarai kwana kijari arai ibwoete yesi icasito kotoma Ejakait. 
1Thessalonians3:9 Naarai aimal anyoin kipedori atacakin Edeke kanukus, kanuka aiyalama kere nakiyalamar kanukus kakonyen nuka Edekewok," 
1Thessalonians3:10 kidunyakinit ailip akuare ka apaaran da ebe kaanyut akusikonyen, ka aitemonokin nuiŋoŋara kotoma aiyuunikus?" 
1Thessalonians3:11 Konye Edeke elopet Papawok ka Ejakaitiwok Yesu kiteten ekosirot aponare mamakus; 
1Thessalonians3:12 Ejakait da koinak yes aiyatanakin ka aidilakin aminanar bonik, ka ituŋa kere, kwape sio da kiminar yes," 
1Thessalonians3:13 tetere kiticat ikusitauon koraas Iuemamei aitoronet kotoma alaunit kakonyen nuka Edeke Papawok, naebunio Ejakaitiwok Yesu nepepe kalukalaunakake kere." 
1Thessalonians4:1 Nuesalito, iinacan, kiŋaiŋait yes ka aicor da kotoma Ejakait Yesu, kwape kijauniata kamakosi kwape ibusakinitor yes alosenen ka aisiyalamikinit Edeke, kwape ilosenenoto, kiyatanakinos bobo kwaŋin," 
1Thessalonians4:2 Naarai ijenete kwape ejaatar aicorakineta nukipou kainakis yes kanuka Ejakait Yesu," 
1Thessalonians4:3 Naarai naekoto Edeke ŋes nata, aitalauniokus: kinacata adoteu;" 
1Thessalonians4:4 kojenu ŋinituŋanan kayesi ajaut kakeberu kotoma alaunite ka ayoŋit," 
1Thessalonians4:5 mere kotoma ainekit naka eimiel kwape ikapirin Iumam ejenete Edeke; 
1Thessalonians4:6 kinyek ediotuŋanan aibucar karaida airod onaceke kotoma akirot, naarai erai Ejakait ekenyaŋan kotoma kaŋun kere, kwape kipou kekwenyariata yes ka aitejenun da noi." 
1Thessalonians4:7 Naarai mam Edeke kinyarakinit oni asilianut, dimarai toma alaunit," 
1Thessalonians4:8 Aso yeneŋeri, mam eŋeri etuŋanan dimarai Edeke, lokiinakini yes Ekemoyo Lokalaunan." 
1Thessalonians4:9 Konye nuka amin iinacan mam ipudasi eoŋ aiwadikakin yes, naarai kisisianakinit Edeke yes aminanara;" 
1Thessalonians4:10 naarai iswamanakinete akirot ŋin iinacan kere luejaas Makedonia kere, Konye, iinacan, keŋaiŋait yes kiyatanakinos adepar nen," 
1Thessalonians4:11 koŋaŋato aiyapaara, kiswamaenenete nukus bonik, kitaaritos da kakusikanin, kwape kipou kecorakiniata yes," 
1Thessalonians4:12 tetere ilosenenete koponesio luejok kama kalukokina komam ilwaritos. 
1Thessalonians4:13 Konye iinacan, mam kikoto yes aolit nuka ŋul kaluejotoete, tetere mam itururwete kwape ice luemamei amun." 
1Thessalonians4:14 Naarai arai kiyuunit ebe abu Yesu kotwana, kojaru da, kwape kwaŋin kanuka Yesu eyauni Edeke nepepe kaŋes ŋul luejotoete." 
1Thessalonians4:15 Naarai kilimokini yes na kakirot naka Ejakait, ebe onilukijari lukipaikinit kiton abunore naka Ejakait, mam kigeikini lueiotoete," 
1Thessalonians4:16 Naarai edokuni Ejakait elopet abunore kotoma akuj kaiworo, keporoto loka emalaika lokapolon, ka arupepe naka Edeke. Ŋul da luketwakete kotoma Kristo, kes eliŋete ajarun;" 
1Thessalonians4:17 kosodi konyet oni lukijari, lukipaikinit, kiwuruporio nepepe kakes toma odoun, airiamun ka Ejakait toma apak; kwaŋin kijaenena ka Ejakait apaarasia kere." 
1Thessalonians4:18 Aso kitalakanaros bonik kakiro kaŋun. 
1Thessalonians5:1 Konye iinacan, mam ipudasi eoŋ aiwadikakin yes nuka apakio ka ikar." 
1Thessalonians5:2 Naarai ijenete yesi jokan ebe ebuni apaaran naka Ejakait kwape ekokolan kuare. 
1Thessalonians5:3 Naineratar ebe, “Ejai ainapakin ka aiyamakina,” eŋesakin do kes amudiar kwape eŋesakinor ariebo aberu naidouni, kwa bo mam ekuete nepepec da." 
1Thessalonians5:4 Konye iinacan, mam ijaas amuton, apaaran ŋin aturiaikin yes kwape ekokolan." 
1Thessalonians5:5 Naarai iraas yesi kere odwe luka aica, ka odwe luka apaaran; mam oni kirai luka akuar karaida luka amuton." 
1Thessalonians5:6 Aso do kenyeisi ajotoor kwape ka ice, konye kakwenyenenete, kenyeis amer," 
1Thessalonians5:7 Naarai luejotoete, ejotoete kuare, luemerasi da emerasi kuare," 
1Thessalonians5:8 Konye do oni kirai luka apaaran, kenyeis amer, kanapa yenikatorob yenika aiyuun ka amin, akopira da korai amun naka aitajario." 
1Thessalonians5:9 Naarai mam Edeke kibwaikinit oni kanuka anyunyura, dimarai adumun aitajario kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo," 
1Thessalonians5:10 loabu kotwanik oni tetere kijari nepepe kaŋes, arai kikwenyi, arai bo kijotoi," 
1Thessalonians5:11 Aso kitalakanaros bonik, kodukonoros ŋinituŋanan kayenice, kwape iswamaata da." 
1Thessalonians5:12 Konye iinacan, kiŋaiŋait yes ajenun ŋul Iuitaaritos kotomakus, lukiyaito yes kotoma Ejakait, ka lukicorete da," 
1Thessalonians5:13 koyoŋito kes noi kamin kanuka aswamukec, Kojaas kainapakina kotomakus," 
1Thessalonians5:14 Konye iinacan, kiŋaiŋait yes, kicorata luitotolikino, kiticasete luipirisiaros itauon, kisigalikis luekalanyaka, kotitiŋikis ituŋa kere," 
1Thessalonians5:15 Koanyutu ebe emamei yenetacakini aronis kanuka aronis, konye komootos apaarasia kere aikonanakin lucekus ejok, ka ituŋa da kere." 
1Thessalonians5:16 Kiyalamasi apaarasia kere," 
1Thessalonians5:17 kilipenenete tiritir," 
1Thessalonians5:18 kimalaenenete kotoma ŋinikirot kere; naarai ŋin ŋes naekoto Edeke kamakus kotoma Kristo Yesu. 
1Thessalonians5:19 Siritudeŋete Emoyo," 
1Thessalonians5:20 sirimenete aidwar," 
1Thessalonians5:21 konye kitemoto akiro kere; kikamutu cut nuejok," 
1Thessalonians5:22 kinacata ŋolipone kere loerono," 
1Thessalonians5:23 Edeke da elopet loka ainapakin kitalau yes cut, kidaritete cut imoyonokus, ka aijarakus, ka awatekus da, komamei aitoronet kiton naebunio Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo." 
1Thessalonians5:24 Lokinyarit yes erai lomunot, ido ebuni aswam." 
1Thessalonians5:25 Iinacan, kilipanakinai sio." 
1Thessalonians5:26 Kiyogaete iinacan kere kainu nakalaunan. 
1Thessalonians5:27 Kesiyapoete kalimite Ejakait ebe kosiomakinai ebalua lo iinacan kere. 
1Thessalonians5:28 Asianut naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kojai kayes. 
2Thessalonians1:1 Paul, ka Siluano, ka Timoteo, Mama ejai ekanisa loka Isesalonikan lokotoma Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo;" 
2Thessalonians1:2 Asianut kojai mama ijaas ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papa ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo. 
2Thessalonians1:3 Iinacan, kiburao sio aimalaenen Edeke apaarasia kere kanukus, kwape kibusakinitor, naarai iyata noi akusiiyuun, idila da akusiminanar ŋinituŋanan kayesi kere mama kayenice." 
2Thessalonians1:4 Kiton sio da kiwolobobot kanukus kotoma okanisan luka Edeke kanuka atitiŋikinikus, ka aiyuun kotoma areokus kere, ka aiticanio naiŋirikinito." 
2Thessalonians1:5 Ŋes aanyunet cut naka etube loedolit loka Edeke, kosodete kitubusikin yes ajakanut naka Edeke, nakiticanere yes kanuke." 
2Thessalonians1:6 Naarai edolit kakonyen nuka Edeke atacakin aiticanio lukiticanete yes," 
2Thessalonians1:7 yes da luiticanio kisiyeŋunio nepepe kasio, kotoma apukorio naka Ejakait Yesu naebunio kotoma akuj nepepe ka imalaikan luka akepedor, kotoma akim naesarani," 
2Thessalonians1:8 inyaŋi kama kaŋul lumam ejenete Edeke, ka ŋul da lumam erimarito Akiro Nukajokak nuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu." 
2Thessalonians1:9 Egelitikec ŋes amudiario naka ikar kere, enyounete kakonyen nuka Ejakait, ka aibuses naka agogoŋuke da," 
2Thessalonians1:10 naebunio ŋesi kapaaran kaŋin, tetere itopoloorio kotoma kalukalaunakake, ka aumokinio da kotoma kaluiyuunito kere, naarai iyuunitos yesi akosiitejenun." 
2Thessalonians1:11 Tape da kilipanakini yes apaarasia kere, tetere kitubusik yes Ewokodeke kanyariteke, kitodolik da kapedor ŋiniwomisioit kere nakajokis, ka aswam da naka aiyuun," 
2Thessalonians1:12 tetere itopoloorio ekiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu kotomakus, yes da kotomakeŋ, kwape ejaar asianut naka Edekewok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo." 
2Thessalonians2:1 Konye iinacan, kiŋaiŋait yes, kakiro nuka abunore naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, ka atukonokiniwok nepepe kaŋes," 
2Thessalonians2:2 kinyeis aisunyit airiaŋiriaŋa kotoma aomisiokus, karaida aiyaloŋoŋ, karaida komoyo, karaida kakirot, karaida kobalua loebuni kamakosi, ebe adolu apaaran naka Ejakait," 
2Thessalonians2:3 Kinyek idiotuŋanan aitapaar yes kopone kere; naarai mam apaaran ŋin ebuni, dimarai isiauni atiakatiakaun ajaun, epukorio da etuŋanan ŋol lokepali, okoku loka amudiar," 
2Thessalonians2:4 loirebirebi, ido loitopoloor bon aitelekarit ibore kere yenenyaritai edeke, arai yenemaio; kosodi iboikin oyekalu loka Edeke, kitodiara ebe ŋes Edeke." 
2Thessalonians2:5 Mam kereka iitunito ebe nakijaar kayes abu kalimok yes ŋun? 
2Thessalonians2:6 Ido ijenete yenitikokinit kwana, tetere epukorio ŋes kapakike." 
2Thessalonians2:7 Naarai ageu aiyeiyea naka epali aswam; konye loitikokinit kwana iswamai aitodol naelemarere ŋol awai. 
2Thessalonians2:8 Kosodi konyet epukorio lokepali, eari Ejakait Yesu ŋes keiyeŋane loka aitukuke, ka amudiar da kotoma atakanun naka abunoreke." 
2Thessalonians2:9 Abunore naka ŋol lokepali naiswamai Satan ejaun kapedor kere, kaanyuneta ka nukaumokin da nukeŋalak," 
2Thessalonians2:10 ka aitapaar kere namam adolit mama ejaas ŋul lueoliorito, naarai mam apotu kocamut amin abeit, kosodete aitajario." 
2Thessalonians2:11 Kanuka ŋun ijukakini kes Edeke aswam naka apaar, tetere iyunete nuka aiŋal," 
2Thessalonians2:12 tetere etubokinio kere lumam iyuunito abeit, konye luisiyalamikinito amamus adolit," 
2Thessalonians2:13 Konye kiburao sio aimalaenen Edeke apaarasia kere kanukus, iinacan luemina Ejakait, naarai abu Edeke koseik yes ameun kageunet aitajario, kanuka aitalaunio naka Emoyo, ka aiyuun da abeit." 
2Thessalonians2:14 Abu konyarak yes ŋin kanuka Akosikiro Nukajokak, kanuka adumun aibuses naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo." 
2Thessalonians2:15 Aso do iinacan, kobwaata kicasito, kikamut iponesio lukisisianakinitai, arai kotoma akirot, arai kotoma obaluakosi," 
2Thessalonians2:16 Konye Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo elopet, ka Edeke Papawok, lokimina oni, loabu koinak da aitalakar naka ikar kere, ka amun naejok kotoma asianut," 
2Thessalonians2:17 kitalaka ikusitauon, kiticat da kotoma kaŋiniswam ka ŋinikirot da naejok." 
2Thessalonians3:1 Nuesalito, iinacan, kilipanakinai sio, tetere ekeri akirot naka Ejakait, koinakinai aibuses, kwape kotomakus," 
2Thessalonians3:2 isio da kayuunos kama ka ituŋa luemamei acoa, ikaronok; naarai ejaas ice lumam iyuunito." 
2Thessalonians3:3 Konye erai Ejakait lomunot; lokiticasi yes, kidari da kama ka lokaronon." 
2Thessalonians3:4 Konye kija kamun kotoma Ejakait kakirokus, ebe iswamaete, ido ipote aswam nukicorakini." 
2Thessalonians3:5 Konye kiteten Ejakait ikusitauon toma amin naka Edeke, ka atitiŋikin da naka Kristo." 
2Thessalonians3:6 Konye iinacan, kicorakini yes kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu Kristo, kinacata onac kere loitotolikino komam elosenenei kwape ejaar epone loipotu kodumut kamakosi." 
2Thessalonians3:7 Naarai ijenete yesi kwape ibusakinitor yes aputorit sio; naarai mam sio kitotolikino kamakus," 
2Thessalonians3:8 mam kipou kanyama inyamat luka idiotuŋanan atitai, konye kaitaaritoi ka ailolony, kipou keswamata akuare ka apaaran da, tetere mam kilaŋirikini idiotuŋanan kayesi." 
2Thessalonians3:9 Mere naarai emamei sio apolou, konye kiinakin yes aanyunet tetere kiputorete sio." 
2Thessalonians3:10 Naarai nakijaar nepepe kayes, kipou kecorakis yes nata ebe: Arai mam ituŋanan ekoto aswam, kinyek ainyam da." 
2Thessalonians3:11 Naarai kipupi ebe ejaas ice luelosete itotolikino kotomakus, mam iswamaete konye iramaitos nuka luce." 
2Thessalonians3:12 Kicorakini kotoma Ejakait Yesu Kristo, kikwenyari da luikote nen ebe, kiswamata kaiyapaara, konyamata ikecenyamat kikulepek." 
2Thessalonians3:13 Konye yes, iinacan, sirikitapalikinos aswam nuejok." 
2Thessalonians3:14 Konye arai etuŋanan kere mam erimari akirotokosi kotoma obalua kalo, koŋicutu ŋol, kinyeis aimorikikin kaŋes, tetere irumete ileic." 
2Thessalonians3:15 Sirikimarata ŋes kwape lokasurup, konye kikwenyanarete kwape onac." 
2Thessalonians3:16 Ejakait da elopet loka ainapakin, koinak yes ainapakin apaarasia kere toma akiro kere. Kojai Ejakait kayes kere." 
2Thessalonians3:17 Eoŋ Paul ewadikai ayogan na kakakan elopet. Ŋes aanyunet kotoma ŋolibalua; ewadikai kwaŋin. 
2Thessalonians3:18 Asianut naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kojai kayes kere. 
1Timothy1:1 Paul ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kwape ejaar aicorakinet naka Edeke Eketajaraniwok, ka naka Yesu Kristo amunowok," 
1Timothy1:2 Mama ejai Timoteo, ikakoku obe kotoma aiyuun: Asianut, ka aitim, ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papa, ka Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok," 
1Timothy1:3 Kwape abu kecorakinia jo asalakin Epeso, naalosio Makedonia, tetere icorakini icetuŋa kinyeis aisisianakin nuegelara," 
1Timothy1:4 karaida aomoom nuka awaragasia nutai, ka iitabon luka aur lumam edaunos, lueyaunete ipegeta itia aijokokinet naka Edeke naejai toma aiyuun;" 
1Timothy1:5 kwabo awasia naka aicorakinet ŋes amin naelomuni kotau loelai, ka aomisio nuejok ka aiyuun namam esoswai." 
1Timothy1:6 Akudosi icetuŋa apaasi alomar toma akiro nutai," 
1Timothy1:7 ekotosi araun ikesisianakinak luka ikisila, komam ejenete nuinerasi karaida akiro nuitogogonito." 
1Timothy1:8 Konye kijeni ebe ejokuka ikisila, arai kitwasam ituŋanan kes kwape ejaatar ikisila," 
1Timothy1:9 kojen na ebe mam ibwaikinitai ikisila kanuka yenedolit, dimarai kanuka lukepali ka luetumaaka, kanuka lumam eyoŋito Edeke ka ikadiakanarak, luemamei alaunit, ka luemunaara, luearete lukapapakee, ka luearete nukatotokec, ka luearete iruna," 
1Timothy1:10 ludotea, iketepak ikiliok, luijoreete ituŋa, ikeŋalak, luiyapoete nuka aiŋal, ka ŋin kere da yenirebirebi aisisianakin naka aijar," 
1Timothy1:11 kwape ejaatar Akiro Nukajokak nukaibuses nuka Edeke loituritoi nuketitiŋitai. 
1Timothy1:12 Emalai ŋol loketogogoni, ŋes Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok naarai abu kaomite eoŋ araun lomunot, kadakak aijaanakin," 
1Timothy1:13 karaida abu kainyanakini ŋes kolo, kareite, ka amoromor da; konye aponi ketimi naarai abu keswama kamamus aijen kotoma amamus aiyuun," 
1Timothy1:14 konye kiyatakin noi asianut naka Ejakaitiwok nepepe kaiyuun ka amin naejai toma Kristo Yesu. 
1Timothy1:15 Namunot akirot na, ido naibusakinit ituŋa kere acamun ebe, Abu Kristo Yesu kobu toma akwap aitajar ikadiakanarak, Eoŋ losodit kakesi." 
1Timothy1:16 Konye kanuka na ŋes ketimere, tetere itodiari Yesu Kristo kotoma eoŋ losodit aketitiŋikin kere, araun aanyunet mama kaŋul luepote aiyuun ŋes kiton aijar naka ikar kere." 
1Timothy1:17 Mama ejai Ekabaka loka ikar, ekabuton, lomam etakani, Edeke ediopet bon, kojai aiturit ka aibuses ikar ka ikar. Amen." 
1Timothy1:18 Ketitiŋi jo, Timoteo okokuka, aicorakinet na kwape ejaatar akiro nuka inabin nukinerakinito jo kolo, tetere ijio kotoma kaŋun ejie lokajokan," 
1Timothy1:19 kikam aiyuun ka aomisio nuejok. Apotu ice koremosi ŋun, kobila ataker naka aiyuunikec." 
1Timothy1:20 Kotomakec ejai Kumenaio ka Alegesanda, luabu kejaik Satan, tetere isisiaete ainyein ainyanakin." 
1Timothy2:1 Aso nasodit kakere, ecori ebe kiswamaenenete aiŋaiŋa, ka ailip, ka aipur, ka aimal da, kanuka ituŋa kere," 
1Timothy2:2 kanuka ikabakan ka ŋul kere luejaas apolou, tetere kijaun kaijar naitenera, naiyamakina, toma ayoŋit Edeke, ka aiyaparit kere." 
1Timothy2:3 Ejok ŋun, ido ecamunitai kakonyen nuka Edeke Eketajaraniwok," 
1Timothy2:4 loekot ituŋa kere aitaiario, adolokin da ajenun abeit." 
1Timothy2:5 Naarai ejai Edeke ediopet, ejai da ekadiekan ediopet loka Edeke ka ituŋa, ŋes etuŋanan Kristo Yesu," 
1Timothy2:6 loabu koluŋakin araun alakunet kanuka kere, aitejenunet naejaun kapakioke." 
1Timothy2:7 Kebwaikinitai eoŋ araun ekalimonokinan, ekiyakia da kanuka ŋun, (enera abeit, mam eŋalai) ekesisianakinan loka Imo kotoma aiyuun ka abeit," 
1Timothy2:8 Ŋes akotor ikiliok ailipenen kotoma ŋiniibois, koriorito akanin nukalaunak komamei anyunyura karaida aŋolopa;" 
1Timothy2:9 kwape kwaŋin da aŋor kisirete anapito nuibusak, kaitasono ka acoit, mere kaicip itim, karaida kesabu, karaida ilulun, karaida igoen luketiai," 
1Timothy2:10 dimarai kaswamisio nuejok, kwape ibusakinitor aŋor nuelimorete ebe eyoŋito Edeke." 
1Timothy2:11 Kisisia aberu kaiyamakina kanonokikinit kere," 
1Timothy2:12 Konye mam esiikinit aberu aisisianakin, karaida ayait ekiliokit, dimarai aiyamaara." 
1Timothy2:13 Naarai kisiau Adam asubio, kosodi konyet Keba." 
1Timothy2:14 Bobo da mam Adam kijodijoditoi, konye Keba ejodijoditoi, kojaikin aibucar." 
1Timothy2:15 Konye itajario aberu kanuka auruun idwe, arai esalete kesi toma aiyuun, ka amin, ka alaunit nepepe kacoit." 
1Timothy3:1 Namunot akirot na ebe: Arai eŋaŋat etuŋanan araun ekaanyanaran, imiela aswam naejok." 
1Timothy3:2 Aso ibusakinit ekaanyanaran araun loemamei aitoronet, ekiliokit loka aberu adiopet, loitikokina, loecoit, loiyapaara, loisukunyikini ipejok, loejeni aisisianakin," 
1Timothy3:3 lomam emer, lomam ibuŋai; dimarai lokaiyapepera, lomam eŋolopana, lomam emin apesan;" 
1Timothy3:4 loeyait ejok lukokaleke, loitononokikini ikedwe kaiyapaara kere;" 
1Timothy3:5 naarai arai mam etuŋanan ejeŋi ayait lukokaleke, ikwaikini ai imukei ekanisa loka Edeke?" 
1Timothy3:6 Mere ekeyuunan lokitetet, kinyek adakunun, ka aibirokin otube loka Satan." 
1Timothy3:7 Konye ibusakinit lukokiŋa aitejen nukajokak kamakeŋ, kinyek aibirokin amorosit, kotoma atacit da naka Satan." 
1Timothy3:8 Ikejaanakinak kwape kwaŋin kiyapaara, mere luideideok, mere luemasete ajon nuipu, mere luiŋobelete apesan," 
1Timothy3:9 luejai aiyeiyea naka aiyuun kotoma aomisio nuelaete. 
1Timothy3:10 Konye kisiautu ber ŋul da aitemio, kosodete konyet aijaanakin, arai eraas luemamei aitoronet," 
1Timothy3:11 Aŋor da kwape kwaŋin kiyapaara, mere akasabak, nuitikokina, numunon kakiro kere." 
1Timothy3:12 Koraut ikejaanakinak ikiliok luka adiopeberu, lueyaito ejok ikecedwe ka lukokaliakec." 
1Timothy3:13 Naarai luejaanakis ejok, edumakina adoket naejok, ka atitiŋ naepol kotoma aiyuun naejai toma Kristo Yesu." 
1Timothy3:14 Kewadikakini jo nu amuno abunore mamakon atipet," 
1Timothy3:15 konye arai etumori, tetere ijenuni kwape ibusakinitor ituŋa ajaut kotoma otogo loka Edeke, loerai ekanisa loka Edeke lokajaran, epir ka eigaŋet loka abeit." 
1Timothy3:16 Ido komamei abuonokin, epol noi aiyeiyea naka ayoŋit Edeke: Abu kitodiar kotoma akuan, Kitojokai kotoma Omoyo, Apotu imalaikan koanyut ŋes, Aponi kolimonokinai kotoma atekerin, Aponi kiyuunai kotoma akwapin, Kodakarai kuju toma aibuses." 
1Timothy4:1 Konye inera Emoyo kaitebeikin ebe kotoma apakio nuepote etiakatiakaunos ice ainyein aiyuun, epupete imoyon luepaarete, ka aisisianakin naka ajokin," 
1Timothy4:2 kanuka aisoswanut naka ikeŋalak, luieweio aomisiokec kemacar loesarani," 
1Timothy4:3 imikete aimany, italeete lunyaman, luabu Edeke kosub tetere ijaunete luiyuunito ka luejenete noi abeit kaimal," 
1Timothy4:4 Naarai ejok ŋinibore kere yenikesubi Edeke, emamei da ibore yeneŋerio, arai ecamunio kaimal;" 
1Timothy4:5 naarai italaunitai kanuka akirot naka Edeke ka ailip da. 
1Timothy4:6 Arai isiituni iinacan akiro ŋun iraun ekejaanakinan loejok loka Kristo Yesu, kitanete jo akiro nuka aiyuun, ka aisisianakin naejok naibu kotup," 
1Timothy4:7 Kinac awaragasia numam eraas nuka edini, nukabaŋaanut. Konye kitwasama bon kotoma ayoŋit Edeke;" 
1Timothy4:8 naarai aitwasam akuan ejai ameda naedit, konye ayoŋit Edeke ejai ameda kakiro kere, naarai ejai aisumunet naka aijar naka tinenikwana, ka aijar da naebuni." 
1Timothy4:9 Namunot akirot na, ido naibusakinit ituŋa kere acamun." 
1Timothy4:10 Naarai kitaaritoi kiwuta da kanuka ŋun, naarai kimunokina Edeke lokajaran, loerai Eketaiaran loka ituŋa kere, aitelekarit loka luiyuunito." 
1Timothy4:11 Kicorak akiro ŋun, kisisianak da kes," 
1Timothy4:12 Kinyek idiotuŋanan aimen atumunikon, konye korau ijo aanyunet mama ejaas luiyuunito kotoma oiner, ka ejautene, kotoma amin, kotoma aiyuun, ka asegara da." 
1Timothy4:13 Aitodol neabunio, kodunyak asoman, ka aicor, ka aisisianakin da." 
1Timothy4:14 Sirikijal ainakinet naejai kotomakon, nakiinakinitai kanuka adwaranut ka aidokokinio akanin nuka imakio." 
1Timothy4:15 Koomitenenei ŋun, kojaenena kotomakec, tetere etakani akonijokiar otuŋa kere." 
1Timothy4:16 Kocoite bon ka aisisianakinikon da; kosalak toma ŋun, naarai arai kiswama kwaŋin itajara bon, ka ŋul da lukipupete joo" 
1Timothy5:1 Sirikitoron ekimat, konye kicorenenei kwape papakon; ikatumunak kwape iinacan," 
1Timothy5:2 amakio kwape nukatoto, akatumunak da kwape ainacan, kotoma asegara kere," 
1Timothy5:3 Koyoŋit apuserun nueraas apuserun cut. 
1Timothy5:4 Konye apuserut arai ejaas kidwe arai itatai, kisiaunete aisisia ayoŋit Edeke kokaliakec, ka atacakin ikauriakakec; naarai ecamunitai ŋin kakonyen nuka Edeke." 
1Timothy5:5 Konye ŋin naerai apuserut cut, kinyeinai bon, emunokina Edeke, kosalak aiŋaiŋa ka ailipenen akuare ka apaaran." 
1Timothy5:6 Konye ŋin naeminakinito aboliasio, etwanit karaida kejari." 
1Timothy5:7 Kicorak kes ŋun da, tetere eraas nuemamei aitoronet." 
1Timothy5:8 Konye ituŋanan kere arai mam idari lukeŋ, aitelekarit lukokaleke ilopet, aŋer ŋesi aiyuun, erono da adepar yenimam iyuunit." 
1Timothy5:9 Siriwadikao apuserut namam edolit ikar akaisakanykape, nakerai aberu naka ekiliokit ediopet;" 
1Timothy5:10 itejenunitai kanuka aswamisio nuejok; arai esait idwe, arai abu kisukuny ipejok, kilot akeje nuka lukalaunak, iŋarakinit luiticanio, arai da edunyit atupit ŋiniswam kere naejok," 
1Timothy5:11 Konye koŋer aiwadik apuserun nukatumunak; naarai naiyatakiniata aipaliikin Kristo, ekotosi adukokin;" 
1Timothy5:12 egwaunete akiro naarai enyeis aiyuunikec nasodit. 
1Timothy5:13 Bobo da isisiaunete araut nuebwalaka, kirimete otogoi; kwabo mere nuebwalaka bon, konye ibeeleaka ka nuiramaaka da, inerasi numam ibusakinito." 
1Timothy5:14 Aso akoto apuserun nukatumunak adukokin, kouriata idwe, koyaito ikalia, komam einakinete lokasurup apak naemoromoroo." 
1Timothy5:15 Naarai ejaas kwana ace nuapaasi atupar Satan. 
1Timothy5:16 Arai ejaas aberu naiyuunit apuserun, kiŋarak ŋin kes, kinyeinai alaŋirikin ekanisa, tetere iŋarakini nueraas apuserun cut," 
1Timothy5:17 Kimarakinai imakio lueyaito ejok araut luibusakinito ayoŋio irwan aarei, ido aitelekarit luitaaritos kotoma akirot ka aisisianakin da;" 
1Timothy5:18 naarai ebala naiwadikatai ebe, “Sirikien aituk naka emoŋ loipudapudai aicom akima.” Ebe da, “Ekeswaman ibusakinit ekeropit.”" 
1Timothy5:19 Sirikicam yeniwosai ekimat, dimarai kama ka ikajenak iarei arai iuni," 
1Timothy5:20 Luediakanarete kitoron kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere, tetere luce da eyoŋete," 
1Timothy5:21 Kecorakinit kakonyen nuka Edeke ka Kristo Yesu, ka imalaikan luseuna koricit ŋun komam isunyit aitub, sirikiswama akirot kere kotiakite ituŋa." 
1Timothy5:22 Sirisunyit aidokokin ituŋanan kere akanin, karaida aimor adiakanareta nuka ituŋa ice; kidarakina kosegara." 
1Timothy5:23 Sirimasenenei bobo akipi bon, konye komat ediobino kanuka akoikikon, naarai idekanakin da irwan ipu." 
1Timothy5:24 Ideleleete adiakanareta nuka icetuŋa, kiŋarenikinete kiton atubokinio; konye nuka ice ideleleunete kokau," 
1Timothy5:25 Kwape kwaŋin da ideleleete aswamisio nuejok; karaida ŋun numam ideleleete, mam epedorete aibwaio." 
1Timothy6:1 Kere lueraas ibulesin kwap kajookot, koomitos ijakakec araut luibusakinito ayoŋio kere, kinyek ekiror loka Edeke ka aisisianakin da ainyanakinio." 
1Timothy6:2 Ido luejaas ijaka luiyuunito, sirikemwaŋata kes, naarai eraas iinacan, konye gwai kiyatakis aijaanakin kes, naarai luedumunete ajokis naka aswamukec eraas luiyuunito, luminan da. Kisisianakin ŋun, kicor da." 
1Timothy6:3 Arai isisianakini ituŋanan nuegelara komam enupit akiro nuejarete nuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, ka aisisianakin da naetupit ayoŋit Edeke," 
1Timothy6:4 edakunun, komam ejeŋi akirot, konye edek ipegeta, ka ijiisio luka akiro, mama eponiata ekokote, aŋolopa, ainyanakin, aomoom nueroko," 
1Timothy6:5 iceleta luka ituŋa luamunaar acoakec, lualemar abeit, lueomito ebe ayoŋit Edeke ŋes adumun ameda," 
1Timothy6:6 Konye ayoŋit Edeke nepepe kalakara ŋes ameda naepol. 
1Timothy6:7 Naarai mam kiyaunit ibore toma akwap, ido mam kipedori ayaŋaar ibore;" 
1Timothy6:8 konye kijaa ka inyamat ka inapen, kalakaros kaŋul." 
1Timothy6:9 Konye luekotos abar ebirokinos acodunio ka atacit, ka eimiel loepol loemamei acoa ka loimadiŋi da, aitulum ituŋa toma aolior ka amudiar." 
1Timothy6:10 Naarai amin apesan ŋes aliasit naka aronisio kere; ejaas ituŋa luiŋaŋatos ŋun, kesodete kitapaaros anyoun kotoma aiyuun, kicumakinos cut kican luipu." 
1Timothy6:11 Konye jo, wu etuŋanan loka Edeke, koker ŋun, kotupenenei adolit, ayoŋit Edeke, aiyuun, amin, atitiŋikin, ka aiyapepera da." 
1Timothy6:12 Koji ejie lokajokan loka aiyuun; kitiŋ aijar naka ikar kere, nakinyarakinitai, nailimorit alimoret naejok kakonyen nuka ikajenak luipu." 
1Timothy6:13 Kecori jo kakonyen nuka Edeke loeinakini kere aijar, ka Kristo Yesu loetejenuni alimoret naejok mama ejai Pontio Pilato," 
1Timothy6:14 kidarenenei aicorakinet komamei akemer, komamei da aitoronet, kiton atakanun naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo;" 
1Timothy6:15 naitodikini kapakioke Elopet apedor ediopet bon loituritoi, Ekabaka loka ikabakan, Ejakait da loka ijaka," 
1Timothy6:16 lobon ejai amamus atwanare, loiboie toma aica namam edolokinio, lomam idiotuŋanan eanyunit, emamei da yenepedori aanyun. Kojai aibuses ka apedor naka ikar kere mamakeŋ, Amen." 
1Timothy6:17 Kicorenenei lukabarak luka ikar kalu kinyeis aitopoloor, karaida amunokin abar namam erai naduc, konye komunokinos Edeke, lokiinakini oni iboro kere kabarara tetere kisiyalamanakin kaŋun," 
1Timothy6:18 Kiswamata nuejok, kobarata kotoma aswamisio nuejok, koraas ikakorak, ikamorak da," 
1Timothy6:19 kidiasete bonik apetetait naejok kanuka apaarasia nuepote, tetere itiŋete aijar naerai aijar obe." 
1Timothy6:20 Wu jo Timoteo, kidar nakititinitai. Kinacite akiro nutai numam eraas nuka edini, ka airebokin akiro nuenyaritai aijen kotoma aiŋal," 
1Timothy6:21 ejaas icetuŋa lualimosi ŋun, kosodete apaar kotoma aiyuun. Kojai asianut kayes." 
2Timothy1:1 Paul ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kanuka akot naka Edeke, kwape ejaar aisumunet naka aijar naejai toma Kristo Yesu," 
2Timothy1:2 Mama ejai Timoteo ikakoku yeniminat: Asianut, aitim, ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papa ka Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok." 
2Timothy1:3 Emalai eoŋ Edeke loejaanakini ameun ka lukapapaaka kaomisio nuelaete, nakeitununio jo komam apali kotoma ailipika, akuare ka apaaran," 
2Timothy1:4 Emuit aanyun jo, naeitunio akonikiyo, tetere ilelebun aiyalamakaŋ." 
2Timothy1:5 Nakesiitunere aiyuun namam esoswai naejai kotomakon, naageuni aiboi kotoma tataakon Lois, ka totokon Eunike; ido etogogoŋit ebe ejai kotomakon da," 
2Timothy1:6 Kanuka ŋun ŋes kesiitunio jo aitunyonokin ainakinet naka Edeke naejai kotomakon, kanuka aidokokinio akaninika," 
2Timothy1:7 Naarai mam Edeke abu koinak oni emoyo loka akurian, dimarai loka apedor ka loka amin, ka loka aiyapaarit da." 
2Timothy1:8 Aso kinyeis ileic airum jo kanuka aitejenun naka Ejakaitiwok, karaida kanukaŋ, eenatake, konye kiticaneneno nepepe kAkiro Nukajokak, kwape ejaar apedor naka Edeke," 
2Timothy1:9 loabu kitajar oni, konyarau da anyarit nakalaunan, mere kwape ejaatar aswamisiowok, dimarai kwape ejaar alosikiniteke elopet ka asianut, naabu koinak oni kotoma Kristo Yesu eriŋa apakio nuka ikar," 
2Timothy1:10 konye kwana etakanun asianut ŋin kanuka aitodikinio naka Eketajaraniwok Kristo Yesu, loabu kitapalau atwanare, kitacau da aijar ka amamus aibos kanuka Akiro Nukajokak," 
2Timothy1:11 nukadakakinere eoŋ araun ekalimonokinan, ka ekiyakia, ka ekesisianakinan da." 
2Timothy1:12 Kanuka ŋun da ŋes ariebar kwaŋin. Konye mam kerumito ileic, naarai ajeni loabu keyuu, ido etogogoŋi ebe epedori ŋesi aidarenen nuketitiŋitai kiton apaaran ŋin." 
2Timothy1:13 Kojau kaanyunet naka akiro nuka aijar nuibu kopup kamakaŋ, kotoma aiyuun ka amin naejai toma Kristo Yesu," 
2Timothy1:14 Kidarenenei ibore yenejok yenikititiŋitai kanuka Emoyo Lokalaunan loiboie kotomawok. 
2Timothy1:15 Ijeni ijo na ebe, kere luejaas toma Asia apotu kebonokis ipuran, kotomakec ejai Pugelo, ka Keremogene," 
2Timothy1:16 Kitim Ejakait eka! loka Onesiporo, naarai abu kesiyenu eoŋ irwan ipu, kwabo mam apotu ileic kiruma ŋes kanuka erikotoka." 
2Timothy1:17 Konye nakejaar Rome, kinyikok amoot eoŋ, kadum da—" 
2Timothy1:18 koinak Ejakait ŋes adumun aitimio kama ka Ejakait kapaaran kaŋin-ido kaijaanakin kere naabu kijaanak ko Epeso, ijeni ijo noi jokan." 
2Timothy2:1 Aso do jo, ikakoku, kogogoŋor kotoma asianut naejai toma Kristo Yesu," 
2Timothy2:2 Nuibu kopup da kamakaŋ kotoma ikajenak luipu, kititiŋ ŋun ituŋa lumunon, ido Iuibusakinito aisisianakin ituŋa ice." 
2Timothy2:3 Kiticaneneno nepepe keoŋ kwape eserikalet lokajokan loka Kristo Yesu," 
2Timothy2:4 Mam eserikalet ekacakin kotoma aitaaritoi naka aijar kana kapak naka ejie, tetere itojoki lokiwadikai ŋes araun eserikalet," 
2Timothy2:5 Arai da eboloboloi ituŋanan, mam einakinio aboko, arai mam eboloboloi kwape icorakinitere." 
2Timothy2:6 Ibusakinit ekakorion loitaaritoi ageun ayaŋaar araito. 
2Timothy2:7 Koomoom nuener, naarai kiinakin Ejakait ajenun kotoma akiro kere." 
2Timothy2:8 Kiitu Yesu Kristo, loetajarunio kotoma okatwak, loka aur naka Daudi, kwape ejaatar Akakiro Nukajokak," 
2Timothy2:9 nueticanitor kiton aenio kwape loiswamai aronis. Konye akirot naka Edeke mam eenio. 
2Timothy2:10 Kanuka ŋun ŋes atitiŋikinio kere, kanuka luseuna, tetere kes da edumunete aitajario naejai toma Kristo Yesu nepepe kaibuses naka ikar kere." 
2Timothy2:11 Namunot akirot ŋin: naarai arai kipou katwaka nepepe kaŋes, kijari da nepepe kaŋes;" 
2Timothy2:12 arai kititiŋikini, kirumi da nepepe kaŋes; arai kiŋeri ŋes, ŋes da kiŋeri oni;" 
2Timothy2:13 arai mam kirai lumunon, esali ŋesi erai Iomunot, naarai mam epedori ŋesi aŋerokin bon." 
2Timothy2:14 Kisiitu kes ŋun, kicor kakonyen nuka Edeke, kinyeis ejie kakiro, numam iŋarakinete, nuitotolikinete luepupete." 
2Timothy2:15 Kinyikok aitoduun bon korai lokitojokit Edeke, ekeswaman lomam ipuda kirumata ileic, loitubi kotenan akirot naka abeit." 
2Timothy2:16 Kinac akiro nutai, numam eraas nuka edini, naarai itedeparos kotoma amamus ayoŋit Edeke," 
2Timothy2:17 enyami kes akecekirot kwape eŋoti. Kotoma kaŋul ejai Kumenaio ka Pileto," 
2Timothy2:18 luapaasi kotoma aiyuun, kinerasi ebe adau ajarun ajaun, itotolikinete da aiyuun naka ituŋa ice." 
2Timothy2:19 Konye icasit apetetait naegogoŋ naka Edeke, ejai aipucet na ebe, “Ejeŋi Ejakait lueraas luke,” ido ebe, “Konyou kotoma amamus adolit, ŋin kere yenelimori ekiror loka Ejakait.”" 
2Timothy2:20 Konye kotoma togo lokapolon mam ejaunos iboro luka esabu ka luka epuesa bonik, dimarai luka akito ka luka elupe, ice da luka aibuses, ice da lumam aibuses." 
2Timothy2:21 Aso arai itesegaar ituŋanan kaŋun, eraun ibore yenika aibuses, yenitalaunitai, yenibusakinit ejakait aitwasam, yenitemonokinitai ŋiniswam naejok." 
2Timothy2:22 Aso koker eimiel loka atumun, konye kotup adolit, aiyuun, amin, ka ainapakin da, nepepe kaŋul luiwoneete Ejakait kotoma otauon luelaete." 
2Timothy2:23 Konye koŋer ipegeta luka abaŋaanut, ka lumam aisisianakinio; ijeni ebe euriete ijiisio." 
2Timothy2:24 Ido mam ibusakinit ebulesit loka Ejakait ejie, dimarai araun loiyapepera mama ejaas kere, ekesisianakinan, loetitiŋikin," 
2Timothy2:25 loicori kaiyapepera luirebirebete. Motoko einakini Edeke kes aitoronikin kodoloto ajenun cut abeit," 
2Timothy2:26 ido ikwaaros anyoun kotoma atacit naka Satan, kedau ŋesi aikamun kes aswam nuekoto Edeke." 
2Timothy3:1 Konye kojen na ebe kapaarasia nukawasia epote apakio nuetioko. 
2Timothy3:2 Naarai eraunos ituŋa lueminas bonik, lueminas apesan, Iuituros, luepogaka, ikainyanakinak, luiulakinito ikauriakakec, lumam imalaete, luemamei alaunit," 
2Timothy3:3 lumam eminanara, Iuiketara, ikasabak, lumam itikokinos, ikadedeŋak, lumam eminas ajokis," 
2Timothy3:4 ikabilak ibotei, luemositos, luedakakina, lueminas aitelelio itia amin Edeke," 
2Timothy3:5 ejaas kaput naka ayoŋit Edeke, konye koŋeritos apedorike. Kiboŋok ŋul epur." 
2Timothy3:6 Naarai kotomakec ejaas ŋul luelomanarete otogoi, kijoreoto aŋor nubaŋiok nuelaŋirikito adiakanareta, nuiriarit aiŋobel naka iponesio luipu," 
2Timothy3:7 isisiaete apaarasia kere, komam epedorete cut adolokin ajenun abeit." 
2Timothy3:8 Kwape aponiata Yane ka Yambure kobwoikiniata Musa, kwape kwaŋin ebwoikiniata kwi da abeit, ituŋa luemunaara acoa, luegiritoi kakiro nuka aiyuun." 
2Timothy3:9 Konye mam iyatanakinos noi, naarai ideleleuni akecebaŋaanut kotuŋa kere, kwape kideleleunio abaŋaanut naka ŋul kaluarei." 
2Timothy3:10 Konye jo ibu kotup akaisisianakin, ka ekapone, ka nualosikinit, ka aiyuun, ka aŋirikin, ka amin, ka atitiŋikin," 
2Timothy3:11 bobo da areio, ka aiticanio, akiro nukadoikinete ko Antiokia, ka Ikonio, ka Lusitura, areio naetia nen naekanyakinit; konye abu Ejakait kayu eoŋ kotoma kaŋun kere." 
2Timothy3:12 Ido da ereunio kere luekotos aijar kayoŋit Edeke kotoma Kristo Yesu. 
2Timothy3:13 Konye ituŋa lukaronok ka ikamodak iyatanakinos aroniar, iŋalaete ido kiŋalas da." 
2Timothy3:14 Konye kosal ijo toma akiro nuisisiat, ka aitogogoŋ, ijeni mama ka lukaŋai kisisiaunia," 
2Timothy3:15 ebe da ameun keiditeu ibu kojen nuiwadikatai nukalaunak, nuepedorete aitocoun jo kiton aitajario kanuka aiyuun naejai toma Kristo Yesu." 
2Timothy3:16 Ŋinikirot naiwadikatai naiyeŋakit Edeke ejai ajokis aisisianakinia, aikwenyaria, aitetenia, aituutooria da toma adolit," 
2Timothy3:17 tetere ilosikino etuŋanan loka Edeke, loisilosikinitai kotoma ŋiniswamisioit naejok." 
2Timothy4:1 Kecorak jo jokan kakonyen nuka Edeke, kakonyen da nuka Kristo Yesu loebuni airabakin ikajarak ka ikatwak da, kanuka atakanunike ka akejakanut;" 
2Timothy4:2 kolimonok akirot, kokapakina kapak naejok, ka apak da namam ejok, kiretak, kitoron, kicor, katitiŋikin kere ka aisisianakin." 
2Timothy4:3 Naarai ebuni apak naegirioto ituŋa aisisianakin naka aijar, ejaas kaki nuipiete, etukonokinete bonik ikesisianakinak kwape ejaar aiŋobelekec bonik," 
2Timothy4:4 eekarete kesi ainyein aiirar abeit, epaarete mama ejaas awaragasia nutai." 
2Timothy4:5 Konye jo, kitikokina kakiro kere, kotitiŋikite nueroko, kiswama aswam naka ekalimonokinan loka Akiro Nukajokak, kitodolik akoniijaanakin." 
2Timothy4:6 Naarai kwana kabukokin eoŋ asubanit; adol apak naka akalosit. 
2Timothy4:7 Aji ejie lokajokan, adau abolobol, aricit aiyuun." 
2Timothy4:8 Amear kwana keŋadakinitai aboko naka adolit, nakainakini Ejakait, ekatubon loedolit, kapaaran kaŋin, ido mere eoŋ bon, konye kere da luaminasi atakanunike." 
2Timothy4:9 Kokukunyuun abunore mamakaŋ katipet. 
2Timothy4:10 Naarai kajalaki Dema, emina ikar luka tinenikwana, alot da Sesalonika; alot Keresike Galatia, ka Tito da Dalamatia." 
2Timothy4:11 Luka bon ejai keoŋ. Kodum Marako koyau; naarai ibus ŋes kamakaŋ kanuka aijaanakin. 
2Timothy4:12 Abu kejuka Tukiko Epeso. 
2Timothy4:13 Naibunio ijo, koyaunia elou loabu kenyek kaneejai Karapo ko Teroa, iitabon da, aitelekarit lukimukulen." 
2Timothy4:14 Abu Alegesanda ekatatan aikomon keswamak nueroko nuipu; etacakini Ejakait ŋes kwape ejaatar akeswamisio," 
2Timothy4:15 Kidara ijo da kamakeŋ, naarai abu kirebok noi akirowok." 
2Timothy4:16 Kaiyarika nasodit amamei yenikowaika, konye kajalakis kere. Kinyeis ŋun aimarakinio kes!" 
2Timothy4:17 Konye abu Ejakait kobwo kodiekaŋ, ketogogoŋ da, tetere etodolikini akiro nualimonokini, kopupete da Imo kere, kayuunio da kotoma aituk naka eŋatuny." 
2Timothy4:18 Kayuuni Ejakait eoŋ kotoma kaŋiniswam kere naerono, ketajari da kiton akejakanut nakokuju. Kojai aibuses mamakeŋ ikar ka ikar. Amen." 
2Timothy4:19 Kiyoga Pirisika ka Akuila, ka lukokal da loka Onesiporo." 
2Timothy4:20 Abu Erasito kosalak Korinto; konye abu kenyek Toropimo Mileto edeka," 
2Timothy4:21 Kokukunyuun abunore eriŋa apaarasia nuka aaterot edoluno. Kiyogai Eubulo jo, Pudes da, ka Lino, ka Kulaudia, ka iinacan kere kiyogaete jo." 
2Timothy4:22 Kojai Ejakait kemoyokon, Asianut kojai kayes." 
Titus1:1 Paul, ebulesit loka Edeke, ekiyakia da loka Yesu Kristo aisilosikinia aiyuun naka luseuna luka Edeke ka ajenunikec naka abeit kiton ayoŋit Edeke," 
Titus1:2 kotoma amun naka aijar naka ikar kere, naabu Edeke, lomam iŋalai, kisumun eriŋa apakio nuka ikar," 
Titus1:3 konye kapakike abu kitodia akekirot kotoma alimonokin nakejokokinio kwape ejaar aicorakinet naka Eketajaraniwok Edeke: 
Titus1:4 Mama ejai Tito ikakoku obe kotoma aiyuun nakimorit: Asianut ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papa, ka Kristo Yesu da Eketajaraniwok." 
Titus1:5 Kanuka nu ŋes kenyeinia jo koKurete, tetere iteteni nuideuna, kodakak da imakio kaŋolire kwape kecorakinia jo," 
Titus1:6 arai ejai loemamei aitoronet, ekiliokit loka aberu adiopet, loiyuunito ikedwe, komam iwosatai ebe eraas luka iponesio lutai, ka luetumaaka." 
Titus1:7 Naarai ibusakinit ekaanyanaran araut loemamei aitoronet, kwape ekeŋadan loka Edeke; mere loisiyalamikina bon, mere loenyunyurana, lomam emer, lomam ibuŋai, lomam iŋobelei apesan," 
Titus1:8 konye loisukunyikini ipejok, loemina ajokis, loecoit, loedolit, lokalaunan, loitikokina da;" 
Titus1:9 loericit akirot naka aiyuun kwape ejaar aisisianakin, tetere epedori aicor kotoma aisisianakin naka aijar, bobo da aitoron luirebirebete." 
Titus1:10 Naarai ejaas luetumaaka luipu, luinerasi aamameak, ka luiŋalas da, aitelekarit lueraas luekepitai." 
Titus1:11 Ibusakinit aisililiŋ kes, naarai itotolikinete ituŋa kere lukokalia, isisianakinete numam ibusakinit kes aisisianakin, kanuka ameda nakileic." 
Titus1:12 Abu ediopet kakesi, enabikec kikulepek, kobala ebe, “Eraas Ikureton ikeŋalak apaarasia kere, itiaŋ lueroko, ikeraŋak lueloŋwaka.”" 
Titus1:13 Aitejenunet ŋin erai nakabeit da, Kanuka ŋun kitoron kes kadedeŋ, tetere eŋaleete kotoma aiyuun," 
Titus1:14 kinyeis acoit awaragasia nutai nuka Iyudayan, ka aicorakineta da nuka ituŋa luepaarete ainyein abeit," 
Titus1:15 Elaete iboro kere mama ejaas luelaete. Konye emamei ibore yenelai mama ejaas luemunaara ka lumam iyuunito; konye emunaara do adamakec ka aomisiokec da. 
Titus1:16 Elimorete ebe ejenete Edeke, konye eŋerito ŋes kaswamisiokec; eraas luesacitai, luiulaka, luegiritoi da kaŋiniswam kere naejok." 
Titus2:1 Konye jo, kiner nuibusakinito aisisianakin naka aijar." 
Titus2:2 Koraas imakio luitikokina, luiyapaara, luecoito, lueŋaleete kotoma aiyuun, ka amin, ka atitiŋikin da." 
Titus2:3 Kwape kwaŋin da koraas amakio nukejautene lokayoŋit, mere akasabak, karaida abulesin nuka ajon nuipu; konye nuisisianakinete nuejok," 
Titus2:4 tetere ituutoorete akatumunak araut nueminasi ikiliokokec, ka nueminasi ikecedwe da," 
Titus2:5 koraas nuecoito, nuesegara, nuiswamaete ore, nuejok, nuenonokikinito ikiliokokec, kinyek akirot naka Edeke ainyanakinio." 
Titus2:6 Kwape kwaŋin, kicor ikatumunak acoit." 
Titus2:7 Kakiro kere kitoduun korai aanyunet naka aswamisio nuejok, kotoma aisisianakin kitoduun korai lomam imunaara, loiyapaara," 
Titus2:8 kakiro nueŋaleete lomam itoronio, tetere isurumio ekapegan ileic, komamei ŋes akirot naerono einer asurokinia oni." 
Titus2:9 Kicor ibulesin kononokikis ikecejaka kakiro kere, koraut luitojokete, mere luirebirebete," 
Titus2:10 mere luelemelemaka iboro, konye kitodiasi kamunonut kere naejok, tetere isirete aisisianakin naka Eketajaraniwok Edeke kakiro kere." 
Titus2:11 Naarai atakanu asianut naka Edeke einunit ituŋa kere aitajario," 
Titus2:12 kituutoori oni ebe, kaŋeroto amamus ayoŋit Edeke, ka aiŋobel naka akwapin, kajarata kacoit, ka adolit, ka ayoŋit da Edeke, kotoma okar luka kwana," 
Titus2:13 kedareto noi amun nakarereŋ naka atakan nakaibuses naka Edeke lokapolon ka Eketajaraniwok Yesu Kristo," 
Titus2:14 loabu koinakin bon kanuwok, tetere kilakuni oni kama kepali kere, ka aitalaun kanukeŋ ituŋake obe, luekokakinito aswamisio nuejok." 
Titus2:15 Kiner ŋun, kicor da, kitoron da kapolou kere. Kinyek idiotuŋanan aimen joo." 
Titus3:1 Kisiitu kes anonokikin ikayaitok ka lukapolou da, korimasi, kitemokino kaŋiniswam kere naejok," 
Titus3:2 kinyeis amoromor idiotuŋanan, kinyeis da aŋolopamit, luiyapaara, kitodikis ituŋa kere aiyapepera kere." 
Titus3:3 Naarai kirai kolo oni da lukibaŋaaka, lukiulaka, lukiŋala, ibulesin luka aiŋobel ka nuisiyalamikinete nukiponesio luipu, ketorito kotoma ameŋeranut ka ekokote, lukilaitai, lukilait luce;" 
Titus3:4 konye naketakanunia asianut ka amin naka Eketajaraniwok Edeke," 
Titus3:5 abu kitajar oni, mere kanuka aswamisio nukiswamat kadolit, dimarai kwape ejaar akeitim, kanuka ailotario naka aurio nakiareit ka aisiteteunio naka Emoyo Lokalaunan," 
Titus3:6 nakibukok akwamakin oni kanuka Yesu Kristo Eketajaraniwok," 
Titus3:7 tetere kitojokio araut lukidolit kanuka akesianut, karaut da ikerumak kwape ejaar amun naka aijar naka ikar kere." 
Titus3:8 Namunot akirot ŋin. Akoto jo aitogogoŋ akiro ŋun, tetere luapotu kiyuut Edeke ibwaikinito itauonokec aigaŋ aswamisio nuejok; eraas ŋun nuejok ido nueinunete ituŋa ajokis." 
Titus3:9 Konye kinac ipegeta lukabaŋaanut, ka iitabon luka aur ka aŋolopa ka ijiisio luka ikisila, naarai eraas lumam ajokis ka lutai da." 
Titus3:10 Koŋer ituŋanan yenekot agitara, kidau aikwenyar irwan atipet ka nakiareit," 
Titus3:11 ijeni ebe yenikoni nen erii, adiak da, itetelekara bon," 
Titus3:12 Nakejukakinia jo Aretemo arai Tukiko, kokukunyuun abunore mamakaŋ Nikopoli, naarai alosikinit aiboi nen adaun apaarasia nuka aaterot." 
Titus3:13 Kokukunyikin aitwar ejok Sena ericakisila, ka Apelo; tetere mam etwakiarete ibore." 
Titus3:14 Konye kisisiaut luwok aigaŋ aswamisio nuejok kiton aijaikin luipudasi, tetere mam eraas luemameete araito." 
Titus3:15 Kiyogaete jo kere luejaas keoŋ, Kiyoga ŋul lukiminasi oni kotoma aiyuun. Asianut kojai kayes kere," 
Philemon1:1 Paul eenat loka Kristo Yesu, ka Timoteo onac, Mama ejai Pilemon lominat, ekeswaman da aupakosi," 
Philemon1:2 ka Apia inac, ka Arikipo ekajion aupawok, ka ekanisa da loejai orekon:" 
Philemon1:3 Asianut kojai mama ijaas ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok, ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo da." 
Philemon1:4 Emalai Ekadeke apaarasia kere nakeitununio jo kailipika," 
Philemon1:5 kapup nuka aminakon ka aiyuun da, naejai mama ejai Ejakait Yesu, ka lukalaunak da kere," 
Philemon1:6 Elipi da ebe eidicane loka aiyuunikon iswamai noi kiton ajenun cut ajokis kere naerai nawok kotoma Kristo. 
Philemon1:7 Naarai abu kadum aiyalama naepol ka aitalakario da kanuka aminakon, onace, naarai ibu kisiyeŋu itauon luka lukalaunak." 
Philemon1:8 Kanuka ŋun karaida ajai katitiŋ naepol toma Kristo aicorakin jo naipudai," 
Philemon1:9 konye gwai kanuka amin, keŋaiŋait-eoŋ loekoni nen Paul ekimat, konye kwana eenat da loka Kristo Yesu,—" 
Philemon1:10 keŋaiŋait jo kanuka ikakoku, Onesimo, loaurit kotoma aenioka." 
Philemon1:11 Kolo amamei ŋes ajokis mamakon, konye kwana ejai ajokis mamakon ka mamakaŋ da." 
Philemon1:12 Enyakuni ŋes mamakon, ŋol loerai ekatau." 
Philemon1:13 Akoto ti aitasal ŋes mamakaŋ, tetere kejaanakin eoŋ kanukon kotoma aenioka kanuka Akiro Nukajokak," 
Philemon1:14 konye mam abu kakoto aswam ibore komam jo ijeni, tetere ejaun akonijokis mere kanuka aitiŋaikin, dimarai kanuka akot." 
Philemon1:15 Diat kanuka ŋun ŋes kitiakere kajo adaun apak, tetere ijaunete kaŋes ikar kere," 
Philemon1:16 mere bobo kwape ebulesit, konye adepar ebulesit, onac lominat, aitelekarit mamakaŋ, konye gwai itelekarit ca ma mamakon, toma akuan ido toma Ejakait da." 
Philemon1:17 Aso arai kidica keoŋ, kisukunyik ŋes kwape kisukunyikinia eoŋ." 
Philemon1:18 Arai abu kiswamak jo adioronis arai bo ejai apesen, kitepesen eoŋ ŋun." 
Philemon1:19 Eoŋ Paul ewadikai nu kakakan elopet, atacakini eoŋ-komam alimokini jo ebe ejai jo apesen mamakaŋ, ijo ilopet obe." 
Philemon1:20 Eebo, onac, akoto adumun ajokis kamakon toma Ejakait. Kisiyeŋu ekatau toma Kristo," 
Philemon1:21 Kewadikak jo kajai kamun naka arimanutukon, ajeni da ebe iswamai ijo adepar nuenera eoŋ," 
Philemon1:22 Bobo da kitemokino aisipejo eoŋ, naarai amuno ebe kanuka ailipikus, kainakinia mamakus." 
Philemon1:23 Kiyogai jo Epapuras, ekijoreoritono aupaka toma Kristo Yesu," 
Philemon1:24 Marako da, ka Aristariko, ka Dema, ka Luka, ikeswamak lukaupaka." 
Philemon1:25 Asianut naka Ejakait Yesu Kristo kojai kimoyonokus. 
Hebrews1:1 Abu kolo Edeke kinera kalukapapaawok koponesio luipu luegelegela kotoma onabin; 
Hebrews1:2 konye kapaarasia kanu nukawasia ener kaoni kotoma Okoku, loabu kodakak araun ekeruman loka kere, kanukeŋ da abu kosub akwapisinei." 
Hebrews1:3 Erai ŋesi ailore naka aibuses naka Edeke, erai da einono loka ejauteneke, edakit iboro kere kakirot naka akepedor. Nakedaunia aitesegaar adiakanareta, kiboikin akan nakoteten naka Loejai kuju kakuj, kotoma akuj," 
Hebrews1:4 korau loedeparit noi imalaikan kajokis, kwape erumitor ekiror loedeparit noi lokec kajokis," 
Hebrews1:5 Naarai iŋai bo komalaikan abu Edeke kobala ebe, “Irai ijo Okokuka, lolo kauri jo”? Bobo da ebe, “Araun eoŋ Papake, ŋes da eraun okokuka”?" 
Hebrews1:6 Bobo da, naayaunia ekiyai toma akwapin ebala ebe, “Komaata ŋes imalaikan kere luka Edeke.”" 
Hebrews1:7 Inera nuka imalaikan ebe, “Loesubi ikemalaikan araut imoyon, Ka ikejaanakinakake da aŋajepa nuka akim.”" 
Hebrews1:8 Konye nuka Okoku ebe, “Wu Edeke, ejaenena ekoniicoloŋ ikar ka ikar, Ebela da lokadolit, ŋes ebela loka ajakanutuke." 
Hebrews1:9 Ido komina adolit, kolaite da epali, Tape Edeke, Ekonideke, kinyonyoikini jo akinyet naka ailel Adepar lukaupakon.”" 
Hebrews1:10 Bobo da ebe, “Ijo, wu Ejakait, ameun kageunet, Ibu kopet apetetait naka akwap, Akuj da erai aswam naka akonikanin;" 
Hebrews1:11 Edaunos ŋun, konye jo ibusenenei; Emojoŋgete da kere kwape anapito;" 
Hebrews1:12 Ido inunuki kes kwape eimukoret, Ilocokinio da kwape anapito. Konye ijo ŋopeŋol, Ikonikar da mam enaŋete.”" 
Hebrews1:13 Konye iŋai bo komalaikan abu ŋesi kobala ebe, “Kiboikin akanika nakoteten, Aitodol naebwaikinia lukasurupokon Araut iicoloŋ yenika akejekon”?" 
Hebrews1:14 Mere kereka kes kere imoyon luijaanakinete, luiyakiaritai aijaanakin, kanuka ŋul luepote airum aitajario?" 
Hebrews2:1 Kanuka ŋun ibusakinit oni aiyatakin noi aibwaikin itauon ŋun nukipupu, kenyeis aikaleleorio kamakec." 
Hebrews2:2 Naarai arai icasit akirot nakineras imalaikan, tape eropio kadolit ŋiniibucaret ka ŋiniiulanut," 
Hebrews2:3 kikwaikini ai kikui oni arai kijali aitajario naetia nen? Abu Ejakait kogeu alimokin ŋin, kosodete lukiirarete ŋes apotu kitogogoŋoto mamawok," 
Hebrews2:4 Edeke da abu kitejen nepepe kakes kotoma aanyuneta ka nukaumokin, ka nukapedor nuka iponesio luegelegela, kotoma akorakineta da nuka Emoyo Lokalaunan, kwape ejaar akoteke elopet." 
Hebrews2:5 Naarai mam einakinit Edeke akwapin nueponito nukinera, anonokikin imalaikan." 
Hebrews2:6 Konye ejai aibois naitejenunitor ediopet, kinera ebe, “Inyo bo etuŋanan, tape jo iitunit ŋes? Arai bo okoku loka etuŋanan, tape jo ianyanari ŋes?" 
Hebrews2:7 Ibu kosub ŋes nepetai airianakin ka imalaikan adaun apak naedit, Itanapit ŋes aboko naka aibuses ka ayoŋio, Isurumit ŋes aswamisio nuka akonikanin." 
Hebrews2:8 Itononokikinit iboro kere aibwaikin kwap kakejeneke.” 
Hebrews2:9 Konye kiseseni Yesu loaponi kosubai nepetai airianakin ka imalaikan adaun apak naedit, kanuka aiticanio naka atwanare, aponi kitanapai aboko naka aibuses ka ayoŋio, tetere kanuka asianut naka Edeke, iiri atwanare kanuka ŋinituŋanan." 
Hebrews2:10 Naarai ebusakinit ŋol, loejaas iboro kere kanukeŋ, ido loepote iboro kere kamakeŋ, naeyaunia odwe luipu toma aibuses, aitodolikin ekapeleunan loka aitajariokec kanuka aisiriebio." 
Hebrews2:11 Naarai loitalauni ka luetalaunitai eraas kere luka ediopet. Kanuka ŋun ŋes mam irumiata ŋes ileic anyarit kes iinacan," 
Hebrews2:12 kinera ebe, “Alimokini ikainacan ekonikiror, Keturenenei jo, kokidiŋ katukot.”" 
Hebrews2:13 Bobo da ebe, “Amunoneno eoŋ ŋes.” Ido bobo ebe, “Koany, eoŋ ka idwe lukainak Edeke.”" 
Hebrews2:14 Aso naarai imorikikinete idwe aokot ka awat, abu ŋesi da elopet komor kakes ejautenekec, tetere kanuka atwanareke emudiari ŋol loejai apedor naka atwanare, ŋes Satan." 
Hebrews2:15 Tetere elacakini da ŋul kere lukejaas toma obulesene apaarasia kere nuka aijarakec, kanuka akurian atwanare," 
Hebrews2:16 Naarai abeit mam iŋarakinit imalaikan, dimarai iŋarakinit aur naka Aburaam." 
Hebrews2:17 Ŋes iburaa ŋes aitupusio ikeinacan kotoma kere, tetere eraun esasedoti lopeti lokaitim lomunot kotoma akiro nuejaas neejai Edeke, kanuka ailuc adiakanareta nuka ituŋa." 
Hebrews2:18 Aso naarai abu ŋesi da elopet korieba ecodunio, ŋes epedoria aiŋarakin ŋul luecodunio." 
Hebrews3:1 Aso, iinacan lukalaunak, luimorete anyaraunio nakokuju, koomoomata Yesu, Ekiyakia ido Esasedoti lopeti lokilimonori oni." 
Hebrews3:2 Kerai ŋesi lomunot mama ejai ŋol loaseuni ŋes, kwape Musa da keraar lomunot kotogoke kere." 
Hebrews3:3 Naarai ibusakinit Yesu ainakinio aibuses naepol adepar Musa, kwape edumunia loeduki etogo ayoŋio adepar etogo." 
Hebrews3:4 Naarai ejai ŋolitogo ekadukonike, konye loaduki kere ŋes Edeke." 
Hebrews3:5 Musa da kerai lomunot kotogoke kere kwape ebulesit, kanuka aitejenun nuepote ainerio," 
Hebrews3:6 konye Kristo kerai lomunot kotogoke kwape okoku. Kirai oni etogoke, arai kikamuni kagogoŋ ati tiŋ ka aolobobot naka amun kiton awasia." 
Hebrews3:7 Aso kwape ebalar Emoyo Lokalaunan ebe, “Lolo, arai kiirasi ekeporoto," 
Hebrews3:8 Sirikitininikata ikusitauon, kwape toma aitunyunyurikinio, Kwape kapaaran naka acodunio toma amodiŋ," 
Hebrews3:9 Nakakoduniata eoŋ lukapapaakus, ketemo, Koanyutu da akaswamisio ikar akaisaoŋon." 
Hebrews3:10 Ŋes abu kanyunyurikinia atur ŋin, Kabala ebe, ‘Epaarete apaarasia kere kotauonokec; Komam ejenete ikarotin,’" 
Hebrews3:11 Kwape keyapoikinia kakanyunyura ebe, ‘Mam cut elomunete aibworareteka.’ ”" 
Hebrews3:12 Kocoito, iinacan, kinyek ajaun kotoma idio kayesi etau loerono lomam iyuunit, lokitonyouni kama ejai Edeke lokajaran." 
Hebrews3:13 Konye kicorenenas ŋinipaaran, naeriŋar enyaritai “naka lolo”, kinyek aiŋal naka adiakar aitininik idio kayesi." 
Hebrews3:14 Naarai kirau ikamorak luka Kristo, arai kikamuni kagogoŋ ageunet naka amunowok kiton awasia." 
Hebrews3:15 Kwape eriŋar inerai ebe, “Lolo, arai kiirasi ekeporoto, Sirikitininikata ikusitauon, kwape toma aitunyunyurikinio.”" 
Hebrews3:16 Naarai lukaŋai bo kiirarete, kitunyunyurikisi? Mere kereka ŋul kere luanyounete koMisiri kanuka Musa?" 
Hebrews3:17 Ido lukaŋai bo luabu konyunyurik ikar akaisaoŋon? Mere kereka ŋul luapotu kodiakas, lukibirokinos akecetesin amodiŋ?" 
Hebrews3:18 Ido lukaŋai bo luabu kiyapoik ebe mam cut elomarete aibworareteke, nabarai ŋul lueulakinete?" 
Hebrews3:19 Ido kianyu ebe mam apotu kopedosi alomar kanuka amamus aiyuun. 
Hebrews4:1 Aso, naeriŋar aisumunet naka alomar aibworareteke esalit, kakuriakaros, kinyek idio kayesi atakanun mam edolokinit." 
Hebrews4:2 Naarai oni da kilimonokinitai Akiro Nukajokak kwape kakesi; konye akirot nakiirarete mam abu koinu kes ajokis, naarai mam aponi kimorikikinai kotoma aiyuun nepepe kaŋul luapotu kiirasi." 
Hebrews4:3 Naarai oni lukidau aiyuun, kilomari toma aibworaret ŋin, kwape abalar ebe, “Kwape keyapoikinia kakanyunyura ebe, ‘Mam cut elomunete aibworareteka,’ ” karaida apotu aswamisioke kodaunos ameun kageunet naka akwapin." 
Hebrews4:4 Naarai ejai neinerar nuka apaaran nakikanyetekaarei ebe, “Abu Edeke kibwora kapaaran nakikanyetekaarei, kotoma aswamisioke kere.”" 
Hebrews4:5 Bobo da kotoma kana ebe, “Mam cut elomunete aibworareteka.”" 
Hebrews4:6 Aso naarai esalit ice alomar tomake, ka ŋul da luageunete alimonokinio akiro nukajokak mam elomarete kanuka aiulanut," 
Hebrews4:7 bobo etiaki ŋesi apaaran ace, ebala kama ka Daudi ketubor apak naetia nen, ebe, “Lolo,” kwape abalar sek ebe, “Lolo arai kiirasi ekeporoto, Sirikitininikata ikusitauon.”" 
Hebrews4:8 Naarai arai kisiyenunit Yosua kes, timam kinera nuka apaaran ace akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun," 
Hebrews4:9 Aso esalit aibworaret naka asabato mama ejaas ituŋa luka Edeke; 
Hebrews4:10 naarai yenelomari aibworareteke, eyenu do ŋesi da kotoma aswamisioke, kwape abu Edeke da kiyenunia kotoma nukeŋ," 
Hebrews4:11 Aso kadunyakis alomar aibworaret ŋin, kinyek Idiotuŋanan aibirokin opone ŋol loka aiulanut." 
Hebrews4:12 Naarai erai akirot naka Edeke nakajaran, nakapedor da, ekwana adepar ŋolikileŋ loekwana kowaitin kere, ipelori da kiton aitiak aijar ka emoyo, ailenyeta ka asum, emisiikin da aomisio ka nuelosikinit etau." 
Hebrews4:13 Kwabo emamei isubat yenimam etakani kakonyeneke, konye imujalalas iboro kere, ido ideleleete kakonyen nuka ŋol loejaas akirowok." 
Hebrews4:14 Aso naarai kija ka esasedoti lopeti lokapolon, lokelomari toma akuj, Yesu Okoku loka Edeke, keketakis noi alimoriwok," 
Hebrews4:15 Naarai emamei oni esasedoti lopeti lomam epedori arieba nepepe kaoni akalanyanutuwok, konye lokecodunio kakiro kere ariaka kaoni, komam adiakar." 
Hebrews4:16 Aso kekunyakis katitiŋ mama ejai eicoloŋ loka asianut, tetere kitimio, kadumutu da asianut nakinarakini oni kapakio nuka eipud." 
Hebrews5:1 Naarai ŋolisasedoti lopeti loketiakunio kotuŋa ibwaikinio kanuka ituŋa kakiro nuka Edeke, tetere ijaikini ainakineta ka asuban da kanuka adiakanar," 
Hebrews5:2 Epedori aiyamiyamar lueolito ka luepaarito, naarai ŋes da elopet igogoleori akalanyanut." 
Hebrews5:3 Kanuka ŋun ŋes da iburao ainakin asuban kanuka adiakarike, kwape kanuka ŋun nuka ituŋa," 
Hebrews5:4 Kwabo emamei etuŋanan kere eyaŋaikin bon apolou ŋin, dimarai ŋol loenyarit Edeke, kwape ka Aaron." 
Hebrews5:5 Kwape kwaŋin Kristo da mam abu kitopoloor bon aluor esasedoti lopeti, dimarai ŋol loabu kolimok ŋes ebe, “Irai ijo Okokuka, lolo kauru jo.”" 
Hebrews5:6 Kwape inerar kamace da ebe, “Irai ijo esasedoti kiton ikar kere, Kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek.”" 
Hebrews5:7 Kapaarasia nuka akuanake, abu Yesu kiŋaiŋa kilip da, kaiworo naepol ka akiyo da, mama ejai ŋol loepedori aitajar ŋes katwanare, kopupunoi da kanuka ayoniteke Edeke." 
Hebrews5:8 Karaida kerai Okoku abu kisisia arimanut kanuka ŋun kanuesiriebete; 
Hebrews5:9 kosodi nakedaunia aitodolikinio, korau loeinakini ŋul kere luerimarete ŋes aitajario naka ikar kere," 
Hebrews5:10 loamaikini Edeke esasedoti lopeti kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek. 
Hebrews5:11 Kija kakiro nuipu einer kamakeŋ, ido nuetioko aitejenun, naarai ikimiŋakaros yesi." 
Hebrews5:12 Naarai kapak kana tikibusakinit araut ikesisianakinak, kwabo ipudasi bobo yenikisisianakini yes nusodit nuegeunete nuka akiro nuka Edeke. Ido iluoros luipudasi akile kwabo mere inyamat luenyakao." 
Hebrews5:13 Naarai yenemasi akile mam ejeni akirot naka adolit, naarai erai ikoku." 
Hebrews5:14 Konye inyamat luenyakao eraas luka lukapolok, ŋul luiruutooritai acoakec kanuka aitwasam, tetere etiakete nuejok ka nueroko da." 
Hebrews6:1 Kanuka ŋun kenyeis einer akiro nusodit nuka Kristo, keyatakinos apoloor; kenyeis bobo aipet apetetait naka aitoronikin kanuka aswamisio nuetwakito, ka aiyuun Edeke," 
Hebrews6:2 aisisianakin naka aibatis, ka aidokokinio akanin, ka ajarun naka lukatwak, ka atubokinio da naka ikar kere," 
Hebrews6:3 Kiswamai da kwaŋin arai ekoto Edeke. 
Hebrews6:4 Naarai ŋul luadaut kolo ainwakakinio, kiirata da ainakinet nakakuj, luaraunos ikamorak Emoyo Lokalaunan," 
Hebrews6:5 kiirata da ajokis naka akirot naka Edeke, ka apedor da naka ikar luepote," 
Hebrews6:6 mam epedorete aiteteun bobo aitoronikin arai kibiroros ainyein ŋun, naarai ebubukis bobo Okoku loka Edeke kanukec, esurumata da ileic kaitebeikin." 
Hebrews6:7 Naarai akwap naamat akiru naetepanakini irwan ipu, kosodi kobwaŋ akui nuibusakinito ŋul luekorionokinio, edumuni arereŋ naebuni kama ejai Edeke." 
Hebrews6:8 Konye arai kitolom ikukwa ka isukukur, eneritoi, ido eapie aikenio; esaŋeke aicweio." 
Hebrews6:9 Konye luminan, karaida kinera ŋun kwaŋin, kitogogoŋ kamakus akiro nuejok adepar, ido nueraas nuka aitajario." 
Hebrews6:10 Naarai Edeke mam erai lomam edolit aimurwokin aswamukus, ka amin naipotu kitodiasi mama ejai ekirorike naijaanakiniata lukalaunak, ido kwana iroko ijaanakinete." 
Hebrews6:11 Konye kiŋata noi ŋinituŋanan kayesi aitodiar adunyanut ŋipeŋin kanuka aitodolikin cut amun ŋin kiton osaŋe," 
Hebrews6:12 kinyeis araut luijalijalasi, konye luipusete ŋul luirumete aisumuneta kanuka aiyuun ka atitiŋikin da." 
Hebrews6:13 Naarai naesumunio Edeke Aburaam, naarai amamei loapol aitelekarit ŋes loelimit iyapoi, abu kiyapo kolimite elopet,"
