Hebrews6:14 kobala ebe, “Abeit kotoma arereŋ kesirereŋenenei jo, ka aiyat keyatanakinenei jo.”" 
Hebrews6:15 Kwape kwaŋin kanuka atitiŋikin abu kodum aisumunet ŋin. 
Hebrews6:16 Naarai iyapoete ituŋa kolimito loepol aitelekarit kes, ido kotoma opegetakec kere, edauni aiyapoet aitogogoŋ," 
Hebrews6:17 Aso naakotor Edeke aitodikin cut noi ikerumak luka aisumunet kwape mam ijulakinor akekot, abu kodiek kaiyaposit," 
Hebrews6:18 tetere kanuka akiro aarei numam ijulakinos, numam epedori Edeke aiŋal, kidumuni aitalakario naegogoŋ, oni lukirurukit aikamun amun naibwaikinitai kakonyenewok." 
Hebrews6:19 Kija kaŋin kwape edobo loka aijar, loicasit loegogoŋ, amun naelomari mama ejai naejai toma aigalisit," 
Hebrews6:20 neabu Yesu koloma kwape ekeŋarenon kanuwok, abu koraun esasedoti lopeti ikar kere kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek" 
Hebrews7:1 Naarai Melukisadek ŋol, ekabaka loko Salem, esasedoti loka Edeke Loejai kuju kakuj, loeriamunos ka Aburaam naaboŋunio kaiar ikabakan, abu kilipak ŋes arereŋ;" 
Hebrews7:2 loabu Aburaam kokorak idiopet kotomon koboroke kere. Nasodit, arai ijulakini ekekiror, erai ŋesi ekabaka loka adolit, bobo da ekabaka Ioka Salem, ŋes atemar ebe ekabaka loka ainapakin." 
Hebrews7:3 Emamei ŋes papa, karaida toto, karaida lukapapaake, emamei ageunet naka apaarasiake, karaida esaŋe loka aijarake, konye itupusitoi ka Okoku loka Edeke, esalakinit erai esasedoti apaarasia kere." 
Hebrews7:4 Aso ca koomito etuŋanan ŋol, kwape keraar loepol! Abu Aburaam papaawok koinak ŋes idiopet kotomon kaluŋatuna." 
Hebrews7:5 Ŋul da lukodwe luka Lebi lueinakinio esasedotene ejaas kaicorakinet ayaŋanar idiopet kotomon kotuŋa kwape ejaatar ikisila, kes iinacanakec, karaida ŋul da kelomunete kotoma akuan naka Aburaam." 
Hebrews7:6 Konye ŋol lomam imaritai lukapapaake kamakec, abu kodum idiopet kotomon kama ka Aburaam, kilipak arereŋ loejaas kaisumuneta." 
Hebrews7:7 Konye emamei epeget nepepec da, ebe, ŋipakini lokapolon lodidi arereŋ." 
Hebrews7:8 Kane da edumunete ituŋa luetwakete idiopet kotomon, konye kalaije, ŋol loiteienunio ebe ejari," 
Hebrews7:9 Epedorio einer ebe Lebi da, loedumuni idiopet kotomon, abu koinak idiopet kotomon kotoma Aburaam," 
Hebrews7:10 naarai koriŋa ejai toma akuan naka papaake naeriamunotor Melukisadek kaŋes," 
Hebrews7:11 Aso arai kejai aitodolikinio kanuka esasedotene loka Ilebin, (naarai apotu ituŋa kodumut ikisila kanuka ŋol,) kanukinyo ipudare bobo esasedoti ece anyoun kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek, komam imarakinio kwape ejaar epone loka Aaron?" 
Hebrews7:12 Naarai naelocokinere esasedotene, ibusakinit ikisila da ailoeokinio." 
Hebrews7:13 Naarai ŋol loalimitere akiro ŋun kerai loka ateker ace, nemam ebunitor etuŋanan kere lokijaanakini kotem." 
Hebrews7:14 Naarai idelelei ebe elomunit Ejakaitiwok kotoma Yuda, ateker namam apeŋo Musa elimitor akiro nuka esasedotene," 
Hebrews7:15 Bobo da iyatasi ŋun aideleleun noi, arai enyounit esasedoti ece kwape ejaar aput naka Melukisadek," 
Hebrews7:16 loaraun esasedoti, mere kwape ejaatar ikisila luka aicorakinet naka akuan, dimarai kwape ejaar apedor naka aijar namam edaun." 
Hebrews7:17 Naarai itejenunitai ebe, “Irai ijo esasedoti kiton ikar kere, Kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek.”" 
Hebrews7:18 Naarai kepuai epaluni aicorakinet nageet kanuka akalanyanut ka amamus ajokisike," 
Hebrews7:19 (naarai emamei ibore yenitodolete ikisila;) kepuai da aponi kitolomikin amun naitelekarit ajokis, nakikunyaria mama ejai Edeke." 
Hebrews7:20 Ido mam abu kojau komamei aiyaposit. 
Hebrews7:21 Naarai koraut kesi isasedotin komamei aiyaposit, konye je kitaraunai kaiyaposit kanuka ŋol lokelimokini ŋes ebe, “Abu Ejakait kiyapo, komam iitokini ebe, ‘Irai ijo esasedoti kiton ikar kere.’”" 
Hebrews7:22 Abu Yesu da korau kwaŋin ekabwoaran loka aitutuket naitelekarit ajokis. 
Hebrews7:23 Kes da aponi kitaraununai isasedotin luipu, naarai etikokinit kes atwanare ajaenena osasedotene;" 
Hebrews7:24 konye ŋol, esasedoteneke mam ikopanar, naarai ejaenena ikar kere." 
Hebrews7:25 Kanuka ŋun ŋes epedoria aitajar cut luepote mama ejai Edeke kotomakeŋ, naarai ebusi ŋesi apaarasia kere apuronokin kes." 
Hebrews7:26 Naarai ibusakinit oni ajaut kesasedoti lopeti loikoni nen, lokalaunan, loemamei aronis, karaida elos, loetiakunitai kama ejaas ikadiakanarak, loitopolooritai da adepar akuj." 
Hebrews7:27 Mam ŋes iburao ŋinipaaran, kwape isasedotin kwi lupeti, ainanakin asuban, naegei kanuka adiakanaretake, kosodi konyet kokau kanuka ŋun nuka ituŋa; naarai abu ŋesi kiswama, kwaŋin irwan atipet bon naejaikinor elopet." 
Hebrews7:28 Naarai eseunete ikisila ituŋa luekalanyaka, araun isasedotin lupeti; konye do akirot naka aiyaposit naetupakini ikisila, abu koseu Okoku loitodolikinitoi kiton ikar kere." 
Hebrews8:1 Akirot alopet nakibala ŋes nata ebe: kija kesasedoti lopeti loikoni nen, lokiboikin akan nakoteten naka eicoloŋ naka Lokapolou toma akuj," 
Hebrews8:2 ekejaanakinan toma aiboisio nukalaunak, ka ewema lokabeit, lokibubukini Ejakait kwabo mere etuŋanan," 
Hebrews8:3 Naarai ŋolisasedoti lopeti edakakinio tetere einakini ainakineta ka asuban; kanuka ŋun ibusakinit esasedoti ŋol da lopeti ajaut kibore yeneinakini. 
Hebrews8:4 Aso arai kejai akwap, timam keraun esasedoti nepetai da, naarai ejaas isasedotin lueinakinete ainakineta kwape ejaatar ikisila." 
Hebrews8:5 Ijaanakinete ŋul aput ka etoribe loka aiboisio nukalaunak nukotoma akuj; kwape kicorakinia Edeke Musa napeapie aiswamaun ewema ebe, “Kocoite ebe iswamauni iboro kere kwape ejaar aput nakiitodikinio jo koroŋat.”" 
Hebrews8:6 Konye kwana abu Kristo kodum aijaanakin naitelekarit noi, naarai erai ekadiekan loka aitutuket naitelekarit noi ajokis, naisilakinitai kotoma aisumuneta nuitelekarito noi aiokis." 
Hebrews8:7 Naarai arai kerai aitutuket nasodit naemamei aitoronet timam kemoi aibois kanuka nakiareit. 
Hebrews8:8 Naarai itoroni kes naebalar ebe: “Ebala Ejakait ebe, epote apaarasia, Nuetodolikinio aitutuket nakitetet kekek loka Isirael, Ka ekek loka Yuda." 
Hebrews8:9 Ebala Ejakait ebe, Mere kwape ejaar aitutuket nakolo etutuki ka lukapapaakec Kapaaran naketiŋia kakan aitonyoun kakwap nako Misiri; Naarai mam ŋul kesalito toma aitutuketeka, Eoŋ da abu kajal kes." 
Hebrews8:10 Ebala Ejakait ebe, Na ŋes aitutuket naetutuki kekek loka Isirael, Akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun; Epikakini ikakisila aomisiokec, Ewadikakini da otauonokec; Eoŋ da araun Ekecedeke, Kes da eraunos ikatuŋa." 
Hebrews8:11 Kwabo mam bobo isisianakinos ŋinituŋanan ikeidunyet, Ka ŋinituŋanan da onaceke, kobalas ebe, ‘Kojen Ejakait,’ Naarai kajenunete rwaru kere, Ameun ka yenididi aitodol yenikapolon kakesi." 
Hebrews8:12 Naarai etimi kes numam adolitekec, Ido mam bobo eituni akecediakar.”" 
Hebrews8:13 Nainerar ebe Aitutuket nakitetet, itomojoŋi nasodit. Konye ŋin naamojoŋiar, naekokosanit da eapie ailicar." 
Hebrews9:1 Aso aitutuket nasodit da kejaas kaicorakineta nuka aima Edeke ka aibois nakalaunan naka akwap. 
Hebrews9:2 Naarai itemokinitoi ewema losodit, lokejai epir loka atalai, ka emesa, ka imugatin luka aitodikin, nen ŋes kenyaritai Aibois nakalaunan." 
Hebrews9:3 Kau naka aigalisit nakiareit kejai ewema lokenyaritai Aibois nakalaunan noi," 
Hebrews9:4 lokejai etem loka lukisupurununo lokesabu, ka asaduku naka aitutuket nakiladaaritai kesabu iwaitin kere, nekejai atido nakesabu nakejai emanu, ka ebela loka Aaron loeburukunyit, ka amor da nuka aitutuket;" 
Hebrews9:5 kujuke da Ikerubin luka aibuses, iteriborito eicoloŋ-lokaitim. Emamei apak kwana einer akiro nuka iboro kaŋul idiopet idiopet." 
Hebrews9:6 Aso kedaut iboro ŋul aitemonokinio kwaŋin, elomanarete isasedotin tiritir owema losodit, itodolikinete akiro nuka aijaanakin;" 
Hebrews9:7 konye owema ŋol lokiareit elomanari esasedoti lopeti bon, irwan atipet ŋolikaru, mere komameete aokot nueinakini kanuke, ido kanuka aibucareta nuka aolit naka ituŋa." 
Hebrews9:8 Isideleleuni Emoyo Lokalaunan ebe mam ber erot etakanuna alomar aiboisio nukalaunak, naeriŋar ewema losodit ebwoi." 
Hebrews9:9 Ŋin ŋes aput naka apak nakwana, naejaas ainakineta ka asuban nueinakinio numam epedorete aitodol aomisio nuka yenemai;" 
Hebrews9:10 naarai eraas ikisila luka akuan bon, lunyaman ka lumatan, ka luka ailoŋ naka iponesio luegelegela, lukicorakinio aitodol apak naka aiteteunio." 
Hebrews9:11 Konye kedau Kristo abunore, loerai esasedoti lopeti loka akiro nuejok nuejaunete, kotoma owema loepol aitelekarit loitodolikinio jokan, lomam kiswamao kakanin, ŋes atemar ebe, mere loka akwap kana," 
Hebrews9:12 kwabo mere kanuka aokot nuka akinei ka itak lurosok, konye kanuka akeokot elopet, abu koloma irwan atipet bon Aibois Nakalaunan, nakedaunia adumun alakun naka ikar kere." 
Hebrews9:13 Naarai arai aokot nuka akinei ka imoŋin, ka ekurwon loka ataok, lukebwatanakinio luemunaara, italaunete kiton aitesegaar akuan," 
Hebrews9:14 itelekarito cama aokot nuka Kristo, lokeinakin bon mama ejai Edeke kotoma Omoyo loka ikar kere, araun asubanit naemamei akemer, itesegarete aomisiokus kaswamisio nukatwak tetere ijaanakinete Edeke lokajaran." 
Hebrews9:15 Kanuka ŋun erai ekadiekan loka aitutuket nakitetet, tetere edumunete ŋul lukenyaraunitai aisumunet naka airumet naka ikar kere, naarai abu atwanare kojau naelakuni kes kotoma apaanareta nukotoma aitutuket nasodit." 
Hebrews9:16 Naarai neejai aitutuket naka airum, ibusakinit kojai atwanare naka yenikitutuki ŋin." 
Hebrews9:17 Naarai icasit aitutuket naka airum nakejaunia atwanare, naarai emamei ŋes agogoŋ arai eroko ejari yenikitutuki." 
Hebrews9:18 Kanuka ŋun kiton aitutuket nasodit da mam itaŋitai komameete aokot. 
Hebrews9:19 Naarai nakedaunia Musa alimokin ituŋa kere ninikicorakinet kwape ejaatar ikisila, abu kolem aokot nuka itak lurosok ka nuka akinei nepepe kakipi ka eusi loereŋ, ka esop da, kobwatanak eitabo ka ituŋa kere," 
Hebrews9:20 kobala ebe, “Nu kes aokot nuka aitutuket nukiicorakini yes Edeke,”" 
Hebrews9:21 kobwatanak aokot kopone kaŋol ewema, ka iboro kere da luka aijaanakin." 
Hebrews9:22 Abeit kotoma ikisila aapiei iboro kere aitesegario kaokot, ido arai emamei abukor aokot emamei aisionio." 
Hebrews9:23 Aso ibusakinit aputosia nuka iboro lukokuju aitesegario kaŋun, konye iboro lukokuju ikulepek ibusakinit aitesegario kasuban nuitelekarito ŋun kajokis." 
Hebrews9:24 Naarai mam Kristo alomarit aibois nakalaunan nakiswamao kakanin, nakeputosi kaŋin kanakabeit, konye toma akuj alopet, atakanu kwana kakonyen nuka Edeke kanuwok." 
Hebrews9:25 Kwabo mere ainanakin bon irwan ipu, kwape elomanaria esasedoti lopeti Aibois Nakalaunan ŋolikaru kaokot numam eraas nuke;" 
Hebrews9:26 naarai tiibusakinit ŋes arieb irwan ipu ameun kaisub akwapin. Konye kwana, atakanu irwan atipet bon kawasia naka ikar alemar adiakanareta kanuka ainakin bon araut asubanit." 
Hebrews9:27 Ido kwape itemokinitere ituŋa atwanare irwan atipet, kosodi akaulo kaŋin atubokinio," 
Hebrews9:28 kwape kwaŋin Kristo da, nakeinakinere irwan atipet aibwok adiakanareta nuka ikepuak, etakanuni irwan nakiareit komamei adiakar mama kaŋul luidareto ŋes kanuka aitaiario," 
Hebrews10:1 Naarai ejai ikisila etoribe loka ajokisio nuepote, kwabo mere aput obe naka akiro kaŋun, mam epedorete cut aitodolikin ŋul luikunyakinete, kanuka asuban ŋupeŋun nueinanakinete tiritir, ŋolikaru ŋolikaru." 
Hebrews10:2 Arai mere kwaŋin, mam ti do kinyeis ainanakin? Naarai luemaete naedauniata aitesegario cut irwan atipet, timam bobo kilepilep adiakar." 
Hebrews10:3 Konye kotoma asuban ŋun ejai aisiitunio adiakanareta ŋolikaru, ŋolikaru." 
Hebrews10:4 Naarai mam epedorete aokot nuka imoŋin ka akinei alemar adiakanareta. 
Hebrews10:5 Naarai naalomunia Kristo toma akwapin abala ebe, “Mam ibu kokoto asubanit ka ainakinet, Konye ibu kitemok akuan kanukaŋ;" 
Hebrews10:6 Mam isiyalamikinit ainakineta nuicweio, karaida ainakineta nuka adiakar," 
Hebrews10:7 Kasodi kener ebe, ‘Koany, abu eoŋ,’ (Iwadikatai nukaŋ oitabo lonunuko) ‘Aswam nuikoto ijo, wu Edeke.’ ”" 
Hebrews10:8 Naarai naenerar kokuju ebe, “Asuban ka ainakineta ka ainakineta nuicweio, ka nuka adiakar, mam ibu kokoto, karaida aisiyalamikin,” (ŋun kes nueinanakinio kwape ejaatar ikisila)," 
Hebrews10:9 kosodi konyet einer ebe, “Koany, abu eoŋ aswam nuikoto ijo.” Elemari nasodit tetere iticasi nakiareit." 
Hebrews10:10 Kotoma akot kaŋin aponi oni kitalaun kanuka ainakinet naka akuan naka Yesu Kristo irwan atipet bon. 
Hebrews10:11 Ŋolisasedoti da ebwoi ŋinipaaran kotoma aijaanakinike, icebokinit ainanakin asuban ŋupeŋun, numam cut epedorete alemar adiakanareta." 
Hebrews10:12 Konye nakedaunia Kristo ainakin asubanit adiopet kanuka adiakanareta naedauni ikar kere, kosodi kiboikin akan nakoteten naka Edeke," 
Hebrews10:13 ameuni kanen idareunit aitodol naibwaikinere lukasurupoke araun iicoloŋ yenika akeieke," 
Hebrews10:14 Naarai kotoma ainakinet adiopet abu kitodolik luitalaunio kiton ikar kere. 
Hebrews10:15 Emoyo Lokalaunan da itejenari nuwok, naarai naadaunia einer ebe," 
Hebrews10:16 “Ebala Ejakait ebe, Na ŋes aitutuket naetutuki kakes, Akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun, Epikakini ikakisila otauonokec, Ewadikakini da aomisiokec.”" 
Hebrews10:17 Kosodi konyet ebala ebe, “Mam bobo eituni adiakanaretakec ka epalikec.”" 
Hebrews10:18 Konye napejaar alemario ŋun, mam bobo einakinio asubanit kanuka adiakar." 
Hebrews10:19 Aso iinacan, naarai kija katitiŋ alomar toma aibois nakalaunan kanuka aokot nuka Yesu," 
Hebrews10:20 kotoma orot lokitetet ka loejari da, lokicilakini oni kotoma aigalisit, ŋes atemar ebe, akekuan," 
Hebrews10:21 ido kwape kijaar kesasedoti lokapolon loeyait etogo loka Edeke," 
Hebrews10:22 kekunyakis ketau lokabeit, ka aiyuun naedoliorit cut, kobwatai itauonowok da ainyein aomisio nueroko, kiloŋai da awatewok kakipi nuelaete." 
Hebrews10:23 Keketakis alimor amunowok komam kiriaŋiriaŋa, naarai lokisumunit erai lomunot." 
Hebrews10:24 Kaomoomas aisinyikokin bonik ka bonik amin ka aswam nuejokuka," 
Hebrews10:25 kenyeis apalun atukonokin nepepe, kwape iswamaata ice, konye kecoras; ido keyatanakinito ŋun kwape ianyuniata apaaran ŋin eyapuunit adolun." 
Hebrews10:26 Naarai arai kilosikinit adiakanar nakiidaunia ainakinio ajenun abeit, mam esalit bobo asubanit kanuka adiakanareta," 
Hebrews10:27 dimarai aidarit kakurian atubokinio, ka adedeŋ naka akim naebunit aicwe lukasurup." 
Hebrews10:28 Yenemwaŋi ikisila luka Musa etwani komam itimio, kanuka ikajenak iarei arai iuni." 
Hebrews10:29 Iwomito biai, nanyoin aiticanet naitelekarit noi naibusakinit ituŋanan yenipudapudai Okoku loka Edeke, komunaa da aokot nuka aitutuket, nuapotu kitalaut ŋes, komor da Emoyo loka asianut?" 
Hebrews10:30 Naarai kijeni ŋol loabu kiner ebe, “Enyaŋit ŋes lokaŋ, eoŋ ataci.” Bobo da ebe, “Irabakini Ejakait iketuŋa.”" 
Hebrews10:31 Erai akirot naesogim aibirokin akanin nuka Edeke lokajaran. 
Hebrews10:32 Konye kiitutu apaarasia nukolo, naidauniata ainwakakinio, nuititiŋikinioto aut naepol naka aisiriebio," 
Hebrews10:33 acepakio araun lusesena kanuka amoromor ka areio, acepakio da naimorianakinotor kaluiswamakinio ŋun," 
Hebrews10:34 Naarai ipotu kitimoto ienan, ido ipotu kotitiŋikis kalakara aŋatario naka ikusiboro, kojenete ebe ejaas yes iboro luejok adepar ido lueperonorete." 
Hebrews10:35 Aso sirikicakasi atitinikus, naejai eropit loepol." 
Hebrews10:36 Naarai ipudasi atitiŋikin, tetere iswamaete nuekoto Edeke, kosodete kijaut naisumunitai." 
Hebrews10:37 “Naarai eriŋa esalit apak naedit noi, Kosodi loebuni ebuni komam itumor;" 
Hebrews10:38 Konye ekadolitonika ejari kanuka aiyuun, Ido arai eboŋori kau, Mam ekatau elelakinit ŋes.”" 
Hebrews10:39 Konye mam oni kirai lukibonori kau toma amudiario, konye kirai luka aiyuun kanuka aitajar aijar," 
Hebrews11:1 Aiyuun ŋes apetetait naka akiro nuemunoi, aitogogoŋet naka akiro numam eanyuna." 
Hebrews11:2 Naarai kotomakeŋ ŋes etejenunere imakio. 
Hebrews11:3 Kanuka aiyuun kijen ebe kesubio akwapin kere kakirot naka Edeke, tetere mam iswamao nueanyuna kotoma kaŋun kanuetakanete." 
Hebrews11:4 Kanuka aiyuun abu Abel koinak Edeke asubanit naitelekarit naka Kain kajokis, kanuka ŋin ŋes kitejenikinere araut loedolit, kitejen Edeke kanuka acamun ainakinetake, ido kanuka aiyuunike, karaida abu kotwana, konye eriŋa inera." 
Hebrews11:5 Kanuka aiyuun aponi koyaŋaarai Enok tetere mam eanyuni atwanare, ido mam abu kotakan, naarai abu Edeke koyaŋa ŋes. Naarai eriŋa eyanaara etejenikinitai ebe abu kitelel Edeke." 
Hebrews11:6 Konye neemamea aiyuun mam epedor aitelel ŋes. Naarai yenikunyakini Edeke ibusakinit aiyuun ebe ejai ŋesi, ido ebe eropi ŋul luemoete ŋes," 
Hebrews11:7 Kanuka aiyuun abu Noa loekwenyarit Edeke kanuka akiro nukeroko etakanuna, koyoŋ ejok, kitemok ataker aitaiaria lukokaleke; kanuka gin kotubok akwapin aitelekario, koraun ekerunan loka adolit naejai toma aiyuun." 
Hebrews11:8 Kanuka aiyuun abu Aburaam korimak nakenyaraunere alomar toma aibois naelosio ainakin araun airumet; abu koloma komam ejeŋi neelosi. 
Hebrews11:9 Kanuka aiyuun abu kiboioror kakwap naka aisumunet, bala akwap namere nakeŋ, iboienenei koweman nepepe ka Isaak ka Yakob ikerumak lukaupake luka aisumunet ŋipeŋin." 
Hebrews11:10 Naarai abu kidareunite ere loejaas apeteta, loapwakun Edeke loaduki da." 
Hebrews11:11 Kanuka aiyuun abu Sara alopet kodum apedor apotuun karaida kedepara ikaruke, naarai abu koomite ŋol loesumuni araut lomunot." 
Hebrews11:12 Kanuka ŋun anyoun kotuŋanan ediopet, ido loasubit bala etwanit, aponi kowuriai lueputosi bala aacer nuka akuj kaipues, ido kwape asiŋe naejai ariri naka aŋolol namam imarun." 
Hebrews11:13 Apotu ŋul kere kotwakikis toma aiyuun, koroko einakina nuesumunitai, konye apotu koanyutu kimalaete da kama elwana, kolimosi ebe keraas imo ka ikalotok kakwap." 
Hebrews11:14 Naarai luinerasi nuikote nen isideleleunito ebe emoete akwap naebeit kes. 
Hebrews11:15 Ido arai kiitunito akwap ŋin naalomuniata, tiejaas kapak aboŋor," 
Hebrews11:16 Konye kwana iŋobeleete akwap naitelekarit ajokis, ŋes nakotoma akuj. Ŋes mam irumiata Edeke ileic anyarao Edekekec, naarai abu kitemok kes ere." 
Hebrews11:17 Kanuka aiyuun, abu Aburaam koinak Isaak, naetemere, ido loabu kodum aisumuneta kalakara etemokino ainakin okokuke loteluna," 
Hebrews11:18 loaponi kinerai ebe, “Kotoma Isaak ŋes enyaraere akoniwur.”" 
Hebrews11:19 Koomite ebe epedori Edeke aitajarun, kiton kokatwak da; neadumunia kotoma aput." 
Hebrews11:20 Kanuka aiyuun abu Isaak kilipak Yakob ka Esau arereŋ kotoma akiro nuepote," 
Hebrews11:21 Kanuka aiyuun keapu Yakob atwanare, abu kilipak odwe luka Yosep kere iarei arereŋ, koma, kokukumi kakou naka ebelake." 
Hebrews11:22 Kanuka aiyuun keapu Yosep atwanare abu kiner nuka anyoun naka idwe luka Isirael, kicorak da nuka akojoke." 
Hebrews11:23 Kanuka aiyuun nakeuriere Musa, apotu ikauriakake kimunonata ŋes ilapio iuni, naarai aanyunito ebe itemelel ikoku; komam ekuriaka aicorakinet naka ekabaka." 
Hebrews11:24 Kanuka aiyuun nakepoloor Musa, kogir anyarao okoku loka apese naka Parao," 
Hebrews11:25 koseu aikonakinio erono nepepe kituŋa luka Edeke itia aitalakara kotoma aronis naka apak naedit. 
Hebrews11:26 Koomite amorosit naka Kristo araut abar naepol itia iboro luka akais nuipu luko Misiri, naarai abu kosesen aropio." 
Hebrews11:27 Kanuka aiyuun abu konyou ko Misiri, komam ekuriana adedeŋ naka ekabaka; naarai abu konirik bala eanyuni lomam etakani." 
Hebrews11:28 Kanuka aiyuun abu koricite Aleleŋ ka aibwat aokot kinyek Ekamudiaran ikiyaik atiror kes. 
Hebrews11:29 Kanuka aiyuun apotu kitoroto Aŋolol Nakareŋan bala akwap naconit; konye naketamakiniata Imisirian aitor nen, kolumosi." 
Hebrews11:30 Kanuka aiyuun kotiyaros arwatatin nuka Yeriko, nakedaunere airimor apaarasia akanykaarei." 
Hebrews11:31 Kanuka aiyuun mam Rakab naadote emudiara nepepe ka lumam erimasi, naarai abu kisukunyik ikarotak kainapakin." 
Hebrews11:32 Kener anyoika bobo? Naarai mam apak kelosikino arai kalimok nuka Gideon, ka Barak, ka Samuson, ka Yeputa, ka Daudi, ka Samuel ka inabin da,—" 
Hebrews11:33 lukipikorete ajakanuto kanuka aiyuun, kiswamata adolit, kodumut aisumuneta, kitubutaasi aituke nuka iŋatunyo," 
Hebrews11:34 kitojonata apedor naka akim, kokuata akwanis naka ekileŋ, kisipedoroi nakekalanyakatar, koraut lukagogoŋ kotoma ojie, kitekerata ajoresio nuka lukacekwapin." 
Hebrews11:35 Apotu aŋor kodumut lukatwakakec kotoma aitajarunio, konye ice aponi kisiriebai kaibworit, komam ecamunete ayuunio, tetere edumunete aitajarunio naejok adepar." 
Hebrews11:36 Aponi ice kitemoi kaisekelio ka aleio, eebo, kiton aeneta ka aidaris da." 
Hebrews11:37 Aponi kibiribiroi kamor, kotuboi kimusumenon, kitemoi, aponi koarai kekileŋ; apotu kirimirimoto enapito imukulen luka imerekekin ka luka akinei; apotu kilwaritos, ereitai, kikonakinitai erono,—" 
Hebrews11:38 ituŋa lumam ebusakinit akwap, apotu kilokidaete kamodiŋo, ka oroŋan, ka abuai ka apanya da nuka akwap." 
Hebrews11:39 Ituŋa ŋul kere da nakedaunere aitejenun kanuka aiyuunikec, mam edumuna aisumunet," 
Hebrews11:40 naarai abu Edeke kojenikinite ibore yenejok aitelekarit kanuwok, tetere ŋul mam itodolikinio komam oni." 
Hebrews12:1 Aso naarai kilukunit oni kere elisina loepol loetia nen, loka ikajenak, kalacasi ŋinibore kere yenelaŋir; adiakar da naepatanikinit aigogo leonor oni, kaboloboloto katitiŋ epeget loibwaikinitai kakonyenewok," 
Hebrews12:2 kasesenete Yesu, ekagean ka eketodolon loka aiyuuniwok, loabu kotitiŋik emusalaba, komen ileic, kanuka aiyalama naebwaikinitai kakonyeneke, iboie kakan nakoteten naka eicoloŋ loka Edeke." 
Hebrews12:3 Koomoomata do noi ŋol loketitiŋikini asurup naetia nen naka ikadiakanarak kanukeŋ, kinyeis aipas, kiiloros kotauonokus." 
Hebrews12:4 Mam ber ijiito kiton abukor aokot, iwutas kadiakar." 
Hebrews12:5 Bobo kimurwok aicor, nainera kayes kwape odwe ebe, “Okokuka, sirimwanenenei alecor naka Ejakait, Kwabo sirikiilor nakiriemeriemaa ŋesi." 
Hebrews12:6 Naarai elecori Ejakait yenemina, Elei da ŋinikoku yenecamunit ŋesi.”" 
Hebrews12:7 Kanuka alecorio ititiŋikinete. Kiswamakini yes Edeke kwape odwe; naarai ikoku inyoin yenimam papake elecori? 
Hebrews12:8 Aso arai mam kilecorio, naimorikikinit kere, kwaŋin iraas lukiwurikinitai okal! kwabo mere odwe," 
Hebrews12:9 Bobo da ajaas oni lukapapawok luka akuan lukiileconorete, oni da kayonito kes. Mam itelekarit noi oni anonokikin Papa loka imoyon, kajara da?" 
Hebrews12:10 Naarai apotu kesi koleconorete oni apaarasia nuikidioko, kwape kekototor, konye ŋol kilecori kanuka ajokis tetere kimori alauniteke." 
Hebrews12:11 Alecorio kere naka apak kana mam esubit bala nakaiyalama, dimarai nakican; konye kokau erai araito nuinapakina nuka adolit, kama kaŋul kaluituutooritai kaŋin." 
Hebrews12:12 Kanuka ŋun koriosi yesi akusikanin nuekalanyaka, kitogogoŋoto da akusikuŋin nuilejekekas," 
Hebrews12:13 kiswamakis akusikejen irotin luitenara, kinyek yenenwalit aitapaario, konye gwai kitaŋaleunoi." 
Hebrews12:14 Kotupata ainapakin nepepe kituŋa kere, ka alaunite da, neemamea ŋin emamei yeneanyuni Ejakait." 
Hebrews12:15 Koanyanasi ebe emamei yeneolikinit asianut naka Edeke; kinyek “Aliasit naka adwaris” alibun ka aitican yes, kosodete luipu amunaar;" 
Hebrews12:16 kinyek idiotuŋanan araun yenidote arai yenimam eyonit Edeke kwape Esau, loabu kogwela apolouke naka ekiyai kanuka adutunet adiopet naka inyamat." 
Hebrews12:17 Naarai ijenete ebe akaulo kaŋun, naakotor airum arereŋ, aponi kogiroi, naarai mam abu kodum apak naka aitoronikin, karaida abu komoote noi kakiyo." 
Hebrews12:18 Naarai mam idolokinito emoru loepedorio atirorio, loenoki da akim, karaida neejai amuton naejesi cucucuc, ka idouon luitolimakito, ka ekwam," 
Hebrews12:19 ka aruo naka arupepe, ka eporoto loka akiro, luapupete apotu kiŋaiŋaata sirikelimokin kes bobo acekirot." 
Hebrews12:20 Naarai mam apotu kopedosi atitiŋikin akirot naecorakinio ebe, “Arai ketiro itiaŋ emoru ŋol ibiribirio kamor.”" 
Hebrews12:21 Ido kerai naetakani nasogim kwaŋin, abu Musa da kobala ebe, “Akurianari noi, amaran da.”" 
Hebrews12:22 Konye idolokinito Emoru Sion ka ere loka Edeke lokajaran, Yerusalem lokotoma akuj, kaneejaas ajoresio nuka imalaikan lumam imarunos," 
Hebrews12:23 ka atukot naka ikiyaik luiwadikatai toma akuj, ka neejai Ekatubon loerai Edeke loka kere, ka neejaas imoyon luka ikadolitok luitodolikinitoi," 
Hebrews12:24 ka neejai Yesu, ekadiekan loka aitutuket nakitetet, ka neejaas aokot nubwatan nuinerasi nuejok aitelekarit kwa nuka Abel." 
Hebrews12:25 Kocoito ebe mam iŋerete ŋol loinera. Naarai arai mam apotu kokuata nakeŋerioto ŋol loekwenyari kes ejai akwapin, kitelekari noi oni amamus aiku, arai kiŋeri ŋol loikwenyari ejai toma akuj." 
Hebrews12:26 Abu eporotoke kitamaran akwap kapak kaya, konye isumuni kwana ebe, “Irwan atipet bobo ejaŋakini, mere akwap bon, konye akuj da.”" 
Hebrews12:27 Konye akirot ŋin ebe, “Irwan atipet bobo,” itejenuni alemario naka ŋul luitamaranio, kwape luesubitai, tetere esalete lumam itamaranio." 
Hebrews12:28 Kanuka ŋun naarai kidumuni ajakanut namam itamaranio, kajaas kasianut, nakijaanakinia Edeke aijaanakin naitoiokit ŋesi, nepepe kayoŋit ka acoit;" 
Hebrews12:29 naarai erai Edekewok akim naenyamiari. 
Hebrews13:1 Kojaenena amin iinacan. 
Hebrews13:2 Sirikiimurwokis aisukuny ipejok, naarai kanuka ŋin apotu ice kisukunyikis imalaikan komam ejenete," 
Hebrews13:3 Kiitunito ienan, bala kienitai nepepe kakes; ka luiswamakinitai erono, naarai ijaas yesi da toma akuan." 
Hebrews13:4 Kitubusikis ituŋa kere adukokin, ejam da korai lomam emunaara; naarai etubokini Edeke ludotea ka lueelosi." 
Hebrews13:5 Kidaras kinyeis amin apesan, kodaut luijaatar; naarai abu ŋesi elopet kobala ebe, “Mam ketukurwori jo cut, karaida aijal.”" 
Hebrews13:6 Ŋes kinerar katitiŋ ebe, “Ejakait ŋes erai ekenarakinanika, Mam akurianari, Inyo bo epedori ituŋanan aiswamakin eoŋ?”" 
Hebrews13:7 Kiitunito ikeŋarenikinokokus, lukilimonokinete akirot naka Edeke; koŋicete noi esaŋe loka ejautenekec, korokosi aiyuunikec." 
Hebrews13:8 Erai Yesu Kristo ŋopeŋol bian ka lolo, ido kiton ikar kere." 
Hebrews13:9 Sirikiyananario kaisisianakin nakiponesio luipu naegelara; naarai ejok aitogogoŋ etau kasianut, kwabo mere kanuka inyamat, lumam apotu kinarakis ŋul lualosioto." 
Hebrews13:10 Ejai oni etem loemamei luijaanakinete ewema apedor ainyam iboroke. 
Hebrews13:11 Naarai itiaŋ lueyaŋaari esasedoti lopeti aokotokec toma aibois nakalaunan kanuka adiakar, icweio awatekec kokiŋ kiidukurun." 
Hebrews13:12 Kanuka ŋun Yesu da, abu korieba kokiŋ kerute, tetere italauni ituŋa kaokotoke elopet." 
Hebrews13:13 Aso kalomasi oni da mamakeŋ kiŋa kiidukurun, kebwokitos amorositike." 
Hebrews13:14 Naarai emamei oni ere loeperonori kane, konye kimoot je loekot ajaun." 
Hebrews13:15 Aso kainanakis Edeke asubanit naka aiturit tiritir kotomakeŋ, ŋes araito nuka aituke nuelimorete ekekiror." 
Hebrews13:16 Konye sirikimurwokis aswam ejok, ka aimor luijaatar, naarai itojokit Edeke asuban nuikote nen." 
Hebrews13:17 Korimarito ikeŋarenikinokokus, kononokikinito da; naarai ekwenyete ŋul kanuka aijarakus, kwape luinyakunete akirot; tetere iswamaete ŋun kaiyalama kwabo mere keidiny; naarai timam ŋin kiiŋarak yes." 
Hebrews13:18 Kilipanakinai sio, naarai kitogogoŋit ebe kija kaomisio nuejok, kikoto ajaut kiponesio luejok kotoma akiro kere." 
Hebrews13:19 Ido aitelekarit noi keŋaiŋait yes aikonenen nen, tetere kenyakunio katipet mamakus." 
Hebrews13:20 Konye Edeke lokainapakin, loetoboŋuni Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kokatwak, ekecokon lokapolon loka amerekekin, kanuka aokot nuka aitutuket naka ikar kere," 
Hebrews13:21 kitodolik yes kotoma kaŋinikirot naejok, tetere iswamaete nuekot ŋesi, kiswamai ŋesi da kotomakus naitojokitai kakonyeneke, kanuka Yesu Kristo; kojai aibuses mamakeŋ ikar ka ikar. Amen." 
Hebrews13:22 Konye iinacan, keŋaiŋait yes, koŋirikis akirot naicori, naarai kewadikakinit yes kanuesupaaka." 
Hebrews13:23 Kojenutu ebe alacakin onacewok Timoteo. Arai kebu ŋol katipet, kaanyuni yes nepepe kaŋes." 
Hebrews13:24 Kiyogaete ikeŋarenikinokokus kere, ka lukalaunak da kere. Kiyogaete yes luko Italia." 
Hebrews13:25 Asianut kojai kayes kere, Amen." 
James1:1 Yakob ebulesit loka Edeke ka loka Ejakait Yesu Kristo, Mama ejaas atekerin atomon kanuarei nuesiarakinos: Yoga." 
James1:2 Iinacanaka, koomitos kere araut nukaiyalama, naidoioto toma acodunio nakiponesio luipu," 
James1:3 kojenete ebe aitemio naka aiyuunikus eyauni atitiŋikin," 
James1:4 Ido kojau atitiŋikin kaswam naedoliorit, tetere iraunos luipolok, luitekoro, komam adiokirot nakiwolikinit." 
James1:5 Arai ejai kayes yenewolikinit acoa, kilip Edeke loeinakini kere kajalit, kwabo mam itoroni, ŋes da einakinio." 
James1:6 Konye kilip kotoma aiyuun, komam ebuonokin, naarai yenebuonokini eputosi bala akailan naka aŋolol, naekutanari ekwam kibukanari." 
James1:7 Kinyek ituŋanan ŋin aomit ebe edumuni ibore kama ejai Ejakait; 
James1:8 ituŋanan yenika itauon iarei, yenimam icasit korotinike kere," 
James1:9 Konye koolobob onace loitisilitoi kanuka aitopoloorioke," 
James1:10 koolobob lokabaran da kanuka aitisilioke, naarai eraraar kwape aturot naka inya." 
James1:11 Naarai elomuni akoloŋ isirinyori amwanis inya, edoi aturotoke, eoliori da ajokis naka aputoke. Isokokoi lokabaran da kwape kwaŋin kotoma alositeke." 
James1:12 Isirereŋitoi etuŋanan loetitiŋikin acodunio, naarai kedau acamunio, edumuni aboko naka aijar naisumunikinit Ejakait lueminasi ŋes." 
James1:13 Kinyek yenecodunio einer ebe, “Edeke kacoduni eoŋ” naarai mam epedori Edeke acodunio kanukaronok, ido ŋes elopet mam ecoduni ituŋanan kere." 
James1:14 Konye ŋinituŋanan ecodunio kiriite ekeimiel elopet kaijodijodio," 
James1:15 Kosodi kepotuu eimiel euriei adiakar, adiakar ŋin da kepoloor idouni atwanare." 
James1:16 Ikainacan luminan, siriŋalas." 
James1:17 Ŋiniinakinet naejok, ka ŋiniijaikina naedolit ebuni kokuju, ijesuni kama ejai Papa loka luecaete, emamei ailoconokin kamakeŋ, karaida etoribe loka aibelonokin." 
James1:18 Kanuka akoteke abu kouri oni kakirot naka abeit, tetere kirauni kwape araito nusodit nuka isubanake." 
James1:19 Ijenete ŋin, iinacanaka luminan. Aso korai ŋinituŋanan yenisunyit aiirar, yeniyapi einer, yeniyapi anyunyura," 
James1:20 naarai anyunyura naka etuŋanan mam iswamai adolit naka Edeke," 
James1:21 Kanuka ŋun kolacasi asilianut kere ka aronis naelitoro, kijaut kaiyapepera akirot nairaitai toma, naepedori aitajar aijarakus." 
James1:22 Konye koraas ikeswamak akirot, kwabo mere ikeirarak bon, luimodas." 
James1:23 Naarai arai iirari ituŋanan akirot, komam iswamai, eputosi ŋin ituŋanan yeneanyuni akonyen nuka aurioke kotoma aroet;" 
James1:24 naarai eanyuni, kolot, atipet imurwokini kwape eputor." 
James1:25 Konye yenirerei ikisila luedolito, luka aosikinio, kodunyakinite kotomakec, sirikeraun ikeiraran yenimurwokini, konye ikeswaman aswam, isirereŋitoi ituŋanan ŋin kotoma kanuiswamai." 
James1:26 Arai eomit ituŋanan kere ebe erai yenikedini, komam itikokin aŋajepeke, kiŋalai etauke, edini loka ituŋanan kaŋin erai lotai." 
James1:27 Edini loelai, loemamei elos kakonyen nuka Edeke Papa ŋes lota: aanyanar ikokiok ka apuserun kotoma ocanikec, ka aidar bon kakwap komamei amasikinet." 
James2:1 Iinacanaka, siritiakito ituŋa naijaatar kaiyuun naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo, Ejakait loka aibuses." 
James2:2 Naarai arai elomuni etuŋanan atukosikus, loenapit egilut loka esabu, ka inapen luibusiak, elomuni da lokican enapit luenyilinyila," 
James2:3 yes da isukunyikinete loenapit luibusiak, itemarete atiar, “Kiboikin ijo ne neejok,” itemarete da lokican atiar, “Kobwo ijo kalaije,” arai bo, “Kiboikin kwap kakejeka,”" 
James2:4 aso mam kereka itiakasi kotomakus, iraunos ikatubok luka aomisio nueroko?" 
James2:5 Kiirasi, iinacanaka luminan, Mam kereka abu Edeke koseu lukican lukakwapin araut ikabarak luka aiyuun, ka ikerumak luka ajakanut naisumunikinit ŋul lueminasi ŋes?" 
James2:6 Konye ipotu yesi komwaŋa lokican. Mere kereka lukabarak kiridakinito yes, kiyaŋaarete airabis?" 
James2:7 Mere kes emoromoroete ekiror loejok lokimaikinitai yes? 
James2:8 Konye arai kitodoloto ekisil loka akabakanut, kwape ejaar naiwadikatai ebe, “Komina ekoniidunyet kwape iminari bon,” iswamaete ejok." 
James2:9 Konye arai itiakito ituŋa iswamata erono, kitoronete ikisila yes kwape ikebucarak." 
James2:10 Naarai yenerici ikisila kere, konye kibuca kediopet, egwauni akiro nuka kere." 
James2:11 Naarai ŋol loabu kiner ebe, “Siridote,” abu kiner da ebe, “Siriari.” Arai mam idotei, konye iari, iraun do ijo yenibili ikisila." 
James2:12 Kinerasi kwaŋin, kiswamata da kwaŋin, kwape luepote atubokinio akiro kokisila luka aosikinio." 
James2:13 Naarai etube mam itimi ŋin yenimam iswamai nukaitim; naarai eoloboboi aitim kotube. 
James2:14 Iinacanaka, ajokis anyoin, arai ebala ituŋanan ebe ejai kaiyuun, konye emameete ŋes aswamisio? Epedori kereka akeiyuun aitajar ŋes?" 
James2:15 Arai inyilinyilitoi onac arai inac, emameete da inyamat luka ŋinipaaran," 
James2:16 konye ebala idiopet kayesi kes ebe, “Koloto inapakina, kodumutu aibuse, kimonikinos,” kwabo mam iinakinete kes nuipuda akuan, ajokis anyoin?" 
James2:17 Kwaŋin aiyuun da, kemamuutu aswamisio, atwana." 
James2:18 Konye inera idiotuŋanan ebe, “Ejai jo aiyuun, eoŋ da kija kaswamisio.” Kitodikinai cani aiyuunikon komameete aswamisio, eoŋ da ketodikini jo akaiyuun kotoma aswamisio." 
James2:19 Iyuunit ijo ebe erai Edeke ediopet; iswamai ejok. Iyuunete ajokin da, komaranete." 
James2:20 Ijo etuŋanan lotai, ikoto kereka ajenun ebe aiyuun komameete aswamisio erai arakan?" 
James2:21 Mam kereka aponi kitojokai Aburaam papaawok araun loedolit kanuka aswamisio, naainakinia okokuke Isaaka kotem?" 
James2:22 Iany aiyuun kwape iswamaa nepepe kaswamisioke, ido etopoloor aiyuun kanuka aswamisio;" 
James2:23 Ido kitodolikinai naiwadikatai nainera ebe, “Kiyuu Aburaam Edeke, kimarakinai araut adolit”; komaikinai epapero loka Edeke." 
James2:24 Ianyut kwape itojokere ituŋanan araun yenedolit kanuka aswamisio, mere kanuka aiyuun bon." 
James2:25 Kwape kwaŋin da mam kereka aponi kitojokai Rakab naadote araun naedolit kanuka aswamisio, nakisukunyikinia ikiyakia, kitotor kes orot ece?" 
James2:26 Naarai kwape etwania akuan emamei emoyo, kwape kwaŋin da etwania aiyuun emameete aswamisio." 
James3:1 Ikainacan, sirikiraut ikesisianakinak luipu; kojenut ebe kidumuni oni atubokinio naitelekarit apolou." 
James3:2 Naarai kibucari oni kere kakiro nuipu; arai mam ibucari ituŋanan kakirot, ŋol ŋes etuŋanan loepol, loepedori aitikokin kiton akuanake kere." 
James3:3 Konye arai kibwaiki iboro luitikokinet aituke nuka ibalasin, tetere kirimarete oni, kibelonokini awatekec kere." 
James3:4 Koany atakerin da, karaida kepolok kwaŋin, eyaŋaarete ikwamin luededeŋ, ibelonokin kes akiŋol naedit noi, kama itojokit ekereŋean kere kotoma akoteke," 
James3:5 Kwape kwaŋin da erai aŋajep atutubet naedit, ilabilabi nuepolok, Koany ikito luipu luetia nen enokete akim naedit!" 
James3:6 Erai aŋajep akim. Erai aŋajep akwap naka amamus adolit kotoma atutubetawok, emunaari akuan kere, isinepuni akokoro naka auruunet, Geena da isinepuni ŋes." 
James3:7 Naarai epedorio aitapatan ŋolipone kere loka itiaŋ, ka akweny, ka lueliatos, ka luka aŋolol da, ido adaut ituŋa aitapatan," 
James3:8 konye emamei ituŋanan kere yenepedori aitapatan aŋajep, erono, iloliana, ileleba aisorit naeari." 
James3:9 Ŋin ŋes kituritor Ejakait ka Papa; ŋin ŋes kikenio ituŋa lukesubio kaput naka Edeke. 
James3:10 Elomunete aiturit ka aiken kotoma aituk ŋin adiopet. Ikainacan, mam ibus akiro ŋun ajaut kwaŋin," 
James3:11 Eleleunete kereka akipi nuejok ka nuedwarak da kotoma akoŋu adiopet naka atan? 
James3:12 Ikainacan, epedori kereka etini aira iseitunin, arai bo emusabibu aira itinin? Mam da epedorete akipi nuejai amunyu aluor nuejok." 
James3:13 Iŋai bo kayes ejai acoa ka ajenun? Kitodu cani aswamisioke koponesioke luejok kotoma aiyapepera naka acoa. 
James3:14 Konye arai kijaunos kekokote loedwar ka aŋolopa toma otauonokus, siriwoloboboete, siriŋalaete da asurokin abeit." 
James3:15 Mam acoa ŋin erai naebuni kokuju, konye erai naka akwap, naka auruunet, naka Satan." 
James3:16 Naarai neejai ekokote ka aŋolopa, nepenen da ejai aitotolikin, ka ŋiniswamisioit kere da naerono." 
James3:17 Konye acoa naebuni kokuju nasodit erai naesegara, kosodi nakainapakin, nakaiyapepera, naenonokikinit, ileleba aitim ka araito nuejok, emamei abuonokin, emamei da esoswai." 
James3:18 Eyeitai araito nuka adolit toma ainapakin mama ejaas ŋul luiswamaete nukainapakin. 
James4:1 Epote kai ijiisio, ai bo da ebunio asurup kotomakus? Mere kane, kotoma kanukisiyalamikinete yes nuejiosi kotoma atutubetakus?" 
James4:2 Iŋobeleete, ido mam idumunete; iarete, ido imielas, kwabo mam ipedorete adumun. Isurorete, ijiosi da, Mam idumunete naarai mam ilipete." 
James4:3 Ilipete, kwabo mam kiinakinio, naarai ilipete erono, tetere imonikinos nukisiyalamikinete yes." 
James4:4 Yes aŋor nudotea, mam ijenete ebe aipaperokin kakwapin ŋes asurup ka Edeke? Aso ituŋanan kere yenekot araun ipapero yenika akwapin ituluor yenikasurup yenika Edeke." 
James4:5 Arai bo iwomitos ebe inera atai naiwadikatai? Imiela kereka emoyo loiboie kotomawok ekolo? 
James4:6 Konye iyatanakini ainakin asianut. Kanuka ŋun ebala ebe, “Itepegi Edeke luiwoŋoko, konye einakini luitasonos asianut.”" 
James4:7 Aso kononokikis Edeke. Kitepegata Satan, kikeri ŋesi da yes." 
James4:8 Kikunyakis neejai Edeke, ŋes da ikunyuni mama ijaas. Yes ikadiakanarak, kilota akaninikus, kitalautu itauon, yes luejaas itauon iarei." 
James4:9 Kitururuoto, kokuudianete, komonyata da. Koluor akienakus akuudian, ka aiyalama da ajuruŋuŋ." 
James4:10 Kitasonokinos kakonyen nuka Ejakait, ŋes da kitopoloori yes." 
James4:11 Iinacan, sirinerenenas nueroko. Yeninera nueroko nuka onac, arai bo yenetubokini onaceke, inera nueroko kokisila, ido etubokini ikisila. Konye arai kitubok ikisila, mam irai ikeswaman yenika ikisila, dimarai ikatubon." 
James4:12 Ejai ekesilakinan ikisila ediopet ka ekatubon, ŋol loepedori aitajar ka amudiar da. Konye iŋai bo ijo yenitubokini iidunyetekon?" 
James4:13 Aso ca yes luineras ebe, “Lolo arai moi kilosi ore mutan, kidauni da kaŋina ekaru ediopet, kigwelanari kimedaun da,”" 
James4:14 kwabo mam ijenete nuka moi. Inyo bo akusiijar? Iraas elisina, loetakanuni apak naedit, kosodi ailicar." 
James4:15 Ti gwai ineras ebe, “Arai ekoto Ejakait, kijari kiswamai da nu ka nu.”" 
James4:16 Konye kwana iwoloboboto kotoma apoganutukus. Erono aolobob kere naikoni nen. 
James4:17 Aso yenejeni aswam nuejok, komam iswamai, erai adiakar kamakeŋ." 
James5:1 Aso ca yes ikabarak, komonyata kibwololoto kanuka ican lukiponikinete yes," 
James5:2 Abos abarakus, anyama ikajekel akusinapito." 
James5:3 Amasiki esabukus ka epuesakus, amasikinikec da eraun ajenanut mamakus, enyami awatekus kwape kakim. Ipotu kidiata iborokus luka akais nuipu toma apaarasia nukawasia." 
James5:4 Koany, iworoi eropit loka ikeswamak luasakata imanikoriakus, loimikitos yesi; aloma aimony naka ikadwenyak aki nuka Ejakait loka ajoresio." 
James5:5 Ipotu kisiyalamikinos kakwap, kominakinito aboliasio; kitutumata ikusitauon kotoma apaaran naka aario." 
James5:6 Ipotu kitetelekasi akiro ekadoliton, koarata da; mam ŋes itepega yesi." 
James5:7 Aso iinacan, kotitiŋonokinete, kiton abunore naka Ejakait. Koany, idarit ekakorion araito nuka akwap nuketiai loepol, etitiŋikinit kes kiton ainakinio akiru naka aiporo ka naka akamu da." 
James5:8 Kotitiŋonokinete yesi da, kiticata itauonokus, naarai eapie abunore naka Ejakait." 
James5:9 Iinacan, siriŋuurianakinos, kinyeis atubokinio; koany, ebwoi ekatubon kokek." 
James5:10 Iinacan, koyaŋaasi inabin araut aanyunet naka aiticanio ka atitiŋikin, luapotu kinerasi kokiror loka Ejakait." 
James5:11 Koany, kinyarit luetitiŋikinete luisirereŋitoi. Ipotu kiirasi nuka atitiŋikin naka Yob, ido ipotu koanyut kwape kiswamakinia Ejakait ŋes kawasia, kwape eraar Ejakait lokasianut naepol ka aitim." 
James5:12 Konye nuitelekarito kere, ikainacan, siriyapoenenete, karaida alimit akuj, karaida akwap, karaida aiyaposit ace kere, konye akusikirot, “eebo,” korai eebo, ka “mam” da korai mam, kinyeis aibirokin atubokinio." 
James5:13 Ejai kereka yeniticanio kotomakus? Kilip. Ejai bo yenelakara? Koye nukaiturit. 
James5:14 Ejai kereka yenedeka kotomakus? Konyarau imakio luka ekanisa, kilipakis ŋes, kinyonyoikis akinyet kokiror loka Ejakait;" 
James5:15 ailip da nakaiyuun itajari ikadekan, itonyouni da Ejakait ŋes; arai da kiswamat nukadiakanar, isionio ŋes." 
James5:16 Aso kolimonokinos akusidiakanareta bonik ka bonik, kilipanakinos da, tetere iŋaleunete. Ailip naka ikadoliton epedori noi aswam," 
James5:17 Kerai Eliya etuŋanan lokepone kwape kalowok, kilip noi kinye akiru aitep, ido mam abu kotepak akwap adaun ikar iuni ka ilapio ikanykape." 
James5:18 Kosodi kilip bobo, koinak da akuj akim, kora akwap araitoke." 
James5:19 Ikainacan, arai kepaa idio kayesi ainyein abeit, kosodi idiopet ainyakun ŋes," 
James5:20 kitejenut ŋes ebe yeninyakuni ikadiakanaran kotoma apaar naka erotoke, itajari akeijar kotoma atwanare, erapari da adiakanareta nukepuak." 
1Peter1:1 Petero, ekiyakia loka Yesu Kristo, Mama ejaas luseuna luesiarakinos luiboiororos kotoma Ponto, ka Galatia, ka Kapadokia, ka Asia, ka Bisunia," 
1Peter1:2 kwape kolo esiaunia Edeke Papa ajenun, kotoma aitalaunio naka Emoyo, kiton arimanut ka abwatakinio aokot nuka Yesu Kristo: Kiyatanakin asianut ka ainapakin mamakus." 
1Peter1:3 Kituritete Edeke ka Papa loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo! Kwape ejaar akeitim naepol abu kouri oni irwan nakiareit, tetere kija kamun naejari, kanuka ajarun naka Yesu Kristo kokatwak," 
1Peter1:4 kadumut airumet namam edaun, naemamei elos, namam erinyori naiŋadakinitai yes toma akuj;," 
1Peter1:5 yes lukigalikinit apedor naka Edeke kanuka aiyuun kiton naidumuniata aitajario naitemokino apukorio kapak nakawasia. 
1Peter1:6 Iyalamasi noi kotomakeŋ, karaida ibusakinit diat aitakadikinio kwana apak naedit, kanuka acodunio naka iponesio luipu," 
1Peter1:7 tetere aitemio naka aiyuunikus naitelekarit noi etiai loka esabu loedaun karaida kitemio kakim, kotakanu ituritoi, itopoloorio, ka aitubusikinio da, kotoma apukorio naka Yesu Kristo." 
1Peter1:8 Iminasi ŋes karaida mam ipotu koanyut ŋes; karaida mam ianyunito ŋes kwana konye iyuunito ŋes, iyalamasi noi kaiyalama namam inerio naitepolooritai." 
1Peter1:9 Idumunete esaŋe loka aiyuunikus ŋes aitajario naka aijarakus. 
1Peter1:10 Apotu inabin, luadwarenenete nuka asianut naekot abunore mamakus, komoenenete ka aiŋic akiro nuka aitajario kaŋin;" 
1Peter1:11 koŋicata ani bo apak, arai ali bo epone lokikwenyaria Emoyo loka Kristo lokejai tomakec, nakegeia aitejen aiticanio naka Kristo ka aibuses naetupakin ŋin." 
1Peter1:12 Aponi kes! kopukokinai ebe mere kanukec bonik, dimarai kanukus, apotu kijaanaki! ŋun nukidaun alimokin yes kwana, kama kaŋul lukilimonokinete yes Akiro Nukajokak, kanuka Emoyo Lokalaunan loejukunio kotoma akuj, akiro ŋun imielas imalaikan aireonokin." 
1Peter1:13 Kanuka ŋun koenata aŋabes nuka acoakus, kinyeis amer, komunosi cut asianut nakiinunio kotoma apukorio naka Yesu Kristo," 
1Peter1:14 Kwape idwe luerimaka, sirituputoro keimiel loka apak nakaolitekus nakolo," 
1Peter1:15 konye kwape eraar lokinyarit yes lokalaunan, koraut yesi da lukalaunak koponesio kus kere," 
1Peter1:16 naarai iwadikatai ebe, “Iraunos yesi lukalaunak, naarai arai eoŋ lokalaunan,”" 
1Peter1:17 Arai inyarito Papa ŋol loetubokini ŋinituŋanan kwape ejaatar aswamisioke, komam etiaki ituŋa, kolosenenete kakurian kapali nairaatar ikalotok," 
1Peter1:18 Kojenete ebe mam aponi kolakun yes kiboro luedaunos, kwape epuesa arai esabu, koponesiokus lutai lukirokunete kama kalukapapaakus," 
1Peter1:19 dimarai kaokot nuketiai Ioepol nuka Kristo, kwape nuka imerekek yenemamei aŋwal, karaida akemer." 
1Peter1:20 Aponi kisiaunai ajenun ŋes koriŋa akwapin kesuba, konye aponi kitakanunai kawasia naka apakio kanukus." 
1Peter1:21 Kotomakeŋ iraut luiyuunito Edeke, loetajaruni ŋes kokatwak, koinak da aibuses, kosodi aiyuunikus ka amunokus ajaut mama ejai Edeke." 
1Peter1:22 Naarai idaut aitalaun aijarakus kotoma arimarite abeit, kiton amin iinacan namam esoswai, kodunyakis noi aminanara kotoma otauon," 
1Peter1:23 Naarai aponi kourii yes irwan nakiareit, mere kikinyom luebosete, dimarai kalumam ebosete, kanuka akirot naka Edeke naejari naeperonori," 
1Peter1:24 Naarai “Akuan kere esubit bala anya, Ka aibusesuke kere da kwape aturot naka anya, Erinyorete anya, aturot da eraraar," 
1Peter1:25 Konye akirot naka Ejakait eperonori ikar kere.” Akirot ŋin da kes Akiro Nukaiokak nuaponi kolimokin yes. 
1Peter2:1 Aso kolemasi awai aronis kere, ka aimod kere, ka aisoswanut, ka ekokote, ka esiomit da kere." 
1Peter2:2 Kwape imukerun lupeurio kwape kwana kimielas akile nukemoyo nuemamei aimod, tetere kitopoloete yes adolore aitajario;" 
1Peter2:3 arai ipotu kiirata ajokis naka Ejakait. 
1Peter2:4 Ipote mamakeg, amoru naejari, naanerete ituŋa, konye kama ejai Edeke erai naseuna, naketiai loepol;" 
1Peter2:5 ka yes da kwape amor nukajarak kidukio koraut etogo lokemoyo, esasedotene lokalaunan, ainanakin asuban nukemoyo, nuitojokit Edeke kanuka Yesu Kristo." 
1Peter2:6 Naarai ejai toma nuiwadikatai ebe: “Koany, apesikini eoŋ koSion amoru nakapolon naka agor, Naseuna, naketiai loepol, Ido yeniyuuni ŋes mam irumete ileic.”" 
1Peter2:7 Aso mamakus luiyuunito erai ŋesi loketiai loepol; konye mamakec lumam iyuunito, “Amoru naanerete ikadukok, Araun nakapolon naka agor.”" 
1Peter2:8 Bobo da, “Amoru naitiguikinet, ka atiiba nakebiroron”; iguikinos akiro naarai mam erimarito, kwape elosikinitere kes." 
1Peter2:9 Konye yes iraas ajena naseuna, esasedotene loka ekabakane, ateker nakalaunan, ituŋa obe luka Edeke, kosodete alimonokin nukajokak nuka ŋol lokinyarauni yes anyoun kamuton alomar toma aicake nakaumokin." 
1Peter2:10 Mam kolo iraas ituŋake, konye kwana iraas ituŋa luka Edeke; mam kolo kitimitoi, konye kwana idumut aitimio." 
1Peter2:11 Luminan, keŋaiŋait yes kwape ikalotok ka ikeboiororok, ainacenen aiŋobel naka akuan, naejio kaijar." 
1Peter2:12 Kojaas kiponesio luejok kotoma Omo, tetere nakisiomiata yes bala ikeswamak nueroko, kitopoloosi Edeke kapaaran naka aanyanario kanuka aswamisiokus nuejokuka." 
1Peter2:13 Kononokikis ŋiniicorakinet naka ituŋa kanuka Ejakait, arai erai naka ekabaka naarai ŋes itelekarit kere;" 
1Peter2:14 arai naka ikayaitok, luijukuni ŋesi aitican luiswamaete nueroko, ka aiturit da ŋul luiswamaete nuejok," 
1Peter2:15 Naarai nuekoto Edeke kes nuta, yes aswam nuejok tetere itubutarete abaŋaanut naka ituŋa lueolito," 
1Peter2:16 Luijakakaete, kwabo mere luitwasamaete aijakak ŋin bala araparet aronis; konye bala ibulesin luka Edeke." 
1Peter2:17 Kitopoloorito ituŋa kere. Kominas iinacan. Koyoŋito Edeke, Kitopoloorito ekabaka," 
1Peter2:18 Yes ibulesin, kononokikis ikusijaka kayoŋite kere, mere lukajokak bonik ka luiyapeperas, konye ka lukadedeŋak da." 
1Peter2:19 Naarai na ŋes itojokitai, ituŋanan aŋirikin ican kanuka aiitun Edeke, isiriebio komameete akiro." 
1Peter2:20 Naarai aiturio anyoin, arai kidiakasi, kibapanar ititiŋikinete? Konye arai kiswamata nuejok, kisiriebi, ititiŋikinete, itojokitai ŋun, kama ejai Edeke." 
1Peter2:21 Naarai aponi konyarakin ŋin, naarai Kristo da aponi kisiriebai kanukus, kinyekinia yes naanyunet tetere ituparete ikukutuke," 
1Peter2:22 Mam ŋes abu kodiaka, karaida aimod adumun kaitukuke." 
1Peter2:23 Naamoromoroere ŋes, mam abu kinyaŋa aimor; naesiriebere, mam abu kitukurian; konye abu kijaikin mama ejai ŋol loetubokini kadolit." 
1Peter2:24 Abu ŋesi elopet kibwok adiakanaretawok kakuanake kokitoi, tetere nakidaunia atwanare kama ejaas adiakanareta, kajarata mama ejai adolit. Imacarinike kes kitaŋaleunete yes." 
1Peter2:25 Naarai ipotu kopaarito kwape amerekekin, konye kwana iboŋut mama ejai Ekecokon Ekaanyanaran da loka aijarakus." 
1Peter3:1 Yes aŋor da kwape kwaŋin, kononokikis ikiliokokus, tetere ice, karaida mam erimasi akirot, kiriasi iponesio luka aŋorokec komamei akirot," 
1Peter3:2 naeanyuniata iponesiokus luesegara, ka luka ayoŋit." 
1Peter3:3 Kinyek aisiritekus araut nakokuju, naka aicip itim, ka aidelonokin esabu, ka ainap inapen," 
1Peter3:4 konye korai etuŋanane loibwaa lokotau, anapito namam edaun naka emoyo loiyapepera ka aiyapaara, loerai loketiai loepol kakonyen nuka Edeke." 
1Peter3:5 Naarai kwape kwaŋin kolo sek kisirenenoto aŋor nukalaunak nuamunosi Edeke, kononokikinito da ikiliokokec." 
1Peter3:6 Kwape kerimaritor Sara Aburaam, konyarite ŋes ejakait. Iraas yesi da idweke, arai iswamaete ejok, komam kitukuriani etasuro kere." 
1Peter3:7 Yes da ikiliok kwape kwaŋin, kiboienenete kakusiŋor koomito nukec, kitopoloorito aberu kwape ibore yenitelekarit akalanyanut, naarai kes da akerumak nukaupakus nuka asianut naka aijar, kinyek akusiilip aitikokinio." 
1Peter3:8 Nakawasia, koraas kere luicamanara, luitimonoros, luiminanara kwape iinacan, luisiaka, luitasonos da." 
1Peter3:9 Sirinyaŋarete aronis kanuka aronis, karaida amorosit kanuka amorosit; konye gwai kilipakis arereŋ, naarai aponi konyarakin ŋin, tetere irumete asianut." 
1Peter3:10 Naarai ebe: “Yenimiela aijar, ka aanyun da apaarasia nuejok, Kitikok aŋajepeke kama karonis, Aitukuke da kinyek einer nukaimod." 
1Peter3:11 Konyou kotoma aronis, kiswama ajokis; Komo ainapakin, kotup da." 
1Peter3:12 Naarai esesenete akonyen nuka Ejakait ikadolitok, Itoikinit da akiike apupun ailipikec. Konye egirito akonyen nuka Ejakait ŋul luiswamaete aronis.”" 
1Peter3:13 Iŋai tope kiswamakini yes erono arai idunyakinito nuejok? 
1Peter3:14 Konye karaida kisiriebio kanuka adolit kisirereŋitoi, Sirikikuriakaros aitukurianakec, kwabo sirikiyaloŋoŋoto," 
1Peter3:15 konye kitalautu Kristo kotauonokus araut Ejakait. Kokapakina apaarasia kere aboŋokin ŋinituŋanan yenikiŋisi yes akiro nuka amun naejai tomakus, konye ca kaiyapepera ka ayoŋit," 
1Peter3:16 Kojaas kaomisio nuejok, tetere kaŋun nukisiomere, irumete ileic ŋul luemoromoroete ikusiponesio luejok kotoma Kristo." 
1Peter3:17 Naarai ejok aisiriebio kanuka aswam nuejok, arai ŋes naekot Edeke, itia kanuka aswam nueroko." 
1Peter3:18 Naarai Kristo da aponi kisiriebai kanuka adiakanar irwan atipet, lokadolit kanuka lumam edolito, tetere kiyauni mama ejai Edeke, nakearere akuanake, konye koinakinai aijar kotoma omoyo," 
1Peter3:19 loalosio da alimonokinia imoyon luejaas aidaris," 
1Peter3:20 lumam kerimasi kolo, naedareunitor atitiŋikin naka Edeke, kapaarasia nuka Noa, naetemonokinere ataker, kama etajarere ituŋa idis, kotoma akipi, kes ituŋa ikanykauni." 
1Peter3:21 Eputosi akiro ŋun kaibatisao, naitajari yes kwana, mere alemar elos loka akuan, dimarai einer kaomisio nuejok mama ejai Edeke, kanuka ajarun naka Yesu Kristo,"

1Peter4:1 Aso naarai Kristo aponi kisiriebai akuan, konapenenete yesi da lujiis luka aomisioit kaŋin, naarai yenisiriebio akuan enyek adiakar," 
1Peter4:2 tetere idaunete apaarasiakus nuideuna iriŋa ijaas toma akuan, mere bobo kanuka aiŋobel naka ituŋa, konye kanuka ŋun nuekot Edeke." 
1Peter4:3 Naarai apaarasia nuatuboros kidaunito aiswamaenen nuekotos Imo, alosenen toma abenyanut, aiŋobel, emeret, aboliasio, edeŋo, ka aima da aputosia nuketal." 
1Peter4:4 Isiwumokinito kes naarai mam ikerete nepepe kakes kotoma oponesio ŋupeŋul luutai, komoromoroete yes;"

1Peter4:7 Eapie awasia naka iboro kere; aso koomito kacoit, kinyeis da amer, tetere ilipenenete."

1Peter4:11 arai ejai yeninera, kwape yeninera akiro nuka Edeke; arai ejai yenijaanakini, kwape kanuka agogoŋ naekori Edeke; tetere itopolooritai Edeke kotoma kere kanuka Yesu Kristo. Aibuses ka ayait kojaas mamakeŋ ikar ka ikar. Amen," 
1Peter4:12 Luminan, siriwumokinete aitemio naka akim nakibunokinit yes, bala kidoik yes ibore yenikaumokin." 
1Peter4:13 Konye kiyalamasi naarai imorete aisiriebio naka Kristo, tetere naepukorere da akeibuses, iyalamas kailel naepol." 
1Peter4:14 Arai kiimoromoroi kanuka ekiror loka Kristo, isirereŋitoi, naarai kidoik yes Emoyo loka aibuses, ka loka Edeke da." 
1Peter4:15 Konye kinyek idio kayesi aisiriebio kanuka araut ikaaran, arai bo ikokolan, arai yeniswamai nueroko, arai kanuka araut yeniramaana;"

1Peter4:18 Bobo da, ebe, “Arai etiono aitajar ikadoliton, Ai bo do etakanunia yenikepali ka ikadiakanaran?”"

2Peter1:1 Simon Petero ebulesit ekiyakia da loka Yesu Kristo, Mama ejaas ŋul luadumutu aiyuun naketiai loepol naeriakas kanakosi kotoma adolit naka Edekewok, Eketajaran da Yesu Kristo:" 
2Peter1:2 Kiyatanakin asianut ka ainapakin mamakus toma ajenun Edeke ka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo. 
2Peter1:3 Naarai abu apedor naka eidekeoneke koinak oni akiro kere nuka aijar ka nuka ayoŋit Edeke, kanuka ajenun ŋol lokinyarauni oni kanuka aibusesuke ka ajokisike elopet;" 
2Peter1:4 nukiinakinia oni aisumunetake nuepolok nuketiai loepol; tetere kotoma kaŋun iraunete ikamorak luka einono loka Edeke, nuipotu kokuiata anyoun kotoma amudiario naejai toma akwapin kanuka aiŋobel."

2Peter1:9 Naarai yenemameete ŋun, erai imuduki yeneturiaitoi, kimurwokinite aitesegario adiakanaretake nukolo,"
